 māyā kalpita mātṛtā mukham ṛṣā dvaita prapañca āśrayaḥ satya jñāna sukha ātmakaḥ śruti śikhā utthā khaṇḍa dhī gocaraḥ mithyā bandha vidhūnanena paramānanda eka tāna ātmakam mokṣam prāpta iva svayam vijayate viṣṇuḥ vikalpa ujjhitaḥ śrī rāma viśva īśvara mādhavānām aikyena sākṣātkṛta mādhavānām sparśena nirdhūta tamaḥ rajobhyaḥ pāda utthitebhyaḥ astu namaḥ  rajobhyaḥ bahubhiḥ vihitā budhaiḥ para artham vijayante amita vistṛtā nibandhāḥ mama tu śrama eṣa nūnam ātmambharitām bhāvayitum bhaviṣyati iha śraddhā dhanena muninā madhusūdanena saṅgṛhya śāstra nicayam racita atiyatnāt bodhāya vādivijayāya ca sa tvarāṇām advaita siddhiḥ iyam astu mude budhānām vipratipatti vākyasya vicāra aṅga tvam tatra advaita siddheḥ dvaita mithyātva siddhi pūrvaka tvāt dvaita mithyā tvam eva prathamam upapādanīyam upapādanam ca sva pakṣa sādhana para pakṣa nirākaraṇābhyām bhavati iti tad ubhayam vāda jalpa vitaṇḍānām anyatamām kathām āśritya sampādanīyam tatra ca vipratipatti janya saṃśayasya vicāra aṅga tvāt madhya sthena ādau vipratipattiḥ pradarśanīyā yadi api vipratipatti janya saṃśayasya na pakṣatā sampādaka tayā upayogaḥ siṣā dhayiṣā viraha saha kṛta sādhaka māna abhāva rūpāyāḥ tasyāḥ saṃśaya aghaṭhita tvāt anyathā śruti ātma niścayavataḥ anumitsayā tad anumānam na syāt  vādya ādīnām niścayavat tvena saṃśaya asambhavāt āhārya saṃśayasya atiprasañjaka tvāt ca na api vipratipatteḥ svarūpata eva pakṣa pratipakṣa parigraha phalaka tayā upayogaḥ ‘tvayā idam sādhanīyaṃ ‘anena idam dūṣaṇīya amiti ādi madhya stha vākyāt eva tad lābhena vipratipatti vaiyarthyāt  tathā api vipratipatti janya saṃśayasya anum iti anaṅga tve api vyudasanīya tayā vicāra aṅga tvam asti eva tādṛśa saṃśayam prati vipratipatteḥ kvacid niścaya ādi pratibandhāt ajanaka tve api sva rūpa yogya tvāt  vādya ādīnām ca niścayavat tve niyama abhāvāt  ‘niścitau hi vādam kuruta iti ābhimānika niścaya abhiprāyam para pakṣam ālambya api ahaṃkāriṇaḥ  viparīta niścayavataḥ  jalpa ādau pravṛtti darśanāt  tasmāt  samaya bandha ādivat  sva kartavya nirvāhāya madhyasthena vipratipattiḥ pradarśanīyā eva tatra mithyātve vipratipattiḥ brahma pramāti riktā bādhya tve sati sattvena prati iti arham cit bhinnam pratipanna upādhau traikālika niṣedha pratiyogi na vā pāramārthikatva ākāreṇa ukta niṣedha pratiyogi na vā iti pakṣa tā avacchedaka vicāraḥ atra ca pakṣa tā avacchedaka sāmāna adhikaraṇyena sādhya siddheḥ uddeśya tvāt  pakṣa eka deśe sādhya siddhau  api siddha sādhana tā iti mate śukti rūpye siddha sādhana vāraṇāya brahma jñān itara ābādhya tvam pakṣa viśeṣaṇam yadi punar  pakṣa tā avacchedaka avacchedena eva sādhya siddhiḥ uddeśyā tadā eka deśe sādhya siddhau  api siddha sādhana abhāvāt tad vārakam viśeṣaṇam anupādeyam itara viśeṣaṇa dvayam tu tucche brahmaṇi ca bādha vāraṇāya ādaraṇīyam eva pratyekam vā vipratipattiḥ viyat mithyā na vā pṛthivī mithyā na vā iti evam viyat ādeḥ pratyekam pakṣa tve api na ghaṭa ādau sandigdha anaikāntika tā pakṣa sama tvāt  ghaṭa ādeḥ tathā hi pakṣe sādhya sandehasya anuguṇa tvāt  pakṣa bhinna eva tasya dūṣaṇa tvam vācyam ata eva uktam ‘sādhya abhāva niścayavati hetu sandehe eva sandigdhā anaikāntikate ati pakṣa tvam tu sādhya sandehavat tvam sādhya gocara sādhaka mānā abhāvavat tvam vā etad ca ghaṭa ādi sādhāraṇam ata eva tatra api sandigdha anaikāntika tvam na doṣaḥ pakṣa samatva uktiḥ tu pratijñā viṣayatva abhāva mātreṇa na ca tarhi pratijñā viṣaya tvam eva pakṣa tvam sva artha anumāne tad abhāvāt evam vipratipattau prācām prayogāḥ vimatam mithyā dṛśya tvāt  jaḍa tvāt  paricchinna tvāt  śukti rūpyavat iti na avayaveṣu āgrahaḥ atra sva niyāmaka niyatayā vipratipattyā laghu bhūtayā pakṣa tāvacchedaḥ  na viruddhaḥ samaya bandha ādinā vyavadhānāt tasya anumāna kāla asattve api upalakṣaṇa tayā pakṣa tāvacchedaka tvam yad vā vipratipatti viṣaya tā avacchedakam eva pakṣa tā avacchedakam prācām prayogeṣu api vimatam iti padam vipratipatti viṣaya tāvacchedaka avacchinnā abhiprāyeṇa ityadoṣaḥ atha sat asat vilakṣaṇatva rūpa prathama mithyātva vicāraḥ nanu kim idam mithyātvam sādhyate na tāvat  ‘mithyā śabdaḥ anirvacanīya tā vacana iti pañcapādikā vacanāt  sat asat anadhikaraṇatva rūpam anirvācya tvam tad hi kim sattva viśiṣṭa asattva abhāvaḥ uta sattva atyanta abhāvā sattva atyanta abhāva rūpam dharma dvayam āhosvit  sattva atyanta abhāvavat tve sati asattva atyanta abhāva rūpam viśiṣṭam na ādyaḥ sattva mātra ādhāre jagati sattva viśiṣṭa asattva anabhyupagamāt viśiṣṭa abhāva sādhane siddha sādhanāt  na dvitīyaḥ sattva asattvayoḥ eka abhāve apara sattva āvaśyaka tvena vyāghātāt  nirdharmaka brahmavat sattva rāhitye api sat rūpa tvena amithyātva upapattyā artha antarāt ca śukti rūpye abādhyatva rūpa sattva vyatirekasya sattvena bādhyatva rūpa asattvasya vyatireka asiddhyā sādhya vaikalyāt ca ata eva na tṛtīyaḥ pūrvavat vyāghātāt  artha antarāt sādhya vaikalyāt ca   iti ced  mā evam sattva atyanta abhāvā sattva atyanta abhāva rūpa dharma dvaya vivakṣāyām doṣa abhāvāt na ca vyāhatiḥ sā hi sattva asattvayoḥ paraspara viraha rūpa tayā vā paraspara viraha vyāpaka tayā vā paraspara viraha vyāpya tayā vā tatra na ādyaḥ tad anaṅgīkārāt  tathā hi atra tri kālābādhyatva rūpa sattva vyatirekaḥ  na asattvam kintu kvacid api upādhau sattvena pratīyamānatva anadhikaraṇa tvam tad vyatirekaḥ ca sādhya tvena vivakṣitaḥ tathā ca tri kāla bādhya vilakṣaṇa tve sati kvacid api upādhau sattvena pratīyamānatva rūpam sādhyam paryavasitam evañca sati na śukti rūpye sādhya vaikalyam api bādhyatva rūpā asattva vyatirekasya sādhya apraveśāt  na api vyāghātaḥ paraspara viraha rūpatva abhāvāt ata eva na dvitīyaḥ api sattva abhāvavati śukti rūpye vivakṣita asattva vyatirekasya vidyamāna tvena vyabhicārāt  na api tṛtīyaḥ tasya vyāghāta aprayojaka tvāt  gaḥtva aśva tvayoḥ paraspara viraha vyāpya tve api tad abhāvayoḥ uṣṭra ādau  ekatra saha upalambhāt  yad ca nirdharmakasya brahmaṇaḥ sattva rāhitye api sat rūpavat prapañcasya sat rūpa tvena amithyātva upapattyā artha antaram uktam tad na ekena eva sarva anugatena sarvatra sat prati iti upapattau brahmavat  prapañcasya pratyekam sat svabhāvatā kalpane māna abhāvāt anugata vyavahāra abhāva prasaṅgāt ca sat pratiyogika asat pratiyogika bheda dvayam vā sādhyam tathā ca ubhaya ātmaka tve anyatara ātmaka tve vā tādṛś bheda asambhavena tābhyām artha antara ana vakāśaḥ na ca asattva vyatireka aṃśasya asat bhedasya ca prapañce siddha tvena aṃśataḥ siddha sādhanam iti vācyam ‘guṇa ādikam guṇyādinā bhinna abhinnam samāna adhikṛta tvāt iti bheda abheda vādi prayoge tārkikā ādi aṅgīkṛtasya bhinna tvasya siddhau  api uddeśya pratītya siddheḥ yathā na siddha sādhanam tathā prakṛte api milita pratīteḥ uddeśya tvāt na siddha sādhanam yathā ca tatra abhede ghaṭaḥ kumbha iti sāmānādhikaraṇya pratīteḥ adarśanena milita siddhiḥ uddeśyā tathā prakṛte api sattva rahite tucche dṛśyatva adarśanena militasya tad prayojaka tayā milita siddhiḥ uddeśya iti samānam ata eva sattva atyanta abhāvavat tve sati asattva atyanta abhāva rūpam viśiṣṭam sādhyam iti api sādhu na ca militasya viśiṣṭasya vā sādhya tve tasya kutra api aprasiddhyā aprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tvam pratyekam siddhyā militasya viśiṣṭasya vā sādhane śaśa śṛṅgayoḥ pratyekam prasiddhyā śaśīyaśṛṅga sādhanam api syāt iti vācyam tathāvidha prasiddheḥ śukti rūpya eva ukta tvāt na ca nirdharmaka tvāt  brahmaṇaḥ sattva asattva rūpa dharma dvaya śūnya tvena tatra ativyāptiḥ sat rūpa tvena brahmaṇaḥ tad atyanta abhāva an adhikaraṇa tvāt nirdharmaka tvena eva abhāva rūpa dharmān adhikaraṇa tvāt ca iti diś  iti sat asat vilakṣaṇatva rūpa prathama mithyātva vicāraḥ atha dvitīya mithyātva upapattiḥ pratipanna upādhau traikālika niṣedha pratiyogi tvam vā mithyātvam nanu pratipanna upādhau traikālika niṣedhasya tāttvika tve advaita hāniḥ prātibhāsika tve siddha sādhanam vyāvahārika tve api tasya bādhya tvena tāttvika sattva avirodhi tayā artha antaram advaita śruteḥ atattva āvedaka tvam ca tad pratiyoginaḥ prātibhāsikasya prapañcasya pāramārthika tvam ca syāt iti ced na prapañca niṣedha adhikaraṇībhūta brahma abhinna tvāt niṣedhasya tāttvika tve api na advaita hānikara tvam na ca tāttvika abhāva pratiyoginaḥ prapañcasya tāttvikatva āpattiḥ tāttvika abhāva pratiyogini śukti rajata ādau kalpite vyabhicārāt  atāttvika eva vā niṣedhaḥ ayam atāt tvika tve api na prātibhāsikaḥ kintu vyāvahārikaḥ na ca tarhi niṣedhasya bādhya tvena tāttvika sattā virodhi tvāt artha antaram iti vācyam svāpna arthasya svāpna niṣedhena bādha darśanāt  niṣedhasya bādhya tvam pāramārthika sattva avirodhi tve na tantram kintu niṣedhya apekṣayā nyūna sattāka tvam prakṛte ca tulya sattāka tvāt  katham na virodhi tvam na ca niṣedhasya niṣedhe pratiyogi sattva āpattiḥ iti vācyam tatra hi niṣedhasya niṣedhe pratiyogisattvam āyāti yatra niṣedhasya niṣedha buddhyā pratiyogi sattvam vyavasthāpyate na niṣedha mātram niṣidhyate yathā rajate na idam rajatam iti jñāna anantaram idam na ārajatam iti jñānena rajatam vyavasthāpyate yatra tu pratiyogi niṣedhayoḥ ubhayoḥ api niṣedhaḥ tatra na pratiyogi sattvam yathā dhvaṃsa samaye prāc abhāva pratiyoginoḥ ubhayoḥ niṣedhaḥ evam ca prakṛte api niṣedha bādhakena pratiyoginaḥ prapañcasya niṣedhasya ca bādhanāt  tad niṣedhasya bādhya tve api prapañcasya tāttvika tvam ubhayoḥ api niṣedhya tāvacchedakasya dṛśyatva ādeḥ tulya tvāt  na ca atāttvika niṣedha bodhaka tve śruteḥ aprāmāṇya āpattiḥ brahma bhinnam prapañca niṣedha ādikam atāt tvikam iti atāttvika tvena bodhayantyāḥ śruteḥ aprāmāṇya asambhavāt  nanu tad niṣedha pratiyogi tvam kim sva rūpeṇa uta asat vilakṣaṇa svarūpānupamardena pāramārthikatva ākāreṇa vā na ādyaḥ śruti ādi siddha utpattikasya artha kriyā samarthasya avidyā upādānakasya tattva jñāna nāśyasya ca viyat ādeḥ rūpya ādeḥ ca dhī kāla vidyamānena asat vilakṣaṇa svarūpeṇa traikālika niṣedha ayogāt na api dvitīyaḥ abādhyatva rūpa pāramārthika tvasya bādhyatva rūpa mithyātva nirūpya tvena anyonya āśrayāt pāramārthika tvasya api sva rūpeṇa niṣedhe prathama pakṣa ukta doṣa āpattiḥ atas tasya api pāramārthikatva ākāreṇa niṣedhe anavasthā syāt  iti ced mā evam sva rūpeṇa eva traikā lika niṣedha pratiyogitvasya prapañce śukti rūpye ca aṅgīkārāt  tathā hi śuktau rajata bhrama anantaram adhiṣṭhāna tattva sākṣātkāre rūpyam na asti na āsīt   abhaviṣyati iti svarūpeṇa iva aneha nāne ati śrutyā ca prapañcasya sva rūpeṇa eva niṣedha pratīteḥ na ca tatra laukika paramārtha rajatam eva sva rūpeṇa niṣedha pratiyogī iti vācyam bhrama bādhayoḥ vaiyadhi karaṇa āpatteḥ aprasakta pratiṣedha āpatteḥ ca na ca tarhi utpatti ādi asambhavaḥ na hi aniṣiddha svarūpa tvam utpatti ādimattve tantram paraiḥ aniṣedhya rūpa tvena aṅgīkṛtasya viyat ādeḥ utpatti ādi anaṅgīkārāt  kintu vastu svabhāva ādikam anyat eva kiñcid  prayojakam vaktavyam tasya mayā api kalpitasya svīkārāt  na ca atra ekālika niṣedham prati sva rūpeṇa āpaṇa stham rūpyam pāramārthikatva ākāreṇa prātibhāsikam vā pratiyogī ati mata hāniḥ syāt iti vācyam asya ācārya vacasaḥ pāramārthika laukika rajata tādātmyena pratītam prātibhāsikam eva rajatam pratiyogi iti arthaḥ tad ca sva rūpeṇa pāramārthika tvena vā iti anāsthāyām vā śabdaḥ etāvat uktiḥ ca puras varti tādātmyena eva rajatam pratīyata iti mata nirāsa artham laukika parama artha rajata tādātmyena api pratīyata iti pratipādayitum ca tad uktam tattva pradīpikāyām atasmāt laukika parama artha rajatam eva na idam rajatam iti niṣedha pratiyogī iti pūrva ācāryāṇām vācoyuktiḥ api puras vartini rajata arthinaḥ pravṛtti darśanāt  laukika parama artha rajata tvena aparokṣa tayā pratītasya kāla traye api laukika parama artha rajatam idam na bhavati iti niṣedha pratiyogi tām aṅgīkṛtya netavye ati ayam āśayaḥ eka vibhakti anta pada upasthāpite dharmiṇi pratiyogini ca nañaḥ anyonya abhāva bodhakatva niyamasya vyutpatti bala siddha tvāt   ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ na bhavatī ti vākya va didam rajatam na bhavatī ti vākyasya anyonya abhāva bodhaka tve sthite abhilāpa janya pratīti tulya tvāt abhilapyamāna pratīteḥ na idam rajatam iti vākya abhilapya pratīteḥ anyonya abhāva viṣaya tvam eva tathā ca idaṃśabda nirdiṣṭe purovarti prātītika rajate rajata śabda nirdiṣṭa vyāvahārika rajata anyonyā bhāva pratīteḥ ārthikam mithyātvam anātra rajata am iti vākya abhilapya tu pratītiḥ atyanta abhāva viṣayā bhinna vibhakti anta pada upasthāpitayoḥ eva dharmi pratiyoginoḥ nañaḥ saṃsarga abhāva bodhakatva niyamāt sā ca puras varti pratīta rajatasya eva vyāvahārikam atyanta abhāvam viṣayīkaroti iti kaṇṭha uktam eva mithyātvam atas  na apasiddhāntaḥ  na anyathā ākhyāti āpattiḥ na vā grantha virodha iti anavadyam nanu evam atyantā sattva apātaḥ pratipanna upādhau traikālika niṣedha pratiyogi tvam hi anyatra asattvena sampratipannasya ghaṭa ādeḥ sarvatra traikālika niṣedha pratiyogi tvam paryavasitam anyathā teṣām anyatra sattva āpātāt  na hi teṣām anyatra sattā sambhavati iti tvad ukteḥ ca tathā ca katham asat vailakṣaṇyam na hi śaśaśṛṅga āderitaḥ anyat asat tvam na ca nirupākhya tvam eva tad asattvam nirupākhyatva padena eva vyākhyāyamāna tvāt  na api apratīyamāna tvam asat tvam asataḥ apratītau asat vailakṣaṇya jñānasya asat pratīti nirāsasya asat pada prayogasya ca ayogāt  na ca aparokṣa tayā apratīyamāna tvam tad  nitya atīndriyeṣu ati vyāpteḥ iti ced mā evam sarvatra traikālika niṣedha pratiyogi tvam yadi api tucchāniḥ vācyayoḥ sādhāraṇam tathā api kvacid api upādhau sattvena prati iti anarha tvam atyanta asattvam śūkti rūpye prapañce ca bādhāt  pūrvam na asti eva iti na tuccha tvāpattiḥ na ca bādhāt  pūrvam śūkti rūpyam prapañcaḥ  vā sattvena na pratīyate etad eva sat arthakena upādhipadena sūcitam śūnya vādibhiḥ sat adhiṣṭhāna bhrama anaṅgīkāreṇa kvacid api upādhau sattvena prati iti anarhatva rūpa asat vailakṣaṇyasya  kvacid api upādhau sattvena prati iti anarhatva rūpasya  śukti rūpye prapañce ca anaṅgīkārāt  nanu evam sati yāvat sat adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam paryavasitam tathā ca kevala anvayi ati anta abhāva pratiyogiṣu avṛttiṣu gagana ādiṣu tārkikāṇām siddha sādhanam yad adhikaraṇam yad sat  tad niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam tasya mithyātvam iti vivakṣāyām adhikaraṇa padena avṛtti nirākaraṇe api saṃyoga sambandhena samavāya sambandhena vā yad  ghaṭa adhikaraṇam samavāya sambandhena saṃyoga sambandhena vā ghaṭasya tad niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tayā sarveṣu vṛttimat su duruddharam siddha sādhanam yena sambandhena yadi asya adhikaraṇam tena sambandhena tad niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogitvam iti vivakṣāyām avyāpya vṛttiṣu saṃyoga ādiṣu siddha sādhanam iti ced na yena rūpeṇa yad adhikaraṇa tayā yad  pratipannam tena rūpeṇa tad niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvasya pratipanna padena sūci tattvāt  tad ca rūpam sambandha viśeṣaḥ avacchedaka viśeṣaḥ ca na hi sambandha viśeṣam antareṇa bhū tale ghaṭa adhikaraṇa tā pratīyate avacchedaka viśeṣam antareṇa vā vṛkṣe kapi saṃyoga adhikaraṇa tā tathā ca yena sambandha viśeṣeṇa yena ca avacchedaka viśeṣeṇa yad adhikaraṇa tā pratītiḥ yatra bhavitum arhati tena eva sambandha viśeṣeṇa tena eva ca avacchedaka viśeṣeṇa tad adhikaraṇaka atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam tasya mithyātvam iti paryavasite kva siddha sādhanam yadi punar  dhvaṃsa prāc abhāva pratiyogi tvam iva atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam ākāśa ādau na syāt  sādhaka māna abhāvasya tulya tvāt  iha ākāśaḥ  na asti iti pratyakṣa pratīti sambhavāt  anumāne ca anukūla tarka abhāvāt sāmānyatas  dṛṣṭa mātreṇa dhvaṃsa prāc abhāva pratiyogi tvasya api siddhi prasaṅgāt  tad vyatirekeṇa kasyacid  kāryasya anupapatteḥ abhāvāt ca evam saṃyoga sambandhena ghaṭavati bhū tale samavāya sambandhena ghaṭa abhāva sattve māna abhāvāt lāghavena ghaṭa atyanta abhāva tvena eva ghaṭa sāmāna adhikaraṇya virodhitva kalpanāt  sambandha viśeṣa praveśe ca gauravāt  ghaṭa samavāya mātra viṣaya tayā pratīteḥ upapatteḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvasya pratyakṣa siddha tvena ghaṭasya avṛttitva śaṅkā anudayāt ukta yukteḥ ca na ghaṭa ādeḥ atyanta abhāva sāmānādhikaraṇyam evam ca saṃyoga tad abhāvayoḥ na eka ādhikaraṇyam aagre vṛkṣaḥ kapi saṃyogī mūle ne ati pratīteḥ agra mūlayoḥ eva saṃyoga tad abhāvavat tayā upapatteḥ tadā sat mātra niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam eva mithyātvam mantavyam na ca evam sati bhāva abhāvayoḥ avirodhāt tad jñānayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ  na syāt iti vācyam bhinna sattākayoḥ avirodhe api sama sattākayoḥ virodhāt  yatra bhū tale yasya ghaṭasya atyanta abhāvaḥ  vyāvahārikaḥ tatra sa ghaṭaḥ  na vyāvahārika iti niyamāt  na ca evam sati aśuktiḥ iyam na rajata am iti jñāna viṣayībhūta abhāvasya vyāvahārika tvena puras varti pratīta rajatasya vyāvahārikatva apahāre api prātītika sattva anapahārāt  bādha uttara kāle api aidam rajata am iti pratītiḥ syāt iti vācyam tatra aiyam śukti ariti aparokṣa pramayā prātītika rajata upādāna ajñāna nivṛttau prātītika sattvasya api apahārāt śukti ajñānasya prātītika rajata upādāna tvena tad asatve prātītika rajata asattvasya āvaśyaka tvāt  ata eva yatra parokṣayā adhiṣṭhāna pramayā na bhrama upādāna ajñāna nivṛttiḥ tatra vyāvahārikatva apahāre api prātītikatva anapahārāt  atiktaḥ  guḍa ityādi pratītiḥ anuvartata eva evam akhaṇḍa brahma sākṣātkārāt pūrvam parokṣa bodhena prapañcasya vyāvahārikatva apahāre api pratītiḥ anuvartata eva adhiṣṭhāna ajñāna nivṛttau tu na anuvartiṣyate etena upādhi śabdena adhikaraṇa mātra vivakṣāyām artha antaram vāyu adhikaraṇaka atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tve api rūpasya āmithyatvāt  adhiṣṭhāna vivakṣāyām tu bhrama upādāna ajñāna viṣayasya adhiṣṭhāna tvena anyonya āśraya tvam jñānasya bhrama tve viṣayasya mithyātvam viṣayasya mithyātve ca jñānasya bhrama tvam iti parāḥ tam ukta rītyā adhikaraṇa vivakṣāyām doṣa abhāvāt na ca asa eva adhastā aditi śrutyā pratipanne deśa kāla ādi upādhau paramārtha taḥ  brahmaṇaḥ abhāvāt tatra ativyāptiḥ iti vācyam nirdharmake tasmin  abhāva pratiyogitva rūpa dharma abhāvāt na ca evam satya tvam api tatra na syāt  tathā ca asatyam jñānam ananta am iti ādi śruti vyākopa iti vācyam adhikaraṇa atirikta abhāva anabhyupagamena ukta mithyātva abhāva rūpa satya tvasya brahma svarūpa avirodhāt etena sva prakāśatva ādi api vyākhyātam para prakāśyatva abhāvaḥ  hi sva prakāśa tvam kāla pariccheda abhāvaḥ  nitya tvam deśa pariccheda abhāvaḥ  vibhu tvam vastu pariccheda abhāvaḥ pūrṇa tvam ityādi tathā ca bhāva bhūta dharmān āśraya tve api brahmaṇaḥ sarva dharma abhāva rūpa tayā na kā api anupapattiḥ iti sarvam avadātam iti sat asat vilakṣaṇatva rūpa dvitīya mithyātva vicāraḥ atha tṛtīya mithyātva vicāraḥ jñāna nivartya tvam vā mithyātvam nanu uttara jñāna nivartye pūrva jñāne ativyāptiḥ mudgara pāta ādi nivartye ca ghaṭa ādau  avyāptiḥ jñāna tvena jñāna nivartyatva vivakṣāyām api ayam doṣaḥ adhiṣṭhāna sākṣātkāra tvena nivartye śukti rajata ādau ca jñāna tvena jñāna nivartyatva abhāvāt sādhya vikala tā jñānatva vyāpya dharmeṇa jñāna nivartyatva vivakṣāyām jñānatva vyāpyena samṛti tvena jñāna nivartye saṃskāre ativyāptiḥ iti ced na jñāna prayukta avasthiti sāmānya viraha pratiyogi tvam hi jñāna nivartya tvam avasthitiḥ ca dvedhā sva rūpeṇa kāraṇa ātmanā ca satkārya vāda abhyupagamāt tathā ca mudgara pātena ghaṭasya sva rūpeṇa avasthiti virahe api kāraṇa ātmanā avasthiti viraha abhāvāt brahma jñāna prayukta eva sa iti na atīta ghaṭa ādau  ativyāptiḥ ata eva uttara jñāna nivartye pūrva jñāne na siddha sādhanam na vā viyat ādau brahma jñāna nāśya tve api tadvat eva mithyātva asiddhyā artha antaram uttara jñānena līnasya pūrva jñānasya sva kāraṇa ātmanā avasthānāt avasthiti sāmānya viraha anupapatteḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādau  avasthiti sāmānya virahe api tasya jñāna prayuktatva abhāvāt na ativyāptiḥ śukti rajata ādeḥ ca aparokṣa prati iti anyathā anupapattyā pratibhāsa kāle avasthiti aṅgīkārān na bādhaka jñānam vinā tad viraha iti na sādhya vikala tā ata eva uktam vivaraṇa ācāryaiḥ aajñānasya sva kāryeṇa pravilīnena vartamānena vā saha jñānena nivṛttiḥ bādha iti vārtika kṛdbhiḥ ca uktam atattvam asya ādi vākya uttha samyak dhī janma mātrataḥ avidyā saha kāryeṇa na āsīt asti bhaviṣyati iti asahakāryeṇa nāsī aditi līnena kāryeṇa saha nivṛtti abhiprāyam asaha kāryeṇa na bhaviṣyatī ati tu bhāvi kārya nivṛtti abhiprāyam iti anyat etad rūpya upādānam ajñānam sva kāryeṇa vartamānena līnena vā saha adhiṣṭhāna sākṣātkārāt nivartate tad tad rūpya upādānānām ajñānānām bheda abhyupagamāt iti na dṛṣṭānte sādhya vaikalyam mudgara pāta anantaram ghaṭaḥ  na asti iti pratītivat adhiṣṭhāna jñāna anantaram śuktyajñānam tad gata rūpyam ca na asti iti pratīteḥ sarva sammata tvāt  jñānatva vyāpya dharmeṇa jñāna nivartya tvam iti api sādhu uttara jñānasya pūrva jñāna nivartaka tvam ca na jñānatva vyāpya dharmeṇa kintu icchādi sādhāraṇena udīcya ātma viśeṣa guṇa tvena udīcya tvena vā iti na siddha sādhana ādi na api icchā ādi nivartye smṛti tve na jñāna nivartye saṃskāre ativyāptiḥ smṛti tvena smṛteḥ saṃskāra nivartaka tve māna abhāvāt smṛtau hi jātāyām saṃskāraḥ  dṛḍhaḥ  bhavati iti anubhava siddham teṣām dṛḍhatara tvam ca samāna viṣayaka saṃskāra aneka tvam iti adoṣaḥ vastutas tu sākṣātkāra tvena jñāna nivartya tvam vivakṣitam atas  na pūrva ukta doṣaḥ na api niścaya tvena jñānatva vyāpya dharmeṇa jñāna nivartye saṃśaye ativyāptiḥ iti sarvam avadātam iti tṛtīya mithyātva vicāraḥ atha caturtha mithyātva vicāraḥ sva āśraya niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva prata yogi tvam vā mithyātvam tad ca sva atyanta abhāva adhikaraṇa eva pratīyamāna tvam atas  pūrva vailakṣaṇyam dūṣaṇa parihāraḥ pūrvavat  na ca saṃyogini samavāyini vā deśe tad atyanta abhāvā sambhavaḥ sambhave tu upādānatva ādi anupapattiḥ iti vācyam kāle saha sambhavavat deśe api saha sambhava avirodhāt prāgabhāva sattvena upādānatva avirodhāt ca na ca atyanta abhāva adhikaraṇe prāgabhāvasya api anupapattiḥ iti vācyam kāle vyabhicārāt  na ca kāle prāc abhāva atyanta abhāvayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam idānīm ghaṭa atyanta abhāva idānīm ghaṭa prāgabhāva iti pratīti bālāt aṅgīkṛtam deśe tu tad ubhaya sāmānādhikaraṇye na kiñcid api pramāṇam iti vācyam mithyātva anumiteḥ śruti ādeḥ ca pramāṇa tvāt  viṣama sattāka bhāva abhāvayoḥ avirodhaḥ pūrvam upapāditaḥ na ca asati ativyāptiḥ sva atyanta abhāva adhikaraṇa eva sattvena pratīyamāna tvasya vivakṣita tvāt  na ca ataddhā eka āhuḥ asat eva idam agra āsī aditi śrutyā asataḥ sattva pratīteḥ tatra ativyāptiḥ duṣparihara iti vācyam asat eva idam agra āsī adityasya arthasya abhāva eva nañā pratipādyate na tvasataḥ sattvam virodhāt  atas  na ati vyāptiḥ sarvam ca anyat  pūrva uktam eva anusandhā iyam iti uparamyate iti caturtha mithyātva vicāraḥ atha pañcama mithyātva nirūpaṇam sat vivikta tvam vā mithyātvam sattvam ca pramāṇa siddha tvam pramāṇa tvam ca doṣa asaha kṛta jñāna karaṇa tvam tena svapna ādivat pramāṇa siddha bhinna tvena mithyātvam siddhyati pramāṇa siddha tvam ca abādhyatva vyāpyam iti anyat  atra api asati nirdharmake brahmaṇi ca ati vyāpti vāraṇāya sattvena pratīyamāna tvam viśeṣaṇam deyam tayoḥ sattva prakāraka pratīti viṣayatva abhāvāt ata eva ‘sat viviktatva amiti atra sattvam sattā jāti adhikaraṇa tvam vā abādhya tvam vā brahma rūpa tvam vā ādye ghaṭa ādau  avidyaka jāteḥ tvayā abhyupagamena asambhavaḥ dvitīye bādhyatva rūpa mithyātva paryavasānam tṛtīye siddha sādhanam iti nirastam anabhyupagamāt eva sat asat vilakṣaṇatva pakṣa ukta yuktayaḥ ca atra anusandheyāḥ avaśiṣṭam ca dṛṣṭānta siddhau vakṣyāmaḥ iti advaita siddhau pañcama mithyātva niruktiḥ atha mithyātva sāmānya upapattiḥ nanu ukta mithyā tvasya mithyātve prapañca satyatva āpātaḥ ekasmin dharmiṇi prasaktayoḥ viruddha dharmayoḥ eka mithyā tve apara satyatva niyamāt mithyātva satya tve ca tadvat eva prapañca satyatva āpatteḥ ubhaya tāpya dvaita vyāghāta iti ced na mithyātva mithyā tve api prapañca satyatva anupapatteḥ tatra hi viruddhayoḥ dharmayoḥ eka mithyā tve apara satvam yatra mithyātvā avacchedakam ubhaya vṛtti na bhavet  yathā paraspara viraha rūpa yaḥ rajatatva tada bhāvayoḥ śuktau yathā vā paraspara viraha vyāpaka yaḥ rajata bhinnatva rajata tvayoḥ tatra eva tatra niṣedhya tāvacchedaka bheda niyamāt prakṛte tu niṣedhya tāvacchedakam ekam eva dṛśyatva ādi yathā gaḥtva aśva tvayoḥ ekasmin gaje niṣedhe gaja tvā atyanta abhāva vyāpya tvam niṣedhya tāvacchedakam ubhayoḥ tulyam iti na ekatara niṣedhe anyatara satvam tadvat  yathā ca satyatva mithyā tvayoḥ na paraspara viraha rūpa tvam na vā paraspara viraha vyāpaka tvam tathā upapāditam adhastāt paraspara viraha rūpa tve api viṣama sattākayoḥ avirodhāt  vyāvahārika mithyā tvena vyāvahārika satyatva apahāre api kālpanika satyatva anapahārāt  tārkika mata siddha saṃyoga tad abhāvavat  satyatva mithyā tvayoḥ samuccaya abhyupagamāt ca ekasya sādhakena aparasya bādhya tvam viṣama sattāka tve prayojakam yathā śukti rūpya tad abhāvayoḥ eka bādhaka bādhya tvam ca sama sattāka tve prayojakam yathā śukti rūpya śukti bhinna tvayoḥ asti ca prapañca tad mithyā tvayoḥ eka brahma jñāna bādhya tvam atas  sama sattāka tvāt mithyātva bādhakena prapañcasya api bādhā anna advaita kṣatiḥ iti kṛtam adhikena iti mithyātva sāmānya upapattiḥ atha dṛśyatva hetu upapattiḥ nanu mithyātve sādhye hetūkṛtam yad dṛśya tvam tad api upapādanīyam tathā hi kim idam dṛśya tvam vṛtti vyāpya tvam vā phala vyāpya tvam vā sādhāraṇam vā kadācid  kathaṃcid cit viṣaya tvam vā sva vyavahāre sva ati rikta saṃvid antara apekṣā niyatiḥ vā asva prakāśa tvam vā na ādyaḥ ātmanaḥ  vedānta janya vṛtti vyāpya tvena tatra vyabhicārāt  ata eva na tṛtīyaḥ api na api dvitīyaḥ nitya atīndriye śukti rūpī ādau ca tad abhāvena bhāga asiddhi sādhana vaikalyayoḥ prasaṅgāt  na api caturthaḥ brahma pūrvam na jñātam idānīm vedāntena jñātam iti anubhavena ātmani vyabhicārāt  na api pañcamaḥ brahmaṇi api advitīyatva ādi viśiṣṭa vyavahāre saṃvid antara apekṣā niyati darśanena vyabhicārāt  na api ṣaṣṭhaḥ sa hi avedya tve satya parokṣa vyavahāra yogyatva abhāva rūpaḥ tathā ca śukti rūpya ādeḥ api aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya tvena sādhana vaikalyāt  iti ced mā evam phala vyāpyatva vyatiriktasya sarvasya api pakṣasya kṣoda kṣama tvāt  na ca vṛtti vyāpyatva pakṣe brahmaṇi vyabhicāraḥ anyathā brahma parāṇām vedāntānām vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt iti vācyam śuddham hi brahma na dṛśyam ayat tad adrā īśya miti śruteḥ kintu upahitam eva tad ca mithyā eva na hi vṛttidaśāyām anupahitam tad bhavati na ca asarva pratyaya vedye asmin brahma rūpe vyavasthite iti sva vacana virodha iti vācyam tasya api upahita para tvāt na ca evam sati śuddha siddhiḥ na syāt iti vācyam svata eva tasya prakāśa tvena siddha tvāt  nanu ajñāte dharmiṇi kasyacid  dharmasya vidhātum niṣeddhum vā aśakya tvena śuddhe dṛśya tvam niṣedha tā śuddhasya jñeya tvam avaśyam svīkaraṇīyam na ca sva prakāśa tvena svatas  siddhe śuddhe śrutyā dṛśyatva niṣedha iti vācyam śuddham sva prakāśam iti śabda janya viśiṣṭa vṛttau śuddhā prakāśe tasya sva prakāśatva asiddheḥ iti ced na vṛtti kāle vṛtti rūpeṇa dharmeṇa śuddhatva asambhavāt  śuddhasya vṛtti viṣaya tvam na sambhavati atas  aśuddham sva prakāśa am iti vākyasya lakṣaṇayā aśuddha tvam asva prakāśatva vyāpakam iti arthaḥ tathā ca aśuddhatva vyāvṛttyā śuddhe sva prakāśyatā paryavasyati yathā bheda niṣedhena abhinna tvam na ca śuddha padena abhidhayā lakṣaṇayā vā śuddhā prakāśe tad prayoga vaiyarthyam iti vācyam paryavasita artham ādāya sārthakatva upapatteḥ evam ca aśuddham na dṛśyam na mithye atyasya api aśuddha tvam dṛśyatva mithyā tvayoḥ vyāpakam iti etad paratvena śuddhe dṛśyatva mithyā tvayoḥ vyatirekaḥ paryavasyati etena sphuraṇa mātram eva mithyātve tantram lāghavāt  atas  asvataḥ sphurat api brahma mithyā eve ati śūnya vādi matam apāstam svatas sphuraṇa rūpa tāyāḥ śukti rūpya ādau  abhāvāt sphuraṇa viṣaya tvasya brahmaṇi asiddheḥ nanu viśiṣṭa jñāne viśeṣyasya api bhāne śrutyā viśiṣṭasya dṛśya tvena eva viśeṣyasya api dṛśya tvāt vyabhicāraḥ na ca aviṣṇave śipiviṣṭāye atyādau viśiṣṭasya devatātvavat viśiṣṭasya viṣaya tvam agnīṣomayoḥ militayoḥ devatā ātvavat vā militasya viṣaya tvam atas  na viśeṣye viṣaya tvam iti vācyam tadvat eva viśeṣaṇasya api aviṣaya tve bhāga asiddhi prasaṅgāt  iti ced na viśeṣyatā āpannasya viṣaya tve api kṣati abhāvāt  tasya mithyātva abhyupagamāt ata eva upahita viṣaya tve api upadheya viṣaya tvam akṣatam eva iti apāstam upahita ātmanā tasya api mithyātva abhyupagamāt jñāna antara viṣaya tvena viśeṣaṇe bhāga asiddhi abhāvāt ca nanu vedānta janyā khaṇḍa vṛtteḥ upahita viṣaya tve tadānīm upādhi antara abhāvena tasyāḥ  eva upadhāyaka tvāt sva viṣayatva āpattiḥ na ceṣṭāpattiḥ śābda bodhe śabdān upasthita ābhāna niyamena vṛtteḥ śabdānupasthitāyā bhāna anupapatteḥ yathā kathañcit upapattau vā na tatas ajñāna tad kāryayoḥ nivṛttiḥ syāt  ajñāna tad kāryā viṣayaka jñānasya eva tad ubhaya nivartaka tvāt  anyathā aaham ajñaḥ ayam ghaṭaḥ ityādi jñānānām api upahita viṣayaka tvena ajñāna nivartakatva prasaṅga iti ced na vṛtteḥ śābda vṛttau  anavabhāsamānāyā eva upadhāyakatva abhyupagamāt tad uktam kalpa taru kṛdbhiḥ aśuddham brahma iti viṣayīkurvāṇā vṛttiḥ sva sva itara upādhi nivṛtti hetuḥ udayate svasyā api upādhitva aviśeṣāt  evam ca na anupahitasya viṣaya tā vṛtti uparāgaḥ atra sattayā upayujyate na bhāsya tayā viṣaya koṭi praveśene ati ayam abhiprāyaḥ yathā ajñāna upahitasya sākṣi tve api na ajñānam sākṣi koṭau praviśati jaḍa tvāt  kintu sākṣya koṭau  eva evam vṛtti upahitasya viṣaya tve api na vṛttiḥ viṣaya koṭau praviśati svasyāḥ sva viṣayatva anupapatteḥ kintu svayam aviṣayaḥ api caitanyasya viṣaya tām sampādayati iti na kā api anupapattiḥ etena jñāna ajñānayoḥ eka viṣaya tvam vyākhyātam ajñānam api hi sva upadhāna daśāyām eva brahma viṣayīkaroti sva anupādhāna daśāyām svasya eva abhāvāt tathā ca jñāna ajñānayoḥ ubhayoḥ api upādhi aviṣayaka tve sati upahita viṣayaka tvāt  samāna viṣaya tvam asti eva etena upādhi viṣaya jñānānām ajñāna anivartaka tvam vyākhyātam ajñānasya upādhi aviṣaya tvena samāna viṣayatva abhāvāt  samāna viṣaya tvena eva tayoḥ nivartya nivartaka bhāvāt vastutas tu śabda ajanya vṛtti viṣaya tvam eva dṛśya tvam anyathā śaśa viṣāṇam tuccham iti ādi śabda janya vṛtiḥ viṣaye tucche vyabhicārasya duruddhara tvāt  evam ca sati śuddhasya vedānta janya vṛtti viṣaya tve api na tatra vyabhicāraḥ tuccha śuddhayoḥ śabda ajanya vṛtti viṣayatva anabhyupagamāt yad vā sa prakāraka vṛtti viṣaya tvam eva dṛśya tvam prakāraḥ ca sā upākhyaḥ kaścid dharmaḥ tena niṣprakāraka jñāna viṣayībhūte śuddhe nirupākhya dharma prakāraka jñāna viṣayībhūte tucche ca na vyabhicāraḥ abhāva tvasya api sa upākhya tvāt abhāvatva prakāraka jñāna viṣayībhūte abhāve na bhāga asiddhiḥ upākhyā ca asti iti dhī viṣayatva ādi iti anyat etena vṛtti vyāpya phala vyāpyayoḥ sādhāraṇam vyavahāra prayojaka viṣayatva rūpam dṛśya tvam api hetuḥ brahmaṇi tucche ca vyabhicāra parihāra upāyasya ukta tvāt yad vā dṛśya tvam cit viṣaya tvam tad ca yathā kathañcid cit sambandhitva rūpam hetuḥ tad ca na caitanye abhede bhedana āntarīyakasya sambandhasya abhāvāt  atas  na vyabhicāraḥ tucche ca vyabhicāraḥ pariharaṇīyaḥ yad vā sva vyavahāre sva ati rikta saṃvid apekṣā niyati rūpam dṛśya tvam hetuḥ saṃvid śabdena viṣaya abhivyaktam vā vṛtti abhivyaktam vā  śuddham vā  caitanya mātram abhipretam tathā ca ghaṭa ādau nitya atīndriye sākṣi bhāsye ca sarvaḥ api vyavahāraḥ sva ati rikta saṃvid sā apekṣa iti na asiddhiḥ vyavahāraḥ ca sphuraṇa abhivadana ādi sādhāraṇaḥ tatra brahmaṇaḥ sphuraṇa rūpe vyavahāre nitya siddhe sva ati rikta saṃvid apekṣā na asti iti niyati padena vyabhicāra vāraṇam sva gocara yāvat vyavahāre sva ati rikta saṃvid apekṣāyām paryavasānāt  ata eva asvaprakāśatva rūpam dṛśya tvam api hetuḥ sva prakāśa tvam hi sva aparokṣa tve sva atirikta anapekṣa tvam ayat sākṣāt aparokṣāt  brahme ati śruteḥ tathā ca anya an adhīna aparokṣa tvam paryavasyati tad nirūpita bhedavat tvam hetuḥ tad ca nitya parokṣe anya adhīna aparokṣe ca ghaṭādau  asti iti na asiddhiḥ na ca brahmaṇaḥ api brahma pratiyogikaka alpanika bhedavat tvāt tatra vyabhicāraḥ akalpita bhedasya kvāpi asiddha tvāt iti vācyam tad bhedasya anya an adhīna aparokṣatva rūpa dharma anirūpita tvāt jīvatveśvaratva ādi rūpasya anya dharmasya tad nirūpaka tvāt  evam ca āvedya tve satya parokṣa vyavahāra yogyatva abhāva rūpam dṛśya tvam api hetuḥ na ca phala vyāpyatva abhāva viśiṣṭam yad aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya tvam tasya brahmaṇi iva avidyā antaḥkaraṇa ādau śukti rūpī ādau ca sattvena asiddhi sādhana vaikalye iti vācyam ajñāna nivartaka vṛtti viṣayatva yogya tvasya aparokṣa vyavahāra yogyatva padena vivakṣita tvāt  tasya ca avidyā ādau śukti rūpī ādau ca asatvāt na asiddhi sādhana vaikalye yathā ca ghaṭa ādeḥ phala vyāpya tvam tathā agre vakṣyāmaḥ avidyā nivṛtteḥ pañcama prakāratva pakṣe tatra vyabhicāra vāraṇāya ajñāna kāla vṛtti tvam hetu viśeṣaṇam deyam tena eva tucche api na vyabhicāraḥ evam eva sarveṣu hetuṣu vyabhicāra parihārāya yatanīyam sat viviktatva mātre tu sādhye tucche pañcama prakāra avidyā nivṛttau ca na vyabhicāra gandhaḥ api iti sarvam avadātam iti advaita siddhau dṛśyatva hetu upapattiḥ atha jaḍatva hetu upapattiḥ jaḍa tvam api hetuḥ nanu   kim idam jaḍa tvam ajñātṛ tvam vā ajñāna tvam vā anātma tvam vā na ādyaḥ tvad mate pakṣa nikṣiptasya eva aham arthasya jñātṛ tvāt tatra asiddheḥ śuddha ātmanaḥ ajñātṛ tvena tatra vyabhicārāt ca na api dvitīyaḥ vṛtti uparakta caitanyasya eva jñāna tvena kevalāyāḥ  vṛtteḥ kevalasya caitanyasya ca ajñāna tvena vṛttau  asiddhi parihāre api caitanye vyabhicāra tādavasthyāt  na api tṛtīyaḥ ātma tvasya eva nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt  tad hi na jāti viśeṣaḥ tvayā ātmana ekatva abhyupagamāt viśiṣṭa ātmanām bhede api teṣām pakṣa kukṣi nikṣipta tvāt  na api ānanda rūpa tvam vaiṣayikā nande tad vyatirekasya hetoḥ asiddheḥ tasya api ātma tve ajñāna pakṣa ukta doṣaḥ prasañjanīya iti ced  mā evam dvitīya tṛtīya pakṣayoḥ doṣa abhāvāt tathā hi aajñāna tvam jaḍa tvam i ati pakṣe na ātmani vyabhicāraḥ artha upalakṣita prakāśasya eva jñāna tvena mokṣa daśāyām api tad anapāyāt  na ca abhāve sa pratiyogi tvavat icchā jñāna ādiṣu api sa viṣayaka tvasya svābhāvika tvāt icchāyām iva jñāne api tasya samāna sattāka tvam iti vācyam jñānasya hi sa viṣaya tvam viṣaya sambandhaḥ sa ca na tāttvikaḥ kintvā adhyāsikaḥ vakṣyamāṇa rītyā tāttvika sambandhasya nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt  atas  na tasya svābhāvika tvam na hi śuktau rūpyam svābhāvikam evañca jñāna upādhikasya eva sa viṣaya tvasya icchā ādiṣu abhyupagamāt nitarām tatra tasya svābhāvika tvam na ca evam jñānavat  viṣaya sambandham vinā api kadācid icchāyāḥ sattva āpattiḥ iti   vācyam sa viṣayatva prayojaka upādhi apekṣayā adhika sattāka tvasya tatra prayojaka tvāt  icchāyāḥ ca tad samāna sattāka tvāt na ca tvayā mokṣa avasthāyām ātmanaḥ  nirviṣayatva aṅgīkārāt ānandā prakāśe tad apum artha tvam syāt iti vācyam tadā hi ānanda eva prakāśaḥ  natu ānandasya prakāśa tvam artha upalakṣita prakāśa tvam vā tadā asti eva iti na jñānatva hāniḥ iti uktam nanu tathā api jñātuḥ abhāvāt  tadā tad na jñānam na hi bhoktṛ hīnā bhuji kriyā bhavati na ca anādi tvena kriyā rūpatva abhāvāt anapekṣa tvam iti vācyam anādeḥ prāgabhāvasya pratiyogini jāteḥ vyaktau jīva brahma vibhāgasya dharma pratiyoginoḥ ajñānasya ca āśraya viṣayayoḥ brahma sattāyāḥ ca kartari apekṣā darśanāt  anyathā aasti brahme atyādau kartari lakāraḥ  na syāt  evam ca atīta ādi jñānasya īśvara jñānasya ca utpatti artham artha anapekṣa tve api tad nirūpyatva darśanena jñānasya jñātṛ jñeya nirūpya tvam svabhāvaḥ anyathā aidam aham jānāmī ati anubhavaḥ  na syāt  ajñātuḥ artha prakāśasya jñāna tvā aditi vivaraṇa virodhaḥ ca syāt    iti ced na jāteḥ vyakti nirūpya tve api kadācid tad asambandhavat upapatteḥ sambandha prayoja ka upa adhi apekṣayā adhika sattāka tvāt ata eva jñānasya sa jñeya tvam sa jñātṛ tvam ca na svābhāvikam tathā hi sa jñeya tvam tāvat  jñeya janya tvam vā jñeya vyāpya tvam vā na ādyaḥ parokṣa jñāne īśvara jñāne ca abhāvāt  na api dvitīyaḥ ayadā jñānam tadā artha iti kālika vyāptau pūrvavat  vyabhicārāt  daiśika vyāptiḥ tu dūra nirastā eva na ca   yadā aaparokṣa jñānam tadā artha iti kālika vyāptau na asti vyabhicāraḥ ātmā ca ayat  sākṣāt  aparokṣāt  brahme ati śruteḥ aparokṣa jñāna rūpa iti saḥ api artha vyāpta iti vācyam īśvara jñāne yogi jñāne ca vyabhicārāt  ayat aindriyakam jñānam tadā artha iti tu vyāptiḥ sarva sammatā na ca ātma rūpe jñāne aindriyaka tvam asti iti na tayā virodhaḥ nanu ayadā aparokṣam jñānam tadā artha iti vyāpti anabhyupagame aidam rajata amiti aparokṣa jñānāni atha anupapattyā anirvacanīya rajata siddhiḥ na syāt  artham vinā api aparokṣatva upapatteḥ iti ced na aidam rajatam aham jānāmī atyanusandhīyamānam yad  jñāna viṣaya tvam tasya āśraya antara anupapattyā anirvacanīya rajata siddheḥ vakṣyamāṇa tvāt  ata eva parokṣa bhrame api anirvacanīya artha siddhiḥ janyā aparokṣa tvena vā artha vyāpyatā ārṣa jñānasya aparokṣatva anabhyupagamāt tathā ca na anirvacanīya rajata siddī anupapattiḥ evam sa jñātṛka tvam api kim jñātṛ janya tvam jñātṛ vyāpya tvam jñātṛ samaveta tvam vā ādye īśvara jñāne vyabhicāraḥ jñāna nitya tvasya sādhayiṣyamāṇa tvāt ca dvitīye api aprayojaka tā na tṛtīyaḥ jñāna janya tvavat jñāna samaveta tvasya api sambhavāt  jñānasya guṇatva kriyā tvayoḥ anabhyupagamena dravya aśrayatva anumāna ayogāt kadācid  jñātṛ jñeya sambandhena eva anubhavasya vivaraṇa vākyasya ca upapatteḥ aasti brahme ati ca lakāraḥ  na brahma sattām prati brahmaṇaḥ kartṛ tvam āha nitya tvena tad asambhavāt  kintu sādhutva artha iti draṣṭavyam nanu pramā bhram abhinnam na jñānam na ca ātma svarūpam jñānam pramā tad viṣayasya avidyā ādeḥ tāttvikatva āpātāt na ca apramā doṣa janyatva āpātāt iti ced na tārkika siddha īśvara jñānavat ghaṭa ādi nirvikalpakavat ca svabhāvata ubhaya vailakṣaṇyena api upapatteḥ tatra api īśvara jñānasya pramātve guṇa janya tvasya bhrama tve doṣa janya tvasya ca āpatteḥ niṣprakārake ca nirvikalpake tadvati tad prakāraka tvasya tad abhāvavati tad prakāraka tvasya ca anupapatteḥ janya sa vikalpaka tvena bhrama pramānyataratva niyame ca asmākam kṣati abhāvāt  vilakṣaṇa vṛtti dvaya uparāgeṇa ca svabhāvataḥ  bhrama pramā vilakṣaṇasya api ātma jñānasya tad ubhaya rūpeṇa vyavahāra upapatteḥ na ca jñāna pada vācya bhinnatva vivakṣāyām upādheḥ api jñāna pada vācya tvāt tatra asiddhiḥ jñāna pada lakṣya bhinnatva vivakṣāyām tu ghaṭa ādeḥ api jñāna pada lakṣya tvāt tatra api asiddhiḥ iti vācyam jñāna pada janya pratīti viśeṣya bhinnatva vivakṣāya amukta doṣa abhāvāt evam ānanda bhinnatva rūpam anātma tvam upapādyam vaiṣayikā ānandasya api brahma rūpa tvāt  tad upādhi mātrasya eva utpatti vināśa pratiyogi tvāt na ca jñāna bhinna tvasya ānanda bhinna tvasya ca kālpanikasya brahmaṇi sattvāt  tatra vyabhicāra iti vācyam dharmi samāna sattāka tad bhedasya hetu tvāt  anaupādhika tvena vā bhedaḥ  viśeṣaṇīyaḥ tucche pañcama prakāra avidyā nivṛttau ca vyabhicāra parihāraḥ pūrvavat  evam asva prakāśa tvam vā jaḍa tvam tad ca pūrvam eva upapāditam iti śivam iti advaita siddhau jaḍatva hetu upapattiḥ atha paricchinnatva hetu upapattiḥ paricchinna tvam api hetuḥ tad ca deśataḥ kālataḥ  vastutas ca iti trividham tatra deśataḥ paricchinna tvam atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam kālataḥ paricchinna tvam dhvaṃsa pratiyogi tvam vastutas  paricchinna tvam anyonya abhāva pratiyogi tvam nanu samavāya sambandhena atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam ātmani vyabhicāri tasya api ākāśa ādivat  kvāpi asamaveta tvāt  saṃyoga sambandhena atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam ākāśa ādau  asiddham tasya yāvat mūrta yogitva niyamāt amūrta niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogitva abhiprāye tu ātmani vyabhicāraḥ tad avasthaḥ sarva sambandhitva abhāva vivakṣāyām api sarva sambandha śūnye parama ātmani vyabhicāraḥ ajñāne sarva sambandhinyasiddhiḥ ca dhvaṃsa pratiyogi tvam api ākāśa ādau  asiddham teṣām paraiḥ nityatva abhyupagamāt anyonya abhāva pratiyogi tvam ca ātmani vyabhicāri tasya jaḍa niṣṭhā anyonya abhāva pratiyogi tvāt anyathā jaḍatva āpatteḥ iti ced na atyanta abhāve anyonya abhāve ca pratiyogi sama sat tākatva aviśeṣaṇena ātmani vyabhicāra parihārāt  ajñāna ākāśa ādau ca sva samāna sattāka atyanta abhāva anyonya abhāva pratiyogitva sattvena asidhya bhāvāt  avidyā kāśa ādeḥ vyāvahārikasya pāramārthika abhāva pakṣe asvān yūna sattāke ati viśeṣaṇam deyam ata eva prātibhāsika śukti rūpya ādeḥ vyāvahārikā bhāva pratiyogi tve api na sādhana vaikalyam nirukta mithyātva prakārāṇām evaṃrūpatva abhāvāt na sādhya aviśiṣṭa tā dhvaṃsa pratiyogi tvam ca ākāśa ādau na asiddham atasmāt vā etasmāt ātmana ākāśaḥ sambhūtaḥ iti śruti siddha janya tvena anumita tvāt  aākāśavat  sarva gataḥ ca nitya iti atra ca ātma nidarśana tvam sva samāna kalīna sarva gata tvena ābhūta samplava avasthāyi tvena ca iti draṣṭavyam aatas anyat ārtha am iti śṛtyā anātma mātrasya eva vināśitva pratipādanāt  ata eva ghaṭa ādayaḥ sva anugata pratibhāse vastuni kalpitāḥ vibhakta tvāt  yathā sarpa mālā ādikam sva anugata pratibhāse rajjvā idam aṃśe vibhajyate evam brahmaṇi anugacchati ghaṭa ādikam vibhajyate asan ghaṭaḥ san paṭa iti ānanda bodha uktam api sādhu vibhakta śabdena sva samāna sattāka bheda pratiyogitva rūpa vastu paricchedasya vivakṣita tvāt  na brahma tucchayoḥ vyabhicāraḥ na ca akhaṇḍaḥ gaurmuṇḍaḥ  gau ariti evamādi sva anugata pratibhāse gaḥtva ādau vyaktīnām akalpita tvāt vyabhicāra iti vācyam sat sāmānya atirikta gaḥ tvā ādi sāmānya anabhyupagamāt gaḥtva ādi abhyupagame api gaḥtva ādi vyañjaka tāvacchedaka sāmānya anabhyupagamāt vyakti viśeṣāṇām eva ananugatānām sāsnādi mattva ādi upādhi anugatānām vā tad vyañjaka tvavat vyakti viśeṣa viśiṣṭa tvena sat sāmānyasya eva tad tad vyavahāra janakatva upapatteḥ ata eva aghaṭa ādikam sat rūpe kalpitam pratyekam tad anuviddha tvena pratīyamāna tvāt  pratyekam candra anuviddha jala taraṅga candravat iti brahma siddhi kāra uktam api sādhu nanu sat arthasya brahmaṇaḥ rūpa ādi hīnasya asaṃsāram ajñāna āvṛtasya śabda eka gamyasya katham ghaṭaḥ san  ityādi buddhi viṣaya tā syāt  tathā ca aghaṭaḥ anityaḥ iti anena ghaṭa gata anitya tā iva aghaṭaḥ sanni atyanena api ghaṭa gatam eva sattvam gṛhyate na ca sva rūpeṇa apratyakṣasya rāhoḥ candra avacchedena iva brahmaṇaḥ api ghaṭa ādi avacchedena eva pratyakṣata iti vācyam śabda ādi avacchinnasya api gagana ādeḥ śrāvaṇatva ādi āpātāt  rāhoḥ tu dūra doṣeṇa ajñātasya nīlasya yogyasya śukla bhāsvara candra sambandhāt cākṣuṣa tā uktā iti ced na yatas  sat ātmanā na brahmaṇaḥ  mūla ajñānena āvṛta tvam kintu ghaṭa ādi avacchinna śakti ajñānena eva tathā ca cakṣuḥ ādi janya vṛttyā tad āvaraṇa bhaṅge sati asan ghaṭa iti atra brahmaṇaḥ sphuraṇe bādhaka abhāvāt na ca rūpa ādi hīna tayā cākṣuṣatva ādi anupapattiḥ bādhikā iti vācyam pratiniyata indriya grāhyeṣu eva rūpa ādi apekṣā niyamāt sarva indriya grāhyam tu sat rūpam brahma na atas  rūpa ādi hīna tve api cākṣuṣatva ādi anupapattiḥ sattāyāḥ paraiḥ api sarva indriya grāhyatva abhyupagamāt ca tad uktam vārtika kṛdbhiḥ aatas anubhava eva ekaḥ  viṣayaḥ ajñāta lakṣaṇaḥ akṣa ādīnām svatas siddhaḥ  yatra teṣām pramāṇa tā iti kālasya ca rūpa ādi hīnasya mīmāṃsaka ādibhiḥ sarva indriya grāhyatva abhyupagamāt na ca śabda avacchinnasya ākāśasya api śrāvaṇa tvam syāt iti vācyam svabhāvataḥ  yogyasya hi kenacid nimittena pratiruddha yogya tākasya avacchedaka ādinā yogya tā sampādyate yathā dūra doṣeṇa pratiruddha yogya tākasya rāhoḥ candra sambandhena evañca āvaraṇena pratiruddha yogya tākam brahma ghaṭa ādi avacchedena yogyam bhavati nabhaḥ tu svabhāva ayogyam eva na pratiruddha yogya tākam yena śabda avacchedena yogyam bhavet  yad vā dravya grahe cakṣuṣaḥ  rūpa apekṣā nanu anya grahe brahma tu na dravyam aasthūlam anaṇva hrasvam adīḥ ghaḥ am iti śrutyā caturvidha parimāṇa niṣedhena dravyatva pratiṣedhāt  atas  na anupapattiḥ astu vā dravyam tathā api adhyasta dravya tvavati guṇa ādau rūpān apekṣa cākṣuṣatva darśanena dharmya nyūna sattāka dravya tvavati eva cakṣū rūpam apekṣate brahmaṇi ca dravya tvam dharmī apekṣayā nyūna sattākam eva iti na tad grahe rūpa ādi apekṣā kalpita tvam ca svābhāvavati pratīyamāna tvam vā svarūpa jñāna nivartya tvam vā iti anyat etad tasmāt  paricchinna tvam api bhavati hetuḥ iti siddham iti paricchinnatva hetu upapattiḥ atha aṃśitva hetu upapattiḥ cit sukha ācāryaiḥ tu ‘ayam paṭaḥ etad tantu niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogī aṃśitvāt  itara aṃśivat  iti uktam tatra tantu padam upādāna param etena upādāna niṣṭhāti anta abhāva pratiyogitva lakṣaṇa mithyātva siddhiḥ na ca kāryasya kāraṇa abhedena tad anāśrita tvāt siddha sādhanam anāśrita tvena ani āśrita tvena vā upapattyā artha antaram ca iti vācyam abhede kārya kāraṇa bhāva vyāhatyā kathañcid api bhedasya avaśya abhyupeya tvāt na ca atat ananya tvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhya iti adhikaraṇa virodhaḥ upādāna vyatirekeṇa upādeyam na asti iti asya eva tad artha tvāt bādhāt tanmātra āśrita tvena pakṣa viśeṣaṇāt vā na artha antaram na ca prakṛte api bādhaḥ tasya uddhariṣyamāṇa tvāt na ca atyanta abhāvasya prāmāṇikatva aprāmāṇikatva vikalpa avakāśaḥ tasya prāk eva nirasta tvāt  na ca kasyacid  paṭasya saṃyoga vṛttyā etad tantuṣu sattvena tatra vyabhicāra iti vācyam tad samavetasya tad niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam aṅgīkurvataḥ tad saṃyoginaḥ tad niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogitva aṅgīkāreṇa pakṣa sama tvāt  na ca avyāpya vṛtti tvena artha antaram paṭa tada bhāvayoḥ eka adhikaraṇa vṛttau virodhasya jagati datta jala añjalitva prasaṅgāt  saṃyoga tadabhāvayoḥ api eka adhikaraṇa vṛttitva anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā etad tantutva avacchinna vṛtti tvam atyanta abhāvasya viśeṣaṇam deyam evam etad kālīna tvam api tena kāla antarīya abhāvam ādāya na artha antaram na ca iha tantuṣu paṭa iti pratyakṣa bādhaḥ tasya bhrama sādhāraṇa tayā candra prādeśikatva pratyakṣa vada prāmāṇya śaṅkā skandita tvena ābādhaka tvāt  bādha uddhāre ca vistareṇa etad vakṣyāmaḥ na ca anyāsamavetasya aṃśi tvam etad tantu samaveta tvam vinā na yuktam iti viruddhaḥ  hetuḥ iti vācyam etad tantu niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tve api etad tantu samavetasya sattvena aṃśitvasya sādhyena avirodhāt  etad niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva pratiyogi tvam hi etad samaveta tve prayojakam na bhavati para mate kevala anvayi dharma mātrasya etad samavetatva āpatteḥ kintu etad niṣṭha prāgabhāva pratiyogitva ādikam tad ca etad niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tve api na viruddham iti upapāditam adhastāt etad samaveta tvam ca etad upādānaka tvam na tu nitya sambandha śāli tvam tasya anabhyupagamāt nanu ayam paṭa etad tantu niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogī na etad tantu ārabdha tvāt  vyatirekeṇa paṭa antaravat iti pratirodhaḥ naca aprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tvam etad niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva pratiyogi tvam kiñcid niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi saṃsarga abhāva pratiyogitva vyāpya tvāt prāc abhāva pratiyogi tvavat iti sāmānyatas tad prasiddheḥ na ca ākāśa atyanta abhāvasya ghaṭa ādau saṃsarga abhāva pratiyogitva vyāpyatva grahāt  tasya ca kevala anvayitvena kiñcid niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogitva abhāvāt tatra vyabhicāra iti vācyam saṃsarga abhāva pratiyogitva anadhikaraṇe kevala anvayini dharme sattvena ākāśa atyanta abhāvasya saṃsarga abhāva pratiyogitva avyāpya tvena vyabhicāra abhāvāt  iti ced na yatra etad tantu niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam tatra etad tantu ārabdhatva abhāva iti vyatireka vyāptau  etad niṣṭha prāgabhāva apratiyogi tvasya upādhi tvena pratirodhasya hīna bala tvāt  etad tantu ārabdhatva abhāva vyāpakasya etad tantu niṣṭha prāgabhāva apratiyogi tvasya pakṣa āvṛtteḥ pakṣa vṛtti tayā sandihyamāna etad tantu niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogitva avyāpaka tvāt  dṛśyatva ādi anupapatti pratikūla tarka parāhateḥ vakṣyamāṇa tvāt ca ata eva etad tantu anārabdha tvam api na upādhiḥ upādhi vyatirekeṇa sādhya vyatireke sādhyamāne sa upādhika tvasya ukta tvāt  avyāpya vṛtti saṃyoga abhyupagame tatra vyabhicārāt ca ata eva yatra etad tantu niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam tatra etad tantu anārabdha tvam iti na sādhya vyāpaka tā grahaḥ api tatra eva vyabhicārāt iti sarvam anavadyam evañca avimatam jñāna vyatirekeṇa asat  jñāna vyatirekeṇa anupalabhyamāna tvāt  svapna ādivat i ati vidyā sāgara uktam api sādhu jñāna vyatirekeṇa asattvam ukta mithyātvā anyatama tvam sādhyam jñāna vyatirekeṇa anupalabhyamāna tvam cit ābhāse sati eva upalabhyamāna tvam hetuḥ iti na kiñcid anupapannam evam anyeṣām api prayogā yathāyogam upapādanīyā iti śivam iti aṃśitva hetu upapattiḥ atha sa upādhikatva nirāsaḥ nanu dṛśyatva ādi hetavaḥ sa upādhikāḥ tathā hi sva bādhaka abhimatā bādhya doṣa prayukta bhāna tvam sva bādhaka ābādhya bādhakam prati niṣedhya tvena viṣaya tvam vā vipakṣāt vyāvṛttam samavyāptam ata eva vyatireka vyāptimat upādhiḥ iti ced na brahma jñāna mātra bādhye deha ātma aikye mithyābhūte sādhya avyāpaka tvāt  parvata avayava vṛtti anyatva ādivat  sādhanavat pakṣa mātra vyāvartaka viśeṣaṇavat tvena pakṣa itaratva tulya tvāt ca na ca bādha unnīta tvāt  saḥ api upādhiḥ bādhasya agre nirasiṣyamāṇa tvāt  api ca yad vyatirekasya sādhya vyatireka sādhaka tvam tasya eva sādhya vyāpaka tvam itara aṃśe anukūla tarka aprasarāt  tathā ca akṣiti ādikam na kartṛ janyam śarīra ajanya tvā aditi atra yathā śarīra viśeṣaṇa vaiyarthyāt na śarīra janya tvam kartṛ janyatva vyāpakam evam aviyada ādikam na mithyā sva bādhaka abhimatā bādhya doṣa prayukta bhānatva rahita tvā aditi sādhya vyatireka sādhane sva bādhaka abhimatā bādhya bhāgasya vaiyarthyāt  sva bādhaka abhimatā bādhya doṣa prayukta bhāna tvam na mithyātva vyāpakam doṣa prayukta bhāna tvam tu bhavati sādhya vyāpakam tad ca sādhana vyāpakam api iti na upādhiḥ dṛśyatva ādinā eva mithyātvavat tasya api sādhanāt  evam dvitīya upādhau  api asvabādhaka ābādhya bādhakam pratī ati viśeṣaṇam vyatireka sādhane vyartham viśeṣya bhāgaḥ tu sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāpaka iti na upādhiḥ ata eva adhiṣṭhānatva abhimata sama sat tāka doṣavat hetu janya jñāna viṣaya tvam upādhiḥ atra ca brahmaṇaḥ api bauddha kalpita doṣavat hetu janya kṣaṇikatva ādi jñāna viṣaya tvāt samavyāpti siddhi artham adhiṣṭhāna sama sattākā iti viśeṣaṇam na tu pakṣa mātra vyāvṛtti artham atas  na pakṣa itara tulya tā iti apāstam brahmaṇi iva brahmaṇi kalpite kṣaṇikatva ādau  api mithyābhūte dharme adhiṣṭhāna sama sat tāka doṣavat hetu janya jñāna aviṣaya tvāt upādheḥ sādhya avyāpteḥ vyatireka sādhane vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvasya ukta tvāt ca na api śruti tātparya aviṣaya tvam upādhiḥ śruti tātparya viṣaya tvasya brahma mātra niṣṭhatayā tad abhāvasya sādhana vyāpaka tvāt  na api prātibhāsika tvam upādhiḥ tad hi brahma jñāna itara bādhya tvam tasya ca deha ātma aikye mithyā bhūte api asattvena sādhya avyāpteḥ vyatireke vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvāt ca prātibhāsa mātra śarīra tvam upādhiḥ dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi pakṣe sādhana vyāpaka tvāt  pareṣām asiddheḥ ca iti iti dṛśyatva ādīnām sa upādhitva bhaṅgaḥ atha ābhāsa sāmya bhaṅgaḥ nanu vimatam prātibhāsikam dṛśya tvāt  brahma mithyā vyavahāra viṣaya tvāt  asat vilakṣaṇa tvāt vā śukti rūpyavat iti ādi ābhāsa sāmyam iti ced na jagataḥ  vyāvahārika sattva bādhe vyavahāra anupapattiḥ brahmaṇaḥ  mithyātve śūnya vāda āpattiḥ ca iti pratikūla tarka parāghātena tayoḥ asādhaka tvāt  prakṛte ca pratikūla tarkasya nirasiṣyamāṇa tvāt  kiñca prātibhāsika tvam brahma jñāna itara bādhya tvam pratibhāsa mātra śarīra tvam vā ādye sādhye deha ātma aikye vyabhicāraḥ aprayojaka tvam ca dvitīye dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi matena siddha sādhanam evam brahmaṇi mithyātve sādhye sa upādhike siddha sādhanam nirupādhike vyavahāra viṣayatva rūpaḥ  hetuḥ asiddhaḥ vedānta janya vṛtti viṣayatva abhyupagame api aprayojakaḥ evam asat vilakṣaṇa tvam api brahmaṇi siddham eva kvacid api upādhau sattvena prati iti anarha tvam hi asattvam tad vilakṣaṇa tvam ca kvacid api upādhau sattvena prati iti arhatva rūpam tad ca śuddhe brahmaṇi na asti eva na ca bādhya tvam asat tvam tad vilakṣaṇa tvam ca abādhya tvam tad ca brahmaṇi asti eva iti vācyam abādhya tvena bādhyatva lakṣaṇa mithyātva sādhane virodhāt  śukti rūpya dṛṣṭāntasya sādhana vikala tvāt ca śūnya vādasya agre nirākariṣyamāṇa tvāt ca tasmāt na dṛśyatva ādīnām ābhāsa sāmyam iti siddham iti ābhāsa sāmya bhaṅgaḥ atha pratyakṣa bādha uddhāre sattva nirvacanam nanu asan ghaṭa ityādi adhyakṣa bādhita viṣayā dṛśya tvādaya iti ced na cakṣuḥ ādi adhyakṣa yogya mithyātva virodhi sattva anirukteḥ tathā hi na tāvat  pramāviṣaya tvam tad yogya tvam bhrama aviṣaya tvam vā tādṛś sattvam cakṣuḥ ādi agamya bhrama pramāghaṭita tvena cakṣuḥ ādya yogya tvāt  vakṣyamāṇa dūṣaṇa gaṇa grāsāt ca tathā hi na ādyaḥ asati pramāṇa apravṛtteḥ pramāviṣaya tvāt prāk sattvasya vaktavya tvena tasya tad anya tvāt  sattva nirūpaṇam vinā sat artha viṣayatva rūpa pramātvasya nirūpaṇe ca anyonya āśrayāt mithyā bhūtasya śukti rajata saṃsargasya vyavasāya dvārā sākṣāt ca niṣedhyatva ādinā pramāviṣayatva abhyupagamāt ca na api dvitīyaḥ yogyatāyā anirūpaṇāt  na tṛtīyaḥ asiddheḥ sarvasya eva kṣaṇikatva ādinā bhrama viṣayatva abhyupagamāt ata eva na asattva aprakāraka pramā viṣaya tvam api anyonya āśrayāt ca na api sattva prakāraka pramā viṣaya tvam ātma āśrayāt na api asattva prakāraka bhrama aviṣaya tvam sattvam anyonya āśrayāt na api pratipanna aupādhau traikālika sattva niṣedha virahaḥ ātma āśrayāt na api sattā jātiḥ artha kriyā kāri tvam asat vailakṣaṇyam vā eteṣām mithyātva avirodhi tvena tad pratyakṣeṇa mithyātva anumāne bādhā bhāvāt  na api vedānti abhimata mithyātva abhāvaḥ sattvam tucche ati vyāpteḥ na api asat vilakṣaṇa tve sati ana āropita tvam anāropita tvam hi āropāviṣaya tvam tad ca asambhavi sarvasya api kṣaṇikatva ādinā āra upaviṣaya tvāt  na api astitva prakāraka pramām prati kadācid  sākṣāt viṣaya tvam kāla sambandhi tvam vā sattvam astitvam ca vartamāna tvam na tu sattvam atas  na ātma āśrayaḥ atīta ādiḥ api kadācid vartata eva iti na avyāptiḥ āropita tvam ca kāla traya asambandhi tvena bādhena bodhitam iti na dvitīya lakṣaṇe ati vyāptiḥ iti vācyam pramātu asya sattva ghaṭita tvena cakṣuḥ ādya yogya tvena ca pūrva ukta doṣāt  vartamānatva prakāraka pramāviṣaya tve api mithyātva avirodhāt ca dvitīyam api na mithyātva virodhi śukti rūpyasya api pratibhāsa kāla sambandhi tvāt bādhena tāttvika kāla traya sambandha niṣedhe api atāttvika kāla sambandhasya aniṣedhāt  na api tāttvika kāla sambandhi tvam tad  tāttvikasya adya api anirūpaṇāt nirūpaṇe vā śeṣa vaiyarthyāt  nanu bhavat mate yad  sattvam brahmaṇi tad eva iha mama uktam hi ayādṛśam brahmaṇaḥ sattvam tādṛśam syāt jagati api tatra syāt tad anirvācyam ced iha api tathā astu naḥ iti na ca tatra aparicchinna tvam sattvam tad ca na jagati iti vācyam tucchasya aparicchinna tve api sattva anabhyupagamāt na aparicchinna tvam sattvam kim tu anyat eva tad ca brahmaṇi iva bhrama adhiṣṭhāna tvāt śuktikā ādeḥ api bhaviṣyati iti ced  nūnam vivāha samaye kanyāyāḥ pitrā nija gotram pṛṣṭhasya yad eva bhavatām gotram tad eva mama api gotram iti vadataḥ  varasya bhrātā bhavān yatas  jāmātṛ śvaśurayoḥ eka gotra tve vivāha anupapattivat jagat brahmaṇoḥ eka sattve jagataḥ asattvam eva syāt  tathā hi sva prakāśa advitīya caitanya rūpa tvam eva brahmaṇaḥ sattvam tad eva ced jaḍasya api jagataḥ tadā rajatatva virodhi śukti sattayā rajatasya iva jaḍatva virodhi svaprakāśa sattayā jagataḥ svarūpataḥ  mithyātva upapatteḥ caitanyasya eva avacchinna an avacchinnā ajñāna viṣaya tvena sarva bhrama adhiṣṭhānatva abhyupagamāt na bhrama adhiṣṭhāna tvena śukti ādeḥ sattva siddhiḥ nanu evam api sarva deśīya tra ekālika niṣedha pratiyogi tvam asat tvam tucchāniḥ vacanīya sādhāraṇam tad abhāvaḥ sattvam tad ca brahmaṇi iva jagatī api iti brūmaḥ na ca saṃyoge avyāptiḥ tasya avyāpya vṛttitva anabhyupagamāt tad abhyupagame ca vyāpya vṛtti tvena abhāvaḥ  viśeṣaṇīyaḥ na api viyati avyāptiḥ tad atyanta abhāvasya kevala anvayitvā anaṅgīkāreṇa lakṣaṇasya vidyamāna tvāt eva na hi kasmiṃścid deśe kāle vā tasya abhāvaḥ nitya vibhutva bhaṅga prasaṅgāt  ākāśa atyanta abhāvasya kevala anvayitva abhyupagame ca vṛttimat pratiyogika tvena abhāvaḥ  viśeṣaṇīya iti ced na cakṣuḥ ādya yogya aneka padārtha ghaṭita tvena etādṛśa sattvasya grahaṇe cakṣuḥ ādeḥ asāmarthyāt  na hi sarva deśīya tra ekālika vṛttimat pratiyogika vyāpya vṛtti niṣedha pratiyogatva m kasya api pratyakṣam yena tad abhāvaḥ pratyakṣaḥ  bhavet  vṛttimat pratiyogikatva vyāpya vṛttitva parityāge api sarva deśīyatva tra ekālika tvayoḥ ayogya tvāt  nanu sva deśa kāla vṛtti niṣedha pratiyogitva abhāve gṛhyamāṇe kāla traya madhye vartamāna kālasya sarva deśa madhye prakṛta deśasya api praveśena tatra niṣedha pratiyogitva abhāvasya gṛhīta tvāt tad saṃvalitam kāla traya vṛtti sarva deśīya niṣedha pratiyogitva rūpam mithyātvam na anumānena grahītum śakyate iti ced na sva deśa kāla vṛtti sakala niṣedha pratiyogitvasya cakṣuḥ ādya yogya tvena tad abhāvasya sutarām tad ayogya tvāt sva deśa kāla vṛttiyat kiñcit niṣedha apratiyogitvasya mithyātva avirodhi tvāt sva pratiyogika atyanta abhāvā sāmāna adhikaraṇasya ca sva pratiyogika atyanta abhāva aprasiddhyā kevala anvayini sambandha bhedena ghaṭa ādau ca asiddheḥ sva atyanta abhāva yāvat adhikaraṇa āvṛtti tvam vā sva atyanta abhāvayat kiñci d adhikaraṇa āvṛtti tvam vā iti vikalpena pūrva ukta doṣāt ca tasmāt tad prakāra antarasya nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt mithyātvā avirodhi tvāt ca sva samāna adhikaraṇa yāvat atyanta abhāva pratiyogitva abhāva rūpam eva sattvam upeyam tad ca na cakṣuḥ ādi yogyam iti uktam nanu yasmin kasmiṃścid  sva deśa kāla vṛtti niṣedhe etad deśa etad kāla vṛtti niṣedha tvam jñātvā tena pratyāsatti bhūtena upasthāpitānām sva deśa kāla vṛtti sakala niṣedhānām pratiyogitvasya abhāvaḥ  ghaṭe grāhyaḥ tatas  sārvadiś sarva deśīya niṣedha pratiyogi tvasya grahaṇam ghaṭe durghaṭam iti ced na evam sāmānya lakṣaṇayā sarva niṣedheṣu upasthiteṣu api tad pratiyogitva abhāvasya cakṣuḥ ādinā grahītum aśakyatvāt  yogya pratiyogika eva hi saṃsarga abhāvaḥ  yogyaḥ na ca aśeṣa niṣedhānām pratiyogi tvam atīndriya sādhāraṇam cakṣuḥ ādi yogyam vastutas tu sāmānyam na indriya pratyāsattiḥ māna abhāvāt na ca mahānasīya dhūma indriya saṃyogena tatra eva vyāpti grahe parvatīya dhūmāt anumitiḥ na syāt  sāmānyasya ca dhūmatva ādeḥ pratyāsatti tve tasya api pratyāsanna tvāt tatra vyāpti grahe tatas anumitiḥ iti vācyam parvatīya dhūma indriya sannikarṣa daśāyām dhūma tvena prakāreṇa gṛhīta smṛta vyāpteḥ tatra vaiśiṣṭya graha sambhavāt  asurabhi candanam i ativat  viśeṣya indriya sannikarṣa viśeṣaṇa jñāna asaṃsarga agraharūpāyāḥ  viśiṣṭa jñāna sāmagryāḥ pūrṇa tvāt  vyāpti smṛti prakāreṇa vā pakṣa dharma tā jñānasya hetu tā mahānasīya eva dhūmaḥ  dhūma tvena vyāpti smṛti viṣayaḥ  bhavati dhūma tvena parvatīya dhūma jñānam ca api jātam tad ca sāmānya lakṣaṇām vinā eva tāvatā eva anumiti siddheḥ na ca sāmānya pratyāsattim vinā dhūmaḥ  vahni vyabhicārī na vā iti anubhūyamāna saṃśayaḥ  na syāt  prasiddha dhūme vahni sambandha avagamāt  aprasiddhasya ca ajñānāt iti vācyam prasiddha dhūma eva tad tad dhūmatva ādinā vyāpti niścaye api dhūma tvena tad saṃśaya upapatteḥ tathā ca uktam maṇi kṛtā aghaṭa tvena itara bheda niścaye api pṛthivītva ādinā tatra saṃśaya siṣā dhayiṣe bhavata eve ati niścite api arthe prāmāṇya saṃśaya āhita saṃśayavat dhūma tvam vahni vyabhicāri vṛtti na vā iti saṃśayāt api tādṛśa saṃśaya upapatteḥ ca etena vāyū rūpavān na vā iti saṃśayaḥ api vyākhyātaḥ nanu siddhe na icchā kintu asiddhe sā ca sva samāna viṣaya jñāna janyā tad ca jñānam na sāmānya pratyāsattim vinā na ca siddha gocara sukhatva prakāraka jñānāt eva ajñāte sukhe bhavati icchā samāna prakārakatva mātrasya niyāmaka tvāt iti vācyam rajata tvena prakāreṇa rajate anubhūyamāne ghaṭa ādau rajatatva prakāraka icchā prasaṅgāt  na ca prakāra āśraya tvam api niyāmakam rajata bhramāt śuktau  icchān udaya prasaṅgāt  tathā ca samāna prakāraka tve sati samāna viṣayaka tvam tantram ata eva ākhyāti pakṣe rajata smaraṇasya eva śukttau pravartaka tvam iti apāstam iti ced na yatas  rajata bhramāt śuktau  icchā na asti eva kim tu anirvacanīye rajata iti anirvacanīya khyātau vakṣyate prakāra āśraya tvam niyāmakam vadannakhyāti vādī param evam vibhīṣaṇīyaḥ tathā ca prakāra āśraya tvasya niyāmaka tvāt anyathā ākhyāti pakṣaḥ api nirasta eva na ca tarhi bhrama tvam na syāt  idam rajatam iti bhramatva abhimata jñānasya vyadhikaraṇa prakāratva anabhyupagamāt iti vācyam bādhita viṣaya tvena hi bhrama tvam na tu vyadhikaraṇa prakāra tvena tasya api viṣaya bādha prayojya tvāt iti hi vakṣyate nanu abhāva jñānasya pratiyogi jñāna janya tvāt  prauḍha prakāśa yāvat tejaḥ viraha rūpasya tamasaḥ pratyakṣatā na syāt  sāmānya pratyāsattim vinā pratiyogi anupasthiteḥ iti ced na asmad mate tamasaḥ  bhāva antara tvāt na ca tathā api tad vyañjaka tvāt tad apekṣā iti vācyam svarūpa sata eva tādṛś tejaḥ virahasya tamaḥ vyañjaka tvam na tu jñānasya māna abhāvāt iti abhyupagamāt anyeṣām mate tādṛś tejaḥ viraha jñānasya apekṣita tve api pratiyogi ta avacchedaka prakāraka jñānāt eva tad sambhavena tad artham sakala pratiyogi jñāna janikāyāḥ sāmānya pratyāsatteḥ anupayogāt  na ca gaḥtva abhāva jñānam gaḥtvatva prakāraka jñāna janyam tad ca gavetarāvṛtti tve sati sakala gaḥ vṛttitva rūpam sāmānya pratyāsattim antareṇa na śakyam avagantum iti sāmpratam yad kiñcid gaḥ vyakteḥ eva gaḥtvatva rūpa tvāt etena prāgabhāva pratītiḥ api vyākhyātā kim ca anāgata jñānasya apekṣita tve anumānāt eva tad bhaviṣyati tathā ca nyāya kusuma añjalau aśaṅkā ced anumā asti eva na ced śaṅkā tatas tarām vyāghāta avadhiḥ āśaṅkā tarkaḥ śaṅkā avadhiḥ mataḥ iti atra śaṅkā upapādakam anāgata jñānam anumānāt eva iti uktam anumānam ca vartamāna pākaḥ pāka pūrva kālīnaḥ pāka tvāt atīta pākavat ityādi na ca carama pāke vyabhicāraḥ sādhya siddhi upajīvakasya vyabhicāra jñānasya adoṣa tvāt anyathā siddhi asiddhi vyāghātāt kiñca śabdāt api sakala dhūma pāka ādi gocara jñāna sambhavaḥ na ca śaṅkā ādi pūrvam śabdasya upasthiti niyama abhāva iti vācyam kadācid eva śabdāt anubhūtasya tadānīm pramṛṣṭa tattāka smṛti sambhavāt  nanu anumiteḥ viśeṣaṇa jñāna janya tvena sāmānya pratyāsatti siddhiḥ na ca anumāna antara dviśeṣaṇa jñānam anavasthānāt iti ced na viśeṣaṇa tāvacchedaka prakāraka jñānāt eva sādhya viśeṣaṇaka pakṣa viśeṣyaka anumiti sambhavāt  etena asurabhi candana amiti ādi viśiṣṭa jñānāya kalpitā jñāna lakṣaṇā pratyāsattiḥ api nirastā candana tvena surabhitva anumāna upapatteḥ anyathā sādhya viśiṣṭa pakṣa pratyakṣa upapatteḥ anumāna mātra uccheda prasaṅgāt  na ca abhāva sādhyaka kevala vyatirekiṇi sādhya prasiddheḥ anaṅga tvāt tatra kḷptāyā anumiti sāmagryāḥ pratyakṣa sāmagrītaḥ  balavat tvam iti vācyam arthāpatti vādibhiḥ asmābhiḥ tad anabhyupagamāt  aparvata vṛtti dhūmaḥ  vahni vyāpya iti parāmarśāt  sādhya viśeṣya ka pakṣa viśeṣaṇa kān um iti abhyupagame tu na eva kā api anupapattiḥ anumiteḥ pakṣa viśeṣyatva niyame māna abhāvāt kiñca dhūmatva ādi sāmānyam na svarūpataḥ pratyāsattiḥ dhūlī paṭale dhūma bhrama anantaram dhūma tvena sakala dhūma niṣṭha vahni vyāpti grahān udaya prasaṅgāt  tatra svarūpataḥ  dhūmatva abhāvāt na ceṣṭāpattiḥ tad uttara kāla manum iti anudaya āpatteḥ tathā ca dhūmatva jñānam pratyāsattiḥ iti vācyam tad ca dhūma indriya sannikarṣa daśāyām dhūma jñānāt prāk na asti eva nirvikalpake māna abhāvāt viśiṣṭa jñāna tvena viśeṣaṇa jñāna tvena ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva anabhyupagamāt avaśya kḷpta kārya kāraṇa bhāva viśeṣeṇa eva sarva vyavahāra upapatteḥ na ca dhūma tvena sannikṛṣṭa dhūma vyakti jñāna anantaram tad samāna ākāram asannikṛṣṭa dhūma gocaram jñāna antaram utpadyata iti atra mānam asti dhūma tvena puras vartinam dhūmam sākṣāt karomi na vyavahitam iti anubhavāt ca anyathā jagatī gata sakala dhūma vyaktīraham sākṣātkaromi iti anuvyavasīyeta na ca evam anubhava mātra śaraṇaiḥ abhyupeyate kiñca sāmānya pratyāsatti aṅgīkāre yad  prameyam tad abhidheyam yad prameyavat  tad abhidheyavat iti ādi vyāpti paricchede sārvajñyāpattiḥ na ceṣṭā eva sā para jñāna viṣayaḥ  ghaṭaḥ  na vā ityādi saṃśaya anupapatteḥ na ca ghaṭatva prakāraka ghaṭa viṣayaka niścayaḥ  ghaṭa saṃśaya virodhī prameyam iti niścayaḥ tu ghaṭa viṣayaḥ api na ghaṭatva prakāraka iti vācyam bhāsa māna vaiśiṣṭya pratiyogina eva prakāra tvāt  ghaṭa tvasya api prameyam iti jñāne bhāsa māna vaiśiṣṭya pratiyogi tvāt ghaṭatva prakāraka niścayasya ghaṭatva jñāna janyatva viśeṣaṇāt adoṣa iti ced  na viśeṣaṇa ajñāna tvena eva tasya janakatā vācyā tasyāḥ prāk eva nirāsāt  svarūpa sambandha viśeṣa abhyupagame ca anirvacanīya vāda āpatteḥ ityādi dūṣaṇāni bahutaram ūhanīyāni tasmāt  sāmānya pratyāsattyā niṣedha mātra pratiyogitva upasthitau tad abhāva grahāt bādha iti anupapannam eva iti sāmānya pratyāsatti bhaṅgena laukika alaukika pratyakṣa bādha uddhāraḥ atha sākṣi bādha uddhāraḥ nanu pratyakṣasya vartamāna mātra grāhi tve śukti rūpya ādeḥ pratipanna upādhau traikālika niṣedha pratiyogitva rūpam mithyātvam katham pratyakṣam syāt  atha tatra rajatatva virodhi śukti tve sākṣātkṛte tad anyathā anupapattyā ca rajatatva abhāve niścite mithyā eva rajatam abhāt iti tādṛś niṣedha pratyayaḥ sva sambandha sarva ābhāsakena sākṣiṇā eva upapannaḥ tarhi sākṣāt  sva viṣayasya gagana ādeḥ bhāvi kāla niṣedha apratiyogi tvam sakala kāla grāhiṇā sākṣiṇā gṛhyatām iti ced na sākṣiṇaḥ  vidyamāna sarva avabhāsaka tvena avidyamāna bhāvi bādha abhāva bhāsakatva anupapatteḥ sākṣi jñānasya bhrama pramāsa ādhāraṇa tvena pramāṇa ābādhaka tvāt ca nanu jñāna prāmāṇyam gṛhṇan sākṣī ghaṭa ādi gatam abādhya tvam gṛhṇāti eva na hi viṣaya ābādham anantar bhāvya prāmāṇya grahaṇam nāma iti ced na vyavahāra kāla abādhyatva mātreṇa pravṛttau  api saṃvāda upapatteḥ tad rūpa gata prāmāṇyasya sākṣiṇā grahaṇe api virodha abhāvāt na hi ghaṭa ādi jñānasya saṃvādi pravṛtti janaka tā avacchedakam prāmāṇyam tri kāla bādhya viṣayaka tvam kintu śukti rūpyādi jñāna vyāvṛttam vyavahāra kāla abādhya viṣaya ka sakala jñāna vṛtti vyavahāra kāla abādhya viṣayaka tvam eva tad ca na bhāvi kāla bādha virodhi iti uktam bhāvi kāla bādha tadabhāvau na ca mānam vinā sākṣiṇā grahītum śakyau tasya vidyamāna mātra grāhi tvāt iti ca uktam nanu tarhi deha ātmā aikya jñāna amuṣṇam jala am ityādi jñānam ca pramā syāt  vyavahāra daśāyām viṣaya ābādhāt iti ced na ābrahma jñānam abādhita tvena teṣām api ghaṭa ādi jñāna samāna yogakṣema tvāt  nanu kāla antara stham api yad  bādhakam tad api kim yad kāla avacchedena anena sva arthaḥ  gṛhītaḥ tad kāla avacchedena eva tad niṣedhati uta anya kāla avacchedena ādye katham asya prāmāṇyam antye anityatva ādikam eva iti ced na abādhyatva rūpa prāmāṇyasya prapañca jñāne mayā anaṅgīkārāt  yad kāla avacchedena eva anena sva arthaḥ  gṛhītaḥ tad kāla avacchedena eva tad niṣedha abhyupagamāt tad ca prāmāṇyam mayā abhyupeyate tad  vyavahāra daśāyām viparīta pramā rūpa bādhakasya anutpanna tvāt asti eva na ca yad  bhavatām ghaṭa ādi buddheḥ prātibhāsika buddhitaḥ  vailakṣaṇyam viṣayasya vyāvahārika sattva sādhakam tad eva iha mama viṣayasya pāramārthika sattva sādhakam astu iti vācyam prātibhāsika buddhi vailakṣaṇyam hi ghaṭa ādi buddheḥ sa prakāraka jñāna abādhya viṣayatva ādi rūpam tad na pāramārthika sattvam ghaṭa ādeḥ sādhayitum śaktam deha ātmā aikya jñāne brahma jñāna avyavahita bhrame ca vyabhicārāt  nanu aghaṭa ssan arūpyam mithye ati pratītyoḥ aviśeṣe katham aghaṭaḥ  mithyā rūpya mithyātvam na mithye ati viśeṣaḥ na ca tad api mithyā eva rūpya tātvikatva āpatteḥ iti ced na mithyātva mithyā tve api yathā na rūpyasya tāttvika tvam tatra upapatteḥ ukta tvāt na ca pāramārthika sattvasya pratyakṣa agocara tve tad niṣedha śrutī nām aprasakta pratiṣedhaka tā syāt iti vācyam tāsām cakṣuḥ ādi prasakta dvaita niṣedha para tvāt pāramārthika tvena dvaita niṣedha paratve api na aprasakta niṣedhaka tvam parokṣa prasakteḥ sambhavāt  anāntarikṣe agniḥ cetavya ityādivat aprasakta pratiṣedhasya api upapatteḥ ca na ca atātvika prapañce yadi tāttvika tvam api adhyakṣeṇa na gṛhyate katham tarhi tasya atattva āvedaka tvam na hi tad eva tattvena āvedayat tāttvikam nāma dṛśyate ca sārvalaukika prapañce pāramārthikatva anubhava iti vācyam na hi asmākam tattva āvedaka tvam tadvati tad prakāraka tvam tad bhinna tvam atattva āvedaka tvam kintva bādhita viṣaya tvam tattva āvedaka tvam bādhita viṣaya tvam ca atattva avedaka tvam abādhita viṣaya tvam ca śraute brahma jñāna eva tad bhinna jñāne tātparyavat veda tvena eva tattva avabodhaka tvāt tathā ca prapañca pratyakṣasya tāttvikatva agocara tve api atattva āvedaka tvam saṅgacchate sārvalaukikī pāramārthikatva prasiddhiḥ tu jala gata pipāsā upaśamana sāmarthya prasiddhivat  parokṣa tayā api upapannā na aparokṣatva paryavasāyinī tasmāt adhyakṣa yogyasya sattvasya iha aniruktitaḥ na adhyakṣa bādhaḥ mithyātva liṅgasya atra upapadyate na laukikam na sāmānya janyam sākṣyātmakam na ca pratyakṣam bādhate liṅgam mithyātvasya anumāpakam iti pratyakṣa yogya sattva aniruktyā pratyakṣa bādha uddhāraḥ atha san ghaṭa iti pratyakṣe adhiṣṭhāna anuvedhaḥ akiñca idam rūpya amiti atra idam itivat  asan ghaṭa iti atra api sat iti adhiṣṭhāna bhūtam brahmā eva bhāsate na ca cākṣuṣa ādi jñāne rūpa ādi hīnasya brahmaṇaḥ katham sphuraṇam iti vācyam rūpa ādi hīnasya api kāla ādi nyāyena sphuraṇasya prāk eva upapādita tvāt nanu evam anīlaḥ  ghaṭaḥ mithyā rūpyam asat nṛśṛṅga am iti ādau  api anīla iti ādiḥ adhiṣṭhāna anuvedha iti syāt  na ca nailyam ghaṭa ādiṣu asti sattvam tu na iti vācyam asya āropitatva siddhi uttara kālīna tvena anyonya āśrayāt anyathā asatyam jñāna amiti atra api satyam iti adhiṣṭhāna anuvedha eva syāt  iti ced na sannityasya aghaṭa iti anena sāmānādhikaraṇyasya bādhi tvāt  tathā hi sattā jāti sphuraṇa nibandhanam vā sva rūpa sattva nibandhanam vā kāla traya abādhyatva nibandhanam vā sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt  na ca abhāva ādi sādhāraṇa sat pratītau sattā jāti sphuraṇam sambhavati abhāva ādiṣu tvayā api tad anaṅgīkārāt  na ca kvacid sākṣāt sambandhena kvacid  paraspara asambandhena sat iti prati iti upapattiḥ vijātīya sambandhena samāna ākāra pratīti anupapatteḥ anyathā sambandha bheda eva na siddhyet  na ca sva rūpa sattvena abhāva ādau tad pratītiḥ ananugamāt  ananugatena api anugata pratītau jāti mātra uccheda prasaṅgāt  ata eva na sarvatra api svarūpa sattvena eva sat vyavahāraḥ ekena eva sarva anugatena sarvatra sat prati iti upapattau bahūnām sat hetutva kalpane māna abhāvāt na api kāla traya abādhyatva nibandhanam tad  tasya cakṣuḥ ādi agamya tvasya ukta tvāt asat idam rajata am iti ādi bhrame abhāvāt ca tasmāt ekam sarva adhiṣṭhānam eva sat iti sarvatra anubhūyata iti yuktam nīla ādeḥ tu ghaṭa ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇye kim api na asti bādhakam na vā nīla ādeḥ adhiṣṭhāna tvam sambhavati prāc asattvāt nīla pīta ādi prātisvika ananta adhiṣṭhāna kalpane gauravāt  adhiṣṭheya tulya yogakṣema tvāt ca adhiṣṭheya viṣama sattākam eva hi adhiṣṭhānam bhavati amithyā rūpyam asat nṛśṛṅga am iti ādau mithyātvā sattvayoḥ adhiṣṭhānatva śaṅkā api na asti iti śūnya vāda āpatteḥ tatra ca anupapattiḥ uktā vakṣyate ca yad tu asatyam jñānam ananta amiti atra api tathā syāt  iti tad na yatas  na tatra sattā sambandhena sattvam kintu sva rūpeṇa eva iti ukta doṣān avakāśāt na ca evam ghaṭa ādau  api sva rūpeṇa eva tathā tvam pūrvam eva nirākṛta tvāt  iti san ghaṭa iti pratyakṣe adhiṣṭhāna anuvedha nirūpaṇam atha jāti upakrama ādi nyāyaiḥ pratyakṣa prābalya nirāsaḥ kiñca niścita prāmāṇyam eva pratyakṣam itara bādhakam bhavet  na ca atra prāmāṇyam niścitam āgama virodhāt  anumāna virodhāt  bhāvi bādha abhāva anirṇayāt ca nanu pratyakṣam eva prabalam anumāna āgama bādhakam na anumāna āgamau pratyakṣā prāmāṇye tad virodha abhāvena anumāna āgamayoḥ prāmāṇyam tayoḥ prāmāṇye ca tad virodhāt  pratyakṣā prāmāṇyam iti anyonya āśrayāt na hi pratyakṣasya prāmāṇyepi evam anyonya āśrayaḥ tasya anapekṣa tvāt iti ced na candra tāraka ādi parimāṇa pratyakṣe anumāna āgama virodhena tasya aprāmāṇya darśanāt tena api sva prāmāṇyasiddhi artham itara avi rodhasya avaśyam apekṣaṇīya tvāt tathā ca anyonya āśraya tulya tvāt paraspara virodhena prāmāṇya sandehe sati anāptā praṇītatva ādinā pramājanakatva vyāpteḥ veda prāmāṇya niścaye jāte tena svatassambhāvita doṣasya pratyakṣasya bādhāt  asmad mate kva anyoni āśrayaḥ anyathā deha ātmā aikya pratyakṣa buddhyā bādhāt deha bhinna tvam api ātmanaḥ  na āgama anumānābhyām siddhyet  nanu pratyakṣam anumāna ādi apekṣayā jātyā eva prabalam katham anyathā auṣṇya pratyakṣeṇa vahni śaitya anumiti pratibandhaḥ na ca tatra upajīvyatva nibandhanam pratyakṣasya bādhaka tvam dharmyādeḥ cakṣuḥ ādinā eva siddheḥ tvacaḥ anupajīvya tvāt kiñca pratyakṣasya prābalyam anumādya gṛhīta rekhā uparekhā ādi grāhaka tvāt anumāna ādya nivartita diś moha ādi nivartaka tvāt ca iti ced na tvāca pratyakṣasya api upajīvya tvena eva śaitya anumiti pratibandhakatva sambhavāt  cakṣuḥ ādinā dharmya ādi grahe api tvacam vinā sādhya prasiddheḥ abhāvāt  tathā ca na jātyā prābalye mānam asti tad agṛhīta grāhi tvam api na prābalye prayojakam pratyakṣa agṛhīta dharma ādi grāhaka tvena parokṣa pramāṇasya eva prābalya āpatteḥ na api anumāna ādya nivartita diś mohana ādi nivartaka tvena prābalyam etāvatā hi vaidharmya mātram siddham na ca tāvatetara pramāṇa apekṣayā prābalyam bhavati anyathā tvāca pratyakṣā nivartita vaṃśa uraga bhrama nivartaka tvāt cakṣuṣaḥ api tvac apekṣayā prābalyam syāt  tatas ca citra nimna unnata jñānasya cākṣuṣasya tad virodhi tvā ca jñānāt bādhaḥ  na syāt  pratyuta āgamasya eva sarvatas  prābalyam smāryate ‘prābalyam āgamasya eva jātyā teṣu triṣu smṛtam ‘ iti na ca tad vaidikā artha viṣayam iti vācyam advaitasya api vaidika artha tvāt kva ca pratyakṣataḥ prāptam anumāgama bādhitam iti tu parīkṣita prāmāṇya pratyakṣa viṣayam nanu pratyakṣasya asan jāta virodhi tvāt upakrama nyāyena eva prābalyam uktam hi ‘a sañjāta virodhi tvāt artha vādaḥ  yathāśrutaḥ āstheyaḥ tad viruddhasya vidhi uddeśasya lakṣaṇā‘ iti ced na yata eka vākya stha paraspara sāpekṣa pada tvena ubhayoḥ sāmye sati upakrama stha veda pada anurodhena upasaṃhāra stharga ādi padānām mantra mātra vācinām kṛtsna veda paratve nirṇīte api na prakṛte tad nyāyaḥ sambhavati ubhayoḥ sāmya abhāvāt  gṛhīta pramāṇa bhāva śruti apekṣayā bhrama vilakṣaṇa tvena aniścitasya pratyakṣasya nyūna bala tvāt  anyathā ‘idam rajatam i ati bhramaḥ api ‘iyam śuktiḥ i ati āpta upadeśa apekṣayā prabalam syāt  etena liṅgāt  śruteḥ iva śīghra gāmi tvāt  pratyakṣasya prābalyam tad uktam ‘pratyakṣe ca anumāne ca yathā loke balābalam śīghra manthara gāmi tvāt tathā eva śruti liṅgayoḥ ‘ iti apāstam parīkṣitasya manthara gāminaḥ api prābalyāt  na ca ‘yat āhavanīye juhotī‘ti asmāt  ‘pade juhoti i‘ti asya viśeṣa viṣaya tvena prābalyavat  ghaṭa viṣaya sattva grāhiṇaḥ pratyakṣasya sāmānyatas  dvaita niṣedhaka śruti apekṣayā prābalyam iti vācyam sāmānya viśeṣa nyāyasya niścita pramāṇa bhāva ubhaya viṣaya tvāt anyathā ‘ayam gauḥ aśva‘ iti ādeḥ api gauḥ aśvaḥ  na bhavati iti āditas  prābalyam bhavet  na ca yathā ‘yat kiñcit prācīnam agnīṣomīyāt tena upāṃśu carati i‘ti atratyasya yad kiñci  śabdasya yad kiñcit prakṛta vāci tvena sāmānya viṣaya tve api dīkṣaṇīya avyatirikte sa avakāśa tvāt  ‘yāvatyā vācā kāmayeta tāvatyā dīkṣaṇīyāyām anubrūyādi atyanena niravakāśena saṅkocaḥ tathā pratyakṣeṇa niravakāśena vṛtti antareṇa aneka artha tvena vā viṣaya antara para tvena sa avakāśāyāḥ śruteḥ saṅkocaḥ kim na syāt iti vācyam tātparyaliṅgaiḥ upakrama ādibhiḥ dvaita niṣedha paratve avadhṛte advaita śruteḥ api niravakāśa tvāt  pratyakṣasya api vyāvahārika dvaita viṣaya tayā sa avakāśa tvāt  viruddhayoḥ ca dvayo‘raham manuṣya‘ ityādi pratyakṣe ‘a ākāśavat sarva gataḥ ca nitya‘ ityādi śrutyoḥ iva tāttvika prāmāṇya anupapattyā kasyacid vyāvahārikam kasyacid tātvikam prāmāṇyam abhyupeyam atyantā prāmāṇyasya anyāyya tvāt  tatra advaita śruteḥ vyāvahārika prāmāṇya sambhave dvaitagrāhi pratyakṣa ādeḥ tāttvikam prāmāṇyam bhavet  tad asambhave tu balādeva advaita śruteḥ tāttvikam prāmāṇyam iti pratyakṣa ādeḥ vyāvahārikam prāmāṇyam paryavasyati iti kṛtabuddhayaḥ vidāṅkurvantu nanu pañca daśa rātre prathame ahani agniṣṭut nāmake nāma atideśena eka aha agniṣṭut dharma bhūtā subrahmaṇi āgneyī prāptā tasyāḥ  alpa viṣaya tvāt caturdaśa ahassu ca udakena prāptayā aindryā subrahmaṇyā bahu viṣayayā yathā bādhaḥ bahu bādhasya anyāyya tvāt tathā dvaitagrāhi pratyakṣa tad upajīvi anumāna karma kāṇḍasa guṇa upāsanā vākī ādi rūpa bahu  pramāṇa ābādhāya advaita vākyasya pratīta artha bādhaḥ kim na syāt  tad uktam abahu pramāṇa virodhe ca ekasya aprāmāṇyam dṛṣṭam śukti rajata ādi jñāne iti ced na dṛṣṭānte bahu viṣaya ābādhaḥ atra bahubhiḥ iti vaiṣamyāt  deha ātma aikye pratyakṣa anumāna śabda ābhāsa ādi sattve api deha ātma bheda bodhakasya ananya paratvena prābalyavat atra api ananya paratvena advaita śruteḥ prābalyāt  vidyā avidyā bhedena vidvada vidvat puruṣa bhedena ca virodha abhāvāt iti iti pratyakṣasya jāti upakrama nyāya ādibhiḥ prābalya nirākaraṇam atha upajīvya tvena pratyakṣa prābalya nirākaraṇam nanu ukta nyāyaiḥ pratyakṣasya jātyā prābalya abhāve api upajīvya tvena prābalyam upajīvya tvam ca anumāna āgama apekṣita aśeṣa artha grāhaka tayā sā ca kvacid  sākṣāt  kvacid paramparayā dṛṣṭam ca apekṣita eka deśa grāhiṇām api upajīvya tvam tad viruddha grahaṇe tena bādhaḥ ca yathā ghaṭa vibhutva anumāne pakṣa grāhiṇā akṣṇā nara śiraḥ śucitva anumāne sādhya grāhakeṇa āgamena manaḥ vaibhava anumāne jñāna asama vāyi ādhāratva hetu grāhakeṇa anumānena kim u vaktavyam apekṣita aśeṣa grāhiṇā sva viruddha grāhakasya bādhaḥ cakṣuḥ ādeḥ ca śabda tad janya jñāna prāmāṇya ādya grāhi tve api tad grāhi śrotra sākṣi ādi sajātīya tvāt upajīvya tvam dṛṣṭam ca nara śiraḥ kapāla aśucitva bodhaka āgamasya tad śucitva anumāna upajīvi aśucitva āgama sajātīya tvena tad anumānāt  prābalyam na ca indriyam api sva jñāna artham anumānam upajīvati iti sama eva upajīvya upajīvaka bhāvaḥ ajñāta karaṇa tayā jñāna janana artham anumāna anapekṣaṇāt anumāna āgama ādinā tu jñāna janana artham eva tad apekṣaṇāt iti viśeṣāt  iti ced na upajīvya avirodhāt  tathā hi yad svarūpam upajīvyate tad na bādhyate bādhyate ca tāttvikatva ākāraḥ sa ca na upajīvyate kāraṇa tve tasya apraveśāt tad uktam apūrva sambandha niyame hetu tve tulya eva nau hetu tattva bahis bhūta sattva asattva kathā vṛthā iti kiñca apekṣita grāhitva mātreṇa ced upajīvyatā tayā ca bādhaka tvam tadā apekṣita pratiyogi grāhaka tvena aidam rajatam i ati bhramasya bādha upajīvya tvāt  katham anedam rajatam i ati bādha buddhiḥ tad viruddha udīyāt atha niṣedhya artha samarpaka tayā pratiyogi jñāna tvena tasya upajīvya tve api tad prāmāṇyam na upajīvyam na hi pratiyogi pramātvena abhāva jñāna janakatā gauravāt  pratiyogi bhramāt api abhāva jñāna darśanāt ca kintu tad jñāna tvena eva lāghavāt  atas tad viruddha viṣaya kam jñāna mudīyāt eva iti brūṣe tulyam idam prakṛte api pakṣa jñānatva ādinā kāraṇa tā na tu tad pramātu ā ādinā api iti atha yad  prāmāṇyam svarūpa siddhi artham apavāda nirāsa artham ca yad  prāmāṇyam upajīvati tad tasya upajīvyam yathā smṛteḥ anubhavaḥ na ca rajata bhramaḥ tathā iti ced  tarhi vyāpti dhiyaḥ api na anum iti upajīvya tvam syāt  liṅga ābhāsāt api vahnimati vahni pramādarśanāt  nanu yena vinā yasya utthānam na asti tad tasya upajīvyam iti eva vaktavyam tathā ca rajata bhramasya upajīvya tvam asti eva na tu prābalyam nahi upajīvyatva mātreṇa prābalyam kintu parīkṣita tayā parīkṣā ca sajātīya vijātīya saṃvāda visaṃvāda abhāva rūpā na ca tau rajata bhrame staḥ prakṛte ca akṣasya parīkṣita tvena prābalyam asti hi asan ghaṭa iti viśeṣa darśana janya jñāna antaram ghaṭa artha kriyā pratyakṣe klṛpta dūra ādi doṣa abhāvāt ca evam eva jīva īśa abheda śrutau niṣedhya arpaka bheda śrutiḥ sākṣi pratyakṣam ca adoṣa tvāt  parīkṣitam iti tad api na bādhyam evam eva ca doṣa abhāva ādi jñāna rūpa parīkṣāyām api anāśvāse vede pauruṣeyatva abhāva jñāne tvad ukta anumāne ca yogyā anupalabdhi ādinā hetvābhāsa ādirāhityajñāne brahmamīmāṃsāyām pratyadhikaraṇam siddhānti abhipreta arthe upakramāt ya anuguṇya jñāne ca anāśvāsaḥ syāt iti pramāṇa tad ābhāsa vyavasthā na syāt  iti ced na parīkṣā hi pravṛtti saṃvāda visaṃvāda abhāva doṣa abhāva ādi rūpā tayā ca sva samāna deśa kālīna viṣaya ābādhya tvam prāmāṇyasya vyavasthāpyate dhūmena sva samāna deśa kālīna vahniḥ iva tathā ca vyavahāra daśā mātra abādhya tvam deha ātmā aikya sādhāraṇam parīkṣita pramāṇe vyavasthitam iti katham atyantā bādhyatva abhāva grāhaka āgama anumānayoḥ pravṛttiḥ na syāt  tasmāt viśvāsa pramāṇa tad ābhāsa vyavasthā jīveśa bheda ādikam ca vyāvahārikam iti upapannam eva sarvam jagat mithyā iti nanu pratyakṣā prāmāṇye tad siddhasya vyāpti ādeḥ bādhena anumeya ādeḥ anumiti ādi prāmāṇyasya ca bādhaḥ anumeya ādeḥ vyāpti ādinā anumiti prāmāṇya ādinā ca samāna yogakṣema tvāt  anyathā prātibhāsika vyāpti ādimatā bāṣpa adhyasta dhūmena tāttvikaḥ  vyāvahāri kaḥ  vā agniḥ vyāvahārika vyāpti ādimatā dhūmena tāttvikaḥ agniḥ vyāvahārikeṇa ābādhena viruddha dharma adhikaraṇa tvena ca viśvasya jīva īśa bhedasya ca tāttvikam sattvam siddhyet  iti ced na etāvatā hi vyāpti ādi samāna sattākam anumeyam siddhyatu iti āpatteḥ phalitaḥ arthaḥ sa ca asmākam iṣṭa eva na hi brahma bhinnam kvacid atyantā bādhyam asti na ca ayam anumeya ādeḥ vyāpti ādinā sama sattākatva niyamaḥ api asti vyabhicāriṇā api liṅgena sādhyavati pakṣe anumiti pramādarśanāt  dhvani dharma hrasvatva dīrghatva ādi viśiṣṭa tvena mithyābhūtaiḥ api nityaiḥ vibhubhiḥ varṇaiḥ satyā śābda pramitiḥ
