niṣedha darśanāt ca na ca tadvat eva vikalpa āpattiḥ siddhe vastuni vikalpa ayogāt  grahaṇa agrahaṇa vākyayoḥ ubhayoḥ api māna antara aprāpta viṣaya tvena tulya bala tvavat iha sattva śruteḥ māna antara prāpta viṣaya tvena niṣedha śruteḥ ca aprāpta viṣaya tvena tulya balatva abhāvāt ca ata eva niṣedha vākya prābalyāt tad anurodhena itarat nīyate atha aprāptāni aprāpti artha tve api alaukikasya ‘āpaḥ ca na pramiṇantī atyādi padārtha saṃsargasya vidheyasya sattvāt na niṣedhya artha anuvādaka tvam iti ced na tad anya paratvasya prāk eva ukta tvāt nanu ‘yattat ne ati niṣedha anuvādaliṅga abhāva at na anuvādaḥ na yad kiṃcid liṅga abhāvena laiṅgika abhāvasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  nanu   tarhi ‘tat satyam i atyādi api ‘na sat tanna asat ucyata iti ‘asat vā idam agra āsī aditi ca niṣedhāya ‘san ghaṭaḥ ‘sat dhaṭa jñānaṃ ‘sat sukha sphuraṇa am ityādi siddha brahma sattva anuvādi syāt    iti ced na brahmatva sāmāna adhikaraṇyena sattvasya pratyakṣa ādibhyaḥ aprāpteḥ śūnya vāda prasaṅgena tasya niṣedha ayogāt ca ‘ya idam sarvam yad ayam ātme atyatra anuvāda liṅga sambhavena kalpanāt ca evam ānanda śruterā api ‘a duḥkham asukham sama am iti niṣedhāya na pratyakṣa prāpta ānanda anuvādi tvam duḥkha sāhacaryeṇa sukhasya api vaiṣayikasya eva grahaṇena tad niṣedhāya brahma rūpa sukha anuvāda ayogāt etad ca sarva m uktam vivaraṇe   niṣprapañca asthūla ādi vākya anusāreṇa ‘idam sarvam yad ayam ātme atyādīni niṣedhya samarpaka tvena eka vākyatām pratipadyante suṣuptau niṣprapañca tāyām puruṣa arthatva darśanāt iti atha   niṣprapañca tā na puruṣa arthaḥ mūrcchāyām tattva adarśanāt na ca   tadā tad ajñāna mātram na tu tad abhāva iti   vācyam samam suṣuptau  api iti ced na mūrcchāyām sva rūpa sukha sphuraṇa abhāvāt tathā ca sūtram   ‘mugdhe ardha saṃpattiḥ pariśeṣā aditi suṣupti mukti kālīna niṣprapañca tāyām svarūpa sukha anubhavena tasyāḥ puruṣa artha tvāt tathā ca śrutiḥ ‘dvitīyāt vai bhayam bhavati iti atha ‘tasmāt ekākī na ramata iti śruteḥ sa prapañca tā api puruṣa arthaḥ na tasyāḥ  duḥkha sādhana tvena puruṣa arthatva ayogāt karma kāṇḍavadasyāḥ śruteḥ aviveka puruṣa para tvāt ca nanu ‘pṛthak ātmānam preritāram ca matvā juṣṭaḥ tatas tena amṛta tvam etī ati bheda jñānasya mokṣa hetutva śravaṇāt  katham na sa prapañca tā puruṣa artha   iti ced na mateḥ pūrvam mama api preraka pṛthak tvat daṣṭeḥ sa guṇa brahma jñānavat preraka tvena brahma jñānasya api paramparayā upakāraka tvāt ‘ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavya amiti ādi vākya svārasya āt abheda jñānasya eva sākṣāt  mokṣa hetu tvāt ata eva prerakatva jñānasya joṣa hetu tvam uktam tathā uttaratra api ‘veda vidaḥ  viditvā līnā brahmaṇi tad parā ye vimuktāḥ tad ātma tattvam prasamīkṣya dehī ekaḥ kṛtārthaḥ  bhavate vīta śoka iti abheda eva śrūyate atas  na bheda jñānasya mokṣa hetu tvam etena ‘na iha nāne ati śrutiḥ eva ‘viśvam satya amiti abādhyatva rūpa bādha niṣedhāya vijñāna vādi prāpta viśva niṣedha anuvādinī kim na syāt iti nirastam bhāva abhāvayoḥ paraspara viraha rūpa tve same api bhāva grahaḥ  ‘nirapekṣa tvāt  na abhāva graham apekṣate abhāva grahaḥ tu sa pratiyogi tayā bhāva graham apekṣate atas  ‘nā iti na iti śruteḥ eva sattva śruti apekṣā na tu sattva śruteḥ na iti śruti apekṣā anyathā anyonya āśraya āpatteḥ nanu   utsarga apavāda nyāyaḥ astu yathā hi ‘na hiṃsyāt  sarvā bhūtānī ati śrutiḥ aviśeṣa pravṛttā api hiṃsātva sāmānyasya pratyakṣa ādi prāpta tvāt niṣedhya upasthitau na agnīṣomīya vākyam api niṣedhya samarpaṇāya apekṣate tathā ‘nā iti na iti āadiśrutiḥ aviśeṣa pravṛttā api pratyakṣa prāpta ghaṭa ādi sattva rūpa niṣedhyam ādāya nirākāṅkṣā satī na pratyakṣa aprāpta dharma adharma ādi satyatva bodhikām ‘viśvam satyam i atya ādi śrutim api niṣedhya samarpaṇāya apekṣitum arhati yatra tu māna antareṇa niṣedhyasya aprāptiḥ tatra niṣedhya samarpaṇāya śruti antaram apekṣata eva yathā ṣoḍaśi grahaṇa agrahaṇayoḥ māna antareṇa niṣedhya upasthitā avāpi vākya apekṣaṇe agnīṣomīyahiṃsāyāḥ  api niṣiddha tvena adharma tvam syāt    iti ced  mā evam agnīṣomīya vākyasya niṣedha viṣaya n yūna viṣaya tvena ananyaśeṣa tayā sva artha tāt paryavat tvena ca na niṣedhya samarpaṇa dvāreṇa niṣedha vāki śeṣa tā ‘viśvam satyam i atyādeḥ tu niṣedha viṣaya sama viṣaya tvena sva artha tātparya rahita tvena ca niṣedhya samarpaṇa dvāreṇa niṣedha vākya śeṣa tā ucitā eva ata eva pratyakṣa aprāpta dharma ādi sattva upasthāpanena vākya sāphalyam api sva artha tātparya rahita tvena ca na agnīṣomīya vākya tulya tvam iti uktam atas  dṛśyatva ādi hetoḥ dharma ādi aṃśe api śrutyā na bādhaḥ athavā   vyāvahārika sattva pareyam viśvasatyatva śrutiḥ na ca vyāvahārika sattve sarva avipratipatteḥ tad pratipādana vaiyarthyam daśā viśeṣe svarga naraka ādi sattva pratipādanena tad prāpti parihāra artham pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ eva tad prayojana tvāt  vyāvahārika tvam ca brahma jñān itara ābādhya tvam na tu abādhya tvam mithyātva bodhaka śruti virodhāt na ca evam dṛḍha bhrānti janaka tvāt  atyantā prāmāṇya āpattiḥ svapna artha pratipādanavat upapatteḥ etāvān eva viśeṣaḥ tad prātibhāsikam idam tu vyāvahārikam iti nanu   mithyātva śruteḥ lakṣaṇayā akhaṇḍa cit mātra paratvena sattva bodhanāt  avirodhi tvam eva na akhaṇḍa artha bodhasya dvitīya abhāva buddhi dvāraka tvena jagat satyatva virodhi tvāt  na ca prapañca satyatva śruteḥ aprāmāṇya prasaṅgaḥ atattva āvedaka tvasya avāntara tātparyam ādāya iṣṭa tvāt parama tātparyeṇa tu tattva āvedaka tvam sarva śrutīnām api samam prātibhāsikavyāvṛttasya vyāvahārikasya tadvati tad prakārakatva ādi rūpasya nirākartum aśakyatvāt  āsām vyāvahārikam prāmāṇyam avyāhatam eva ‘asat vā idam agra āsīt i ati ādi śruti anurodhena api ‘tad satyam i atya ādi śrutiḥ na brahmaṇi vyāvahārika sattva parā brahmaṇaḥ  vyavahāra atīta tvāt  tasya aparamārtha tvena ca niradhiṣṭhāna tayā śūnya vāda āpatteḥ kiṃcid tattvam agṛhītvā ca bādha anupapatteḥ ata eva satyatva śruti virodhena mithyātva śrutiḥ eva anya parā iti api na ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅga upeta tvena mithyātva śruteḥ ananya para tayā prabala tvāt  vaidika tātparya viṣayasya ca tāttvikatva niyamena tātparyajñāpakānām api liṅgānām artha tathātva eva paryavasānāt  sattva śruti vākya stha padānām ca anya para tvāt na sattve tātpari aliṅga āśaṅkā nanu yadi sattva śrutiḥ pratyakṣa prāpta artha tvāt na sva artha parā tarhi mithyātva śrutiḥ api tad viruddha artha tvāt sva artha parā na syāt  tad prāpti tad virodhayoḥ tātparya abhāva hetvoḥ ubhayatra api sama tvāt    iti ced na pratyakṣa apekṣayā candra adhika parimāṇa bodhaka āgamasya iva mithyātva bodhaka āgamasya api balavat tvena pratyakṣa prāpta anuvādi sattva śruti apekṣayā api balavat tvāt  anyathā ubhayoḥ api aprāmāṇya āpatteḥ tad uktam saṃkṣepa śārīrake ‘a tatparā tad para veda vākyaiḥ virudhyamānā guṇavāda eva iti ata eva ananya śeṣa mithyātva śruti virodhāt na pratyakṣā gṛhīta tri kāla abādhyatva rūpa satyatva parā jagat satyatva śrutiḥ iti uktam advaita śruteḥ ca prābalye niravakāśa tvatāt paryavattva ādikam eva prayojakam na niṣedha vākya tvam etena niṣedha vākya tvena prābalye kiti tad hite vṛddhi vidhāyakāt  ‘kiti ce ati sūtrāt  sāmānyatas  guṇa vṛddhi niṣedhakam ‘kṅiti ce ati sūtram balavat syāt  agnīṣomīya vākyāt ahiṃsā vākyam ṣoḍaśinaḥ grahaṇa vākyāt agrahaṇa vākyam ‘satyam jñānam i atyādi vākyāt  ‘asat vā idam agra āsīt i atyādi vākyam ca balavatsyāt iti apāstam sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva ādinā sāvakāśatva niravakāśatva ādi rūpa bala vaiparītyāt ‘viśvam satyam i atyādeḥ tu vyāvahārika satya viṣaya tayā anya śeṣa tayā ca sa avakāśatva ādeḥ prāk ukta tvāt  tasmāt na sattva śruti virodhaḥ na api asatyam apratiṣṭham te jagat āhuḥ anīśvaram etām buddhim avaṣṭabhya naṣṭa ātmānaḥ alpabuddhayaḥ ityādi smṛti virodhaḥ sat viviktatva vādinaḥ  mama jagati asat vailakṣaṇya aṅgīkāreṇa tad pratipādaka smṛti virodha abhāvāt nanu   ‘na abhāva upalabdheḥ ‘vaidharmyāt ca na svapna ādivat i ati sūtra dvayena jagataḥ pāramārthika sattva bodhanena virodhaḥ na ca anena śūnya vādi nirāsa arthena asat vailakṣaṇya mātra pratipādanāt na virodhaḥ artha kriyā kāritva lakṣaṇyasya asat vailakṣaṇyasya śūnya vādi mate api sattvena tad mata nirāsa arthatva anupapatteḥ niṣedha apratiyogitva rūpasya asat vailakṣaṇyasya tvayā api anaṅgīkārāt  asat vailakṣaṇya mātrasya sādhane sūtre svapna vailakṣaṇya ukti ayogāt ca vyāvahārika satyatva mātreṇa svapna vailakṣaṇyasya tvayā api aṅgīkārāt asat vailakṣaṇya mātrasya tad mate api sattvāt ca tad uktam bauddhaiḥ ‘dve sattve samupāśritya buddhānām dharma deśanā iti ced na sūtra artha anavabodhāt tathā hi   sat rūpāt  brahmaṇaḥ  jagat sargam vadataḥ samanvayasya sarvam asat iti anumānena virodha sandehe ‘na san  āsanna sat asat na ca anubhaya tattvakam vimatam tarka pīḍya tvāt marīciṣu yathā udakam iti brahma sādha araṇyāt nistattva tāyām prāptāyām sūtreṇa parihāraḥ sataḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  na abhāvaḥ na śūnya tvam upalabdheḥ sattvena pramāṇāt  pratīteḥ tathā ca kiṃcid parama artha sat avaśyam śūnya vādinā api svīkāryam anyathā bādhasya niravadhikatva prasaṅgāt iti sūtra arthaḥ sa ca na prapañca mithyātva virodhī tathā ca uktam   ‘bādhitaḥ apahnavaḥ  mānaiḥ vyāvahārikam āna tā mānānām tāttvikam kiṃcid  vastu na aśritya durbhaṇe ati na api svapna vaidharmya uktya yogaḥ tasyāḥ ‘vimatam nistattvam tarka pīḍya tvāt  maru marīcikā jalava aditi anumāne bādhyatva pramāṇa agamyatva doṣa janyatva ādi upādhi pradarśana para tvāt vijñāna vāda nirākaraṇa pareṇa api na anena sūtreṇa virodhaḥ rūpa ādi rahita brahma jagat upādānatva pratipādaka samanvayasya nīla ādi ākāram vijñānam sādhayatā anumānena virodha sandehe ‘svapna dhī sāmyataḥ  buddheḥ buddhyā arthasya saha īkṣaṇāt  tad bhedena anirūpya tvāt  jñāna ākāraḥ artha  iṣyatām vimatā dhīḥ na jñāna vyatirikta ālambanā dhī tvāt  svapna dhīvat vipakṣe ca jñāna ābhāne api artha bhāna prasaṅgaḥ  bādhakaḥ na hi bhinnayoḥ aśva mahiṣayoḥ saha upalambha niyamaḥ asti tasmāt na jñāna atiriktam sat iti prāpte parihāra sūtram ‘na abhāva upalabdheḥ i atyādi bādhena sa upādhika tā anumāne upāya abhāvena saha upalambhaḥ sārūpyataḥ  buddhi tad artha bheda sthūla artha bhaṅgaḥ  bhavataḥ api tulyaḥ sūtra arthaḥ tu na abhāvaḥ jñāna atiriktasya arthasya na asatvam kiṃtu vyavahāra daśa abādhya artha kriyā kāritva rūpam sattvam eva upalabdheḥ jñāna atirekeṇa pramāṇaiḥ upalabdheḥ svapna vaidharmya uktiḥ bādhyatva ādi upādhi pradarśanāya tena bādhāt  sa upādhika tvāt ca pūrva anumānam duṣṭam iti arthaḥ tasmāt na evam api virodha śaṅkā tad uktam tasmāt na jñāna ākāraḥ arthaḥ kiṃtu bāhyaḥ sa ca artha kriyā kāritva sattva upetaḥ api advaita śruti vaśāt  brahmaṇi kalpitaḥ  na paramārtha san  iti siddhāntasya sugata matādbhedaḥ iti uktam ca ātma tattva viveke ana grāhya bhedam avadhūya dhiyaḥ asti vṛttiḥ tad bādhane balini veda naye jaya śrīḥ nocedanityam idam īdṛśam eva viśvam tathyam tathāgata matasya tu kaḥ avakāśaḥ iti dharmi grāhaka māna bādhaḥ ca prāk eva parihṛta iti śivam iti viśvamithyā tvasya āgama ādi bādha uddhāraḥ atha asata ssādhakatva upapattiḥ nanu sattva sādhakānām mithyātva sādhaka anumānebhyaḥ prābalyam mithyātva sādhaka pratijñā ādi upanīta pakṣa ādīnām mithyātvā bodhane sarva mithyātvā siddhiḥ tad bodhane paraspara vyāhatiḥ āśraya asiddhi ādikam ca iti ced na mithyātva sādhaka pratijñā ādi upanīta pakṣa ādīnām mithyātva bodhane api vyāhati abhāvāt  pratijña ādibhiḥ teṣām tri kālābādhyatva rūpa sattva apratipādanāt  nanu sādhaka tvāni atha anupapattyā parama artha sattvam āyāti paramārtha sata eva sādhaka tvāt  sādhaka tāyāḥ prāk  sattva ghaṭita tvāt  na tu dhī mātra viṣaya tvam aparokṣa dhī viṣaya tvam sattvena tādṛśa dhī viṣaya tvam vā sādhaka tā prayojakam tucche nitya atīndriye ca ati vyāpti avyāptibhyām tattvena jñānam api na tatra prayojakam vahni tvena ajñāte api vahnau dāhakatva darśanāt vahni tvena jñāte api guñjā puñje tad adarśanāt ca na api tricatura kakṣyā su abādhita asattva pratītiḥ tantram ātmanaḥ  gaura tvena anitya tvasya nabhasaḥ  nailyena sparśavatu asya ca āpatteḥ gauraḥ aham ‘nīlam nabha ityādi pratītau  api tricatura kakṣyā su abādhāt yauktika bādhasya tvad mate prakṛte api bhāvāt iti ced na yāddaśyā budhyā tava nabhonailya ādi dhī vyāvṛttayā ghaṭa ādau sattva siddhiḥ tādṛś buddhi viṣaya tvasya eva sādhaka tve tantra tvāt ata eva loka prasiddhiḥ tantram iti iṣṭa siddhi uktam api ukta abhiprāyeṇa samyak eva evam tricatura kakṣyā su abādhitau  ādi prativādi prāśnika ādīnām sattva buddhiḥ tantram iti upapannam eva guñjā puñjasya vahni tve ātmanaḥ  gaura tve nabhasaḥ  nīlatve ca tādṛś buddhi viṣaya tvasya tava api asaṃpratipatteḥ anyathā teṣām api tatra sattva siddhi prasaṅgāt  atha—yā adṛśyā śabde klapta doṣa rahitayā buddhyā tava brahmaṇi sattva siddhiḥ tādṛśyā pratyakṣe kṛpta doṣa rahitayā mama jagati sattva siddhiḥ astu sādhaka tulya tvāt iti ced na brahma sattva buddhivat  jagat sattva buddheḥ avādhitatva abhāvāt tri kālābādhyatva rūpasya sattvasya pratyakṣa aviṣaya tāyāḥ  ukta tvāt ca na ca buddhi viṣaya tvasya tantra tve vahni tvena ajñātasya vahneḥ adāhakatva prasaṅgaḥ amṛta tvena jñātasya ca viṣasya sañjīvakatva prasaṅga iti vācyam vahnau tādṛś vuddhi viṣaya tvasya īśvara ādi sādhāraṇasya sattvāt  viṣe sañjīvakatva prasaṅgasya nabhaḥ nailya ādi tulya tvāt vastutas tu jñāta ajñāta sādhāraṇam vyāvahārikam sattvam eva sādhaka tve tantram tad ca brahma jñān itara abādhya tvam eva tad ca na mithyātva ghaṭitam atyantā bādhye brahma jñāna bādhye ca tulya tvāt  ata eva na idam parama artha sattva vyāpyam evam ca parama artha sattvasya sādhaka tāyām atantra tvena tad abhāve api na sādhaka tā anupapattiḥ etena vyāvahārika tvam brahma jñāna bādhya tvam vā vyāvahārika viṣaya tve sati sattvam vā sattvena vyavahāra mātram vā na ādyaḥ mithyātva siddheḥ prāk  tad asiddhyā anyonya āśrayāt na api dvitīyaḥ tasya asmākam mithyātva avirodhi tvena iṣṭa tvāt na tṛtīyaḥ sattva abhāve sādhakatva anupapatteḥ iti— nirastam ukta nirukteḥ aduṣṭa tvāt  na ca hetu ādīnām vyāvahārika sattve sādhyasya api vyāvahārika sattvam eva syāt anumiti viṣaya sādhyasya parāmarśa viṣaya hetunā samāna sattākatva niyamāt iti vācyam dṛśya tvavat mithyā tvasya api vyāvahārika tvena samāna sattāka tvasya iṣṭa tvāt  samāna sattākatva niyama asiddheḥ ca dhūlī paṭale dhūma bhramāt api vahni anumiti pramādarśanāt  gandha vyāpya pṛthivītva pramātaḥ api gandha prāgabhāva avacchinne ghaṭe pakṣe bādhā sphūrti daśāyām anumiti bhrama darśanāt ca mithyātvasya mithyātve api tattva āvedaka śruti vedyatva upapattiḥ sattvena sata iva mithyātvena mithyābhūtasya api pramāṇa gamyatva avirodhāt  eka aṃśe tattva āvedakatva abhāve api apara aṃśe tattva āvedakatva upapatteḥ nanu vyāvahārika tvam sādhaka tāyām atantram ajñāna ādi sādhake paramārtha sati sākṣiṇi tad abhāvāt iti ced na brahma jñān itara abādhya tvasya atyanta abādhye api sattvasya ukta tvāt traividhya vibhāge pārama arthika vyāvṛtta vyāvahārikatva niruktau  api janakatāyām tad sādhāraṇye api adoṣāt vastu tas tu  sākṣi api ajñāna upahita eva ajñāna ādi sādhakaḥ sa ca vyāvahārika eva anupahitena parama artha sat ākāreṇa tasya asādhaka tvāt evam ca vyāvahārika sattvam eva sarvatra sādhaka tāyām prayojakam iti sthitam yathā ca ajñāna upahitasya sākṣi tve api na ātma āśraya ādi doṣaḥ tathā uktam dṛśyatva hetu upapādane prāk  agre ca vakṣyate yatra ca yad sādhakam vyāvahārikam tatra tad vyāvahārikam yatra tu sādhakam prātītikam tatra phalam api tathā eva na tu vyāvahārikam iti sarva vidhi pratiṣedha ādi vyavahāra asaṅkaraḥ ata eva lokasya api vyatikrame vicārasya yādṛcchika bādhāt bhrāntatva āpattiḥ iti udayana uktam api nirastam vyāvahārika sattvena loka maryādā anatikramāt bhaṭṭa ācārya vacanāni viruddha tvena bhāsamānāni sattva vidhyā nirūpaṇāyām virodhena vyākhyāsyante tasmāt  pakṣa ādi sarva mithyātva sādhane api na vyāhatiḥ iti advaita siddhau asataḥ sādhakatva upapattiḥ atha asataḥ sādhakatva abhāve bādhaka nirūpaṇam nanu sattva apekṣayā tuccha vilakṣaṇa tvādeḥ agauravatara tvena sādhaka tve katham tantra tvam iti ced na tri kāla bādha viraha rūpasya sattvasya laghutva abhāvāt jāti ādi rūpasya tasya mithyātva avirodhi tvāt ubhaya siddhe sa t vivikte sādhakatva darśanena pāramārthika sattvasya sādhakatva aprayojaka tvāt ca tathā hi pratibimbe bimba sādhaka tvam tāvat asti tasya bimba ātmanā sattve api pratibimba ākāreṇa asatvāt parama artha sattvam na sādhaka tve prayojakam evam svapna arthasya asataḥ api bhāvi śubha aśubha sūcaka tvam yadi api tatratya darśanasya eva sūcaka tvam  puruṣam kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇadantam paśyati i ti ādi śruti balāt  tathā api darśana mātrasya ati prasakta tvena viṣayaḥ api avaśyam apekṣaṇīya eva evam sphaṭika lauhityasya upādhi sannidhāna sādhaka tvam ca na ca lauhityam sphaṭike na mithyā kiṃtu dharma mātra pratibimba iti na pṛthak udāharaṇam iti vācyam dharmi bhūta mukha ādinaiḥ apekṣyeṇa tad dharma bhūta rūpa ādi pratibimba adarśanāt  pratibimbasya avyāpya vṛttitva niyamena lauhityasya sphaṭike vyāpya vṛtti pratīti ayogāt ca lauhitye sphaṭikasya tu ārope tasya pratibimba tvam sphaṭike lauhitya ārope tu tasya mithyātvam iti vivekaḥ sphaṭika maṇeḥ iva upadhāna nimittaḥ  lohitim eti lohitimnaḥ mithyātvam darśitam pratibimba satyatva vādibhiḥ pañcapādika akṛt dhiḥ evam rekhā tādātmyena āropitānām varṇānām artha sādhaka tvam na ca rekhā smāritā varṇā eva artha sādhakā iti vācyam āśaiśava mayam kakāraḥ ayam gakāra iti anubhavāt abhedena eva smaraṇāt  viveke sati api dṛḍhatara saṃskāra vaśāt  nāropanivṛttiḥ ata eva kakāram paṭhati likhati ca iti sārvalaukikaḥ  vyavahāraḥ varṇa ropita dīrgha hrasvatva ādīnām ca nagaḥ  nāga iti ādau  artha viśeṣa pratyāyaka tvam na ca varṇeṣu anāropita dhvani sāhityam tad abhivyakti rūpam vā dairghyam pratyāyakam evam hrasvatva ādikam api iti vācyam dhvanīnāma sphuraṇe api dīrghaḥ  varṇa ityādi pratyayāt nanu āropitena varṇa dairghya ādinā katham tāttvika artha siddhiḥ na hi āropitena dhūmena tāttvika vahri siddhiḥ iti ced na sādhaka tāvacchedaka rūpava tvam eva sādhaka tāyāḥ prayojakam na tu āropita tvam anāropita tvam vā dhūma ābhāsasya tu asādhaka tvam sādhaka tāvacchedaka rūpa vyāpti abhāvāt na asattvāt  anābhāsatva grahaḥ ca tatra bahula ūrdhva tā ādi grahaṇavat vyāpti grahaṇa artham eva apekṣitaḥ tad uktam vācaspati miśraiḥ  yathā satyatva aviśeṣe api cakṣuṣā rūpam eva jñāpyate na rasaḥ tathā eva asattva aviśeṣe api varṇa dairghya ādinā satyam jñāpyate na tu dhūma ābhāsa ādinā iti dṛṣṭam hi māyā kalpita hasti ādeḥ rajju sarpa ādeḥ ca bhaya ādi hetu tvam savitṛ suṣiḥ asya ca maraṇa sūcaka tvam śaṅkā viṣasya ca maraṇa hetu tvam nanu tatra śaṅkā eva bhayam utpādya dhātu vyākula tām utpādayati iti sā eva maraṇa hetuḥ na tu śaṅkitam viṣam api evam savitṛ suṣira māyā kalpita gaja ādīnām api jñānam eva tad tad artha kriyā kāri na tu arthaḥ api tathā ca sarvatra udāhṛta sthaleṣu jñānam eva hetuḥ tad ca svarūpataḥ satyam eva anvaya vyatirekau  api jñānasya eva kāraṇa tā grāhayataḥ na hi sannihitam sarpam ajānānaḥ  bibheti na ca artha anavacchinnasya jñānasya hetu tve ati prasaṅgāt artha avacchinnam eva jñānam hetuḥ tathā ca arthaḥ api hetuḥ eva iti vācyam artha avacchinnasya jñānasya hetu tve api avacchedakasya arthasya tāṭasthyena ahetutva upapatteḥ     ghaṭa avacchinnasya tad atyanta abhāva tad dhvaṃsa ādeḥ ghaṭa deśa kāla bhinna deśa kāla ādi tve api avacchedakasya ghaṭasya tad abhāvavat      ghaṭa icchā brahma jñānayoḥ ghaṭa jñāna vedānta sādhya tve api ghaṭa brahmaṇoḥ tad abhāvavat      ghaṭa prāgabhāvasya ghaṭam prati janakatve api ghaṭasya ajanaka tvavat      viśeṣa adarśanasya bhramam prati janakatve api viśeṣa darśanasya tad abhāvavat      vihita akaraṇasya pratyavāya janaka tve api vihita karaṇasya tad abhāvavat      svarga kāmanāyāḥ yāga janaka tve api svargasya tad ajanakatvavat     atīta ādi smṛti ādeḥ duḥkha ādi janaka tve api atīta ādeḥ tad ajanakatvavat     asat viṣaya kapa rokṣa jñānasya tad vyavahāra hetu tve api asataḥ tad abhāvavat      cikīrṣita ghaṭa buddheḥ ghaṭa hetu tve api ghaṭasya tad ahetutvavat     brahma jñānasya tad ajñāna nivartaka tve api udāsīna svabhāvasya brahmaṇaḥ tad abhāvavat      brahma ajñānasya jagat pariṇāmi kāraṇa tve api brahmaṇaḥ tabhāvavat ca na ca tathā api mithyā arthe jñāna vyāvartaka tā asti iti asataḥ api hetu tvam iti vācyam na hi vyāvṛtta dhī hetu tvam vyāvartaka tvam kiṃtu vyāvṛtti dhīhetudhī viṣaya tvam eva sati api daṇḍe tad ajñāne vyāvṛtti ajñānāt atha avacchedakasya mithyātve avacchinnasya api tad niyamaḥ na tuccha jñāne tuccha vailakṣaṇye ca tuccha tvasya pratibhāsikādvailakṣaṇye pratibhāsika tvasya pañcama prakārāyām ātma svarūpa bhūtāyām vā anirvacanīya ajñānasya nivṛttau caturtha prakāra anirvacanīya tvasya pāramārthika ātma svarūpe tad bhinne vā anṛta dvaitasya abhāve anṛta tvasya ca adarśanāt  tatra avacchedakānām asat ādīnām tāṭasthye atra api tathā astu iti ced  atra ucyate yad uktam tāṭasthya lakṣaṇam upalakṣaṇa tvam eva sarvatra avacchedasya iti tad na viśeṣaṇa tve saṃbhavati upalakṣaṇatva ayogāt viśeṣaṇa bādha pūrvaka tvāt upalakṣaṇatva kalpanāyāḥ anyathā adaṇḍī praiṣavān anvāha ‘lohita uṣṇīṣā ṛtvijaḥ pracarantī atyādau  api vede daṇḍalauhityādeḥ upalakṣaṇa tvāt tad abhāve api anuṣṭhāna prasaṅgaḥ ‘sarva ādīni sarva nāmānī atyatra sarva śabdasya sarvanāma saṃjñā na syāt  ‘janmādyasya yata iti atra janmanaḥ  brahma lakṣaṇa tvam na syāt  viśeṣaṇa artha tvena tad guṇa saṃvijñāna bahu vrīhi saṃbhave api upalakṣaṇa artha tvena āta huṇa saṃ vijñāna bahu vrīhi svīkāra prasaṅgāt  evam ‘asi pāṇayaḥ praveśyantāmi atyādi laukika prayoge api pratibimba ādi jñānānām janaka tve ca viśeṣaṇa tayā pratibimba ādīnām api janaka tve bādhā bhāvāt  na upalakṣaṇatva pakṣaḥ  yujyate udāhṛta sthaleṣu sarvatra bādhakam asti eva iti viśeṣaḥ tathā hi prathame ghaṭa deśa kālau gṛhītvā tad bhinna deśa kāla tvam tad atyanta abhāva ādau grāhyam ghaṭasya api tad saṃbandhe tad deśa kāla bhinna deśa kāla tvam eva vyāhatam syāt  dvitīye tu iṣṭāpattiḥ kvacid  ghaṭa jñānasya ghaṭa icchā janakatvavat  ghaṭam pratyapi janakatvāt  brahmaṇaḥ  vedānta sādhya tve tu nityatva virodhaḥ tṛtīye prāgabhāvavat  ghaṭasya sva janaka tve pratiyogi prāgabhāvayoḥ samāna kālīnatva āpattiḥ svau  adhika pūrvatva ghaṭita janaka tvasya svasmin vyāhata tvam ca caturthe pañcame ca pratiyogi tada bhāvayoḥ saha āvṛttyā bhrama pratyavāyayoḥ anutpatti prasaṅgaḥ ṣaṣṭhe kāmanāvat  kāmanā viṣayasya yāga janaka tve tasya prāk sat tayā tad kāmanā eva vyāhanyeta siddhe icchā virahāt saptame atītasya janaka tve kārya avyavahita pūrva kāle sva sva vyāpya anyatara sattva āpattiḥ aṣṭame asataḥ  janaka tve niḥsvarūpatva vyāghātaḥ navame cikīrṣita ghaṭa jñānavat svasya janaka tve pūrvavat vyāghātaḥ daśame udāsīnasya brahmaṇaḥ  na nivartaka tvam svarūpataḥ upahitasya eva vṛtti viṣaya tvena tasyāḥ  viṣaya tvāt  upahitasya ca nivartaka tvam asti eva ekādaśe brahma ajñānasya pariṇāmi kāraṇa tve api na brahmaṇaḥ  jagat kāraṇa tvam kārye jaḍatva upalambhāt  evaṃvidha bādhaka balena tatra upalakṣaṇatva svīkārāt na ca prakṛte bādhakam asti avyavahita deśa kāla ādi vṛtti tvasya pratibhāsika sādhāraṇa tvāt idānīm atra sarpa ityādi pratītyaviśeṣāt na hi kvacid  bādhaka balena mukhya parityāgaḥ kṛta iti sarvatra tathā eva bhaviṣyati utkarṣa ādi anuvidhānāt ca tathā hi svapne jāgare ca utkṛṣṭa kaladhauta darśanāt utkṛṣṭam sukham utkṛṣṭa sarpa ādi darśanāt ca utkṛṣṭam bhaya ādi dṛśyate viṣayasya akāraṇa tve tad utkarṣa anuvidhānam kārye na syāt  na hi akāraṇa utkarṣaḥ kāryam anuvidhatte iti nyāyāt  na ca jñāna prakarṣāt eva tad prakarṣam jñāne api viṣaya gata prakarṣa vihāya ani asya prakarṣasya abhāvāt  atha jñāna gatā jātiḥ eva prakarṣaḥ na cākṣuṣatva ādinā saṅkara prasaṅgāt  viṣaya prakarṣeṇa eva upapattau cākṣuṣatva ādi vyāpyanānā jāti aṅgīkāre gauravāt mānābhāvāt ca kiṃca jñānasya bhaya ādi janaka tve sarpa ādi avacchinna tvam eva kāraṇa tāvacchedakamāthā iyam jñāna tvena janaka tve atiprasaṅgāt  tathā ca mithyātvā avacchinnatva ākāreṇa jñānasya mithyātvāt  bhrama sthale jñāna mātrasya janakatve api mithyā bhūtasya janaka tvam āgatam eva janakatā avacchedaka rūpeṇa ca mithyātve rūpa antareṇa sattvam apasattvāt na atiricyate anupayogāt  tad uktam khaṇḍana kṛdbhiḥ   anyadā sattvam tu pāṭaccara luṇṭhita veśmani yāmika ja āgaraṇa vṛttāntam anusarati iti sva rūpeṇa api tu bhrama jñānasya mithyātvam asti eva svarūpataḥ  bādha abhāve viṣayataḥ api abādha prasaṅgāt na ca guṇa janya tvam upādhiḥ tasya api āpādya tvena vahni anumāne vahni sāmagryā iva sādhana vyāpaka tvena anupādhi tvāt viṣaya iva mithyātva prayojaka doṣa ādi samavahita sāmagryā ajñāne api aviśeṣāt ca tuccha jñāna tad vaiṣamya ādau ca tuccha tvā adarśanam abādhakam avacchedya avacchedakayoḥ sarvatra sārūpya niyama anabhyupagamāt prakṛte ca avacchedaka iva avacchedye api mithyātva prayojaka rūpa tulya tvena sārūpya upapatteḥ sarva sādhāraṇam ca ekam kāraṇa tvam abhyupagamya etad avocāma vastutas tu daṇḍa tantu ādi sādhāraṇam ekam kāraṇa tvam na asti eva yatra tava sattvam avacchedakam tatra na mama tuccha vilakṣaṇatva ādikam kim tu kārya tā avacchedakam ghaṭatva paṭatva ādi kāraṇa tāvacchedakaṃca daṇḍa tantu ādi tad bhedāt ca kāraṇa tvam bhinnam yathā gaḥ gavaya sādṛśyam anyat  bhrātṛ bhagini ādi sādṛśyam anyat  tatra na ekam avacchedakam kiṃtu gavayatu bhaginītva ādikam eva tadvat atra api daṇḍatva ādikam eva sattva asattva udāsīnam avacchedakam vācyam tathā ca janakatvā anusāreṇa na sattva asattva asiddhiḥ tad uktam khaṇḍana kṛdbhiḥ  pūrva saṃbandha niyame hetu tve tulya eva nau hetu sattva bahis bhūta sattva asattva kathā vṛthā iti ‘antar bhāvita sattvam ced  kāraṇam tad asat tatas na antar bhāvita sattvam ced  kāraṇam tad asat tatas iti ca na ca evam  ‘antar bhāvita sattvam ced adhiṣṭhānam asat tatas na antar bhāvita sattvam ced adhiṣṭhānam asat tatas iti tava api samānam iti vācyam mama adhiṣṭhāne svarūpata eva satta aṅgīkāraḥ tava tu kāraṇe svarūpa atirikta satta aṅgīkāra iti viśeṣāt  yad tu arthaḥ  na jñānasya janakatāyām avacchedakaḥ apiḥ māna abhāvāt na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ viṣaya avacchedakam anapekṣya eva sarpa jñānasya asarpa jñānāt vyāvṛtti siddheḥ tathā hi sarpa jñānasya asarpa jñānāt vyāvṛttiḥ yāvartaka adhīnā na ca viṣayaḥ tad sambandhaḥ  vā vyāvartaka svarūpa atirikta dvi niṣṭha saṃbandhasya abhāvāt  asaṃbandhasya ca avyāvartaka tvāt  atha saṃbandha antaram antareṇa viśiṣṭa vyavahāra janana yogyam jñāna svarūpam eva vā jñāna mātra niṣṭhaḥ kaścid dharmaḥ  vā saṃbandhaḥ tarhi viṣayam anantarbhāvyā eva jñānāt tad gata dharmāt vā viśeṣa siddhiḥ iti āyātam kiṃca sarpa jñānam asarpa jñānāt dharmi ペntara saṃbandham anapekṣya vilakṣaṇam tad janaka vilakṣaṇa janya tvāt yava aṅkurāt  kalama aṅkaraṃvat tad janya vilakṣaṇa janaka tvāt vā yava bījāt kalama bījavat na ca vilakṣaṇa viṣaya saṃbandhena eva hetvoḥ upapattau  aprayojaka tvam tathā tve hi yava bīja tadaṅkura vilakṣaṇa janya janake kalama aṅka rata dvīje api yava aṅkura tad bīja aṅkurābhyām kalama aṅkura tad bījatva rūpa svābhāvika vailakṣaṇyam vinā kadācid upalakṣaṇī bhūta caitra ādi saṃbandhitva mātreṇa vilakṣaṇe syātām sākṣātkāraḥ api parokṣa jñānāt anya saṃbandhi tā mātreṇa vilakṣaṇaḥ syāt  evam ca yathā pratiyoginam anantarbhāvyā eva ghaṭasya abhāvaḥ  bhāva antarāt yathā ca viṣayam anantarbhāvyā eva śilā uddharaṇa kṛtiḥ māṣa uddharaṇa kṛtitaḥ yathā ca atīta ādi jñānam asat viṣaya kaparokṣa jñāna vyavahārau ca jñāna antara āditas  anyathā tad kārya saṅkaraḥ syāt  evam sarpa jñānam api rajjau sarpa jñānasya bhrama tvena adhika janya tve api sarpa jñāna tvena tad hetu janya tvāt svata eva vā asarpa jñānāt vilakṣaṇam iti na kaḥ api doṣaḥ na ca abhāva ādau  api pratiyogi ādeḥ avacchedaka tvam dhvaṃsa ādeḥ kṛteḥ atīta ādi jñānasya ca sattā samaye pratiyogi viṣayayoḥ asattvāt iti tad na sarpa jñānatva avacchinnasya asarpa jñānāt vyāvṛttau prayojakam na tad tad svarūpam eva sarva jñāna sādha araṇya abhāvāt kiṃtu anugataḥ  dharmaḥ kaścid  saḥ api sarpa jñāna mātre na jāti rūpaḥ pratyakṣatvā anumānatva ādinā saṅkara prasaṅgāt  kiṃtu upādhi rūpaḥ sa ca svarūpa saṃbandhena adhyāsika saṃbandhena vā saṃbandhi bhūta viṣayāt anyaḥ  na bhavati māna abhāvāt ata eva dharmi antara saṃbandham anapekṣya vilakṣaṇam iti ukta anumānam bādhitam draṣṭavyam vyabhicāri ca tathā hi ghaṭa saṃyogaḥ paṭa saṃyogāt na jātyā bhidyate tad avṛtti jāti anadhikaraṇa tvāt kiṃtu ghaṭa rūpa upādhinā eva iti dharmi antara sambandham apekṣya eva vilakṣaṇe ghaṭa saṃyogatva avacchinne sādhya abhāvavati ukta hetu sattvāt vyabhicāraḥ aprayojakam ca na ca   upalakṣaṇībhūta caitra saṃbandhena api kalama aṅkura ādeḥ vyāvṛtta tā āpattiḥ vipakṣa bādhāyām iṣṭa āpatteḥ na hi jāteḥ vyāvartaka tve upādhiḥ avyāvartakaḥ  bhavati evam śilā uddharaṇa māṣa uddharaṇa kṛtyoḥ parasparam jātyā vyāvṛttau  api viṣaya rūpa upādhinā api vyāvṛttiḥ aviruddhā śilā uddharaṇe ca jāti viśeṣa viśiṣṭāyāḥ kṛteḥ janaka tvena tad rahitāyāḥ  māṣa uddharaṇa kṛteḥ tad aniṣpattiḥ aviruddhā vyāvṛtteḥ anyatas api siddhi saṃbhave kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādi nirvāhāya jāti viśeṣasya api kalpanāt  atīta asat viṣaya ka jñāna vyavahāra ādau ca atīta asatoḥ eva vyāvartaka tvam na hi vyāvṛttidhī janaka tvam tad  yena sattva abhāve prāk sattva śarīra tayā na syāt  kim tu vyāvṛttidhījanaka dhī viṣayatvam iti uktam tad ca atīta ādau sulabham eva ata eva abhāva ādi nidarśanam api nirastam ukta rūpa vyāvartaka tvasya atyantā asati api sambhavena kadācid  sati saṃbhavasya kaimutika nyāya siddha tvāt nanu viṣayasya vyāvartaka tve api sarvatra viśeṣaṇatva asaṃbhavāt  upalakṣaṇa tvam eva vācyam upalakṣaṇena ca upalakṣya gata sva saṃbandha vyatiriktaḥ kaścid dharma eva upasthāpyate kākena iva gṛha saṃbandhinā tad gata saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ tathā ca sa eva vyāvartaka iti viṣaya saṃbandham anapekṣya sva gatena eva dharmeṇa jñānasya vyāvṛttiḥ iti ced na viṣayasya viśeṣaṇa tvavat upalakṣaṇa tvasya api anabhyupagamāt yena hi sva uparāgāt viśeṣye vyāvṛtti buddhiḥ janyate tad viśeṣaṇam vyāvṛtti buddhi kāle viśeṣya uparañjakam iti arthaḥ yathā gaḥtva ādi yena ca sva uparāgam udāsīnam kurvatā viśeṣya gata vyāvartaka dharma upasthāpanena vyāvṛtti buddhiḥ janyate tad upalakṣaṇam yathā kāka ādi yad tu viśeṣye na uparañjakam na vā dharma antara upasthāpakam atha ca vyāvartakam tad upādhiḥ yathā paṅkaja śabda prayoge padma tvam yathā vā udbhida ādi śabda prayoge yāgatva avāntara jāti viśeṣaḥ atra hi padma tvayā āgatvauvāntara dharmaḥ  paṅkaja nikartari phala udbhedana kartari ca na dharma antaram upasthāpayataḥ apratīteḥ na vā sva uparaktām buddhim janayataḥ samudāye śakti antara anabhyupagamāt atha ca kumuda jyotiṣṭoma ādibhyaḥ  vyāvartakau  iti upādhī eva idam ca prābhākarāṇām bhāṭṭānām ca saṃmatam udāharaṇa yugalam tārkikāṇām tu ākāśa śabda prayoge śabda āśraya tvam udāharaṇam ata eva avidyā ādikam sākṣitva ādau  upādhiḥ iti siddhāntaḥ  vedāntinām atas  yatra viṣayasya viśeṣaṇa tvam na saṃbhavati tad kāla asattvāt tatra upādhitva abhyupagamāt na upalakṣaṇatva nivandhana doṣa avakāśaḥ sandehe tu viśeṣaṇa tvam eva abhyarhita tvāt upeyate tasmāt viṣaya eva sarvatra jñāne vyāvartakaḥ eka viṣayaka smṛti anubhavayoḥ parokṣa aparokṣayoḥ ca viṣayam anapekṣya jātyā paraspara vyāvṛtti darśanāt  sarvatra viṣaya nirapekṣā jātiḥ eva vyāvartaka iti na yuktam bhinna viṣayake samāna jātīye tasaṃbhavāt  na ca tatra api jātiḥ asti kṣīrā dimādhuryavat iti vācyam cākṣuṣatva ādinā saṅkarasya ukta tvāt na ca tava mate tad tad vṛtteḥ tad tad ākāra tvena caitanyasya tad pratibimbita tvena vā mama tu tad tad jñānasya tad tadīya svabhāva tvena tad tad vyavahāra janana śakta tvena vā svata eva vailakṣaṇyam iti vācyam viṣayasya eva ākāra samarpaka tvena svabhāva vyavahārayoḥ paricāyaka tvena ca tad naiḥ apekṣyeṇa vyāvartaka tāyāḥ  vaktum aśakyatvāt  asmābhiḥ ca tucche janakatvasya anukta tvāt  viśeṣaṇatva upādhi tvayoḥ saṃbhave ca na upalakṣaṇa tvam iti uktam na ca ‘katham asataḥ sat jāyeta iti śrutyā ‘nāsataḥ adṛṣṭa tvāt iti sūtreṇa śaśa viṣāṇa ādibhyaḥ sat utpatti adarśanāt ityādi bhāṣyeṇa ca virodhaḥ teṣām tucche janakatva niṣedha paratvāt asmābhiḥ ca tucche janakatvasya anukta tvāt  tasmāt  sat vivikta tvam sādhanam iti siddham iti advaita siddhau asataḥ sādhakatva abhāve bādhakam atha dṛś dṛśya saṃbandha bhaṅgaḥ nanu mithyātva anumānam aprayojakam satya tve api dṛśyatva upapatteḥ iti ced na dṛś dṛśya saṃbandha anupapatteḥ na hi jñānam jñeya asaṃbaddham eva prakāśakam atiprasaṅgāt  na api saṃbaddham ātma svarūpasya tad guṇasya vā jñānasya jñeyena saṃyoga samavāyayoḥ abhāvāt anyasya ca anādhyāsikasya saṃbandhasya abhāvāt  na ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ saḥ tasya viṣayitva viṣayatva rūpasya ekaika mātra niṣṭha tvena dvi niṣṭha saṃbandha ātmakatva asaṃbhavāt durnirūpa tvāt ca tathā hi     viṣaya tvam kim jñāna janya phala ādhāra tvam     kiṃvā jñāna janya hāna ādi buddhi gocara tvam     uta jñāna karma tvam     jñāna ākāra arpaka tvam vā     dṛśyamāna tve sati tattvam vā     jñāna janya vyavahāra yogya tvam vā     sannikṛṣṭa karaṇena yad jñānam utpādyate tattvam vā     yasyām saṃvidi yaḥ arthaḥ avabhāsate sa tasyāḥ  viṣayaḥ tathā ca saṃvidi bhāsamāna tvam iti vā     saṃbandha antaram antarā jñāna avacchedaka tvam vā ādye phalam na tāvat  jñāta tā anaṅgīkārāt  atīta ādau  abhāvāt ca na api hāna ādiḥ gagana ādau tad abhāvāt kaladhauta mala ādeḥ api tad jñāna viṣayatva prasaṅgāt ca na api abhijñā abhilapane tayoḥ jñeya āvṛtti tvāt na ca viṣaya viṣayi bhāvena te tatra sta iti vācyam tasya eva vicāryamāṇa tvāt  ata eva na dvitīyaḥ api na tṛtīyaḥ īśvara jñānasya atīta ādi jñānasya ca karma kārakā janya tvena nirviṣaya tu prasaṅgāt  na caturthaḥ jñāna tad ākārayoḥ abhedena sarveṣām jñāna hetūnām viṣayatva āpātāt anumiti ādi viṣaye tad abhāvāt ca ne pañcamaḥ dṛśyamāna tvasya viṣayatva ghaṭita tvena ātma āśrayāt na ṣaṣṭhaḥ yogyatāyām yogya tā antara abhāvāt na ca yogya tā yogyatām vinā eva yogyā yathā dṛśya tvam dṛśyatva antaram vinā eva dṛśyam iti vācyam avacchedaka rūpa aparicaye yogyatāyā eva grahītum aśakyatvāt  na ca jñāna viṣaya tvam tad avacchedakam ātma āśrayāt na saptama nitya īśvara jñānasya nirviṣaya tu prasaṅgāt  na aṣṭamaḥ saṃvidi iti na tāvat adhikaraṇa saptamī jñānasya jñeyān adhikaraṇa tvāt na api viṣaya saptamī tasya eva nirūpyamāṇa tvāt  saṃvidaḥ  viṣaya tvam saṃvedyasya ca viṣayi tvam iti vaiparītyā pātāt ca na api sati saptamī bhāsamāna tvasya viṣaya tā ghaṭita tvena ātma āśrayāt na api navamaḥ mad samavetam rūpa jñānam iti atra rūpa jñāna samavāyasya saṃbandha antaram vinā eva rūpa jñāna avacchedakasya ‘idam rūpam i ati jñāne api viṣayatva āpātāt nanujñāna viṣaya iti abhiyukta prayoga eva jñāna viṣayayoḥ saṃbandhaḥ yathā abhiyuktasya mantra iti prayoga viṣaya tvam eva mantra lakṣaṇam na ca anyonya āśrayaḥ pūrva pūrva prayogam apekṣya uttarottara prayogāt iti ced na etāvatā hi jñeyatva mātram sāmānyatas  syāt  na tu etad ajñāna viṣaya tvam na ca asmin sādau pūrva prayogam apekṣya uttarottara prayogaḥ  vaktum śakyate tasya anādi mātra viśrānta tvāt  kim ca prayogaḥ api sva viṣaye saṃbandha iti ātma āśrayaḥ api nanu yad jñānam yad abhilapana rūpa vyavahāra kāraṇam sa tasya viṣayaḥ karaṇa pāṭava ādya bhāvena vyavahāra anudaye api sahakāri viraha prayukta kārya abhāvavattva rūpam kāraṇa tvam asti eva na ca nirvikalpaka viṣaye avyāptiḥ tasya aṅgīkārāt  na ca yad tadbhyām ananugamaḥ  doṣaḥ kasya kaḥ  viṣaya iti ananugatasya eva praśna viṣaya tvena tasya adoṣa tvāt  na ghaṭa jñāna anantaram pramādāya yadi atra paṭa iti vyavahāraḥ tatra ghaṭa jñānasya paṭa abhilapana rūpa vyavahāra janaka tvena paṭa viṣayatva āpattiḥ samāna viṣaya abhilāpam pratyeva jñānasya janakatayā bhinna viṣaya tayā tatra ajanaka tvāt iti ca id naḥ abhilapana rūpa vyavahāra janana yogya tvam na prātisvika rūpeṇa nirṇeyam avacchedaka tvasya phala nirṇeya tvāt  pratisvam ca phala adarśanāt  ajanita phale prātisvika yogya tāyām māna abhāvāt kiṃtu tatra tatra anugata tatta vṛtti viṣaya tvena tathā ca ātma āśrayaḥ ataeva jñāna karma tvam viṣaya tvam karma tvam ca na kāraka viśeṣaḥ yena atīta ādau tad abhāvaḥ  bhavet  kiṃtu kriyā adhīna vyavahāra yogyatva rūpa atiśayavat tvam anyathā ghaṭam karoti iti ādau  asiddham ghaṭa ādi janakam siddham ca na kṛti karma iti dvitīyā vibhaktiḥ anarthikā syāt iti nirastam vyavahāra yogya tvam na vyavahāra rūpa phala upahita tvam kutracid  pratiruddhe vyavahāre avyāpteḥ na api tad svarūpa yogya tvam viṣaya tvāt anyasya tasya asaṃbhavāt iti pūrva ukta doṣāt  na ca avacchedakāt  bhinnam sahakāri viraha prayukta kārya abhāvava tvam tad iti vācyam anugata avacchedaka dharmam vinā tasya api grahītum aśakyatvāt  ghaṭam karoti iti atra siddhasya eva kapāla ādeḥ kṛti karma tā vyāpāra kārya tayā siddhasya eva kṛti karmatā aṅgīkārāt ataeva niṣpādana avāci dhātu sabha bhi vyāhṛta karma pade śakya avayave nirūḍha lakṣaṇām āhuḥ asat kārya vādinaḥ satkārya vādinām tu pūrva sataḥ api abhivyañjanīya tayā na kārakatva kṛti karma tvayoḥ anupapattiḥ etena  ‘yasyām saṃvidī atyādi pūrva ukte api na doṣaḥ saṃvidi iti sati saptamī bhāsamāna tvam ca vyavahāra yogya tvam tad ca sati kāraṇa antare vyavahāra avaśyambhāva iti etad api nirastam nanu yaḥ saṃbandha antaram anapekṣya yad jñāna avacchedakaḥ  yad jñāna anavacchinna svabhāvaḥ ca sa tasya viṣayaḥ yadi api ātmā sva viṣaya jñāna samavāyavān tathā api na tasya jñāna avacchede samavāya apekṣā jñāna asamavāyinaḥ api ghaṭa ādeḥ tad avacchedakatva darśanāt yadi api ca rūpa jñānam mad samavetam dhvastam iṣṭam iti ādau rūpa jñāna āviṣayā api ātma samavāya icchā dhvaṃsa ādayaḥ saṃbandha antaram anapekṣya jñāna avacchedakāḥ tathā api sama veta iṣyamāṇa pratiyogi ātmaka rūpa jñāna avacchinna svabhāvā eva saṃbandha icchā ādīnām saṃbandhīṣyamāṇa ādi avacchinna svabhāva tvāt iti na ati vyāptiḥ jñāna viṣayaḥ tu na jñāna avacchinna svabhāvaḥ jñānasya ghaṭa ādi avacchinna svabhāva tvavat ghaṭa ādeḥ jñāna avacchinna svabhāvatva adarśanāt  yadi api sva grāhaka jñāna viṣayībhūtam jñāna viṣaya kānum iti anuvyavasāya ādikam jñānam jñāna avacchinna svabhāvam tathā api svayam yad  jñānam prati viṣayaḥ tad avacchinna svabhāvam na iti na avyāptiḥ iti ced na mad samavetam rūpa jñānam iti ākāraka jñānasya ātma samavāya viṣayakatva abhāva prasaṅgāt  ātma samavāyasya saṃbandha tvena saṃbandhi bhūta sva jñāna avacchinna tvāt ghaṭasya jñānam iti pratītyai  ghaṭa avacchinna svabhāva tvam yathā jñānasya tathā jñātaḥ  ghaṭa iti pratītyai  ghaṭasya api jñāna avacchinna svabhāva tvena asaṃbhavāt ca atha yad jñānam yadīya svabhāvam sa tasya viṣayaḥ mad samavetam rūpa jñānam iti atra tu samavāya eva rūpa jñāna avacchinna svabhāvaḥ  na tu rūpa jñānam tad avacchinna svabhāvam idaṃca jñānasya eva viṣaya tvam uktam na tu icchādi sādhāraṇam iti na avyāptiḥ iti ced na yadīyasvābhāvam iti tad hitasya yad viṣaya katva arthaka tve ātma āśrayāt artha antarasya nirūpayitum aśakyatvāt  rūpa jñāna abhāva abhāvasya rūpa jñāna rūpa tvena rūpa jñānasya api abhāvīyatayā tad viṣayatva āpatteḥ nanu jñāna janaka karaṇa sannikarṣa āśraya tvam tad viṣaya tvam na ca rūpa jñāna karaṇa manassannikarṣa āśrayasya ātmanaḥ tad viṣayatva āpattiḥ karaṇa padena asādhāraṇa jñāna karaṇasya eva vivakṣita tvāt  na ca sādhāraṇa jñāna karaṇa cakṣuḥ sannikarṣa āśrayasya manasaḥ api rūpa jñāna viṣayatva āpattiḥ sannikarṣa padena api asādhāraṇa jñāna janaka sannikarṣasya eva ukta tvāt iti ced na cakṣuḥ mana ssaṃyogasya api cākṣuṣa jñānāsā dhāraṇa kāraṇa tvena manasaḥ api cākṣuṣa jñāna viṣayatva āpatteḥ parokṣa viṣaye avyāpteḥ ca na ca tatra liṅga jñānam karaṇam tatra ca liṅginaḥ tad vyāpta tvam saṃbandhaḥ asti iti vācyam liṅgasya api sva jñāna saṃbandhi tvena anumiti viṣayatva āpatteḥ na ca anumitau tad vyāpta tārūpa saṃbandha eva viṣaya tā niyāmakaḥ vyāpaka tāvacchedaka vyāpaka saṃbandha ādīnām aviṣayatva āpatteḥ na ca  jñāna karaṇa sannikarṣa samāna adhikaraṇaḥ  jñāna avacchedakatva sākṣāt vyāpya dharmaḥ  viṣaya tvam idaṃca nitya parokṣa sādhāraṇam iti vācyam vastutva ādikam eva viṣaya tvam iti āpatteḥ jñāna avacchedaka tvasya rūpa jñāna aviṣaye samavāye api sattvena ati vyāpteḥ ca na ca jñāna jñeyayoḥ svarūpa saṃbandha eva viṣaya tvam iti vācyam asiddheḥ tathā hi svarūpa saṃbandha iti asya svarūpam saṃbandha iti artha tve saṃyoga ādau  ativyāptiḥ na ca tad ubhaya anyatvam viśeṣaṇam himavat vindhyayoḥ api svarūpa saṃbandha āpatteḥ saṃbandha antaram antareṇa viśiṣṭa pratīti janana yogya tvam svarūpa saṃbandha iti ced na ātmānam jānāmi iti atra avyāpteḥ tatra saṃbandha antarasya samavāyasya eva sattvāt  atīndriya abhāva ādau  avyāpteḥ ca na hi tasya viśiṣṭa pratīti janana yogya tve mānam asti anyathā tena viśiṣṭa pratyaya janana āpatteḥ kiṃca viśiṣṭa pratīti janana yogya tvam dharmaḥ  vā saṃbandhaḥ tādṛśa svarūpa dvayam eva vā ādye svarūpasya saṃbandhatva vyāghātaḥ pratīti ghaṭitasya api acākṣuṣa ādi jñāna agocaratva prasaṅgaḥ ca na dvitīyaḥ ananugamāt  kiṃca evam abhāva bhrama anupapattiḥ tatra api viśiṣṭa pratīti saṃbhave svarūpa saṃbandhasya sattvāt  na ca pramātu ghaṭitam tad lakṣaṇam vāstava saṃbandha sattve pramātu asya api āpādya tvāt  anyathā tatra tasya apramātve saṃbandha abhāvaḥ tasmin  ca tasya pramātvam iti anyonya āśrayāt nanu saṃbandha antaram antareṇa viśiṣṭa pratīti janana yogya tāvacchedaka avacchinna svarūpasya saṃbandha tvam saṃyogatva avacchinnasya daṇḍī ityādau saṃbandha tvavat  viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ ca avacchedikā viṣayiṇī ā iva avacchedya viṣayā atas  na svarūpa saṃbandha gocara viśiṣṭa buddheḥ cākṣuṣatva virodhaḥ na ca tarhi abhāva prama bhramayoḥ sva rūpa dvaya mātra viṣayatva aviśeṣāt  pramābhram avyavasthā anupapattiḥ iti vācyam ghaṭa abhāvavati ghaṭa abhāva jñāna tvena tad bhinna jñāna tvena ca vyavasthā upapatteḥ nanu atirikta aviṣaya tve tasya eva anupapattiḥ na hi bhavat rītyā tasya ubhaya ātmaka tvena tad ubhaya sattvena vyadhikaraṇa prakāratva rūpa bhrama tu asya eva abhāve bhrama tadanya tvābhyām vyavasthā saṃbhavati iti  ced na ghaṭa abhāva abhāvasya ghaṭa tvena tadvati ghaṭa abhāva jñānasya vyadhikaraṇa prakārakatva saṃbhavāt kiṃca bhramasya vastu gatyā yad  ghaṭavat sa viṣayaḥ na tu pramāyā iti atirikta viṣaya tvam asti eva na ca ati indriya abhāve avyāptiḥ atyanta abhāve pratiyogi deśāni adeśa tvam prāc abhāva ādau pratiyogi deśa tve sati pratiyogi kāla ani akāla tvam anyonya abhāve pratiyogi ta avacchedaka deśa anyadeśa tvam viśiṣṭa pratyaya janana yogya tāvacchedakam tad avacchinna tvam ca viśiṣṭa pratītya janake api atīndriya abhāve sulabham na hi araṇya sthaḥ  daṇḍaḥ  na ghaṭa janana yogya tāvacchedaka avacchinna iti ced  mā evam nityasya atīndriyasya ākāśa atyanta abhāva ādeḥ viśiṣṭa pratīti janana yogya tāvacchedaka avacchinna tve avaśyam viśiṣṭa pratyaya janakatva prasaṅgāt  nityasya svarūpa yogyasya sahakāri samavadhāna niyamāt kiṃca viśiṣṭasya pratyaya iti atra svarūpa saṃbandhasya ṣaṣṭhī artha tve ātma āśrayaḥ saṃbandha mātrasya tad artha tve ātmatva ādi viśiṣṭa ātma saṃbandhi samūha ālambana viṣaye ghaṭa paṭa ādau  ativyāptiḥ tayoḥ api viśiṣṭa saṃbandhya viśiṣṭa viṣaya jñāna janaka tvāt  jñānasya abhāvaḥ jñātaḥ abhāva iti pratītyoḥ vailakṣaṇyam na syāt  jñāna abhāvayoḥ ubhayoḥ eva ubhayatra svarūpa saṃbandha tve viṣaya kṛta viśeṣa abhāvāt ataeva viśiṣṭa pratīti janana yogya tvam jñāna jñeya ādi sthale atiriktam eva saṃbandha iti nirastam atīndriye nitya abhāve avyāpteḥ na hi tatra viśiṣṭa pratīti janana yogya tā phala upadhāna āpatteḥ pratīti ghaṭitasya cākṣuṣa ādi pratītau  aviṣayatva prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt satya tve saṃbandha anupapatteḥ ādhyāsika eva dṛś dṛśyayoḥ saṃbandha iti iti advaita siddhau prapañca satya tve dṛś dṛśya saṃbandha bhaṅgaḥ atha anukūla tarka nirūpaṇam syāt etad  sarvasya api dṛśyasya brahma ātmaka dṛś adhyastatve api kasyacid  kadācid  kiṃcid  pratiprakāśāya tvayā api tad tad sannikṛṣṭa indriya janya tad tad ākāra vṛtti dvāraka eva anāvṛta dṛś saṃbandhaḥ svīkṛtaḥ tathā ca satya tve api tad vāraka eva saṃbandhaḥ astu kimādhyāsika saṃbandha durvyasanena na hi bhavatām vijñāna vādinām iva tad tad jñāne tad tad artha adhyāsa svīkāraḥ śuddha dṛśaḥ svatas  bheda abhāvāt upādhi viśiṣṭāyā bhede api ghaṭa ādivat tasyāḥ  api mithyā tvena adhiṣṭhānatva ayogāt iti ced na prakāśasya sākṣāt  sva saṃsṛṣṭa prakāśakatva niyamena caitanyasya paramparā saṃbandhena viṣaya prakāśaka tvā yogāt na hi pradīpaḥ paramparā saṃbaddham prakāśayati atas  viṣaya adhiṣṭhāna caitanyam anāvṛtam eva prakāśakam āvaraṇa bhaṅgaḥ ca vṛttyā atas  vṛtteḥ pūrvam ādhyāsika saṃbandhe vidyamāne api dṛśyā apratītiḥ upapannā ata eva vṛtti prati bimbita caitanyasya ghaṭa prakāśaka tve ādhyāsika saṃbandhasya atantra tā āpātaḥ ghaṭa abhivyakta caitanyasya ghaṭa prakāśaka tve āvaśyakena vṛtti pratibimbita caitanyena eva ghaṭa prakāśakatva upapattau tad adhiṣṭhāna cit abhivyakti kalpanā yoga iti nirastam parokṣa vilakṣaṇa sphuṭatara vyavahāra artha viṣaya adhiṣṭhāna caitanya abhivyakti kalpanāyāḥ  yukta tvat  na ca śuddha caitanyasya carama sākṣātkārāt pūrvam nābhi vyaktiḥ abhivyaktasya ca ghaṭa ādi avacchinna caitanyasya na tad adhiṣṭhāna tvam ātma āśrayāt iti vācyam carama sākṣātkārāt pūrvam api śuddha caitanyasya avidyā vaśāt adhiṣṭhāna bhūtasya mūla ajñāna nivṛtti lakṣaṇa abhivyakti abhāve api tad avasthā viśeṣa ādi nivṛtti lakṣaṇa abhivyaktyā viṣaya prakāśakatva upapatteḥ naca  ghaṭa prakāśikāyāḥ dṛśaḥ  mithyā tvena adhiṣṭhāna tvam satya tve doṣa ajanya tvena pramātvāt  satyam sva viṣayam prati na adhiṣṭhāna tvam iti ubhayatas pāśā rajuḥ iti vācyam yatas  doṣa janya tvam na pramātva prayojakam caitanyasya sarvatra doṣa ajanya tvāt  kiṃtu doṣa janya vṛtti avacchinna tvam prakṛte ca tad abhāvāt na viṣayasya satya tvam atas  mithyā bhūta viṣayam pratyadhiṣṭhāna tvam satyāyāḥ  dṛśaḥ  yuktam nanu tāttvika saṃbandha asaṃbhave ādhyāsika saṃbandha kalpanam sa eva tu kutas  klṛpta saṃyoga bādhe guṇa guṇinoḥ samavāyavat tad ubhaya bādhe tṛtīyasya saṃbhavāt  na ca tatra māna abhāvaḥ samavāyavat anuma adhyakṣayoḥ sattvāt  tathā hi paraspara asaṃyuktā samaveta viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyaka vi śiṣṭa dhīḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya saṃbandha viśiṣṭa viṣayā viśiṣṭa dhī tvāt  daṇḍī iti viśiṣṭa dhīvat uktā janya pramā viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya saṃbandha nimittakā abādhita janya viśiṣṭa dhī tvāt  saṃmatavat  vimatā dhīḥ abādhita viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya saṃbandha viṣayā abādhita viśiṣṭa dhī tvāt daṇḍī iti viśiṣṭa dhīvat gomān  caitra iti ādeḥ api pakṣa kukṣi nikṣepa eva iti na tatra vyabhicāra śaṅkā tathā ca saṃyoga samavāya atirikta saṃbandha siddhiḥ iti ced na prathame dvitīye ca artha antaram ādhyāsika sambandhasya eva viṣaya tvena nimitta tvena ca upapatteḥ dvitīye parokṣa dhīṣu vyabhicāraḥ ca tṛtīye brahma jñāna paryanta ābādhita tvena siddha sādhanam eva sarvathā abādhita dhī viṣaya tve sādhye sādhya vaikalyam na ca tāttvika saṃbandha bādhe ādhyāsika saṃbandha siddhiḥ tathā ca saṃyoga samavāya atirikta tāttvika saṃbandha bādha paryantam na adhyāsika saṃbandha saṃbhāvanā tathā ca katham artha antara siddha sādhana sādhya vaikalyāni iti vācyam tāttvika saṃbandhasya vyāpaka an upalabdhi ābādhāt tathā hi tāttvika saṃbandhasya vyāpakaḥ  deśa kāla viprakarṣa abhāvaḥ sa ca atīta ādi viṣaya ka jñāna ādīnām na asti eva iti katham tāttvikaḥ teṣām saṃbandhaḥ na ca  samavāyavat  saṃbandhya bhāva viprakarṣa ādi aviruddha tvena eva tad saddhiḥ iti vācyam samavāyasya api deśa kāla viprakṛṣṭayoḥ saṃbandha vyavahārā prayojaka tvāt  na hi saṃbandhya bhāve api san samavāyaḥ adya naṣṭam ghaṭam śvastanena rūpeṇa viśinaṣṭi na ca adhyāsika tve saṃbandhasya sādhye dharmi grāhaka māna bādhaḥ viśiṣṭa buddhi tvena prathama tāttvikā tāttvika sādhāraṇa saṃvandha tvasya eva siddheḥ kiṃca saṃbandha grāhaka eva tāttvika saṃbandha vyāpaka anupalabdhi rūpa bādha saha kṛta adhyāsika saṃbandhe paryavasyati atas  na dharmi grāhaka bādha śaṅkā api na ca evam yuta siddhayoḥ eva saṃyoga rūpa saṃbandha darśanāt ayuta siddhiḥ api saṃyogasya bādhikā syāt iti vācyam ayutasiddhayoḥ api kvacid saṃbandha adarśanena yuta siddhatvasya saṃbandhā prayojaka tvāt  yasmin satya vaśyam saṃbandhaḥ sa eva saṃbandhasya prayojaka iti samavyāptatva abhāvena yuta siddhi anupalabdheḥ abādhaka tvāt  yatra saṃbandhaḥ tatra avaśyam yuta siddhiḥ iti viṣama vyāpti kalpane api māna abhāvāt anukūla tarka adarśanāt  deśa kāla viprakarṣa abhāvavatām tu sarveṣām saṃbandha darśanena viprakarṣe tad arśanena ca samavyāpta tayā prayojakasya deśa kāla viprakarṣa abhā  asya anupalabdheḥ saṃbandha bādhaka tvasya avaśyam aṅgīkaraṇīya tvāt na hi prayojaka abhāve prayojya saṃbhavaḥ nanu evam dhvaṃsa ādeḥ atīta ādinā mithyātva lakṣaṇa antargatasya atyanta abhāvasya pratiyoginā śakteḥ śakyena ajñānasya ajñeyena icchāyā iṣyamāṇena vyavahārasya vyavahartavyena vākyasya arthena vṛtti rūpa jñānasya jñeyena saṃbandhaḥ  na iti tvad vākya ukta saṃbandha abhāvasya jñānena asaṃbandhāt sva nyāya sva kriyā su avacana virodhāḥ syuḥ na hi jñāne jñeyam iva pratiyogi ādikamabhāvāt au  adhyastam iti ced na yadi api ukta nyāya sāmyena dhvaṃsa ādīnām sva pratiyogi ādibhiḥ tāttvikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ  na asti eva adhyāsaḥ api na jñāna jñeya nyāyena ubhayoḥ api mithyātvāt  tathā api pratīyamānam pratiyogi anuyogi bhāva ādikam sarvathā na nirākurmaḥ kiṃtu tāttvika adhyāsābhyām bhinnam eva jñeya kukṣi nikṣipta tvāt  mithyābhūtam aṅgīkurmaḥ sa ca saṃyoga ādivat atiriktaḥ  vā svarūpam vā para aṅgīkṛta padārtha antargataḥ  vā tad atiriktaḥ  vā iti asyām kāka danta parīkṣāyām na naḥ nirbandhaḥ na ca mithyātva siddheḥ prāk  tad asiddhyā anyonya āśrayaḥ dṛś dṛśya saṃbandha anupapattyā jñeya mātrasya adhyāsika tve siddhe tad madhya patitasya pratiyogi abhāva ādi saṃbandhasya api mithyātvam na tu pratiyogi abhāva ādi saṃbandha mithyātva siddhi anantaram dṛśya mithyātva siddhiḥ iti vyavahāra upayukta saṃbandha sāmānyasya apratikṣepāt  na sva vacana ādi virodhaḥ tad uktam khaṇḍana kṛdbhiḥ ‘bādhe adṛḍhe anya sāmyāt  kim dṛḍhe tad api bādhyatām kva mamatvam mumukṣūṇa ām anirvacana vādinām iti na ca adṛḍha tvam bādhasya vyāpaka anupalabdhi rūpa tarkasya ukta tvāt sva kriyā ādi virodha rūpa pratikūla tarkasya parihṛta tvāt ca ataeva na jāti vādi sāmyam tena hi niyama sāpekṣā nityatva sādhaka kṛtakatva ādau niyama anapekṣaṇa darśana mātreṇa rūpavatva ādikam āpādyate na tu asmābhiḥ tathā niyama nirapekṣeṇa sāhacarya mātreṇa kiṃcid āpādyate na ca evan jñāna jñeyayoḥ api pratiyogi abhāva ādi sama kakṣya eva saṃbandhaḥ astu iti vācyam paraspara adhyāsa ātmaka saṃbandha asaṃbhavena eva saṃbandha antara kalpanāt  tad sambhave tasya eva saṃbandha tvāt  na ca ajñāna viṣayasya brahmaṇaḥ  viṣayiṇī ajñāne anadhyāsena viṣayasya viṣayiṇī adhyāsa niyamaḥ  na siddha iti vācyam evam niyama anabhyupagamāt kim tu jñāna ājñānayoḥ adhyāsa eva viṣayeṇa saṃbandhaḥ sa ca jñāne jñeyasya ajñeye ca ajñānasya adhyāsāt upapadyate ata eva adhyāsika saṃbandha vyatireka pradarśane ajñānasya ajñeyena iti anudāharaṇam nanu śravaṇa ādīnām carama sākṣātkāra antānām sva viṣayeṇa brahmaṇā saṃbandha anupapattiḥ na hi śravaṇa ādau sākṣātkāre vā brahmā adhyastam iti ced na sākṣātkāraḥ  hi vṛttiḥ vā tad abhivyakta caitanyam vā ādye tasyāḥ brahmaṇi adhyasta tvena ajñāna ajñeyayoḥ iva saṃbandha upapatteḥ ataeva śravaṇa ādinā api mānasa kriyā rūpeṇa na saṃbandha anupapattiḥ dvitīye tu abhedena saṃbandha anupayogāt tad saṃbandha anupapattiḥ na doṣāya ataeva carama sākṣātkārasya brahmaṇi adhyasta tvāt  yadi tad viṣaya tvam tadā ghaṭa sākṣātkārasya api brahmaṇi adhyasta tvāt  tad viṣayatva āpattiḥ iti nirastam ghaṭa sākṣātkārasya ghaṭa abhivyakta caitanya rūpa tve brahmaṇi anadhyāsāt vṛtti rūpa tve tasyāḥ brahmaṇi adhyāse api na adhiṣṭhāna bhūta brahmaṇaḥ  viṣaya tvam brahma viṣaya tā prayojakasya adhyāsa viśeṣasya tatra abhāvāt tasya ca phala bala kalpya tvāt na hi carama vṛttau brahma ākāra tāvat atrā api sā anubhūyate iccheṣyamāṇayoḥ tu jñāna dvāraka eva saṃbandha iti na pṛthak saṃbandha apekṣā na ca jñāne sannikarṣa adhīnasya iva smṛtau  anubhava adhīnasya iva icchāyām jñāna adhīnasya viṣaya saṃbandhasya anubhavāt  sannikarṣa ādibhyaḥ  bhinna iva jñānāt  bhinna eva saṃbandhaḥ  vaktavya iti vācyam saṃbandha anubhavasya jñāna dvāraka saṃbandhena api upapatteḥ atirikta saṃbandha kalpane māna abhāvāt jñāna adhīna saṃbandha antarasya ananubhavāt  jñāne tu indriya sannikarṣa ādinā na saṃbandha anubhava upapattiḥ indriya sannikarṣa ādīnām atīndriya tvena teṣām anum ityādinā upasthitim vinā eva ghaṭa jñānam ityādi saṃbandha anubhavāt  smṛtau tu anubhava adhīna saṃbandhasya śaṅkā eva na asti anubhavasya tadānīm asattvāt ubhayoḥ api jñāna tvena tulyavat eva saṃbandha saṃbhavāt ca na ca  samūha ālambana janyā eka viṣayecchāyām ubhaya viṣayatva āpattiḥ janaka jñānasya ubhaya viṣaya tvāt iti vācyam atirikta saṃbandha pakṣe api tulya tvāt  atha eka viṣaya avacchedena eva jñānasya janakatvāt  na ubhaya viṣaya tvam samam mamā api janaka jñāne janakatā avacchedaka viṣaya tvasya eva saṃbandha tvāt  na ca nityeśvara icchāyā viṣayatva saṃbandha anupapattiḥ tasyāḥ asmābhiḥ anaṅgīkārāt  tārkikāṇām api tad sādhaka māna balena vilakṣaṇa saṃbandha kalpane api janya jñāna janyecchayoḥ ukta prakāreṇa eva viṣaya tā abhyupagamāt na ca putra ādi dhī janya sukha ādeḥ putra ādi viṣayatva āpattiḥ icchā anyāyāt iti vācyam vaiṣamyāt  jñānasya samāna tve api icchā ādau  eva sa viṣayatva pratītiḥ na tu sukha ādau vastu svābhāvyāt  tvayā api asya eva arthasya vaktavya tvāt anyathā sphaṭike japā kusuma sannidhānāt lauhityavat loṣṭe api āpadyeta atha dharme tātparyasya anadhyāsāt ta aparya saṃbandhaḥ  na syāt  na tātparyam hi tad pratīti uddeśyaka tvam pratīteḥ ca jñeya antareṇa iva dharmeṇā api saṃbandhaḥ adhyasya eva pratīti dvārā ca dharma tātparyayoḥ saṃbandha iti anupapatti abhāvāt na ca  jñānasya prakāśa tvena pradīpa sāmye api āntara tvena tad vailakṣaṇyam aṅgīkartavyam ata icchā ādivat viprakṛṣṭena api saṃbandhaḥ syāt  anyathā pradīpavat eva adhyāsika saṃbandhaḥ api na syāt  parokṣa vṛttau viprakṛṣṭa saṃbandha darśanāt ca iti vācyam deśa kāla viprakarṣa abhāvasya saṃbandha sāmānya prayojaka tve saṃbhavati āntara pratiyogika saṃbandha bhinna saṃbandha eva asya prayojaka tvam iti kalpanā bīja abhāvāt icchāyāḥ tu neṣyamāṇena sākṣāt saṃbandhaḥ kim tu jñāna dvārakaḥ paraṃparā saṃbandha eva iti uktam parokṣa sthale tu yadi api adhiṣṭhāna caitanyena sākṣāt eva saṃbandhaḥ tathā api viṣaya ākāra vṛttyā sākṣāt saṃbandha abhāvāt vṛti avacchinna caitanyena viṣayasya paraṃparā saṃbandha eva nanu tava api mate jñeyasya na sva jñāne adhyastatva niyamaḥ anadhyastasya tucchasya pañcama prakāratva pakṣe avidyā nivṛtteḥ bhāva advaita pakṣe abhāvasya dṛś rūpa tve api sva jñāne anadhyāsāt aparokṣa eka rase brahmaṇi adhyastasya vyāvahārikasya atīta ādeḥ nitya ati indriyasya ca parokṣa anubhava rūpe sva jñāne anadhyāsāt smaryamāṇasya ca smṛti rūpe sva jñāne anadhyāsāt pratibhāsikasya ca pratibhāsike sva jñāne anadhyāsāt tvad mate bhrama rūpa jñānasya api kalpita tvāt iti ced  mā evam tucchasya ajñeya tvena jñāne adhyāsa abhāvāt  jñeyasya hi jñāne adhyāsaḥ tucchasya tu na jñeyatā iti agre vakṣyate pañcama prakāra avidyā nivṛtteḥ api pratiyogi adhikaraṇe dhvaṃsasya api tatra vṛtteḥ avaśyaṃbhāvāt  adhyāsa eva saṃbandhaḥ vastu tastu avidyā nivṛtteḥ pañcama prakāra tvam ca bhāva advaitam ca anabhyupagama parāhatam yathā ca avidyā nivṛtteḥ brahma rūpa tvam sarva advaitam ca tathā upariṣṭāt vakṣyate aparokṣeka rase brahmaṇi adhyastasya atīta ādeḥ anum iti ādi rūpa jñāne anadhyāse api yasmin  caitanye tad adhyastam tad eva caitanyam anum iti ādi rūpa vṛtti avacchinnam iti na adhyāsa anupapattiḥ ati prasaṅga parihāra artham caitanyasya viṣaya saṃbandhe vṛtti uparāga apekṣāyām api na adhiṣṭhāna tvena tad apekṣā evam eva nitya parokṣa sthale smṛti sthale api pratibhāsikasya pratibhāsikyām vṛttau  anadhyāse api adhiṣṭhāna viṣaya ka vṛti abhivyakta caitanya eva adhyāsa iti na kā api anupapattiḥ na ca  rūpya ādikam idam aṃśa avacchinna caitanye adhyastam bhāsate ca avidyā vṛtti pratibimbita caitanyena iti viṣayiṇi jñāne viṣayasya adhyāsaḥ katham iti vācyam eka avacchinna eva apara avacchedena nirapekṣā upādheḥ iva atra bhedakatva abhāvāt ata eva abhiyuktaiḥ phala aikyāt aikyam jñānasya ucyate na ca rūpya ādeḥ sva jñāne adhyasta tve rūpya jñānasya jñāne bhrama utpattiḥ tad jñānena tad nivṛttiḥ iti ca syāt  adhiṣṭhāna ajñāna jñānābhyām adhyāsasya janma nivṛttyoḥ niyata tvāt jñānam rajatam iti pratīti prasaṅgāt ca iti vācyam rajata ākāra vṛtti avacchinna caitanyasya rajata bhrama adhiṣṭhānatva anabhyupagamāt  idam aṃśa avacchinna caitanyam eva tu rajata bhrama adhiṣṭhānam tad ca daivāt rajata ākāra vṛtti avacchinna caitanyam api na etāvatā bhrama adhiṣṭhāna tve tad apekṣā tasya ca bhrama virodhi śukti vādya akāraṇa ajñānam bhrama kāraṇam tena ākāreṇa jñānam bhrama nivartakam ataeva na jñānam rajatam iti bhrama ākāra āpattiḥ vṛtti avacchinnasya eva jñāna tvāt tasya ca adhiṣṭhānatva abhāvāt  adhiṣṭhāna tādātmyena cāropya pratītiḥ iti idam rajatam iti eva bhrama ākāraḥ nanu  ghaṭa ādeḥ kha sat nikṛṣṭa indriya janya sva jñānāt pūrva sattvena tatra adhyāsaḥ  na yuktaḥ na ca yā ghaṭa indriya sannikarṣa jā vṛttiḥ tayā ghaṭaḥ  na prakāśyaḥ yena ca prakāśyaḥ  ghaṭa adhiṣṭhāna caitanyena na tad sannikarṣa jam iti vācyam vṛtti atirikta jñāne māna abhāvāt ajñāna nivṛtteḥ api tatas  eva bhāvāt iti ced na vṛtti udayāt prāc ajñāta artha siddhi artham vṛtti atirikta jñānasya avaśyam abhyupeya tvāt  anyathā tasya sādhaka abhāvena śaśaśṛṅga tulya tayā sannikarṣa tad janya jñāna hetu tvena prāk  sattva kalpanā niṣprāmāṇikī syāt  tasmāt yādṛśasya ghaṭa ādeḥ indriya sannikarṣa āśraya tvena jñāna kāraṇa tvam tādṛśasya sādhakam kiñcid mānam avaśyam abhyupeyam anyathā anvaya vyatirekayoḥ agraheṇa kārya kāraṇa bhāva agrahāt sarva m ānameya ādi vyavasthā ucchidyeta tad ca mānam na vṛtti rūpam tadānīm vṛtti kāraṇa apravṛtteḥ iti tad vilakṣaṇam nityam sva prakāśam eva lāghavāt  vṛtti gata utpatti vināśa jaḍatva ādibhiḥ tad asaṃsparśāt tad eva ca nānāvidha upādhi saṃbandhāt nānāvidha vyavahāra bhāj  bhavati nabha iva ghaṭa maṇi mallikā ādi upādhi bhedena tad ca ajñāna sādhaka tvāt svarūpataḥ na ajñāna nivartakam vṛti uparaktam tu ajñāna nivartakam iti na vṛtteḥ anupayogaḥ tathā ca sarva ajñāna sādhake sākṣi caitanye tasmin ghaṭa ādeḥ adhyāsa iti kā anupapattiḥ tad uktam sureśvara ācāryaiḥ ‘sarva tīrtha dṛśām siddhiḥ sva abhipretasya vastunaḥ yad abhyupagamāt eva tad siddhiḥ vāryate kutas  iti ‘sarva tīrtha dṛśām tāvat sāmānyam māna lakṣaṇam ajñāta artha avagamanam tvad ukte tad na yujyate svatas  siddhaḥ athavā asiddhaḥ  deha ādiḥ te bhavan bhavet  pramāṇānām pramāṇa tvam na ubhayatra api labhyate pramāṇāni antareṇa api deha ādiḥ ced  prasidhyati vada pramāṇaiḥ kaḥ anvarthaḥ  na hi siddhasya sādhanam svatas asiddhe prameye tu na asataḥ  vyañjikā pramā na abhivyanakti savitā śaśa śṛṅgam sphuran  api iti na ca ‘ghaṭaḥ ayam iti asau vṛttiḥ ābhāsasya prasādataḥ vijñātaḥ  ghaṭa iti uktiḥ brahma anubhavataḥ  bhavet  iti vadatā vṛtti pratibimbitasya ghaṭān adhiṣṭhāna caitanyasya ghaṭa anubhava tu ukti virodha iti vācyam vṛtti prativimbita caitanyasya ghaṭa adhiṣṭhāna caitanyena saha bheda abhāvāt caitanyasya eka tvāt  yathā ca ekasya eva caitanyasya sarva bhāsaka tvam tathā vistareṇa upapāditam na abhāva upalabdheḥ iti asmin  adhikaraṇe bhāṣya kṛdbhiḥ nanu  dṛśya tvāni athā anupapattyā mithyātvam iti artha āpattiḥ vivakṣitā kim vā satya tve dṛśya tvam na syāt iti anukūla tarka mātram na ādyaḥ tad sāmagrya bhāvāt  tathā hi ākṣepyasya upapādaka tvam pramāṇa aviruddha tvam ākṣepakasya anupapadyamāna tvam pramita tvam ca iti arthāpatti sāmagrī prakṛte cākṣepya saṃbandhinaḥ  mithyātvam na ākṣepakasya saṃbandhasya upapādakam pratyuta pratikūlam eva naca adhyastatva rūpa saṃbandhasya na tad pratikūla tvam tasyādya apya siddheḥ anākṣepaka tvāt  pratyakṣa ādi viruddham ca idam ākṣepyam na api ekasya dṛśya tvasya upapattaye pramita an ekasya tyāgaḥ  yuktaḥ ākṣepakam ca na dṛś adhyasta tvam tasya eva phalata ākṣepya tvāt  na api dṛś viṣayatva rūpaḥ  dṛś saṃbandhaḥ tava asiddheḥ dṛś adhīna siddhika tvam dṛś viṣayatva atiriktasya tasya asiddheḥ na antyaḥ sattve api ukta rītyā saṃbandha antareṇa eva dṛśya tvasya upapanna tayā anupapatteḥ eva abhāvāt iti ced na anukūla tarkasya eva prakrānta tvena arthāpattiḥ vā ityādi vikalpa an avakāśāt ubhayathā api adoṣāt ca tathā hi satya tve dṛś dṛśya saṃbandha anupapattiḥ mithyātvam ca tad upapādakam na tad saṃbandha pratikūlam mithyātve api śukti rūpasya idam aṃśe adhyastatva rūpa saṃbandha darśanena saṃbandha sāmānye pratikūlatva abhāvāt  ākṣepakaḥ api dṛś viṣayatva rūpaḥ  dṛś saṃbandha eva adhyāsa rūpasya dṛś viṣaya tvasya mamā api saṃpratipatteḥ tāttvikasya eva tasya niṣedhāt  na ca adhyasta tvasya adya api asiddhiḥ dṛś saṃbandha sāmānyasya ākṣepakasya prasakta viśeṣa niṣedhe api adhyastatva rūpa viśeṣa paryavasānena asiddhi abhāvāt na hi adhyasta saṃbandha tvena ākṣepaka tā kim tu saṃbandha tvena sa ca adhyastatva saṃbandha saṃbhāvanayā api abādhita eva iti na ca ghaṭasya jñānam iti dhī siddha saṃbandha sāmānyasya adhyasta tvam na viśeṣaḥ na hi rūpyasya śuktiḥ iti pratītiḥ asti iti vācyam rūpyasya śuktiḥ iti prati iti abhāve api rūpyasya śuktiḥ adhiṣṭhānam iti pratītyai  adhyasta tvasya saṃbandha viśeṣatva siddheḥ caitrasya maitra iti prati iti abhāve api caitrasya pitā maitra iti pratītivat  ākṣepyam atra pramāṇa aviruddham eva adhyakṣa ādi virodhasya prāk eva parihṛta tvāt  ākṣepake ca pramita tvam anapekṣitam eva apramitena api pratibimbena bimba ākṣepa darśanāt tarka para tāyām api na aprayojaka tā satya tve saṃbandha anupapatteḥ bhavat ukta nyāya khaṇḍanena prathamata eva upapādita tvāt dṛśyatva abhāvasya āpādakam atra sattvam anirvācyatva abhāvaḥ  vā tri kālābādhya tvam vā ubhayathā api na doṣaḥ na ca anirvācyatva abhāvasya tucche parokṣadhī vet yatayā dṛśye api sattvena vyabhicāraḥ kāraṇa asāmarthyena tatra tad ākāra vṛtti samullāse api dṛś saṃbandha rūpasya dṛśya tvasya tuccha virodhinaḥ tatra abhāvāt tuccha ākāra tāyāḥ  vṛtti gata tve api vṛtti saṃbandhasya tuccha gatatva abhāva upapatteḥ na api yathā sataḥ  brahmaṇaḥ sva vyavahṛtyā saṃbandhaḥ tathā ghaṭa ādeḥ api sata eva sva jñānena saṃbandhaḥ astu iti vācyam dṛṣṭānte brahmaṇi adhyāsasya eva vyavahṛti saṃbandha tvāt  tathā ca ubhaya saṃbandhi satve viṣaya viṣayi bhāva anupapattiḥ na aprayojakatva ādinā paribhūyate etena ādhyāsikaḥ saṃbandhaḥ  nāma adhyasta saṃbandhaḥ  vā adhyasta tvam eva vā ādye saṃbandhasya mithyātve api saṃbandhinaḥ  dṛśyasya dṛśa iva mithyātva anupapattiḥ dvitīye jñānasya api adhyasta tvena tatra adhyāsa anupapattiḥ sva jñāna paraṃparāyām adhyāsa svīkāre anavasthā ca iti nirastam jñānam hi vṛtti avacchinnam caitanyam tatra avacchedikāyāḥ  vṛtteḥ jaḍāyāḥ  adhyasta tve api avacchedyasya caitanyasya prakāśa rūpasya anadhyasta tvena tatra dṛśyasya adhyāsāt  dṛśya mithyātve api anavasthā virahasya upapatteḥ ata eva śābda vṛtti viṣayaḥ  brahma na vṛttau kalpitam avidyā viṣayaḥ  brahmā avidyāyām na kalpitam yathā tathā dṛśyam na dṛśi kalpitam tathā ca dṛś dṛśya ādeḥ tāttvika eva saṃbandhaḥ sāmānya saṃvandhena eva atiprasaṅge niraste viśeṣa jijñāsā viśeṣa uktiḥ ca viśeṣa jijñāsā ādivat anarthikā eva iti nirastam vṛtti avidyayoḥ brahmaṇaḥ anadhyāse api tayoḥ eva brahmaṇi adhyāsāt  saṃbandha upapatteḥ atas tatra tāttvika saṃbandha abhāvāt katham tad dṛṣṭāntena dṛś dṛśyayoḥ api tāttvika saṃbandha iti ucyate tathā ca prasiddha viśeṣe bodhite sāmānyasya eva bādhaka śaṅkāyāḥ  atiprasaṅge prāpte viśeṣa jijñāsāyā viśeṣa ukteḥ ca sāphalyāt  na te nirarthike etena saṃbandhasya prāmāṇika tve yathā kathaṃcana lakṣaṇam bhaviṣyati tathā hi saṃyoga samavāya antarbhāve tad lakṣaṇam eva lakṣaṇam bhaviṣyati tad anantarbhāve tu tad ubhaya bhinna saṃbandha tvam eva lakṣaṇam astu iti nirastam ukta yuktyā prāmāṇika saṃvandhasya saṃyoga samavāya antarbhāvasya ca dūṣita tvāt  tad ubhaya bahis bhūta saṃbandha tvam tu vayam api na nirākurmaḥ kim tu tasya prāmāṇika tvam kiṃca dṛś dṛśyayoḥ na tāttvika saṃbandhaḥ saṃbandhi bhinna tve anavasthānāt  na ca dṛśyatva antara hīnasya dṛśyatva ādeḥ iva saṃbandhasya api sa nirvāhaka tvam kvacid  bhaviṣyati iti vācyam dṛśya tvam api dṛś saṃbandha eva tasya ca sva nirvāhaka tvam na māyika tvam vinā iti na asmākam pratikūlam abhyadhāyi devānāṃpriyeṇa abhinna tve saṃbandhatva ayogāt na ca evam ādhyāsika saṃbandha tve api etad doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tasya māyika tvena māyāyāḥ ca aghaṭita ghaṭanā paṭīyaḥ tvena sarva anupapatteḥ bhūṣaṇa tvāt  na ca atiprasaṅga nirākaraṇa artham dṛś dṛśyayoḥ saṃbandha nirvacanam prakṛtam na tu viṣayatva nirvacanam atas  viṣayatva khaṇḍanam anukta upālambhanam iti vācyam viṣayatva khaṇḍanena nirucyamāna prakṛta saṃbandhasya eva khaṇḍanāt  na ca viṣayi tvā niruktau  api viṣayiṇaḥ satya tvavat  viṣayi tvā niruktau  api viṣayaḥ satyaḥ syāt iti vācyam viṣayi tvā niruktau  api viṣaya adhyāsena eva tad upapattyā viṣayiṇaḥ satya tvam yuktam viṣayatva aniruktau tu viṣayasya satya tvam na yuktam viṣayiṇaḥ anadhyastatve viṣaya adhyāsam antareṇa anyasya upapādakasya abhāvāt  yatra tu viṣayiṇa eva adhyāsaḥ tatra viṣayaḥ satya eva yathā jñāna viṣayaḥ  brahma na ca ubhayā adhyāsaḥ śūnya vāda prasaṅgāt  anyatara adhyāse ca vinigamakam anuvṛttatva vyāvṛttatva prakāśa jaḍatva ādikam eva tasmāt viṣayiṇaḥ nitya dṛśaḥ anadhyāsāt  viṣayasya eva atra adhyāsaḥ na ca ‘ pramāṇa jātam sva viṣaya āvaraṇe atyādi yuktyā dṛś viṣayatva rūpa dṛśya tvasya hetūkaraṇena ca tvayā api viṣaya tvam nirvācyam eva iti vācyam tattvataḥ anirvācya tve api adhyasta tvena ghaṭa ādi sama kakṣa nirvācya tvasya saṃbhavāt  nanu  katham pramāṇa jñāna viṣayaḥ adhyasta iti ced na prapañca viṣaya ka jñāne tattva āvedakatva lakṣaṇa prāmāṇya abhāvāt iti gṛhāṇa ataeva yādṛśam viṣaya tvam te vṛttim prati cit ātmanaḥ tādṛśam viṣaya tvam me dṛśyasya api dṛśam pratīti nirastam cit ātmanaḥ anadhyāse api vṛtteḥ tatra adhyasta tvena tad dṛṣṭāntena prakṛte api anadhyāsasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  syāt etad  mithyātva nirvacanāt tad sādhanam dṛśyatva ādikam nirvaktavyam eva na hi ghaṭa ādi asaṅkīrṇa ākāra jñānam vinā tad vilakṣaṇa vyavahāraḥ atha niruktā saṅkīrṇa ākāra jñāna mātreṇa tad upapattiḥ tarhi tulyam mama api iyān  tu viśeṣaḥ yad tava sa ākāraḥ sat vilakṣaṇaḥ mama tu tvad mata siddha prātibhāsika vailakṣaṇya sādhaka māna siddham asattākaḥ na hi lakṣaṇa ukti anuktibhyām sat asat vailakṣaṇya rūpā nirvacanīyatva hāni lābhau brahmaṇi api śrautasya api jagat kāraṇatva ādi lakṣaṇasya khaṇḍanarītyā asaṃbhavāt  tvayā eva‘ kīdṛś tad pratyak iti cetādṛgīdṛś iti dvayam yatra na prasarati etad pratyak iti avadhāraye ati brahmaṇaḥ api durnirūpatvā ukteḥ ca prapañce api tvad uktā nirvācyatva sama kakṣa lakṣaṇa saṃbhavāt ca ‘yat kaṭhinam sā pṛthivī atyādi śrutyā pṛthivī ādīnām api lakṣaṇatva ukteḥ ca tasmāt anirvācya tvam na sattva virodhi sattve api anudbhūta tvāt eva anirvācyatva upapatteḥ na ca nirvācya tvam api sattva prayojakam na hi śukti rūpyasya api itara bheda sādhakam rūpya tvam prātītika jāti rūpa tayā su vacam api satyam kiṃca brahmaṇa ānandatva jñānatva satyatva sva prakāśatva ādi khaṇḍanā ukta rītyā durvacam iti brahma tattu atas anānanda ādi ātmakam syāt  tasmāt ikṣu kṣīra ādi mādhuryavat anirvācyam api viṣaya tvam sat eva iti atra ucyate  dṛśya tvādeḥ anirvacanīya tvam kim sattvena uta sva rūpeṇa na ādyaḥ sattvena anirvacanīya tve api tad tad ābhāsa lakṣaṇa anāliṅgitatva mātreṇa hetutva upapatteḥ tad nirvacana anapekṣaṇāt na dvitīyaḥ tāttvikā tāttvika sādhāraṇena dṛś saṃbandhitva ādinā rūpeṇa dṛś viṣaya tvasya nirvaktum aśakyatvāt  lakṣaṇa ukti anuktyoḥ na sat asat vailakṣaṇya rūpā nirvācyatva hā anilābha kara tvam iti yad avocaḥ tad api na pūrva ukta vyāpaka anupalabdhi sahitāyāḥ  lakṣaṇa anirukteḥ ukta rūpā nirvacanīyatva prayojaka tvāt yadtva ānandatva ādinā dharmeṇa kīdṛś iti ādinā sva rūpeṇa ca durnirūpa tvāt  brahmaṇaḥ api anirvacanīyatva prasaṅga iti tad na ānandatva ādi dharmavat tayā durnirūpa tve api duḥkha pratyanīkatva ādi upalakṣita svarūpasya sattvena nirvaktum śakya tvāt  na ca evam prapañce sattvam śakya nirvacanam bādhaka sadbhāvāt ataeva kaṭhina sparśava tu ādinā pṛthivītva ādīnām nirvacanam asti eva sattve api udbhūtatva ādinā nirvācyatva upapattiḥ iti— nirastam na hi nirukti viraha mātreṇa anirvācya tvam brūmaḥ kiṃtu sattva ādinā nirukti viraheṇa sa ca prapañce bādhakāt asti eva na ca jñāne viṣayasya adhyasta tve tad ajñāna janyam tad jñāna nivartyam ca adhyāsam prati viṣaya tvam tad anuviddha tayā pratītyabhāvaḥ ca na saṃbhavati iti vācyam caitanya mātra ajñāna janya tvāt tad jñāna nivartya tvāt ca ghaṭa ādi prapañcasya iti ukta tvāt  sat iti pratīyamāna adhiṣṭhāna caitanya anuviddha tayā pratīyamāna tvam api asti eva tasmāt satya tve dṛś dṛśya saṃbandhatva anupapattiḥ dṛḍhā eva atha pratikarma vyavasthā upapattiḥ nanu viśvasya adhyāsika tve prātibhāsika sthala iva viṣaya indriya sannikarṣa adhīnāyāḥ pratikarma vyavasthāyāḥ  anupapattiḥ iti   ced na vṛtteḥ pūrvam eva ghaṭa ādīnām caitanye adhyāsena prātibhāsika sthalā apekṣayā vailakṣaṇyāt  tathā hi   antaḥkaraṇam cakṣuḥvat tejaḥ vayavi tad ca indriya dvāreṇa tad saṃyuktam viṣayam vyāpya tad ākāram bhavati yathā nadī ādi udakam praṇāḍyā niḥsṛtya kedāra ādi ākāram bhavati sā eva vṛttiḥ itti ucyate tatra jīva caitanyam avidyā upādhikam sat  sarva gatam antaḥkaraṇa upādhikam sat  paricinnam iti mata dvayam tatra ādye viṣaya prakāśakam jīva caitanyam dvitīye brahmacaitanyam ādye pakṣe api jīva caitanyam avidyā anāvṛtam āvṛtam ca tatra ādye vṛttiḥ jīva caitanyasya viṣaya uparāga arthā dvitīye tu āvaraṇa abhibhava arthā paricchinnatva pakṣe tu jīva caitanyasya viṣaya prakāśaka tad adhiṣṭhāna caitanya abheda abhivyakti arthā anāvṛtatva pakṣe hi anāvṛtam sarva gatam api jīva caitanyam tad tad ākāra vṛttyā eva uparajyate na tu viṣayaiḥ asaṅga tvāt  yathā gaḥ tvam sarva gatam api sāsnādimat vyaktyā abhivyajyate na tu kesara ādi mayaktyā yathā vā pradīpa prabhā ākāśa gandha rasa ādi vyāpinī api tān na prakāśayantī rūpa saṃsargi tayā rūpam eva prakāśayati tadvat  kevala agni adāhyasya api ayaḥ piṇḍa ādi samārūḍha agni dāhya tvavat ca kevala caitanyā prakāśyasya api ghaṭa ādeḥ tad tad ākāra vṛti upārūḍha caitanya prakāśya tvam yuktam evañcāna āvṛtatva pakṣe tad tad ākāra vṛtti dvārā caitanyasya tad tad uparāge tad tad artha prakāśaḥ āvṛtatva pakṣe tad tad ākāra vṛttyā tad tad viṣaya avacchinna caitanya āvaraṇa abhibhavena tad tad artha prakāśaḥ antaḥkaraṇa avacchinna caitanya rūpa tve jīvasya avacchedaka antaḥkaraṇa tad tad viṣaya ākāra vṛttyā tad tad viṣaya avacchinna caitanya abhivyaktau tad tad prakāśaḥ yadi api prakāśakam adhiṣṭhāna caitanyam sarva gatam jīva caitanyam ca antaḥkaraṇa avacchinnam tathā api caitanya abhedena abhivyakta tvāt  vyavasthā upapattiḥ nanu iyam pratikarma vyavasthā na upapadyate tathā hi svasannikṛṣṭa indriya janya sva jñānāt pūrvam ghaṭa ādeḥ sattve pratīti mātra śarīratva vyāptaka alpa nikatvā yogaḥ na ca kālpanikatva viśeṣaḥ prātibhāsikatva ādiḥ eva tad vyāptaḥ gauravāt  na ca pratīti mātra śarīratva abhāve api jñāna nivartyatva ādinā eva kalpita tvam bhaviṣyati pratīti mātra śarīratva abhāvena jñāna nivartyatva abhāvasya api āpādya tvāt  pratīteḥ viśva satya tvena vā mithyātve api svapna ādivat indriya sannikarṣa nirapekṣa tayā vā upapatteḥ vyāvahārika tvasya api bhrānti dairghya mātreṇa upapatteḥ ca iti ced  mā evam pratīti mātra śarīra tvasya kalpita tvam na vyāpyam dṛś dṛśya saṃbandha anupapatti ādi saha kṛta ukta anumānāt prapañce kalpita tve siddhe pratyabhijñā balāt ca sthāyi tve tatra eva vyabhicārāt  na ca śukti rūpya ādi pratyabhijñā sāmyam prakṛta pratyabhijñāyā iti vācyam pratītyaviśeṣe api vaṇij vīthī stha śukti rūpyayoḥ parīkṣitatva aparīkṣita tvābhyām sthāyitvā āsthāyitva rūpa viśeṣa saṃbhavāt tathā api vā parokṣa vṛtteḥ iva aparokṣa vṛtteḥ api prakāśa tvam astu kim tad uparakta caitanyena iti ced na parokṣa sthale api parokṣa vṛtti uparakta caitanyasya eva prakāśaka tvāt  atha tatra api aparokṣa eka rasa caitanya uparāge viṣaya aparokṣya prasaṅgaḥ na viṣaya caitanya abhivyaktau  eva viṣayasya aparokṣyam na ca parokṣa sthale tad asti viṣaya indriya sannikarṣa abhāvena viṣaya paryantam vṛtteḥ agamanāt  antar ā iva tatra dhī samullāsāt  aparokṣa sthale tu pramātṛ caitanya abheda abhivyakta adhiṣṭhāna caitanya uparāgaḥ  viṣaye asti tatra viṣayasya karma kāraka tvāt  na ca vṛtti gata viśeṣāt āparokṣyam tatra hi viśeṣa viṣaya kṛtaḥ ced om iti brūmaḥ jāti kṛtaḥ tu viśeṣaḥ  na saṃbhavati saḥ ayam iti pratyabhijñāyām parokṣatva aparokṣa tvayoḥ saṃkara prasaṅgāt  avyāpya vṛtti tvāt pramātu ā ādinā saṃkara prasaṅgāt ca kiṃca vṛtteḥ jaḍa tvāt eva na prakāśaka tvam na ca vṛttau  antaḥkaraṇa āvṛttyā api sva prakāśa tvam jñāna tvavat iti vācyam sva prakāśa ātma saṃbandhena eva tasyāḥ prakāśatva upapattau tad sva prakāśa tve māna abhāvāt kiṃca ghaṭam jānāmi iti anubhūya mānasa karmaka vṛtti anyā saṃvid  ghaṭa prakāśa rūpā ghaṭaḥ prakāśata iti ākāraka anubhava sidvā eva na ca karoti yatate calati gacchati iti ādau  eka artha tve api sa karmakā karmaka svabhāvatva darśanāt atra api ekārtha tve api tathā syāt iti vācyam tatra api ekārthatva abhāvāt  anukūla yatnaḥ  hi kṛñdhātu arthaḥ yati arthaḥ tu yatna mātram evam gamī artha uttara saṃyoga phalakaḥ spandaḥ calati arthaḥ tu spanda mātram tathā ca eka arthaka tve kutra api na sa karmakatva akarmakatva vyavasthā na ca  tvad mate pariṇateḥ akarmaka tvāt pariṇati viśeṣa bhūtāyā vṛtteḥ katham sa karmaka tvam iti vācyam ekasya hi sa karmakatva akarmaka tve eka rūpeṇa viruddhe na tu rūpa antareṇa api māna abhāvāt yathā sthiteḥ akarmikāyāḥ  api agamana tvena rūpeṇa sa karmaka tvam tathā pariṇati tvena rūpeṇa ākarmikāyāḥ  api vṛtteḥ jñāna tvena sa karmaka tvam bhaviṣyati iti adoṣaḥ nanu tarhi atītaḥ prakāśate iti dhīḥ na syāt  na iṣṭa āpatteḥ tatra api vṛtti pratibimbita caitanya sattvena prakāśata ityādi prayoga saṃbhavāt ca nanu yathā jñāna virodhi vṛttau  anubhava tvam na asti kiṃtu anyatra tathā dveṣa virodhi vṛtteḥ anyatra icchātvam iti api syāt iti ced na bādhaka sattva asattvābhyām viśeṣāt  atra eva tatra sa karmakā karmaka vilakṣaṇa kriyān anubhavāt ca yathā ca vṛtti atirikta bhāna siddhiḥ tathā svayam jyotiṣṭva prastāve vistareṇa vakṣyāmaḥ nanu astu caitanyasya viṣaya prakāśaka tvam tathā api antaḥkaraṇasya dehāt nirgatiḥ na kalpyā parokṣa vailakṣaṇyāya viṣayasya abhivyakta aparokṣa cit uparāga eva vaktavyaḥ cit uparāga ādau ca aparokṣa vṛtteḥ tad ākāra tvam eva tantram tasya ca tad saṃśleṣam vinā api parokṣa vṛtteḥ iva tad sannikṛṣṭa karaṇa janya tvena eva upapattiḥ na tu prabhāyā iva vṛtteḥ tad āvaraṇa nivartakatva ādau tad saṃśleṣaḥ tantram netrāt nirgacchat dhruva ādi ākāra vṛttyā eva sva saṃśliṣṭa netra stha kajjala ādeḥ dhruva netra madhya vartinaḥ paramāṇu ādeḥ ca aparokṣatva āpātāt iti ced  na viṣayeṣu abhivyakta cit uparāge na tad ākāratva mātram tantram parokṣa sthale api prasaṅgāt  kiṃtu tad saṃśleṣaḥ prabhāyā viṣaya sannikṛṣṭa tejaḥ tvena āvaraṇa abhibhāvakatva darśanāt taijasasya manasaḥ api ajñāna rūpa āvaraṇa abhibhavāya tad saṃśleṣa āvaśyakaḥ dhruva ādi deha madhya varti paramāṇu ādau  atiprasaṅgaḥ tu tad ākāratva prayojaka sāmagrī virahāt eva pariharaṇīyaḥ anyathā indriya sannikarṣa ādeḥ vidyamāna tvāt  paramāṇu ādi ākāra tāyāḥ  durnivāratva āpatteḥ tasmāt  prabhā viśeṣa anvaya vyatirekābhyām yad  klṛptam sannikṛṣṭa tejaḥ tvena āvaraṇa abhibhāvaka tvam tasya tad ākāratva rūpa viśeṣa apekṣāyām api na tyāgaḥ na hi pṛthivī tvac andhatva ādinā kārya kāraṇa bhāve āvaśyake anitya guṇatva dravyatva ādinā tad tyāgaḥ ataeva— tad itara hetu sākalye sati ghaṭa cakṣuḥ sannikarṣasya eva ghaṭa anubhava janaka tvam na tu ghaṭa manaḥ sannikarṣasya tad vilambena tad vilamba abhāvāt iti nirastam āvaraṇa bhaṅge sannikṛṣṭa tejaḥ kāraṇatva avadhāraṇena tasya api āvaśyaka tvāt na ca sparśana pratyakṣe cakṣuḥ ādivat niyata golaka dvāra abhāvena antaḥkaraṇa nirgatya yogāt āvaraṇa abhibhava anupapattiḥ iti vācyam sarvatra tad tad indriya adhiṣṭhānasya eva dvāratva saṃbhavāt na ca antaḥkaraṇa vṛttitva aviśeṣāt icchā dveṣa ādi rūpa vṛttayaḥ api dehān nirgatya viṣaya saṃsṛṣṭā bhavanti iti katham na svīkriyata iti vācyam āvaraṇa abhibhāvaka tejaḥ tu asya tad pramāpakasya jñānavat  tatra abhāvāt nanu ghaṭa prakāśakam caitanyam upadeśa sāhasri anusāreṇa ghaṭa ākāra dhī sthā cit vā parāgartha prameyeṣu iti ādi vārttika ukta rītyā dhī pratibimbita caitanya abheda abhivyakta viṣaya adhiṣṭhāna caitanyam vā na ādyaḥ ādhyāsika saṃbandhasya atantra tā āpātāt na dvitīyaḥ āvaśyakena viṣaya saṃśliṣṭa vṛtti pratibimbita caitanyena eva tad ajñāna nivṛttivat  tad prakāśasya api upapattau kim viṣaya adhiṣṭhāna caitanya abhivyakti kalpanena iti ced na prakāśakam tāvat  adhiṣṭhāna caitanyam tad ca adhyāsena viṣayaiḥ saha sākṣāt saṃbaddham prakāśasya ca svayam bhāsamānasya sva saṃbaddha sarva bhāsaka tvam api klṛptam eva etad anabhyupagame kalpanā antara gaurava āpatteḥ tad ca anabhivyaktam nirvikalpaka rūpam ācchādita dīpavat na prakāśakam iti tad abhivyaktiḥ apekṣitā tad ca parokṣa sthale vṛtti avacchedena eva abhivyajyate aparokṣa sthale tu vṛtti saṃparkāt āvaraṇa ajñāna abhibhave viṣayaḥ abhivyajyate vṛtteḥ viṣaya paryanta tvāt  na ca parokṣa sthale api evam prasaṅgaḥ dvāra abhāvena antaḥkaraṇa nirgatya bhāvāt nanu vṛtteḥ tad ākāra tvam na tāvat tad viṣaya tvam tvayā eva nirāsāt  na api tasmin caitanya uparāga yogya tāpādaka tvam tad ajñāna abhibhāvaka tvam vā ubhayoḥ api tad ākāratva prayojya tvena tattva ayogāt na api ghaṭa ādivat  pṛthu budhna udara ādi ākāra tvam sa ākāravāda āpātāt saṃsthāna hīna jāti guṇa ādi vṛtteḥ nirākāratva prasaṅgāt ca ghaṭa paṭau  iti samūha ālambane viruddha nānā ākāratva āpatteḥ ca iti ced na asti ityādi tad viṣaya ka vyavahāra pratibandhaka ajñāna nivartana yogya tvasya tad sannikṛṣṭa karaṇa janya tvasya vā tad ākāratva rūpa tvāt tad ubhayam ca sva kāraṇa adhīna svabhāva viśeṣāt na ca ātma āśrayaḥ nivṛtti janana svarūpa yogya tayā phala upadhānasya sādhya tvena sva anapekṣaṇāt  nanu dṛśi viṣaya adhyāsa svīkartuḥ jīva caitanyam vā viṣaya dṛś  brahmacaitanyam vā na ādyaḥ jīve avacchinna cit svarūpe kalpite adhyāsa ayogāt  na ca viṣaya dṛś  jīva caitanyam eva adhyāsaḥ tu brahmacaitanya iti vācyam dṛśyayoḥ eva adhyāsika saṃbandha āpatteḥ adhyasta adhiṣṭhānayoḥ ubhayoḥ api dṛś bhinna tvāt  ata eva na dvitīyaḥ api brahmaṇaḥ api kalpita tvena tatra adhyāsa ayogāt ca na ca śuddha caitanyam ekam eva tad eva adhiṣṭhānam tatra avacchedakam avidyā ādikam na adhiṣṭhāna koṭau praviśati tad eva ca jīva śabdena brahma śabdena ca vyapadiśyate upādhi viśeṣāt  tathā ca jīva caitanyasya dṛś tve api dṛśya adhyāsaḥ  na anupapanna iti vācyam śuddha caitanyasya āsaṃsāram āvṛta tvena jagat āndhya prasaṅgāt iti ced na mūla avidyā nivṛtti abhāvena sarvata āvaraṇa abhibhava abhāve api ghaṭa ādi avacchedena āvaraṇa abhibhavāt āndhya viraha upapatteḥ nanu  tarhi idānīm api brahma sphuraṇe carama vṛtti vaiyarthyam adhika bhāge api tasya sphuraṇāt  na hi akhaṇḍa artha vedānta janyāyām vṛttau bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ  vā viśeṣaṇam upalakṣaṇam vā prakāraḥ prakāśata iti ced na upādhi aviṣaya kabrahma sphuraṇasya carama vṛtti prayukta tvena tasyāḥ sāphalyāt  prakāra asphuraṇam tu tasyāḥ bhūṣaṇam eva idānīntana sphuraṇasya sa prakāra tvena upādhi viṣaya tvāt aekadhā eva anudraṣṭavya am ityādi śruti balāt  sva samāna viṣaya jñānāt eva ca ajñāna vṛtteḥ akhaṇḍa cit mātra jñānasya eva mokṣa hetutva avadhāraṇāt na ca antaḥkaraṇa avacchinna caitanyasya jīva tve suṣupti daśāyām tad abhāvena kṛta hāni ādi āpattiḥ iti vācyam tadā api asya kāraṇa ātmanā avasthānāt sthūla sūkṣma sādhāraṇasya antaḥkaraṇasya upādhi tvāt  ‘tad apīteḥ saṃsāra vyapadeśā aditi asmin sūtre ca ayam arthaḥ spaṣṭataraḥ na ca vṛtti uparakta tvam caitanyasya na tad pratibimbita tvam darpaṇe mukhasya iva anudbhūta rūpe antaḥkaraṇe śabdāni apratibimbana upādhitāyā acākṣuṣa caitanyasya pratibimbitāyāḥ ca ayogāt iti vācyam udbhūta rūpava tvam na pratibimbita upādhita aprayojakam asvacche api loṣṭa ādau pratibimba āpatteḥ kiṃtu svaccha tvam tad ca prakāśa svabhāva tvena manasaḥ tad pariṇāma bhūtāyā vṛtteḥ ca asti eva triguṇa ātmakasya api ajñānasya su accha sattva ātmaka tāyā api sattvena tatra api prativimbita upādhitāyāḥ sattvāt  na api cākṣuṣa tvam pratibimbitatva prayojakam acākṣuṣasya api ākāśa ādeḥ pratibimbitatva darśanāt  nanu cākṣuṣa vṛtti upārūḍha citaḥ katham rūpa mātra prakāśaka tvam na ca prabhāvat niyamaḥ vaiṣamyāt  tathā hi prabhāyām tamaḥ virodhi tvam rūpam pratīva gandha ādīn pratyapi samam na hi sā gandha deśa stham tamaḥ  na nivartayati na ca ajñāna nirodhitva lakṣaṇa prakāśaka tvam rūpam pratyeva na tu rasa ādīn prati iti vācyam ajñāna nivartaka tvasya vṛtti bhinne anaṅgīkārāt  prabhāyā rūpa grāhaka cakṣuḥ sahakāri tvavat  gandha ādi grāhi ghrāṇa ādi sahakāritva abhāve api citaḥ  grāhaka antara asahakāri tvena tadvat sahakāri vilambena vilambasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  tathā ca citaḥ sarva gata tvena sarva saṃbandhāt rūpa ādivat  gurutva ādeḥ api āśraya dvārā sākṣāt vā saṃbandhi tvāt  prakāśa āpattiḥ vṛtti uparakta cit saṃbandhasya eva prakāśaka tvāt  ‘asaṅgaḥ  hi ayam puruṣa iti śrutiḥ tu tad kṛta lepa abhāva parā na tu saṃbandha niṣedhikā ‘sa yad tatra yad kiṃcid paśyati ananvāgataḥ tena bhavati iti pūrva vākyāt  ‘yathā ākāśa sthitaḥ  nityam vāyuḥ sarvatragaḥ mahān iti ādi smṛteḥ ca iti ced na prabhāyā rūpa rasa ādi deśa gata
