tamaḥ nāśaka tvam tad saṃbandhāt yujyate caitanyasya tu svabhāvataḥ asaṃbaddha tvāt tad ākāra vṛttyā tad eka saṃbandhasya upādānāt katham anya avabhāsakatva prasaṅgaḥ svabhāvataḥ  hi asaṅga tve ‘asaṅgaḥ  hi ayam puruṣa iti śrutiḥ pramāṇam na ca eṣā lepa abhāva parā akartṛtva pratipādanāya saṃbandha abhāva paratvāt yathā ca etad tathā vyaktam ākare evam smṛtiḥ api etad śṛti anurodhena neyā atas  sarvaiḥ saha saṃbandha abhāvāt  na sarva avabhāsaḥ kiṃtu yad ākārā vṛttiḥ tasya eva ata evam ‘idam rajata miti bhrame idam ākāra vṛti avacchinna caitanyena rajata bhāna anupapatteḥ rajata ākārā api avidyā vṛttiḥ abhyupeyate svataścit vimba āgrāhake caitanyasya tad ākāratva ayogāt svataścid bimba grāhake tu antaḥkaraṇa vṛtti ādau na vṛtti apekṣā iti na anavasthā na ca āśraya saṃbandha aviśeṣe api rūpa ākārā vṛttiḥ na gandha ādi ākāra iti kuta iti vācyam yathā tava cākṣuṣa jñāne āśraya saṃbandha aviśeṣe api na gandhaḥ  viṣayaḥ tathā asmākam api cakṣuḥ dvāraka vṛttau na gandha ādi ākāra tvam indriya viṣaya saṃbandhānām svabhāvasya niyāmakasya samāna tvāt  nanu ādhyāsika saṃbandhaḥ  vṛtteḥ pūrvam api asti eva anyaḥ tu uparāgaḥ  na dṛśya tve tantram iti kim tad arthayā vṛttyā iti ced na jīva caitanyasya adhiṣṭhāna caitanyasya vā abheda abhivyakti artha tvāt vṛtteḥ anyathā mayā idam viditam iti saṃbandha avabhāsaḥ  na syāt  nanu jīva caitanyasya āsaṅga tve brahmacaitanyam suta rām asaṅgam tathā ca māyā upādhika viṣaya uparāga tvāt svatas  sārvajñyam na syāt  na ca brahma sarva upādāna tvāt upādhim vinā eva sva svarūpa vatsva abhinnam jagat avabhāsayati iti vācyam upādāna tvam na tāvat viśiṣṭa niṣṭham pariṇāmi tvam ādhyāsika saṃbandhasya atantra tā āpatteḥ anādya vidyā ādikam prati tad abhāvāt ca na api śuddha niṣṭham adhiṣṭhāna tvam śuddhasya sarvajñatva sarva śaktitva ādeḥ abhāvāt iti ced na brahmaṇaḥ asaṃga tve api sarveṣām tatra adhyāsena māyā upādhim vinā eva tasya sarva prakāśaka tayā sārvajñya upapatteḥ na ca śuddha niṣṭham adhiṣṭhāna tvam na upādāna tvam sārvajñya abhāvāt iti uktam iti vācyam avidyā kalpitānām sarvajñatva ādīnām śuddhe sattvāt  anyathā teṣām taṭa stha lakṣaṇa tvam api na syāt  nanu āvaraṇa abhibhava arthatva pakṣaḥ  na yuktaḥ vivartā adhiṣṭhānasya cit mātrasya ajñāna ādi sākṣi tvena sadā prakāśanāt  anyasya ajñāna kalpitasya āvaraṇasya abhāvāt iti ced na ajñāna ādi sākṣi tvena sva prakāśe api aśanāya ādi atītatva ādinā prakāśa abhāvāt āvaraṇasya avaśya tvāt  nanua jñānasya nayana paṭalavat  puṃgata tve caitrasya ajñāna nāśe api maitrasya tad anāśāt aprakāśaḥ  yuktaḥ viṣaya gata tve tu caitra arjitayā vṛttyā ajñāne dīpena tamasi iva nāśite maitrasya api prakāśaḥ syāt iti ced na caitra āvaraṇa śakteḥ eva ajñāna gatāyāḥ caitra arjita vṛttyā nāśita tvena sa paśyati na maitraḥ tad pratiyogika āvaraṇa śakteḥ anāśāt āvaraṇa śaktīnām draṣṭṛ viṣaya bhedābhyām bhinna tvāt  tamastu na tathā iti eka ānīta pradīpena api anyān prati prakāśaḥ  yujyate etena eka jñāna pakṣe śukti jñānena tad ajñāna nivṛttau sadya eva mokṣa āpātaḥ anivṛttau rūpya ādeḥ sa vilāsā vidyā nivṛtti rūpa bādhā yoga iti nirastam āvaraṇa śakti nāśe api mūla ajñāna nāśa abhāvena sadyas  mokṣa abhāvasya rūpya ādau sa vilāsa śakti mat avidyā nivṛtti rūpa bādhasya copapatteḥ nanu—eka ajñāna pakṣe rūpya ādeḥ śukti jñānena sva kāraṇe pravilaya mātram kriyate mudgara prahāreṇa iva ghaṭasya na tu ajñānam nivartyata iti te matam na yuktam yatas  jñānam ajñānasya eva nivartakam iti vyāpti balāt  jñānasya ajñāna nivṛtti dvārā eva anya virodhi tvena ajñānam anivartya rūpya ādi nivartakatva ayogāt śukti jñānena ajñāna nivṛttau  abhivyakta caitanya saṃbandha abhāvena bhrāntau  iva bādhe api śukteḥ aprakāśa āpatteḥ ca iti ced na yatas  jñānam ajñāna nivartakam iti vyāpteḥ uccheda viṣaya tvāt sva kāraṇe sūkṣma rūpeṇa avasthāne tad anaṅgīkārāt  śukti jñānasya ca anavacchinna caitanya āvaraṇa rūpa mūla ajñāna anivartaka tve api avacchinna caitanya āvaraṇa rūpa tūla ajñāna nivartaka tvena abhivyakta caitanya saṃbandhāt bādhadaśāyām rūpya nivṛtti śukti prakāśayoḥ api upapatteḥ naca  upādeya bhūtayā vṛttyā upādāna bhūta avidyā abhibhavaḥ  na ghaṭate upādeyena upādāna abhibhava adarśanāt iti vācyam vṛścika ādinā gomaya ādeḥ upādānasya api abhibhava darśanāt ārambha vāda anabhyupagamāt ca na gomaya avayavānām upādānatva śaṅkā nanu cakṣuḥ ādi janya śakti ādi vṛtteḥ sa prakārikāyāḥ niṣprakāraka śuddha caitanya aviṣaya tayā tad āvaraṇa rūpa mūla ajñāna abhibhava abhāve api avacchinna viṣayayā tayā avacchinna caitanya āvaraṇa rūpa tūla ajñāna abhibhavaḥ  yujyata iti te matam ayuktam avacchinne avidyā kalpite aprasakta prakāśe mūlāvidyāyā iva tad āvaraṇa śakteḥ ayogāt  tvayā anabhyupagata tvāt ca jaḍa viśiṣṭa ātmānam prati tad abhyupagame ca viśeṣaṇa anāvāraka viśiṣṭau  āraka śakti abhibhavasya viśeṣyāvāraka śakti abhibhavam vinā ayogena śukti ākāra vṛttyā eva śuddha ātma prakāśa āpātāt iti ced na anavabodhāt  na hi avidyā kalpite avacchinne asmābhiḥ avidyā vā tad śaktiḥ vā abhyupeyate kiṃtu caitanya mātra eva tasmin  tu sarvam jaḍa madhyaḥ tam asti iti eka āśraya āśritatva saṃbandhāt jaḍa avacchinna caitanyam āvṛtam iti vyapadeśaḥ ghaṭa ādi ākāra vṛttyā tu tad adhiṣṭhāna caitanya abhivyaktau tad avacchedena eva tad niṣṭhā āvaraṇa abhibhavaḥ  jāyata iti na śuddha ātma prakāśa āpattiḥ tad uktam saṃkṣepa śārīrake ‘a āśrayatva viṣayatva bhāginī nirvibhāga citiḥ eva kevalā pūrva siddha tamasaḥ  hi paścimaḥ  na āśrayaḥ  bhavati na api gocaraḥ ‘bahu nigadya kim atra vadāmi aham śṛṇuta saṃgraham advaya śāsane sakala vāc manasā atigatā citiḥ sakala vāc manasa vyavahāra bhāj  iti ca tasmāt avidyāyām satyām api śakti abhibhavāt vā tūla ajñāna nāśāt vā avasthā viśeṣa pracyavāt vā eka deśa nāśāt vā bhīru bhaṭavat apasaraṇāt vā kaṭavat saṃveṣṭanāt vā āvaraṇa bhaṅgā nirmokṣa bādhānām upapattiḥ nanu avasthā śeṣāṇām ajñāna abhinna tve eka ajñāna pakṣa kṣatiḥ ajñāna bhinna tve ca sākṣāt  jñānena nivṛttiḥ bhrama ādi upādāna tvam ca na syāt  teṣām iva rūpyasya eva upādāna nāśam vinā nāśa prasaṅgaḥ ca śuktyajñānam naṣṭam iti anubhava virodhaḥ ca iti ced na yatas avasthā tāvat avasthāvataḥ abhinnā eva ajñāna aikyam tu sarva avasthā anusyūta eka ākāram ādāya evam ca ajñāna avasthāyāḥ  ajñāna tvena na jñāna sākṣāt nivartyatva ādi anupapattiḥ yad tu avasthā viśeṣāṇām iva rūpyasya eva upādāna nivṛttim vinā nivṛtti āpādānam tad ayuktam ajñāna eva jñānasya sākṣāt virodha avadhāraṇena ajñāna avasthāya asta bhinnāyāḥ jñāna sākṣāt nivartyatva arha tvāt na tu rūpya ādīnām anīdṛś tvāt  aneka ajñāna pakṣe tu śaṅkā api na udeti nanu asmin pakṣe ekayā vṛttyā sarva tad ajñānasya nivṛttiḥ uta eka tad ajñānasya ādye punar  śukteḥ kadāpi aprakāśaḥ  na syāt  antye vṛtti kāle api prakāśaḥ  na syāt  ekasya āvaraṇasya nivṛttau  api āvaraṇa antara anivṛtteḥ iti ced na ekayā vṛttyā eka ajñāna nāśe api tayā eva āvaraṇa antarāṇām pratiruddha tvāt  yāvat  sā tiṣṭhati tāvat prakāśaḥ tasyām apagatāyām punar aprakāśaḥ ca upapadyate ajñānasya jñāna prāgabhāva sthānīya tvāt  yathā tava ekam jñānam ekam eva prāc abhāvam nāśayati tad nāśa rūpeṇa udayāt prāc abhāva antara nibandhanam ajñātatva ādi vyavahāram ca pratibadhnāti tathā mama api ekam jñānam ekam eva ajñānam nivartayati ajñāna antara nibandhanam ca prayojanam pratibadhnāti iti kim anupapannam atra ca prativandha padena kārya anutpatti prayojaka tvam kāraṇa abhāva pratibandhaka sādhāraṇam abhihitam evam avasthā viśeṣa pakṣe api prakāśa aprakāśau  upapādanīyau evam amūrtasya ajñānasya yadi api daṇḍa ādinā gavā ādīnām iva apasaraṇam kara ādinā kaṭa ādīnām iva saṃveṣṭanam ca na saṃbhavati tathā api kārya akṣamatva sāmyena āvaraṇa saṃveṣṭana pakṣau yojanīyau yathā hi uttejaka abhāva saha kṛtasya maṇeḥ pratibandhaka tāyām uttejaka satve pratibandhaka kārya akṣama tvam tathā vṛtti abhāva saha kṛtasya ajñānasya pratibandhaka tāyām vṛttau satyām tad kāryān udaya iti draṣṭavyam nanu caitanyasya niravayava tvāt  tasya eka deśena prakāśaḥ  na yujyate atha ākāśa iva tad tad artha avacchinna tvam eka deśa śabda arthaḥ tarhi na āgantuka padārtha avacchinna caitanyam anādya jñānasya viṣayaḥ nirviṣayasya āvaraṇasya ayogāt  prāk anavacchinna āvaraṇam eva idānīm avacchinna āvaraṇam jātam iti api na avacchinna caitanya jñānena eva anavacchinna āvaraṇa nāśa āpatteḥ etena vyaktitaḥ pūrvam jātiḥ iva viṣayāt pūrvam ajñānam asti iti nirastam iti ced na anādya jñāna viṣaye anādi caitanye tad tad āgantuka padārtha avaccheda abhyupagamāt ‘a āśrayatva viṣayatva bhāginī nirvibhāga citiḥ eva kevale tyukta tvāt  yad avacchinna gocarā ca vṛttiḥ tad avacchedena eva āvaraṇa apasaraṇāt na anavacchinna caitanya āvaraṇa bhaṅga prasaṅgaḥ ata eva vṛtti viṣaya avacchinna caitanyāt prāc ajñānam asti iti abhiprāyeṇa viṣayāt prāc ajñānam asti iti sādhu uktam tasmāt adhiṣṭhāna caitanyam svādhyastam bhāsayati iti siddham tad ayam atra niṣkarṣaḥ yadi api viṣaya prakāśakam viṣaya adhiṣṭhāna bhūta  prameya caitanyam antaḥkaraṇa avacchinna caitanyam tu tasya pramātṛ antaḥkaraṇa vṛtti avacchinna caitanyam tu pramāṇam tathā api yadīya antaḥkaraṇa vṛttyā viṣaya paryantam cakṣuḥ ādi dvārā nissṛtayā yad prakāśakam caitanyam yad pramātṛ caitanya abhedena abhivyajyate tam eva sa eva jānāti na anyam na anyaḥ  vā ata eva eka vṛtti upārūḍha lakṣaṇa eka lolībhāva āpannam pramātṛ pramāṇa prameya caitanyam bhavati tatas tad avacchedena ajñāna nivṛttyā  nivṛttyā  bhāsamānam prameya caitanyam aparokṣam phalam iti ucyate tad  svayam bhāsamānam sat  svādhyastam ghaṭa ādi api bhāsayati iti tad  phala vyāpyam iti upeyate yad niṣṭhā ca yad ākārā vṛttiḥ bhavati tad niṣṭham tad ākāram ajñānam sā nāśayati iti niyamāt  pramātṛ prameya ubhaya vyāpini aparokṣa vṛttiḥ svāvacchedena āvaraṇam apasārayati prakāśasya sva avacchedena āvaraṇa apasārakatva darśanāt atas  pramātṛ avacchinnasya asattva āvaraṇasya prameya avacchinnasya ābhāna āvaraṇasya ca apasaraṇāt  ghaṭaḥ ayam me sphurati ityādi parokṣa vyavahāraḥ parokṣa sthale tu indriya sannikarṣa lakṣaṇa dvāra abhāva antaḥkaraṇa nissaraṇa abhāvena viṣaya paryantam vṛtteḥ agamanāt viṣaya avacchinna prameya caitanyena saha pramātṛ caitanyasya eka vṛtti upārūḍhatva abhāvena aparokṣa tayā abhivyakti abhāve api pramātṛ pramāṇa caitanyayoḥ eka lolībhāva āpattyā pramātṛ avat chinnam asattva āvaraṇa mātram nivartate tāvat mātrasya vṛtti avacchinna tvāt idam eva suṣupti vyāvṛtti śabdena vivaraṇa ācāryaiḥ vyākhyātam viṣaya avacchinna abhānāvaraṇa tad kārya sadbhāve api pramātṛ avacchinnā sattva āvaraṇa nivṛttyā anumāna ādau vyavahāra upapattiḥ ata eva jānāmi aham parvate vahniḥ asti iti sa tu kīdṛśa iti me na bhāti iti ādi vyavahāraḥ trayāṇām eka lolībhāve aparokṣa tvam dvayoḥ eka lolībhāve tu parokṣa tvam iti na saṅkaraḥ vṛtteḥ ca viṣayeṇa sarvam sākṣāt eva aparokṣa sthale saṃbandhaḥ parokṣa sthale tu anumiteḥ anumeyena tad vyāpya jñāna janya tvam śābdyāḥ saṃsargeṇa saha tad āśraya vācaka pada janya tvam smṛteḥ smartavyena saha tad viṣaya anubhava janya tvam evam anyatra api paramparā saṃbandha eva iti parokṣa aparokṣa vibhāgaḥ vistareṇa vyutpāditā asmābhiḥ iyam prakriyā siddhānta bindau tasmāt viṣayasya mithyātve api pratikarma vyavasthā upapannā iti diś  iti advaita siddhau pratikarma vyavasthā upapattiḥ iti advaita siddhau prapañca mithyātvā anukūla tarka nirūpaṇam atha pratikūla tarka nirākaraṇam nanu mithyātva anumānam pratikūla tarka parāhatam tathā hi viśvam yadi kalpitam syāt  satya adhiṣṭhānam syāt  na ca evam sāmānyatas  jñāta tve satyajñāta viśeṣavat tvasya adhiṣṭhānatva prayojakasya nirviśeṣe nissāmānye ca brahmaṇi asaṃbhavāt iti ced na sva rūpeṇa jñāta tve sati viśeṣeṇa ajñāta tvasya adhiṣṭhānatva prayojaka tvena jñāta viśeṣavat tvasya aprayojaka tvāt  ‘puruṣaḥ  na vā iti saṃśaya dharmiṇaḥ sthāṇoḥ api anyatra jñāta sthāṇutva rūpa viśeṣava tvāt tatra ajñāta viśeṣavat tvam api na prayojakam viśeṣavatvena ajñāta tvasya eva laghu tvena prayojaka tvāt  tathā ca nissāmānye nirviśeṣe ca brahmaṇi sva prakāśa tvena jñānāt  paripūrṇatva ānandatva ādinā ca ajñānāt adhiṣṭhāna tvam upapannam vastutas tu kalpita sāmānya viśeṣavat tvam brahmaṇi api sulabham eva akalpita sāmānya viśeṣava tvam ca aprasiddham na ca tad kalpane anyonya āśrayaḥ kalpita sāmānya viśeṣāṇām pravāha an ādi tvāt satyatva ānandatva ādīnām eva kalpita vyakti bhedena sāmānya tvāt  paripūrṇa ānandatva ādīnām ca viśeṣa tvāt  ata eva sāmānya ākāra jñānam vinā saṃskārān udbodhāt  katham adhyāsa iti na vācyam sat ātmanā sva rūpa jñānasya eva sāmānya jñāna tvāt na hi adhyasanīyam sat ātmanā na bhāti etāvān eva viśeṣaḥ yad adhiṣṭhānam svata eva sat ātmanā bhāti adhyasanīyam tu tad saṃbandhāt nanu adhiṣṭhāna tirodhānam vinā bhrama asaṃbhavaḥ prakāśa rūpa tirodhāne tu tad adhyasta avidyā ādeḥ prakāśa anupapattiḥ iti ced  na ekasya eva ānanda ādi ātmanā tirohitasya sat ātmanā prakāśa saṃbhavāt  tad uktam vārtikakāra pādaiḥ ayat prasādāt avidyā ādi sidhyati iva divāniśam tam api apahnute avidyā na ajñānasya asti duṣkaram iti na ca bādha kāle api sat viśeṣa jñānam asti iti vācyam paripūrṇa ānandatva ādeḥ sata eva viśeṣa tvena tadā tad ajñāna abhāvāt dharmatva mātrasya eva kalpita tvāt  yad vā bhrama virodhi jñāna abhāva eva tantram na tu viśeṣa ajñānam viśva upādāna gocara ajñānasya śravaṇa ādi janyam ātma mātra viṣaya kam vṛtti rūpam jñānam virodhi na tu cit rūpam svatas siddham jñānam bhrama virodhinaḥ ca vṛtti rūpasya jñānasya idānīm abhāvaḥ asti eva nanu ātmānātmanoḥ draṣṭṛ dṛśyatva ātmanā ātmatva ādinā bheda jñānāt  katham adhyasta adhiṣṭhāna bhāva iti ced na idam anidam na bhavati iti puras varti apurovartinoḥ bheda grahe api idam rajatam iti adhyāsavat san ghaṭa ityādi adhyāsaḥ  bhaviṣyati na hi rūpa antareṇa bheda grahaḥ  rūpa antareṇa adhyāsa virodhī san ghaṭa ityādi pratyaye ca sat rūpasya ātmanaḥ  ghaṭa ādi anuviddha tayā bhānāt na tasya ghaṭa ādi adhyāsa adhiṣṭhāna tā anupapattiḥ sat rūpeṇa ca sarva jñāna viṣaya tā upapatteḥ na rūpa ādi hīnasya api ātmanaḥ kālasya iva cākṣuṣatva ādi anupapattiḥ nanu viśvam yadi kalpitam syāt tadā sa pradhānam syāt  na ca evam tasmāt  na kalpitam iti ced na atra api pradhānasya sajātīyasya sattvāt  pūrva prapañcasa jātīyasya eva uttara prapañcasya adhyasanāt  adhyāsaḥ  hi sva kāraṇa tayā saṃskāram apekṣate na tu saṃskāra viṣayasya satya tām anupayogāt  na ca pramājanya eva saṃskāraḥ  bhrama hetuḥ atas  viṣaya satya tvam āvaśyakam iti vācyam māna abhāvāt viparīte lāghavāt ca ataeva adhyasta sajātīyam pūrva madhyastāpekṣayā adhika sattākam apekṣaṇīyam iti api nirastam satya tau  adhika sattāyā api anupayogāt  pūrvam tu jñāna mātram apekṣate tad ca asti eva nanu evam adhiṣṭhānasya api jñāna mātram eva hetuḥ na tu tad iti na sat adhiṣṭhāna apekṣā syāt iti śūnya vādāpattiḥ iti   ced na adhiṣṭhānasya jñāna dvārā bhrama hetu tve api ajñāna dvārā bhrama hetutvena sattva niyamāt  bhrama upādāna ajñāna viṣayaḥ  hi adhiṣṭhānam iti ucyate tad ca satyam eva asatyasya sarvasya api ajñāna kalpita tvena ajñāna aviṣaya tvāt tad asatya tve tad jñānasya bhrama ābādhakatva prasaṅgāt  jagati bhrama bādha vyavasthā ca na syāt  bādhena hi kiṃcid viruddham tattvam upadarśayatā āropita mata tvam bādhanīyam ubhaya adhyāse tu kim kena bādhyate ata eva bhagavatā bhāṣya kāreṇa  satya anṛte mithunīkṛtye ati uktam nanu etad prapañca sadhyā artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ prapañca antarasya abhāvena sva ucita artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ asya na mithyātvam iti ced na svāpna māyā ādau vyabhicārāt  sva ucita artha kriyā kāritvasya pāramārthika sattva aprayojaka tvāt  na api śruti ādi siddha utpatti ādimat tvam sattve tantram svapna prapañce vyabhicārāt  tasya api  na tatra rathā na ratha yogā na panthānaḥ  bhavanti atha rathān ratha yogān pathassṛjata  iti ādi śrutyā utpatti ādi pratipādanāt  na ca kalpa ādi abhramā yogaḥ kalpa antarīya saṃskārasya tatra hetu tvāt  na ca janmāntarīya saṃskārasya kārya janaka tve atiprasaṅgaḥ adṛṣṭa ādi vaśena kvacid udbodhe api anyatra anudbodha upapatteḥ kārya unneya dharmāṇām yathā akāryam unnayanāt  anyathā jātasya stanya pāna ādau pravṛttine syāt  nanu caitreṇa maitre saṃskāra adhyāse api maitrasya bhrama adarśanāt  jagat bhrama hetu saṃskārasya sattvam durvāram na ca svena adhyastāt saṃskārāt bhramaḥ bhramāt  pūrvam svasya kārya anumeya saṃskāra adhyāsa niyama abhāvāt iti ced na śukti rūpyasya kuṇḍala ajanakatva vañcaitra adhya sta saṃskārasya maitrabhrama ājanaka tve api vaṇij vīthī stha rūpyasya kuṇḍala janaka tvavat svena adhyastasya saṃskārasya viyat ādi adhyāsa janakatva upapatteḥ tad prati iti abhāve api tad adhyāsasya pūrvam sattvāt  kṛtsnasya api vyāvahārika padārthasya ajñāta sattva abhyupagamāt nanu  prātibhāsika rūpye traikālika niṣedhasya tvad mate vyāvahārika rūpya viṣaya tvavat vyāvahārika prapañce api ‘na iha nāne ati traikālika niṣedhasya pāramārthika prapañca antara viṣaya tā avaśyam vācya iti ced na bhrama bādha vaiyadhi karaṇya āpātena asya pakṣasya anaṅgīkāra parāhata tvāt aṅgīkāre api vyāvahārika niṣedhe pāramārthika niṣedha tvam na saṃbhavati apratītasya niṣedha ayogāt  pratītyai  saha adhyāsa atirikta saṃbandha abhāvena pāramārthike pratītatva abhāvāt  nanu pradhāna adhiṣṭhānayoḥ sādṛśya abhāvāt katham adhyāsaḥ atha nirguṇayoḥ api guṇayoḥ sādṛśyavat atra api kiṃcid sādṛśyam bhaviṣyati iti tad na nirdharmake brahmaṇi tasya api adhyāsa adhīna tvena anyonya āśrayāt yadi api sādṛśyam sa upādhika adhyāse na kāraṇam vyabhicārāt  tathā api nirupādhika adhyāse anvaya vyatirekābhyām tasya avaśyam apekṣaṇīya tvāt sa upādhike api ‘raktaḥ sphaṭika iti ādau dravyatva ādinā sādṛśyasya sattvāt ca iti ced na avidyā adhyāsasya anādi tvena kāraṇa anapekṣasya sādṛśya anapekṣa tvāt antaḥkaraṇa adhyāse api avidyā saṃbandhi tvasya eva sādṛśyasya vidyamāna tvāt  vastutas tu na bhrame sādṛśya apekṣā niyamaḥ nirupādhike api ‘pītaḥ śaṅkha iti ādau vyabhicārāt  ‘raktaḥ sphaṭika iti ādau  api dravyatva ādinā sādṛśyam asti iti api na pradhāna mātra vṛtti tayā prāc avagatam adhyāsa samaye ca adhiṣṭhāna vṛtti tayā gṛhītam yad  tad eva hi sādṛśyam viparyaya prayojakam iti tvayā api vācyam na tu prāk eva pradhāna adhiṣṭhāna ubhaya vṛtti tayā gṛhītam tasya sāṃśayika tvāt  dravyatva ādi ca lohita ālohita vṛtti tayā prāk gṛhītam iti na viparyaya prayojakam kiṃca sādṛśyam na svatas  bhrama kāraṇam māna abhāvāt kiṃtu saṃskāra udbodhena sāmagrī saṃpādaka tayā saṃskāra udbodhaḥ ca na sādṛśya eka niyataḥ adṛṣṭa ādinā api tad saṃbhavāt tad uktam ‘ sadṛśa adṛṣṭa cintā ādyāḥ smṛti bījasya bodhakāḥ iti cintā ādikam ca praṇidhāna sūtre vyākhyātam tathā ca anyatas  saṃskāra udbodhe sati sādṛśyam anupayogi tad uktam vivaraṇe ‘ nirupādhika bhrama kārya darśanam eva guṇa avayava sāmānya abhāve api ketakī gandha sadṛśaḥ sarpa gandha itivat  sādṛśya antaram vā śaṅkha pītim ādau  iva kāraṇa antaram vā kalpayati iti nanu doṣam vinā bhramasvīkāre tad aprāmāṇyasya svataḥ tu āpattiḥ doṣa janyatva svīkāre tu doṣasya api adhyasanīya tvena anavasthāpattiḥ iti ced na anādi avidyā adhyāsasya doṣa an apekṣa tvāt  sādi adhyāsasya ca avidyāt oṣa janya tvāt na aprāmāṇyasya svatas tvam na api anavasthā anyathā tārkikāṇām api anādi pramā guṇam vinā api iti prāmāṇya paratas tvam bhajyeta janya pramā mātrasya guṇa janya tvam tu janyā adhyāsa mātrasya doṣa janya tvena samam nanu lāghavena prathama upasthita tvena ca pravṛtti mātram prati saṃsarga dhiya iva dhūma mātram prati doṣa ādīnām janaka tvāt avidyā adhyāsaḥ api katham klṛpta kāraṇena vinā bhavatu anyathā saṃsarga dhīḥ api pravṛtti viśeṣe vahniḥ api dhūma viśeṣe hetuḥ iti syāt  tathā ca ākhyātivādaḥ ca anumāna mātra ucchedaḥ ca āpadyeyātām kiṃca avidyā rūpa viṣayasya anādi tve api tad pratīteḥ doṣa ajanya tve aprāmāṇyāpātaḥ aprāmāṇya prayojakasya doṣa janya tvasya abhāvāt artha bhedavat avidyā ākhya doṣasya sva para nirvāhaka tvam evam api bhedaḥ  bhinna itivat  ‘a jñāna jñāta am iti vyavahāraḥ  bhavatu pratīti mātra śarīrasya sva viṣaya dhī hetu tvam kutas  svasya svasmāt  pūrva vṛttitva asaṃbhavāt iti ced na adhyāsa tvasya laghu tve api prathama upasthita tve api na doṣa janya tāyām tantra tvam doṣasya api dṛśya tvena adhyasanīya tayā anavasthā patteḥ yathā nitya jñāna vādinām jñāna tvasya na śarīra janyatā dau  avacchedaka tvam navā guṇa janya tvasya prāmāṇya prayojaka tvam bādhaka balāt  tadvat  janyā adhyāsam pratyeva doṣa ādīnām kāraṇa tvam guṇa ajanya tve api abādhita viṣaya tayā nitya jñāna prāmāṇyavat  doṣa ajanya tve api bādhita viṣaya tayā anādi adhyāsasya api aprāmāṇya upapattiḥ bādhita viṣaya tve api na doṣa janya tvam avacchedakam doṣa janya tve api avacchedaka antara anveṣaṇe anavasthā pātāt  bādhita viṣaya tvasya doṣa ajanya vṛtti tve api doṣa janya tvasya tad vyāpyatva upapatteḥ ata eva śabara svāminā ‘yasya duṣṭam karaṇam yatra ca mithyā iti pratyayaḥ sa eva asamīcīnaḥ  na anya iti vadatā duṣṭa karaṇa janya tvam antareṇa api arthānyathā tvam aprāmāṇya prayojakam uktam avidyā dhyāsa rūpasya sākṣi caitanyasya avidyā janyatva anabhyupagamāt na pratīti mātra śarīratva vyāghātaḥ ‘aham ajña ityādi abhilāpa kāraṇībhūta vṛtti rūpa adhyāsam prati tu avidyāyāḥ kāraṇa tvam asya iva ghaṭa ādīnām iva sva pratyakṣam prati vahni viśiṣṭa dhiyoḥ tu bādhaka abhāvāt sāmānyena eva dhūma pravṛttī prati hetutā iti na pūrva ukta doṣa āpātaḥ nanu avidyā adhyāsasya anādi tvena doṣa ādi anapekṣāvat adhiṣṭhāna an apekṣā api syāt iti ced na janaka tvena adhiṣṭhāna anapekṣāyām api āśraya tvena tad apekṣā niyamāt parama mahattva ādeḥ āśraya apekṣāvat  adhyāsasya sa adhiṣṭhānakatva niyamena atra api paratantra tvasya sama tvāt  bhāsyasya avidyā adhyāsasya bhāsaka tayā api adhiṣṭhāna apekṣaṇāt ca avidyā avacchinna caitanyasya avidyā ādi sakala dvaitat raṣṭṛ tvāt tasya eva ca antaḥkaraṇa avacchedena pramātṛ tvāt bhrama pramayoḥ sāmāna adhikaraṇya upapatteḥ bhramasya samāna adhikaraṇa pramā nivartya tvam upapadyate nanu deha indriya ādikam vinā katham antaḥkaraṇa adhyāsaḥ kā atra anupapattiḥ adhiṣṭhāna aparokṣa tvam hi aparokṣa bhrame kāraṇam tad  yatra adhiṣṭhānam svatas  na aparokṣam yathā śukti ādi avacchinna caitanyam tatra tad aparokṣata artham deha indriya ādi apekṣā prakṛteca avidyā avacchinnam caitanyam adhiṣṭhānam tatra caitanyasya sva prakāśa tvena avidyāyāḥ ca tad adhyasta tvena tena eva sākṣiṇā aparokṣa tvāt  kutra deha indriya ādi apekṣā atha evam pralaye deha indriya ādi abhāve api ajñāna sadbhāvena antaḥkaraṇa adhyāsa prasaṅgaḥ na tadā deha indriya ādi sarjana vilamba hetunā eva tad vilamba saṃbhavāt anyathā tadā deha indriya ādikam api kutaḥ na utpadyeta na ca doṣa ādīnām adhyastatvena tad abhāvasya tāttvika tvāt  atāttvikena tāttvika kārya pratibandhasya ayukta tvāt  bauddhena duṣṭa tayā kalpitasya veda janya jñānasya iva kalpita doṣa janyasya dvaita vijñānasya prāmāṇya āpāta iti vācyam bauddha kalpitasya prātibhāsika doṣasya vyāvahārika veda apekṣayā nyūna sattāka tvena tad aprāmāṇyā prayojaka tve api avidyā ākhya doṣa dvaita prapañcayoḥ sama sattāka tvena kārya kāraṇa bhāva niyamena ca kāraṇībhūtā avidyā ākhya doṣa abhāve kārya bhūta dvaita prapañca tad vijñānayoḥ abhāva niyamena na avidyā mithyā tvena dvaita jñāna satya tāpātaḥ kāraṇa mithyā tve kārya mithyā tvasya āvaśyaka tvāt  brahma jñān itara abādhyatva rūpa vyāvahārika tvasya bādhya abādhya sādhāraṇasya mithyātva siddhi anapekṣa tvāt na sattva vibhāga asiddhiḥ nanu doṣa ādīnām rūpya ādi bhrama hetūnām pāramārthika sattvam autsargika prāmāṇyena siddham iti paramārtha satām eva teṣām hetu tvam iti ced na vyāvahārika prāmāṇyasya sākṣiṇā grahaṇe api tri kālābādhyatva rūpa tāttvika prāmāṇyam na kena api gṛhyata iti pratyakṣa bādha uddhāre prāk eva abhihita tvāt  na ca rūpya ādi adhyāse doṣa ādīnām adhiṣṭhāna sama sattāka tvam dṛṣṭam iti iha api tathā iti vācyam sādharmya sama jāti uttara tvāt vastutas tu sarvatra caitanyasya eva adhiṣṭhāna tvena kutra api doṣa ādīnām adhiṣṭhāna sama sattākatva abhāvāt na ca bādhaka jñānam satyam eva vaktavyam anyathā bādha paramparāyā anavasthā patteḥ iti vācyam vedānta vākya janya caram citta vṛtteḥ kataka rajaḥ nyāyena sva para bādhaka tayā anavasthāyā abhāvāt  dṛśyatva mātreṇa yugapad kṛtsna bādha saṃbhavāt na hi guhāyām na śabda iti śabdaḥ svam na niṣedhati anyathā svasya svena aniṣedhe tatra api anavasthāpattiḥ śabda mātra niṣedha anubhava virodhaḥ ca yadi api bādhaka jñānam vṛtti uparakta caitanya rūpam svatas  satyam eva tathā api tad avacchedikāyāḥ  vṛtteḥ dṛśya tvena mithyātvāt  bādha upapattiḥ nanubandhasya atyanta abhāva pratiyogitva rūpa mithyā tve tad abhāva artham yatnaḥ  na syāt  atyanta abhāvasya asādhya tvāt  ataeva na tad prati ityabhāva artham api yatnaḥ tasyāḥ  api mithyātvāt  anyathā mokṣe api bandha pratītyā tad daśāyām api prātibhāsika bandha āpātāt  atha pāramārthikatva ākāreṇa mithyātvam sva rūpeṇa tu nivṛttiḥ eva na tasyāḥ svarūpa ābādhena api upapatteḥ iti ced na satyasya brahmaṇaḥ  nivṛtti adarśanena svarūpataḥ  mithyātva abhāve nivṛtti ayogāt  mithyātvam nivṛtti anukūlam eva na ca tad artham pravṛtti anupapattiḥ adhiṣṭhāna sākṣātkāra anantaram tathā eva tatas  pūrvam tu kaṇṭha gata vismṛta cāmīkara prāptaya iva bhrama bādhaka jñāna utpattaye pravṛtti upapatteḥ atyanta abhāva adhikaraṇe ca pratiyogivat tad nivṛttiḥ api upapāditā eva na ca tra ekālika niṣedha pratiyogini tucche nivṛttiḥ na dṛṣṭā iti katham tādṛśi prapañce sā syāt iti vācyam yathākathaṃcid  sajātīye adarśanasya aprayojaka tvāt  anyathā anutpanne nivṛttiḥ na dṛṣṭā iti prāc abhāvaḥ api na nivarteta tasmāt  svabhāva viśeṣa eva tuccha nitya vilakṣaṇaḥ  nivṛtti prayojaka iti vācyam sā ca nivṛttiḥ adhikaraṇa svarūpā iti pakṣe ghaṭa nāśa artham mudgara pāta ādau  iva mananādau pravṛttiḥ ūhanīyā atiriktā iti pakṣe tu anirvacanīyā pañcama prakārā carama vṛtti rūpā vā sā sarvathā janyā eva iti na kā api anupapattiḥ nanu bandhasya brahmaṇi adhyasta tve tad nididhya āsana sādhya tad sākṣātkāra nivartya tvam śravaṇa ādi niyama adṛṣṭa sāpekṣa brahma jñāna nivartya tvam ca na syāt  na hi devatā nididhya āsana sādhya tad sākṣātkāra nivartyam duritam tatra adhyastam na vā dūra āgamana ādi niyama adṛṣṭa sāpekṣa setu darśana nivartyam duritam tatra adhyastam iti ced na ātma adhyasta gauratva ādeḥ śukti ādi adhyasta rūpi ādeḥ ca tad tad sākṣātkāra nivartyatva darśanena prapañcasya api brahmaṇi adhyasta tayā tad sākṣātkāra nivartya tvasya āvaśyaka tvāt  na hi śukti ādi adhyastam rūpya ādi śukti ādi jñānam vinā nivartate devatā darśa na ādinā tu prāyaścitta samaya kakṣyeṇa duritasya kāraṇa ātmanā avasthāna mātram kriyate na tu śukti jñānena rūpyasya iva nivṛttiḥ adhiṣṭhāna ajñāna rūpa upādānakasya āropitasya tad nivṛttim vinā nivṛtti ayogāt  ajñāna nivṛttiḥ ca adhiṣṭhāna jñānāt eva iti uktam prāk  śravaṇa ādi niyama adṛṣṭam ca na muktim prati kāraṇam kiṃtu brahma aparokṣyam prati nanu avaghāta sādhya vaituṣyāni āpūrvasi iva śravaṇa ādi sādhya aparokṣya ani amukteḥ eva tad sādhya tvam anyathā śravaṇa niyama adṛṣṭa sādhye sākṣātkāre śravaṇa nirapekṣasya upāya antarasya aprasaktyā tad prasakti adhīna niyama vidhi ayogāt na ca parokṣa jñānam śravaṇāt  aparokṣam tu niyama adṛṣṭāt iti yuktam śravaṇa ādi vidhau parokṣa jñāna pravāha rūpa nididhi āsana sādhya aparokṣasya eva dṛśinā uddeśāt  tvad mate parokṣa jñāne kāmanāyāḥ  ayogena tasya uddeśyatva ayogāt ca iti ced na tatra kratu arthasya niyamāpūrvasya parama apūrva sādhaka tve api puruṣa artha hiraṇya dhāraṇa ādi niyama adṛṣṭasya tad abhāvavat  śravaṇa ādi sādhya sākṣātkāra ani phala abhāve api tena eva phalavatva upapatteḥ asarva apekṣā ca yajña ādi śruteḥ aśvavat i ati nyāyāt  ‘sarvam karma akhilam pārtha jñāne parisamāpyate iti smṛteḥ ca atra sarva akhila padābhyām karma śabda vācyā pūrva mātrasya jñāne samāptiḥ darśitā mokṣasya avidyā nivṛtti rūpasya jñāna atirikta asādhyatva niyamāt ca jñāne tu asaṃbhāvana ādi nivṛttyā pratibandhaka durita nivṛttyā ca dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa aṃśa upayogaḥ sāmānya puraskāreṇa ca prasaktasya sādhana antarasya nivṛttiḥ sarvatra niyama vidheḥ phalam viśeṣa rūpeṇa tu apūrva vidhi tvam eva yathā hi ‘vrīhīn avahantī ati ādau  apūrva sādhanībhūta vrīhi vaituṣye viśiṣya avaghāta atirikta sādhana antara aprasaktau  api vrīhi vaituṣya mātre prasaktasya nakha vilana ādeḥ nivṛttiḥ viśiṣya kārya kāraṇa bhāva bodhanāt tathā nirviśeṣa brahma ātmā abheda sākṣātkāra pratibandha nivṛttau śravaṇa ādi atirikta sādhana antara aprasaktau  api ātma jñāna mātra pratibandha nivṛttau sa aṅkhya ādi śāstrasya api prasakteḥ tad nivṛttiḥ viśiṣya vedānta vākya vicāra vidhānāt iti parama gambhīraḥ ayam grantha arthaḥ nanu yadi viśvam kalpitam syāt  tadā ‘janmādyasya yata iti sūtre ‘yataḥ  vā imānī atyādi śrutau ca janma ādyuktiḥ ‘īkṣateḥ na aśabdam i ati sūtre atadaikṣate ati ādi śrutau ca īśvarasya īkṣā pūrvaka kartṛtva uktiḥ ‘lokavat tu līlā kaivalyam i ati sūtre ‘āpta kāmasya kā spṛhe ati ādi śrutau ca prayojana abhāve api līlayā sṛṣṭi āt i uktiḥ ‘vaiṣamyanaiḥ ghṛṇye na sa apekṣatva ādi ati sūtre ‘puṇyena puṇyam lokam nayatī atyādi śrutau ca karma sāpekṣa tvena avaiṣamya uktiḥ atejaḥ atas tathā hi āhe ati sūtre avāyoḥ agniḥ ityādi śrutau ca tejaā ādeḥ vāyu ādi janyatva uktiḥ ‘viparyayeṇa tu kramaḥ ata upapadyate ca iti sūtre ‘pṛthivī apsu pralīyata ityādi smṛtau ca pṛthivī ādīnām abādau layoktiḥ ityādya yuktam syāt  na hi kalpite tad tad virodha śaṅkā tad nirākaraṇam ca yuktam iti ced na prapañcasya kalpitasya api vyāvahārika sattva abhyupagamena tad daśāyām virodha śaṅkā tad parihārayorucita tvāt  indrajāla ādau  adhyaste api aindrajālika āderīkṣā pūrvaka sraṣṭṛ tvā ādeḥ darśanāt ca yathā ca kalpitasya api janma ādi upapattiḥ tathā anirvacanīya vāde vakṣyate svapne api sṛṣṭi ādeḥ śrutyā pratipādanāt ca adhyastasya api sarpasya bhaya kampa ādi janakatvavat  vāyu ādīnām tejaā ādi janaka tvam api upapannam  tad abhidhyānāt eva tu tad liṅgāt sa iti sūtre ca tad tad bhāva āpannasya brahmaṇa eva kāraṇatva abhidhānāt ap ādau pṛthivī ādilayoktiḥ api tad tad bhāva āpanna caitanye vyākhyeya iti na adhiṣṭhāna atirikte layoktiḥ vaiṣamyanaiḥ ghṛṇya prayojana ādi śaṅkā parihāra ādikam tu upāsana avasthāyām bhoktrā patteḥ avibhāgaḥ ced syāt loka vadi ati āpātatas  pariṇāma vāda abhyupagamena ‘tad ananya tvam ārambhaṇa śabda ādibhya iti tu vivartavāde parama siddhānta daśāyām na śaṅkā na ca uttaram māyāvina iva īśvarasya sva pratibimba bhūta jīva bhramayitṛ tvena sarva virodha nirāsa upapatteḥ nanu—īśvarasya api sa parikarasya jīvena adhyasta tvāt  katham bhramayitṛ tvam na avidyā upahita cita eva anādeḥ īśvara tvena antaḥkaraṇa upahita jīva kalpitatva ayogāt jīva kalpitatva pakṣe api tādṛś dharma viśiṣṭa tayā eva kalpanena tasya bhramayitṛtva ādi upapatteḥ ‘parikalpitaḥ api maraṇāya bhavet uragaḥ  yathā na tu nabhaḥ  malinam iti nyāyāt  nanu jīvānām vāyu ādibhyaḥ agni ādi utpattiḥ iti bhramaḥ asti yaḥ svāpna bhrama iva śruteḥ ālambanam syāt  na ca bhrāntim vinā kalpitam asti na ca etad vākya ja bhrānti kalpitam eva etad vākya ālambanam vedasya bhrama janakatva prasaṅgāt  anuvāde tu na doṣaḥ na ca īśvara eva tad kalpakaḥ tasya bhrāntatva prasaṅgāt  tad abhyupagame api na vistāraḥ bhrānteḥ deha indriya ādi kāryatvāt teṣām ca pṛthivī ādi kārya tvāt pṛthivī ādi utpatteḥ prāk  bhrāntyayogāt iti ced na bhrānti mātre deha indriya ādi apekṣāyāḥ prāk eva nirāsāt  īśvara adhyastava āyu ādi hetukā agni ādi utpatti ālambana tvena vedasya bhrama ajanaka tvāt  adhyastasya ca adhyasta tvena sphuraṇāt na māyāvina iva īśvarasya bhrāntatva prasaṅgaḥ na ca adhyasta tve utpatti ādi anupapattiḥ anadhyastasya kvāpi utpatti ādi adarśanena adhyasta tvasya eva tad upapādaka tvāt  satkārya vāda asat kārya vāda niṣedhena anirvacanīya kārya vāda mātre kārya kāraṇa bhāva paryavasānāt tad evam kṛtsnasya prapañcasya advaye brahmaṇi kalpanā upapatteḥ na pratikūla tarka parāhatiḥ iti advaita siddhau brahmaṇi prapañca kalpanā upapādanena pratikūla tarka nirākaraṇam atha sāmānyena mithyātva śruti upapattiḥ etad anumānam ekam eva advitīya am ityādi śrutiḥ api anugṛhṇāti nanu śrutyā sva svarūpa sva prāmāṇyasva yogya tā ādeḥ mithyātvā bodhanena pratyakṣa ādi siddha tad sattva upajīvanena ca brahma itara sakala mithyātva asiddhiḥ ‘sannipāta lakṣaṇaḥ  vidhiḥ animittam tad vighātasya iti nyāyena pratyakṣa ādi siddha ghaṭa ādi mithyātva asiddhiḥ ca yogyatā ādi mithyātva bodhane ca śruti arthasya atāt tvikatva āpattiḥ śābda bodhasya śabda tad prāmāṇya yogya tā ādinā sama sattākatva niyamāt  na ca sat artha svāpna devatā vākye vyabhicāraḥ āptatva apauruṣeyatva ayogena tasya śabda tvena prāmāṇya ayogāt kim tu upaśrutivat tādṛśa śabda jñānam liṅga tvena pramāṇam iti ced na nirdoṣa śabda tvena tasya śabda vidhayā eva prāmāṇya saṃbhavāt āptatva apauruṣeya tvayoḥ dāṣa abhāva eva upakṣayāt vyāpti ādi upasthiti kalpane gauravāt  vaktuḥ kalpita tve api tad gata doṣasya artha saṃvādena kalpayitum aśakya tvāt ca tathā ca śabda sama sattāka tvasya vyabhicārāt  yogyatā ādi sama sat tākatva niyama siddheḥ aprayojaka tvāt ca parokṣatva anityatva ādi upādhi saṃbhavāt ca śrutyā yogyatā ādi sakala mithyātva bodhane api tad arthasya na mithyātvam mithyātva prayojaka rūpa abhāvāt mahā bhāṣya ukta nyāya udāharaṇam api na yuktam viṣaya vaiṣamyāt  tathā hi ‘śatāni sahasrāṇī atyatra sarvanāma sthāna saṃjña kaśi sannipātena vihitaḥ  num ‘ṣṇā antā ṣaṣ iti ṣaṣ saṃjñā dvārā ‘ṣaḍbhyaḥ  luj iti śisva rūpa sarvanāma sthānasya pañca ityādau  iva luk nimittam na bhavati tad sannipātena eva vihita tvāt  tad sadbhāva niyamena eva vihita tvāt iti arthaḥ aluptasya eva sarvanāma sthānasya nud nimitta tvāt  ana lumata aṅgasye ati lumatā lupte aṅga kārya niṣedhāt tathā cālupta pratyaya tvena yatra nimitta tā tatra sannipāta lakṣaṇa nyāya avatāraḥ yatra tu ‘pratyaya lope pratyaya lakṣaṇam i ati nyāyena lupte api pratyaye kāryam bhavati tatra aluptatva viśeṣaṇa nairapekṣyeṇa pratyayatva mātreṇa eva nimitta tvāt  na sannipāta lakṣaṇa nyāya avatāraḥ pratyaya sadbhāvasya tatra anupajīvya tvāt evam sthite yadi amithyā bhūta tvena pratyakṣa ādeḥ nimitta tā syāt  tadā pratyayasya alupta tvena nimitta tāyām iva bhavet etad nyāya avatāraḥ pratyakṣa ādeḥ tu sva rūpeṇa eva nimitta tā svapna ādi arthasya api artha kriyā kāritva darśanena prāk eva upapāditā atas  yad  bādhyate tāttvika tvam tad na upajīvyam yad ca upajīvyam artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇa vyāvahārika prāmāṇyam tad ca na bādhyata iti kim kena saṅgatam tad uktam ṭīkā kṛdbhiḥ ‘utpādaka apratidvandvi tvāt iti ataeva jyotiṣṭoma ādi vidheḥ upajīvya agni vidyāvat viṣaya tvena iva dvaita niṣedhasya api sva upajīvya yogya tā ādi itara viṣaya tvena saṅkocasya vā sṛṣṭi ādi śruteḥ iva kalpita viṣaya tvasya vā upapattau na tāttvika sarva mithyātva paratva kalpanam yuktam iti apāstam dṛṣṭānte agni vidyā ādeḥ iva dārṣṭa antike yogyatā ādeḥ tāttvikasya anupajīvya tvāt na hi yogya tā tāttvika yogya tā tvena nimittam kiṃtu yogyatā tvena eva sakala dvaita abhāvasya adhikaraṇa svarūpa tvena tad adhikaraṇasya ca brahmaṇaḥ ‘satyam jñānam anantam brahma ‘tat satyam sa ātme atyādi śrutyā satyatva pratipādanāt  na sṛṣṭi ādi śruteḥ iva kalpita viṣayatva upapattiḥ tasmāt yogyatā ādeḥ mithyā tve api vedānta bodhyam satyam eva iti sthitam yathā ca avidyā tad kāryasya svarūpataḥ  niṣedhe api tuccha vailakṣaṇyam pāramārthikatva ākāreṇa niṣedhe vā pāramārthikatva dharma śūnyasya api brahmaṇaḥ sva rūpeṇa sattvam tathā upapāditam adhastāt nanu  tattvam asya ādi vākyena pratyakṣa ādi avirodhāya tattu aṃpada lakṣitayoḥ aikyam iva mithyātva śrutyā api tad avirodhāya pratyakṣa ādi siddhāt anyasya eva mithyātvam bodhyam anyathā pratyakṣa ādi anugrahāya vyāvahārikam api sattvam na kalpyeta ‘na iha nāne atyādi niṣedhena atyanta sattva vodhanāt iti ced na viśiṣṭayoḥ aikye viśeṣaṇayoḥ api aikyā pātena sarvatra viśiṣṭa abheda para vākyasya lakṣita viśeṣī aikya paratva niyamena ‘tattva m asī atyatra api tathā abhyupagamāt tad uktam  ‘aviruddha viśeṣaṇa dvaya prabhava tve api viśiṣṭayoḥ dvayoḥ ghaṭate na yadā ekatā tadā natarām tad viparīta rūpayoḥ iti mithyātva bodhaka śrutau tu na asti pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ tāttvikatva aṃśasya anupajīvya tvāt vyāvahārika sattvasya ca upajīvya tvāt na atyantā sattva kalpanam iti asya api ukta prāya tvāt nanu śruteḥ tātparyam caitanya mātre vā dvitīya abhāva viśiṣṭe vā tad upalakṣite vā na ādyaḥ viśva mithyātva asiddheḥ iṣṭa āpatteḥ tasya sva prakāśa tayā nitya siddha tvena śruti vaiyarthyāt ca na dvitīyaḥ akhaṇḍa arthatva hānāt ataeva na tṛtīyaḥ kākavat itivat  dvitīya abhāvavat iti anena api sa prakāraka jñāna jananena akhaṇḍa arthatva ayogāt cit mātrasya nitya siddha tvena tad anyasya ca mumukṣu ajñeya tvena kākena saṃsthāna viśeṣasya iva dvitīya abhāvena upalakṣyasya anyasya abhāvāt  tasya upalakṣaṇatva ayogāt ca iti ced na kākasya saṃsthāna viśeṣa iva dvitīya abhāvasya svarūpam eva upalakṣyam iti upalakṣya abhāva nibandhana upalakṣaṇatva anupapatteḥ abhāvāt  upalakṣaṇa tve hi upalakṣya sattva mātram tantram na tu tasya svarūpa atirikta tvam api gauravāt  upalakṣya ta avacchedaka rūpa abhāve api svatas  vyāvṛtta jātivat upalakṣyatva saṃbhavāt ataeva na sa prakārakatva āpattiḥ kākavat iti atra api upalakṣaṇasya aprakāra tvāt kiṃtu svarūpa atirikta dharmasya tatra upalakṣaṇa tvena sa prakāra tvam iha tu tad na iti vaiṣamyam na ca upalakṣaṇa vaiyartham anartha nivṛtti hetu tvena dvitīya abhāva dvāraka svarūpa jñānasya uddeśya tvāt tasya prāc asiddha tvāt na ca mithyātva asiddhyeṣṭāpattiḥ avāntara tātparyasya tatra api sattvāt  tad dvārā eva sva rūpa caitanye mahātātparyāt  ataeva  śruti bodhyasya viśeṣaṇasya upalakṣaṇasya vā dvitīya abhāvasya sattve advaita hāniḥ asattve ca adaṇḍe daṇḍī iti vākyavat  kāka hīne kākavat iti vākyavat ca advaita vākyasya atava avedakatva āpattiḥ iti nirastam ādye dvitīya abhāva sattvena dvitīya abhāva asidhi āpādanasya anucita tvāt abhāvasya adhikaraṇa atireka anabhyupagamāt ca dvitīye tu sṛṣṭi ādi vākyavat upalakṣya svarūpa satya tvam ādāya tattva avedaka tvāt  mukhya tātparya viṣayasya asatya tāyām eva atattva āvedakatva abhyupagamāt ataeva mahātātparya abhiprāyeṇa caitanya mātre tātparyam iti ādya pakṣe api na doṣaḥ avāntara tātparyeṇa mithyātva siddheḥ api svīkāreṇa iṣṭa āpatteḥ api asaṃbhavāt nanu dvitīya abhāve mahātātparya abhāvaḥ kim pramāṇa antara prāptyā yathā vāyu kṣepiṣṭhatva ādau uta tad virodhi tvena yathā ātma vapa utkhanana ādau uta uddeśya viśeṣaṇatva ādinā yathā graha ekatva ādau na ādyaḥ tvayā eva dvitīya abhāvasya pramāṇa antara prāpti anabhyupagamāt dvitīye api virodhimānam na tāvat pratyakṣa ādi dvaita grāhi tvad mate tasya eva śruti bādhya tvāt  na advaita vākya antaram tasya ātma mātra paratve dvitīya abhāva avirodhi tvāt na hi viśeṣya viṣayam ‘agni hotram juhotī ati vākyam viśiṣṭa viṣayeṇa ‘dadhnā juhoti iti vākyena virudhyate dvaita abhāva paratve tu eka viṣaya tvena sutarām avirodhāt  na api tṛtīyaḥ ‘graham saṃmārṭī atyatra saṃmārjanasya īva akhaṇḍa artha pare vākye vidheya antarasya abhāvena viśeṣyasya śāstra gamyasya cit mātrasya aprāpta tvena uddeśyatva ayogāt ca dvitīya abhāvasya uddeśya viśeṣaṇatva anupapatteḥ avivakṣā hetoḥ anuvādya tvasya api abhāvāt ca iti ced na svayam eva sva bodhitam api dvitīya abhāvam dvitīya tvāt eva niṣedhati iti sva virodhāt eva śruteḥ tatra ātātparyāt  māna virodhitva mātrasya tātparya abhāve prayojaka tvāt  sva virodhe api na kṣatiḥ nanu ekena eva pramāṇena ekasya prāpti niṣedhau  anupapannau na rūpa bhedena avirodhāt  dvitīya abhāva svarūpam hi śāstreṇa prāpyate tasya ca prāpya tāvacchedaka rūpam dvitīya abhāva tvam tad ca na niṣedhya tāvacchedakam kiṃtu dvitīya tvam eva niṣedhya mātra anugatam tatra tad anabhyupagame tu na tasya niṣedhya tvam na vā tena ātmanaḥ sa dvitīyatva āpattiḥ ita na kaḥ api doṣaḥ yatra tu prāpyata avacchedakam eva niṣedhya ta avacchedakam tatra prāpti niṣedha śāstrayoḥ atulya viṣaya tve api viśeṣa śāstra viṣaya parityāgena sāmānya śāstra pravṛttiḥ tulya viṣaya tve tvagatyā vikalpa iti na niṣedhasya asaṅkocena pravṛttiḥ yathā ‘na hiṃsyāt sarvā bhūtānī ati niṣedha śāstrasya ‘agnīṣomīyam paśu māla bhete ati ādi prāpti śāstra viṣaya itara viṣaya tvam  atirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇāti ‘nātirātre ṣoḍaśinam gṛhṇātī tyādi prāpti niṣedha śāstrayoḥ tu vikalpena eka viṣaya tvam ekasya eva hiṃsā tvasya ṣoḍaśigraha tvasya ca prāpti niṣedhayoḥ avacchedaka tvāt  tatra niṣedha śāstrasya asaṃkucadvṛtti tve prāpti śāstrasya sarva ātmanā vaiyarthya āpattiḥ prakṛte ca dvitīya tvena rūpeṇa niṣedhasya eva śāstra artha tvāt na kasya api vaiyarthya śaṅkā ataeva dvitīya abhāva niṣedhe punar dvitīya unmajana āpattiḥ iti nirastam upapāditam etad  mithyātva mithyātva sādhane yathā pratiyogi abhāvayoḥ niṣedhyatā avacchedaka aikye na eka niṣedhe apara sattva āpattiḥ iti na ca  svena eva niṣiddhasya dvitīya abhāvasya dvitīyasya iva viśeṣaṇa tvena upalakṣaṇa tvena vā punar upādānam na yuktam iti vācyam abhāva buddhau niṣiddhasya api pratiyoginaḥ ‘sā śuktiri atyatra pratiṣiddhasya api pūrva pratīta rajatasya upalakṣaṇa tayā upādāna darśanāt asaṅkīrṇa jñāna prayojaka tvasya prakṛte api tulya tvāt  tasmāt  ‘ekam eva advitīyam ityādi śrutiḥ viśvamithyā tve pramāṇam iti siddham iti advaita siddhau sāmānyena mithyātva śruti upapattiḥ atha advaita śruteḥ bodha uddhāraḥ nanuāpāta pratipanna eva na tāvat śṛti arthaḥ ‘kaḥ chandasām yogam āveda dhīra iti śrutyā ‘bibheti alpa śrutāt veda iti smṛtyā ca veda arthasya ati gahana tā ukteḥ mīmāṃsā vaii arthya prasaṅgāt ca kiṃtu māna antareṇa pūrva uttareṇa ca aviruddha eva arthaḥ avirodha grahaṇa artham ca mīmāṃsā sāphalyam ata eva ‘a ājyaiḥ stuvate aākāśāt eva samutpadyanta iti ādau  āpāta pratīta ghṛta gagana ādi parityāgena ājya ākāśa ādi padānām sāma param ātmā ādi artha tvam sthāpitam pūrva uttaramīmāṃsayoḥ citra ākāśa ādi adhikaraṇeṣu anyathā tad tad pūrva pakṣa abhyupagama āpatteḥ tathā ca uktam vārtikakāraiḥ śāstram śabda vijñānāt asat nikṛṣṭe arthe vijñānam iti atra  asat nikṛṣṭa vācā ca dvayam atra jihāsitam tādrūpyeṇa paricchedaḥ tad viparyayataḥ api ca viṣaya aviṣayau jñātvā tena utsargā pavādayoḥ bādhā bādhau vivektavyau na tu sāmānya darśanāt  anya eva eka deśena śāstrasya arthaḥ pratīyate anyaḥ tu paripūrṇena samasta aṅga upasaṃhṛtau iti anyatra api uktam  ‘viruddhavat pratīyanta āgamā yatra ye mithas  tatra dṛṣṭa anusāreṇa teṣām arthā vivakṣitāḥ iti tathā ca pratyakṣa ādi virodhāt pūrva uttara virodhāt ca na advaita paratvam ekam eva ityādi vākyānām iti ced na dvaita pratyakṣasya candra prādeśikatva pratyakṣavat  saṃbhāvitā prāmāṇyatayā advaita śruti virodhitva abhāvāt yathā ca śrutyā pratyakṣam bādhyate tathā prapañcitam adhastāt kiṃca pratyakṣam niyata viṣayam śrutiḥ sarva viṣayā tathā ca yatra pratyakṣeṇa bhedaḥ  na gṛhītaḥ tatra eva abheda śruteḥ avakāśaḥ nanu yayoḥ aikyam śrutyā bodhyate tayoḥ bhedaḥ prasaktaḥ  na vā na antyaḥ aprasakta pratiṣedha āpātāt  na ādyaḥ prasañjaka pramāṇa virodhena aikyasya bodhayitum aśakyatvāt iti ced na antya pakṣa abhyupagame doṣa abhāvāt aprasakta pratiṣedha iti ca kim aprasiddha pratiyogi tvam kim vā niṣprayojana tvam iti vivecanīyam na ādyaḥ anyatra prasiddhasya eva bhedasya bheda tvena upasthitasya paraspara pratiyogi anuyogi bhāvena anyatra niṣedha saṃbhavāt  na ca tatra eva prasiddhiḥ tantram niṣedha pramā mātra uccheda prasaṅgāt  na dvitīyaḥ anartha nivṛtteḥ eva prayojana tvāt  anāntarikṣe agniḥ cetavya iti ādau stuti mātra prayojanena api aprayojanena api aprasakta niṣedha darśanāt ca atha śrutyā yayoḥ abhedaḥ  bodhyate tayoḥ upasthitiḥ asti na vā na antyaḥ anupasthitayoḥ abheda bodhana ayogāt ādye sā kim śruti janyā pratyakṣa ādi janyā vā na ādyaḥ śruteḥ māna antara agocara abheda mātra paratvena ghaṭa ādi upasthiteḥ tad janyatva abhāvena sarva advaitāsiddheḥ śruti stha kiṃcana ityādi padānām anuvādakatva abhyupagamāt dvitīye tu tayoḥ bhedaḥ api pratyakṣa ādi siddha iti kva advaita śruti avakāśaḥ mā evam yad  pratyakṣa ādinā gṛhyate tad bhadaḥ api tena gṛhyata eva iti niyama abhāvāt  tathā hi na tāvat padārtha svarūpa jñānam eva bheda jñānam abheda bhrama uccheda prasaṅgāt  svarūpa bheda vādinām api svarūpa jñānāt ghaṭatva ādi prakārakāt bhedatva prakārakam bheda jñānam vilakṣaṇam eva anyathā bheda āgraha nibandhana vyavahārān udaya prasaṅgāt  ataeva sva rūpa jñāna uttara kālam avaśyam bheda jñānam iti api na anavasthā prasaṅgāt ca tathā hi ‘ghaṭa paṭau bhinnau jānāmi iti ghaṭa paṭa bheda dhīḥ sva prakāśā vā anuvyavasāya siddhā vā sākṣi siddhā vā na sva pratiyogika bheda viṣayā bheda dhiyaḥ pratiyogi dhī janyatva niyamena pratiyogi dhīvyakti bhinna vyaktitva āvaśyaka tvāt  svasyā eva sva janyatva anupapatteḥ jñāna antareṇa ca tad bheda grahe kvacid  bheda dhī dhārā viśrāntiḥ avaśyam vācyā anyathā suṣupti viṣaya antara sañcāra ādikam na syāt  atas  tatra api carama bheda dhīrā iva udāharaṇam tathā ca bādhakatva abhimatā yā ghaṭa paṭa bheda dhīḥ sva bheda āviṣayā bhāsate tayā saha bādhyatva abhimatāyāḥ  aikya dhiya aikyam bodhayitvā nirbādhā satī śrutiḥ sarva abhede paryavasyati na hi abhede api bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ svasya api sva bādhaka tā āpatteḥ tad uktam khaṇḍana kṛdbhiḥ ‘sudūra dhāvana śrāntā bādha buddhi paramparā nivṛttau  advaya āmnāyaiḥ pārṣṇigrāhaiḥ vijīyate iti na ca siddhānte ghaṭa tad dhī bheda grāhiṇā sva prakāśena sākṣiṇā svasmin  itara bhedasya api grahaṇa at na anavasthā anyathā svasya ghaṭa ādibhyaḥ abheda saṃśayaḥ syāt iti vācyam sākṣiṇaḥ sva prakāśa tve api sva niṣṭhā itara pratiyogika bheda grahe itara pratiyogi upasthiti sāpekṣa tvāt anyathā svasya antaḥkaraṇa ādi abheda bhramaḥ  na syāt  sva prakāśena bheda agrahe api māna antareṇa bheda grahāt  na ghaṭa ādi abheda saṃśaya iti na kiṃcid etad  syāt etad ‘ ghaṭa paṭau bhinnau  iti pratyakṣam svasya advaita jñāna ādinā bhedam vinā anupapatteḥ tam api ākṣipati iti sarvatra bhedasya apratyakṣa tve api na advaita śruteḥ avakāśaḥ atra ucyate ākṣepaḥ  hi anumānam arthāpattiḥ vā tatra vivāda adhyāsitā buddhiḥ sarvatas  bhinna iti na anumānam saṃbhavati svataḥ api bheda sādhane bādhāt  dṛṣṭāntasya ca sādhya vikala tvāt  yatas  kutaścid  bheda sādhane tu anumāna aviṣaye labdha avakāśā śrutiḥ abhedam bodhayiṣyati na ca sva vyatiriktāt  sarvatas  bhinna iti sādhyam advaita vādinam pratyaprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tvāt  etena sarvam sarvasmāt bhinnam iti vākyam api nirastam tad uktam  ‘hetu ādya bhāva sārvajñye sarvam pakṣayatā aasthite kiṃcid tu tyajatā dattā sā eva dvāra dvaya śruteḥ iti na api arthāpattiḥ sarva bheda viṣayā svāviṣaya tvāt  yayoḥ hi bhedam vinā yatra anupapattiḥ gṛhītā tayoḥ tatra bheda grahe api anupapattau  anupapatti antara agrahaṇāt  sarvatra tad grahaṇe tu dhārā viśrāntau caramadhīḥ udāharaṇam tad uktam  ‘ādya dhī vet ya bhedīyā api anyathā anupapanna tā sva jñāna apekṣaṇāt ante bādhate na advaya śrutim iti nanu ayāvat upapādakam tad sarvam artha āpatteḥ viṣayaḥ na tu yad kiñcit upapādakam tathā ca arthāpatteḥ itarasmāt  bheda abhāve tatra eva abheda śruteḥ labdha avakāśa tvāt ghaṭa paṭa bheda asiddhi āpatteḥ arthāpatti bhedasya api ghaṭa paṭa bheda upapādaka tvena arthāpatti viṣaya tvam vācyam anyathā dṛś dṛśya saṃbandha anupapatti jñāna nivartyatva anupapattiḥ ca sva mithyātva viṣayā na syāt  ‘sarvam khalu idam brahme ati śrutiḥ ‘na iha nānā aiti brahmaṇi bheda mātra niṣedha anupapattiḥ ca sva abheda viṣayā na syāt  tathā ca tatra api śruti antaram artha apatti antaram vā vācyam iti tava api anavasthāpattiḥ iti mā evam vocaḥ vastuta upapādaka tvam na arthāpatti viṣaya tve tantram kiṃtu upapādaka tvena jñāta tvam anyathā arthāpatti bhrama anupapatteḥ tathā ca yena rūpeṇa upapādaka tvam gṛhītam tad rūpa avacchinnam upapādakam arthāpatteḥ viṣayaḥ tatra yadi arthāpatti gata bheda sādhāraṇam upapādaka tāva  chedakam ekam bhavet  tadā saḥ api bhāyāt eva na ca evam asti tad anirūpaṇāt  tathā hi—ghaṭa paṭa bhinna tvam upapādyam tad upapādakam ca na sarva bhinna tvam svataḥ api bheda apatyā tad asaṃbhavāt na api svātirikta sarva bhinna tvam advaita vādinam prati svātiḥ eka viśeṣaṇā siddheḥ sva tvān anugamāt ca tathā ca tena tena rūpeṇa tad tad bhinna tvam eva upapādakam upeyam ata upapādaka tāvacchedaka nānātvāt na sarvam upapādakam arthāpatteḥ viṣaya iti pṛthak pṛthak anupapatti jñāna apekṣāyām sarvatra anupapatti jñāne anavasthānāt  kvacid dhārā viśrāntau tatra eva labdha avakāśā śrutiḥ sarva advaite paryavasyati iti kim anupapannam dṛṣṭānte ca sarvatra sva sādhāraṇam upapādaka tāvacchedakam ekam eva iti tad avacchinna tayā svasya api bhānam iti vaiṣamyam tathā hi dṛśyatva avacchinna mithyā tvam vinā dṛś saṃbandha anupapatti grahāt tad avacchinna mithyātvam arthāpatteḥ viṣaya iti sva mithyā tvam api sva viṣayaḥ evam eva jñāna nivartyatva anupapatteḥ api sva viṣaya tvam tatra api dṛśyatva ādeḥ ekasya eva avacchedaka tvāt  evam ca brahmaṇi sarva abheda bodhikāyāḥ śruteḥ bheda mātra niṣedhānyathā anupapatteḥ ca sva abheda viṣaya tvam aviruddham na hi sarva bhede sva bheda āpattiḥ iva sarva abhede svābhedaḥ  doṣāya tasmāt advaita śrutiḥ bādhya bādhakayoḥ aikya bodhanena nirābādhā sarva advaitam pratipādayati nanu śabda buddhi karmaṇām viramya vyāpāra abhāvāt  katham ādau  alpa viṣayā buddhiḥ paścāt  bahu viṣaya api bhavati iti ucyata iti ced na śrutitaḥ  drāk eva jātāyāḥ sarva viṣayāyā advaita buddheḥ prāmāṇyam vyavasthāpayantīnām asmad buddhīnām eva krameṇa jāyamāna tvāt  ayogya tā jñānam ca na śābda bodhe pratibandhakam na vā yogya tā jñānam hetuḥ yena prathamam sarva advaita buddhiḥ na syāt  tad uktam  ‘atyanta asati api jñānam arthe śabdaḥ karoti hi abādhāt tu pramām atra svatas prāmāṇya niścalām iti vedānta kalpalatikāyām asya arthasya prapañcaḥ  draṣṭavyaḥ etena caram jñāna mithyā tve api na tad viṣayasya mithyātvam jñāna mithyātvasya viṣaya mithyātva asa adhaka tvāt advaita jñāne vyabhicārāt iti nirastam śrutyā eva dvaita mātra niṣedhyatva bodhanāt  advaita jñāna viṣaye ca mithyātva bodhaka abhāvāt eva satya tvam na tu jñāna mithyā tvāt iti na kiṃcid etad  nanu  dvaita jñānāt vaita jñānayoḥ abhede katham bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ na ca vyāvahārika bheda mātreṇa saḥ dvaita jñānasya api bādhakatva āpatteḥ  iti ced na vyāvahārika bheda mātrasya bādhakatva aprayojaka tvāt  yad hi parīkṣita pramāṇa bhāva tvena balavat  tad  bādhakam yad tu sandigdha pramāṇa bhāva tvena durbalam tad  bādhyam iti vyavasthāyām dvaita jñānasya durbala tvena ābādhaka tvasya advaita jñānasya ca balavat tvena bādhaka tvasya śabda pratyakṣa bala abala vicāre darśita tvāt  yad tu  apaḥ  vā idam sarvam bhūtami atyādi śrutiḥ ‘vimatam jala abhinnam pratīta tvāt  jalavat iti anumānam vā sva bādhakasya jala abhedam gṛhītvā nirbādham sat  tvad ukta nyāyena sarvasya jala abhedam bodhayet  iti tad na jala abheda bodhane api bādhya bādhakayoḥ aikyā bodhanāt bādhakasya bādhakatva upapatteḥ aikya jñāna bheda jñānayoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvasya jala abheda jñānena anapāyāt bādhakā bhedaḥ  hi bādhakatva abhāve prayojakaḥ bādhakasya sva bādhakatva adarśanāt  atas  na bādhya bādha kaikya jñānasya jala abheda jñāna sāmyam etena sarvam sarvasmāt bhinnam iti mad vākyam advaita vākya tad bhāna tad viṣayāṇām tebhyaḥ  bhedam ādau gṛhītvā nirbādham sat sarva bhede paryavasyati iti nirastam bādhya bādhakayoḥ abhede bādhakatva abhāvavat  bhede api bādhaka tvam na syāt iti atra hetu abhāvāt  pūrva ukta doṣāt ca iti diś  sarva asattvam sarva mithyātvān na atiricyate atas  ‘sarvam asat iti pratyavasthānam anavakāśam nanu śrutyā sarvasya mithyātvam vā bodhyate brahma abhinna tvam vā ādye ‘sarvam khalu idam brahma aiti sāmānādhikaraṇyam na syāt  satya anṛtayoḥ aikya ayogāt dvitīye aidam rajataṃ ‘gauraḥ aham i atyādi bhramāṇām pramātvam syāt  ātmani deha ādi bhedasya anṛtāt vyāvṛtteḥ ca bodhakānām vedāntānām ‘nedam rajatami atyādi bādhakasya ca aprāmāṇyam syāt  ghaṭa jñānena eva tad abhinna brahma tada bheda ādeḥ sarvasya api vastu tas  jñāta tvena sārvajñyam vedāntānām vaiyarthyam sadyas  mokṣaḥ ca syāt  sukha duḥkha bandha mokṣa bheda abheda dūṣaṇa bhūṣaṇa jaya parājaya bhrānti pramāda ādeḥ api vastu tas  bheda abhāvena sarva saṅkara āpattyā sva kriyāsu anyāya sva vacana virodhāḥ ca syuḥ iti ced na ādye ‘mṛd ghaṭaḥ ‘idam rajatami atyādau  iva upādāna upādeya bhāvena api sāmānādhikaraṇya upapatteḥ dvitīye vastu tas  bheda abhāve api āvidyaka bhedam ādāya sarva vyavasthā upapatteḥ na ca bhedasya api anāvidyaka brahma abhinna tvena avidyakatva ayoga iti vācyam āvidyaka tvasya api āvidyakasya eva aṅgīkārāt atha avidyaka tvasya api brahma abhinna tvāt  katham āvidyaka tvam iti ced  tasmin  api tasya kalpita tvāt iti gṛhāṇa nanu muktāvā vidyakasya api bhedasya abhāvena ānandasya duḥkha abhinna tvena apuruṣa arthatva apātaḥ tad tad asādhāraṇa svabhāvasya tatra tatra abhāve api tad tad abhede pāribhāṣikaḥ ayam abhedaḥ  bhede paryavasyet  asādhāraṇa rūpeṇa bhedam abhyupetya sat rūpeṇa bheda niṣedhe api iṣṭāpattiḥ aprasakta niṣedhaḥ ca iti ced na ekasyām eva brahma vyaktau tad tad asādhāraṇa svabhāvānām kalpita tvena asattvāt sarva kalpanā niṣedha kāle kalpita dharma avacchinna bheda abheda ādi prasakteḥ ayogāt  ataeva na aprasakta pratiṣedha iṣṭāpattiḥ vā ‘sad dravyaṃ ‘san guṇa ityādi pratītyā prasaktānām tad tad dharmāṇām brahmaṇi pratiṣedhāt  atas  sarva dharma śūnyāyā ekasya eva sat vyakteḥ cit ānanda rūpāyāḥ pratipādanāt na pāribhāṣikaḥ ayam abheda iti siddham tad evam ‘sarvam brahma abhinnam i ati mate mithyā bhūtasya brahma bhede api sat mātram eva brahma abhinnam iti mate vā na pratyakṣa ādi virodhaḥ na api pūrva uttara virodhaḥ iti advaita śruteḥ bādha uddhāraḥ atha ekam eva ityādi śruti artha vicāraḥ nanu yadi api asalila ekaḥ  draṣṭā advaita iti atra salila śabdasya tad sādṛśyāt  svacchatva mātra paratvāt tasya ca sarva mala asaṃsargitva svarūpasya advaite api upapatteḥ ‘sat eva somya idam agra āsī adityatra ca agra padasya ‘tadā aikṣata nāma rūpe vyākara ut iti ādeḥ ca kāla īkṣaṇa nāma rūpa ātmaka prapañca prāpakasya avidyaka dvaita viṣayaka tvena vāstava advaita virodhitva abhāvaḥ tathā api ‘sat eva somya idam agra āsīt i atyanena idam śabda uditasya viśvasya sat abhedena sattvam uktvā punar advitīya padena tad niṣedhe vyāghātaḥ na hi ‘sadāsī adityasya asat āsīt iti artha iti ced na sat vyatirekeṇa na āsīt iti arthasya eva niṣedha artha tvāt vivṛtam ca etad  bhāṣya kāra ādibhiḥ ārambhaṇa adhikaraṇe na ca sat vyatirekeṇa asattva uktau sat ātmanā satya tvam āgacchati iti vācyam āgacchatu nāma kaḥ  hi brahma abhinnasya asattva sādhanāya pravṛttaḥ  yaḥ  bibhīyāt  advaita vākyasya ca ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅgavat tayā balavatu ena avidyaka dvaita pratipādaka tvam sṛṣṭi ādi vākyānām iti śravaṇa svarūpa nirūpaṇe vedānta kalpa latikāyām abhihitam asmābhiḥ iha api abhidhāsyate ṣaḍvidhatātparya liṅgāni pradarśayadbhiḥ ata eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna pratijñayā upakramāt aaitadātmyam idam sarvam tad satyam sa ātmā tad tvam asī atyupasaṃhārāt ca advaitasya eva mahā prākaraṇika tayā tad anusāreṇa tad vākya sthapadānām vyākhyeyatva avadhāraṇāt nānā artha padānām artha antara upasthāpakatva saṃbhave api prakṛta vākya arthān anvayitayā tad parityāgena prakṛta vākya artha anukūla padārtha upasthiti paratvam eva āstheyam tatra na dvitīyam advitīyam iti tad puruṣa abhyupagame na dvitīyam kiṃtu prathamam tṛtīyam ca iti arthaḥ syāt  sa ca na saṃbhavati tayoḥ api kiṃcid apekṣya dvitīya tvāt  atas  na vidyate dvitīyam yatra iti bahuvrīhiḥ eva ādaraṇīyaḥ na ca ekena eva advitīya padena bheda traya niṣedha saṃbhave eka avadhāraṇa padayoḥ vaiyarthyam iti vācyam vijātīyam kiṃcid apekṣya dvitīyatva avacchinna niṣedhasya advitīya śabda artha tvāt ayam ca atra saṅkocaḥ  balīvarda pada sannidhānāt  gopada iva sajātīya sva gata bheda niṣedhaka eka avadhāraṇa pada sannidhi prayukta eva tad uktam  ‘vṛkṣasya sva gataḥ  bhedaḥ patra puṣpa phala ādibhiḥ vṛkṣa antarāt sa jātīyaḥ  vijātīyaḥ śilāditaḥ tathā sat vastunaḥ  bheda trayam prāptam nivāryate eka avadhāraṇa dvaita pratiṣedhaiḥ tribhiḥ kramāt  iti sva gata bhedaḥ nānātva rūpa jīva īśvara bhedaḥ sajātīya bhedaḥ atra dravyatva ādinā sajātīya pṛthivī ādi bhedaḥ vijātīya bhedaḥ  guṇa ādi bhedaḥ athavā jaḍa bhedaḥ  vijātīya bhedaḥ caitanya bhedaḥ sajātīya bhedaḥ jñāna ānanda ādi dharma bhedaḥ sva gata bhedaḥ yadi ca  asya goḥ dvitīyaḥ anveṣṭavya  iti ukte agauḥ eva dvitīyaḥ anviṣyate na aśvaḥ  na gardabha iti mahābhāṣya anusārāt samāna jātīya dvitīya para tvam dvitīya śabdasya tadā advitīya śabdasya sajātīya bheda niṣedha paratvam vijātīya sva gata bheda niṣedha para tvam tu eka avadhāraṇa padayoḥ yatheṣṭam vyākhyeyam athavā advitīya padena eva bheda traya niṣedhaḥ eka avadhāraṇa pade tu saṅkoca śaṅkā parihārāya yad tu kenacid  pralapitaṃ dvitīya śabdaḥ sahāya vācī ‘asi dvitīyaḥ anusasāra pāṇḍava am iti prayogāt  ‘asi dvitīyaḥ asi sahāyaḥ iti mahābhāṣya ukteḥ ca tathā ca advitīyam asahāyam iti arthaḥ astu evam eka śabdasya api nānā artha tvena aviruddha artham ādāya upapattau na mithyātva paryavasāyitā aastheyā tathā ca ‘eke mukhyānyakevalā iti amaraḥ  eka śabdaḥ ayam anya pradhāna asahāya saṅkhyā prathama samāna vācī ti ‘ekaḥ  gotra iti sūtre kaiyaṭaḥ aṣṇā antā ṣaṣ i ati sūtre mahābhāṣya kāraḥ api eka śabdaḥ ayam bahu arthaḥ asti saṅkhyā arthaḥ asti asahāya vācī asti anya artha ityādi vyākhyātavān tathā ca jīva ādibhyaḥ anya tvam prādhānyam vā eka śabda arthaḥ astu evam anyāni api śruti padāni vyākhyeyāni iti tad  pūrva ukta yuktibhiḥ apāstam vistareṇa ca vakṣyate tātparya nirūpaṇe tad evam sat rūpe brahmaṇi pada trayeṇa bheda traya niṣedhāt  tad bhinna mithyā tve paryavasitam ‘ekam eva advitīya mi ati vākyam evam anyā api śrutayaḥ smṛtayaḥ ca grantha vistara bhayāt na udāhṛtāḥ svayam eva sūribhiḥ ākare draṣṭavyāḥ iti advaita siddhau sarva advaita śruteḥ advaitatāt paryakatva nirṇayaḥ atha jñāna nivarttya tvāni atha anupapattiḥ ‘tarati śokam ātma vit ‘tathā vidvān nāma rūpāt vimuktaḥ ‘  bhidyate hṛdaya granthiḥ chidyante sarva saṃśayāḥ kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi tasmin dṛṣṭe parāvare ityādi śruti smṛti bodhita jñāna nivartya tvānyathā anupapattiḥ api bandha mithyā tve pramāṇam satya tve brahma vada nivartyatva āpatteḥ tathā hi śukti rūpya rajju sarpa ādau jñāna nivartya tve na tāvat tad tad rūpavat tvam jñāna nivartya ta avacchedakam ananugamāt  kiṃtu sarva anugatam amithyā tvam eva ajñāna kalpitatva apara paryāyam avacchedakam evam jñānasya api tad nivartaka tve na śukti ādi viṣaya tvam avacchedakam ananugamāt  kiṃtu sarva anugatam adhiṣṭhāna pramātvam eva tathā ca yatra jñānasya adhiṣṭhāna pramātvena nivartaka tā tatra mithyā tvena eva nivartyata iti niyamaḥ siddhyati etādṛśa niyama anabhyupagame ca ananta niyama kalpanā gaurava rūpaḥ  bādhakaḥ tarkaḥ tathā hi—yat niṣṭhā yad ākārā pramā rūpa antaḥkaraṇa vṛttiḥ udeti tad niṣṭham tad ākāram ajñānam nāśayati iti niyamasya siddha tvāt  upādāna nāśasya ca upādeya nivartaka tvāt  śukti ādi jñānena tad tad ākāra ajñāna nāśe tad upādeyānām rajata ādīnām nivṛttiḥ aucitya āvarjitā eva iti niyama antara akalpanena lāghavam anukūlaḥ tarkaḥ asmat pakṣe ajñāna upādeya tvam ca śukti rajata ādīnām anvaya vyatireka siddham agre sthāsyati evam sthite kṛtsnasya api prapañcasya ātma pramāni vartya tve tad ajñāna kalpita tvam eva tatra avacchedakam kalpyate na tu ananugatam ākāśatva ādi na vā brahma bhinna tvam sat bhinna tvam vā sarva anugatam api tucche ati prasakteḥ tad vāraka viśeṣaṇa prakṣepe tu sat asat vilakṣaṇatva rūpa mithyā tvam eva nivartyatā prayojakam paryavasitam anyathā niyama antara kalpanā gaurava āpatteḥ tathā ca śukti ādi jñānasya yena rūpeṇa nivartaka tvam tena rūpeṇa ātma jñānasya nivartaka tvam rūpya ādau yena rūpeṇa nivartya tvam prapañce tad rūpam vinā anupapadyamānam sva upapādaka tayā tatra tad  kalpayati iti siddham mithyātvam nanu—bhavet etad evam yadi ātma jñānasya prapañce kā nivartye śukti ādi jñāna sādhāraṇam adhiṣṭhāna pramātvam eva avacchedakam iti atra kiṃcid mānam bhavet  rūpa antareṇa api nivartakatva saṃbhavāt  śrutiḥ tu dvaita prapañcasya advitīya ātma jñānam nivartakam iti etāvat mātre pramāṇam na tu avacchedaka viśeṣe api na ca jñāna nivartyatā mātrāt mithyātva siddhiḥ setu darśana ādi nivarti durita ādiṣu vyabhicārāt  tatra vihita kriyātva ādinā nivartaka tvāt na vyabhicāra iti ced  prakṛte api rūpa antaram na avacchedakam iti kutaḥ niraṇāyi jñānasya hi sva prāgabhāvam prati pratiyogi tvena nivartaka tā pūrva jñāna ādikam prati tu uttara virodhi guṇa tvena saṃskāram prati phala tvena rāga ādikam prati viṣaya doṣa darśana tvena viṣam prati garuḍadhyāna tvena setu ādi darśanasya duritam prati vihita kriyā tvena evam ca mithyātvam vinā api jñāna nivartyatva darśanāt  na tad mithyātvasya sādhakam udāhṛteṣu api satyatva asaṃpratipattyā mithyātvam eva asti iti ced  astu vā mā astu jñāna nivartyatva mātram tu na tasya sādhakam iti brūmaḥ hetu antareṇa   siddhau ca etad upanyāsaḥ  vyarthaḥ śukti rūpī ādau katham iti ced śruṇu adhiṣṭhāna jñāna tvena tatra jñānasya nivartaka tvāt  adhiṣṭhāna jñāna tvam hi ajñāna nāśaka jñāna tvam vā ajñāna samāna viṣayaka pramātvam vā iti tena rūpeṇa nivartaka tve tad nivartyasya tad jñāna samāna viṣaya ka ajñāna upādānakatva rūpa mithyā tvam sidhyati iti yuktam śukti ādi jñāna samāna viṣaya ka ajñāna upādānaka tvena rajata ādeḥ mithyātvam setu ādi darśana ādi nivarti durita ādeḥ tu na nivartaka jñāna samāna viṣayaka ajñāna upādānaka tvam iti na mithyātvam evam ca ātma jñānasya api vihita kriyā tvena nivartakatva saṃbhavāt  adhiṣṭhāna jñāna tvena ca nivartaka tve māna abhāvāt na ātma ajñāna upādānakatva rūpa mithyātva siddhiḥ prapañcasya iti prāptam atra ucyate ātma jñānasya api adhiṣṭhāna jñāna tvena eva prapañcam prati nivartaka tvam prakāra antara asaṃbhavāt tathā hi pratiyogi tvam tāvat na avacchedakam prapañcasya bhāva rūpa tvāt  jñānasya prāgabhāva nivṛtti rūpa tvena pratiyogi tvena prāc abhāva nivartakatva asiddheḥ ca na api uttara guṇa tvam ākāśa ādeḥ ātma viśeṣa guṇatva abhāvāt icchā ādeḥ api prapañca nivartakatva apātāt ca na api phala tvam saṃskārasya smaraṇa janaka tvavat ākāśa ādeḥ ātma jñāna janakatva abhāvāt saṃskārasya smṛtyanāśya tvena udāharaṇa asiddheḥ ca viṣaya doṣa darśanasya tu rāga ādi nivartaka tvam rāga ādi kāraṇī bhūta balavat aniṣṭān anubandhi iṣṭa sādhanatva bhrama rūpa tad kāraṇa nivartaka tvena iti na prakṛta udāharaṇāt atiricyate śakti rūpya tulya tvāt garuḍa dhyānam tu na pratyudāharaṇam dhyānasya rāga ādeḥ iva jñānatva anabhyupagamāt  jñānasya icchā anadhīna tvena tad adhīna jñāna apekṣayā vailakṣaṇyāt  spaṣṭam ca etad ākare jñāna tve api tasya setu darśana pakṣān na atirekaḥ śāstra vihitatva aviśeṣāt  kevalam setu ādi darśanavat vihita kriyā tvam avaśiṣyate tad ca na saṃbhavati jñānasya kartum akaṛtum aśakyatvena vidheyatva ayogāt vistareṇa ca jñāne vidhiḥ ākareṣu nirākṛtaḥ nirākariṣyate ca iha api setu darśane katham iti ced  viśiṣṭa ākāreṇa vidheyatva upapattiḥ na hi setu darśana mātrasya durita nāśaka tvam tatratī amla icchānām api durita nāśa prasaṅgāt  kiṃtu para rāṣṭrāt upasthāna ādi pūrvaka vrata kalāpa viśiṣṭasya tathā ca chatra pādukā ādi varjana doṣa udghoṣaṇa dūra deśa gāmitva bhikṣā bhojitva ādi niyamānām kṛti sādhya tvāt  tad viśiṣṭam setu darśanam api kṛti sādhyam iti viśiṣṭa rūpeṇa vidhāna upapattiḥ ātma jñāne tu na asti kiṃcid viśeṣaṇam api kṛti sādhyam yena tad viśiṣṭa tvena api vidheya tvam syāt  karmasamuccayasya nirākariṣyamāṇa tvāt  bandhasya ajñāna mātra hetuka tvena jñāna atirikta nivartaka anapekṣaṇāt ca bandhasya ajñāna hetuka tvam ca ‘māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt   jñānena āvṛtam jñānam tena muhyanti jantavaḥ ityādi śruti smṛti nyāya siddham vakṣyate ca agre ajñāna nivartaka jñānasya ca utpattim antareṇa anya apekṣā na asti iti śukti ādi jñāne dṛṣṭam tathā ca uktam vārtika kṛdbhiḥ  tattvam asya ādi vākya uttha samyak dhī janma mātrataḥ avidyā saha kāryeṇa na āsīt asti bhaviṣyati iti ‘pratyagyāthātmya dhīḥ eva pratyak ajñāna hāni kṛt  sā ca ātma utpattitaḥ  na anyat hānta dhvastau  apekṣate iti ca ata eva ayatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaram paśyati yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhū tad kena kam paśyet i atyādi śrutiḥ ‘yā aniśā sarva bhūtānām tasyām jāgarti saṃyamī yasyām jāgrati bhūtāni sā niśā paśyataḥ  muneḥ ityādi smṛtiḥ ca avidyā avasthāyām saṃsāra upalambham vidyā avasthāyām ca tad anupalambham darśayati tasmāt adhiṣṭhāna pramātvena ātma jñāna nivartya tvāt śukti rūpī ādiṣu iva bandhe api mithyātvam siddham yatvīśvara jñānena satyam ghaṭa ādi nivartata iti pratyudāharaṇam tad na īśvara jñānasya tārkika mate api upādāna gocara aparokṣa jñāna tvena eva kāraṇa tvāt  abhāvasya ca nirupādāna tvāt  abhāvam prati kāraṇa tve māna abhāvāt sa upādāna tve tu samaveta tvena tasya api bhāvatva āpatteḥ atyanta abhāva ādivat ca tad ajanya tve api dhvaṃsasya tad viṣayatva upapatteḥ na ca tādṛś īśvara jñāne saṃpratipattiḥ api anyeṣām iti na kā api anupapattiḥ yathā ca śukti ādi jñānasya rūpya ādi nivartaka tvam aprāmāṇya jñāna viraham apekṣya eva evam ātma jñānasya api śravaṇa ādi nivṛttau  asaṃbhāvana ādi nivṛtti rūpā prāmāṇya jñāna viraha apekṣa tvam iti na kiṃcid api adhikam kalpitam ātma jñānasya sarva su kṛta sādhya tvam śukti ādi jñāna apekṣayā vilakṣaṇam iti tu dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭantikayoḥ vaidharmya mātra udbhāvanāt vaidharmya samā jātiḥ ājñanasya ca samāna adhikaraṇa samāna ākāra jñāna nivartya tvam jīvanmuktau ca prārabdha karma pratibandhena bandha nāśa vilamba ityādi sarvam upariṣṭāt upapādayiṣyate satyasya jñāna nivartya tve tu āśraya viṣaya ubhaya saṃbandhitva ādinā atiprasaṅgaḥ  vivaraṇa kāraiḥ varṇitaḥ tasmāt adhiṣṭhāna jñāna tvena jñāna nivartya tvam mithyātve pramāṇam iti siddham iti advaita siddhau jñāna nivartya tvāni athā anupapattiḥ atha dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi upapattiḥ śukti rūpya svapna ādivat  dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi anyathā anupapattyā api jagataḥ  mithyātva siddhiḥ atha kā iyam dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭiḥ     dṛṣṭiḥ eva sṛṣṭiḥ iti vā     dṛṣṭi vyatirikta sṛṣṭi abhāvaḥ  vā     dṛṣṭi vyatirekeṇa sṛjya abhāvaḥ  vā     dṛṣṭi sāmagrī janya tvam vā     dṛṣṭi samāna kālīna sṛṣṭiḥ vā     dṛṣṭi samāna sattāka sṛṣṭiḥ vā     sat asat vilakṣaṇa tvam vā     trividha sattva bahis bhūta tve satya sat vilakṣaṇa tvam vā     ajñāta sattva abhāvaḥ  vā     jñāta eka sattvam vā ādye vṛtti rūpā caitanya rūpā vā dṛṣṭiḥ abhimatā prathame carama vṛtti viṣaya brahmaṇaḥ api dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭyāpattiḥ dvitīye sarvadā api sṛṣṭi āpattiḥ na dvitīyaḥ caitreṇa sṛṣṭaḥ  mayā dṛṣṭa iti vailakṣaṇyena vyavahāra anupapatteḥ na tṛtīyaḥ ‘jñātaḥ  ghaṭaḥ  na jñānam iati anubhava virodhāt  na caturthaḥ eka sāmagrī prasūta tvena ghaṭa ādeḥ dṛṣṭi abhinna tvena anantara ukta doṣāt na pañcamaḥ śābda ādi jñāna sama kāla utpanna ghaṭa ādau asiddha sādhanāt  tadvat anyatra artha antara tā āpatteḥ ca na ṣaṣṭhaḥ ubhaya sattve api upapatteḥ siddha sādhanāt  na saptamaḥ asya eva mithyātva rūpa tvena tad sādhanāya eva tad upanyāsa anupapatteḥ na aṣṭamaḥ trividha sattva madhye prātibhāsika sattvasya api antarbhāvena dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi pakṣe tadvati jagati tad bahirbhāva anupapatteḥ na navamaḥ tuccha sādhāraṇyāt  na daśamaḥ sukha ādau siddha sādhanāt  tadvat anyatra artha antarāt ca iti ced na doṣa prayuktatva nibandhanasya jñāta eka sattvasya ajñāta sattva abhāvasya vā pratipanna upādhi dṛṣṭi janya jñāta eka sattvasya vā draṣṭṛ antarāvedya tve sati jñāta eka sattvasya vā vivakṣita tvāt  tathā ca na sukha ādi aṃśe siddha sādhanam tadvat anyatra artha antaram vā nanu ‘jīva īśaḥ  viśuddhā cit  tathā jīveśayoḥ bhidā avidyā tad citoḥ yogaḥ ṣaṣ asmākam anādayaḥ iti prācām vacanena bauddham prati pratyabhijñāna ādinā viśvasya sthāyitva pratipādakena ca sūtra bhāṣya vivaraṇa ādi granthena virodha iti ced na anādi atirikta sṛṣṭi viṣaya eva dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi svīkārāt kāraṇa ātmanā sthāyitva svīkārāt ca tāvatā eva bauddha abhimata kṣaṇikatva nirākaraṇa upapatteḥ na ākara virodhaḥ pratyuta ākareṣu bahuśas  dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭiḥ upapāditā eva nanu evaṃ—pratīti mātra śarīra tvena niyata kāraṇā janya tve śrutiṣu svarga ādi artham jyotiṣṭoma ādi vidheḥ brahma sākṣātkāra artham śravaṇa ādi vidheḥ ākāśa ādeḥ vāyu ādi hetutvasya ca uktiḥ ayuktā iti ced na svāpna kārya kāraṇa bhāva bodhaka vākyavat upapatteḥ na ca evam vedānta vākyasya tad mīmāṃsāyāḥ ca svapna vākya tad mī māṃsā tulya tā āpattiḥ viṣaya bādha ābādhābhyām viśeṣa upapatteḥ ata eva tṛpyartham bhojane para pratyāyana artham śabda ādau ca pravṛtteḥ ayogena sva kriyā vyāghāta iti nirastam svāpna vyavahāravat upapatteḥ atha evaṃ—ghaṭa ādeḥ sva jñānāt pūrvam asattvena pratikarma vyavasthā anupapattiḥ adhiṣṭhānasya api śuktīdam aṃśasya rūpya ādivat  ‘idam rajatam i ati jñānāt prāc asattvena saṃprayoga ādi hetu traya janyatva rūpa adhyāsa taṭa stha lakṣaṇasya satyasya vastunaḥ  mithyā vastu saṃbheda avabhāsa iti asya svarūpa lakṣaṇasya ca ayoga iti ced na pratikarma vyavasthāyāḥ saṃprayoga ādi hetu traya janyatva rūpa adhyāsa taṭa stha lakṣaṇasya ca manda adhikāri viṣaya tvāt satyasya vastunaḥ  mithyā vastu saṃbheda avabhāsa iti svarūpa lakṣaṇam tu dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi pakṣe api aviruddham na hi idam aṃśa avacchinnam caitanyam na vastu na vā mithyā ārūpyasya tena saha na saṃbheda avabhāsaḥ na ca idam rūpyam iti jñāna kāle śuktitva ādeḥ abhāvena adhyāsasya tad ajñāna kāryatva ādi prakriyā virodha iti vācyam ‘idam rūpya am iti jñāna kāle śukti tvasya abhāve api tad ajñāna sthiti avirodhāt na hi sattā kāla iva sattā viraha kāle api ajñānam virudhyate na ca ‘idam rūpyam na idam rūpyam i ati jñānayoḥ bhinna aviṣaya tvena bādhya bādhaka bhāva anupapattiḥ iti vācyam bhinna viṣaya tve api viṣayayoḥ sārūpyāt  svapna bādhya bādhakayoḥ iva bādhya bādhaka bhāva upapatteḥ na ca  rūpya ādi bādhasya api dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi tve tena rūpya ādeḥ mithyātvā siddhiḥ iti vācyam bādhya an yūna sattāka tvam eva bādhaka tve prayojakam na tu adhika sattāka tvam iti asya upapādita tvena vyāvahārikeṇa vyāvahārika bādhavat  prātibhāsikena prātibhāsika bādhā virodhāt na ca suṣupti pralaya ādau jīva brahma vibhāgasya apratīta tvena avidyamāna tayā pratisuṣupti pratipralayam ca muktasya punarāvṛtti āpattiḥ iti vācyam jīva brahma vibhāga ādeḥ anādi tvena dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭitva anabhyupagamasya ukta tvāt na ca suṣuptam prati saṃskāra ādeḥ api abhāvena tasya punar  prabodha ayogaḥ kāraṇa ātmanā saṃskāra ādeḥ sattvāt  na ca mokṣasya dṛś anya tvena svāpna mokṣavat  dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭyāpattiḥ mokṣasya brahma svarūpa tvena dṛś bhid na tvā siddheḥ na ca caitanya mātra rūpā dṛṣṭiḥ na sṛṣṭiḥ kiṃtu vṛtti viśiṣṭa caitanya rūpā vā vṛtti rūpā vā dṛṣṭiḥ sṛṣṭiḥ iti vācyam tathā ca tasyāḥ  api dṛṣṭi antaram sṛṣṭiḥ iti anavasthā iti vācyam caitanya mātrasya dṛṣṭi tve yadi api tad samāna sattāka tayā ghaṭa ādeḥ sadātanatva āpattiḥ tathā api vṛtti upahita caitanyam eva dṛṣṭi śabda arthaḥ vṛttau  api vṛttiḥ eva sva svarūpā caitanya upādhiḥ iti na anavasthā ata eva doṣa ajñāna adṛṣṭa deha indriya ādīnām abhāve na bhrama iti teṣām api dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi tve anavasthā iti nirastam svāpna bhramavat deha indriya ādi naiḥ apekṣyeṇa api upapatteḥ anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam ca tadvat eva na ca dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭeḥ api dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi tvena ghaṭa ādeḥ adṛṣṭi sṛṣṭitva āpattiḥ iti vācyam jñānasya jñeya tve api viṣayasya ajñeyatva abhāvavat  dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭeḥ dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi tve api ghaṭa ādeḥ dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭitva upapatteḥ nanu aikya pratyabhijñā virodhaḥ pūrva kāla pratītasya idānīm abhāvāt na ca eṣā bhrāntiḥ dīpa ādau pariṇāma bhedasya iva iha bādhakasya abhāvāt  tad abhāve api bhrānti tve ghaṭa ādeḥ api ekasmin kṣaṇe bhedasya ātmanaḥ api pratikṣaṇam bhedasya prasaṅga iti ced na ‘na iha nāne ati ādi śrutibhiḥ prapañcasya mithyātve avadhṛte rajju sarpa ādivat  pratibhāsa mātra śarīra tvam eva pratibhāsa kāla atirikta kāla sattve bādhakam atas  bhinna kālānām ātma bhinnānām pratyabhijñā bhrāntiḥ ātmani eka pratītireka kāla avacchedena ghaṭa ādau ca aikya pratyabhijñā na bhrāntiḥ eka kāla avacchinna ghaṭā dau  ātmani ca abhede bādhaka abhāvāt puruṣa antara pratītena saha eka kāla avacchedena api ghaṭa ādau pratyabhijñānam bhrama eva pratibhāsasya bhedāt  yathā ekasyām eva rajjvām manda andhakāra vartinyām daśānām yugapad  sarpa bhrameṇa palāyamānānām paraspara saṃvādena eka eva sarpaḥ sarvaiḥ anubhūyata iti pratyabhijñā bhramaḥ anya bhrama siddhasya anyena jñātum aśakyatvāt  nanu atra katham abheda bhramaḥ tad kāraṇasya sādṛśya ādeḥ kasya api abhāvāt iti ced na svapna abheda bhramavat dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi siddha sādṛśya ādi saṃbhavāt na ca evam abheda eva utpadyatām iti vācyam iṣṭa āpatteḥ raju sarpa ādivat utpannasya eva grahaṇa niyamāt  na ca kvacid utpadyate kvacid na iti atra niyāmaka abhāvaḥ māyāyāḥ  vicitra śaktikatva abhyupagamāt na ca saḥ ayam devadatta iti dṛṣṭāntena tad tvam asya ādi vākye jahat ajahat lakṣaṇayā aikya paratva uktya yoga iti vācyam yadi api dharmavat dharmya bhedaḥ api bādhita eva iti jahat ajahat lakṣaṇā api na yujyate tathā api yadā dharma abhedaḥ  bādhān na gṛhītaḥ kiṃtu dharmya bheda eva tadā ‘saḥ ayami atyādau jahat ajahat lakṣaṇa asaṃbhavena dṛṣṭāntatva upapattiḥ na ca abhedasya api dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi tvena tad jñānasya bādhakatva ayogaḥ ātma abhedasya ātma rūpa tvena dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭitva abhāvāt anyūna sattākatva mātreṇa bādhakatva upapatteḥ ca na ca sākṣātkārasya api dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi tvena pramāṇa janyatva abhāvāt tattva jñānatva abhāvena tatas  muktiḥ na syāt iti vācyam abādhita viṣaya tvena eva tattva jñānatva upapatteḥ tasya ca dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi tve api akṣateḥ na ca ‘dhruvā dyauḥ dhruvā pṛthivī dhruvāsaḥ parvatā ime adhruvam viśvam idam jagadi atyādi śruti virodhaḥ anitya tāvādibhiḥ api dhruva iti asyāni athā ānayane āvaśyake dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi pratipādaka śruti anurodhena ākalpam saṃtāna aviccheda paratvasya eva yukta tvāt  anyathā ‘dhuvaḥ  rāje ati ādau  avagateḥ dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭau ca ‘evam eva asmāt ātmanaḥ sarve prāṇāḥ sarve lokāḥ sarve vedāḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni sarva eta ātmanaḥ  vyuccarantī ati śrutiḥ supta utthita jīvāt  prāṇa ādi sṛṣṭim pratipādayantī pramāṇam na ca suṣuptau prāṇa ādi pañcakasya sattvāt kim artham punar  sṛṣṭiḥ iti vācyam ‘na tu tad dvitīyam asti tatas anyat vibhaktam yad paśye adityādinā suṣuptau sakala kārya prapañca laya śravaṇāt  na ca suṣuptau ahitā nāma nāḍya‘ iti nāḍī sattva pratipādaka vākya virodhaḥ kena krameṇa suṣuptau bhavati iti apekṣāyām hitā nāma nāḍyaḥ  hṛdayāt purītatam abhipratiṣṭhante tābhiḥ pratyavasṛpya purītati śeta ityādinā suṣupti avyavahita kāle krama uktaye nāḍī sattvam pratipādyate na tu suṣupti kāle api vākya antara virodhāt prāk  sattva mātreṇa ca krama abhidhāna paryāpteḥ nanu yatra eṣa etad suptaḥ abhūt iti yad śabdena supta ādhāra tvena uktasya brahmaṇa eva asmāt ātmana iti anena parāmarśāt tad kartṛkā eva prāṇa ādi sṛṣṭiḥ na tu supta utthita jīva kartṛkā anyathā agni ūrṇa nābhyādeḥ tantu visphuliṅga ādi janana uktiḥ atra api vākye sarva loka sṛṣṭi uktiḥ ca alīka arthā syāt  na hi dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi pakṣe agni ūrṇanābhi ādeḥ tantu ādi janaka tvam sarva loka sṛṣṭiḥ vāsti iti ced  na yatra iti asya kāla paratvena yad śabdena brahmaṇaḥ  nirdeśa abhāvāt na ca yatra iti asya brahma rūpa adhikaraṇa para tvam kāla para tvam vā iti atra vinigamanā virahaḥ anantara vākye kaiṣa tadā abhūt iti atra tadā iti pada dvaya upādānasya eva vinigamaka tvāt  yatra iti anena deśa nirdeśe kā iti deśa praśna anupapatteḥ kālāniḥ deśe ca tadā iti pratinirdeśa anupapatteḥ bhāṣya kāra ādibhiḥ ca sthūla adhikāriṇam prati tathā vyākhyānāt  ūrṇanābhyādeḥ tantu ādi janma utpattiḥ tu laukika bhrama siddha kārya kāraṇa bhāva prasiddhim anurudhya sarva loka ādi sṛṣṭiḥ ca tad tad dṛṣṭi vyaktim abhipretya yadā yad  paśyati tad sama kālam tad  sṛjati iti atra tātparyāt  na ca avidyā saha kṛta jīva kāraṇaka tve jagat vaicitrya anupapattiḥ jagat upādānasya ajñānasya vicitra śaktika tvāt  upapatti antaram ca atra siddhānta bindu kalpa latikā ādau  asmābhiḥ abhihitam vāsiṣṭha vārtikā amṛta ādā  ākare ca spaṣṭam eva uktam yathā ‘avidyā yonayaḥ  bhāvāḥ sarve amī budbudā iva kṣaṇam udbhūya gacchanti jñāna eka jaladhau layam ityādi tasmāt  brahmā atiriktam kṛtsnam dvaita jātam jñāna jñeya rūpam āvidyakam eva iti prātītika sattvam sarvasya iti siddham rajju sarpa ādivat viśvam na ajñātam sat iti sthitam prabuddha dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi tvāt suṣuptau ca laya śruteḥ iti advaita siddhau dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi upapattiḥ atha eka jīva ajñāna kalpitatva upapattiḥ sa ca draṣṭā eka  eva tad nānā tve māna abhāvāt nanu katham eka eva jīvaḥ pratiśarīram aaham sukhī aham duḥkhī aham saṃsārī aham asva apsa am ityādi anubhava virodhāt iti ced na avidyā vaśāt  brahma evekam saṃsarati sa eva jīvaḥ tasya eva pratiśarīram aham ityādi buddhiḥ svāpna śarīre ‘ayam sukhī ayam duḥkhī ati eva yatra buddhiḥ na tu aham sukhī ityādi tad tu nirjīvam yatra tu aham ityādi tad  sa jīvam jāgrat śarīra antare aham iti pratīti avacchedake sa jīva toktiḥ na dvitīyena jīvena sa jīva tvam iti abhipretya tatra māna abhāvāt bandha mokṣa ādi vyavasthā anupapattiḥ tatra mānam iti ced na bandha mokṣa guru śiṣya ādi vyavasthāyāḥ svapnavat yāvat āvidyam upapatteḥ na ca evam tasmin  ekasmin  eva jīve supte samasta jagat aprati itya apātaḥ samaṣṭi abhimāninaḥ  mukhya jīvasya asupta tvāt tasmin   u laya kāle prasupte jagat apratīteḥ antaḥkaraṇa avacchinne jīva ābhāse tu supte tam eva prati jagat apratītiḥ na tu anyān api prati tad upādhīnām apralīna tvāt saṃskārasya kāraṇa ātmanā sthiteḥ na suptasya punar utthāna anupapattiḥ iti uktam etena mama kalpaka tve tava mokṣa artham pravṛtti ayogaḥ tava kalpaka tve tvad kalpitāḥ sat ādi bodha artham tava śabda prayoga ādi anupapattiḥ na ca svapnavat  paryanuyoga ayogaḥ evam apari anuyojya tve nirmaryāda tayā kathā anadhikāra prasaṅgāt iti nirastam caitra maitra ādi sarva abhimāninaḥ  jīvasya kalpaka tvena tava mama ityādi vikalpa anupapatteḥ na api sva kriyā ādi virodhaḥ sva kriyāyāḥ kalpitatva ādi niścaya viraha kālīna tvena paryanuyoga ayogāt atha brahmaṇa eva jīva tvena tasya eva bandha mokṣau  iti tasya nitya muktatva ādi śruti virodhaḥ na mukteḥ sva svarūpa tvena bandhasya ca avidyaka tvena tad virodhaḥ na hi mṛgatṛṣṇakā kalpita udakena svabhāva śuṣkā maru bhūmiḥ ādrā bhavati etena kalpitasya jīvasya kalpakam prati pratyaktvā ayogaḥ tena kalpakena pratyaktvena ajñānāt anyasya anubhavituḥ abhāvāt tathā anubhava apalāpe eka jīvā dvaita śruti ādeḥ api asiddhiḥ iti  nirastam aneka śarīre eka jīva vādasya aṅgīkārāt  na ca tarhi tam eva prati pratyaktva parāktvayoḥ ayogaḥ maitram prati tvam iti dhī viṣayasya caitrasya tam eva prati aham iti dhī viṣayatva ayogaḥ ca iti vācyam bhinna bhinna antaḥkaraṇa abheda adhyāsena tad tad antaḥkaraṇam ādāya pratyaktva parāktvā aham ityādi buddhi viṣayatva vyavasthā upapatteḥ na ca caitra sukha duḥkha ādīnām maitreṇa anusandhānāpattiḥ antaḥkaraṇa avacchinnena avidyā avacchinnena vā na ādyaḥ tatra parasparam bhedāt  na dvitīyaḥ iṣṭa āpatteḥ ata eva caitrasya śukti sākṣātkāreṇa rajata bhrama nivṛttau  anyeṣām api tad nivṛttiḥ syāt iti nirastam antaḥkaraṇa bhedena vyavasthā upapatteḥ nanu evam muktau  api caitra ādi anyatama antaḥkaraṇa avacchedena sākṣātkāre utpanne tad avacchedena eva saṃsāra nivṛttiḥ syāt  na tu tad itara antaḥkaraṇa avacchedena iti ced na tad sākṣātkārasya sa vilāsa mūla ajñāna nivṛtti rūpa tayā tad kāle antaḥkaraṇasya abhāvena vaiṣamyāt  nanu  śrutiṣu ‘avidyāyām antare vartamānā iti ādau  avidyā aramaṇīya caraṇā iti ādau karma bandhaḥ asati sampadya na viduri atyādau sati suṣuptiḥ ‘vedānta vijñāna su niścitā iti ādau tattva jñānam ‘para amṛtāt parimucyanti sarva iti ādau muktiḥ ca cetana dharmaḥ katham anekeṣu ucyata iti ced na ‘anādi māyayā suptaḥ  yadā jīvaḥ prabudhyate ityādi śrutiṣu eka vacana prāpta ekatva virodhena udāhṛta śrutīnām anekatva paratva abhāvāt sārvajanīna bhrama siddha tad anuvādena avirodhāt na ca udāhṛta śruti virodhena ‘iti sṛṣṭau viniścitā iti pūrveṇa ‘sa pūjyaḥ sarva bhūtānām i ati uttareṇa ca virodhena idam eka vacanam ‘yadā nīti paraḥ  rājā ‘svarga kāmaḥ  yajete atyādivat na ekatva param iti eva kim na syāt iti vācyam pratyaktu aparāktva tvam aham ityādi vyavahāra prayojaka antaḥkaraṇa abheda adhyāsa balāt bahutvasya prāpta tvena pūrva uttara vākya udāhṛta śruti ādīn ām atatparatvāt na ca mukta bahu tvam na anyatas  prāptam iti vācyam jīva bahutvasya prāpta tvena mukti aṃśa eva aprāptatva paryavasānāt na ca ekasya eva jīvasya sarva kalpaka tve jīvasya kāraṇa tvam niṣidhya īśvara kāraṇatva vidhāyakaiḥ śruti ādibhiḥ virodhaḥ avidyā cit mātra āśrayatva upapādane nirasiṣyamāṇa tvāt  na ca evam sarvajñatva sarva kartṛtva ādi bodhaka śrutīnām nirviṣaya tvam śuddha caitanye sattvasya eva abhāvāt īśvarasya ca jīva bhinnasya abhāvāt  jīve sārvajñyasya anubhava bādhita tvāt iti vācyam samaṣṭi abhimāninaḥ  jīvasya sarvajñatva sarva kartṛtva ādi svīkārāt na ca anubhava virodhaḥ antaḥkaraṇa abheda adhyāsa balāt tad ananubhavata dviparīta anubhavayoḥ upapatteḥ sarva abhimāninaḥ tu sārvajñya anubhavaḥ asti eva ata eva ‘tāni aham veda sarvāṇi na tvam vettha paraṃtape atyādi upapadyate na ca  ‘a ācāryavān puruṣaḥ  vede ati śruteḥ upadeśam vinā jīvasya tattva jñānam anupapannam upadeṣṭa vyādanyasya caitanyasya abhāvāt ca na upadeśaḥ  yujyata iti vācyam svapna iva upadeṣṭuḥ kalpitasya saṃbhavāt  nanu upadeṣṭṛ tvam na kalpita mātrasya kiṃtu tattva vid tvena kalpitasya tathā ca upadeśāt prāk  tattva jñāne tadā eva mokṣa āpattiḥ upadeśa vaiyarthyam ca na ca evam svapne api tulyam tadā hi śabda viśeṣa vaktṛ tvena eva guru kalpanā na tu upadeśa sādhya jñāna viṣaya viśeṣa vid tvena iti viśeṣāt iti ced na atra api tadvat eva vākya viśeṣa vaktṛ tvena eva tad kalpana saṃbhavat nanu tarhi ‘yat eva bhagavān veda tad eva me brūhī ati ādi śrutiḥ ‘upadekṣyanti te jñānam jñāninaḥ tattva darśina ityādi smṛtiḥ ca
