ayuktā syāt iti  ced na sāmānyatas  mokṣa upayogi jñāna viṣaya vid tvena ajñāta tattva vid tvena tattvam asya ādi vākya vaktṛ tvena vā kalpitasya upadeṣṭṛtva saṃbhavena udāhṛta vākya avirodhāt anyathā tava api mate tattva vid tvena pramita eva ācārya tvena anusaraṇīya iti prathamata eva tattva jñāne tad kāla mokṣa apatti upadeśa vaiyarthya ādikam ca syāt  etena  svādhyāya pravacanābhyām na pramaditavyam ityādi vidhiḥ api bhāvi tattva jñāni kalpaka cetanam pratyeva na ca tasya śiṣyaḥ sva ajñāna kalpita iti jñānataḥ tad mokṣa arthī pravacane pravṛttiḥ yuktā na ca svapnavat  kalpi tattva jñānāt pravṛttiḥ tattva vidaḥ tad jñāna anupapatteḥ iti— nirastam svapna guruvat  kalpita tvena guroḥ aparyanuyojya tvāt  na ca  tattva jñāna hetu tvena vedasya mīmāṃsyatvavat  guroḥ api paryanuyojya tvam iti vācyam tarkeṇa veda iva tad tad rūpa kalpanayā gurau  api tad parihārāt  na ca kathāsu api sat uttara aparisphūrta āvaham tvad kalpitaḥ  na paryanuyojya iti uttaram syāt iti vācyam kathāyāḥ kalpitatva aniścaya kālīna tvena samaya bandha viśeṣa nibandhana tvena ca tādṛś uttarān avakāśāt tasmāt śiṣyavat  guroḥ api kalpita tvāt  svapnavat sarva vyavasthā upapattiḥ atha kalpakaḥ  na niścitā dvaitas  śāstra praṇayana vaiyarthyāt  na api aniścita advaitaḥ śāstrasya pramā mūlakatva abhāva prasaṅgāt iti ced na pramā mūlakatva abhāve api abādhita viṣaya tvena śāstra prāmāṇya upapatteḥ antya pakṣa abhyupagamāt na cāmukaḥ sa iti aniścaye bahu āyāsa sādhya mokṣa artha pravṛtti ayogaḥ prati śarīra m aham ahamikayā ‘baddhaḥ aham i ati niścayasya sva anubhava sākṣika tvena pravṛtti saṃbhavāt  ekena eva jīvena caitra maitra ādi śarīrāṇām sa jīvatva saṃbhavasya prāgaiva ukta tvāt kiṃca caitra maitra ādiṣu kaḥ asau  iti praśnasya kim kenacid  kroḍīkṛtam caitanyam viṣayaḥ kim vā nirasta samasta bhedam na ādyaḥ tasya kalpita tvena akalpaka tvāt na dvitīyaḥ tasya ekatvena tad aniścaya asiddheḥ śuddha citta eka tvena vastutas asaṃsāri tve api āvaraṇa vikṣepa śakti dvaya śāli sva āśrita avidyā vaśāt saṃsāritva kalpakatva mokṣa artha yata mānatva ādi upapattiḥ nanu anādau saṃsāre kasyacid tattva jñānam muktiḥ ca abhūt na vā ādya idānīm saṃsāra upalabdhiḥ na syāt  jīvasya eka tvāt  antye saṃpradāya asaṃbhavena tattva jñāna asaṃbhava iti ced na na hi asāṃpradāyika tvam utpatti virodhi apūrva jātīya anutpatti prasaṅgāt  kiṃtu kāraṇa asattvam tad na idānīm upadeṣṭṛtva ādi kāraṇasya kalpanāsu dṛḍhasya sattvāt  jīva aikyasya pramāṇa siddha tve saṃsāra upalambha eva atas  pūrvam tattva jñāna anutpattau pramāṇam na ca  tattva vid tvena śruti ādi siddhānām śuka vāmadeva ādīnām muktiḥ mā abhūt mama tu bhaviṣyati iti katham śraddadhyāt iti vācyam śāstra prāmāṇya dārḍhyāt iti gṛhāṇa anyathā teṣām mahā anubhāvānām mukta tve api mama bhaviṣyati na vā iti śaṅkā piśācya apravṛtti pratibandha āpatteḥ nanu tarhi śruti prāmāṇya balāt eva tad siddhaḥ  jīva bhedaḥ pūrvam api keṣāṃcid mokṣaḥ ca abhyupeya tām śrūyate hi— atad yaḥ yaḥ  devānām pratyabudhyata sa eva tad abhavat tathā ṛṣīṇām tathā manuṣyāṇām ‘ajaḥ  hi ekaḥ  juṣamāṇaḥ anuśete jahāti enām bhukta bhogām ajaḥ anyaḥ ‘nityaḥ  nityānām cetanaḥ cetanānām ityādi smaryate ca abahavaḥ  jñāna tapasā pūtā mad bhāvam āśritāḥ idam jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ ityādi iti ced na ukta vākyānām sārvalaukika bhrama siddha bheda anuvādaka tvena tad paratva abhāvāt jīva aikya bodhaka vākyānām ca māna antara aprāpta sva artha paratvāt svapna nyāyena bhedasya kalpitatva upapatteḥ ca jñāna stuti parāṇi vākyāni na ātma bhedam pramātum śaknuvanti tātparyavat vākya avirodhena ātāt paryavat vākyānām guṇavādatva upapatteḥ atīta anāgatāḥ ca eva yāvantaḥ sahitāḥ kṣaṇāḥ tatas api ananta guṇitā jīvānām rāśayaḥ pṛthak  ityādi smṛtiḥ api jīva upādhi bheda anuvādaka tayā vyākhyeyā tasmāt avidyā upādhikaḥ  jīva eka eva iti siddham iti advaita siddhau eka jīva ajñāna kalpitatva upapattiḥ atha avidyā lakṣaṇa upapattiḥ atha kā iyam avidyā na tāvat anādi bhāva rūpa tve sati jñāna nivartyā sā iti sādi śukti ādi avacchinna caitanyauvāraka ajñāne avyāpteḥ tasya anāditva abhāvāt abhāva upādāna ajñāne ca bhāvatva abhāvāt tatra avyāptiḥ abhāvasya bhāva upādānaka tve asatyasya api satya upādānaka tvam syāt  ajñāna anupādānaka tve tasya jñānāt nivṛttiḥ na syāt    iti atra brūmaḥ rūpya upādāna ajñānam api anādi caitanya āśrita tvāt anādi eva udīcyam śukti ādikam tu tad avacchedakam iti na tatra avyāptiḥ bhāva tvam ca atra abhāva vilakṣaṇatva mātram vivakṣitam atas  āropita abhāva upādāna ajñāne api abhāva vilakṣaṇatva svīkārān na avyāptiḥ na ca sajātīya upādanakatva niyamaḥ anyathā asatyasya api satyam upādānam syāt iti vācyam sarvathā sājātye sarvathā vaijātye vā upādāna upādeya bhāvā darśanena tathā sa ajātyasya vaijātyasya vā āpādayitum aśakyatvāt  na hi kārya akāra kāraṇa ākārataḥ api abhede kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ satyasya tu asatyā upādāna tve satyasya nivṛtti sambhavena tad upādeyasya asatyasya api nivṛttiḥ na syāt  upādāna nivṛttim antareṇa upādeyā nivṛtteḥ atas  na satyam asati asya upādānam satyasya apariṇāmi tvāt ca vivartā adhiṣṭhāna tvam tu abhyupeyata eva na ca brahma ajñāne brahmaṇaḥ  vṛtti avyāpyatva pakṣe avyāptiḥ tasya jñāna anivartya tvāt iti vācyam sva rūpa sat upādhimat tad viṣaya ka jñāna nivartya tvasya tad mate api bhāvāt  upapāditam ca etad  dṛśyatva hetu upapādane atha aupādhika bhrama upādāna ajñāne brahma sākṣātkāra anantara vidyamāna jīvanmuktā jñāne ca jñāna nivartyatva abhāvāt avyāptiḥ tayoḥ jñāna nivartya tve upādhi kāla jīvanmukti kālayoḥ eva jñāna prāgabhāvavat tad nivṛtti āpattiḥ iti ced na upādhi prārabdha karmaṇoḥ pratibandha kayoḥ abhāva vilambena nivṛtti vilambe api tayoḥ jñāna nivartya tvānapāyāt  na hi kvacid avilambena janakasya kvacid  pratibandhena vilambe janakatā apaiti na ca tarhi jñāte api tatra ajñāta iti vyavahāra āpattiḥ tādṛś vyavahāre āvaraṇa śakti mat ajñānasya kāraṇa tvena tad āvaraṇa śakti abhāvāt eva īdṛś vyavahāra an āpatteḥ yathā ca etad tathā upapādayiṣyate na ca avidyā caitanya sambandhe ativyāptiḥ sākṣāt jñāna nivartya tvasya vivakṣita tvāt  tasya api avidyā ātmaka tvāt vā na ca viśeṣaṇa antara vaiyarthyam anādi padasya uttara jñāna nivartye pūrva jñāne bhāva padasya jñāna prāc abhāve jñāna janya kārya prāgabhāve ca ati vyāpti vāraka tvena sārthaka tvāt  jñāna tvena sākṣāt tad nivartya tvam tu bhavati lakṣaṇa antaram nanu asambhavaḥ kalpita tvena doṣa janya dhī mātra śarīrasya ajñānasya jñāna nivartyasya abhāva vilakṣaṇasya ca rūpya vadana āditva ayogāt iti ced na kalpitatva mātram hi na doṣa janya dhī mātra śarīra tve sādi tve vā tantram kintu pratibhāsa kalpaka samāna kālīnakalpakavat tvam sādi kalpakavat tvam vidyā nivṛttya prayukta nivṛtti pratiyogi tvam prāc abhāva pratiyogi tvam vā tantram na ca tad prakṛte asti jñāna nivartyatva samāna adhikaraṇa abhāva vilakṣaṇa tvena avidyāyāḥ sāditva sādhane ‘ajām ekām ‘ana ādi māyaye ati ādi śāstra virodhaḥ anāditva sādhakena jñāna nivartya tve sati bhāva vilakṣaṇa tvena sat pratipakṣaḥ ca bhāva tvasya upādhitvañca na ca abhāva vilakṣaṇa avidyā ādau bhāva vilakṣaṇa tvam asambhavi paraspara virodhāt iti vācyam bhāvatva abhāva tvayoḥ bādhaka sattvena tṛtīya prakāratva siddhau paraspara viraha vyāpakatva rūpa virodha asiddheḥ paraspara viraha vyāpyatva rūpaḥ tu virodhaḥ  na eka viraheṇa aparam ākṣipati na hi gaḥtva virahaḥ aśva tvam ākṣipati iti uktam na ca ātma vadana ādeḥ abhāva vilakṣaṇasya anivartya tvam ātma tvasya eva upādhi tvāt na ca atyanta abhāva anyonya abhāvayoḥ sādhya avyāptiḥ adhikaraṇa atiriktasya anivartyasya atyanta abhāva ādeḥ anabhyupagamāt  na ca tucche sādhya avyāptiḥ abhāva vilakṣaṇatva rūpa sādhana avacchinna sādhya vyāpakatva upapatteḥ kiñca sādi tvam anādi tvam vā na nivartyatva anivartya tvayoḥ prayojakam dhvaṃsa prāgabhāvayoḥ tad abhāvāt na api bhāvatva viśeṣitam tad tathā abhāve tad asattvena bhinna bhinna prayojaka kalpanā patteḥ bhāva nivṛtti anivṛttyoḥ eva tayoḥ prayojaka tve ca bhāva vilakṣaṇa avidyā ādau tābhyām tayoḥ anāpādanāt tasmāt nāśasāmagrī sannipāta asannipātau  eva nivartyatva anivartya tvayoḥ prayojakau  iti mantavyam tau ca phala bala kalpyau  iti na kaḥ api doṣaḥ api ca yadi avidyā ādeḥ abhāva vilakṣaṇatva samāna adhiraṇa anādi tvena ātmavat anivartya tvam sādhyate tarhi bhāva vilaṇa tvena prāgabhāvavat nivartya tvam eva kim na sādhyate na ca dhvaṃsa atyantānyonya abhāveṣu vyabhicāraḥ adhikaraṇa atireke teṣām api nivartya ātvā abhyupagamāt na ca ajñānasya yāvat sva viṣaya dhīrūpa sākṣi sattvam anuvṛtti niyamena nivṛtti yoga iti   vācyam duḥkha śukti rūpī ādeḥ sva bhāsake sākṣiṇi sati eva nivṛtti abhyupagamena sa akṣi bha āsyānām yāvat sākṣi sattvam avasthāna niyama anabhyupagamāt kiñca kevala cit mātram na sākṣi kintva vidyā vṛtti upahitam tathā ca asthira avidyā vṛtti upahitasya sākṣiṇaḥ api asthira tvena tad sattva paryantam avasthāne api avidyā ādeḥ nivṛttiḥ upapadyate na ca vṛtti anupadhāna daśāyāma vidyā ādeḥ śukti rūpīvat asattva āpattiḥ sādi padārtha eva eta adṛś niyamāt  dhārāvāhika avidyā vṛtti paramparāyā ati sūkṣmāyāḥ  abhyupagamāt ca iti śivam yad vā bhrama upādāna tvam ajñāna lakṣaṇam idam ca lakṣaṇam viśva bhrama upādāna māyā adhiṣṭhānam brahma iti pakṣe na tu brahma mātra upādānatva pakṣe brahma sahita avidyā upādānatva pakṣe vā atas  brahmaṇi na ati vyāptiḥ itaratra tu pakṣe pariṇāmi tvena acetana tvena vā bhrama upādānam viśeṣaṇīyam iti na doṣaḥ na vā abhāva āropa nivartaka pramāni vartye avyāptiḥ tasya api bhrama upādāna tvāt  nanu bhrame bhāva vilakṣaṇa ajñāna upādānaka tvam na ghaṭate bhramasya bhāva vilakṣaṇa tve upādeyatva ayogāt bhāva tve ca bhāva upādānakatva niyamāt iti ced na ajñānasya bhramasya ca bhāva vilakṣaṇa tve api upādāna upādeya bhāva upapatteḥ na hi bhāva tvam upādāna tve upādeya tve vā prayojakam ātmani tad adarśanāt  kintu anvayi kāraṇa tvam upādāna tve tantram sādi tvam upādeya tve tad ubhayam ca na bhāvatva niyatam ata upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ api na bhāvatva niyataḥ na ca evam dhvaṃsasya api upādeyatva āpattiḥ iṣṭa āpatteḥ na ca evam jñāna prāgabhāvasya eva bhrama upādāna tvam astu kim abhāva vilakṣaṇa ajñāna upādāna kalpanena iti vācyam prāgabhāvasya pratiyogi mātra janakatva niyamena bhramam prati janakatvasya api asiddheḥ tad viśeṣa rūpa upādāna tvasya eva dūra nirasta tvāt  atas  sat vilakṣaṇayoḥ ajñāna bhramayoḥ yukta upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ bhramasya ca sat vilakṣaṇa tvam uktam vakṣyate ca na ca evam ajñāna anuviddha tayā bhramasya pratītyāpattiḥ mṛd anuviddha tayā ghaṭasya iva iti vācyam yad  yad upādānakam tad  tad anuviddha tayā eva pratīyata iti vyāpti asiddheḥ na hi ghaṭa upādānakam rūpam ghaṭa iti pratīyate prakṛti dvi aṇuka ādi anuviddha tayā pratīteḥ paraiḥ api anabhyupagamāt  kenacid dharmeṇa tad anuvedhaḥ tu prakṛte api iṣṭa eva na ca yāvanti jñānāni tāvanti ajñānāni iti pakṣe bhrama apūrvaka pramāni vartye ajñāne avyāptiḥ bhrama upāda āna tā yogya tvasya vivakṣita tvāt  sahakāri vaikalyāt  kārya anudaye api yogyatā anapāyāt  atha yogya tā avacche ka rūpa paricaye katham tad grahaṇam prathama lakṣaṇasya eva yogya tāvacchedaka tvāt  ekam eva ajñānam iti pakṣe tu tatra bhrama upādāna tvam akṣatam eva na ca evam śukti jñānena eva ajñāna nāśe mokṣa āpattiḥ tasya avasthā viśeṣa nāśakatva aṅgīkārāt vyutpāditam ca etad asmābhiḥ siddhānta bindau jñāna tvena rūpeṇa sākṣāt jñāna nivartya tvam vā tad lakṣaṇam iti ca prāk uktam eva tasmāt na avidyā lakṣaṇa asaṃbhava iti sarvam avadātam iti advaita siddhau  avidyā lakṣaṇa upapattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde tatra pratyakṣa pramāṇa upapattiḥ tatra ca ajñāne aaham ajñau mām anyam ca na jānāmī ati pratyakṣam atvat uktam artham na jānāmī ati viśeṣataḥ pratyakṣam ‘etauvantam kālam sukham aham asva apsam na kiṃcid avediṣa am iti parāmarśa siddham sauṣupta pratyakṣam ca pramāṇam na ca aham arthasya ajñāna anāśraya tvena katham ayam pratyayaḥ bhāva rūpa ajñāna pakṣe upapadyata iti vācyam ajñāna āśrayī bhūta caitanye antaḥkaraṇa tādātmya adhyāsena eka āśrayatva saṃbandhena upapatteḥ ata eva jaḍe āvaraṇa kṛtya abhāvāt ‘ghaṭam na jānāmī atyādi pratīteḥ jñāna abhāva viṣaya tve prakṛte api tathā astu iti nirastam tad tad avacchinna caitanyasya eva ajñāna āśraya tve tatra api tad vyavahāra upapatteḥ na ca sa akṣivedye sukha duḥkha ajñāna ādau prātibhāsike ca bhāva rūpa ajñāna abhāvena tatra na jānāmi iti pratītiḥ katham upapadyata iti vācyam svasmin vidyamāne sa akṣivedye sukha ādau sva bhrama siddhe rūpya ādau ca ana jānāmī ati vyavahāra asaṃbhavāt  para sukha ādau ana jānāmī ati vyavahārasya parokṣa jñāna nivartyena pramātṛ gata ajñānena eva upapatteḥ ata eva parokṣa jñānena pramātṛ gata ajñāne nāśite api viṣaya gata ajñāna sattvena ‘na jānāmi iti vyavahāra āpattiḥ iti nirastam pramātṛ gata ajñāna kāryasya ana jānāmī ati vyavahārasya viṣaya gata ajñānena āpādayitum aśakyatvāt nanu—bhāva rūpa ajñāna viṣaya tvena abhimatasya ‘aham ajña iti pratyayasya ‘mayi jñānam na astī ati jñāna abhāva viṣayāt pratyayāt  ‘aghaṭam bhū talam i ati pratyayasya ‘ghaṭaḥ  na astī ati pratyayāt iva viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva vyatyāsam vinā icchā dveṣa abhāva jñānayoḥ iva viṣaya bheda apratītiḥ iti ced  satyam dharmi pratiyogi jñāna ajñānābhyām jñāna sāmānya abhāva jñānasya vyāhata tvena ‘mayi jñānam na astī atyasya api bhāva rūpa ajñāna viṣaya tvena viṣaya bheda apratīteḥ yukta tvāt  tathā hi ‘mayi jñānam na astī ati pratītiḥ ‘vāyau rūpam na astī ati pratītivat yāvat viśeṣa abhāva anya sāmānya abhāva viṣayā sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tāka yāvat viśeṣa abhāva viṣayā vā abhyupeyā tathā ca tad kāraṇībhūta dharmi pratiyogi jñāna ajñānābhyām katham na vyāghātaḥ yad kiñcidviśeṣa abhāvasya sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tākatva abhāvāt abhāva jñāne pratiyogi aṃśe prakārībhūta dharmasya eva pratiyogi ta avacchedaka tvāt  anyathā sāmānya abhāva siddhiḥ na syāt  yāvat viśeṣa abhāva anya sāmānya abhāva anabhyupagame api ayam doṣaḥ yad kiñcidviśeṣa abhāvasya sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tve ghaṭavatī api bhū tale ‘nirghaṭam bhū talam i ati pratītiḥ syāt  ‘vāyau rūpam na asti ‘puraḥ deśe rajatam na astī ati ādi āpta vākya janya pratīti anantaram api tad tad saṃśaya nivṛttiḥ na syāt  eka viśeṣa abhāva bodhane api viśeṣa antaram ādāya saṃśaya upapatteḥ atha bhāva bodhe prakārībhūta dharmasya avacchedaka tvam pūrvānupasthitam api saṃsarga maryādayā śābda bodhe anyatra ca bhāsate na hi avacchedaka tvasya kha rūpa saṃbandha viśeṣasya grahe anyā sāmagrī klṛptā tathā ca tad tad viśeṣa abhāvānām tad tad viśeṣa avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvāt sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvam yāvat viśeṣa abhāva kūṭe vā vyāsa jya vṛtti tad vyatirikta sāmānya abhāve vā pratyeka viśrāntam iti tādṛś abhāva pratīteḥ yāvat viśeṣa pratīti virodhi tvāt  kutaḥ viśeṣa saṃśaya ādiḥ iti ced  satyam prakṛte api jñānatva sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogitākā bhāva pratītiḥ yāvat jñāna viśeṣa virodhinī iti katham tad tad kāraṇatva abhimata jñāna viśeṣe sati sā na vyāhanyate tathā ca klṛpta abhāva pratīti vailakṣaṇye avaśya kalpye lāghavāt viṣayasya eva abhāva vailakṣaṇyam kalpayitum ucitam viṣaya availakṣaṇye pratīti vailakṣaṇya ayogāt viṣaya ajñānam anubhūya ca puruṣaḥ tad nivṛtti artham vicāre pravartata iti sarva anubhava siddham tad yadi jñāna viśeṣa abhāvaḥ  ana jānāmī ati pratīteḥ viṣayaḥ tadā jñāte api tathā prati iti āpātaḥ tad vicāra artham ca pravṛttiḥ syāt  sāmānya abhāve ca bādhakam uktam eva tasmāt abhāva vilakṣaṇam eva ajñānam ‘mayi jñānam na asti aham ajña ityādi dhī viṣaya iti siddham nanu abhāva vilakṣaṇam api ajñānam ana jānāmī ati jñāna virodhi tvena eva bhāsate moha ādi pade api pralaya ādi padavat tad anullekha mātram uktam ca vivaraṇe aajñānam iti dvayasa apekṣa jñāna paryudāsena abhidhāna ādi ati anyathā jñānasya ajñāna virodhi tvam aprāmāṇikam syāt  tathā ca virodha nirūpaka jñānasya jñāna ajñānābhyām tava api katham na vyāghātaḥ evam nirviṣaya ajñāna apratīteḥ viṣaya jñāna ajñānayoḥ api vyāghāta āpādanīyaḥ tathā ca ‘yatra ubhayoḥ samaḥ  doṣaḥ parihāraḥ api vā samaḥ na ekaḥ paryanuyoktavyaḥ tādṛś artha vicāraṇe iti nyāyena ubhaya pariharaṇīyasya vyāghātasya jñāna abhāva pakṣa eva apānam anucitam iti ced na pramāṇa vṛtti nivarti asya api bhāva rūpa ajñānasya sākṣi vedyasya virodhi nirūpaka jñāna tad vyāvartaka viṣaya grāhakeṇa sākṣiṇā tad sādhakena tad anāśāt vyāhati anupapatteḥ ajñāna grahe viṣaya gocara pramāpekṣāyām vyāhatiḥ syāt eva sā ca na asti tad uktam vivaraṇe  sarvam vastu jñāta tayā ajñāta tayā vā sākṣi caitanyasya viṣaya eva i ti na ca evaṃ jñāna abhāva pakṣe api viṣaya ādi jñānam sākṣi rūpam ana jānāmī ati dhīḥ tu pramāṇa vṛtti abhāva viṣaya iti na vyāhatiḥ iti vācyam bhāva rūpa ajñānasya sākṣāt  sa akṣi vedya tvena tad avacchedaka viṣaya ādeḥ tad dvārā sa akṣi vedyatva saṃbhave api abhāvasya anupalabdhi gamya tvena sākṣāt  sa akṣi vedyatva abhāvāt na tad dvārā tad avacchedaka viṣaya ādeḥ sākṣi vedya tvam iti vaiṣamyāt  yadi api jñānam sākṣi vedyam tad dvārā tad avacchedakaḥ  viṣayaḥ ca sa akṣivedyaḥ tathā api jñāna abhāvaḥ  na sa akṣivedyaḥ tasya anupalabdha tvāt utpannam ca jñānam sākṣāt  sākṣi vedyam tasmin  ca utpanne tad viṣayaḥ api sphurati iti kutaḥ jñāna abhāvaḥ api ajñāna viśeṣaṇa tayā tu anutpannam api jñānam sākṣi vedyam iti na doṣa sāmyam na ca avacchedakasya viṣaya ādeḥ prāc ajñāne katham tad viśiṣṭa ajñāna jñānam viśeṣaṇa jñāna adhīna tvāt viśiṣṭa jñānasya iti vācyam viśeṣaṇa jñānasya viśiṣṭa jñāna janaka tve māna abhāvāt pratiyogitva abhāva tvayoḥ pūrvānupasthitayoḥ api tārkikaiḥ abhāva bodhe prakārībhūya bhāna abhyupagamāt tathā api viśeṣaṇa tāvacchedaka prakāraka jñānam vinā katham viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya buddhiḥ iti ced na viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya buddhi tvena viśeṣaṇa tāvacchedaka prakāraka jñāna tvena ca kārya kāraṇa bhāve māna abhāvāt pratyakṣatva ādi rūpeṇa pṛthak  pṛthak  klṛpta kārya kāraṇa bhāvena eva upapatteḥ viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya buddhi tvasya artha samāja siddha tvāt iha ca sāmagrī tulya tvena ‘viśeṣye viśeṣaṇam tatra ca viśeṣaṇa antaraḥ am iti nyāyena viśiṣṭa vaiśiṣṭya jñāna saṃbhavāt anyathā tārkikāṇām api īśvarasya bhrānti jña tvam na syāt  bhrama viṣayasya svātantryeṇa grahe bhrāntatva āpattyā bhrama avacchedaka tayā eva tad rahaṇam vācyam tathā ca kva prāc tad avacchedaka graha niyamaḥ grahaṇa sāmagrī tulya tvam ca prakṛte api samam nanu śravaṇa ādi sādhya mokṣa hetu brahma jñāna prāgabhāvasya sattvena tad jñānam tvayā api vācyam tathā ca tatra api vyāhatiḥ tulya iti ced na śravaṇa ādi sādhya mokṣa hetu brahma jñāna rūpasya pratiyoginaḥ  jñāna ajñānābhyām vyāhati abhāvāt  na hi śravaṇa ādi sādhyatva mokṣa hetutva ādi prakāraka brahma jñāna jñānam brahma jñānam api sat  śravaṇa ādi sādhyam mokṣa hetuḥ vā yena tasmin sati tādṛś jñāna prāc abhāvaḥ  vyāhanyeta nanu evaṃ ‘na jānāmī ati dhiyaḥ  jñāna abhāva viṣaya tve api na pratiyogi jñāna ādinā vyāhatiḥ sāmānyatas  viṣaya pratiyogi jñāne api viśeṣataḥ tad abhāva saṃbhavāt anyathā prāgabhāva dhīḥ na syāt  tad pratiyogi viśeṣasya sāmānya dharmam vinā viśeṣataḥ  jñātum aśakya tvāt iti ced na viśeṣa jñāna abhāve hi viśeṣa jñānatva avacchinnam pratiyogi iti tasya jñāne sa viśeṣaḥ api jñāta eva iti viśeṣa jñāna abhāva vyāghātāt yad kiñcidviśeṣa abhāvaḥ ca na sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogitāka iti uktam pratiyogi ta avacchedaka prakāraka jñāna abhāvena prāc abhāva pratītiḥ asiddhā eva nanu pratiyogi ta avacchedaka prakāraka jñānam na abhāva jñāne kāraṇam kiṃtu abhāva jñāne bhāsamāna pratiyogi vṛtti dharma prakārakam jñānam sāmānya lakṣaṇa apratyāsatti abhyupagame tu pratiyogi viṣaya tvam api tasya adhikam itarathā tu tad eva iṣṭa vṛtti sāmānya dharma prakāraka jñānam iva asiddha vyakti viṣaya icchā kṛtyoḥ na ca pratiyogita anavacchedaka dharmeṇa katham pratiyogitā gṛhyatām iti vācyam viśeṣa avacchinnāyā vyāpteḥ iva sāmānyena grahaṇa saṃbhavāt  tathā hi ‘idam abhidheyavat  prameya ādi ati anumāne ‘yatra prameyam tatra abhidheyam i ati vyāpti grahaṇa samaye vṛttim aprameyatva avacchedena eva sāmānādhikaraṇya rūpa vyāpti sattve api tasyāḥ prameyatva rūpeṇa eva grahaṇam na tu vṛttim aprameya tvena gauravāt  vṛttimattva viśeṣaṇasya vyabhicāra āvāraka tvena vaiyarthyāt ca avṛttiṣu sādhya sāmānādhikaraṇya rūpa vyāpya bhāvavat sādhya abhāva sā mānādhikaraṇya rūpa vyabhicārasya api abhāvāt vyartha viśeṣaṇatva rahita tve sati vyabhicāri vyāvṛttatva mātreṇa eva vyāpya tāvacchedakatva saṃbhavāt ca tathā ca yathā vṛttim aprameya gatā api vyāptiḥ prameya tvena eva gṛhyate tathā tad tad nīla ādi vyakti gata apratiyogitā nīlatva ādi rūpeṇa gṛhyata iti na kācid anupapattiḥ evam ca ‘iha idānīm ghaṭaḥ  na astī ati pratītiḥ iva ghaṭa upādāna gata tad prāgabhāva viṣayā ‘mayi jñānam na asti iti pratītiḥ api pramātṛ gata tad prāgabhāva viṣaya iti na kā api anupapattiḥ ita ced na abhāva jñāne pratiyogi aṃśe bhāsamānasya dharmasya eva pratiyogi ta avacchedaka tayā yad kiṃcid viśeṣa abhāvasya sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tve ghaṭavatī api bhū tale ‘nirghaṭam bhū talam i ati ghaṭa jñānavatī api svasmianmayi ghaṭa jñānam na astī ati ca pratīteḥ āpatteḥ pūrva ukta doṣāt  yad kiṃcid ghaṭa jñānam ghaṭa abhāva jñāne pratibandhakam iti tu jñāna jñāne api tulyam udāhṛta vyāpti grahaṇe tu bādhaka abhāvāt sāmānya avacchede api na doṣaḥ atha evam prāc abhāva pratītiḥ eva na syāt  na syāt eva ‘ghaṭaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti pratīteḥ dhātu artha bhaviṣyat tā viṣaya tvena prāgabhāva aviṣaya tvāt anyathā dina antara utpatsyamāna ghaṭe etad dina vṛtti prāgabhāva pratiyogi tvena ‘adya ghaṭaḥ  bhaviṣyatī ati dhī prasaṅgaḥ bhaviṣya tvam ca pratiyogi tad dhvaṃsa anādhāra kāla saṃbandhi tvam dhvaṃsa tvam ca prāgabhāvān aṅgīkartṛmate kādācid ka abhāva tvam eva tad aṅgīkartṛ mate api pratiyogi ajanaka kādācid ka abhāva tvam janaka tvam ca svarūpa saṃbandha viśeṣaḥ na prāc abhāva ghaṭitaḥ prāc abhāvasya ajanakatva āpatteḥ anyathā ātma āśrayāt atas  prāgabhāvam aṅgīkurvataḥ api tad pratyakṣa tvam durlabham tam anaṅgīkurvataḥ tu na kā api hāniḥ aiha idānīm ghaṭaḥ  na asti iti ati pratītiḥ tu sāmānya dharma vacchinna pratiyogi tāka tad kāla avacchinna yāvat viśeṣa abhāva viṣayā samaya viśeṣasya api abhāva avacchedaka tvāt  anyathā ‘āt yakṣaṇe ghaṭaḥ  nīrūpa ityādi pratītiḥ na syāt  atha asmin pakṣe sāmānya abhāvaḥ  na siddhyet iti ced  prāc abhāva abhyupagame api tulyam etad  sāmānya abhāva prāgabhāvayoḥ sunda upasundayoḥ iva paraspara parāhata tvāt  tathā hi prāc abhāva siddhau viśeṣa abhāvasya api sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvāt na tāvat mātra pramāṇaka sāmānya abhāva siddhiḥ sāmānya abhāva siddhau ca viśeṣa abhāvasya sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tākatva abhāvāt kādācid ka abhāvasya ca sāmānya abhāvatva ayogāt na sāmānya dharma avacchinna pratiyogi tāka viśeṣa pratīti mātra śaraṇa prāgabhāva siddhiḥ iti na tad ubhayam api vipaścitām cetasi camatkāram āvahati nanu yāvat viśeṣa abhāva niścaye api ‘rūpam vāyu vṛtti na vā ‘vāyu rūpavān na ve ati rūpa abhāva sandehāt niścite ca saṃśaya ayogāt yāvat viśeṣa abhāva anya sāmānya abhāva siddhiḥ ata etāvanti eva rūpāṇi iti niścaya daśāyām etādṛśa saṃśayasya ananubhūyamāna tvena tad aniścaya daśāyām eva etādṛśaḥ saṃśayaḥ  vācyaḥ tathā ca ‘rūpa tvam pārthiva apya taijasa rūpa tritaya atirikta vṛtti bhaviṣyatī atyadhika saṃbhāvanayā niściteṣu eva saṃśayaḥ ukta saṃbhāvanā viraha saha kṛta niścayasya eva pratibandhaka tvāt iti ced na evam pratibandhaka kalpane māna abhāvāt ukta saṃbhāvanā viraha daśāyām api etādṛśa saṃśaya darśanāt ca nanu yathā yāvat viśeṣa abhāvebhyaḥ atiriktaḥ sāmānya abhāvaḥ  rūpasya saṃśaya koṭiḥ tathā rūpa sāmānyam api yāvat viśeṣebhyaḥ atiriktam saṃśaya koṭiḥ na abhyupagantum śakyate tathā ca katham rūpasya saṃśaya koṭi tvam sarva rūpa abhāva niścayāt yadi tu nīla pīta ādi abhāva tvena niścaye api rūpa abhāva tvena aniścayāt rūpa asaṃśaya iti brūṣe tadā kim sāmānya abhāvena rūpatva avacchinna pratiyogi tākā bhāva tvena saṃśaya saṃbhavāt  dharmi kalpanātaḥ  dharma kalpanāyā laghu tvena yāvat viśeṣa abhāvānām eva rūpatva avacchinna pratiyogi tākatva kalpanāt  atas  na yad kiṃcid abhāvam ādāya ‘ghaṭaḥ  nīrūpa iti pratīti prasaṅga iti ced na yāvat viśeṣa abhāveṣu yad rūpatva avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvam tad  pratyekam viśrāntam vyāsa jya vṛtti vā ādye yad kiṃcid abhāvam ādāya ‘ghaṭaḥ  nīrūpa iti pratīti prasaṅgaḥ dvitīye tad tad rūpatva avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvasya avyāsa jya vṛtti svabhāva tvena tad vyatiriktam rūpatva avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvam vyāsa jya vṛtti kalpanīyam tad varam rūpatva avacchinna pratiyogitāka eka eva abhāvaḥ kalpyate mama ekaḥ abhāvaḥ rūpatva avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvam ca iti vastu dvayam kalpyam tava tu rūpatva avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvam tasya ca vyāsa jya vṛtti tvena bahuṣu abhāveṣu pratyekam saṃbandhā iti bahu kalpyam ‘dharmi kalpanātaḥ  dharma kalpanāyā laghutvam iti nyāyaḥ tu kalpanīya ādhikya apekṣaḥ kiṃca ghaṭa dvaye yāvat viśeṣa abhāva sattve api rūpa sāmānya abhāva budhi anudayāt aika adhikaraṇyā avacchedena api abhāvā viśeṣaṇīyāḥ tathā ca ati gauravam api ca vyāsajya vṛtti dharma grahe yāvat āśraya grahaḥ tad bheda grahaḥ ca hetuḥ agṛhīteṣu bhinna tayā vā agṛhīteṣu vastra ādiṣu dvitva ādi buddhi anudayāt tathā ca yāvat abhāva tad bheda agrahe prathamata eva nīrūpa iti dhīḥ na syāt  vyāsa jya vṛtti sāmānya pratiyogi tāka tvasya agrahaṇāt  atas  sāmānya abhāvasya prāmāṇika tvāt  katham tad parāhatiḥ iti ced  atra brūmaḥ evam tarhi sāmānya prakāreṇa viśeṣa abhāva apratīteḥ jñāna viśeṣa prāgabhāvaḥ  na jānāmi iti dhiyaḥ  jñānatva avacchinna pratiyogitākaḥ  na viṣaya iti siddham naḥ samīhitam na hi prāc abhāvaḥ api kaścid sāmānya abhāvaḥ asti yena tad pratiyogitā sāmānya dharmeṇa avacchidyeta viśeṣa abhāva pratiyogi tā tu tad tad haṭatva ādinā viśeṣeṇa avacchidyate na ca tena tena rūpeṇa bhaviṣyat dhaṭa ādi jñātum śakyam tad janma anantaram tu tad tad rūpeṇa tad jñāna saṃbhave api na prāgabhāva dhīḥ pratyakṣā syāt  tadānīm prāgabhāva asattvāt pratyakṣasya viṣaya janya tvāt  sāmānya prakāraka jñānam ca na viśeṣa abhāva jñāne hetuḥ iti uktam pratiyogi ta avacchedaka prakāraka pratiyogi jñānasya abhāvatva prakāraka abhāva jñāne hetu tvāt  tasya anumāna gamya tve api na jānāmi iti dhiyaḥ aparokṣāyāḥ tad viṣayatva ayogāt avyabhicāri liṅga ādi abhāvāt tad anumānam api dūra nirastam eva nanu ‘idam mā bhūt itī acchā viṣaya tayā tad siddhiḥ na prāgabhāvasya svarūpataḥ asādhya tvena pratiyogi janaka vighaṭanena tad saṃbandhasya iva atyanta abhāva saṃbandhasya api sādhya tvāt tena eva anyathā siddheḥ atha utpannasya dvitīya kṣaṇe punar utpatti abhāvāt tad pūrvakṣaṇe sāmagrya bhāvaḥ  vācyaḥ sa ca prāgabhāva abhāvāt eva anya hetūnām sattvāt iti ced na sāmayikā atyanta abhāvena eva anyathā siddheḥ utpannasya eva sva utpatti virodhi tvāt ca apica sāmagrī kārya sattve prayojikā na tu tasya ādya kāla saṃbandha rūpa utpattau  api ādya kāla saṃbandhaḥ  hi sva samāna kālīna padārtha dhvaṃsa anādhāra kāla ādhāra tvam tatra sāmagrī kāryasya kāla ādhāratva aṃśa mātre prayojikā na tu viśeṣaṇa aṃśe api tasya tādṛś padārtha dhvaṃsa sāmagrī virahāt eva siddheḥ pākaja rūpa ādi bhedaḥ api agni saṃyoga bhedāt pūrvarūpa ādi dhvaṃsa bhedāt vā na tu prāc abhāva bhedāt  pratiyogi bhedam vinā prāc abhāva bheda ayogāt ca na api upādānatva vyavasthā tatra mānam tantutva ādinā eva tad siddheḥ anyathā prāgabhāvasya saṃbandhi viśeṣaḥ api kutas  siddhyet  na ca tad atyanta abhāvavataḥ katham tad upādāna tvam saṃbandha antareṇa tvayā api abhyupagamāt samayā avaccheda tad anavacchedābhyām vailakṣaṇya abhyupagamāt ca iti alam ati vistareṇa evam sāmānya abhāvaḥ api gaurava parāhata eva tathā hi sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvam abhāvaḥ tasya ca tad tad adhikaraṇa saṃbandhā iti trayam vā kalpyatām klṛpta tad tad adhikaraṇa saṃbandhānām eka adhikaraṇa vṛttitva avacchedena siddhānām abhāvānām sāmānya avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvam tasya ca vyāsajya vṛtti tvam iti dvayam vā kalpyatām tatra uttaraḥ pakṣa eva prekṣāvadbhyaḥ  rocate ādi akṣaṇe ‘ghaṭaḥ  nīrūpa iti pratīteḥ sarva siddha tvāt yāvat āśraya tadbheda grahasya dvitva ādi grahe hetu tve api ukta pratiyogita agrahe hetutva anabhyupagamāt kārya unneya dharmāṇām yathā akāryam unnayanāt  na ca evam ati lāghavāt  klṛptānām adhikaraṇānām eva abhāva dhī hetu tvam astu kim viśeṣa abhāvaiḥ api iti vācyam asmākam iṣṭa āpatteḥ ghaṭa abhāvaḥ  na iti ādau  atirikta abhāvasya tvayā api anabhyupagamena bhāvasya api abhāvatva prakāraka pramā hetutvasya ubhaya vādi siddha tvāt yad api kaścid āha pratiyogi ta avacchedaka bhedasya abhāva bheda niyāmaka tvāt viśeṣa abhāva ani sāmānya abhāva siddhiḥ anyathā abhāva bheda asiddheḥ pratiyogi bhedasya abhāva bhedaka tve eka ghaṭa pratiyogikasya prāgabhāva ādi catuṣṭayasya abheda prasaṅgāt  avacchedaka bhedāt tu tad bhade na kaḥ api doṣaḥ kvacid tādātmyasya kvacid saṃsargasya kvacid  pūrva aparaka ālīna taddhaṭatva ādeḥ ca bhedāt  iti tad na saṃsarga pratiyogi viśeṣaṇa sādhāraṇasya ekasya avacchedaka tvasya durvaca tvāt  tādātmya ādeḥ ca pratiyogita avacchedaka tve māna abhāvāt bheda siddhiḥ tu bhāvavat abhāvasya api viruddha dharma adhyāsāt eva avacchedaka bhedasya abhāva bheda niyāmaka tvam liṅga vidhayā tad jñāpaka tvam eva vācyam na tu tad janaka tvam tad ca na vipakṣa bādhaka tarka abhāvena sāmāna adhikaraṇya abhāvena ca vyāpteḥ eva asiddheḥ ata eva tad itara dharma avacchinna pratiyogi tāka tvam tad avacchinna pratiyogitākā anyatva vyāpyam iti api nirastam evam ca āvṛttīnām gagana ādīnām sama niyatānām vā anyeṣām dharmāṇām eka eva atyanta abhāvaḥ yugapad vinaṣṭānām utpannānām vā samāna deśānām asati bādhake eka eva dhvaṃsaḥ prāgabhāvaḥ  vā vyadhikaraṇa dharma avacchinna pratiyogitākaḥ api ced abhāvaḥ prāmāṇikaḥ tadā tasya ekasya eva pratiyogitāḥ sarvaiḥ eva vyadhikaraṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ ca samāna adhikaraṇaiḥ saṃbandhaiḥ eva avacchidyantām ākāśa abhāva eva vā tathā astām ekena eva upapattauvabhāva bheda kalpane māna abhāvāt na ca evam eka eva jagatī tale bhavatu abhāvaḥ sa eva tad tad avacchedaka deśa kāla ādi bhedena tad tad vyavahāra bhedam janayiṣyati iti kim adhika kalpanayā iti vācyam upapadyate ced aḥ tu prakṛte tu na bādhakam kiṃcid  ata eva vaiśeṣikāṇām sva abhyupagata kāla padārthasya eva sarva vyavahāra hetutva upapattau na padārtha antara siddhiḥ iti advaita vādinaḥ  vadanti tad evam ‘aham ajña iti jñānasya abhāva jñāna sāmagrī vilakṣaṇa sāmagrī janya tvāt abhāva vilakṣaṇa viṣaya tvam siddham evam tvad uktam artham na jānāmi iti pratyakṣasya api nanu sākṣāt tvad ukta artha viṣayam pramāṇa jñānam mayi na asti iti etad viṣayakam udāhṛta jñānam tad ca na sākṣāt artha viṣayam pramāṇa jñāna avacchedaka taya arthasya bhānāt  atas  na vyāghāta iti ced na sākṣāt tvad ukta artham avetya hi tad abhāvaḥ  grāhyaḥ tad jñānam ca na sākṣiṇā svasmin  tādṛś pramāṇa jñāna abhāvāt anya niṣṭham tu śabda ādinā grāhyam śabda ādiḥ ca tvad ukta artham bodhayan  eva tad viṣaya tvam jñāne bodhayet  tathā ca prathamatas tvad ukta artha viṣaya kam sākṣāt eva jñānam āgatam iti tad niṣedhe na kutaḥ vyāghātaḥ ata eva— viśeṣasya svarūpataḥ  jñāne api viśeṣa prakāraka jñāna abhāvaḥ  na vyāhata iti apāstam kara tala āmalaka jñāne sva viṣaya vyāvartaka dharma viṣaya tvam prasiddham iha niṣidhyata iti api na tvad ukta tvasya api mad uktāt vyāvartaka tvena sāmānyatas  vyāvartaka dharma viṣaya tvasya niṣeddhum aśakyatvāt  nanu avacchedaka tayā viśeṣa jñāne jāte api na vyāhatiḥ tathā hi na hi viśeṣa jñāna abhāvaḥ tvad ukta artha viṣayaka jñāna abhāvaḥ  vātra pratīyate kiṃtu tvad ukta artha viśeṣyaka viśeṣa prakāraka jñāna abhāvaḥ tatra ca tvad ukta artha viśeṣyaka viśeṣa prakāraka jñāna tvena pratiyogi jñāne api tādṛś prakāraka tad viśeṣyaka jñāna abhāva saṃbhavaḥ asya jñānasya jñāne viśeṣye viśeṣa prakārakatva prakāraka tvāt  yatra api tvad ukta viśeṣam na jānāmi iti abhilāpaḥ tatra api evam eva vyāhati abhāvaḥ kathaṃcid unneyaḥ na ca yatra ukta pratiyogyaprasiddhiḥ tatra katham abhāva pratītiḥ iti vācyam samaveta vācya tvam na asti iti atra iva viśeṣye viśeṣaṇa abhāva viṣaya tvena vyadhikaraṇa dharma avacchinna pratiyogi tākā bhāva viṣaya tvena vā upapatteḥ iti ced na anubhava virodhāt  viśeṣa jñāna abhāvasya tvad ukta artha jñāna abhāvasya vā anabhyupagame tad viṣaya jñāna sattvena tad vyavahāra āpatteḥ ca na ca evam dṛśyate svatas prāmāṇya mate tu tad prakāraka tve tad viśeṣyaka tve ca gṛhyamāṇe tadvattva grahaṇasya āvaśyaka tayā tad aṃśe tad prakāraka tad viśeṣyaka tvasya tādṛśa pratiyogi jñāne saṃbhavāt  spaṣṭa eva vyāghātaḥ bhāva rūpa ajñāna pakṣe tu sarvasya api sa akṣi vedya tayā na vyāghāta iti uktam tad evam tvad uktam artham na jānāmi iti pratyakṣa bhāva rūpa ajñāna viṣayam iti siddham evam etauvantam kālam na kiṃcid avediṣam iti parāmarśa siddham sauṣuptam pratyakṣam api bhāva rūpa ajñāna viṣayam eva nanu parāmarśaḥ kim anumānam kim vā smaraṇam ādye jñāna abhāva eva anumīyatām kim bhāva rūpa ajñānena tathā hi—saṃpratipanna udaya astamaya kālavat vivāda padayoḥ api udaya astamayayoḥ antarāla kālam anumāya tad kālam aham jñāna abhāvavān avasthā viśeṣavat tvāt  jñāna sāmagrī virahavat tvāt tulya yogakṣema ātma ādau smaryamāṇe api tadvat tayā niyamena asmaryamāṇa tvāt vā iti prayoga saṃbhavāt  dvitīye tu na asti upapattiḥ saṃskāra asaṃbhavāt  vinaśyadeva hi jñānam saṃskāram janayati vinā vyāpāram vyavahita kārya janana akṣama tvāt  avinaśyatā tu tena svayam eva tad kāryasya janayitum śakya tvāt  kim iti saṃskāraḥ  janyeta na hi saṃskāraḥ api pratyakṣaḥ yena kāryānyathā anupapattim antareṇa api abhyupeyate sauṣuptam ca anādya jñāna uparaktam sākṣi caitanya rūpam jñānam svatas  vā upādhitaḥ  vā na vinaśyati iti saṃskāram katham janayet  tad abhāvāt katham smaryeta asmaryamāṇam vā katham pramāṇa tvena udāhriyeta iti ced na na tāvat anumānam tatra saṃbhavati hetoḥ pakṣa viśeṣaṇasya ca ajñānāt  na hi jñāna abhāvam antareṇa avasthāyām viśeṣaḥ  vaktum śakyaḥ jñāna sāmagrī virahaḥ ca jñāna abhāva anumeya tvena anyonya āśraya grastaḥ na ced ānīntanena indriya prasādena pūrva kālīnam tad uparama m anumāya sāmagrī viraha anumānam indriya prasādasya sukha anubhava hetukasya tad uparama hetukatva asiddheḥ niyamena asmaryamāṇa tvam ca yathāśrutam vā suṣupti kāla avacchedena iti vā ādya asiddhiḥ dvitīye tu upekṣaṇīya jñāna abhāvaḥ  na siddhyet  tatra eva vyabhicāraḥ ca na ca tarhi prātar anubhūta catvare gaja jñāna abhāva jñānam katham iti vācyam jñāna anupalabdhyā eva iti avehi anupalabdhi jñānam ca bhāva rūpa ajñānena liṅgena tathā hi pūrva kāle aham gaja jñāna abhāvavān gaja ajñānavat tvāt yad na evam tad na evam yathā gaja jñānavān aham iti evam sarvatra ajñānasya jñāna abhāva vyāpya tvena tad anumāpaka tvam na ca suṣupti kāle jñāna abhāva anumāna artham bhāva rūpa ajñānam iva rāga abhāva anumāna artham dveṣaḥ api svīkaraṇīyaḥ tad virodhi padārtha anubhavam vinā tad abhāva anumāna ayogāt iti vācyam bhāva rūpa ajñānena jñāna abhāvena vā rāga abhāva anumāna saṃbhavāt tasya api tad virodhi tvāt atha aparokṣataḥ  jñāte ajñāna abhāvāt katham parokṣa jñāna abhāva anumānam sāmagrī viraha ādinā iti gṛhāṇa na ca atra api anyonya āśrayaḥ śabda ādīnām yogyānām yogyā anupalabdhyā abhāva niścayena parokṣa jñāna viraha jñānam vinā eva sāmagrī viraha niścayāt suṣupti kāle ca indriya ādi ghaṭita sāmagrī virahasya phala abhāvam vinā jñātum aśakyatvena anyonya āśraya ukteḥ na ca smaraṇa pakṣe saṃskāra anupapattiḥ ajñānasya ajñāna vṛtti pratibimbita sākṣibha āsya tvena vṛtti nāśāt eva saṃskāra upapatteḥ ajñāna vṛtti pratibimbita caitanyasya eva sākṣipadārtha tvāt na ca  jāgare api ajñānasya vṛtti vedya tve vṛtti abhāva daśāyām saṃśaya ādi āpattiḥ iti vācyam ajñāna viṣaya ajñāna abhāvena tad ayogāt  saṃśaya ādeḥ tad kāraṇībhūta ajñāna samāna viṣayatva niyamāt bhāvatva ādinā saṃśaye tu iṣṭāpattiḥ eva bhāvatva ādeḥ sa akṣi vedyatva abhāvena ajñāna viṣaya tvāt ajñānasya sva rūpeṇa eva sa akṣi vedya tvāt  nanu tadā jñāna abhāvaḥ api sva rūpeṇa eva bhāsatām sa pratiyogika tvena abhava jñāna eva pratiyogi jñānasya hetu tvāt  anyathā ‘prameya am iti jñāne api abhāvaḥ  na bhāseta iti ced na sākṣiṇā tāvat na sva rūpeṇa abhāva avagāhanam tasya sākṣāt sākṣya vedya tvāt na api śabda ādinā tadānīm teṣām abhāvāt  na api anupalabdhyā tasyāḥ pratiyogi jñāna nirapekṣāyā ajanaka tvāt  na ca dṛṣṭa abhāva antara vilakṣaṇa svabhāva eva ayam abhāva iti sva rūpeṇa sākṣi vedyaḥ astu iti vācyam nirvikalpaka buddhi vedya tve bhāva tvasya eva aucityāt  anyathā paribhāṣā mātra āpatteḥ nanu jñāna virodhitva ādeḥ tadā ananubhavena ‘nāvediṣam i ati tena ākāreṇa katham parāmarśaḥ na draṣṭuḥ hi antaḥkaraṇa tādātmyena aham ullekhasya iva jñāna virodhitva ādeḥ api tadā eva anubhūyamāna tvena tad aṃśe parāmarśatva anabhyupagamāt  suṣupti kālīnasya draṣṭuḥ eva parāmṛṣṭa tvāt  nanu ajñāna vṛtti pratibimbita caitanya rūpasya ajñāna anubhavasya jāgrati api vidyamāna tvāt  katham ajñāna smaraṇam na hi dhārāvāhikeṣu anubhaveṣu tulya sāmagrīkeṣu smaraṇa vyavahāraḥ tathā ca dhārāvāhikaḥ ajñāna anubhava iti vaktavyam na tu parāmarśa iti satyam suṣupti ākhyāyāḥ tām asyā ajñāna vṛtteḥ nāśe jāgrati tad viśiṣṭa ajñānasya sākṣiṇā anubhūyamānatva abhāvena saṃskāra janyā avidyā vṛttyā eva suṣupti viśiṣṭa jñāna bhānāt  parāmarśatva upapatteḥ kevala ajñāna aṃśe tu tulya sāmagrīka tvāt dhārā vāhika tvam eva ata eva kārya upādhi vināśa saṃskṛtam ajñāna mātram eva pralaya upamam suṣuptiḥ iti abhipretya vārtikakāra pādaiḥ sauṣupta ajñāna smaraṇam apākṛtam tathā ca uktam ‘na suṣupti gavijñānam na ājñāsiṣam iti smṛtiḥ kāla ādi avyavadhāna tvāt na hi ātma stham atīta bhāj  na bhūta kāla spṛś pratyak na ca āgāmi spṛgīkṣate sva artha deśaḥ para arthaḥ atha vikalpaḥ tena sa smṛtaḥ iti ādya vyākṛta prakriyāyām vivaraṇa kāraiḥ tu aabhāva pratyaya ālambanā vṛttiḥ nidre ati yoga sūtra anusāreṇa tamaḥ guṇa ātmaka āvaraṇa mātra ālambanā kācid vṛttiḥ suṣuptiḥ iti abhipretya tad uparakta caitanyasya tad nāśena eva nāśāt tad kālīna ajñāna anubhava janita saṃskāra vaśena ana kiṃcid avediṣa am iti ‘smaraṇam abhyupeta am iti vārtika vi varaṇayoḥ api avirodhaḥ ata eva uktam vārtikakāraiḥ uṣastibrāhmaṇena ced anubhava vyāptiḥ suṣuptasya abhyupeyate na āvediṣam suṣuptaḥ aham iti dhīḥ kiṃvalāt bhavet  ityādi abhiprāyaḥ tu varṇitaḥ evam ca sākṣya jñāna sukha ākārāḥ tisraḥ avidyā vṛttayaḥ suṣupti ākhyā ekā eva vā vṛttiḥ iti anyat etad nirvikalpakasya api smaraṇa janaka tvam ahaṃkāra uparāga kālīnatva abhāvena tad tān ullekha ityādi sarvam upapāditam asmābhiḥ siddhānta bindau tasmāt  sauṣupta anubhavaḥ api bhāva rūpa ajñāna viṣaya iti siddham iti advaita siddhau ajñāna pratyakṣatva upapattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde anumāna upapattiḥ anumānam api tatra vivaraṇa uktam pramāṇam ‘vivāda padam pramāṇa jñānam sva prāgabhāva vyatirikta sva viṣaya āvaraṇa sva nivartya sva deśa gata vastu antara pūrvakam aprakāśita artha prakāśaka tvāt  andhakāre prathama utpanna pradīpa prabhāva di ati atra pramāṇa padam pramāṇa vṛtteḥ eva pakṣa tvena sukha ādi pramāyām sākṣi caitanya rūpa āyām jñānā nivartikāyām bādha vāraṇāya dharmi aṃśa pramāṇa vṛtteḥ idam iti ākārāyā ajñāna anivartikāyāḥ pakṣa bahirbhāvasya vivāda padam iti viśeṣaṇam viśeṣa ākāra pramāṇa vṛttiḥ iti phalitaḥ arthaḥ parokṣa pramāyā api asattva āvaraṇa rūpa pramātṛtva gata ajñāna nivartaka tvāt  na tad aṃśe api bādhaḥ nanu idam iti pramāṇa vṛtteḥ ajñānā nivartaka tve ajñāta jñāpakatva rūpa pramātvena vyavahāraḥ  na syāt  na idam ākāra bhrama saṃśaya adarśanena tad gocara ajñāna kalpane māna abhāvena tatra sukha ādi jñānavat yathārthatva mātreṇa pramātva vyavahāra upapatteḥ yad āhuḥ ‘dharmi aṃśe sarvam abhra antam prakāre tu viparyayaḥ iti yadi tu bhrama saṃśaya ajanakam api tadā akaram ajñānam anubhava balāt āsthīyeta tarhi sā api pakṣe antar bhavatu pramāṇa vṛttitva avacchedena eva ajñāna nivartaka tvānapayāt  tadā ca vivāda padam iti viśeṣaṇam anādeyam etasmin pakṣe bhrama upādanatva yogya tvam avidyā lakṣaṇam draṣṭavyam bhrama upādāna tvasya dharmi aṃśa jñāna nivartya ajñāne avyāpteḥ iti avadheyam dhārāvāhika buddhīnāñca tad tad kāla avacchinna artha viṣaya tvena ajñāta jñāpaka tvam asti eva kālasya sarva pramāṇa vedyatva abhyupagamāt anātma ākāra pramāṇa vṛttīnām ca tad tad avacchinna caitanya viṣaya tvena sva viṣaya āvaraṇa nivartaka tvam asti eva cit tvena eva prakāśa prasakteḥ na tu anavacchinna cittvena gauravāt  ‘etauvantam kālam mayā na jñātaḥ ayam idānīm jñāta iti anubhavāt ca rūpa ādi hīnasya api tad tad avacchinna caitanyasya pratyakṣa ādi viṣaya tvam uktam prāk  pratikarma vyavasthām abhyupagamya ca idam anumānam na tu dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi pakṣa iti dhyeyam sādhye ca ādyam viśeṣaṇam pratiyogi atiriktā prāgabhāva nivṛttiḥ iti mate prāc abhāvena artha antara vāraṇāya tad udīcya dhvaṃsa ādikam ādāya na artha antara prasaktiḥ kintu pūrva vṛtti abhāvam ādāya iti vastu gatim anurudhya prāc padam avaiyarthyam ca pratiyogi viśeṣaṇa tvena akhaṇḍa abhāva sampādaka tayā etena yatas  jñānam ajñānasya eva nivartakam iti niyamaḥ tasmāt  sva nivartya padena eva prāc abhāva vyudāse kim ādya viśeṣaṇena iti nirastam pramātvena jñāna nivartya tvam anyeṣām na iti atra tātparyāt  na ca sva viṣaya āvaraṇa padena eva tad vyudāsaḥ ‘asti prakāśata iti vyavahāra virodhitva rūpasya āvaraṇa tvasya bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇa tvāt vṛtti jana kāt adṛṣṭena artha antara vāraṇāya tu viśeṣaṇam idam na ca āvaraṇa padena eva tad vyudāse sva viṣaya iti vyartham yad adṛṣṭam sva viṣaya jñāna janakam viṣaya antara jñāna pratibandhaka tayā tadāvārakam tādṛśa adṛṣṭa pūrvaka tvena artha antara vāraka tvāt na ca jaḍe ajñānasya anaṅgīkārāt citaḥ ca ajñāna ādi sākṣitayā bhāsamāna tvāt  kva āvaraṇam iti vācyam ājñāna ādi sākṣitayā citaḥ prakāśamāna tve api ‘asti prakāśata iti vyavahāra abhāvena tad aṃśe ajñāna āvaraṇasya āvaśyaka tvāt  vakṣyate ca etad  sva nivartya iti ca viśeṣaṇam vṛtti pratibandhaka adṛṣṭena artha antara vāraṇāya na ca carama sākṣātkāra utpatti pratibandhaka adṛṣṭasya tad anivartya tve mithyātva asiddhiḥ tad nivartya tve tad vyudasanam aśakyam iti vācyam pratibandhaka adṛṣṭe vidyamāne na jñāna utpattiḥ iti prathamam tad nivṛtteḥ kāraṇa ātmanā sthitasya jñāna nivartya tvāt ca mithyātvam na ca evam api sva nivartya tvam avyāhatam sva nivartya svarūpa tve tātparyāt  andhakāreṇa artha antara vāraṇa artham idam iti kecid  tad na sva deśa gata iti anena eva tad vyudāsāt yathā ca vṛtti pratibimbita caitanyasya viṣaya avacchinna caitanyena saha eka lolībhāvāt ajñāna nivartaka tvam tathā uktam prāk  sva deśa gata iti ca viśeṣaṇam viṣaya gata ajñāta tvena artha antara vāraṇāya yadi api avidyā viṣayatva rūpam ajñāta tvam asiddham jñātatva abhāva rūpam tu prathama viśeṣaṇena eva parāḥ tam tathā api prathamena prāgabhāva vyudāsā atyanta abhāva vyudāsāya caturtham iti draṣṭavyam nanu katham jñāna āśraya gata tvam ajñānasya vṛtti ādi rūpasya jñānasya ajñāna āśraya cit ana āśrita tvāt iti ced na antaḥkaraṇasya cit āśrita tvena tad vṛtteḥ tad pratiphalita caitanyasya vā jñānasya cit āśritatva saṃbhavāt kiṃcid avacchinna tad āśritasya api tad āśrita tvānapāyāt karṇa śaṣkulī avacchinna ākāśa āśritasya śabdasya ākāśa āśrita tvavat evam ca bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇam āvaraṇam iti matena sādhyam upapāditam abhāvaḥ  nāvāraka iti siddhānte tu sādhya dvaye tātparyam sva prāgabhāva atirikta sva nivartya sva deśa gata vastu antara pūrvakam iti ekam sva viṣaya āvaraṇa  sva nivarti asva deśa gata vastu antara  pūrvakam iti aparam iti na kiṃcid asamañjasam hetau ca prakāśaka tvam prakāśaka pada vācya tvam aprakāśa virodhi tvam vā jñāna ālokayoḥ sādhāraṇam yadi api prakāśaka pada vācya tvam nāmakaraṇa vaśāt  kasmiṃścid  puruṣe api asti tathā api prakāśaka śabdena śāstre sarva deśa kālayoḥ vā vyavahriyamāṇa tvam tad vivakṣitam athavā astu sādhāraṇam aprakāśita artha gocara iti viśeṣaṇāt  vyabhicāra vyudāsaḥ aprakāśita tvam ca ‘na prakāśata iti vyavahāra gocara tvam tad ca sva prakāśa caitanye api asti iti upapāditam evam niruktā prakāśa virodhi tvam api jñāna ālokayoḥ pratyakṣa siddham uktam ca vivaraṇe ‘jñāna prakāśya tvāt ajñāna virodhi tvāt anyat eva āloka prakāśya tvam tamaḥ virodhi tvam nāma iti ata ubhayoḥ eva sākṣāt aprakāśa virodhitva saṃbhavāt na indriya sannikaṣa ādau vyabhicāraḥ evam ca aprakāśita artha gocara tve sati prakāśa śabda vācya tvāt aprakāśa virodhi prakāśa tvāt iti vā hetuḥ paryavasitaḥ viparyaya viṣayaḥ tu na ajñātaḥ viparyaya ani akāla asattvena tasya anirvacanīyasya māna gocaratva abhāvena prakāśa prāk kāla sattva ghaṭita aprakāśitatva asaṃbhavāt ata eva sa na aprakāśa virodhī sva viṣaye aprakāśa abhāvāt adhiṣṭhāna aprakāśaḥ tu tasya janaka eva smaraṇe ca vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ spaṣṭaḥ anukūla tarkaḥ ca tvad uktam artham na jānāmi iti prati iti anyathā anupapatti ādi rūpaḥ prāk ukta eva etena gaḥ śabda vācya tvena pṛthivyāḥ  api śṛṅgitvā anumāna apātaḥ apāstaḥ tatra anukūla tarka abhāvāt ajñānasya sva rūpeṇa ajñāna āviṣaya tve api tad bhāvatva ādikam ajñāna viṣayaḥ  bhavati eva tasya ajñāna grāhaka sākṣya grāhya tvāt anyathā tatra vivādaḥ  na syāt  evam pramāyā sva viṣaya āvaraṇa bhāva pūrvaka tvam api na pramā svarūpa grāhaka sākṣi grāhyam tathā ca tad grāhikāyā etasyāḥ  anumiteḥ sādhya sādhana ubhaya adhikaraṇa tvāt na kaḥ api doṣaḥ dṛṣṭānte ca andhakāra avyavahita utpattika tvam viśeṣaṇam tena na prathama pada vaiyarthyam na vā dvitīya ādi prabhāyām sādhya sādhana vaikalpyam vistareṇa ca anyatra vyutpāditam idam asmābhiḥ nanu anādi tve sati bhāva tvam abhāva vilakṣaṇa tvam vā na nivartya niṣṭham anādi bhāva mātra vṛtti dharma tvāt anādya bhāva vilakṣaṇa mātra vṛtti tvāt vā ātma tvavat  nivartya tvam vā nānā ādi bhāva niṣṭham anādya bhāva vilakṣaṇa niṣṭham na iti vā nivartya mātra vṛtti tvāt prāgabhāva tvavat  anādi tvam vā na āvaraṇa niṣṭham anādi mātra vṛtti tvāt prāgabhāva tvavat  pramāṇa jñānam vā anādya bhāvānyāna ādya nivartakam jñāna tvāt  bhramavat ityādinā sat pratipakṣatā kṛtya bhāva mātreṇa akṛtasya kṛtivat  pūrva prakāśa abhāva mātreṇa aprakāśitasya prakāśa upapatteḥ aprayojaka tvam ca iti ced na anukūla tarka abhāvena aprayojaka tvāt  siddhānti hetoḥ ca anukūla tarka sadbhāvena sādhya vyāpya tve niścite sat pratipakṣā prayojakatva ādīnām anavakāśāt anādi bhāva tvasya nivartya avṛtti tve api avidyāyā bhāva vilakṣaṇāyāḥ  nivartyatva upapatteḥ ādya anumānena avirodhaḥ ca dvitīye tu anāśrita mātra vṛtti tvam upādhiḥ tṛtīya caturthayoḥ sakala nivartyāvṛtti tvam upādhiḥ pañcame sakala anādya vṛtti tvam upādhiḥ ṣaṣṭhe pratiyogi aprasiddhyā sādhya aprasiddhiḥ iti ca dūṣaṇāni tattva pradīpikā uktam ca caitra pramā caitra gata pramā prāga bhāva atiriktā anādi nivartikā pramātvāt maitra pramāvat  vigītaḥ  vibhramaḥ etad janakābādhya atirikta upādānakaḥ vibhrama tvāt  saṃmatavat iti atra ādye sukha ādi jñāneṣu na bādhaḥ antaḥkaraṇa vṛtteḥ eva pramāpadena ukteḥ caitra gata tvam ca nānā ādeḥ viśeṣaṇam maitra pramāyāḥ caitra niṣṭhāna ādi nivartakatva abhāvena dṛṣṭānte sādhya vaikalya āpātāt  kiṃtu pramāta da bhāvayoḥ anyatarasya pramāyāḥ ca ātma gata tvam prāc vyākhyātam sādhye tu pramāpadam uparañjakam eva yadi tu abhāve prāk iti viśeṣaṇam na asti ‘tadā bhāva rūpa ajñānasya api svābhāva abhāva tvena tad atirikta anādi nivartaka tve bādha vāraṇāya caitra asamaveta tvam caitra ani samaveta tvam ca na upādhiḥ caitra sukha ādau vyabhicāreṇa sādhya avyāpaka tvāt  na ca caitra pramā caitra gatasya abhāva atiriktasya anādeḥ nivartikā na pramātvāt  maitra pramādivat iti sat pratipakṣaḥ pratiyogi prasiddhi aprasiddhibhyām vyāhateḥ caitra gata pramā bhāva atirikta abhāva nivartaka tvam tu na upādhiḥ caitra gata pramā bhāva atiriktasya sva janya vyavahāra prāgabhāvasya nivartaka tayā pakṣe sādhana vyāpaka tvāt  vipakṣa bādhaka sattvāt ca na ābhāsa sāmyam ata eva dvitīya anumānam api samyak  na ca vigītaḥ  vibhramaḥ etad jñāna janaka bādhya atirikta upādānakaḥ vibhrama tvāt  saṃmatavat iti sat pratipakṣa iti vācyam bādhyasya tvad mate ajanaka tvāt  sādhya aprasiddheḥ brahma avidyā ubhaya upādānaka tvena avirodhāt ca navyāḥ tu vimatā pramā pramābhāva atiriktasya anādeḥ nivartikā kāryatvāt  ghaṭavat  bhrama anuttara pramā svābhāva atirikta sva virodhi nivartikā pramātvāt  pramottara pramāvat  jñāna tvam sva viṣaya āvaraṇa nivartaka niṣṭham aprakāśita artha prakāśa vṛtti tvāt ālokatvavat  anitya jñānam abhāva tvānadhikaraṇa sva virodhi samāna adhikaraṇam prayatna anya tve sati sa viṣaya tve satya nitya tvāt  anitya icchāvat  sā hi tādṛś dveṣa samāna adhikaraṇā na ca eteṣu aprayojakatva śaṅkā vipakṣa bādhaka tarkasya ukta tvāt  evam anyat api ūhanīyam jñāna virodhi tvam anādi bhāvatva samāna adhikaraṇam sakala jñāna virodhi vṛtti tvāt dṛśya tvavat  yad vā anādya bhāva vilakṣaṇa tvam jñāna virodhi vṛtti anādya bhāva vilakṣaṇa mātra vṛtti tvāt abhidheya tvavat iti evam abhāva vilakṣaṇa ajñāne anumānāni ūhanīyāni iti advaita siddhau  avidyā anumāna upapattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde śruti upapattiḥ evam śrutayaḥ ca tatra chāndogye aṣṭama adhyāye  atat yathā api hiraṇyam nidhi nihitam akṣetrajñā upari upari saṃcarantaḥ  na vindeyuḥ evam eva imāḥ sarvāḥ prajā aharahar gacchanti etam brahma lokam na vindanti anṛtena pratyūḍhā iti śrutiḥ brahma jñāna pratibandhaka tvena anṛtam bruvāṇā tādṛś ajñāne pramāṇam na ca ṛta śabdasya ‘ṛtam pibanta avi atyatra sat karmaṇi prayoga darśanāt  ‘ṛtam satyam tathā dharma  iti smṛteḥ ca ṛta śabdasya sat karma para tvāt anṛta śabdasya duṣkarma paratvam iti vācyam uttaratra ‘ya ātma apahata pāpme‘tyādinā ātmanaḥ apahata pāpmatva pratipādanena duṣkarma pratyūḍhatva virodhāt suṣuptau karma mātra nāśe duṣkarmaṇaḥ api abhāvāt kāraṇa ātmanā avasthāne ca ajñānasya āvaśyaka tvāt  karmaṇa āvaraṇatva anupapatteḥ ca brahma vedana pratibandhaka tayā hi anādi brahmāvārakam jñāna nivartyam vācyam tathā ca karma iva pradhānam api na anṛta pada abhidheyam tayoḥ jñāna anivartya tvāt jñāna nivartya tve ca ‘bhūyas ca ante viśva māyā nivṛttiḥ i‘ti ādi śrutiḥ mānam na ca atra nivṛttiḥ taraṇa mātram ‘māyām etām taranti te iti smṛteḥ iti vācyam jñāna hetuka taraṇasya nivṛtti atiriktasya asambhavena ubhayośa mātra artha tvāt na ca ‘tama āsī adityasya sattva pratipādakasya bādhakam vinā pāramārthika sattva paratvena katham āvaraṇasya anṛta tvam iti vācyam ‘nāsat āsīt na usadāsī aditi anena pāramārthikatva tuccha tvayoḥ niṣedhena vyāvahārika sattva paratvāt na ca anena māyā pratipādyate māyā śabda arthaḥ ca na ajñānam māyinaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ ajñāni tve sarvajñatva niravadyatva ādi śruti virodhāt iti vācyam upādheḥ pratibimba pakṣa pāti tvena īśvara āsārvaiya ādi āpādanā yogāt sārvajña ādi aśvaiḥ yasya māyā nibandhana tvāt ca na ca amaya jñāna‘ iti dhātu artha anusārāt  māyā katham ajñānam iti vācyam ‘evam eva eṣā māyā sva avyatiriktāni paripūrṇāni kṣetrāṇi darśayitvā jīveśau  ābhāsīkaroti māyā ca avidyā ca svayam eva bhavatī‘ti śrutyā māyā vidyayoḥ aikya pratipādanāt māyā ajñānam eva ‘ghaṭa ceṣṭāyāḥ am iti dhātu jasya api ghaṭa śabdasya ceṣṭā vācakatva abhāvavat atra api jñāna vācakatva abhāvāt māyā prajñā vayunam iti jñāna paryāye nighaṇṭu kāra vacanam ca jñāna ākāra pariṇāmi tvāt ajñānasya upapannam vṛtti jñānasya ajñāna abhinna tvāt ajñānasya eva anirvacanīya vicitra śakti yogāt na vicitra śaktimati māyā śabda prayoga anupapattiḥ kvacid maṇi mantra ādau tad prayogaḥ tu upacārāt na ca śukti rūpī ādau māyā śabda aprayogāt  na mṛṣā arthaḥ ayam iti vācyam vajra ādau pṛthivītva ādi vyavahāra abhāve api pṛthivī tvavat  vyavahāra abhāve api māyā tvān apāyāt aindrajālikā ādau bahuśas  māyā śabda prayoga darśanāt ca māyāyāḥ  ajñāna anya tve jñāna nivartyatva virodhāt ca nīhāra tamaḥ śabdau  api asmin mate ajñānasya āvāraka tvāt yujyete na anya mate anṛta nīhāra ādi śabdānām duṣkarma paratve śruti antara ukta jīva īśa bhedakatva upādānatva ādi virodhaḥ ca ‘tasmāt anṛtena pratyūḍhāḥ anīhāreṇa prāvṛtāḥ‘ ‘tama āsīt ‘māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt ‘ ‘ajām ekām lohita śukla kṛṣṇām‘ ‘avidyāyām antare vartamānāḥ‘ ‘bhūyas ca ante viśva māyā nivṛttiḥ i‘ti ādyāḥ śrutayaḥ varṇitā ajñāne pramāṇam iti sthitam iti advaita siddhau  avidyā pratipādaka śruti upapattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde artha apatyupapattiḥ jīvasya anavacchinna brahma ānandā prakāśāni atha anupapattiḥ ca tatra mānam na ca jīvasya brahma bhedena eva tādṛś aprakāśa upapattiḥ jīva brahma bhedasya agre nirasiṣyamāṇa tvāt  na ca anavacchinna ānandasya api prakāśamāna pratyak mātra tvena aprakāśa mānatva anupapattiḥ śarīra pratiyogikasya ātmani svarūpa bhedasya ātma ākāreṇa prakāśamāna tve api bheda ākāreṇa aprakāśa māna tvavat rūpa antareṇa brahmaṇaḥ prakāśamāna tve api ukta ākāreṇa avidyā vaśāda prakāśa mānatva upapatteḥ ukta tvāt    bhramasya sa upādāna tvāni atha anupapattiḥ api avidyāyām pramāṇam na ca antaḥkaraṇam upādānam antaḥkaraṇasya jñāna janane pramāṇa vyāpāra sāpekṣa tvena pramāṇa aviṣaye śukti rūpī ādau jñāna ajanaka tvāt  sādi tvena anādi bhrama paramparā anupādāna tvāt ca na ca brahma eva upādānam tasya apariṇāmi tvāt na ca vivartā adhiṣṭhāna tvena śukti ādeḥ iva upādāna tvam avidyām antareṇa atāttvikān yatha abhāva lakṣaṇasya vivartasya eva asambhavāt  śukti ādeḥ adhiṣṭhāna avacchedaka tayā vivartā adhiṣṭhānatva abhāvāt  na ca u pādāna apekṣasya vivartasya tāttvika atirikta upādāna kalpanavada vidyā ādeḥ āśraya sāpekṣasya brahma atiriktam atāt tvikam adhikaraṇam kalpyam syāt iti vācyam brahmaṇa eva vikāri tve anityatva ādi prasaktivat  brahmaṇa eva adhiṣṭhāna tve bādhaka abhāvena dvitīyasya adhikaraṇasya akalpanāt  na ca asatyasya satya rūpa antarāpatti lakṣaṇa pariṇāmi anapekṣa tvena pariṇāmi tvena api na avidyā kalpanam iti vācyam pariṇāmi satta asamāna sattākatva niyamena asatya tvasya eva abhāvāt na ca ghaṭa ādau sva samāna sattāka upādānakatva darśanena prapañce api tādṛśa upādāna kalpane ghaṭa ādeḥ svāghika sattākā upādāna anapekṣa tvavat viyat ādeḥ api brahma anupādānaka tvam syāt iti vācyam ‘tad abhidhyānāt eva tu tad liṅgāt saḥ iti anena nyāyena ghaṭa ādeḥ api mṛdavastha caitanya upādānaka tayā tādṛśa upādāna anapekṣatva asiddheḥ ata eva rūpye api sva samāna sattākasya nimittasya api kalpanā āpattiḥ iti nirastam nimitta mātre vā iyam kalpanā viśeṣe vā na ādyaḥ adhiṣṭhāna rūpa nimittasya sarvatra adhika sattāka tvāt dvitīye tu uttarottara bhrame pūrva pūrva bhramasya nimitta tvena iṣṭā āpatteḥ na ca triguṇa ātmakam pradhānam upādānam iti vācyam tasya asatya tve avidyānatirekāt  satya tve api sa avayavam niravayavam vā ādye anāditva bhaṅgaḥ dvitīye pariṇāmitva ayogaḥ  brahmavat  na ca avidyā pakṣe api samaḥ paryanuyogaḥ tasyāḥ kālpanika tvena paryanuyoga ayogāt tasmāt apattiḥ avidyāyām pramāṇam iti advaita siddhau  avidyāyām arthāpattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde tad prati iti upapattiḥ sā ca avidyā sākṣivedyā na tu śuddha cit prakāśyā sākṣī ca avidyā vṛtti prativimbita caitanyam tena nirdoṣa cit prakāśya tvena ajñānasya pāramārthikatva āpattiḥ mokṣe api tad prakāśa āpattiḥ na ca tadānīm avidyāyā nivṛtta tvāt  prakāśa abhāvaḥ pratīti mātra śarīrasya prati iti anuvṛttau nivṛtti ayogāt ityādi doṣān avakāśaḥ ata eva ucyate rāhuvat  sva āvṛta caitanya prakāśyā avidyā iti na ca evam kadācid avidyāyāḥ  apratītya āpattiḥ iṣṭa āpatteḥ samādhau tathā abhyupagamāt na ca avidyā vṛtteḥ doṣa janya tvāt atra katham avidyā vṛttiḥ avidyāyāḥ  eva doṣa tvāt  na ca vṛtteḥ api vṛtti antara pratibimbita cit bhāsya tve anavasthā svasyā eva sva bhāna upādhi tvāt nanu pramāṇa āgamyāyām avidyāyām pramāṇa upanyāsa vaiyarthyam na ca pramāṇaiḥ asat vyāvṛtti mātram bodhyata iti vācyam ajñānam agṛhṇatām tatra asat vyāvṛtti bodhe api asāmarthyāt iti ced na pramāṇa upanīta asat vyāvṛtti viśiṣṭa jñānam hi sākṣiṇā gṛhyate tathā ca asat vyāvṛtti upanayane pramāṇānām caritārtha tvāt na kā api anupapattiḥ iti advaita siddhau  avidyā prati iti upapattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde avidyāyāḥ cit mātra āśrayatva upapattiḥ avidyāyāḥ  āśrayaḥ tu śuddham brahmā eva tad uktam  ‘āśrayatva viṣayatva bhāginī nirvibhāga citiḥ eva kevalā pūrva siddha tamasaḥ  hi paścimaḥ  bhavati na api gocaraḥ iti darpaṇasya mukha mātra saṃbandhe api pratimukhe mālinyavat  pratibimbe jīve saṃsāraḥ na bimbe brahmaṇi upādheḥ prativimba pakṣa pāti tvāt  nanu katham caitanyam ajñāna āśrayaḥ tasya prakāśa svarūpa tvāt tayoḥ ca tamaḥ prakāśavat viruddha svabhāva tvāt iti ced na ajñāna virodhi jñānam hi na caitanya mātram kiṃtu vṛtti prativimbitam tad ca na avidyā āśrayaḥ yad ca avidyā āśrayaḥ tad ca na ajñāna virodhi na ca tarhi śuddha citaḥ ajñāna virodhitva abhāve ghaṭa ādivat aprakāśatva āpattiḥ vṛtti avacchedena tasyāḥ  eva ajñāna virodhi tvāt svatas tṛṇa tūla ādi bhāsakasya saurālokasya sūrya kānta avacchedena sva bhāsya tṛṇa tūla ādi dāhaka tvavat svatas avidyā tad kārya bhāsakasya caitanyasya vṛtti avacchedena tad dāhaka tvāt  nanu aham ajña iti dharma grāhakeṇa sākṣiṇā ahaṅkāra āśrita tvena ajñānasya grahaṇāt  bādhaḥ na ca sthaulya āśraya deha aikya adhyāsāt aham sthūla iti vada jñāna āśraya cit aikya adhyāsāt dagdhṛtva ayasoḥ eka agni saṃvandhādayaḥ  dahati iti vada jñāna ahaṅkārayoḥ ekacit aikya adhyāsāt vā ‘aham ajña iti dhī bhrānta iti vācyam citaḥ ajñāna āśrayatva asiddhyā anyonya āśrayāt iti ced na ahaṃkārasya avidyā adhīna tvena tad anāśraya tayā cita eva ajñāna āśraya tve siddhe ‘aham ajña iti pratīteḥ aikya adhyāsa nibandhana tvena ābādhaka tvāt  na ca avidyā āśraya tvāt eva ahaṅkāraḥ akalpitaḥ astu kalpita eva vā tad āśraya tvam astu avidyāyām anupapatteḥ alaṅkāra tvāt iti vācyam aham arthasya jñāna nivartya tvena dṛśya tvena akalpitatva ayogāt cit mātra āśrita tvam vinā tad gocara caram avṛtti nivartyatva āpātāt  sva kalpitasya sva āśrita tvena sva āśrayatva ayogāt na ca avidyāyām anupapattiḥ alaṅkāraḥ anupapatti mātram na alaṅkāraḥ kiṃtu sattva ādi prāpaka yuktau  anupapattiḥ anyathā vādi vacasaḥ anavakāśa āpatteḥ nanu ‘niraniṣṭaḥ  niravadyaḥ śokam moham atyeti nitya mukta iti śruti virodhāt  na śuddha citaḥ avidyā āśraya tvam na hi mauḍhyam na doṣaḥ na api bandhaka ajñāna āśrayaḥ  muktaḥ na ca tāttvika avidyā ādeḥ eva niṣedhaḥ tvad mate tasya aprasakteḥ jīve api tad abhāvena jīva brahmaṇoḥ sā avadyatva niravadyatva vyavasthā śruti virodha iti ced na avadyasya citi kārya kāritva abhāvena kārya karatva akārya kara tvābhyām eva sā avadyatva niravadyatva vyavasthā upapatteḥ upādheḥ pratibimba pakṣa pāti tvāt  na ca cit mātrasya avidyā āśraya tve prabhāṇa abhāvaḥ jīva āśrita tve ca pramāṇam asti iti vācyam ‘māyām tu prakṛtim vidyāt māyinam tu maheśvaram iti śruteḥ eva pramāṇa tvāt  na ca ‘jñā jñā  īśān īśā aviti jīva ajñāna pratipādaka śruti virodhaḥ tad āśrayatva abhāve api tad kārya yogi tayā ajñatva vyapadeśa upapatteḥ na ca brahmaṇaḥ api jīva āśrita ajñāna viṣaya tvena māyitvā upapattiḥ iti vācyam jīva tvasya āśraya tā avacchedaka tve paraspara āśraya prasaṅgāt  nanu śukti ādi ajñānavat jñātuḥ artha aprakāśa rūpam idam api ajñānam sva kāryeṇa bhrānti ādinā sva nivartakena tattva jñāna ādinā sva samāna yogakṣemeṇa jñāna prāc abhāvena ca sāmānādhikaraṇyāya jñātra ātma niṣṭham na tu caitanya rūpa jñāna āśritam iti ced  na caitanyasya eva jñātṛ tvena jñātuḥ artha aprakāśa rūpa tvasya samyak jñāna āśraya tvasya bhrānti ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇyasya ca upapatteḥ na ca evam jñātṛ tve satya vidyā āśraya tvam avidyāyām jñātṛ tvam iti anyonya āśraya iti vācyam avidyāyāḥ  jñātṛtva anapekṣa tvena anyonya āśraya abhāvāt na hi sāmānādhikaraṇyam asti iti etāvatā eva tad apekṣayā anayā bhavitavyam na ca śarīre api jñātṛtva adhyāsa saṃbhavena tatra api ajñāna āśrayatva āpattiḥ iti vācyam na hi jñātṛtva adhyāsaḥ  ajñāna āśraya tve prayojakaḥ yena tanmātreṇa tad āpadyeta kiṃtu prasakta prakāśa tvam ajñāna anāśrita tvam ca na ca evam avidyā āśrayasya jñātṛtva bhoktṛtva ādimattve jīva āśrita ajñāna pakṣa praveśa iti vācyam avidyāvat chinnasya hi jñātṛ tvam avidyā ca na avidyā avacchedena sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca avacchedya aṃśa aikyam ādāya yathā upādhi saṃbandhaḥ  mukha mātra eva aupādhika mālinya saṃbandhaḥ tu upādhi avacchinne bimba pratibimbayoḥ aikyāt  tathā sāmānādhikaraṇyam api yathā pratibimbaḥ  na vastu antaram tathā vakṣyate nanu śukti ajñānam api śukti avacchinna caitanya gatam vācyam tathā aca aham jānāmi icchāmī ativat  ‘aham na jānāmī‘ti jñātṛ sthatva anubhava virodha iti ced na ajñāna dvaividhyāt ekam hi śukti avacchinna caitanya āśritam tad gata aparokṣa bhrama janakam tad viṣaya aparokṣa pramāna āśyam aparam ca parokṣa bhrama janakam tad viṣaya pramā mātra nāśyam pramātṛtva prayojaka upādhi avacchinna caitanya āśritam iti uktam prāk  tatra pramātṛtva prayojaka upādhi avacchinna caitanya gata ajñāna viṣayakaḥ ayam anubhavaḥ tena pramātṛ niṣṭhatva viṣaya tā asya na virudhyate ata eva viṣaya gatā ajñāne vidyamāne api pramātṛ gata ajñāna nāśena na jānāmi iti vyavahāra abhāvaḥ nanu upādheḥ pratibimba pakṣa pāti tvāt na brahmaṇaḥ saṃsāri tvam iti uktam tad ayuktam bimba pratibimba bhāvasya eva asaṃbhavāt tathā hi—a cākṣuṣasya caitanyasya gandha rasa ādivat  pratibimba tānarha tvāt pratibimba tve jīvasya sāditva apātāt ca sūryasya sarit jala iva marīcikā jaleṣu aprati phalanena cit asamāna sattākasya ajñānasya citam pratyupādhitva ayogāt asvacchasya ajñānasya pratibimba tā upa adhitva ayogāt ca avidyāyāḥ ci mātra abhimukhya asaṃbhavāt ca ajñānasya ākāśa ādi ātmanā pariṇāme pratibimba apāya apātāt ca iti ced na rūpavata eva pratibimba iti asyā vyāpteḥ rūpa ādau vyabhicārāt  yathā bhaṅgaḥ evam ākāśa ādau vyabhicāra ācākṣuṣasya eva pratibimba iti asyā api vyāpteḥ bhaṅgaḥ vastutas tu śruti balāt citaḥ pratibimbe siddhe tatra eva vyabhicārāt na iyam vyāptiḥ tathā ca rasa ādi vyāvṛttam phala ekoneyam pratibimba prayojakam na api jīvasya sāditva āpattiḥ upādhi bimba sambandha anādi tvena anāditvā upapatteḥ vistaraḥ tu siddhānta bindau yad tu uktam marīcikā jale sūrya pratibimba adarśanāt  bimba samāna sattāka tvam pratibimba udgrāhi tve prayojakam iti tad na adhyastasya sphaṭika lauhityasya darpaṇe pratibimba darśanāt  tasmāt marīcikā jala vyāvṛttam svaccha tvam phala ekonneyam ananugatam eva pratibimba udgrāhi tve prayojakam tad ca prakṛte api asti ata eva ajñānasya asvacchatvāt na pratibimba upādhi tvam iti nirastam yad ca uktam cit mātra abhimukhya abhāvāt iti tad kim sarva ātmanā cit ābhimukhya abhāvāt vā ābhimukhya mātra abhāvāt vā na ādyaḥ caitanyavat vibhutva pakṣe sarva ātmanā api saṃbhavāt  nyūna parimāṇa tve api na doṣaḥ nyūna parimāṇasya api adhika parimāṇa ākāśa ādi pratibimba udgrāhitva darśanāt na dvitīyaḥ caitanyasya sarvatas api prasṛta tvena vyavadhāna abhāvena ca ābhimukhyasya sadbhāvāt  na ca ākāśa ādi ātmanā pariṇāme pratibimba apāya āpattiḥ pratibimba prayojaka rūpa avirodhi pariṇāmasya pratibimba avirodhi tvena pratibimbānapāyāt  na ca mukha pratimukha anugata mukhatva atirikta mukha mātra rūpa vyakyantarasya iva jīva brahma anugata citvā atirikta cit mātra rūpasya ajñāna āśrayatva yogya vyakti antarasya abhāvāt mukha mātra saṃbandhya ādarśavat cit mātra saṃbandhya jñā katham iti vācyam aparāmṛṣṭa bhedasya mukha ādeḥ mātrā artha tvena anugata dharmī atireka saṃbhavāt nanu upādhiḥ pratibimba pakṣapāti iti sāmānya vyāpteḥ ajñānam sva āśraya eva bhrānti ādi hetuḥ iti viśeṣa vyāptyā bādha iti ced na viśeṣa vyāpti grāhaka sahacāra darśanasya vivāda viṣaya atirikte asaṃbhavena viśeṣa vyāpti asaṃbhavāt  na ca bandhasya cit mātra āśrita mokṣa sāmānādhikaraṇyā anupapattiḥ avacchedya aṃśam ādāya sāmānādhikaraṇyasya ukta tvāt nanu—upādheḥ pratibimba pakṣa pāti tvam tatra svadharma pratibhāsaka tvam vā sva kārya pratibhāsaka tvam vā sva kārya niṣṭha dharma pratibhāsaka tvam vā pratibimbam prati sva viṣaya ācchādaka tvam vā na ādyaḥ suṣupti ādi anuvṛttasya avidyā rūpasya avidyā avacchinnatva rūpasya vā tad pratibimbita tvasya vā suṣupta ādau  ananuvṛttasya kartṛtva pramātṛtva ādi rūpasya vā saṃsārasya ajñāna niṣṭhatva abhāvāt jñāna kriyā saṃskāra ādīnām tvad mate ajñāna niṣṭhatve api nitya atīndriyāṇām teṣām ātmani kadāpi apratīteḥ ‘avidyāḥ tamayaḥ  mokṣaḥ sā ca bandha udāhṛtaḥ ‘ iti tvad mate api avidyā bandhikā bandhaḥ vā na tu baddhā yena sva niṣṭha bandha rūpa dharma saṃkrāmaka tvam syāt  na dvitīyaḥ viccheda ādeḥ upādhi kāryasya bimbe mahākāśe ca darśanāt  mukhasya bimba tu ādeḥ brahma stha sārvajñyādeḥ ca ana aupādhikatva apātāt ca na api tṛtīya caturthau darpaṇa ghaṭa ādau  adṛṣṭeḥ evam buddhi rūpa upādhiḥ api na pratibimba pakṣapāti iti ced na atiśayena kārya kara tvam eva tad pakṣa pāti tvam tathā ca viccheda ādi rūpa kārya karatva sāmye api sthaulya ādi ava bhāsa rūpa kārya kara tvena darpaṇa ādeḥ pratibimba pakṣa pāti tvavat  kartṛtva bhoktṛtva ādi saṃsāra rūpa kārya paratvena avidyāyām api pratibimba pakṣa pātitva upapatteḥ yad tu uktam mukha ādi gata bimba tvam brahma gatam sārvajñi ādikam ca anaupādhikam syāt iti tad na upādhau bimba kārya kara tvam eva na iti iti na brūmaḥ kiṃtu pratibimbe atiśayena iti yad api buddhi rūpa upādheḥ api na pratibimba pakṣa pāti tvam tasya pratibimba apakṣa pāti japā ku suma sthānīya tvena tad pakṣapāti ādarśa sthānīyatva abhāvāt iti tad na sva niṣṭha sthaulya avabhāsaka tvena ādarśasya iva asya api sva niṣṭha dharma avabhāsaka tvena tadvat  pakṣapātitva saṃbhavāt  tasmāt avidyā kṛta vicchedena brahmaṇi eva nitya muktatva saṃsāritva sarvajñatva kiṃcid jñatva ādi vyavasthā upapattiḥ etena asarvajñatva ādinā anubhava siddhāt jīvāt anyasya cetanasya abhāvena sārvajñi ādi śrutiḥ nirviṣayā syāt  eka jīva vāde saṃsārya saṃsāri vyavasthā ayogāt ‘dvā suparṇā ‘ya ātmani tiṣṭhan ityādi śrutibhiḥ  anyaḥ ca paramaḥ  rājan tathā anyaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ tāni aham veda sarvāṇi na tvam vettha paraṃtapa  ityādi smṛtibhiḥ ‘śārīraḥ ca ubhaye api hi bhedena enam adhīyate ‘bheda vyapadeśāt ca ityādi sūtraiḥ tasmāt śārīrāt anya eva īśvaraḥ ātmānau tau  etau cetanau ekaḥ kartā bhoktā anyaḥ tad viparītaḥ apahata pāpmatva ādi guṇa ityādi bhāṣyaiḥ ‘tattva jñāna saṃsaraṇe ca avadātatva śyāmatva ādivat na itara itaratra avatiṣṭhete ityādi vivaraṇa granyaiḥ ca virodha iti nirastam nanu cit mātrasya ajñānam svābhāvikam aupādhikam vā na ādyaḥ ātmavat anivṛtti prasaṅgāt  na antyaḥ svasya eva upādhi tve ātma āśrayāt etad apekṣā anya apekṣa tve anyonya āśrayāt tad anyānya apekṣa tve ca anavasthānāt iti ced na svasya eva āśrayatva upādhi tvāt na ca ātma āśrayaḥ bhedasya sva bhedakatvavat upapatteḥ svābhāvikasya api ghaṭa rūpasya tad prāgabhāvasya ca nivṛtti darśanāt  iti advaita siddhau ajñānasya cit mātra āśrayatva upapattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde avidyāyāḥ sarvajña āśrayatva upapattiḥ nanu śuddha brahmaṇaḥ cit mātrasya ajñāna āśraya tve sārvajñya virodhaḥ na ca viśiṣṭa eva sārvajñyam ‘turīyam sarva dṛś sadā iti śuddhasya eva sarvajñatva ukteḥ iti ced na sarvadṛś padena sarveṣām dṛś bhūtam caitanyam iti ucyate na tu sarvajñam turīyam tasmāt viśiṣṭa eva sārvajñyam tad ca avidyām vinā na saṃbhavati iti avidyā siddhiḥ tathā hi sarvajñaḥ  hi pramāṇataḥ svarūpa jñaptyā vā tatra pramāṇasya bhrānteḥ ca avidyā mūla tvāt asaṅga svarūpa jñapteḥ ca avidyām vinā viṣaya asaṅgateḥ tad uktam  ‘ svarūpataḥ pramāṇā eva sarvajña tvam dvidhā sthitam tad ca ubhayam vinā avidyā saṃbandham na eva sidhyati iti na ca svarūpa jñapteḥ svatas  kāla ādi asaṃbandhe asattva āpātena svatas saṃbandha abhāve asarva gatatva āpātena ca avidyayā iva svata eva anyena saṃbandhaḥ  vaktavya iti vācyam avidyā saṃbandhasya api āvidyaka tvena avidyayā iva iti dṛṣṭānta anupapatteḥ svatas  paratas  vā kāla ādi saṃbandhena sarva saṃbandhena ca asat vailakṣaṇya sarva gata tvayoḥ upapatteḥ na tayorthe svatas  kāla saṃbandha sarva saṃbandha apekṣā asaṅgatva śrutiḥ api svatas  saṅga abhāva viṣaya tvena upapadyate ata eva ajña tā akhila saṃvettuḥ ghaṭate na kutaścanā iti nirastam tasmāñcit mātra āśritā eva avidyā iti ajñāna vāde sarvajñasya avidyā āśrayatva upapattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde avidyāyā vācaspati sammata jīva āśrayatva upapattiḥ vācaspati miśraiḥ tu jīva āśritā evā avidyā nigadyate nanu jīva āśritā avidyā tad pratibimbita caitanyam vā tad avacchinna catanyam vā tad kalpita bhedam vā jīvaḥ tathā ca anyonya āśraya iti ced na kim ayam anyonya āśraya utpattau jñaptau sthitau vā na ādyaḥ anādi tvāt ubhayoḥ na dvitīyaḥ ajñānasya cit bhā āsya tve api citeḥ sva prakāśa tvena tad abhāsya tvāt na tṛtīyaḥ sa kim paraspara āśrita tvena vā paraspara sa apekṣa sthitika tvena vā syāt  tad na ubhayasya api asiddheḥ ajñānasya cit āśraya tve cit adhīna sthitika tve api citi avidyā āśritatva tad adhīna sthitika tvayoḥ abhāvāt na ca evam anyonya adhīna tā kṣatiḥ samāna kālīnayoḥ api avacchedyāvacchedaka bhāva mātreṇa tad upapatteḥ ghaṭa tad avacchinna ākāśayoḥ iva pramāṇa prameyayoḥ iva ca tad uktam ‘svena eva kalpite deśe vyomni yadvat  ghaṭa ādikam tathā jīva āśraya avidyām manyante jñāna kovidāḥ iti etena yadi utpatti jñapti mātra pratibandhaka tvena anyonya apekṣatāyāḥ  adoṣa tvam tadā caitra maitra ādeḥ anyonya ārohaṇa ādi āpattiḥ iti—nirastam parasparam āśraya āśrayi bhāvasya anaṅgīkārāt  na ca īśvara jīvayoḥ īśvara jīva kalpita tve ātma āśrayaḥ jīveśa kalpita tve ca anyonya āśrayaḥ na ca śuddhā cit  kalpikā tasyāḥ  ajñāna abhāvāt iti vācyam jīva āśritāyāḥ  avidyāyāḥ  eva jīveśa kalpaka tvena etad vikalpa anavakāśāt tasmāt jīvāśraya tve api adoṣaḥ iti advaita siddhau ajñānasya jīva āśrayatva upapattiḥ atha ajñāna vāde ajñāna viṣaya nirūpaṇam avidyāyāḥ  viṣayaḥ api su vacaḥ tathā hi cit mātram eva avidyā viṣayaḥ tasya akalpita tvena anyonya āśraya ādi doṣa aprasakteḥ sva prakāśa tvena prasakta prakāśe tasmin āvaraṇa kṛtya saṃbhavāt ca na anyat  tasya ajñāna kalpita tvāt aprasakta prakāśa tvena āvaraṇa kṛtya abhāvāt ca nanu kim āvaraṇa kṛtyam     siddha prakāśa lopaḥ  vā     asiddha prakāśān utpattiḥ vā     sataḥ prakāśasya viṣaya asaṃbandhaḥ  vā     prākaṭī ākhya kārya pratibandhaḥ  vā     na asti na prakāśata iti vyavahāraḥ  vā     asti prakāśata iti vyavahāra abhāvaḥ  vā     na asti ityādi vyavahāra yogya tvam vā     asti ityādi vyavahāra ayogya tvam vā nādya dvitīyau svarūpa prakāśasya nitya siddha tvena tad lopa anutpattyoḥ asaṃbhavāt tad anyasya ca sva prakāśe tasmin  anapekṣita tvāt  na tṛtīyaḥ jñānasya viṣaya saṃbandha eka svabhāva tvāt  svayam jñāna rūpa tvena tvad mate saṃbandha anapekṣaṇāt ca na api caturthaḥ tvad mate caitanya atiriktasya tasya abhāvāt  na api pañcamaḥ suṣuptau vyavahāra abhāvena anāvaraṇa āpātāt  na api ṣaṣṭhaḥ vyavahārasya abhijñātve svarūpa abhijñāyā idānīm api sattvāt vṛtteḥ ca mokṣe api asattvāt abhilapana rūpa tve mokṣe api āvaraṇa prasaṅgāt  na api saptama aṣṭamau tayoḥ api āropita tvena āvaraṇa vinā yogāt iti ced na na asti na prakāśata iti vyavahāra eva abhijña ādi sādhāraṇaḥ asti prakāśata iti etad vyavahāra abhāvaḥ  vā āvaraṇa kṛtyam āvaraṇam ca tad yogya tā ajñāna saṃbandha rūpā suṣupti ādi sādhāraṇī ābrahma jñānam avatiṣṭhate tena suṣupti kāle nānā āvaraṇam mokṣa kāle ca na āvaraṇam yad uktam asya api āropita tvena āvaraṇa sāpekṣa tvam iti tad naḥ ajñāna saṃbandha rūpasya āvaraṇasya anādi tvena cit prakāśya tvena ca utpattau jñaptau sthitau vā sva anapekṣaṇāt  nanu dvitīyatva ādi viśiṣṭe tathā vyavahāre api avasthā traye api asandigdha aviparyasta tvena prakāśamāna ātma rūpe adhyāsa adhiṣṭhāne sukha ādi jñāna rūpe cit mātre tad abhāvena tad kalpyayoḥ yogyatva ayogya tvayoḥ abhāva iti ced na śuddha rūpa ayaḥ citaḥ prakāśamāna tve api tasyāḥ  eva paripūrṇa ādi ākāreṇa aprakāśa māna tvāt  tad artham tasyāḥ  eva āvaraṇa kalpanāt  paripūrṇa ādi ākārasya mokṣa daśa anuvṛtta tvena śuddha cit mātra tvāt  na ca nirvibhāga citaḥ katham evam ghaṭata iti vācyam āvaraṇamahimnā eva paripūrṇam brahma na asti na prakāśata iti vyavahāraḥ asti prakāśata iti vyavahāra pratibandhaḥ ca adhyāsa adhiṣṭhānatva ādinā prakāśamānatā ca aviruddhā iti ata eva avedya tve satya parokṣa vyavahāra yogyatva rūpa sva prakāśatva viruddhe yogyatva ayogya tve katham idānīm api brahmaṇi syātām na ca ajñāna ādimattvena aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya tvam sva rūpeṇa ca tad ayogya tvam iti avirodha iti vācyam svarūpasya aprakāśa tvāt iti nirastam paripūrṇa ādi ākāreṇa idānīm vyavahāra abhāve api aparokṣa vyavahāra yogyatva anapāyāt na ca evaṃ sukha āderajñāna avacchinna cit prakāśya tve ‘sukha ādikam na prakāśata iti anubhava āpātena sukha ādikam prakāśata iti anubhava artham citaḥ ajñāna anavacchedena prakāśaḥ aṅgīkaraṇīya iti vācyam iṣṭa āpatteḥ anukta upālambhana tvāt  na hi ajñāna avacchedena cit  prakāśata iti brūmaḥ ata eva ca nitya atīndriye api ajñāna avacchedaka tayā aparokṣa vyavahāreṇa tatra api sva prakāśa āpattiḥ iti nirastam ajñāna anavacchedena tādṛśasya vyavahārasya ukteḥ nanu pradīpau  āraka ghaṭa ādivat caitanya āvāraka avidyā caitanyasya anya saṃbandham pratibadhnātu anyam prati caitanyam ācchādayatu na tu caitanyam pratyeva caitanye ukta yogyatva rūpa prakāśa virodhinī sā na hi dīpaḥ  ghaṭa āvṛtaḥ api svayam na prakāśate tamaḥ saṃbandha pātāt  na ca   kalpita bhedam jīva caitanyam prati śuddha caitanyam ācchādayati iti   vācyam āvaraṇam vinā bheda kalpanasya eva ayogāt yaḥ  mokṣe bhāvī cit mātrasya eva cit mātram prati prakāśaḥ tad abhāvasya eva idānīm ajñānena sādhanīya tvāt ca iti ced na kalpita bhedam jīvam prati śuddha caitanyasya āvṛta tvāt  na ca bheda kalpanasya āvaraṇa uttara kālīna tvāt idama yuktam iti vācyam bheda āvaraṇayoḥ ubhayoḥ api anādi tvena parasparam ānantarya abhāvāt yad ca uktaṃ yaḥ  mokṣe bhāvī caitanyam prati prakāśaḥ tad abhāva idānīm ajñāna sādhya  iti tad na mokṣe janyasya caitanya prakāśasya abhāvāt  kalpita bheda apagame śuddha caitanyam pratyeva prakāśasya jīvam pratyapi saṃbhavāt  yad ca uktaṃ  prakāśa svarūpe caitanye katham ajñānam na hi āloke tamaḥ iti tad na ajñāna tamasoḥ virodhitāyām anubhava siddha viśeṣāt tathā hi tvad uktam artham na jānāmi iti prakāśamāne vastuni ajñānasya anubhavāt  sva rūpa caitanyam sākṣī vā na ajñāna virodhi tamasaḥ tu āloke satyananubhavāt  āloka mātram tad virodhi vastutas tu  avatamase viṣaya prakāśa kāloka sahabhāva darśanena tamasi api na āloka mātram virodhi na ca tvad ukta artham na prakāśata  iti anubhavāt aḥ tu tatra bhāsamāne ajñānam sukha ādi sphuraṇam bhāsamāne na prakāśata iti ananubhavāt  katham tatra ajñānam iti vācyam sukha ādi sphuraṇam na prakāśata iti anubhava abhāve api anavacchinna ākāreṇa na prakāśata iti anubhavāt āvāraka ajñānasya tatra api āvaśyaka tvāt yad api   ‘tvat uktam artham na jānāmī atyatra bhāsamāne na ajñānam kiṃtu guhā stham tamaḥ channam itivat  tvad uktam na jānāmi iti anāvṛta sāmānya avacchedena eva viśeṣa ajñānam anubhūyate na hi para citta stham ajñānam prātisvika rūpeṇa anūdyate evam ca tad viśeṣa saṃśayam prati tad sāmānya niścaya iva tad viśeṣa avacchinna ajñāna jñānam prati tad sāmānya jñānam eva hetuḥ tathā darśanāt  na hi viśeṣe jñāte tad ajñāna dhīḥ dṛṣṭā avacchedaka jñānasya hi avacchinna jñāna hetu tā api darśanāt eva kalpyā na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvasya eva niyāmaka tvāt  iti tad na ajñānam hi viśeṣa avacchinna tayā bhāsate sāmānya avacchinna tayā vā ādye viśeṣe bhāsamāna tvam āgatam eva na hi viśeṣam abhāsayan viśeṣa ajñānam iti avabhāsayati tathā ca sāmānya niścaya janitaḥ api saṃśayaḥ  viśeṣam avagāhate yathā tathā sāmānya jñāna janitaḥ api ajñāna pratyayaḥ viśeṣam viṣayīkariṣyati iti kutaḥ bhāsamāne na ajñānam iti na dvitīyaḥ sāmānya jñānena tad avacchinna tayā eva gṛhītasya ajñānasya viśeṣa saṃbandhi tve māna abhāvena bhāsamāne sāmānya eva jñānam avagatam vastunaḥ pratīti pramāṇaka tvāt  tathā ca para citta stham yathā anūdyate tathā jñānam tathā eva ajñānam ca iti siddham nanu yathā dveṣasya iṣṭa tve api dviṣṭasya na iṣṭa tvam īśvarasya bhrānti jña tve api na bhrama viṣa ya jña tvam asmad ādīnām īśvara sārvajñya jñāne api na sarvajña tvam evam ajñāta jñāna abhāve api ajñāna jñānam iti ced na dṛṣṭānta asaṃpratipatteḥ tathā hi icchā tāvat jñāna samāna viṣayā jñānam cāvacchedaka tayā dviṣṭam api viṣayīkaroti iti icchāyā api avacchedaka tayā tad viṣaya tvāt na hi icchā iṣṭa tā avacchedaka āviṣayā bhavati etāvān eva viśeṣaḥ kiṃcid  sādhya tayā viṣayīkaroti kiṃcid  avacchedaka tayā īśvaraḥ api bhrama viṣayam agṛhītvā bhramam na gṛhṇāti bhramaḥ  hi bhrama tvena grāhyaḥ bhrama tvam ca rajata abhāvavati rajata khyāti tvam vā asat khyāti tvam vā anirvacanīya khyāti tvam vā tasmin gṛhyamāṇe sarvathā viṣaya grahaḥ iyān  tu viśeṣaḥ yad  bhrāntaḥ svātantryeṇa gṛhṇāti īśvaraḥ tu tad jñāna avacchedakatayā iti īśvara sārvajñya jñānam asmākam tu sarvajña padena tatra sarva pada pratipādyam jānan  eva asmad ādiḥ tatra jñāna saṃbandham gṛhṇāti iti īdṛśam sārvajñyam iṣṭam eva viśeṣaḥ tu īśvarasya na kutra api ajñānam asmādṛśām tu viśaṣeṣu ajñānam iti kṛtvā evam ca jñāta eva viśeṣe ajñāna jñānam iti na ca ghaṭa ādeḥ ajñāna avacchedaka tayā bhāne api ghaṭa ādi ajñāna nivṛttim vinā tad avacchinna saṃyoga ādi jñāna adarśanena prakṛte api viṣaya avacchinna ajñāna jñāna artham tad avacchedaka viṣaya ajñāna nivṛtteḥ api vaktavya tvena ajñāna avirodhi jñānavat ajñāna avirodhinī ajñāna nivṛttiḥ api svīkāryā syāt iti vācyam saṃyoga ādi sattvasya avacchedaka ghaṭa ādi sattva sāpekṣa tve api yathā abhāve na svādhikaraṇīya pratiyogi rūpa avacchedaka sattva apekṣā virodhāt  tathā ajñāna jñānasya api na sva viṣaya ajñāna nivṛtti apekṣā virodhāt  na ca evam   tad viṣayaka jñāna apekṣā api mā astu virodhasya samāna tvāt  avirodha kalpanā bījasya jñāna iva ajñāna nivṛttau  api samāna tvāt  tathā ca viṣaye ajñāta eva ajñānam jñāyate viṣaya viśeṣa avacchinna buddhiḥ tu tamasi iva viśeṣa jñāna anantaram ‘etāvat kālam amum artham na ājñā siṣam i ati evaṃrūpā jāyata iti vācyam hanta evam abhāva svabhāva virodhi pratiyogi jñāna nirapekṣa jñāna viṣaya tvam abhāva vailakṣaṇya sādhakam ajñāne upapāditam āyuṣma tā kiṃca yadi ajñānam sva kāle viṣaya avacchinna tayā na bhāsayet  tadā tu ‘tvat uktam artham na jānāmī ati viṣaya avacchinna ajñānasya vartamāna artha pratyayaḥ viruddhi eta tasmāt  viṣaya ajñāna sādhaka tvāt sākṣi rūpa viṣaya prakāśaḥ api na ajñāna virodhī kiṃtu pramāṇa vṛttiḥ eka viṣaya tve api pramāṇa vṛtti tad ati rikta vṛttyoḥ ajñāna virodhitva avirodhi tve ghaṭa viṣayakayoḥ saurāloka jñānayoḥ saura cākṣuṣa prakāśayoḥ vā tamaḥ virodhitvā virodhi tvavat upapadyete na ca vṛttiḥ caitanyasya viṣaya uparāga artha iti mate asyāḥ  ajñāna nivartakatva abhāvāt idam ayuktam iti vācyam ajñāna nivartaka tvena nivṛtti prayojaka tvasya eva ukta tvāt  tad ca saṃbandha saṃpādana dvārā asmin pakṣe api asti eva na ca ajñānasya sva virodhi jñāna abhāva vyāpaka tvena mokṣe api ajñāna āpāta iti vācyam mokṣa daśa āyāma jñāna nivṛtti śravaṇena sva virodhi jñāna prāgabhāva mātra vyāpaka tvāt  na ca katham pramāṇa vṛtti mātra virodhi tve ajñānasya jñāna mātra virodhi tvena eva na jānāmi iti ākāreṇa pratyayaḥ iti vācyam ghaṭa ādi mātra virodhinaḥ  ghaṭa abhāva ādeḥ bhāva sāmānya virodhi tvena abhāva tvena pratītivat  jñāna viśeṣa virodhinaḥ api ajñānasya jñāna sāmānya virodhi tvena pratīti saṃbhavāt  na hi abhāva pada ādinā abhāva pratītau ghaṭa abhāvaḥ  na bhāsate atha sā virodhitā tatra viśeṣa mātra paryavasannā samam prakṛte api anyatra abhiniveśāt  na ca ana jānāmī ati jñapti virodhi tvasya eva anubhavāt  katham vṛtti virodhi tvam tvad mate caitanyasya eva jñapti tvāt  caitanya ajñānayoḥ avirodhe jñānatva ajñānatva ayogāt iti vācyam mad mate vṛtti pratibimbita caitanyam jānāmi iti vyavahāra viṣayaḥ tathā ca na jānāmi iti anena vṛtti citorubhayoḥ api ajñāna virodhi tvam viṣayīkriyate evam ca na caitanye ajñāna virodhi tvam na api vṛttau vṛti upārūḍha cita eva artha prakāśaka tvena tathā tvāt  nanu vṛtteḥ api artha prakāśaka tvam vinā jāti viśeṣeṇa eva ajñāna tad kārya nivartaka tve icchā ādi nivarti adveṣa ādivat  sattva āpattyā śuktyādi jñānavat artha prakāśaka tvena tad nivartaka tve vaktavye caitanyasya api tad sattvena tad nivartakatva avaśyambhāvena tad nivṛtti āpātaḥ nitya atīndriye parokṣa vṛttau satyām api ajñāna anivṛttyā sukha ādau  aparokṣa vṛtti abhāve api sphuraṇa mātreṇa ajñāna adarśanena ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām sphuraṇasya eva ajñāna virodhi tvāt iti ced na pramāṇa vṛtti upārūḍha prakāśa tvena nivartaka tvam brūmaḥ na tu jāti viśeṣeṇa prakāśatva mātreṇa vā atas  na icchā ādi nivarti dveṣa ādivat etad nivartyānām sattva āpattiḥ na vā caitanya mātrasya nivartakatva āpattiḥ ata eva śābda ādi vṛttau satyām api ajñāna anivṛttyā sukha ādau pramāṇa vṛtti abhāve sphuraṇa mātreṇa ajñāna darśanena anvaya vyatirekābhyām sphuraṇasya eva ajñāna ādau virodhi tvam iti nirastam parokṣa vṛtteḥ viṣaya paryantatva abhāvena na viṣaya gata ajñāna nivartaka tvam sukha ādau ca jñāta eka sattvāt ajñāna nivṛttim vinā eva ajñāna adarśanam atas anvaya vyatirekayoḥ anyathā siddhyā sphuraṇa mātram na ajñāna virodhi na ca ātmanaḥ ajñāna āśraya viṣaya tve sva sattāya āma prakāśa vidhura tvena sva prakāśatva sādhana ayogaḥ paripūrṇatva ādinā aprakāśa vidhuratva abhāve api adhyāsa adhiṣṭhānatva ādinā prakāśamānatayā aprakāśa vidhuratva saṃbhavāt na ca vṛtti citoḥ vaiṣamya uktiḥ ayuktā vṛttivat sākṣiṇaḥ api samāna viṣaya tayā ajñāna virodhi tvā anubhavāt  anyathā sa akṣivedye caitra icchā sukha ādau maitrasya iva caitrasya api ajñānam syāt  naḥ ced maitrasya api ajñānam na syāt iti vācyam sākṣiṇi yad ajñāna virodhi tvam anubhūyate tad na ajñāna nivartakatva nibandhanam kiṃtu sva viṣaya icchā ādau yāvat sattvam prakāśāt ajñāna aprasakti nibandhanam vṛtteḥ ca sva viṣaye prasakta ajñāna nivṛtti nibandhanam eva iti ubhayoḥ vaiṣamya uktiḥ yuktā eva ajñāna aprasakteḥ eva caitra icchā ādau caitrasya na ajñāna vyavahāraḥ maitrasya tu pramātrajñānāt eva tad vyavahāraḥ na ca tarhi ātmani api tatas  eva tad aprasaktiḥ iti vācyam datta uttara tvāt  kiṃca sa akṣi vedya tvam tad aprasaktau
