adhimat tvāt ca na ca tāvatā sa dvitīya tvam tāttvikasya dvitīyasya evam api abhāvāt na ca evam atāt tvika tve dhvaṃsa nivṛttiḥ iṣṭa tvāt  na ca pratiyogi unmajjanam tādṛś dhvaṃsa upalakṣita svarūpasya eva virodhi tvāt  prāgabhāvasya pratiyogi dhvaṃsā ādau  iva nanu katham dṛś rūpasya brahmaṇaḥ sākṣāt draṣṭṛtva rūpam sākṣi tvam ‘sākṣāt draṣṭari saṃjñāyāḥ am iti anuśāsanāt iti ced  avidyā tad kārya anyatara pratiphalita caitanyasya eva sākṣi tvāt  tathā ca dṛś rūpasya api upādhinā draṣṭṛ tvam na ca upādheḥ api sākṣī adhīna siddhika prātītika avidyā kārya tvena cakraka ādi āpattiḥ utpatti jñapti pratibandhasya abhāvāt avidyā tad upādhika draṣṭṛ tvayoḥ ubhayoḥ api anādi tvāt nanu   sākṣī jīva koṭiḥ vā brahma koṭiḥ vā ubhaya anugatam cit mātram vā na ādyaḥ jīvaḥ  budhyupādhikaḥ aṇuḥ iti pakṣe idam aṃśa avacchinnacit vedyasya śukti rūpasya sa akṣi vedyatva ayogāt cakraka ādi āpātāt  ajñāna upādhikaḥ sarvagata iti pakṣe api ajñānasya api sākṣī adhīna siddhika tvena anyonya āśrayāt na dvitīyaḥ brahmaṇa eva sa akṣi vedya duḥkha ādi dhīḥ na jīvasya iti vaiparītya āpātāt  anyathā anavacchinna ānandadhīḥ api jīvasya iti syāt  brahmacaitanyam ghaṭa ādi prakāśakam iti mate ajñāna abhibhava dvārā tasya jīva caitanya abheda abhivyañjaka antaḥkaraṇa vṛttivat tādṛśa vṛtti abhāvāt ca na tṛtīyaḥ īśvareṇa iva cit mātreṇa api saṃsāri duḥkhasya tad gata tvena grahaṇe api yad bhāgaḥ  muktaḥ tasya cit mātrasya duḥkha ādi ullekha rūpa upaplava āpātāt supta maitram prati maitrīyājñāna ādeḥ maitrīyatayā iva jāgrat caitrīya duḥkha ādeḥ api caitrīyatayā supta maitram prati pratīti prasaṅgena maitreṇa etāvantam kālam duḥkham na avediṣam iti parāmarśa ayogāt iti ced na śuddha brahma atiriktasya budhi upādhika jīva atiriktasya sākṣiṇaḥ aṅgīkṛta tvena tad pakṣa ukta doṣa abhāvāt tathā ca avidyā vṛtti pratiphalitam caitanyam sākṣī suptau  api avidyā vṛtti svīkārasya prāk ukteḥ na ca anyonya āśrayaḥ prāk eva nirāsāt  śuddhasya sākṣitva abhāvena mukta upaplava apāta abhāvāt yaḥ tu supta maitre caitra duḥkha grahaṇa āpattyā etāvantam kālam duḥkham na avediṣam iti parāmarśa virodha uktaḥ tad na sākṣiṇaḥ sarva jīva sādhāraṇye api tad tad jīva caitanya abhedena abhivyaktasya tad tad duḥkha ādi bhāsaka tayā atiprasaṅga abhāvāt yad ca sukha ādeḥ sva anantara bhāvya vidyā vṛtti pratiphalita cit vedya tve jñāta eka sattva ayoga iti tad na mānasatva vādi mate api asya samāna tvāt  na hi tad mate jñāta eka sthitikatva atiriktam jñāta eka sattvam asti duḥkha ādi sama samaya utpanna vṛttyā api jñāta eka sattva upapatteḥ ca tasmāt  jñāna ānanda eka rūpam advitīyam nityam sākṣi ca brahma iti siddham iti advaita siddhau brahmaṇaḥ  jñānatva ānandatva advitīyatva nityatva sākṣitva upapattiḥ atha brahmaṇaḥ abhinna nimitta upādānatva upapattiḥ nanu nirviśeṣam ced  brahma katham tad eva nimittam upādānam iti abhinna nimitta upādānaka tvam jagataḥ vikāravat kāraṇasya eva upādāna tvāt  brahmaṇaḥ avikāra tvāt anyathā ‘nirvikāraḥ  haraḥ śuddha ityādi śruti virodha āpatteḥ iti ced na pariṇāmitayā upādānatva abhāve api vivartā adhiṣṭhāna tayā upādānatva saṃbhavāt vivartā adhiṣṭhāna tvam ca vivarta kāraṇa ajñāna viṣaya tvam eva tad uktam vārtika kṛdbhiḥ  ‘asya dvaita indrajālasya yad upādānakāraṇam ajñānam tad upāśritya brahma kāraṇam ucyate iti na ca upādāna lakṣaṇa abhāva ātmani kārya jani hetu tvasya eva upādāna lakṣaṇa tvāt  tasya ca pariṇāmyapariṇāmi u bhaya sādhāraṇa tvāt nanu brahma eva upādāna muta ajñānam api ādye satya upādāna tve satyatva āpattyā ajñāna upādānakatva kalpana virodhaḥ dvitīye sūtra dvayasya rajjum pratīva brahma ajñānayoḥ sama prādhānyena vā upādāna tvam nirvikāra śrutiḥ tu kevala brahma para iti vivakṣitam uta māyā śaktimat brahma upādānam nirvikāra stutiḥ tu tad anuparakta brahma viṣaya iti vivakṣitam uta māyā dvārā brahma kāraṇam aṃśuḥ iva tantu dvārā paṭam prati nirvikāra śrutiḥ tu advāraka vikāra niṣedhikā iti vivakṣitam na ādyaḥ ubhayoḥ samataya eva vikāri tvena brahmaṇaḥ  viśiṣya nirvikāratva ukti ayogāt  sita asita sūtra ārabdha paṭe sita asitatvavat jagati pāramārthikatva aniḥ vacanīya tvayoḥ āpātāt brahma svabhāvasya pāramārthika tvasya upādeya dhīmātra stha tve avidyā svabhāvasya anirvācya tvasya api dhī mātra sthatva āpātāt  tanmātra upādānaka tvasya tad tad sattva prayojaka tve anirvācya tvasya api abhāva prasaṅgāt  tanmātra upādānakatva abhāvāt dvitīye brahmaṇaḥ  māyā ākhya hetu uparāgam apekṣya vikāri tve mṛd ādivat  pariṇāmitva āpattiḥ viśiṣṭasya brahma tve nirvikāra śruti virodhaḥ abrahma tve brahmaṇaḥ kāraṇatva asiddhiḥ viśiṣṭasya mṛd ādivat dharmi sama sat tāka rūpa antarāpatti rūpa pariṇāmāt vivarta mata hāniḥ ca naca viśiṣṭa apekṣayā pariṇāma tvam śuddha apekṣayā vivartatvam iti vācyam śuddhe api vivartā artham āropita vikārasya āvaśyaka tvena nirvikāra śruteḥ tad paratva abhāva prasaṅgāt  tasyāḥ  viśeṣye tāttvika vikāra abhāva paratve viśiṣṭe vikāra ukti ayogaḥ tattvataḥ  nirvikāre āropita vikāra avirodhāt na tṛtīyaḥ aṃśoḥ tantum pratīva brahmaṇaḥ  māyām pratyupādānatva abhāvāt iti ced na ubhaya apariṇāmi tvena tayoḥ kāraṇatva aṅgīkārāt na ca tad pakṣa ukta doṣa avakāśaḥ ubhayoḥ pariṇāmitayā kāraṇatva anaṅgīkārāt  kiṃtu ajñānasya eva ata eva asādhāraṇyena nirvikāra tvam api na hi avidyā sā hitye api brahma pariṇamate kiṃtu vivartata iti na ca avidyā pariṇāma tve api satyatva āpattiḥ pariṇāmi upādāna sama sattākatva rūpasya satya tvasya pariṇāmatva nirvāhaka tvāt  brahma sama sattākatva abhāvena tad apekṣayā pariṇāmatva abhāvāt  sva samāna sattāka vikārā hetu tayā nirvikāratva upapatteḥ ca na ca satya upādāna tve satyatva āpattiḥ pariṇāmi upādāna dharmāṇām eva mṛdtva suvarṇatva ādīnām kārye anvaya darśanāt  satya upādāna tve api asatyatva upapatteḥ na ca satya asatya dhūma anugata dhūma tvasya iva satya asatya anugata upādāna tvasya ekasya abhāva iti vācyam sva niṣṭha kārya jani hetu tvasya ukta tvāt na hi satyāsatyatva vaidharmya sādharmya virodhi anyathā kiṃcid vaidharmyasya eva sādharmya virodhi tve sādharmya kathā uccheda āpatteḥ anābhāsa viṣaya saṃskāra janya jñāna viṣaya tvādeḥ ābhāsān ābhāsa sādhāraṇasya dṛṣṭānte api satvāt ca nanu avidyā upādānatva kalpanā na yuktā brahmaṇa eva rūpya ākāśa ādi upādānatva saṃbhavāt avidyā anvaya vyatirekasya nimitta tā mātreṇa anyathā siddheḥ iti ced na ghaṭa kuṇḍala ādeḥ pariṇāmi apekṣā darśanena gagana ādau  aja bovidyāyāḥ pariṇāmi upādāna tvasya āvaśyaka tvāt  na ca satyasya rūpya ādeḥ satya rūpa āpattimat pariṇāmi apekṣā na asti iti na sarvatra upādeye tad apekṣā niyama iti   vācyam sva viṣaya ka ajñāna anapekṣasya tad bhāva iti eva satya rūpa āpatti padena vivakṣita tvāt  na hi brahma ajñānasya rūpya ādi bhāva āpattau sva viṣaya ka ajñānam vyavadhāyakam asti kim ca vikāri tvena api avidyāyā upādānatva kalpanam na ca brahmaṇa eva atāttvika vikāra saṃbhavāt na tad kalpanam iti vācyam tad viṣaya kājñāna pariṇāmatva vyatirekeṇa vikāre atātvika tvā nirvāhāt  kim ca kārya apekṣita sva samāna sattāka upādāna tvena api avidyā upādāna tvam samāna sattāka tvam ca rūpya sthale sattva dvaividhyena vā brahma jñāna itara bādhyatva rūpa prātibhāsika tvam ādāya vā upapadyate tasmāt rūpya tad tādātmyayoḥ avidyā vikāra tve api idamaḥ  rūpya rūpā patti rūpaḥ  vikāraḥ katham idam rūpya rūpam āpannam iti apratīteḥ āropitasya āropam vinā ayogāt iti  nirastam rūpya ākāra pariṇata ajñāna adhiṣṭhāna caitanya avacchedaka mātra tayedamaḥ  rūpya āpatteḥ anaṅgīkārāt  yad tu kim idam upādāna tvam rūpa antara āpatti pratītim prati viṣaya tvam vā rūpa antara abheda dhī viṣaya tvam vā kārya abheda dhī viṣaya tvam vā na ādyaḥ asiddheḥ ‘śuktī rūpya bhāvam āpanna abrahma ākāśa bhāvam āpannam i atya pratīteḥ na dvitīyaḥ tad tvaṃpadārthayoḥ kṣīra nīrayoḥ muṇḍa gaḥ tvayoḥ ca upādāna upādeya tā āpatteḥ na tṛtīyaḥ sadṛśe sannihite nimitte api kārya abheda bhrama saṃbhavena avyāpteḥ iti tad anukta upālambhana tayā apāstam yad api bhrama adhiṣṭhāna tvena brahmaṇaḥ  na upādāna tvam atīta asatoḥ anupādānayoḥ api bhrama adhiṣṭhānatva darśanāt bhrama adhiṣṭhāne api śukti ādau  upādānatva avyavahārāt ca iti tad na caitanyasya eva adhiṣṭhāna tvena atīta ādeḥ anadhiṣṭhāna tvāt  kiṃca na hi vyavahāra abhāva mātreṇa vastu vyatirekaḥ vṛkṣa ādiṣu pṛthivī iti vyavahāra abhāve api pṛthivītva sattvāt yad tu māyā upādānam īśvaraḥ  nimittam śuddham brahma adhiṣṭhānam iti pakṣe abhinna nimitta upāda ānatva abhāvena tvad mate tad arthasya prakṛti adhikaraṇa ādeḥ anupapattiḥ iti tad na ekasya eva avidyā upahita tvena upādāna tvasya avidyā pariṇāma icchā ākṛtya ādi āśraya tvena nimittattvasya api saṃbhavāt  iti advaita siddhau brahmaṇaḥ  jagat upādānatva upapattiḥ atha brahmaṇaḥ  viśvakartṛtva upapattiḥ nanu evam kulāla ādivat upādāna gocara prayatna ādimat tvam kartṛ tvam uktam syāt  tad ca kāryasya kalpita tve na ghaṭate kulāla ādeḥ akalpitam pratyeva kartṛtva darśanāt  kalpitam ca rūpya ādikam prati bhrāntasya anyasya vā kartṛtva adarśanāt ca iti   ced na kulāla kārya ghaṭa ādau  api akalpita tvasya asampratipatteḥ rūpya ādeḥ api akartṛkatva asiddheḥ ca tatra api sākṣiṇa eva kartṛ tvāt na hi adarśana mātreṇa kartṛ apalāpaḥ tvad mate api sarvajña kartuḥ asiddhi āpatteḥ etena adhiṣṭhāna tvam na kartṛ tvam evam sati atirikta upādānatva abhāvena kartṛtva upādāna tvayoḥ sāmāna adhikaraṇya ukti ayogāt  na api bhrāntavat adhyāsat raṣṭṛ tvam bhrāntasya prekṣā pūrvakam āropita kartṛ tvasya abhāvāt  na api māyau  ivat vyāmohaka tvam eva kartṛ tvam vyāmohanīya jīva adarśane vyāmohakatva abhāvāt tad darśane bhrāntyāpatteḥ vyāmohaka tvasya api āropita tvena anyonya āśrayāt ca anāma rūpe vyākara vāṇī atiśruti anupapatteḥ ca na hi māyāvī jagat ādikam karavāṇi iti saṅkalpya karoti kim tu darśayāni iti saṅkalpya darśayati pakṣa traye api janma ādi sūtre artha labdha sārvaiya ādi sphuraṇa artha śāstra yoni tvāt iti sūtram iti yad  paramatam tad bhaṅgaḥ syāt  bhrama adhiṣṭhānatva ādinā sārvajñya alābhāt  na api upādāna gocara prayatna ādimat tvam kalpitam prati tad ayogāt  tasmāt  ‘adhiṣṭhāne tathā bhrānte bhrāmake ca na kartṛ tā laukikī kṛtimat tā tu na dṛṣṭā kalpitam pratī ati nirastam abhimata caturtha pakṣasya samarthita tvāt  yad tu uktam tṛtīya pakṣe vyāmugdha jīvat raṣṭṛ tve bhrāntatva āpattiḥ iti tad bhūṣaṇam eva bhrānti jñasya abhrānta tvāt yad api māyāvinaḥ saṅkalpa pūrvaka kartṛtva adarśanena vyākaravāṇi iti śruti anupapattiḥ iti tad na tādṛśa saṅkapā darśanasya māyā vinya saṃpratipatteḥ yad api uktam janma ādi sūtra artha siddha sārvajña sphorakam aśāstra yonitva ādi ati sūtram iti para mata bhaṅgaḥ syāt iti tad na māyā avitve api srakṣyamāṇa māyika viśva ākāra māyā sattva aṃśa pariṇāma ādhāra tayā sārvajñi alābhāt  tasmāt  brahmaṇaḥ  nimitta tvam upādāna tvam ca iti advaita siddhau brahmaṇaḥ  viśvakartṛ ta upapattiḥ atha brahmaṇaḥ abhinna nimitta upādānave pramāṇa upapattiḥ ayataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyanta iti ‘janikartuḥ prakṛti ariti sūtra prakṛti artha vihita pañcamī śrutyā ayat  prayanti abhisaṃviśantī ati sthiti laya ādhāratva liṅgāt ca upādānatva siddhiḥ ‘tadā aikṣata vyākaravāṇi iti īkṣaṇa ādi ādhāra tayā kartṛtva siddhiḥ ca atha vṛttau aputrāt  pramodaḥ  jāyata iti ādau  anupādāne api pañcamī darśanāt  prakṛti padam hetu mātra param iti uktam nyāse api imā iva āśritya ‘asati prakṛti grahaṇe upādānasya eva apādāna saṃjñā syāt  pratyāsatteḥ na itarasya prakṛti grahaṇāt  kāraṇa mātrasya bhavati iti prakṛti padam anupādāne api apādāna saṃjñā siddhi artham i ati uktam mahābhāṣye api ‘ayam api yogaḥ śakyaḥ avaktum golomāja lomā vilom abhyaḥ  dūrvā jāyante apakrāmanti tāḥ tebhya ityādinā loma ādīnām dūrvā ādīn pratyavadhi tvāt  ‘dhruvam apāye apādānam i atyanena eva apādāna saṃjñā siddheḥ idam sūtram anārambhaṇīyam iti sūtram pratyākhyātam kaiyaṭe api apakramaṇa  adhi tve loma ādiṣu kāryasya pratītiḥ na saṃbhavati iti āśaṅkaya bilāt niṣkrāmataḥ  dīrgha bhogasya bhoginaḥ avacchinna tayā tatra upalabdhivat kāryasya api dūrvā ādeḥ tatra upalabdhiḥ iti avadhi tvam eva tatra upapāditam tatas ca mata dvaye api ‘janikartuḥ prakṛtiḥ iati anena ‘upādāna eva pañcamī ati niyamaḥ  na siddhyati iti ced  mā evam apaśunā yajete atyādau paśu śabdasya paśu mātra vācaka tve api ‘chāgasya vapāyā iti vākya śeṣa anusāreṇa paśu viśeṣa paratvavat atra api kāraṇa mātra artha tve api upādāna paratva upapatteḥ avadhi pañcamīpakṣe ‘śṛṅgāt śara iti ādau śṛṅga ādi padasya niyāmaka abhāvāt nimitta para tve api prakṛte niyāmaka sattvena nimitta paratva abhāvāt ata eva ‘a ātmana ākāśaḥ saṃbhūta iti ādau  api prakṛti pañcamī ‘sat ca tyat ca abhava aditi vākya śeṣeṇa asaḥ akāmayate ati etad śākhā antara sthita vākyena ca pratīti sāmānā adhikaraṇyasya niyāmaka tvāt  na ca asa tapaḥ atapyata sa tapaḥ taptvā idam sarvam asṛjata tad sṛṣṭvā tad eva anuprāviśat tad anupraviśya sat ca tyat ca abhavat i atyādi śrutyā sat ādi bhavanasya jagat sṛṣṭi tad anupraveśa anantara bhāvi tvena jagat sṛṣṭitva anupapattau parameśvarasya sattva ādi guṇa abhivyakti para tvena brahma upādāna tve na asya prāmāṇyam anyathā katham abhavat iti uktam syāt  na hi śuktiḥ rūpyam abhavat iti ucyata iti vācyam sat ādi bhavanasya eva jagat sṛṣṭi rūpa tayā tad ānantarya abhāvāt tad anupraviśya iti asya mukham vyādāya itivat upapatteḥ na ca idam sarvam asṛjata iti anena paunaruktyam nimittatva mātra bhrānti vyudāsa paratvāt yad ca śuktiḥ rūpyam abhavat iti anubhavāt aśanamuktam tad śukteḥ anupādānatva prayuktam iti tad adarśanasya anudāha raṇa tvāt na ca mūrta amūrta prapañcasya sattyat padābhyām eva ukta tvena nirukta ādi pada vaiyarthyam iti śaṅkyam saṃgraha vivaraṇa rūpa tayā upapatteḥ nanu ‘saḥ akāmayata bahu syāmi ati vākyam na sṛjya sāhacaryam āha yena tad sāmānādhikaraṇyam īśvarasya pratīyate kiṃtu parameśvarasya ‘ajāyamānaḥ  bahudhā vijāyate yad ekam avyaktam i atya ādi śruti siddha tad tad ananta padārtha preraka ananta rūpaiḥ bahu bhāva saṅkalpam āha na ca svasya ananta rūpaiḥ bahu bhāvam saṅkalpya ‘idam sarvam asṛjate ati jagat sarjana anupapattiḥ niyāmaka rūpaiḥ bahu bhāvasya niyamya sāpekṣa tvāt  niyamyam sarvam sṛṣṭvā niyāmaka rūpaiḥ praveśa ukti upapatteḥ anyathā syām iti sattva uktiḥ na syāt  sṛṣṭeḥ prāc antaḥkaraṇa abhāvena tad viśiṣṭa aham artha abhāvena uttama puruṣa anupapattiḥ ca syāt iti ced na syām iti anena sukhī syām ityādivat  bhāvi sattva uktau tad anupapatti asaṃbhavāt anyathā saṅkalpa viṣayatva anupapatteḥ siddhe icchā virahāt idam eva ca bahu padasya sṛjya paratve vinigamakam niyāmaka rūpāṇām ca tava api mate īśvara abhinna tayā siddha tvāt  tathā ca id chāyā niyamya eva tvad mate api paryavasānāt  tathā ca icchāyāḥ tejaḥ prabhṛti viṣaya tvena bahu syām iti saṅkalpya tejaḥ prabhṛti sarjanam guruḥ syām iti saṅkalpya śiṣya saṃpādana ādivat iti nirastam yad ca uktam uttama puruṣa anupapattiḥ iti tad na tādṛśa avidyā pariṇāma viśiṣṭe aham iti prayoga saṃbhavena uttama puruṣa upapatteḥ evam eva atadaikṣata bahu syāmi atyāt yatra mānam bodhyam nanu ca yad tejaḥ prabhṛti sṛjyam tad ātmanā hi tvayā bahu bhāvaḥ  vācyaḥ teṣām tu tejaā ādīnām īkṣitṛtva sraṣṭṛtva devatā ātmatva śravaṇa at tāni cetanāni na ca cetanam pratyupādānam nāma iti   ced  satyam sṛjyānām īkṣitṛtva ādya saṃbhavena īkṣaṇa ādi kartṛ pratipādaka tejaa ādi padaiḥ teja ādi avacchinna ātmā bodhyate pūrva pūrva kārya avacchinnasya tasya eva uttarottara kārya nimitta tvāt tathā ca avacchedake tejaā ādau na caitanya nibandhana doṣa avakāśaḥ ‘asat vā idam agra āsīt  tatas  vai sat ajāyata tadātmānam svayam akurute atyādi api ukta arthe pramāṇam na ca ātmanaḥ karaṇe akuruta iti sattva ukti anupapattiḥ ākāśa ādi ātmanā kriyamāṇa tve api sva rūpeṇa sattva upapatteḥ etad artham eva ātmānam ākāśa ādi ātmanā akurutā iti aśrūyamāṇaḥ api arthaḥ kalpyate evam atadātmānam sṛjāmi aham i atyādi smṛtiṣu dharma sthāpaka śarīra ādi ātmanā iti vyākhyeyam na ca   ‘tatas  vai sat ajāyata iti tad śabda upātta brahmaṇaḥ prapañca utpatteḥ prāk  siddha tvāt tad ātmānam iti vyartham iti   vācyam nimitta tve pūrva vākyena labdhe api upādānatva bodhanena asya api saphala tvāt  nanu yad uktam brahmaṇi eva sṛṣṭi laya śravaṇāt  brahma upādānam iti tad na ūrṇanābhau tantu nimitte tantu layasya darśanāt  tatra hi yathā putram prati pitṛ deha dhātoḥ upādāna tve api na pitā tad upādānam kiṃtu nimitta mātram tathā ūrṇana abhidhātoḥ tad upādāna tve api tasya nimitta tvam eva brahmaṇaḥ api ūrṇanābhivat eva saṃhartṛ tvasya yathā ūrṇanābhiḥ ityādinā śravaṇāt ca iti ced na yadi api ūrṇanābheḥ na tantu upādāna tvam tasmin  aṣṭe api tantu upalambhāt kiṃtu bhukta āhārasya eva tathā api tatra na tantoḥ layaḥ kiṃtu bahiṣṭhasya antar praveśa mātram ata eva ‘yathā ūrṇanābhiḥ sṛjate gṛhṇate ce ati uktam na ca brahmaṇaḥ tad nyāyena saṃhartṛtva uktyā tadvat eva tad astu iti vācyam ‘tad jalāni atyādinā tatra laya śravaṇāt  tirobhāva mātre ca tasya nidarśana tvāt  sarva sāmyasya dṛṣṭāntatva aprayojaka tvāt  atad bhūta yonim i ati yoni śrutyā ca upādāna tvam na ca ‘yoniṣṭa indra sadane atyādau nimitte api yoni śabda prayogāt  na tena upādāna tā siddhiḥ ‘mukhyaḥ tu śabda svarasa ādi ati nyāyena kadācid anyatra kathañcid nimitte prayoge api autsargika mukhya artha tyāgasya prakṛte ayogāt  eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna śrutiḥ api upādāna tve mānam yathā ca na sādṛśya prādhānyābhyām upapattiḥ tathā uktam prāk  sarvam khalu idam brahme ati sāmānādhikaraṇya śrutiḥ api tatra mānam na ca   asarvam samāpnoṣi tatas asi sarva iti smṛtyā anyathā vyākhyāta tvāt na tatra mānatā iti vācyam adhiṣṭhāna tayā sarva vyāpi tvasya sarveśabda prayoga nimitta tvāt anyathā ākāśe api sarva pada prayoga āpatteḥ anupādāna tve prakṛti adhikaraṇa virodha āpatteḥ ca upādāna tvam śruti anugṛhīta anumānam api atra vivaraṇa ukta madhyavaseyam tathā hi   ‘mahābhūtāni sat vastu prakṛtikāni sat svabhāva anurakta tve sati vividha vikāra tvāt  mṛd anusyūta ghaṭa ādi vadi ati na ca vivartamate upādānatva anupapattiḥ sat pradhāna prakṛtika tvena artha antara tā vā ādau  eva tad upādāna tvasya sthāpita tvāt  prakṛteḥ sattva abhāvasya prasādhita tvena artha antara anavakāśāt ca na ca ‘khaṇḍaḥ  gaurmuṇḍaḥ  gauḥ i ati gaḥtva anurakta khaṇḍa ādau vyabhicāraḥ tad anurakta tve sati tad vikāratva āt iti atra tātparyāt  sat ati rikta gaḥtva ādi anabhyupagamāt ca ata eva ‘san ghaṭa itivat atra idānīm asan ghaṭaḥ asat nṛśṛṅgam ityādi prati iti anusāreṇa ghaṭa nṛśṛṅga ādeḥ asat upādānatva āpattiḥ iti nirastam na api brahma na dravya upādānam cetana tvāt caitravat  jaganna ānanda prakṛtikam tad svabhāvān anurakta tvāt yad  yad svabhāvān anuraktam tad  na tad prakṛtikam yathā ghaṭa svabhāvān anuraktam paṭa ādi na ghaṭopādānakam ityādinā sat pratipakṣa tvam vyāpti pakṣa dharma tayoḥ āpāta pratītyā sāmye api śruti anugraheṇa sthāpanāyā balavat tvāt  dvitīya anumāne kapāla svabhāvān anurakte ghaṭe vyabhicāraḥ ‘kapālam ghaṭa iti apratīteḥ na ca mṛd tvena tad anurakta tvam asti iti   vācyam sattvena atra api anurakta tvasya samāna tvāt  evam ca jagat abhinna nimitta upādānakam prekṣā pūrvaka janita kārya tvāt sukha duḥkha ādi vaditi abhinna nimitta upādānam brahma sidhyati na ca vyartha viśeṣaṇa tvam prekṣā pūrvaka tvāt kārya tvāt iti hetu dvaye tātparyāt  na ca tvad mate duḥkha ādīnām antaḥkaraṇa upādānaka tvena sādhya vaikalyam iti vācyam asmad mate antaḥkaraṇasya pariṇāmi upādāna tve api antaḥkaraṇa rūpeṇa pariṇata ajñāna ādhāra tayā vivartā upādāna tvasya anapāyāt kārya tvāt iti hetau sarva kārya nimitta kāla ghaṭa saṃyogasya ubhaya vādi saṃpratipannasya dṛṣṭāntasya lābhāt ca na ca jagat upādānam na kartṛ  dravya upādāna tvāt  mṛdvat  jagatkartā vā na dravya upādānam kartṛ tvāt kulāla ādivat ityādinā sat pratipakṣa tvam śruti virodhena hīna bala tvāt  ādye anumāne jaḍa tvasya dvitīya anumāne sarva anantaryāmi tvasya ca upādhi tvāt  bādha unnīta tayā pakṣetara tve api doṣa tvāt  tasmāt jagat upādānam brahma kartṛ  ca iti siddham iti advaita siddhau brahmaṇaḥ  jagat abhinna nimitta upādāna tve pramāṇa upapattiḥ atha brahmaṇaḥ sva prakāśatva lakṣaṇa upapattiḥ nanu pariṇama māna avidyā adhiṣṭhāna tvena upādāna tvam vācyam adhiṣṭhāna tvam tu na āvedyasya tad vedanā artham pramāṇa apekṣāyām anyonya āśrayāt na ca sva prakāśa tad apekṣam eva adhiṣṭhāna tvam iti vācyam sva prakāśa tāyā vaktum aśakyatvāt  tathā hi   kim idam sva prakāśa tvam vṛtti avyāpya tvam vā phala avyāpya tvam vā avedya tve satya parokṣa vyavahāra viṣaya tvam vā tad yogya tvam vā tad yogyatva atyanta abhāva anadhikaraṇa tvam vā na ādyaḥ brahmaṇaḥ api āvaraṇa bhaṅgāya carama vṛtti vyāpya tvāt na dvitīyaḥ atīta ādau nitya atīndriye ca ati vyāpteḥ na tṛtīyaḥ suṣupti ādau vyavahāra abhāvena avyāpteḥ na caturthaḥ yogyatva rūpa dharmasya mokṣa kāle abhāvena tadā brahmaṇi avyāpteḥ na api pañcamaḥ anadhikaraṇa tvasya api dharma tvena mokṣa daśāyām tasya api abhāvena avyāpteḥ ata eva na tādṛś anadhikaraṇatva upalakṣitam api tad  tasya api dharma tve muktau  abhāvāt iti ced na pañcama pakṣasya eva kṣoda saha tvāt  na ca mokṣe avyāptiḥ anadhikaraṇa tvasya sva rūpa tayā tadā api sattvāt  na ca svarūpa tve lakṣaṇatva anupapattiḥ tvad naye brahma abhinna ānanda ādau guṇatva vyavahāravat  svarūpa bhūte api anadhikaraṇa tve lakṣaṇatva vyavahārāt  na ca tvad mate yogya tvam api brahmaṇi mithyā iti tad atyanta abhāvaḥ api vācyaḥ tathā ca katham tad atyanta abhāva an adhikaraṇa tvam iti vācyam yogyatva virodhi atyanta abhāvasya vivakṣita tvāt  sva āśraya niṣṭhā atyanta abhāvasya mithyātva prayojakasya sva āśraya niṣṭha tvena eva avirodhi tvāt yad vā   vyāvahārikā atyanta abhāvaḥ  vivakṣitaḥ brahmaṇi ca yogya tā atyanta abhāvasya brahma svarūpa tvena tāttvika tvāt  na api avedyatva aniruktiḥ phala avyāpya tvasya eva tattvāt  āvaraṇa bhaṅge cita eva phala tvāt  na ca evam ghaṭa ādeḥ api vṛtti vedya tayā phala viṣayatva abhāvāt rūpya sukha ādeḥ api aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya tayā viśiṣṭa lakṣaṇasya ati vyāptiḥ iti   vācyam ghaṭa ādau phala vyāpya tvasya samarthita tvāt rūpya sukha ādau sākṣi bhāsyatayā aparokṣa vyavahāre api pramāṇa janyā aparokṣa vṛtti viṣayatva abhāvāt tathā ca phala avyāpyatva samāna adhikaraṇa tadvat tvasya paryavasita tayā sakala doṣa nirāsāt  na ca brahmaṇaḥ api vṛtti pratibimbita cit rūpa phala bhāsya tvena asaṃbhavaḥ tasya phala rūpa tvena tad viṣayatva abhāvāt na ca cit sukha ācāryaiḥ tad svabhāvasya api sphuraṇasya tad viṣaya tvam iti ukteḥ asaṃbhavaḥ tasya ācārya vacasaḥ tad prayukta vyavahāra viṣaya tayā tad viṣayatva upacāra nibandhana tvāt  ayam atra niṣkarṣaḥ vṛtti pratibimbita cit janyā atiśaya yogi tvam vṛttyā tad pratiphalita citā vā abhivyakta adhiṣṭhāna cit viṣaya tvam vā phala vyāpya tvam cit janyā atiśayaḥ ca na āvaraṇa bhaṅgaḥ na api vyavahāraḥ  vivakṣitaḥ kiṃtu bhagna āvaraṇa cit saṃbandhaḥ sa ca ghaṭādau  asti na ātmani saṃbandhasya bheda garbha tvāt  evam ukta cit viṣaya tvam api bheda ghaṭitam ghaṭādau  asti na ātmani iti sthitam pratikarma vyavasthāyām na api aparokṣa vyavahāraḥ  durvacaḥ aparokṣa iti śabda prayogasya eva vivakṣita tvāt  na ca alaukika pratyakṣa viṣaya dharma adharma ādau tādṛśa vyavahāra yogi tayā ativyāptiḥ yoga ja dharma atiriktā laukika pratyāsatteḥ anaṅgīkārāt tasya api sva yogya vyavahita eva sāmarthya āpādaka tvāt  na tu dharma ādau tad uktam   ayatra api atiśayaḥ  dṛṣṭa ityādi etena kaḥ ca ayam aparokṣa vyavahāraḥ  nāma aparokṣa jñāna janyaḥ  vā aparokṣa vastu viṣayaḥ  vā aparokṣa iti ākāraḥ  vā na ādyaḥ dharma ādau  apeya parokṣa yogi jñāna anuvyavasāya vyāpti jñāna janya vyavahāra sattvena ati vyāpteḥ na dvitīyaḥ vastuna āparokṣyam aparokṣa jñāna viṣaya tvam ced  ātmanaḥ api ghaṭa ādivat  vedyatva āpātāt  aparokṣa vyavahāra viṣaya tvam ced  vastu vyavahārayoḥ āparokṣye anyonya sāpekṣa tayā anyonya āśrayāt na tṛtīyaḥ nirākāra śuddha brahma viṣayasya akhaṇḍa artha niṣṭha vedānta janya vyavahārasya aparokṣa iti ākāra ayogāt iti nirastam vyavahāra padena abhivadanasya vivakṣita tvena carama vṛtteḥ tad anākāra tve api kṣati abhāvāt  na ca anupalabdhi gamya tayā avedye aparokṣa iti loka vyavahāra sattvena abhāve ativyāptiḥ prāmāṇika vyavahārasya vivakṣita tvāt  nanu aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya tvam na tāvat sarvān prati caitra ajñāne maitrasya tad abhāvāt na api jñānam prati tasya avyavahartṛ tvāt na api jñāna āśrayam prati jñānasya citaḥ anāśrita tvāt iti   ced na pramātāram yam kaṃcid  pratyeva aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya tvam vivakṣitam pramātā ca aham artha eva sarva saṃmataḥ yad tu uktam caitrasya jñāne maitrasya avyavahāra iti tasya caitra jñāna nimittakaḥ  maitrasya avyavahāra iti vā arthaḥ caitra jñāna viṣaya kaḥ  maitrasya avyavahāra iti vā arthaḥ ādye caitra jñānena maitrasya avyavahāre api sva jñānena eva ghaṭe brahmaṇi ca aparokṣa vyavahāra saṃbhavena vyartha viśeṣaṇatva asaṃbhavayoḥ abhāvāt dvitīye caitra jñāne tādṛś vyavahāra abhāve api kṣati abhāvāt  asmākam api hi citiḥ eva sva prakāśā na tu caitra jñāna tvena vyapadiśyamāna vṛtti upahita cit api vṛtteḥ asva prakāśa tvāt  evam ca sarva pramātṝn prati tādṛś vyavahāra viṣaya tā yogya tvam api saṅgacchata eva nanu vedya tve satya parokṣa vyavahāra viṣaya tvam tad yogya tvam ca vyāhatam tad aparokṣa vyavahāre tad viṣayaka sphuraṇasya hetu tvāt iti   ced na anyatra tad viṣayasya tad vyavahāra janaka tve api sphuraṇasya sva aviṣayasya svasmin vyavahāra janaka tvam svabhāva bhedāt  na ca ghaṭa ādau  api tathā eva astu teṣām asphuraṇa rūpa tvena tad viṣaya tvam vinā niyāmaka antara abhāvāt tārkika kalpitasya anuvyavasāyasya api ghaṭa jñāna jñānatva apekṣayā laghunā ghaṭa jñāna tvena eva ghaṭa jñāna vyavahāra hetutva kalpanāt ca nanu anavasthā abhiyā sphuraṇa antara anaṅgīkārāt svasya eva sva viṣaya tvam astu anyatra klṛptasya tad viṣaya tvasya niyāmakasya tyaktum ayukta tvāt  anyathā prameya tvasya sva vṛtti tvam vinā eva svata eva prameyam iti vyavahāra janakatva upapattyā kevala anvayitva bhaṅga prasaṅga iti ced na anavasthayā sphuraṇa antara tyāgavat abhede bheda niyatasya viṣayi viṣaya bhāvasya api ayukta tayā tyāga upapatteḥ prameyatva ādau kevala anvayitva bhaṅgasya iṣṭa tvāt  na ca evam gatiḥ api grāma iva svasmin  api sva kāryam karotu iti vācyam bheda aviśeṣāt tantuḥ iva mṛd api paṭam karotu iti asya api āpatteḥ svabhāva bhedena parihāraḥ ca sarvatra samānaḥ yad vā cit aviṣaya svarūpa tvam eva sva prakāśa tvam cit anyasya sarvasya cit viṣaya tvāt tucchasya niḥsvarūpa tvena na ati vyāpti śaṅkā na api asaṃbhavaḥ sva ātmani vṛtti virodhena chidāyā acchedya tvavat svasya sva vedyatva ayogāt na ca evam mithyātva anumiteḥ api asva viṣayatva āpattiḥ iti vācyam svapa rasādhāraṇasya ekasya viṣaya tā niyāmakasya tatra sattvena viśeṣāt  ata eva yathā chid ādau paraśu saṃyogaḥ  na svapa rasādhāraṇa iti svasmin vṛtti virodhaḥ tathā prakṛte api na ca tarhi chidā kāryasya chidāyām iva cit janya vyavahārasya citi anāpattiḥ iti vācyam phala darśanasya eva chidā apekṣayā svabhāva bheda niyāmaka tvāt  yad vā sva vyavahāre sva ati rikta saṃvid anapekṣa tvam sva avacchinna saṃvid anapekṣa tvam vā sva prakāśa tvam na ca sva vedya tve api upapattyā sva abhimata prakāśatva anupapattiḥ sva vedya tvasya bādhita tvena tad ādāya upapatti asaṃbhavāt nanu sva prakāśatva dharmasya tāttvika tve advaita vyāghātaḥ atāttvika tve asva prakāśa tvasya eva tāttvikatva apatyā tad sādhaka anumāna ādeḥ bādha iti ced na svarūpa tvasya ukta tvāt na ca pareṣām idam iṣṭam vedyatva virodhi svarūpasya paraiḥ anaṅgīkārāt  iti advaita siddhau brahma sva prakāśatva lakṣaṇa upapattiḥ atha anubhūti sva prakāśatva upapattiḥ na ca pramāṇa abhāvaḥ anubhūtitva hetoḥ vyatirekiṇa eva pramāṇa tvāt  nanu   atra sādhya aprasiddhiḥ na ca vedya tvam kiṃcid niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi dharma tvāt iti anumānena sāmānyatas  prasiddhiḥ iti vācyam avedyatva prasiddhau  api viśiṣṭa sādhya aprasiddheḥ tad avastha tvāt  na ca anubhūti tvena api tāvat eva sādhyam vedya tvasya vṛtti vyāpyatva rūpa tve tad abhāvasya carama vṛtti vyāpya anubhūtau bādhāt  phala vyāpyatva rūpa tve tu tad abhāvasya mama ghaṭa ādau tava dharma ādau śukti rūpī ādau ca pakṣa bhinne prasiddha tvena asādhāraṇa anaikāntika tā āpatteḥ asva prakāśatva rūpa tve pratiyogi aprasiddhyā aprasiddhiḥ eva kiṃca atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam kutaścid vyāvartate ced  tatra eva vyabhicāraḥ na ced atra vyabhicāra iti ced na cit aviṣaya svarūpatva rūpam sva prakāśa tvam anubhūti tvena yadā sādhyate tadā vedya tvam cit viṣaya tvam eva cit anya mātra vṛtti pakṣaḥ atyanta abhāva pratiyogi svarūpa tvam sādhyam yathā ca vṛtti pratiphalita cit viṣaya tā ghaṭa ādau na brahmaṇi tathā upapāditam iti nāsādhāraṇya bādhau na api atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvasya atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tve vyabhicāraḥ atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvasya mithyātvena atyanta abhāva pratiyogini eva atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tayā yad niṣṭhā ati anta abhāva pratiyogi tvam tasya kevala anvayitva abhāvāt na ca evam brahmaṇi cit viṣaya tve api tad atyanta abhāva upapattyā artha antaram ghaṭa ādau  api evam sādhya sattvena asādha araṇyam ca iti vācyam cit viṣayatva virodhi atyanta abhāva pratiyogitva rūpasya sādhya tvāt na artha antarāsādhāraṇye ghaṭa ādau tayoḥ saha avasthityā avirodhāt  brahmaṇi virodhāt  na ca tarhi virodhitvā aṃśam ādāya punar aprasiddhiḥ vedya tvam virodhi atyanta abhāva pratiyogi atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvāt ghaṭavat iti prasiddhi saṃbhavāt  yadā tu avedya tve sati aparokṣa vyavahāra yogyatva rūpam sva prakāśa tvam pūrva anumāne sādhyam tadā phala vyāpyatva rūpam vedya tvam pakṣaḥ aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya kiṃcid niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam sādhyam tathā ca aparokṣa vyavahāra yogyatva samāna adhikaraṇa āvedya tvasya sāmānyatas  prasiddhyā na aprasiddha viśeṣaṇatva asādhāraṇye atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvam kiṃcid niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogī ityādi vikalpa nibandhana doṣaḥ parihṛta eva etena ayam ghaṭaḥ etad ghaṭa anya tve sati vedya tvān adhikaraṇānyaḥ padārtha tvāt ityādi mahā vidyayā api sādhya prasiddhiḥ na ca vedyatva aniruktiḥ cit aviṣayatva mātrasya sva prakāśa rūpa tve cit viṣaya tvasya eva vedyatva rūpa tā prathama pakṣe tu phala vyāpya tvam eva vedya tvam na ca tarhi atīndriya anya tvena artha antaram siddha sādhanam vā aparokṣa vyavahāra viṣayatva samāna adhikaraṇasya eva vivakṣita tvāt  na ca ayam ghaṭaḥ etad ghaṭa anya tve sati vedya tvān adhikaraṇa anyatvān adhikaraṇam padārtha tvāt iti prakaraṇa sama tā śruti ādi rūpa anukūla tarka sadbhāvena sthāpanāyā adhika bala tvāt  pratipakṣa nibandhana sādhya sandehe api saṃśaya rūpa sādhya prasiddheḥ anivāraṇāt ca na api asiddhiḥ anubhūtitva jāteḥ kalpita vyakti bhedam ādāya śuddhe api sattvāt  na ca jāteḥ dharmi sama sattāka bhedavat vyakti sāpekṣatva niyamaḥ jāti anyūna sattāka bhedavat vyakti sāpekṣa tayā eva atiprasaṅga nirāse dharmi sama sattāka bhedavat vyakti sāpekṣa tvasya gaurava kara tvāt samatvasya anyūna anatirikta arthaka tvāt  na ca anubhāvya abhāve anubhūtitva ayogaḥ kadācid anubhāvya sattvena eva tad upapatteḥ anyathā āsīt iti ādi vākya janya jñānasya ananubhūtitva āpatteḥ na ca anubhūti tvam vipakṣāt avyāvṛttam anubhūti śabda vācyān ātmani sattvāt iti vācyam anātmani anubhūti śabda vācya tvasya eva abhāvāt vṛttau jñāna padasya iva anubhūti padasya gauṇa tvāt  ata eva parokṣa anubhavasya pakṣa tve bādhaḥ aparokṣasya pakṣa tve tatra vyabhicāra iti nirastam citva rūpa anubhūti tvasya vivakṣita tvāt  na ca aprayojaka tvam śruti anugraha sattvāt na ca parokṣa anubhavam api aparokṣataḥ  jānāmi iti ātmanaḥ  vedyatva grāhiṇā pratyakṣeṇa tad ā ātmānam eva aved iti śrutyā ca bādha iti vācyam ādyasya sākṣi anubhavasya vṛtti rūpa guṇa anubhava viṣaya tvāt na ca jānāmi iti jñapti viṣaya tvam eva anubhūyata iti vācyam aham arthasya jñapti āśrayatva ayogena jñāna padasya vṛttau gauṇa tvāt  ‘duḥkham jānāmī ati ādau  api duḥkha ādi ākāra avidyā vṛtteḥ eva vivakṣita tvāt ca dvitīyasya ca aham artha viṣaya tvāt tad anātma tvasya ukta tvāt  śruteḥ ca upaniṣad janya vṛtti rūpa vitti viṣayatva avagāhitayā cit viṣaya tvasya phala vyāpya tvasya aviṣayīkaraṇāt na api anubhūtiḥ sphuraṇa viṣayaḥ aparokṣa vyavahāra viṣaya tvāt ghaṭavat  caitrīya anubhūtiḥ caitra aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya aparokṣa jñapti viṣayaḥ caitra aparokṣa vyavahāra viṣaya tvāt ghaṭavat  caitrīya anubhūti caitra aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya aparokṣa jñapti aviṣayaḥ  na avatiṣṭhate caitram pratyaprakāśamānatva rahita tvāt  caitra icchāvat iti sat pratipakṣa tvam sphuraṇa prayukta vyavahāra śālitva rūpasya viṣaya tvasya mayā api aṅgīkāreṇa siddha sādhanāt  tad anyasya svasmin vṛtti virodhena bādhāt  jaḍa tvasya upādhi tvāt ca para vedya tve anavasthānāt  sva vedya tvasya viruddha tvāt  nanu svasmin sva vedya tvam katham viruddham na tāvat sva janaka indriya āsannikṛṣṭa tvāt svājanaka tvāt vā nitya cit viṣaya tvasya tad dvayam vinā eva ghaṭa ādau sattvāt  na api viṣaya viṣayi bhāva saṃbandhasya dviṣṭha tvāt  atīta āropita atyanta āsatām jñāna darśanena tasya ubhaya niṣṭha tvāt na api kriyātva karma tvayoḥ virodhāt kṛtya ādi viśeṣasya kāryatva ādi darśanāt  na api viṣayiṇaḥ viṣaya tve kartuḥ karma tā āpātāt  mithyātva anum iti ādeḥ viṣayiṇyā eva viṣaya darśanāt  mām aham jānāmi iti anubhava darśanena ca tad ā ātmānam eva aved iti śrutyā ca kartuḥ karmatva avirodhāt  evam ca para samaveta kriyā phala śāli tvam na karma tvam kiṃtu kriyā viṣayatva ādikam tad ca abhede api upapādyam iti ced  mā evam viṣaya viṣayi bhāvasya saṃbandha tvena bheda niyatayā svasmin sva vedya tvasya viruddha tvāt  na hi ukta atīta ādi sthale bhedaḥ  na asti ata eva kṛtiḥ kṛti antaram prati icchā icchā antaram prati vyavahṛtiḥ vyavahṛti antaram prati abhidhā abhidhā antaram pratyeva viṣayaḥ na tu sva ātmānam prati iti na sva viṣaya tve kiṃcid udāharaṇam asti nanu gati ādau gati antarāviṣaya tve api vastūnām vicitra svabhāva tvāt kṛtyā ādau kṛti antara ādi viṣaya tvavat anubhūteḥ api sva viṣaya tvam astu anyathā svasmin vyavahāra janaka tvam api na syāt  vyāpti jñāna anum iti ādeḥ svāviṣaya tve sarva upasaṃhāravatī vyāptiḥ anumiti mithyā tvam ca na syāt iti ced na vyavahāra upapādana artham sva viṣayatva svabhāva kalpanā apekṣayā svāviṣaya tve api sva vyavahāra janakatva svabhāva tvam eva kalpyatām lāghavāt  tāvatā eva tad upapatteḥ vyāpti anumiti ādeḥ tu avaccheda kaikya lābhāt tathātvam iti ukta tvāt ca evam ca kriyā karmatva virodhāt api na svasmin sva vedya tvam mithyātva anumiteḥ ca na sva karma tā parokṣasya akarma tvāt  yad uktam kartuḥ eva karma tvam tad ayuktam udāhṛta mithyātva anum iti ādeḥ akarma tvāt  mām aham jānāmi ityādau sākṣiṇaḥ kartṛ tvāt aham arthasya karma tvāt  tadā ātmānam ityādau ca aham arthasya kartṛ tvāt cit karma abhede tad dvaya adarśanāt  ata eva na bheda ghaṭita karma lakṣaṇa parityāgaḥ kriyā viṣaya tvam tu na karma tvam āsana ādi kriyāyāḥ  api ādhāra ādi viṣaya tvena sa karmakatva āpatteḥ atha avedya tve avedyatva sādhaka pramāṇa vedyatva āvedya tvābhyām vyāghātaḥ vedāntānām brahmaṇi prāmāṇya ayogaḥ brahma vicāra vidhi vaiyarthyam brahma ajñāna nivṛtti yogaḥ ityādi pratikūla tarka parāhatiḥ iti ced na cit aviṣaya tvam phala avyāpya tvam vā avedya tvam tasya tad sādhaka pramāṇa janya vṛtti vedya tvena vyāhati abhāvāt  vṛtti viṣayatva mātreṇa eva vedānta prāmāṇyavicāra vidhi ajñāna nivṛttīnām saṃbhavāt ca etena ajñāna nivartakatva mātreṇa vedānta prāmāṇye ātmanaḥ asiddhi prasaṅga iti nirastam ātmanaḥ svatas  siddha tvāt  nanu svata iti asya svena eva iti arthe sva viṣaya katva āpattiḥ pramāṇam vinā iti artha upāya antarasya anupanyāsena asiddhyāya āpattiḥ anyathā nṛśṛṅga ādeḥ api siddhyāpāta iti ced na māna anapekṣa siddheḥ eva svatas siddhi śabda artha tvāt na ca nṛ śṛṅga ādau  evam prasaṅgaḥ tad asattva vyāvṛtti phalaka pramāṇa abhāvāt prakṛte ca vṛtti viṣaya tā mātreṇa tad sattvāt  siddhirūpa ātmani siddha iti vyavahārasya siddhi prayukta vyavahāra viṣaya tayā gauṇa tvāt  na ca evam muktau vedya abhāve vittitva anupapattiḥ anubhūti nyāyasya atra api sulabha tvāt  na ca svāviṣaya tve sva viṣayaka saṃśaya nivartakatva ayogaḥ sva mahimnā eva svadharmiṇi vyavahāravat  saṃśaya ādi virodhi tvā upapatteḥ na ca ananugamaḥ tava viṣaya tāyām iva ananugatasya eva niyāmaka tvāt sva karmatva abhāve api sva nirvāhaka tayā svasmin vyavahāra ādi upapatteḥ ca na ca sva nirvāhaka padena nirvahaṇa kriyā kartṛtva karmatva uktyā virodhaḥ sva ati rikta nirvāhaka an apekṣatva mātreṇa sva nirvāhakatva upacārāt ‘svayam dāsāḥ tapasvinaḥ iti ādau sva ati rikta dāsa abhāva mātreṇa sva dāsatva vyapadeśavat na ca sva nirvāhaka adhyayana vidhi dīpa prabhā ādau svasmin kārya kara tvam sva viṣaya tvena vyāptam iti atra api tathā iti vācyam adhyayana vidhau  eka avacchedaka mātreṇa ātma āśraya an avakāśāt dīpa prabhā ādau sva viṣayatva asiddheḥ tad uktam khaṇḍane ‘gāṅkuṭa ādibhya iti atra bahuvrīhiḥ sva aviṣaye kuṭe api sva kāryam karoti tathā iha api iti na ca audbhūta avayava bhedaḥ samudāyaḥ samāsa artha iti kaiyaṭa ukta rītyā kuṭa ghaṭita samudāya eva bahu vrīhi viṣayaḥ sa ca vaiyākaraṇānām mīmāṃsakānām ca śaktyā anyeṣām lakṣaṇayā iti anyat etad yathā acaitra śālīyā ānīyantā amiti atra upalakṣaṇasya api caitrasya sva śālā sthasya tad śabda viṣaya tvam tathā kuṭasya api puṭa ādivat anya padārtha bhūta samudāya antargatasya bahu vrīhi viṣayatva upapatteḥ tathā ca dṛṣṭānta āsiddhiḥ iti vācyam sva aviṣaya iti asya autsargika viṣaya ani apadārtha bhinna iti arthaka tvam tathā ca sva pada artha saṃbandhāt anyatra iva sva pada arthe api yathā tatra phalam tathā sva saṃbandhāt anyatra iva svasmin  api cit phalam iti atra dṛṣṭānta paryavasānāt sva viṣaya vyatirekeṇa samudāya prayojaka rūpeṇa viṣaya tve api samudāyita aprayojaka rūpeṇa aviṣaya tvāt sva aviṣayatva ukteḥ vā nanu etāvatā svasmāt anyatra vyavahāra janane tad viṣaya tvam svasmin sva abheda eva iti paryavasitaḥ arthaḥ sa ca ayuktaḥ pakṣāt anyatra eva ayam niyama iti asya sarvatra su vaca tvāt  sva abhede sati api sva viṣaya iva svasmin viṣayatva vyatirekeṇa dveṣa icchā virodhi tvasya ajñāne svāvāraka tvasya smṛti ādi rūpa parokṣa jñāne sva vyavahāra janaka tvasya maitra caitanye suṣuptau caitra caitanyena pāramārthika ka alpa nikabhedayaḥ rāhitye api tad vyavahāra janaka tvasya adarśanāt ca ātmānam jānāmi iti ātma abhinna jñāne sva viṣayatva anubhavāt ca iti ced na tarhi dveṣa ādau sva abhede api sva viṣayatva adarśanāt  prakṛte api tathā syāt  atha vyavahāra rūpa phala darśanāt prakṛta eva sva abhedasya anyatra adṛṣṭam api sva viṣaya tā niyāmaka tvam kalpyata iti ced  tarhi sva vyavahāra rūpa phala darśanāt atra eva sva abhedasya sva kārya janakatā niyāmaka tvam na dveṣa ādau tathā phala adarśanāt iti samaḥ samādhiḥ na ca atra gṛhīta tad viṣaya tvasya tūṣṇīm tyāge sarvatra evam prasaṅga iti vācyam tad viṣayatva tyāga bījasya bādhakasya prāk eva ukta tvāt sarvatra tasya abhāvāt  yad tu uktam maitra caitanya ityādi tad na tadā eka viraha kāle maitra caitanya iti asya eva abhāvāt sākṣi caitanyena vyavahāra āpādanasya iṣṭa tvāt  yadi ca saṃskāra ātmanā avasthita antaḥkaraṇam tadā api bhedakam tadā bhedasya eva sattvāt ca yatu uktam ātmānam ityādi tad api na aham artha āśrita vṛtti rūpa jñāna viṣaya tvasya eva tatra anubhavāt  na ca ghaṭaḥ sva prakāśaḥ ghaṭa tvāt iti ābhāsa sāmyam prayojakatva parihāreṇa parihṛta tvāt  ghaṭe sphuraṇa abheda tad viṣaya tvayoḥ abhāve vyavahāra abhāva prasaṅgena sāmya abhāvāt ca nanu anubhūti padena vṛtteḥ pakṣa tve bādhaḥ tad anyasya āśraya asiddhiḥ iti ced na vṛtteḥ jaḍa tayā aprakāśa tve prakāśa tvam yatra viśrāmyati tasya eva pakṣa tvāt  pratikarma vyavasthāyām eva vṛtti atirikta anubhavasya sādhanāt ca evam ca tvadīya aparokṣa vyavahāra yogyatva jñānam tvadīya aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya tve sati vedya tvān adhikaraṇam jñāna tvāt  madīya jñānavat vivāda padāni jñānāni ghaṭa jñāna anya tve sati vedya tvān adhikaraṇāni jñāna tvāt  ghaṭa jñānavat iti api sādhu na ca  tvad jñānam tvad aparokṣa vyavahāra yogya tve sati avedya tvānadhikaraṇam jñāna tvāt  madīya jñānavat ghaṭa jñānam paṭa jñāna anya tve sati cit aviṣaya tvānadhikaraṇam jñāna tvāt  paṭa jñānavat iti ca yathāyogyam prakaraṇa samatā iti vācyam vipakṣe bādhakasya ukta tvena sthāpanāyā adhika bala tvāt  iti advaita siddhau  anubhūteḥ sva prakāśatva upapattiḥ atha ātma sva prakāśatva upapattiḥ evam ca cit abhinnasya ātmanaḥ api sva prakāśa tvam cit rūpa tvāt  sādhanīyam yathā ca na ātmani cit rūpatva asiddhiḥ tathā upapāditam upapādayiṣyate ca śrutyā na ca ‘vijñātā prajñāte ati śruti virodhaḥ vakṣyamāṇa aneka śruti virodhena tasyāḥ vṛtti rūpa jñāna āśrayatva paratvāt yad tu vidyā sāgara uktam avimatam jñānam bhinna āśraya viṣaya kam jñāna tvāt  jñāna antaravat vimatam na sva āśraya viṣaya kam guṇa tvāt  agni auṣṇya ādivat i ati sva prakāśatva sādhanam tad  para rītyā asmad mate sva prakāśe jñāna tvasya ātmani abhāvāt tādṛś jñāne guṇatva abhāvāt ca ‘mām aham jānāmī ati pratyakṣasya vṛtti viṣaya tayā upapādita tvena virodha abhāvāt na ca ajñāna iva sva āśraya viṣayatva upapattyā aprayojakam iti vācyam vedya tve ātmanaḥ  vedanā bhāvāt ajñāna daśā āyām ā ātmani saṃśaya viparyaya vyatireka nirṇaya prasaṅgāt  na ca ātmani aham anaham vā iti kaścid sandigdhe anya eva iti vā viparyasyati na aham iti vā vyatirekam nirṇayati iti asva prakāśa tve bādhaka sattvāt  na ca tvad mate sandeha ādya viṣayasya aham arthasya anātma tvāt tad anyasmin śabda eka gamya ātmani sandeha ādi sattvāt aprayojaka tvam tad avastham eva iti vācyam aham arthasya cit acit granthi rūpa tayā ahaṃtvā avacchedenācidaṃśe sandeha ādi bhāvavat cit aṃśe api sandeha ādi abhāvāt  na ca śabda ja antaḥkaraṇa viṣaya tad vṛttau vyabhicāri jñāna tvam iti vācyam tasya sphuraṇa arthaka tvāt  na ca dvitīya hetoḥ tejaḥ rūpasya ghaṭa iva sva āśraye api tamaḥ nivartaka tayā tad viṣaye vyabhicāraḥ rūpasya jñāna ādivat  sa viṣayatva abhāvāt ‘atra ayam puruṣaḥ svayaṃjyotiri atyādi śrutiḥ api atra pramāṇam tathā hi aastam ita āditye yājñavalkye atyādinā ‘kim jyotiḥ eva ayam puruṣa iti antena jñāna sādhana āloka ādi abhāve jīvasya katham sphuraṇam iti ukte ‘ātmā eva asya jyotiḥ svayaṃjyotiri atyādinā sva atirikta anapekṣa tayā sva prakāśa tvam uktam na ca ātma śabdasya paramātma paratvam pūrva vākye ātmani nāḍī saṃbandha pratipādanāt  uttara vākye ca ‘katama ātmā yaḥ ayam vijñāna mayaḥ prāṇeṣu hṛdi antarjyotiḥ i ati uttara vākya paryālocanayā saṃdaṃśa nyāyena jīva paratvāt  na ca dyubhva ādi adhikaraṇa nyāyena ātma śabdasya tatra eva mukhya tvam pradhāna ādi anā ātma nirākaraṇa artha tayā sva śabdāt iti ātma śabdaḥ  hetu tvena uktaḥ na tu mukhyatva abhiprāyeṇa jīvasya aprasakteḥ mukhya tvasya ubhaya sādhāraṇyāt ca ata eva aatra ayam puruṣaḥ svayami atyupasaṃhārasya asya iti pada anuṣaṅgeṇa ayam īśvaraḥ  jīvasya svayam eva jyotiḥ jñāna hetuḥ iti evaṃpara tvam nirastam ukta nyāyena upakrama virodhāt  na ca vācā eva ayam jyotiṣā asta iti jyotiḥ śabdasya vāci jñāna sādhane prayogāt atratyajyotiḥ śabdasya api jñāna sādhana paratvam na tu jñāna paratvam iti vācyam laukika jyotiṣi rūḍhasya jyotiḥ śabdasya vāci jñāna sādhana tvena pravṛttivat atra api tamaḥ virodhi tvena rūpeṇa ajñāna virodhinī api prayoga saṃbhavāt  na ca sva prakāśa paratve sadā sva prakāśa tvena śrutau  atra iti asya vaiyarthyam jāgrat avasthāyāmāditya ādi jyotiḥ saṃbhavena durviveka tayā asyām avasthāyām su viveka tayā atra iti viśeṣaṇa sāphalyāt  na ca asya iti ṣaṣṭhyā viṣayatva abhidhānam svayam dāsā iti ādau  iva ananya vedyatva paratvāt na ca amukhya arthatva āpattiḥ mukhya viṣaya asaṃbhavena iṣṭa tvāt  na ca pradīpa ādau sva viṣaya tvena sva prakāśatva vyavahāraḥ sajātīya prakāśa aprakāśya prakāśa tvasya eva tatra api vyavahāra nidāna tvāt  ata eva na ghaṭādau  aprakāśe atiprasaṅgaḥ vivaraṇa anumānāni ca ātmā sva prakāśaḥ sva sattāyām prakāśa vyatireka vidhura tvāt  prakāśa āśraya tvāt prakāśa kartṛ tvāt pradīpavat  nanu ca avedya tvam ced  sādhyam sādhya vaikalyam sajātīya prakāśā prakāśya tvam ced artha antaram ghaṭa ādau  ivāsu aprakāśa tve api upapatteḥ jñāna prabhā anugata prakāśatva asiddhiḥ ca jñātā ekasati duḥkha ādau  ādya hetoḥ vyabhicāraḥ dvitīya tṛtīyayoḥ tvad mata ātmanaḥ prakāśa tvena asiddhiḥ iti ced na sva prakāśya tvasya bādhita tayā tad aprakāśya tvena pakṣasya viśeṣita tayā vā artha antara abhāvāt sajātīya prakāśā prakāśya prakāśa tvam eva sādhyam evam ca na ghaṭa ādivat su aprakāśa tvena upapattiḥ sva aprakāśya sa jātīyā prakāśya tvena āvedya tvasya lābhāt  vijātīyasya aprakāśa tvāt  jñāna prabhā anugatam ca prakāśa tvam āvaraṇa abhibhāvaka tvam tad ca jñānasya cit tvena anyatra tejaḥ viśeṣatva ādinā iti anyat etad āvaraṇa tvam ca ajñāna tamasoḥ artha vyavahāra pratibandhaka tvam anugatam eva tad ca ajñānasya sākṣāt  tamasaḥ  jñāna pratibandha dvāra iti anyat etad na ca duḥkhe vyabhicāraḥ tasyāt yakṣaṇe prakāśa vyatireka sattvāt  prakāśa tvena viśeṣaṇāt ca na api dvitīya tṛtīyayoḥ asiddhiḥ para rītyā tayoḥ ukteḥ pratibimbasya bimba adhīna tayā tad āśrita tvena bimba jñāna hetutva upapatteḥ ca ata eva ātmā sva anantara utpattika prakāśa āśrayaḥ  na prakāśa āśraya tvāt ādityavat iti api sādhu na ca siddha sādhanam ghaṭa ādi viṣaya ka jñānasya tvayā api janyatva svīkārāt ānada bodhokam ca vivāda adhyāsitā saṃvid  sva samāna āśraya sva samāna kāla sva gocara jñāna viraha prayukta vyavahāra virahavatī na bhavati saṃvid tvāt anantara vyavahriyamāṇa saṃvidvat  na ca sva vedya tvena upapattyā siddha sādhanam asya para vedya tā aṅgīkartṛ viṣaya tvāt svāviṣayatva rūpa pakṣa viśeṣaṇa mahimnā tava anabhimata paryavasānāt avedya tvam tu brahmaṇaḥ śruti siddham eva na ca sākalyena āvedyatva parā saṅkoce kāraṇa abhāvāt etena jñāta tā liṅga anumeya tve ‘aham sukhī ativat  aham jānāmi iti parokṣa anubhava virodhaḥ guru mate ayam ghaṭa iti asya eva sva viṣaya tve sva janaka indriya sannikarṣa āśrayatva prasaṅgaḥ vyavasāya anuvyavasāyayoḥ pārthakya anubhava virodhaḥ ca nyāya mate anuvyavasāyasya api para vedya tve jñānasya pratyakṣa ātma viśeṣa guṇa tvena icchā ādivat avaśya vedya tvāt jñāna dhārā anubhava āpattiḥ vicchede caramasya niṣprāmāṇikatva āpattiḥ sāmānya pratyāsatteḥ abhāvāt evam ca vyavasāya sukha ādi gocaram sva viṣayam nityam eva jñānam sidhyati sva viṣaya tāyām ca na sva janaka sannikarṣa ādi apekṣā sannikarṣa ādi anapekṣā īśvara sarva viṣaya nitya jñānavat tathā ca evam prayogaḥ caitra sukha duḥkha ādikam caitrīya nitya aparokṣa jñāna viṣayaḥ tam prati jñāta eka sattvāt yadyam prati jñāta eka sat tad tam prati tādṛś bhāna viṣayaḥ yathā īśvara prayatna iti nitya jñāna siddhau tad  sva viṣayam nitya jñāna tvāt  sva vyavahāre anya anapekṣa tvāt  sva saṃśaya ādi virodhi tvāt ca īśvara jñānavat iti tasmāt ātmanaḥ  nitya guṇa bhūta jñānam sva viṣayatva rūpa sva prakāśa tvavat ātmā api tad viṣayaḥ yāvat dravya bhāvinā tena abhinna tvāt  mām aham jānāmi iti anubhavāt  ātma svarūpā saṃvid  sva viṣayā sva janya vyavahāra viṣaya tvāt uktā saṃvid  sva viṣayiṇī sva samāna adhikaraṇa svatva prakāraka sva viśeṣyaka saṃśaya virodhi tvāt ukta viśeṣaṇavat viparyaya virodhi tvāt veti  nirastam ādya anumāne sākṣi rūpa aparokṣa nitya jñāna viṣaya tvena siddha lādhanam saha utpanna jñānena api jñāta eka sattva upapattyā jñāna gata nitya tā paryanta sādhane tasya asāmarthyam ca na ca caitrasya tādṛś jñāna abhāve supta utthitasya parāmarśa anupapattiḥ saṃskāreṇa tad upapatteḥ nitya jñānasya parāmarśa virodhi tvāt ca sva viṣayatva anumāne ca dṛṣṭānta asiddhiḥ īśvare api sva viṣayaka nitya jñāna asiddheḥ aprayojaka tvam ca svāviṣaya tve api vyavahāra ādeḥ upapādita tvāt  kiṃca caitra nitya jñānasya sva viṣaya tve na ekam niyāmakam īśvara jñānasya nyāya mate vastu tvavat  sarva viṣayatva upapatteḥ na api abhedaḥ duḥkha ādau  abhāvāt na api samāna adhikaraṇa tvam ātmani abhāvāt dharma ādau tad sadbhāvāt ca iti ananugatam eva vācyam tathā ca kim aparāddham vyavasāya sva prakāśatva vādinā guruṇā anyatra sannikarṣasya niyāmaka tve api svasmin  abhedasya saṃbhavāt  pārthakya anubhavān anubhava rūpasya anubhava kalahasya tvad mata samāna tvāt  tasmāt vyavahāra eva ananugatam kāraṇam astu tad prayojaka anugama artham kim iti nirbandhaḥ paścāt api ananugama eva paryavasānāt  evam ca na sva viṣayatva rūpam sva prakāśa tvam kiṃtu avedya tve satya parokṣa vyavahāra yogya tvam iti siddham iti advaita siddhau ātmanaḥ sva prakāśatva upapattiḥ atha brahmaṇaḥ śabda avācyatva upapattiḥ nirdharmaka tayā avedya tayā ca brahma ānanda ādi pada lakṣyam na vācyam pravṛtti nimitta abhāvāt iti nanu avācya śabdena ucyate ced  vācyatva siddhiḥ lakṣyate ced  avācya rūpa mukhya arthasya abhāvāt  katham lakṣaṇā bhāve vā brahma na avācyam kiṃtu tīravat avācya rūpa mukhya artha saṃbandhi mātram iti syāt  mukhya artha hīnasya api brahma lakṣaka tve ghaṭa padam api paṭa lakṣakam syāt iti ced na avācya rūpa mukhya artha abhāve api nañsamabhivyāhṛta vācya śabdena vācyatva atyanta abhāva bodhana dvārā svarūpe lakṣaṇayā eva paryavasānāt  evam nirviśeṣa padam api akhaṇḍa pada lakṣaka tāyām eva mukhya artha avaśyambhāva niyamāt nanu evam lakṣya padena api lakṣya tve tīrasya agaṅgātvavat  brahmaṇaḥ alakṣyatva āpattiḥ iti ced na iṣṭa tvāt  sarvathā nirdharmaka tvāt  lakṣya vyavahārasya ca vācyatva abhāva nibandhana tvāt  tathā pratipāditam prāk  na ca evam lakṣyatva abhāvena vācyatva vyavahāra prasaṅgaḥ gauṇasya tasya api iṣṭa tvāt satya jñāna ādi padānām ca kalpita dharma vācinām brahma rūpa vyakti lakṣaka tayā akhaṇḍa arthatva anapāyāt  na ca sattva ādi dharma āśraya tayā lakṣyatva abhāve mañca saṃbandhitva mātreṇa lakṣyasya puṃsaḥ amañca tvavat  sattva ādi saṃbandhitva mātreṇa lakṣyasya brahmaṇaḥ asatva ādi āpattiḥ iti vācyam kalpita candratva ādi jāteḥ parama artha candra ādi vyakti tādātmyena acandratva abhāvavat atra api sattva ādi abhāva an āpatteḥ tad uktam ‘lakṣya vyaktiḥ api brahme ati ata eva sva prakāśa ādeḥ abrahmatve yad yad brahmatayā iṣṭam tad tad brahma iti sādhu samarthitaḥ  brahma vāda iti nirastam yad tu nirviśeṣa ādi padānām ca samāsa para tayā lakṣya ādi padānām yaugikatayā vākya tulya tvāt na vācakatā iti vaktum aśakyam anvita abhidhāna pakṣe teṣām api vācaka tvāt  abhihita anvaya pakṣe api vākya eva abhihita anvaya svīkāreṇa prakṛti pratyayayoḥ anvita abhidhāyaka tvāt  vākya tulyasya api vācaka tvāt  brahmaṇaḥ padārtha saṃsarga rūpa tve sa khaṇḍatva āpattyā padārtha tve vācyatva aparihārāt iti tad na pada lakṣya tve api apadārthatva upapatteḥ akhaṇḍa tve api vākya artha tvasya upapādita tvāt anvita abhidhāne anvita vācakasya api svarūpe lakṣaṇa aṅgīkārāt  na ca tarhi avācyatva asiddhiḥ akhaṇḍa brahma siddhi upāya tvena prāptasya avācyatva ādeḥ nivāraka abhāvena anuṣaṅgika tayā siddheḥ ayataḥ  vācaḥ  nivartante aaśabdam asparśam i atyādi śrutayaḥ ca atra anusandheyāḥ avācya śabdavat aśabda śabde api vyāghāta abhāvāt na ca iyam śrutiḥ adbhutatva abhiprāyā śrūyamāṇa artha tve bādhaka abhāvāt na ca ‘yataḥ  vāca iti atra api manasā saha iti śruta manaḥ vṛtteḥ iva antaḥkaraṇa vṛtti vyāpye brahmaṇi vāc vṛtteḥ api sarvathā niṣedha ayogaḥ lakṣaṇāyāḥ svīkāreṇa śakti mātrasya eva nirākaraṇāt  na ca ānanda ādi aneka padā mukhya arthatva apekṣayā nivartanta iti eka padārtha amukhya tvam eva yuktam iti vācyam brahmaṇaḥ  nirdharmaka tayā tatra śakti abhāvena bahu tvasya aprayojaka tvāt vācyatva virodhi artha dvāra evā khaṇḍa artha para tayā tad virodha tādavasthyāt  ata eva kasmāt ucyate param brahma ityādi śruteḥ paramātmā iti ca api ukta ityādi smṛteḥ ca tad tad śabda bodhyatva mātreṇa vācyatva abhilāpaḥ na tu śakyatva abhiprāyeṇa iti tābhyām na virodhaḥ tātparya viṣayaḥ  brahma vācyam vastu tvāt lakṣya tvāt ca tīravat iti ced  nirdharmaka tayā vācyatva bādhāt tad unnīta sadharmakatva ādi upādhi saṃbhavāt ca parama artha satya pada ādikam kasyacid vācakam padatvāt iti api na kim atra padatvam na tāvat suptiṅanta tvam samāsapadasya aśakta tvena rāja puruṣa ādau vyabhicārāt  na api śakta tvam sādhya aviśeṣāt avayava dvārā samāsapadasya vācaka tvam ced  iṣṭam eva na api satya jñāna ādi vākyam vācya artha tātparyavat śabda yuktam vākya tvāt iti api viṣam bhuṅkṣva ityādau vyabhicārāt  nanu avācya tve lakṣyatva anupapattiḥ vācya artha saṃbandhi tvena jñātasya eva lakṣya tvāt  tad jñānam ca na śabda bhinnena upaniṣad mātra gamya tvāt na api sva prakāśa tayā nitya siddhe śabda vaiyarthyāt  avācya śabdasya ca lakṣakasya eva vaktavya tvāt tatra api vācya saṃbandhi tvena jñeya tve anavasthā iti ced na tathā jñānam upasthitau  upayogi brahma sva prakāśa tayā svata eva upasthitam iti kim tena na ca evam śabda vaiyarthyam āvaraṇa abhibhāvaka vṛttau  upayogāt ata eva na anavasthā tasmāt  pravṛtti nimittasya durnirūpa tvāt avācya tvam tad uktam   adṛṣṭā guṇa kriyā jāti saṃbandhāḥ śabda hetavaḥ na ātmani anyatamaḥ  hi eṣām tena ātmā na abhidhīyate iti na ca āropita guṇa āśraya tayā vācya tā tasya tātparyā viṣaya tayā tātparya viṣaye avācya tvasya sthita tvāt  na ca satya ādi padānām lakṣaka tve siddhe nimitta abhāvaḥ tasmin  ca lakṣaka tvam iti paraspara āśrayaḥ nirviśeṣa vākyena na iti na iti iti anena eva nimitta abhāvasya siddha tvāt  na ca nirviśeṣa vākyasya sva rūpa mātra paratve pravṛtti nimitta avirodhaḥ nirviśeṣatva viśiṣṭa paratve ca tasya eva sattvena nirviśeṣa pada vācya tvasya eva prasaṅga iti vācyam dvāratayā upasthitasya sva para virodhi tvāt nirviśeṣasya vācyatva asaṃbhavāt ca tasmāt nirviśeṣa tvāt eva jīva brahma abhedaḥ siddhaḥ bhedaka asaṃbhavāt tathā ca brahmaṇi avācye yaḥ  vidvān vācya tām adhigacchati sa nistrapaḥ  nimittānām virahaiḥ pratibodhyatām iti advaita siddhau brahmaṇaḥ śabda avācyatva upapattiḥ atha sāmānyatas  bheda khaṇḍanam syāt etad  idam ayuktam bhedasya pramāṇa siddha tvāt  na ca bhedasya svarūpa tve anapekṣatva apatyā dharma tvam tathā ca anavasthā stambha kumbhayoḥ paraspara bheda grahaḥ anyonya bheda graha sāpekṣa iti anyonya āśrayaḥ ca evam ca bheda asiddhiḥ iti vācyam tad  kim bhede pratītiḥ eva na asti kāraṇā janyā vā bādhya viṣayā vā na ādyaḥ vikalpa adhikaraṇa rūpa vyavahāra viplava āpatteḥ na hi bhinna tayā ajñātena vikalpaḥ na dvitīyaḥ akāraṇaka utpatteḥ vyāhata tvena nityatva āpattyā tad nirāsaka mokṣa upāyān anusaraṇa āpatteḥ na tṛtīyaḥ ukta śuṣka tarkasya ābādhaka tvāt  anyathā aikyasya svarūpa tve anapekṣatva āpattiḥ dharma tve advaita hā niritya ādinā aikya buddhiḥ api bādhita viṣayā syāt  na ca   mama vaitaṇḍikasya para pakṣa mātram khaṇḍanīyam iti vācyam sva pakṣa sattve api tava tathā tve mama api tathātva avirodhāt na ca mama para pakṣa khaṇḍana mātreṇa sva mata bhūta aikya siddhiḥ mama api tāvat mātreṇa sva mata bhūta bheda siddhi saṃbhavāt na ca mām pratibheda khaṇḍana mātra niyoge mama eva vaitaṇḍika tvam iti vācyam mām pratyapi aikya khaṇḍana mātra niyoga saṃbhavāt madhyasthasya tvad anadhīna tvāt asvavyāghātakaiḥ eva tvayā aikyam dūṣyam iti yadā tadā asvavyāghātakaiḥ eva tvayā bhedaḥ  dūṣya iti api syāt iti ced  mā evam na hi vayam bheda pratīteḥ svarūpam kāraṇam vāpala pāmaḥ kiṃtu bādhita viṣaya tvam brūmaḥ vyāpti sadhrīcīnatayā aśuṣkaiḥ tarkaiḥ eva ananya parayā śrutyā smṛtyā ca bhedasya bādhita tvāt  viṣaya bheda ādinā pratyakṣa virodhasya parihṛta tvena śruti ādau  upacarita arthatva abhāvāt yadtva bhedasya api evam nirāsaḥ na ca abheda khaṇḍana yuktīnām svasya svābhedaḥ api na sidhyet iti sva vyāghātādābhāsa tā bheda khaṇḍana yuktīnām api bhūṣaṇa yukti abhedena sva vyāghātaka tāyāḥ samāna tvāt iti tad na bheda khaṇḍana yuktīnām tattvataḥ  bheda nivāraka tve api vyāvahārika bhedasya anirākaraṇena sva avyāghātaka tā upapatteḥ na ca evam brahmaṇi anṛta bhedasya tattvataḥ  niṣedhe tatra tad tādātmya āpattiḥ ghaṭe kalpita ghaṭa antara bheda bhrama sthale tad tādātmya adarśanāt  na ca evam abhedaḥ api tattvataḥ  niṣedhyaḥ tarhi svarūpa aparyavasānena śūnya vāda āpatteḥ kiṃca brahmā atiriktam aikyam asmākam na asti eva tasya ca tathā niṣedhe śruti virodhaḥ na ca mama ghaṭa atiriktaḥ  bhedaḥ  na asti tasya niṣedhe pratyakṣa virodha iti vācyam pratyakṣasya pāramārthika sattva aviṣaya tvena avirodhi tvasya prāk eva ukta tvāt nanu bheda bādhakam na bheda viṣayam eva tad sādhaka tā āpatteḥ na api abheda viṣayam evam hi tad anyaḥ tad virodhi tad abhāvaḥ  vā nañarthaḥ  viṣayaḥ  vācyaḥ sarvathā ca bhedaḥ  duṣpariharaḥ tad ananya tve tad virodha tadabhāva tvayoḥ ayogāt bheda abhāva grāhiṇā api pratiyogi vilakṣaṇa tayā eva abhāvasya grahaṇāt ca audāsīnyena pravṛttasya idam iti jñānavabādhaka tvāt ca iti ced na pāramārthikatva ākāreṇa bheda abhāva viṣayasya eva bādhaka tvāt  na ca bhede duṣparihara tā vyāvahārika bhedena eva vyāvahārika tad virodhitva tad abhāva tvayoḥ upapatti saṃbhavāt ‘yakṣa anurūpaḥ  bali ariti nyāyāt  bheda bhrama adhiṣṭhāna tattva gocaram jñānam bhrama bādhakam iti upapannam ukta rītyā bheda vailakṣaṇyena tad brahaṇa upapatteḥ yad tu ‘nāyam bhedaḥ  na asti atra bhedaḥ anyat eva bheda ātmanā pratyabhādi ati evam ākārakam bādhaka jñānam vācyam ‘nedam rajatami ativat  idam ca sarvathā bheda avagāhi iti katham tatra bādhakam iti tad na pratiyogitayā tad grahaṇasya tad bādhakatva avirodhi tvāt na ca atra bhedaḥ  na asti iti dhīḥ sarvathā na bheda abhāvam avagāhata iti vācyam anyatra bheda sattve tad bhedasya atra āvaśyaka tvena atra bhedaḥ  na asti iti asya eva kutra api na asti iti atra paryavasānāt  ekam eva nānā ātmanā abhāt ityādi bādhakam anusandheyam koṭyoḥ vyāvahārika bhedena tadvat tayā grahaṇāt ca yathā bādhakatva yogaḥ tathā uktam eva etena bhedāt  bhinna tayā sva artham bādha dhīrgāhate na vā ādye bhedaḥ sthiraḥ antye tu na sā syāt  bheda bādhikā iti nirastam sva rūpeṇa sthairye api tattvataḥ asthiratva saṃbhavāt evam ca āklṛpta viṣaya tvāt anyonya āśrayatva ādeḥ utthānam utthitasya ca nābhā satvam kim ca ayam deśya ābhāsaḥ anirvacana vādinaḥ prati na asmān vayam hi bhāsamānaḥ  yaḥ  bhedaḥ sa svarūpa ādi pakṣa antarbhāva bahirbhāvābhyām vā anyena dharma antareṇa anirvācya iti brūmaḥ na ca tarka ābhāsena anirvācya tve aikyasya api tad prasaṅgaḥ bheda bādhakasya anābhāsatāyā ukta tvāt  aikya bhedayoḥ śruti anugrahān anugrahābhyām viśeṣāt ca nanu brahmaṇi anṛta ādi vyāvṛttiḥ brahma jñāna ābādhyā vācyā śūnya ādi anā ātmaka ghaṭa ādau śūnya āditaḥ sva jñāna abādhya bheda darśanāt iti ced  brahma ghaṭayoḥ adhiṣṭhāna adhyasta tvābhyām viśeṣāt  anṛta tvasya mṛṣā tvena tad vyāvṛtteḥ api mṛṣātvasya yukta tvena ghaṭe tad jñāna bādhya tvasya ubhayoḥ samāna tvāt  na ca evam prātibhāsika rūpya ādi vyāvṛtteḥ api prātibhāsikatva āpattiḥ tathā ca bhrānti bādha vyavasthā na syāt iti vācyam viśeṣa darśana janyatva tada janya tvābhyām bādha bhrānti vyavasthā upapattyā prātibhāsika tvasya iṣṭa tvāt  na ca evam satya ādi vākyasya anṛta vyāvṛtti bodhakasya aprāmāṇya āpattiḥ tasyāḥ  ārtha tvāt  na ca evam vyāvṛttivat mṛṣā pratiyogikasya atyanta abhāvasya api mṛṣā tvena adhiṣṭhāna jñāna abādhya atyanta abhāva pratiyogitva rūpa mithyā tvam na syāt iti vācyam adhiṣṭhāna jñāna abādhya tvasya tatra aviśeṣaṇa tvāt  na ca evam ātmani dehabhedasya bādhya tve deha ātmā aikyasya mithyātvam na syāt iti vācyam bheda mithyā tvasya pratiyogi aikyā mithyātva aprayojaka tvasya ukta tvāt na ca nitya anitya vastu vivekasya sādhana catuṣṭaya antargatasya jñānam bhramaḥ syāt  tathā ca tena anitya parihāreṇa nitye pravṛttiḥ na syāt iti vācyam hāna upādāna upayukta rūpa avagāhi buddheḥ vyāvahārika prāmāṇya śāli tayā vyāvahārika hāna upādānasya nivartayitum aśakyatvāt  etena prapañce sat vailakṣaṇyasya mithyātve sat aikya āpattiḥ jagat mithyātva pramāṇānām ca atattva avedakatva āpata iti nirastam mithyātva niruktā yukta uttara tvāt ca etena bheda abhedasya bheda abhāve anyatara khaṇḍana sādhanābhyām ubhaya khaṇḍana sādhane iti nirastam tāttvika bheda abhāve api kalpita bhedena vyavasthā upapatteḥ na ca kalpitena akalpita kārya pratibandha ayogaḥ avidyayā sva prakāśa rūpa brahma kārya pratibandha darśanāt kalpita kāntayā viśleṣa kārya pratibandha darśanāt ca nanu bhedasya vyāvahārika sattva artham api tvayā anyonya āśraya ādikam uddharaṇīyam paraspara sāpekṣeṇa vyavahārasya api abhāvāt na hi vyāvahārika mṛdaḥ sva janya ghaṭa sāpekṣa tvam kiṃca atra na bheda mātreṇa tad darśana mātreṇa vā anyonya āśraya ādi āpādanam tathā sati vyāvahārikayoḥ api tayoḥ asiddhiḥ syāt  na api tad pratīti vāstava tvena tad āpattiḥ carama vṛttya vāstava tve api tad viṣaya vāstava tvavat upapatteḥ vāstave anyonya āśraya adarśanena vyāsya siddheḥ ca na ca pramā rūpa tad pratītyā tad āpādanam pratīti sāmānya eva tvayā anyonya āśrayasya ukta tvena pramātva paryante tatra doṣa abhāvāt na api tad pratīteḥ dharmi pratiyogi sāpekṣa tvena tad āpādanam tāvatā api tad sa apekṣatā mātrasya eva nivṛttiḥ iti ced na asmākam avidyā sāmarthyāt  sarva anupapatti vidhūnana upapatteḥ na hi māyāyām asaṃbhāvanīyam nāma tathā ca paraspara āśritam api indrajālavat darśayiṣyati na ca īśvara sāmarthyāt tādṛśam api satyam syāt iti vācyam ubhaya siddham ṛṣābhūta indrajāla sthale kāraṇa ādi vyavasthā ullaṅghi kārī ādi darśanavat anyatra tathā adarśanāt  darśane ca mṛṣātva eva paryavasānāt  āpādanam ca bhedaḥ tad pratītiḥ ca yadi māyikī na syāt  sarva vyavasthā ullaṅghinī na syāt  sarva vyavasthā ullaṅghinī ca iyam tasmāt māyikī iti viparyaya paryavasānāt  māyike vyavasthā ullaṅghanasya darśanena vyāpti siddheḥ ukta śrutyā asvavyāghātaka yuktyā ca bhedasya bādhāt abhedasya ābādhāt ca sva abheda sva bhedayoḥ vyāvahārika tve samāne api sva abhedam parityajya bheda eva sarvathā pradveṣaḥ  na akāraṇakaḥ iti advaita siddhau sāmānyatas  bheda khaṇḍanam atha viśeṣataḥ  bheda khaṇḍanam nanu nirapekṣa svarūpa tve sa apekṣatva anupapattiḥ iti yad uktam tad tāvat ayuktam avidyā nivṛtteḥ jīva brahma aikyasya ca tava mate mata dvaye api sthitau vyakti sāpekṣasya jāti mātrasya pratītau sa apekṣasya nīlataratva ādeḥ iva artha prakāśa ātmaka jñānasya brahmaṇi brahma abhedasya ‘asti brahme atyādau kāla sāpekṣasya astitvasya nirapekṣa brahma vyakti ādi rūpa tāyā darśanāt iti ced na avidyā nivṛtti jīva brahma aikyayoḥ pratītau sa apekṣa tvasya avidyaka tayā tāttvika nirapekṣatva virodhitva abhāvāt jāti mātrasya vyakti abheda asiddhiḥ vyakti samāna sattāka ghaṭatva ādau tad abhāvāt vyakti asamāna sattāka sattā ādi jātau tu sa apekṣa tvasya kālpanika tvāt  nīlataratva ādeḥ vyakti rūpatva asiddhau hetoḥ abhāvāt artha prakāśa ātmaka jñānasya brahma abhedasya ca sa apekṣatāyāḥ kālpanika tvāt  asti brahma ityādau  api evam eva tathā ca tattvataḥ  nirapekṣasya sāmānādhikaraṇyā siddhyā na tarka ābhāsa tā vyāpti siddhiḥ ata eva aikyasya asvarūpa tve advaita hāniḥ mithyātve bhedasya satyatva prasaṅgaḥ yatra yad adhyastam tatra tad virodhi tad jñāna abādhyam yathā śuktāvarūpya tvam yatra yadā aikyam bādhya tatra tad bhedaḥ tad jñāna abādhyaḥ yathā dūra stha vanaspatyoḥ bheda iti vā yatra yad adhyastam tatra tad virodhi tāttvikam yathā brahmaṇi anṛta tvasya adhyasta tve satya tvam tāttvikam iti vā vyāpteḥ iti nirastam aikyasya brahma bheda anaṅgīkārāt  virodhi anurodhinām sarveṣām brahmaṇi kalpita tvena tad jñāna bādhya tvena vyāptīnām asiddheḥ nanu—aikyasya nirapekṣa tve tad tvaṃpadārtha parāṇām asatyam vijñāna ghana ityādīnām aikya para mahā vākya eka vākyatva abhāvena vaiyarthyam syāt iti ced na aikyasya sva prakāśa brahma abhinna tayā sthiti prati iti ādau nirapekṣa tve api yathālakṣita artha bheda bhrama nivartaka vṛtti janane padārtha sāpekṣa tayā svarūpa para vākyānām eka vākyatāyāḥ sattvāt  bheda rūpa pratiyogi sāpekṣa tvena tatra sa apekṣatva vyavahārāt na ca ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ na iti nañarthasya bhedasya eva tādātmya niṣedha rūpa tvena vaiparītyam tādātmyasya tad niṣṭhā sā dhāraṇa dharma rūpa tve bhedasya abheda anapekṣa tvāt abheda rūpa tve bheda sāpekṣa tvena eva tasya tad anapekṣa tvāt na ca etāvatā aikyasya sa apekṣatva āpattiḥ kālpanikasya iṣṭa tvāt  ata eva ajñāna hānivat brahma rūpadhī vada bhedavat svarūpa tve api bhedasya sa apekṣa tvam hi yujyata iti nirastam tava sa apekṣatva nirapekṣa tvayoḥ tāttvika tayā dṛṣṭānta vaiṣamyāt  na ca bhede api evam eva astu bhedasya niṣedha pratiyogi tayā śrutatvena brahma rūpatva abhāvāt na ca tatra abheda śrutiḥ asti etena sva rūpeṇa nirapekṣasya api abhedasya abheda tvena sa apekṣa tvavat  sva rūpeṇa nirapekṣasya api ghaṭasya bheda tvena sa apekṣa tvam astu avacchedaka bhedena sa pratiyogitva apratiyogi tve api yathā tadvat iti nirastam bhedasya svarūpataḥ  nirapekṣa tve niṣpratiyogika tve ca parān pratīva svam api prati aviśiṣṭa tayā sva vyāghātaḥ na ca evam abhedasya api svān pratīva parān prati tathā asati tathātva āpattiḥ iṣṭa āpatteḥ ghaṭatva ādinā bhedaḥ para kalpitaḥ svarūpataḥ tu abheda eva tathā sati para tvam param vyāhatam na svarūpa tvam api yad tu sa pratiyogikatva niṣpratiyogikatva vyavasthā tu yad asādhāraṇyena sva vācaka pravṛtti nimitta avacchedena pratītau pratiyogi pratīti sāpekṣam tad sa pratiyogikam anyat tu niṣpratiyogikam iti tad na bhedasya svarūpa tve tad anyatva asiddheḥ etena ekasya arthasya laghutva kaṭhinatva ādinā ullekhena nirapekṣa tve api agurutva adravatva ādinā ullekhena sa apekṣa tvam api yathā tathā ghaṭa iti ullekhena nirapekṣasya api bheda iti ullekhe sa apekṣatva upapattiḥ iti  nirastam śabdānullekhe api sa apekṣa nirapekṣayoḥ anubhavāt ca laya ādivat  naña nud lekha mātreṇa dṛṣṭānta asaṃpratipatteḥ ca na ca ekasya eva gamanasya gacchati calati śabda ullekhābhyām ekasya eva ca prayatnasya karoti pravartata iti śabda ullekhābhyām karma sāpekṣatva nirapekṣa tvayoḥ śabda svabhāva prayukti darśanāt atra api ghaṭa bheda śabda ullekhena sa apekṣatva nirapekṣa tve syātām iti vācyam artha gata sakarmakatva ādīnām śabda svabhāva an adhīna tvāt  pratyuta ekasmin  eva tapadhātau  artha bhedena tayoḥ darśanāt  tapati ṛṣiḥ tapati pṛthivīm savitā iti ādau evam ca dṛṣṭānteṣu artha bheda eva phalam dhātu artha iti mate saṃyoga rūpa artha bhedāt  mata antare tu uttara saṃyoga avacchinna spandasya gamī artha tvam pūrva vibhāgā phalaka spandasya calati artha tvam anukūla yatnasya karoti artha tvam yatna mātrasya yati artha tvam iti na ca bheda tvam eva sa apekṣam na tu bheda iti vācyam sa apekṣa tayā viśeṣyasya eva anubhavāt  anyathā ghaṭa pratiyogikam bheda tvam iti ullekhaḥ syāt  etena ‘bhāva abhāva svarūpa tvāt na anyonya abhāva tā pṛthak  iti ukteḥ na sva rūpa mātram bhedaḥ kiṃtu anyonya abhāvaḥ sa ca vastunaḥ sa viśeṣa abhinna iti ukteḥ ca ghaṭa ādiḥ eva bhāva abhāva rūpa tayā bheda iti nirastam ghaṭa tada bhāva sthale bhāvatva abhāva tvayoḥ viruddha tvena kalpanāt  katham tad āśraya aikyam na ca avidyā nivṛtti advaitayoḥ api katham brahma aikyam iti vācyam asmad mate tatra abhāva tvasya kalpita tvena māyika tayā virodha abhāvāt tava tu dvayoḥ api tāttvika tvena virodhasya duṣparihara tvāt  ata eva tad tādātmya ayogya tvam vā tad aikya pramityaviṣaya tvam vā yatra yad darśanam tatra tad tādātmya adhyāsa virodhita tvam vā svāvṛttiyat kiṃcid dharmān ādhāra niṣṭhayat kiṃcid dharmān ādhāratva svarūpam vā svāvṛttiyat kiṃcid dharma ādhārā niṣṭha dharma ādhāratva rūpam vā svarūpa tvam tad abheda tvam anādhāra tvam ca ādhāra rāhityam na tu ādhārāt anyatvam iti na anyonya āśraya iti nirastam svarūpa tve sa apekṣatva anupapatteḥ atireke anavasthānāt  atyanta abhāva anyonya abhāvayoḥ ekyā patteḥ pramiti darśana ādi ghaṭita tvena cakṣuḥ ādi agamyatā āpatteḥ ca kiṃca bhedasya ghaṭa svarūpa tve tad nirūpaka pratiyoginaḥ api tad svarūpa tā āpattiḥ na hi bheda rūpa mātram ghaṭaḥ kiṃtu paṭa pratiyogika bheda rūpa iti nanu  na ayam doṣaḥ bheda pratiyogina upalakṣaṇa tvena svarūpa tāyām ananvayāt  anyathā duḥkha nivṛtteḥ pum artha tayā duḥkhasya api pum artha tvam doṣa abhāvasya sādhaka tā prayojaka tve doṣasya api sādhaka tā prayojaka tvam anṛta vyāvṛttyajñāna nivṛttyoḥ ajñāna ādi prakāśa rūpa jñānasya ca brahma rūpa tve anṛta ādīnām api tad rūpa tvam ajñāna nivṛtteḥ mokṣa tve ajñānasya ca mokṣa tvam ca syāt  na ca lamba karṇa ādau karṇa ādeḥ viśeṣaṇa tayā anvaya darśanāt atra api tathā citragvādiṣu ananvayāt tathā eva kim na syāt  anyathā udāhṛta sthale agateḥ na ca pratiyogina upalakṣaṇa tve tad ajñāne api kāka ajñāne gṛha jñānavat tad jñāna āpattiḥ iṣṭa āpatteḥ anyathā udāhṛta āgateḥ ca kecid tu pratiyoginaḥ ananvaye api śabdaḥ anitya iti ādau śabdatva ādeḥ viśeṣaṇa tvam iva atra api viśeṣaṇa tvam iti āhuḥ iti ced na na hi vayam paṭa bhedaḥ  ghaṭa svarūpam iti anvaya praviṣṭa tvena pratiyogitayā nirūpakatva mātreṇa vā paṭasya ghaṭa rūpa tām āpādayāmaḥ kiṃtu samāna adhikaraṇa pratīti viṣaya svarūpam prati pratiyogitayā nirūpaka tvena abheda nirūpaka pratiyogivat  na ca ajñāna nivṛtti ādayaḥ samāna adhikaraṇa pratīti viṣayāḥ bhedaḥ tu ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ na iti samāna adhikaraṇa pratīti viṣayaḥ anyathā samāna adhikaraṇa niṣedha buddhi viṣaya tvam bheda lakṣaṇam na syāt  etena  ‘puruṣa arthe duḥkham iva brahmaṇi ajñānavat tathā mokṣe ca mohavat na antargatam kumbha ādikam paṭe taṭa stha tve api kumbha ādeḥ apratītau na bheda dhīḥ ajñāna ādeḥ apratītau tad hi anyādi apratītivat  iti nirastam kiṃca vidāraṇa ātmanaḥ  bhedasya ghaṭava rūpa tve ghaṭasya api vidāraṇam syāt  evam tad avayavānām api iti paramāṇuḥ api na eka iti śūnyatā āpatteḥ eka abhāve tad samāhāra rūpa anekasya api abhāvāt nanu vidāraṇa ātmakasya abhedasya brahma rūpa tve pāramārthika brahmaṇaḥ  vyāvahārika prātibhāsika śūnyaiḥ api avidāraṇe tad aikyam api syāt  na ca jīva abheda eva svarūpam na tu ghaṭa ādi abhedaḥ tarhi atra api ghaṭa ādibhyaḥ  bheda eva paṭa svarūm na tu svasmāt iti samam iti ced na svarūpa tve bhedasya sva jñāna apratibadhya jñāna pratiyogika tve sva svarūpa tvena abhedavat sva pratiyogitva niyamena sva vidāraka tvasya āvaśyaka tvāt  ghaṭa dharmeṣu paṭa pratiyogika bheda tvavat  ghaṭa pratiyogika bheda tvasya api abhyupagamāt  paṭāt  bhinnaḥ ghaṭa itivat  ghaṭāt bhinnaḥ ghaṭa iti pratīteḥ vajra lepa tvāt ca yad tu svasmāt vidāraka tve avayavānām vibhāgena sūkṣma tvam eva syāt  na tu śūnya tvam na hi śūnya saṃyogāt  kiṃcid utpannam iti tad na vibhājaka tvam na vidāraka tvam kiṃtu ekatva virodhi tvam tathā ca ekasya abhāve anekasya sutarām abhāvāt śūnya tāyām eva paryavasānāt ca etena vidāra kalavitra ādeḥ sva saṃbandhini eva vidāraka tvam na tu svasmin  iti bhedaḥ ced svarūpam tadā svam na vidārayet  kiṃca bhedasya na vidāraka tvam bhāva vyutpattyā vidāraṇa tvāt  tathā ca svarūpa bhedena ghaṭasya na vidāraṇam syāt  sva vṛtti virodhāt iti nirastam bhedasya vidāraṇa rūpa vibhāga ātmaka tvena vibhāgasya vibhajyamāna vṛttitva niyamena avayavān avasthayā śūnyatā patteḥ tādavasthyāt  ata eva vibhāga rūpa vidāraṇa ātmā na bhedaḥ kiṃtu anyonya abhāvaḥ dhātūnām aneka artha tvāt tad uktam ‘kriyā vāci tvam ākhyātum ekopi arthaḥ pradaśyate prayogataḥ anusartavyā aneka arthā hi dhātavaḥ iti anyathā saṃyuktayoḥ bhinnau  iti vyavahāraḥ  na syāt iti nirastam anyonya abhāva svarūpa tve kapāla ādi rūpa āśraya pratiyogika bhedasya ghaṭa ādi rūpa āśrita rūpa tayā sva pratiyogika bheda āśraya tvāt eka tvam kapāla ādiṣu bhajyeta iti avayavān avasthayā śūnya tāyām eva paryavasānāt  ata eva na anekatva eka artha samavāyinā bhedena eka tvam nirākṛtya tena punar anekatva nirākaraṇam yujyate upajīvya virodhāt iti nirastam aneka tvam aspṛṣṭvā eva sva pratiyogika bheda mātreṇa aikya virahasya āpādya tvāt  ata eva uktam ācāryaiḥ ‘apada eka artha samavāyinyā ekatāyā bhedena virodha ādi ati yad uktam svasmin vṛtti virodhāt iti tad na vibhāga ādi rūpa vyāpārasya anaṅgīkārāt  itara virodhita ādi rūpa vyāpārasya sarvatra sattvāt  kiṃca svarūpa tve bhedasya saṃśaya ādiḥ na syāt  dharmi jñāne bheda ajñāna abhāvāt tad ajñāne hetoḥ eva abhāvāt  nanu abhedasya api svarūpa tve saṃśaya ādi anupapattiḥ tava api samā yadi ca abheda tvena ajñānāt tathā mama api bheda tvena ajñānāt tad iti ced na bhadasya svarūpa tve śūnyatā pādaka yuktyā koṭīnām eva ucchedāt na ca  abhedasya api svarūpa tve bheda koṭī ucchedaḥ tava api iti vācyam kalpita koṭim ādāya saṃśaya upapatteḥ na ca tava api bhedaka sattva ādi koṭiḥ kalpitā śūnyatā patteḥ iti ukta tvāt  yad tu prāk  caitanye svayaṃbhāte api tad abhinnasya ekyasya anavacchinnasya ānandasya ca aprakāśavat dharmiṇaḥ prakāśe api tad abhinnasya bhedasya aprakāśaḥ  bhaviṣyati kiñca aikya prakāśe tatra vipati pattiḥ na syāt  tad upadeśa ānarthakyam ca syāt iti tad na aikya ādīnām sva prakāśa svarūpa tve api tasya ajñāna tad kārya vipratipatti ādīn prati avirodhitayā tad gocara virodhi vṛtti paryanta muktā anupapatti abhāvāt na ca tarhi pratyak arthe api vipratipattiḥ syāt  cārvāka ādīnām tasyāḥ  api darśanāt  tasmāt ajñāna āśrayatva ādinā pratyagartha prakāśam upajīvyam na avidyā āvṛṇoti aikya ādi aṃśam tu āvṛṇoti eva iti tatra vipratipatti ādayaḥ na ca evam sādṛśya ādi doṣāt atra api bheda aṃśa āvṛta iti vācyam koṭī anupasthiteḥ pradhāna pūrva kāra upavādinaḥ tava tad asaṃbhavāt yad tu svarūpa bhedaḥ  bheda tvena bhāsata eva prāyas  sarva bhinna tvena eva pratīteḥ anyathā sarva koṭikaḥ saṃśayaḥ syāt  tatra ca ghaṭa pratiyogikatva ādi rūpā aneka  dharmāḥ sādṛśya ādi vaśāda gṛhītāḥ saṃśaya viṣayā bhaviṣyanti na ca aneka nirūpyasya bhedasya nirūpaka aneka tvāt anekatva āpattiḥ tādṛśasya api īśvara jñāna ādeḥ aneka dvaita nirūpya advaitasya ca aikya darśanāt  eka nirūpya prāc abhāva dhvaṃsayoḥ anaikya darśanāt ca iti tad na na vayam nirūpaka bhedena bhedam brūmaḥ kiṃtu pratiyogita avacchedaka bhedena abhāva bhedasya āvaśyaka tayā anyathā eka ghaṭa pratiyoginām caturṇām dhvaṃsa ādīnām aikya āpatteḥ na ca adhikaraṇa rūpa abhāva vādinām adhikaraṇa bhedena iva abhāva bhedaḥ dhvaṃsa prāc abhāvayoḥ ekyā pattau vilakṣaṇa vyavahāra an āpatteḥ na ca evam advaite api aikya anupapattiḥ brahma itaratva rūpa pratiyogi tāvacchedakasya aikyāt  pratiyogi bheda abhedayoḥ atantra tvāt yad api bheda jñānam na bhrama virodhi kiṃtu adhiṣṭhāna āropya viruddha dharma ādi jñānam iti tad na śabda abheda bhramasya śābda bheda jñānāt anivṛtti āpatteḥ yad api kaiścid uktaṃ doṣa mūlā tādrūpyeṇa apratītau pratītiḥ sarūpa bheda lakṣaṇam śukteḥ ca śukti ātmanā apratītiḥ doṣa mūla iti na tatra ativyāptiḥ adoṣa mūla iti asya yadi api saptamī anta viśeṣaṇa tvam na saṃbhavati tathā api viśiṣṭa viśeṣaṇa tvena tad viśeṣaṇatva paryavasānāt iti tad na tādrūpyeṇa apratītau pratīteḥ abheda sādhāraṇyena adoṣa mūlatva paryanta jñānam bheda vyavahāra kāraṇam vācyam tatra adoṣa mūla tvam phala ekonneyam iti cākṣuṣa tvam na syāt  pratīti ghaṭita tvāt  apratyaya kāle ca bhedaḥ  na syāt  kiṃca rajata ātmanā śukteḥ pratīti samaye tatra tad bhedaḥ te na syāt  adoṣa mūla iti asya abhāva viśeṣaṇa tvena avyāpti vāraṇe asāmarthyāt  viśeṣya an adhikaraṇasya sutarām viśiṣṭān adhikaraṇa tvāt na hi puruṣa hīne daṇḍi puruṣa saṃbhavaḥ na ca adoṣa mūla iti aśarīra janya tvam iti atra śarīram iva pratiyogi viśeṣaṇam bādhita saṃgrahāya nañā samasta pratīteḥ asamastena ananvayāt  na hi abrāhmaṇaḥ samīcīna iti anena samīcīna vipra abhāvaḥ pratīyate adoṣa mūla tādātmya prakāraka pratīti abhāva uktau ca śukte rūpya ātmanā apratīti kāle sāmagrī virahāt śukti ātmanā ca apratītau sva bheda āpatteḥ tādavasthyāt  na ca tadā api pratīyamāna śakti ātmanā pratīyamāna tvam īśvara jñānam ādāya asti eva iti vācyam evam satya pratīti daśā viraheṇa pratīyamāna pada vaiyarthyāt  na ca anyonya abhāva tvam tad  tasya anirūpaṇāt tad uktam ācāryaiḥ   ‘sā apekṣa tvāt sa avadheḥ ca tattve advaita prasaṅgataḥ eka abhāvāt asan dehān na rūpam vastunaḥ  bhidā iti kiṃca ghaṭasya bheda tve ekatara pariśeṣa āpattiḥ nanu aikyasya jñānasya ānandasya ca brahma svarūpa tve ekatara pariśeṣa āpattiḥ tava api samānā na ca vastuna eka tvena iṣṭāpattiḥ prakṛte api sāmyāditi ced na ekatara pariśeṣa āpattyā ghaṭa iti bheda iti vilakṣaṇa vyavahāra abhāvasya āpādanāt  na ca pravṛtti nimitta ghaṭatva bheda tvayoḥ bhedāt tad upapattiḥ bheda tvasya nirvaktum aśakyatvāt  tathā hi na tāvat jātiḥ jāti ādi sādhāraṇa tvāt na upādhiḥ tādātmya avacchinna pratiyogika abhāvatva ādi rūpaḥ tādātmyasya bheda viraha rūpa tve anyonya āśrayāt tad niṣṭhā sā dhāraṇa dharma rūpa tve tad avacchinna pratiyogika atyanta abhāve ati vyāpteḥ tasya api svarūpa tve anugata vyavahāra an āpatteḥ na ca  jñāna ānanda ādau  api vilakṣaṇa vyavahāraḥ  na syāt iti vācyam kalpita dharma bhedam ādāya upapatteḥ na ca bheda tvam api tathā astu iti vācyam tarhi anirākāryaḥ asi kiṃca bhedasya svarūpa tve idam bhinnam asya bheda iti saṃbandhi tvena dhīḥ na syāt  na ca ānandaḥ  brahmaṇa itivat upapattiḥ pramāṇa siddhe haikye bheda vyavahārasya aupacārika tvam kalpyate rāhoḥ śira ityādivat  na ca prakṛte tathā aikye māna abhāvāt bādhakāt ca na ca pakṣa antara anupapatteḥ eva pakṣa antara parigrahaḥ śaśaśṛṅga ādau bhāvatva abhāva tvayoḥ anyatara anupapattyā anyatara grahaṇa āpatteḥ na ca tatra ubhayatra bādha kālīka tvena upapattiḥ prakṛte api ubhayatra bādhaka ādāvidyaka tvena upapatteḥ saṃbhavāt  nanu asti bhedasya svarūpa tve mānam mṛd ghaṭa itivat  ghaṭaḥ paṭa ātmakaḥ  na iti paṭa tādātmya niṣedha rūpasya bhedasya ghaṭa sāmāna ādhikaraṇyena abheda pratyakṣam tathā ghaṭa bhedayoḥ ekaikasya pratītau  itarasya niyamena pratīyamānatva ādikam liṅgam asatyam bhedaḥ tu vastūnām svarūpam na atra saṃśayaḥ iti ādya āgamaḥ ca iti ced na ghaṭaḥ paṭa ātmakaḥ  na ityādeḥ anyonya abhāva bheda viṣaya tayā bheda abheda aviṣaya tvāt anyathā nīlaḥ  ghaṭa iti ādeḥ api rūpa abheda viṣayatva āpatteḥ liṅgasya ca abheda siddheḥ pūrvam asiddha tvāt sāmānya vyāpteḥ jāti vyakti ādau samāna saṃvid saṃvedye vyabhicārāt viśeṣa vyāptau  api pratiyogini vyabhicārāt ca āgamasya ca adhiṣṭhāna atirekeṇa asattva paratvāt kiṃca paṭāt  bhedaḥ ghaṭa mātra rūpam vā ghaṭa kuḍya ādi sarva rūpam vā ādye kuḍya ādiḥ paṭa bhedaḥ  na syāt  dvitīye sva rūpāṇām ananugata tvāt paṭa bheda anugata pratītiḥ na syāt  na ca paṭa jñāna icchā ādau yathā paṭa viṣaya tvena anugatena anugata vyavahāraḥ tathā paṭa pratiyogika tvena atra api anugata vyavahāra iti vācyam etāvatā hi jñāna ādiṣu paṭa viṣayam jñānam paṭa viṣaya icchā iti paṭa viṣayatva aṃśe anugamavat  paṭa pratiyogikatva aṃśa eva anugamaḥ syāt  na bheda aṃśe api na ca bheda tvam api ekam iti uktam kiṃca idam asmāt  bhinnam iti vā asya amuṣmāt  bheda iti vā dharmi pratiyogi ghaṭita tvena bheda grahaṇe paraspara āśrayaḥ dharmi pratiyogi jñāne bheda jñānam tasmin  ca satyasya amuṣmāt iti vilakṣaṇa dharmi pratiyogi jñānam iti ghaṭa paṭau bhinnau  iti ghaṭa paṭa viśeṣaṇa tayā tayoḥ bheda iti tad viśeṣya tayā vā grahaṇe api anyonya āśraya eva ghaṭa paṭa pratītau tad viśeṣyatva ādinā bheda grahaḥ bheda grahe ca dvitva avacchinna ghaṭa paṭa pratītiḥ iti na ca bhedasya svarūpa tvāt  svarūpa pratīteḥ eva bheda dhī tvena dhī dvaya abhāvāt na ukta doṣa iti śaṅkyam sva rūpa jñānasya dvitīyatva abhāve api pratiyogi jñānasya sva rūpa jñāna atiriktasya dvitīyasya apekṣaṇāt  na ca  sarva ātmakam idam iti viparyaya adarśanena idam na sarva ātmakam iti sāmānyatas  sarvatas  vyāvṛttam vastu anubhūyata iti pratiyogi viśeṣa jñāna anapekṣaṇāt na anyonya āśraya iti vācyam sarva ātmakam na iti atra sarva tvam vā pratiyogita avacchedakam svetara sarva tvam vā ādye svasmāt vailakṣaṇye sva asiddhi prasaṅgāt  dvitīye anyonya āśrayasya spaṣṭa tvāt  na ca   asarvam khalu idam brahme atyatra yathā brahma ātma tvena apratītam sarvam ucyate tadvat atra api sarvasmāt iti anena tad ātmaka tvena ajñātam sarvam vivakṣyata iti vācyam sva grahāt  pūrvam svasya api sva ātmanā ajñāta tvāt  svasya pratiyogita āpatteḥ dṛṣṭānte sarva śabdasya asaṃkucita tve tava asaṃpratipatteḥ ca na ca vastu tas  bheda āśrayasya abhedena ajñātasya jñānam pratiyogi jñāna tvena kāraṇam na tu bhinnatva prakāraka jñāna tvena iti vācyam evam hi candre dvitva bhramaḥ  na syāt  vastu tas  bheda abhāvāt nanu ‘asti idam na jānāmi ‘sarvam khalu idam brahme atyādiṣu sākṣi siddha kāla viṣaya sarvaiḥ saha vastu ajñāna abhedānām iva iha api sākṣi siddhena pratiyoginā saha eva vyāvṛtteḥ pratīteḥ na anyonya āśraya iti ced na viśiṣṭa jñānasya viśeṣaṇa jñāna ajanya tve api pratiyogi sa vikalpakasya abhāva jñānam pratyanvaya vyatirekābhyām janakatvāt  sākṣī ca pramāṇam anapekṣya pratiyogi paṭa ādikam dharmi bhinna tayā na gṛhṇāti iti katham sākṣi siddha pratiyoginā bheda graha upapattiḥ syāt  tad uktam cintāmaṇau ‘anyathā  nirvikalpakāt api ghaṭaḥ  na asti iti vṛtti āpatte ariti na ca etāvatā pratiyogi ta avacchedaka paṭatva ādi prakāraka jñāna mātram arthanīyam na tu dharmi bhinnatva jñāna paryantam iti vācyam dharmi ta avacchedaka bheda ajñāne pratiyogi ta avacchedaka tayā abhāva nirūpaka tvasya eva abhāvāt anyonya dharma bheda jñāne ca viśiṣya stambhāt  kumbhasya bheda pratītau kumbhāt  stambhasya bheda dhīḥ iti anyonya āśraya tā davasthyāt nanu tvad mate api bimba brahma jīvānām pratibimba vrahma abhede ‘idam anena abhinnamasya āmuṣmāda bhedaḥ etayoḥ abheda iti evam pratītiḥ syāt  tathā ca dharmi pratiyogi bhāva dhīḥ dvi tvā avacchinna dhīḥ ca bheda jñāna adhīnā iti tad viruddha abheda jñāna anupapattiḥ iti ced na kālpanika bheda jñānasya dharmi pratiyogi bhāva dvitva avacchinna jñāna nirvāhakasya tāttvika abheda jñāna pratibandhakatva ayogāt kiṃca abheda jñāne na dharmi rūpa pratiyogi jñāna apekṣā tasya niṣpratiyogika vastu svarūpa tvāt sa pratiyogikatva vyavahāraḥ tu nirūpaka bhedasa pratiyogika tvena ata eva  jīvasya pratiyogitayā brahma abheda nirūpaka tvam tad abhinnatayā jñātasya eva iti anyonya āśrayaḥ dharmiṇā saha ābhadena pratītasya eva abheda pratiyogi tvāt anyathā dahanasya api tuhinā bhedasa pratiyogitva āpatteḥ iti  nirastam bheda grahasya tatra pratibandhaka tvāt ca ata eva atattva m asī atyatra tu aṃpada
