vācyasya viśiṣṭasya brahma abheda pratiyogitva prasaṅga vinivāraṇāya vidyamānā bhedasya asati pratibandhake abheda yogya cittva ādi rūpeṇa pratītiḥ abheda dhī hetuḥ bheda bhrame tu doṣaḥ pratibandhaka iti nābheda dhīḥ iti para siddhāntam parikalpya svarūpa bheda pakṣe vastutas anyonya pratiyogikayoḥ ghaṭa paṭa svarūpa bhedayoḥ anyonya pratiyogitva yogya ghaṭa paṭatva ādi rūpeṇa pratītayoḥ asati pratibandhe anyonya pratiyogi tayā viśiṣṭa dhīḥ dharma bheda pakṣe api vidyamāna bhedasya asati pratibandhake bheda yogya nīla pītatva ādi rūpeṇa pratītiḥ bheda hetuḥ dūra stha vanaspati ādau tu dūra ādi doṣaḥ pratibandhaka iti na bheda dhīḥ iti sāmyena samādhānam nirastam vaiṣamyasya ukta tvāt nanu yathā gauḥ ga vaya sadṛśī ityādau gavaya ādīnām gavā ādibhyaḥ  bhedaḥ san  ā iva pratiyogitva hetuḥ na tu jñātaḥ na hi gauḥ gavaya sadṛśī iti pratyakṣadhīḥ api niyamena gavayaḥ  gaḥ bhinna iti dhī pūrvikā anubhūyate sutarām śābda dhīḥ tatra bheda vāci śabda abhāvāt tathā prakṛte api anyathā caitrasya maitra pitṛtva ādau jñāta eva maitrasya caitra putratva ādi jñānam gavayasya gaḥ sādṛśye jñāta eva gauḥ gavaya sadṛśī iti jñānam iti sa pratiyogika padārtha mātre anyonya āśrayaḥ syāt iti ced na iṣṭa āpatteḥ ata eva sa pratiyogi tvena niṣpratiyogi tvena ca bheda sādṛśya ādi durvacam sarvatra bādhaka sattvāt iti asmākam siddhāntaḥ yad tu uktam pratiyogi dharmi bheda graha pūrvakatva niyamaḥ  na anubhūyata iti tad iṣṭam eva tasya eva sa pratiyogi tve bādhaka tvāt  pratyakṣa eva sa pratiyogika padārtha grahe evam anyonya āśrayasya āpādya tve śābde bheda vācaka pada asattvasya asmān pratyadūṣaṇa tvāt  evam ca pratiyogi dhī mātram na bheda dhī hetuḥ tad nirvikalpakāt api tad āpatteḥ kiṃtu pratiyogi tvena tatra api na anyam prati pratiyogi tvena kiṃtu bhedam prati tathā ca anyonya āśrayaḥ na ca sa pratiyogika sādṛśya ādau  evam syāt  iṣṭa āpatteḥ abhedaḥ ca na sa pratiyogika iti ukta tvāt ca yad tu yatra dharmi pratiyoginau sannihitau tatra dharmi pratiyogi sadbhāvayoḥ tad bhedasya ca yugapad dhīḥ idam anena sadṛśam itivat  tathā viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvasya ca yugapad dhīḥ imau sadṛśau  itivat  sarvasya yogyasya indriya sannikarṣeṇa yugapad sarva viṣaya eka jñāna saṃbhavāt na hi mad mate daṇḍī iti dhīḥ api daṇḍa jñāna sādhyā uktam ca etad  yatra dharmi pratiyoginoḥ anyatarasya asannidhānam tatra api saṃskāra saciva indriya sannikarṣeṇa ekam eva jñānam utpadyate tad anena sadṛśam ityādivat  anyathā abheda jñānam api na syāt  tathā ca anyonya āśrayaḥ tad uktam   ‘dharmitva pratiyogitva tad bhāvā yugapad yadi viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyam ca tad bhāvaḥ ca eva gṛhyata iti tad na prameyatva ādinā ghaṭe jñāte api ghaṭa abhāva iti apratīteḥ ghaṭatva ādinā ghaṭasya pūrvam avaśyam jñeya tvena yugapad eva dharmi pratiyogi ādi buddhi asiddheḥ na ca tatra ghaṭatva ādi jñāna sāmagrī vilambāt eva vilambaḥ tad sattve iṣṭāpattiḥ iti vācyam pratiyogi aviṣaya ka abhāva pratyaya āpādanasya evam api aparihārāt na ca tādṛś pratiyogi graha sāmagrī kāraṇam tad apekṣayā pratiyogi grahasya eva laghu tvāt  nanu aanyatva agrahaṇe proktaḥ katham anyonya saṃśrayaḥ anya tvam yadi siddham syāt  katham anyonya saṃśrayaḥ iti ubhayatas pāśā rajjuḥ iti ced na na hi anyatva buddhim vyavahāra kṣamām api nirākurmaḥ kiṃtu anāvidyaka tve na upapadyata iti brūmaḥ kiṃca bhedasya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvena eva jñeya tvāt  tad tad bhāva pratīteḥ ca bheda prati iti anadhīna tayā daṇḍa caitra ādau dṛṣṭa tvena bheda pratīti paramparā anavasthā syāt  na ca brahma jīva abhinnam jagat mithyā ityādau  api abheda ādeḥ viśeṣaṇa tayā bheda jñānasya apekṣaṇīyatayā anavasthā patteḥ na prāthamikā bheda ādi dhīḥ iti tava api samānam iti vācyam avidyā kalpita bhedena ajñātena api viśeṣaṇatva ādi upapatteḥ na ca evam tava api bheda bhedyayoḥ svarūpataḥ  bheda abhāvāt bhedasya adhikaraṇānatiḥ ekāt  dharmaḥ  bheda iti pakṣe tu pratīti anavasthā uddhāre api viṣayān avasthāyā duṣpariharatva āpatteḥ na ca avidyaka bheda pakṣe api anavasthā ādi doṣaḥ anupapatteḥ alaṅkāra tvāt  ata eva abhinnam brahma iti atra abhedasya bhinna tayā jñātasya viśeṣaṇa tvena tena saha brahma abheda bodhana anupapattiḥ prācīnabheda dhiyā pratibandhāt iti nirastam anirvacanīya bheda jñānasya tāttvika abheda jñāna apratibandhaka tvāt  kiṃca dharma bheda pakṣe pratyakṣam kim bhedam eva gocarayati uta vastu api na ādyaḥ bheda iti eva apratīteḥ dvitīye api kim bheda pūrvakam vastu gocarayet  uta vastu pūrvakam bhedam yugapad vā ubhayam na ādyaḥ bheda iti eva apratīteḥ viramya vyāpāra ayogāt ca ataeva na dvitīyaḥ na tṛtīyaḥ vastu grahasya bheda graha janaka tāyāḥ sthāpita tvāt  na ca vastu mātra jñāna anantara bhāvinā viśiṣṭa jñānena yugapad u bhaya grahaḥ pratiyogitva ādinā jñānasya eva bheda dhī hetu tvāt  anyathā pañcamī prayoga ādi anupapatteḥ tatra ca prāk uktaḥ  doṣaḥ ata eva viśiṣṭa dhiyaḥ viśeṣaṇa jñāna janyatva mate anayoḥ bheda iti jñāna anantaram imau bhinnau  iti dhiyaḥ saṃbhavaḥ viśeṣaṇa jñāna ajanya tve api yugapad eva ubhaya gocara dhiyaḥ saṃbhava iti nirastam anayoḥ bheda iti ādau ṣaṭhyā ullikhyamāna saṃbandha graha artham bheda grahasya pūrvam avaśya apekṣaṇīya tayā anavasthāyāḥ  duṣparihara tvāt  na ca bimba pratibimbayoḥ jīva brahmaṇoḥ ca abheda grāhi pratyakṣam śabdaḥ ca kim abhedam eva gocarayet ityādi vikalpa sāmyam abhedasya vastu svarūpa tvena īdṛś vikalpa an avakāśāt kiṃca bhedasya anyonya abhāva tve tad pratiyoginoḥ stambha kumbhayoḥ tādātmyasya aprāmāṇika tvena anyonya abhāvasya aprāmāṇika tvam syāt  na ca dvaita āderaprāmāṇika tve tad virahasya aprāmāṇikatva āpattiḥ atireka pakṣe iṣṭa āpatteḥ anatireka pakṣe tu adhikaraṇa prāmāṇika tvasya eva prāmāṇika tve tantra tayā pratiyogi aprāmāṇika tve api prāmāṇikatva upapatteḥ na ca anyonya abhāve api tad pakṣe tathā aṅgīkriyatām iti vācyam tasya adhikaraṇa rūpa tāyām śūnyavāda ādi āpatteḥ ukta tvāt  yadtva prāmāṇikasya niṣedha pratiyogi tvam iti uktam paraiḥ tad na vārayāmaḥ kiṃtu adhikaraṇa atireke niṣedhasya aprāmāṇikatva mātram brūmaḥ nanu atra na kumbha stambhaḥ bhaya tādātmyam niṣedha pratiyogi kiṃtu stambha tādātmyam stambhe pramitam kumbha gatam niṣidhyata iti na pratiyogi aprāmāṇika tvam iti ced na tādātmya mātrasya niṣedha pratiyogi tve dūra stha vanaspatyoḥ iva bādha uttara kālam imau vanaspatī itivat ime śukti rajate iti prati iti āpatteḥ na ca asannidhāna kṛtaḥ  viśeṣaḥ etāvatā api śukti tadrajate iti prati iti āpatteḥ yad tu anyonya abhāva saṃsarga abhāvayoḥ lakṣaṇam yatra adhikaraṇe pratiyogita avacchedakam āropya niṣedha avagamaḥ saḥ anyonya abhāvaḥ yatra adhikaraṇe pratiyoginam āropya niṣedha avabhāsaḥ sa saṃsarga abhāva iti tad na atīndriye bhede saṃsarga abhāve ca tad mate avyāpteḥ śabda janyā bhāva buddhau vyabhicāreṇa āropasya abhāva buddhau  ahetutvāt ca kim bhede svetara bhedasya vaktavya tayā sva vṛtti virodhaḥ anavasthā vā na ca brahma abhede api sva abhedasya vaktavya tayā sva vṛtti tvam samānam iti vācyam abhedasya sva nirvāhakatva āditya vehi na ca bhede tathā bheda adhikaraṇaka bheda vyavahārasya sva rūpeṇa nirvāhe ghaṭe api tathā tve dharma pakṣaka bheda anupapatteḥ kiṃca bhede bheda tvam upādhi rūpam jāti rūpam vā vācyam tatra punar bhedaḥ  vācyaḥ anyathā bheda tvasya anyasmāt  bhedaḥ  na syāt  tathā ca anyonya vṛttyā sva vṛtti āpatteḥ sva vṛtti tvavat tasya api viruddha tvāt  na ca bhede api abheda tvam vācyam tatra punar abhedaḥ  vācyaḥ anyathā tasya svābhedaḥ  na syāt iti tatra api tathātva āpattiḥ prameyatva abhidheyatva ādivat anyonya vṛtti tvasya abhede adoṣa tve bhede api sāmyam iti vācyam asmākam abheda mātrasya abheda tvasya ca brahma abheda abhinna tayā anyonyam iti asya eva abhāvena anyonya vṛtti tvasya eva āpādayitum aśakyatvāt na ca tarhi ghaṭe ghaṭābhedasya jīve jīva abhedasya vā jīva brahma abheda tve vedānta vaiyarthyam bheda bhrama nivartaka vṛtteḥ mahā vākyam vinā anupapatteḥ ukta tvāt  yad tu prameyatva ādau pramita tvāt anyonya vṛttiḥ adoṣa iti tad na ātma āśraya ādi tattva doṣeṇa tatra api pramitatva asiddheḥ ata eva na kaścid  kevala anvayī kiṃca bhedaḥ kim bhinne niviśate abhinne vā ādya ātma āśrayaḥ anyonya āśrayaḥ  vā dvitīye virodhaḥ na ca abheda anirvācyatva ādikam kim tadvati tad abhāvavati ca ityādi vikalpasya atra api sāmyam iti vācyam abhedasya svarūpa tvena tatra tad vikalpa an avakāśāt anirvācya ādā  asya vikalpasya anirvācyatva prayojakasya asmākam anukūla tvāt  na ca bhedaḥ api svarūpam prāk eva nirāsāt  na ca bhedaḥ sva āśrayatva yogye vartate yogya tā ca pramā rūpa phala eka unneyā iti vācyam yogyatāyā bhedam vinā vaktum aśakyatvāt  na hi abhinne kadāpi tad yogya tā dharma antarasya api bhedam apuraskṛtya yogyatva aprayojaka tvāt  bheda abheda avajñātvā bhrama pramā rūpa phala bhedasya eva ajñānena bheda yogya tāyāḥ pramā rūpa phala bhedān unneya tvāt ca ‘asu avyāghātakaiḥ eva jāti bhinnaiḥ sat uttaraiḥ nirastam bhedam ādāya sva ātmā bhedaḥ  niṣīdati iti advaita siddhau viśeṣataḥ  bheda khaṇḍanam atha viśeṣa khaṇḍanam nanu asmākam bhedaḥ  na sva rūpa mātram kim tu anyonya abhāvaḥ sa ca vastunaḥ sa viśeṣa abhinnaḥ tatas ca abhinna tvāt na anavasthā ādiḥ bheda pratinidheḥ viśeṣasya vidyamāna tvāt na paryāyatva ādikam viśeṣaḥ ca bheda hīne api ekatara pariśeṣa abhāva ādi nirvāhaka iti ced na paryāyatva ādi pramājanakasya sva rūpa atiriktasya viśeṣasya aṅgīkāre tasya eva bheda tvena bhedasya dharma bheda uktya yogāt  viśeṣasya api bhedaḥ sa viśeṣa abhinna eva vācyaḥ tathā ca anavasthā tādavasthyam na ca vaiśeṣika abhimata viśeṣa vattasya sva para nirvāhaka tvam etādṛśa viśeṣe māna abhāvāt nanu avijñānam ānandam brahme atyādi vākya bodhya vijñāna ānanda ādīnām tvad mate api bhedasya bheda abhedayoḥ vā akhaṇḍa arthaka tvena ‘ekadhā eva anudraṣṭavya amiti ādi śruti virodhena ca aṅgīkartum aśakyatayā bheda pratinidheḥ viśeṣasya aparyāyatva ādi artham avaśyam svīkāra iti arthāpattiḥ eva mānam iti ced na bhede aikarasya śruti rodhavat  atra api tad tādavasthyāt  lakṣya artha abhede api vācya artha bhedena aparyāya tvasya vyāvartya bhedāt avaiyarthyasya ca anyathā eva upapatteḥ kiṃca tava api jñāna ānandatva ādi nimitta bhedāt eva aparyāya tvam astu kim viśeṣeṇa na ca ‘evam dharmā aniti śrutyā tayoḥ api bheda niṣedhāt  na evam iti vācyam tarhi viśeṣasya api āśrita tvena dharma tayā asya api bheda niṣedhāt tena api anupapattiḥ na ca jñānatva ānanda tvayoḥ artha prakāśatva nirupādhika iṣṭatva rūpayoḥ artha prakāśa nirupādhika iṣṭa rūpa āśraya viśeṣa āvaśyaka iti vācyam jñānatva ānanda tvayoḥ jāti rūpa tvena ukta rūpatva abhāvāt na ca ākāśa śabda āśraya śabdayoḥ pravṛtti nimitta abhedena paryāyatva āpattiḥ tad parihārāya viśeṣaḥ  vācya iti vācyam paryāya tve api saha prayogasya vyākhyāna vyākhyeya bhāva ādinā api upapatteḥ na ca evam jñāna ānandayoḥ ekatara pariśeṣeṇa mokṣe ānanda prakāśaḥ  na syāt iti vācyam tayoḥ bheda abhāvena ekatara tvasya eva abhāvāt dvayoḥ vacane tarabvidhānāt  etena śodhita tad padārthāt aikyasya na bhedaḥ na api bheda abhedau kiṃtu atyanta abhedaḥ evam ca viśeṣa anaṅgīkāre sva prakāśa caitanya bhāne aikya abhāna āpattiḥ tad prakāśasya bheda bhrama avirodhi tve api aikya prakāśasya tad virodhaḥ tasya nirapekṣa tve api aikyasya sa apekṣa tvam ca na upapadyata iti nirastam āvāraka ajñāna kalpita aṃśam ādāya sarvasya upapatteḥ na ca ekasya eva śukteḥ āvṛta anāvṛta tve śukti aṃśa bheda evam syāt iti vācyam tad aṃśa kalpakasya phalasya abhāvāt  nanu ‘evam dharmāni ati śrutiḥ astu mānam atra hi brahma dharmānuktvā bhedaḥ  niṣidhyate na ca bheda pratinidheḥ abhāve dharma dharma bhāvaḥ  dharmāṇām aneka tvam ca yuktam iti ced na dharma anityasya niṣedha anuvāda tvena dharmatva anekatva ādau tātparya abhāvāt na ca śrutitaḥ anyatas  brahma dharmāḥ prāptāḥ āvidyaka mātrasya sākṣi siddha tayā prāpteḥ nanu guṇa guṇinā uḥ abheda pakṣe ghaṭa upalambhe śukla ādi anupalambha artham bheda abheda pakṣe tayoḥ avirodha artham atyanta bheda pakṣe api samavāyaḥ saṃbandhaḥ sattā satī antya viśeṣaḥ  vyāvṛttaḥ kālaḥ sadā asti deśaḥ sarvatra asti iti abādhita vyavahāra artha viśeṣaḥ aṅgī kāryaḥ abhāva ādau  api astitva ādiḥ nābhāva āditas  bhinnaḥ guṇa ādiṣu anantarbhāvena ṣaṭ eva padārthā iti niyama bhaṅga āpatteḥ aniyama pakṣe api astitve api astitva antaram iti anavasthāpatteḥ tatra api saḥ aṅgī kārya iti ced na svabhāva viśeṣāt eva sarvasya upapatteḥ na ca tarhi viśeṣasya aṅgīkāreṇa mad mata praveśa iti vācyam tad tad asādhāraṇa svarūpasya eva svabhāva viśeṣa śabda artha tvena tvad ukta viśeṣa anukteḥ tad tad asādhāraṇa rūpeṇa samavāya ādeḥ sva nirvāhaka tvāt  ata eva sva nirvāhaka tvam hi sva karmaka nirvahaṇa kartṛ tvam tad ca ekasmin viruddham iti tad upapādanāya api viśeṣa aṅgīkāra iti nirastam sva nirvāhaka śabdasya svetara anapekṣa vyavahāra viṣayatva mātra arthaka tvāt  anyathā viśeṣaḥ api anavasthā abhiyā vastu abhinna iti tava aṅgīkāreṇa tad dūṣaṇa āpātāt  svarūpa bheda pakṣa ukta ekatara pariśeṣa ādi dūṣaṇa tādavasthya āpatteḥ ca na ca antya viśeṣa vadasya dharmi grāhaka mānena tādṛś svabhāva tayā siddheḥ paryanuyoga ayoga iti vācyam dṛṣṭānta iva dārṣṭa antike svarūpa atirekasya tvayā eva anaṅgīkāreṇa vaiṣamyāt  yad tu yatra eva bheda abhāvaḥ abheda kāryam ca pramitam tatra eva viśeṣaḥ kalpyate na tu pramita bhede ghaṭa paṭa ādau viśeṣam ādāya bheda tyāgaḥ na hi soma abhāve pratīka iti tad lābhe api sa iti tad na mukhyatva niyāmakasya tatra eva atra abhāvāt viśeṣa bhedayoḥ ubhayoḥ api svarūpa paryavasanna tvena tvad vāc bhaṅgeḥ anavakāśāt  kiṃca bhedaḥ svayam eva sva kāryam karotu abheda kārya artham tad pratinidhiḥ astu iti ādi āpatteḥ ca na ca ānanda ādau  abhedavat  bhedasya bodha abhāvaḥ alaukika sthale dvayoḥ sāmyāt  nanu anumānam atra mānam tathā hi—brahma svarūpa bhūtayoḥ vijñāna ānandayoḥ brahma abhedayoḥ ca ekatara pariśeṣa abhāvaḥ prameyatva ādeḥ sva āśritatva ādikam vā bhedāni aniyamyam bheda aniyamya tve sati niyamya tvāt  yad  yad aniyamya tve sati niyamyam tad  tad anya niyamyam yathā saṃmatam brahma svarūpa bhūtam vijñāna ānanda ādikam vā bheda ani ekatara apariśeṣa nirvāhakavat  bheda hīna tve sati ekatara apariśeṣa rūpa nirvāhyavat tvāt yadyena hīna tve sati yad nirvāhyavat  tad tad anya nirvāhakavat yathā saṃmatam sva āśritam prameyatva ādikam vā bhedāni āśraya āśrayi bhāva nirvāhakavat bheda hīna tve satya āśraya āśrayi bhāva rūpa nirvāhyavat tvāt yathā saṃmatam iti ādikam iti ced na tvad abhimata viśeṣāt anyasya eva avidyā ādeḥ sarvatra niyāmakatva saṃbhavena artha antarāt āvidyaka bheda niyamya tvena bādhāt asiddheḥ ca nanu tathā api pratyakṣam atra mānam tathā hi tantu paṭa ādi buddhīnām bhinna ghaṭa ādi buddhitaḥ  vailakṣaṇyam tāvat anubhūyate tad ca na tāvat saṃbandha viṣaya tvena kuṇḍa badara ādi buddhitaḥ  vailakṣaṇya anubhavāt  na api saṃyoga ani asaṃbandha viṣaya tvena ghaṭa tad jñāna tadabhāva buddhitaḥ api vailakṣaṇya anubhavāt  na api sva rūpa pratyāsatti saṃyogāni asaṃbandha viṣaya tvena ghaṭa tad harmikā anyoni abhāva buddheḥ ghaṭa paṭa ādi buddhitaḥ  vailakṣaṇya abhāva āpātāt na api ayuta siddhi viṣaya tvena āśraya āśrayi bhāva niyamaḥ  hi ayuta siddhiḥ tatra ca tadānīṃtana āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ kuṇḍa badara ādau  api bhāti niyamaḥ tu na tantu paṭa ādi buddhau  api na hi tantu paṭa ādi dhīḥ pratyakṣā anayoḥ saṃbandha nāśaḥ  vā vibhāgaḥ  vā na bhaviṣyati iti ākārā na vā kuṇḍa badara ādi dhīḥ tayoḥ saṃbandha nāśaḥ  vā vibhāgaḥ  vā bhaviṣyati iti ākārikā na api samavāya viṣaya tvena ukta nyāyena saṃbandha nitya tvasya saṃbandhyayuta siddha tvasya vā tatra asphuraṇāt  tasmāt abheda viṣaya tvena eva vailakṣaṇyam vācyam ayam ghaṭaḥ gaja ādikam senā patram eva tāṭaṅka iti ādau puras vartinā ghaṭādeḥ iva ātānavitāna ātmakāḥ tantava rūpa eva paṭaḥ śukla paṭa iti ādau  api tantu ādinā paṭasya abheda pratīteḥ na ca atra paṭatva śukla tvayoḥ eka stha tvam eva bhāti iti vācyam paṭa śuklayoḥ aikyasya api tatra antargateḥ anyathā kvāpi abhedaḥ  na syāt  ‘ghaṭaḥ paṭaḥ na iti dhīḥ ca bheda viṣayā na syāt  adaṇḍī caitra iti ādau  api daṇḍinā caitrasya abhedaḥ  bhāti eva na ca śukla paṭa iti atra śuklavān eva iti pratīyata iti vācyam śuklam rūpam iti atra yad  śuklam tasya eva iha pratīteḥ anyathā iha api daṇḍī itivat  śuklī iti syāt  matu blopa ādi kalpanam śabda viṣaya ka vyavahāre na tu pratītau paṭasya śauklyam ityādi dhīḥ na bheda viṣayā kiṃtu saṃbandha viṣayā sati sattā ityādivat  bheda abhāve api upapannā ca paṭasya tantu anya tve ca gurutva dvaya āpattiḥ tantumati paṭa vṛttiḥ ca na syāt  mūrtīnām samāna deśatā virodhāt vyavahāra artha kriyā bheda ādikam tu patra tā āṭaṅka ādivat yuktam tasmāt tantu paṭa ādi buddhiḥ abheda viṣayā eva yadi ca evam kevala abheda viṣayā tarhi sāmānādhikaraṇya vyavahāram na janayet  ghaṭaḥ kalaśa iti ādya vyavahārāt  tena jñāyate adhikaḥ api asya viṣayaḥ asti na ca ayam bhedaḥ ghaṭaḥ na śukla iti ullekhā pātāt  bheda abheda avirodhāya viśeṣasya āvaśyaka tvāt ca tasmāt yaḥ adhikaḥ  viṣayaḥ sa viśeṣa iti ced na sati api abhede kālpanika bhedam ādāya tathā avyavahāra upapattyā viśeṣasya asiddheḥ na ca ghaṭaḥ  na śuklaḥ iti pratītyāpattiḥ phala balena kālpanika bhedasya sāmānādhikaraṇya ādi vyavahāra mātra nirvāhakatva kalpanena viparīta ullekhanam pratyahetutvāt  tasmāt evam viśeṣaḥ ayam na māna viṣayaḥ sakhe viṣādam jahi mad siddha avidyayā sarva saṅgatiḥ iti advaita siddhau viśeṣa khaṇḍanam atha bheda pañcake pratyakṣa pramāṇa bhaṅgaḥ evam pratyakṣataḥ prāpta bhedasya eva nivāraṇāt  asākṣātkṛta jīva īśa bheda ādau kā kathā tava tathā hi īśvarasya apratyakṣa tvena tad harmikasya tad pratiyogikasya vā bhedasya grahītum aśakyatvāt  nanu īśa dharmika bhedasya jīvā pratyakṣa tve api sva dharmika bhedaḥ tathā api tad pratyakṣaḥ ‘nā aham sarvajñaḥ  na aham nirduḥkha ityādi anubhavāt na ca yogya pratiyogika tvam abhāva yogya tve prayojakam iti vācyam stambhaḥ piśācaḥ  na ityādi pratyakṣa rūpa phala balena saṃsarga abhāve tathā ātve api anyonya abhāve adhikaraṇa yogya tāyā eva tantra tvāt vastutas tu saṃsarga abhāve api na tanmātram yogya tā jala paramāṇau yogya pṛthivītva abhāva graha prasaṅgāt  kiṃtu yatra yad sattvam anupalabdhi virodhi tatra tasya abhāvaḥ  yogya iti adhikaraṇa niyatā eva sarva abhāva sādhāraṇī yogya tā sā ca prakṛte api asi eva anyathā abheda śruteḥ aprasakta pratiṣedhaka tā āpatteḥ bheda śruteḥ ca tvad ukta pratyakṣa siddha bheda anuvādi tvam na syāt  īśa dharmika jīva bhede api ‘tāni aham veda sarvāṇi na tvam vettha parantapa uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ tu anya iti ādi tad vacana anumita pratyakṣa siddha tvam eva iti ced na ukta anubhavasya antaḥkaraṇa ādi avacchinna caitanyasya tad avacchinna caitanya pratiyogika bheda avagāhitayā śuddha caitanya dharmika nirduḥkha ādi pratiyogika bhedān avagāhi tvāt  śrutiḥ api avacchinna bheda anuvādinī bheda niṣedha śrutiḥ tu anumāna ādi prasakta bheda niṣedha parā na ca ‘yaḥ aham asva apsam yasya mama ajñāna saṃsāra ādi saḥ aham nirduḥkhaḥ  ne ati suṣupti kālīna antaḥkaraṇa avacchinna abhedena ajñāna ādi āśraya abhedena ca pratyabhijñāyamāne śuddhe bheda pratītiḥ saṃsāra ādhārasya tad anādhārāt  bheda eva hi āvayoḥ vivādaḥ na tu caitanyasya caitanyāt iti vācyam etāvatā ajñāna avacchinna eva bheda grahaḥ  na tu śuddhe na hi suṣupti kāle antaḥkaraṇa anavacchinna tvavat ajñāna an avacchinna tvam api asti yad tu caitanyasya caitanyāt  bhedaḥ  na asti iti tad asmākam anukūlam caitanye svābhāvikasya abhedasya eva asmad rahasya tvāt bhavat pratikūlam ca na hi bhavatām caitra maitra ādi caitanyānām aikyam iti matam aham arthasya yathā na śuddha ātma tvam tathā uktam prāk  sākṣi pratyakṣasya adhyasta ādi sādhāraṇa tayā tad siddhatva mātreṇa bhede abādhita tvam asaṃbhāvitam eva etena jīvānām parasparam bhede pratyakṣam pramāṇam iti nirastam na aham caitra iti ādeḥ avacchinna bheda viṣaya tvāt ‘ghaṭaḥ  na brahma ghaṭaḥ  na paṭaḥ na aham ghaṭa ityādi pratyakṣasya kalpita bheda viṣaya tvena tāttvika bheda asiddheḥ tasmāt  bheda pañcake na pratyakṣam pramāṇam iti advaita siddhau bheda pañcake pratyakṣa bhaṅgaḥ atha jīva brahma bheda anumāna bhaṅgaḥ na api anumānam   jīveśvarau bhinnau viruddha dharma adhikaraṇa tvāt dahana tuhinavat iti atra duḥkha ādeḥ antaḥkaraṇa ādi dharma tvena svarūpa asiddheḥ ekatra eva nirduḥkhatva duḥkhavat tvayoḥ avacchedaka bhedena dṛṣṭa tayā dharmi bheda asādhaka tvāt bheda mātre siddha sādhanāt  tāttvika bhede sādhya vaikalyāt    brahma tattvataḥ  jīvāt  bhinnam sarvajña tvāt vyatirekeṇa jīvavat iti atra aprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tvāt     brahma dharmi sattā samāna sattāka bhedavat iti sādhya karaṇe asādhāraṇyāt      ātma tvam nānā vyakti niṣṭham jāti tvāt  pṛthivī tvavat iti atra ātma aikya vādinam pratyasiddheḥ kalpita vyakti niṣṭha tvena siddha sādhanāt ca   duḥkham guṇatva avāntara jātyā sajātīya āśrayāt bhinna āśritam guṇa tvāt rūpavat iti atra śabde vyabhicārāt  duḥkha ādīnām antaḥkaraṇa dharma tvena siddha sādhanāt ca     vimatāni śarīrāṇi sva saṃkhyā saṃkhyeya ātmavanti śarīra tvāt  saṃmatavat iti atra yogi śarīre vyabhicārāt    ātmā dharmi sattā samāna sattāka ātma pratiyogika bhedavān dravya tvāt  ghaṭavat      ātmā dravyatva vyāpya jātyā nānā aśrāvaṇa viśeṣa guṇa adhikaraṇa tvāt ghaṭavat iti atra ca ātmanaḥ  nirguṇa tvena asiddheḥ caitraḥ caitra pratiyogika ukta bhedavān ukta hetoḥ ukta dṛṣṭāntavat iti ābhāsa sāmyāt ca etena navīnā anumānāni api nirastāni     īśvaraḥ jīva pratiyogika tāttvika bhedvān sarva śakti tvāt sarvajña tvāt sarva kārya kartṛ tvāt svatantra tvāt vā vyatirekeṇa jīvavat    jīvaḥ  vā brahma pratiyogika tāttvika bhedavān alpa śakti tvāt  alpa jña tvāt  alpa kartṛ tvāt saṃsāri tvāt vā vyatirekeṇa brahmavat  ityādiṣu bhedasya svarūpa tvena tadvattva sādhane bādhāt  na ca viśeṣam ādāya tad upapādanam tasya sva rūpa anatiḥ ekeṇa tadvatva sampādaka tvāt  aprasiddha viśeṣaṇa tā āpatteḥ ca na ca jīva brahma abhede aniṣṭa prasaktyā aṣṭa dravya atirikta dravyatva ādeḥ iva tvad siddha sva prakāśatva ādeḥ iva ca sādhyasya māna yogyatva saṃbhava iti vācyam tāttvika bheda vyatireke api upādhi kalpita bhedena sarva aniṣṭa parihāra saṃbhavāt na ca jīvaḥ  brahma vā kiṃcid harmika pratiyogi jñāna abādhya bheda pratiyogī adhiṣṭhāna tvāt  śuktivat iti sāmānyatas  sādhya prasiddhiḥ iti vācyam yad kiṃcid abhāva pratiyogi ghaṭa ādi jñāna abādhya bheda pratiyogi tvena ātma jñānābādhya bheda asiddheḥ sva pratiyogi jñāna abādhya bheda pratiyogi tve sādhye dṛṣṭānte sva padena śukteḥ dārṣṭa antike sva padena ātmana ukteḥ vyāpti graha anupapatteḥ yad tu jīvāt  bhinna iti eva sādhyam mithyā bhedena siddha sādhanam paścāt nirasanīyam iti tad na nirasana upāyasya nirasiṣyamāṇa tvāt  na ca brahma jīva pratiyogika dharmi sattā samāna sattāka bhedavat iti eva sādhyam dharmi padena brahmaṇa uktau  aprasiddha viśeṣaṇatva tādavasthyāt  yad kiṃcid dharmi uktau ghaṭa ādi dharma samāna sattvena siddha sādhanāt  vipakṣa bādhaka rūpa viśeṣa abhāve pūrva ukta asādhāraṇyāpatteḥ ca yad tu brahma jīva pratiyogika tāttvikā bhedavat na iti tad na evam api tāttvika abhedasya atāttvika abhāvena siddha sādhanāt  abhāve api tāttvikatva viśeṣaṇe aprasiddhi tādavasthyāt  nanu atra jīva pratiyogika tāttvika bhedasya anyonya abhāva rūpa tvāt na aprasiddhi doṣaḥ yatra hi abhāva vyāpaka tayā hetu abhāvaḥ  gṛhyate tatra eva sādhya prasiddhiḥ aṅgam iha tu jīva tādātmya vyāpaka tā hetu abhāvasya grāhyā tad abhāvaḥ  hetunā sādhyata iti kim sādhya prasiddhyā tām vinā api vyāpta graha upapatteḥ sandeha rūpa pakṣatā sampattaye api na tad apekṣā tasya assiṣā dhayiṣā viraha saha kṛta sādhaka māna abhāva rūpa tvena sandeha āghaṭita tvāt ‘brahma tattvataḥ  jīva bhinnam na ve ati sandeha abhāve api ajīva brahmaṇoḥ bhede tāttvika tvam asti nave ati sandeha saṃbhavāt ca prameya tvam etad niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi na vā iti sandehavat iti ced  na evam hi prasiddha itara bhedaḥ pṛthivyām iva prasiddha jīva bhedaḥ  brahmaṇi siddhyatu na tad gata tāttvika tvam api vyāpaka vyatirekasya vyāpya vyatireka mātra sādhana samartha tvāt anyathā ati prasaṅgāt  yad api bheda tāt tvika tvam dharma niṣṭha tvena udaśaṅki tad api sādhya aprasiddhyā duṣṭam na api brahma jīvāt  bhinnam duḥkhān anubhavitṛ tvāt ghaṭavat iti anvayi sarva anubhavitari hetoḥ asiddheḥ sva niṣṭhā iti viśeṣaṇe jīve vyabhicāraḥ duḥkhasya antaḥkaraṇa niṣṭhatvāt mithyā bhedena siddha sādhanāt ca na ca bhede sādhye artha śūnya bhrāntyā siddha sādhana ukti ayoga iti vācyam bhrānteḥ vastu śūnya tvasya eva abhāvāt uktam idam anirvācya vāde na ca etad anumiti viṣaya tayā prāmāṇika tvena siddhi atas  katham mithyātvam anumiti viṣaya tāyāḥ prāmāṇika tve atantra tvāt  na ca evam mithyātva ādi anumāne api kalpita mithyātva ādinā siddha sādhana āpattiḥ kalpita tvam vyāvahārika tvam abhipretam pratibhāsika tvam vā ādya iṣṭa āpatteḥ antye hetossvasamāna sattāka sādhya sādhaka tayā prātibhāsikatva aprasakteḥ etena brahma jīva pratiyogika dharmi sattā samāna sattāka bhedavat  duḥkhān anubhavitṛ tvāt abhrānta tvāt  asaṃsāri tvāt  ghaṭavat  jīvaḥ  vā brahma pratiyogika tādṛś bhedavān asarva śakti ādibhya iti nirastam upahitasya pakṣa tve dharmi sama sattāka tve siddhe api tāttvikatva asiddheḥ siddha sādhanāt  śodhita tattvam padārthayoḥ pakṣa tve tayoḥ dharmitva abhāvena bādhāpatteḥ na ca dharmitva abhāvam prati dharmitvā adharmi tvābhyām vyāghātaḥ brahmaṇaḥ sarva niṣedha svarūpa tvena vyāghāta abhāvāt na ca dharmi śabdena āśraya mātra vivakṣā dharmi tvavat āśraya tvasya api tatra asattvāt yad tu dharmi śabdasya pitṛ ādi śabdavat saṃbandhi śabda tvena yad kiṃcid dharmi sama sattāka tayā na siddha sādhanam iti tad na śabda svabhāva upanyāsasya anumānam pratyanupayogāt  etena  dharmi pada sthāne sva padam iti apāstam dharmi pada tulya yogakṣema tvāt  ata eva dharmi sattā samāna sattāka pada sthāne pāramārthikā iti vā yāvat svarūpam anuvartamānā iti vā sva ajñāna akārya iti vā sva jñāna abādhya iti vā viśeṣaṇam deyam sva padasya samabhivyāhṛta tad tad paratvasya vyutpatti siddha tvāt iti nirastam ādye sādhya vaikalyāt ca na ca ghaṭaḥ  jīva pratiyogika pratiyogi jñāna abādhya bhedavān jīva dharmika dharmi jñāna ābādhya abheda apratiyogi tvāt yad  yad jñāna abādhyayat harmikā bheda apratiyogi tad  tad jñāna abādhya tad pratiyogika bhedavat yathā dūra stha vanaspatyoḥ eka iti ādi anumānena sādhya siddheḥ na aprasiddhiḥ iti vācyam yad śabdān anugamena pakṣa dharma hetau vyāpti agrahāt dharmitva pratiyogitva ādi sāmānya ākāreṇa vyāpti grahe viśiṣya sādhana ayogāt  na ca evam sva prāgabhāva vyatiriktā ityādau kā gatiḥ iti vācyam tatra api etad doṣaṇa sañcāreṇa vyatirekiṇi vā anumāna antare vā tātparyāt  na api brahma tattvataḥ  jīva abhinnam na iti sādhyam evam ca na sādhya vaikalya śaṅkā api tvad mate api kalpita ghaṭe kalpita jīvāt  tāttvika bhedavat tāttvikā bhedasya api abhāvāt iti vācyam tāttvika abhedasya atāttvikena abhāvena siddha sādhanasya ukta tvāt na api jīva īśvarau dharmi jñāna abādhya paraspara pratiyogika bhedavantau viruddha dharma adhikaraṇa tvāt dahana tuhinavat  virodhaḥ ca paraspara atyanta abhāva rūpa tvam tad vyāpya tvam vā kāla bhedena api sāmānādhikaraṇyā yogya tvam vā saṃyoga tad atyanta abhāvayoḥ ca sāmānādhikaraṇyam mata dvaye api na iti na tad āśraye vyabhicāra iti vācyam dharmi padam ādāya doṣasya prāk eva ukta tvāt avyāpya vṛtti duḥkha śabda ādi adhikaraṇe vyabhicārāt ca jīva vrahma abheda siddhau svatantratva asvatantratva ādīnām sāmānādhikaraṇyā yogyatva rūpa virodhasya eva asiddhyā svarūpa asiddheḥ kalpita sārvajñyāsā arvajñi ādi vyavasthāyā varṇe hrasvatva dīrghatva ādi vyavasthāvat  kalpita bhedena eva upapattyā svābhāvika bhedam pratyaprayojaka tvāt ca na ca ‘alpa śaktiḥ asārvajñyam pāratantryam apūrṇa tā upajīvaka tvam jīva tvam īśa tvam tad viparyayaḥ svābhāvikam tayoḥ etad na anyathā tu kathañcana ityādi śrutyā sārvajñi ādeḥ svābhāvikatva uktyā kalpitatva asiddhiḥ anādya vidyā siddha tvena idānīntanatva abhāvena ca svābhāvikatva ukteḥ tad śabdena upahitayoḥ eva parāmarśāt  na tatra svābhāvikatva ukti virodhaḥ na hi upahite api sarvajñatva ādikam āgantukam na api brahma sva jñāna abādhya jīva pratiyogika bhedavat padārtha tvāt ghaṭavat  cetana tvam jīvatvā avacchinna pratiyogi tāka dharmi jñāna abādhya bhedavat vṛtti sarva caitana vṛtti tvāt cetanā vṛttitva rahita tvāt vā śabda artha tvavat iti  vācyam sva pada dharmi padān anugama tādavasthyāt antya hetoḥ jīva tve vyabhicārāt ca jaḍa vṛttitva ādi upādhi sattvena vipakṣa bādhaka abhāvena ca aprayojaka tvāt  brahmaṇaḥ  jīvavat saṃsāritva āpatta āviṣṭa āpattiḥ kalpita bhedena vā parihāraḥ  vidheyaḥ tad uktam   aaprameye anumānasya pravṛttiḥ na kathaṃcana prameyasya tu anātma tvāt tatra bheda anumeṣyate śuddha caitanye dharmān adhikaraṇa tayā anumāna aprasaraḥ yatra prasaraḥ tatra iṣṭāpattiḥ iti arthaḥ na ca evam aikya anumānam api katham bhavat padyasya tad aikya anumitiḥ katham iti paṭhitum śakya tvāt iti vācyam śuddha caitanya aikyasya śabda eka gamya tvena tatra ananumeya tvasya iṣṭa tvāt  na ca tarhi aikya anumāna upanyāsa ānarthakyam tasya bhede tāttvikatva bhrama mātra nirāsa phalaka tvāt  tasmāt  ‘a prasiddha viśeṣa tvāt anyathā eva upapattitaḥ sarva śakti alpa śakti ādeḥ na bhede tantra tā tatas  iti advaita siddhau jīva brahma bheda anumāna bhaṅgaḥ atha jīva paraspara bheda anumāna bhaṅgaḥ evam jīvānām api na paraspara bheda anumānam caitraḥ  maitra pratiyogika dharmi jñāna abādhya bhedavān maitra pratiyogika tāttvikā bhedavān na iti vā maitra anusaṃhita duḥkhān anusandhātṛ tvāt maitra smṛta sarva asmatṛ tvāt maitra anubhūta sarvān anubhavitṛ tvāt ca ghaṭavat iti atra prathama sādhye dharmi pada vikalpena dvitīya sādhye tāttvikā bhedasya atāttvika bhedena siddha sādhanāt  upahitasya pakṣa tve artha antarāt caitanya mātra pakṣa tve hetu asiddheḥ sādhana eka deśasya ananusandha anādeḥ upādhitva saṃbhavāt ca vimataḥ  bandha dhvaṃsaḥ sva pratiyogi ta avacchedaka avacchinnā ādhāra pratiyogika pratiyogi jñāna abādhya bhedavat niṣṭhaḥ bandha dhvaṃsa tvāt  saṃmatavat  jīvaḥ saṃsārī saṃsāra dhvaṃsa ādhāraḥ  vā sva jñāna abādhya jīva pratiyogika bhedavān saṃsāri pratiyogika sva jñānābādhya bhedavān vā sva jñāna abādhya saṃsāra dhvaṃsa adhikaraṇa pratiyogika bhodavān vā padārtha tvāt ghaṭavat  vimata ānandaḥ sva niṣṭha duḥkha virodhitva vyāpya dharmeṇa sajātīya pratiyogika sva jñānābādhya bhedavān duḥkha virodhi tvāt  duḥkha abhāvavat ityādiṣu bandha pratiyogika bhedavati kāla ādau dhvaṃsasya vidyamāna tvena artha antarāt duḥkha nigala sādhāraṇa bandhatva asaṃbhavāt ca sva padān anugamāt ca caitra bandha dhvaṃsaḥ caitra bandha ādhāra pratiyogika bhedavat niṣṭhaḥ bandha dhvaṃsattvāt  saṃmatavat iti ābhāsa sāmyāt ca vipakṣa bādhaka abhāvāt ca dhvaṃsa pratiyogita avacchedakam na nānā bandha anugata bandha tvam tasya sāmānya abhāvatva abhāvāt etena ātma mātra bhede ātmā ātma pratiyogika sva jñānābādhya bhedavān padārtha tvāt ghaṭavat  ātma vaibhava pakṣe ākāśaḥ ātma pratiyogika dharmi jñāna ābādhya bheda ādhāra viśeṣa guṇavat vibhu vyatiriktaḥ dravya tvāt  pṛthivīvat  pṛthivī tvam jalatva tejaḥ tu avāyutva manaḥ tvā itara dravyatva sākṣāt vyāpya jāti bhinnam prameya tvāt jala tvavat  gaganatva jāti pakṣe tad itara tvam api viśeṣaṇam sattā dravya tvāni ātma niṣṭha jāti anyā dravya tvam vā sattāni ātma niṣṭha jātu anyat meya tvāt  ghaṭavat  ātma aṇutva mate ātmā dravya tu api api ajātimān avibhudravya tvāt  ghaṭavat ityādibhiḥ ātmatva jāti siddhau tāttvika ātma bheda siddhiḥ iti  nirastam ādye jaḍa tvam upādhiḥ ātma padayoḥ sthāne caitra padam prakṣipya ābhāsa sāmyam ca dvitīye śabdān āśraya tvam upādhiḥ vibhāva ātmā anya tvam viśeṣaṇam dattvā ātma ākāśa bhinnasya vibhoḥ viśeṣa guṇavataḥ sādhana prasaṅgāt ca jāti pakṣaka anumāneṣu kalpita vyakti bhedena api tasyāḥ jāteḥ upapattyā tāttvika vyakti bheda paryavasāyi tvena artha antarāt na ca jāteḥ dharmi jñāna abādhya bhedam vinā ayogaḥ anyathā vyakti abhedaḥ kvāpi jāti bādhakaḥ  na syāt iti vācyam jāteḥ vyakti bheda samāna sattākatva niyamena prātibhāsika bhedasya vyāvahārika jātim prati na sādhaka tvam iti vyakti abhedasya jāti bādhakatva saṃbhavāt iti advaita siddhau jīva bheda anumāna bhaṅgaḥ atha jīva bheda anukūla tarka bhaṅgaḥ nanu yadi ātma aikyam syāt  caitreṇa sarva duḥkha ādi anusandhānam syāt  iti ced na aupādhika bhedena ananusandhāna upapatteḥ nanu hasta pāda ādi upādhi bhede api anusandhāna darśanāt upādhi bhedaḥ aprayojakaḥ na ca viśliṣṭa upādhi bhedaḥ tatra tantram mātṛ sukha ādeḥ garbha sthena anusandhānāpātāt  bhārate ‘udyata āyudha dos daṇḍāḥ patita sva śira ukṣibhiḥ paśyantaḥ pātayanti sma kabandhā api arīn yudhi ityādinā viśleṣe api anusandhāna ukteḥ ca iti ced na na hi vayam yad kiṃcid upādhi mātram ananu sandhāna prayojakam brūmaḥ kiṃtu antaḥkaraṇa rūpa upādhi bhedam avidyā bhedam vā sa ca bhedaḥ kabandhe yogini ca na asti eva tena tatra anusandhānam caitra maitrayoḥ ca asti iti ananu sandhānam etena śarīra rūpa upādhi bhedasya ananusandhāna prayojaka tve bālya anubhūtasya yauvane jāti smareṇa pūrva janma anubhūtasya yoginā nānā śarīra anubhūtasya ca smaraṇam na syāt iti nirastam śarīra bhedasya tatra atantra tvāt yogi jāta smartṛṇām antaḥkaraṇa aikyāt na ca  caitanya aikye antaḥkaraṇa bhedasya na ananusandhāna prayojaka tvam cakṣuḥ ādi karaṇa bhede api anusandhāna darśanāt iti vācyam anya karaṇa bhedena tathā darśane api antaḥkaraṇa bhedasya tad aikya adhyāsa āpanne ananusandhāna prayojaka tvam kalpyate anyathā brahma aikyasya jīve śruti siddha tayā sarva anusandhānāpatteḥ na ca antaḥkaraṇasya pratyaham suṣuptau vilayena pūrva dina anubhūtasya ananusandhān āpattiḥ iti vācyam saṃskāra ātmanā avasthitasya eva punar udbodhena tatra antaḥkaraṇa bheda abhāvāt  na ca evam suṣupta pralīna m uktānām ananu sandhāna prayojaka antaḥkaraṇa bheda abhāvāt  saṃsāri duḥkha anusandhān āpattiḥ iti vācyam teṣām anusandhāna prayojaka antaḥkaraṇa aikya adhyāsa rūpa sāmagrī virahāt na hi pratibandhaka mātreṇa kārya virahaḥ kiṃtu sāmagrī viraheṇa api na ca evam muktasya svarūpa sukha anubhāvaḥ api na syāt iti vācyam tasya ājanya tvena antaḥkaraṇa anapekṣa tvāt jīva vibhājaka upādhya jñāna bheda abhedābhyām anusandhāna ananu sandhāna upapatteḥ ca na ca jñāna prāc abhāvavat ajñānasya api bheda abhedayoḥ tatra aprayojaka tvam yāvanti jñānāni tāvanti ajñānāni iti mate ekasmin  api jīve brahma viṣaya ka ajñānānām bhinna tvena anusandhāna viraha prasaṅga iti vācyam jñāna prāc abhāvānām jñāna sama saṅkhyā jñānānām ca jīva vibhājakatva abhāvena anusandhānā dau  aprayojaka tvāt  yad tu—muktasya evam saṃsāra duḥkha anusandhānāpattiḥ avidyā rūpa upādhi bheda ananu sandhāne sva rūpa sukhasya api ananubhava āpātaḥ—iti tad na vaiṣayika sukha ādi anusandhāne tasya tantra tvena sva prakāśa svarūpa sphuraṇe tad anapekṣa tvāt nanu evam aneka avidyā saṃbandhasya duḥkha anusandhāna svarūpasya anarthasya ca viśiṣṭa gata tve bandha mokṣayoḥ vaiyadhi karaṇyā pātena śuddha gata tve vācye yad śuddham caitrīya duḥkha anusandhātṛ tad eva maitrīya duḥkha anusandhātriti katham anusandhāna ananu sandhāna vyavasthā iti ced na avidyā ātmaka bandha nivṛtti ātmaka mokṣasya śuddha gata tve api duḥkha ādi anusandhātṛ tvasya upahita vṛtti tayā śuddha bheda āpādanā yogāt na ca saṃsārasya śuddha gata tve brahmaṇaḥ api saṃsāritva āpattiḥ bimba pratibimbayoḥ avadātatva śyāma tvavat ghaṭa ākāśa mahā ākāśayoḥ paricchinnatva aparicchinna tvavat ekasya eva nabhasaḥ tad tad karṇa puṭa avacchedena tatra tatra śrotra tāvat ca aupādhika bhedena saṃsāri tvā saṃsāritva vyavasthā upapatteḥ ata eva duḥkha anusandhāna rūpasya anarthasya upahita niṣṭha tvena tasya kalpita tvena baddhasya nivṛttiḥ eva na tu mokṣa iti āpāta iti nirastam upādheḥ kalpita tvena nivṛttau  api upadheyasya akalpita tayā tad nivṛtti ayogāt mokṣa anvaya upapatteḥ na ca pratibimbasya chāyāvat vastu antara tvena ākāśasya api tvad mate api kārya dravya tayā sāvayava tvena taijasa ahaṅkāra kāryāṇām śrotrāṇām svata eva bhinna tvena dṛṣṭānta asaṃmatiḥ iti vācyam pratibimbe vastu antaratvasya nirasiṣyamāṇa tvāt  ākāśa śrotra bhāvasya para rītyā dṛṣṭānta tvāt   ātma indriya manaḥ yuktam bhoktā iti āhuḥ manīṣiṇa iti śruteḥ viśiṣṭasya eva bhoktṛ tvāt tasya bhinna tvāt  vyavasthā iti kaumudyukta prakāreṇa api anusandhāna ananu sandhāna upapatteḥ ca ata eva śuddha cit mātra gata tve tatra bheda apratītyā bhedasya kalpitasya api abhāvaḥ bhāve vā bhedasya eva vyavasthā rūpa sva kārya kāriṇaḥ  vahnau  uṣṇa tvavat dharmi jñāna avādhya tvam abhedasya tu avyavasthā rūpa sva kārya akāriṇaḥ anuṣṇa tvavat mithyā tvam iti āpātaḥ āvidyaka bheda hīnasya muktasya saṃsāri duḥkha anubhava āpātaḥ ca iti nirastam vyavasthāyāḥ sva samāna sattāka bheda kārya tvena sva adhika sattāka bhede anākṣepaka tvāt  avyavasthāyāḥ śuddha caitanya abheda akārya tvena tad akāritva prayukta mithyā tvasya āpādayitum aśakyatvāt upādhi abhedasya eva tatra tantra tvāt kiṃca upādhi kalpita aṃśa jīvānām vā anusandhānam āpādyate aṃśinaḥ brahmaṇaḥ  vā na ādyaḥ hasta avacchinnena pāda avacchinna duḥkha ādi ananusandhānāt na ca na vayam bhoga āyatanānām sa aṅkaryam āpādayāmaḥ yena pāde me vedanā śirasi me sukham iti na syāt  kiṃtu anusandhāna mātram tad ca aṃśānām asti eva anyathā caitra deha lagna kaṇṭaka uddharaṇāya maitrasya iva pāda lagna kaṇṭaka uddharaṇāya hastasya vyāpāraḥ  na syāt iti vācyam pāda avacchinna duḥkhasya hasta avacchinne anutpādanavat  caitrīya duḥkha ādi anusandhānasya maitre anutpādaḥ haste duḥkha prayojaka sāmagrī virahavat  maitre anusandhāna prayojaka upādhi aikya abhāvāt tathā ca hasta avacchedena anusandhānam asti eva iti na tatra vyāpāra abhāva āpattiḥ na antyaḥ tasya abhoktṛ tvena bhoga aprasaṅgāt  duḥkha ādi jñāna mātrasya ca sarvajñe tasmin  iṣṭa tvāt  na ca bhoktṛ jīvā bhinna tvena brahmaṇaḥ api bhoktṛ tvā āpattiḥ bimba pratibimbavat vyavasthā upapatteḥ anusandhānasya avacchinna gata tayā śuddha brahmaṇi āpādana ayogāt ca na ca etāvatā bandha mokṣayoḥ vaiyadhi karaṇyam avidyā ātmaka bandhasya śuddha gata tvena sāmānādhikaraṇya upapatteḥ avacchinnasya anusandhātṛ tve api avasthā traya anusyūta avidyā avacchinna dvārā śuddhe anusandhātṛ tvasya iṣṭa tvāt  ‘anena jīvene ati ādi śruteḥ kiṃca yathā sva karṇa puṭa paricchinna nāda upalambhe bhāga antara varti nāda anupalambhaḥ tathā sukha duḥkha ādi upalambhānupalambhau na ca ātma bhede karṇa puṭānām tad tadīyatva niyāmakavat eka ātma vāde sarva dehānām svīya tvena tad tadīyatva niyama abhāvena vyavasthā anupapattiḥ iti vācyam tava ātma bhedena iva avacchedaka ajñāna ādi bhedena mama vyavasthā upapatteḥ kiṃca vyavasthayā bhedam vadan praṣṭavyaḥ kā iyam vyavasthā na tāvat dharma bhedaḥ ekasmin  eva sukha duḥkha darśanena vyabhicārāt  bhinna āśraya dharma uktau anyonya āśrayāt viruddha dharma uktau tu viruddha tvasya saha anavasthāna rūpa tve asiddheḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāva rūpa tve tasya eka āśraya tvena upapattyā bheda asādhaka tvāt na api anusandhāna ananusandhāne tayoḥ uktena prakāreṇa upādhi bhedena upapatteḥ ātma bheda asādhaka tvasya ukta tvāt ata eva bandha mukti ādi vyavasthā api na svābhāvika bheda sādhanāya tad tad upādhi upagama apagamābhyām eva vyavasthā upapatteḥ na ca upādheḥ api upahita niṣṭhatvena ātma āśraya ādi doṣaḥ upādheḥ aviśeṣaṇa tvena vyakti antara anapekṣa tvena ca ātma āśraya ādi caturṇām anavakāśāt  etena śuddha niṣṭhatve kim ekaika upādhi apagamaḥ  muktiḥ uta sarva upādhi apagamaḥ na ādyaḥ sadā muktiḥ eva na tu bandha iti āpātāt  na antyaḥ adhunā bandha eva na kasya api muktiḥ iti āpātāt iti nirastam yena upādhinā yasya caitanyasya paricchinna tvam tasmin caitanye tad upādhi apagamasya eva mukti tve nānā jīva vāde pūrva ukta doṣa an avakāśāt eka jīva vāde sarva upādhi apagamasya eva mukti tayā idānīm mukti abhāvasya iṣṭa tvāt  nanuupādheḥ katham bhedaka tvam tathā hi—u pādhiḥ kim eka deśena saṃbadhyate kṛtsnena vā ādye tvad mate svābhāvika aṃśa abhāvena aupādhika tvam vācyam tathā ca anavasthā antye na bhedaka tā kṛtsnasya eka upādhigrasta tvāt gagana ādau  api svābhāvika aṃśa abhāve ghaṭa ādi upādhi saṃbandhaḥ  na syāt eva tad uktam ana ced upādhi saṃbandha eka deśe atha sarvagaḥ eka deśe anavasthā syāt  sarva gacet na bhedakaḥ iti ced na sarva vikalpa asaha tvena mithyā bhūtasya eva upādheḥ mithyā bheda prayojaka tvasya prāk eva upapādanāt  yathā ca ātmanām sarva gatānām bhede vyavasthā anupapattiḥ tathā prapañcitam bhāṣya kṛdbhiḥ iti advaita siddhau jīva bheda anukūla tarka bhaṅgaḥ atha bheda pañcake anumāna bhaṅgaḥ evam jaḍa īśa bhede jaḍa jīva bhede ca tāttvike pramāṇam na asti   brahma jīvaḥ  vā anātma pratiyogika dharmi jñāna abādhya bhedavān padārtha tvāt ghaṭavat      brahma jīvaḥ  vā ghaṭa pratiyogika dharmi jñāna abādhya bhedavān ghaṭa asaṃbandhi kāla saṃbandhi tvāt tad asaṃbandhi deśa saṃbandhi tvāt tad janakā janya tvāt vā paṭavat      brahma jīvaḥ  vā jaḍa pratiyogika dharmi jñāna abādhya bhedavān jaḍāna ātmaka tvāt  yad evam tad evam yathā dūra stha vanaspatyoḥ eka ityādiṣu pūrva ukta doṣān ativṛtteḥ paricchinna tvasya jaḍa tvasya janya tvasya ca upādhi tvāt  aprayojaka tvāt ca jīvaḥ  brahma vā ātma pratiyogika tādṛś bheda adhikaraṇam padārtha tvāt ityādi ābhāsa sāmyāt ca na ca ghaṭā bhede ghaṭa siddhyā eva tad siddhyā vedānta vaiyarthyam brahmaṇaḥ  jaḍatva anityatva ādi āpattiḥ mukti samāna adhikaraṇa bandha ādhārasya jīvasya jaḍavat nivṛtti āpattiḥ gauraḥ aham iti ādi pratītiḥ ca pramā syāt ityādi vipakṣa bādhaka anna ābhāsa sāmya ādikam iti vācyam sva prakāśa tvena sarva pratyaya vedya tvena ca brahma siddhau  api sa vilāsā jñāna nivartaka jñānāya vedānta sāphalyasya bahudhā abhidhānāt ghaṭa ādau kalpita vyakti antareṇa akalpita bhedasya abhāve api na yathā kalpita vyakti ātmaka tvam tadvat  prātibhāsika tvam tadvat viśeṣa darśanena nivṛttiḥ vā kalpita vyakti antar aikya jñāna pramātvam vā tathā prakṛte api kalpita jaḍena tad abhāve api na tad ātmaka tvāt iti na vipakṣa bādhakasya api aprasaraḥ evam jaḍānām anyonya bhede api na anumānam ghaṭaḥ tattvataḥ śukti abhijñaḥ  na śukti saṃbaddha kāla asaṃbandhi tvāt tad janaka ajanya tvāt tatra āropita rūpyavat  vyāvahārika bhedasya tvayā api aṅgīkāreṇa na pakṣa dṛṣṭānta ādi anupapattiḥ anyathā bheda sidhya siddhyoḥ doṣa tadabhāvayoḥ ca abhedena sva kriyā virodhaḥ syāt iti atra tāttvika śukti abhinnatva rūpa pratiyogya prasiddhyā sādhya aprasiddheḥ tad tvata iti asya na iti atra viśeṣaṇa tve suta rām aprasiddheḥ ghaṭa ādi sama sattāka bheda mātreṇa hetoḥ upapattyā aprayojaka tvāt ca bhedasya tāttvika tve bādhasya ukta tvena bādhāt ca   anātmā sva vṛtti dharma an ādhāra jñāna bādhya antar gaṇika bhedavān padārtha tvāt ātmavat  vipakṣe ca dūra stha vanaspatyoḥ śukti rūpyayoḥ ca abheda grāhi pratyakṣam na tattva avedakam syāt  mukti saṃsāra ādi sāṃkaryam ca syāt iti ādi bādhakam iti yad  tad na ekatra ghaṭe kalpitā ye aneke ghaṭāḥ teṣu sva vṛtti dharmān adhikaraṇa ghaṭa jñāna bādhya bhedavatsu vyabhicārāt  yad kiṃcid sva vṛtti dharmān ādhāra uktau ghaṭatva anadhikaraṇa paṭa jñāna abādhya bhedena ātma jñāna bādhyena artha antaram sva vṛtti aśeṣa dharmānādhāra uktau tava mate brahmaṇaḥ api vācyatva ādi kevala anvayi dharma ādhāra tvena sādhya aprasiddheḥ kalpitena saha tāttvika bheda abhāvavat  tāttvika abhedasya api abhāvena ūhā hṛta sthale tattva āvedakatva sāṅkarya ādīnām aprasaṅgāt  yad tu ātmānātmanoḥ ca parasparam tāttvika bhede anātmā svāvṛtti dharma adhikaraṇa pratiyogika pratiyogi jñāna abādhya bheda adhikaraṇam yad svāvṛtti dharma adhikaraṇam tad pratiyogika pratiyogi jñāna ābādhya bheda adhikaraṇam padārtha tvāt ātmavat  pakṣe svāvṛtti dharma adhikaraṇam ātmā tatas  bhinnāt ātma antarāt bhinna tvena sādhya siddhiḥ dṛṣṭānte ca svāvṛtti dharma adhikaraṇam jaḍam tatas  bhinnāt  jaḍa antarāt bhinna tvena sādhya sattvam iti tad na pakṣa dṛṣṭāntayoḥ sva padārtha pratiyogi padārthayoḥ ananugamena vyāpyatva asiddheḥ ajaḍa tvasya upādhi tvāt ca jaḍa tvena vyatirekiṇā sat pratipakṣāt ca yad api jīvasya brahmataḥ  jīvāt ca jaḍasya satyabhede pṛthivī brahma pratiyogika dharmi jñāna abādhya bheda adhikaraṇam yad aptva ādi anadhikaraṇam tad pratiyogika pratiyogi jñāna ābādhya bhedavatī vastu tvāt toyavat aptu ādi ityādi śabdena tad tad vādinaḥ prati tad tad vādi siddhāḥ pṛthivītva bhinnāḥ jaḍa niṣṭha dharmā vivakṣitāḥ pakṣe brahma bhinnāt jīvāt bhinna tvena sādhya siddhiḥ dṛṣṭānte tu brahma bhinna pārthiva bhinna tvena iti tad na aptva ādi anadhikaraṇa tvavat jīva tvānadhikaraṇa iti api viśeṣaṇam dattvā jīva brahma bhinna ātmanaḥ api sādhana prasaṅgāt  gandha ādhāratva ādi vyatirekiṇā sat pratipakṣa saṃbhavāt ca dharmi pada vikalpa nibandhana doṣa tādavasthyāt ca etena jīvasya brahma jīva antarābhyām jīvāt ca jaḍasya bhede pūrva prayoga eva jīvasya jīva antarāt bheda siddhi artham antar gaṇika bhedana uditi aptvā anadhikaraṇa iti atra viśeṣaṇam dattvā anumānam atra ca pakṣe brahmaṇaḥ parasparam ca bhinnāt jīvāt bhinna tvena sādhya siddhiḥ dṛṣṭānte tu brahmaṇaḥ parasparañca bhinnāt  pārthivāt  bhinna tvena iti nirastam jīvasya brahma jīva antarābhyām jaḍasya ca jīvāt  brahmaṇaḥ  jaḍāt ca bhede pṛthivī brahma pratiyogika dharmi jñāna abādhya bheda adhikaraṇam aptu ādi anadhikaraṇam antar gaṇika bhedavat ca yad tad pratiyogika pratiyogi jñāna abādhya bhedavat tve sati aptva ādi anadhikaraṇā saṃsāri dharmika dharmi jñāna abādhya bheda pratiyoginī vastu tvāt ambuvat iti atra brahmaṇaḥ  jaḍāt api bheda artham pūrvasmāt adhikam aptvā anadhikaraṇa asaṃsārī ityādi viśeṣaṇam atra pakṣe aptva ādi anadhikaraṇam asaṃsāri brahma tad harmika bheda pratiyogi tvena sādhya siddhiḥ dṛṣṭānte tvap tvā ādi anadhikaraṇa asaṃsāri pārthivam tad harmika bheda pratiyogi tvena jñeyam atra jīva tvāt adhikaraṇa tvasya aptvā an adhikaraṇa iti atra viśeṣaṇa tvena pūrvavat ābhāsa sāmyāt  pākaja rūpa adhikaraṇatva ādinā sat pratipakṣāt ca dharma ādi pada vikalpa grāsāt ca evam bheda mātre api na anumānam brahma bheda hīnam na avatiṣṭhate sva jñāna abādhya bhedavat vā padārtha tvāt ghaṭavat  iti mukti asaha vṛtti tvasya jaḍa tvasya ca upādhi tvāt  sva pada vikalpa grāsāt ca etena anātmā sva anya jñāna abādhya bheda adhikaraṇam padārtha tvāt ātmavat iti nirastam brahma bhedaḥ  na sarva niṣṭhā atyanta abhāva pratiyogi brahma nirūpya tvāt  brahmā abhedavat iti atra brahma abhinnauvṛtti tvam upādhiḥ brahma abhedasya abrahma nirūpya tvena tad anirūpyatayā sādhana vaikalyam ca brahma jñānam sva bādhya bhedavat viṣayakam jñāna tvāt śukti jñāna vaditi atra anātma viṣaya tvam upādhiḥ sva padena brahma jñāna uktau tad abādhya bheda aprasiddhyā sādhya aprasiddhiḥ śukti jñāna uktau siddha sādhanam ghaṭaḥ  ghaṭa saṃsarga an avacchinna pratiyogi tāka paṭa ādi dharmika traikālikā bhāva pratiyogi dravya tvāt  paṭavat iti atra kālpanikā bhāvasya api kāla traya vṛttitva saṃbhavena siddha sādhanam ghaṭa saṃsarga an avacchinna itivat tādātmyān avacchinnā iti api viśeṣaṇam dattvā pañcama abhāva sādhanasya api prasaṅgaḥ ca vipakṣa bādhaka abhāvasya ubhayatra sattvāt  samāna adhikaraṇa karma prāgabhāva samāna kālīna jñāna bādhā yogyaḥ  bhedaḥ paramārtha san prātibhāsika tvān adhikaraṇa tve satya sattvān adhikaraṇa tvāt svāsattva agocara pramām prati sākṣāt viṣaya tvāt  āropita mithyātvaka tvāt  kalpaka rahita tvāt  sva viṣayaka sākṣātkārāt pūrva bhāvi tvāt  ātmavat  brahma jīva pratiyogi kaḥ  bhedaḥ paramārtha san anādi tvāt ātmavat sa akṣi vedya sukha duḥkha ādi bhedaḥ paramārtha san aniṣedhya tvena doṣa ajanya jñānam prati sākṣāt viṣaya tvāt  dharma adharma yāga dāna ādi bhedaḥ paramārtha san śruti tātparya viṣaya tvāt ityādiṣu ātma asādhāraṇa dharmāṇām cetanatva ādīnām upādhi tvam jaḍatva ādinā sat pratipakṣaḥ ca mithyātva sādhakānām prābalyasya ukta tvena taiḥ bādhaḥ ca ādye ca prātibhāsika tvasya doṣa prayukta bhānatva ātmaka tve asiddhiḥ brahma jñāna itara bādhyatva uktau carama vṛttya vyavahita prātibhāsike vyabhicāraḥ ca dvitīya hetau tādṛś pramā viṣaya tvasya bheda pāramārthikatva siddhi adhīna tvena sādhya aviśeṣa paryavasānam tṛtīye carama vṛtti anya bādhya mithyā tvaka tvasya upādhi tvam caturthe avidyā rūpa kalpaka sattvena asiddhiḥ pañcame dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi pakṣe asiddhiḥ itaratra aprayojaka tā anādi tvam ca ajñāna ādau vyabhicāri doṣa ajanya jñānam pratīti atra śruti tātparya viṣaya tvāt iti atra ca asiddhiḥ sākṣi avacchedaka vṛtteḥ doṣa janya tvāt  mukhyatas tāt paryasya tatra abhāvāt tasmāt  bheda pañcakam na anumāna viṣayaḥ iti advaita siddhau bheda pañcake anumāna bhaṅgaḥ atha bheda śruteḥ anuvādatva upapattiḥ nanu bheda tāttvika tve advāsuparṇā ya ātmani tiṣṭhan nityaḥ  nityānām cetanaḥ cetanānām ajaḥ hi ekaḥ  juṣamāṇaḥ anuśete jahāti enām bhukta bhogām ajaḥ anya iti śrutayaḥ mānam iti ced na dvāsuparṇā iti atra pūrva ardham na bhedaḥ prameyaḥ apadārtha tvāt avākya artha tvāt ca dvi tvasya sva āśraya pratiyogika bheda samāna adhikaraṇatva niyamāt śruta dvitva artha āpatti samadhi gamyasya api bhedasya śrauta tvam iti ced  na dvau candram asau  iti atra iva kalpita bhedena api upapatteḥ tāttvika bhedān ākṣepaka tvāt  ata eva na uttara ardhasya api tāttvika bheda paratvam vastutas tu asyāḥ śruteḥ paiṅgi rahasi abrāhmaṇe buddhi jīva para tayā vyākṛta tvena jīva īśa bheda paratvasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  ‘ya ātmani tiṣṭhan iti ādau  ādhāra ādheya bhāvasya acetanaḥ cetanānām i ati nirdhāraṇasya aajaḥ anya iti atra bheda vyapadeśasya kālpanika bhedam ādāya api upapatteḥ bheda tāttvikatva aparyavasāyi tvāt śruti antara virodhāt ca na ca etad śruti virodhāt sā eva śrutiḥ anya parā bheda śruteḥ pratyakṣa siddha bheda anuvāda tvena hīna bala tvāt  na ca jīvatvā avacchinna jīva bhedasya aprāptyā ‘na hiṃsi ādi atyādivat ananuvāda tvam jīve īśvara bhedasya pratyakṣa siddha tayā tad anyathā anupapatti siddha īśa dharmika jīvatva avacchinna bhedasya api pratyakṣa siddha tulya kakṣya tayā tad bodhaka śruteḥ anuvādatva upapatteḥ na hiṃsi āditi atra na anuvādatva śaṅkā api brāhmaṇaḥ  na hantavya iti ādeḥ purovādakatva nirṇāyaka abhāvāt na ca puṃviśeṣam pratyasya arthavat tvam śākhā antara stha vidhi vākyavat iti vācyam ekasya aneka śākhā adhyayanā saṃbhavāt pratyakṣasya sarva puruṣa sādhāraṇyena prāthamika prasara tvena ca puruṣa viśeṣam pratyapi sārthaka tvasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  na ca  advayoḥ praṇayantī atyādivat  vartamāna mātra grāhi pratyakṣa aprāpta kāla traya ābādhya bheda prāpaka tvam iti vācyam ajaḥ hi anya iti ādau tri kālābādhyatva bodhaka pada abhāvāt na ca abhede ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅgavat dārḍya artha tvam bheda śruteḥ iti vācyam tatra prayojanavat tve api anuvādatva aparihārāt agniḥ himasya bheṣajam itivat  na ca ‘ṣaviṃśatiḥ iti eva brūyādi ativat  pratiprasava artha tvam tad apekṣayā hīna bala tvena pratiprasava ayogāt bheda niṣedhaka śruteḥ bheda tāt tvikatva niṣedha paratvena bheda svarūpa pratipādaka vākyasya tad pratiprasava ayogāt na ca pratyakṣasya aprāmāṇye śruteḥ tad siddha anuvādakatva ayogaḥ tasyāḥ  jñāta jñāpakatva mātreṇa anuvādakatva upapatteḥ na ca evam api nirapekṣa anuvāda tvena dhārāvāhika dvitīya ādi jñānavat  pramātvā upapattiḥ iti vācyam nirapekṣasa apekṣa sādhāraṇa anuvādatva mātrasya aprāmāṇya prayojaka tvāt  dṛṣṭāntasya atirikta kāla kalā viṣaya tu ena anadhigata artha viṣaya tayā viṣama tvāt  na ca vidvat vākyavat  sa prayojana anuvāda tvena sva artha para tā tasya sva artha bodhaka tve api dvitva saṃpādaka tayā sva artha paratva abhāvāt na ca yad tad na ityādi niṣedha artha anuvāda liṅga abhāvena vidheya antara śravaṇena ca niṣedha artha anuvādatva ayogaḥ yad tad iti ādeḥ anuvāda liṅga tve api anuvāda vyāpakatva abhāvāt anyena api hi unnayana saṃbhavāt  ‘brāhmaṇaḥ  na hantavya iti ādau yad tad pada abhāve api niṣedha anuvāda darśanāt  vidheya antara sattve tu niṣedha artha anuvādakatva abhāve api tad artha anuvādatva aparihārāt na ca evam vidhāna artha anuvāde tāttvikatva niyamaḥ yad rajatam tadānayā ityādau anya vidhāna artham bhrānti siddha anuvāde tāttvikatva adarśanāt  na ca anuvāda tve api yathārthatva rūpa prāmāṇya aha aniriti vācyam tasya bādhaka abhāva nibandhana tvena prakṛte asaṃbhavāt  nanu aupaniṣadasya brahmaṇaḥ śāstra atiriktena aprāpteḥ tad harmikasya tad pratiyogikasya vā bhedasya katham śāstra nirapekṣa pratyakṣa ādinā prāptiḥ iti ced na pratiyogi graha artham tad apekṣa tve api sva samāna viṣaya pramāṇa pūrvakatva aniyamena pratyakṣasya bheda prāpakatva upapatteḥ yadi api īśa dhārmikasya bhedasya pratyakṣeṇa aprāptiḥ tathā api pratyakṣa siddha jīva dharmi keśa bhedāni atha anupapatti siddhasya api tasya śruta arthāpatti siddhasya śrauta tvavat  pratyakṣa siddhatva upapatteḥ iti advaita siddhau bheda śruteḥ anuvādaka tvam atha bheda śruteḥ vyāvahārika bheda paratva upapattiḥ athavā anuvādakatva abhāve api vyāvahārika bheda paratvena eva śruti upapattiḥ na ca aprāmāṇi āpātaḥ arthavāda vākyavat upapatteḥ pratīyamāna arthe ca abheda śruti virodhena aprāmāṇyasya iṣṭa tvāt ca na ca abheda śruteḥ akhaṇḍa cit mātra paratvena bheda avirodhi tvam tad vārībhūta artham ādāya tad virodhāt  na api vaiparītyam prāpta aprāpta artha tvābhyām viśeṣāt  na ca aikya śruteḥ api pratyakṣa viruddha tvāt aprāmāṇyam māna antara prāptivat  tad virodhasya api daurbalya hetu tvāt iti vācyam virodhe virodhinaḥ  māna tvavat  anuvādakatva upapādakasya mānatāyāḥ  anapekṣita tvāt  kiṃca ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅgava tvāt aikya śruteḥ prābalyam na ca tātparya mātra jñāpaka tvena teṣām artha tathātva ājñāpaka tvam iti vācyam śruteḥ tad paratva jñāpanena paramparayā upayogāt etad viruddha śruteḥ śrūyamāṇe arthe tātparya abhāva saṃpādanena adhika bala saṃpādaka tvāt ca na ca ‘atrā api svādu atti anaśnan pūrṇaḥ paraḥ jīva saṃghaḥ  hi apūrṇa ityādi upapatti rūpam ‘satyam bhidā satyam bhidā satyam bhide ati abhyāsa ādi rūpam tātparyaliṅgam asti iti bheda śrutiḥ api tad para iti vācyam atti iti apūrṇa iti ca jīva anuvādena tasya pūrṇa brahma rūpa tā vidhāna artha tvena bheda upapattitva abhāvāt satyam bhidā iti na bheda abhyāsaḥ etad vākyasya aprāmāṇika tvāt  prāmāṇika tve vā bādhāyām sāmānādhikaraṇyena abhede paryavasānāt  nanu—bheda śrutiḥ eva prabalā  sañjāta virodhi tvāt  pratyakṣa ādi saṃvādāt niravakāśa tvāt ca iti ced na abheda śruti rūpa virodhinaḥ  jāta tvāt  pratyakṣa ādeḥ apramāṇa tvena tad saṃvādasya prābalyā prayojaka tvāt  śatam api andhānām iti nyāyāt  vyāvahārika bheda viṣaya tvena sa avakāśa tvāt ca nanu  na ayam bhedaḥ  vyāvahārikaḥ muktau  api bhedasya śruti smṛtibhyām siddheḥ iti ced na tasyāḥ  mukteḥ avāntara tvāt  nanu ‘idam jñānam upāśritya mama sādharmyam āgatāḥ sarge api na upajāyante pralaye na vyathanti ca ityādi smṛtau sarga ādi abhāva ukteḥ ‘na yatra māyā kim uta apare hareḥ anuvratā yatra sura asura arcitāḥ śyāma avadātāḥ śatapatra locanāḥ piśaṅga vastrāḥ su rucaḥ supeśasa iti smṛtau māyā niṣedhāt ca ‘yaḥ  veda nihitam guhāyām saḥ aśrute sarvān kāmān saha brahmaṇā vipaścite atyatra śuddha brahma jñāna phalatva ukteḥ ca tvayā api śuddha brahma viṣaya tvena svīkṛtāyāḥ bhūma vidyāyāḥ phala ukti avasare ‘tasya sarveṣu lokeṣu kāma cāraḥ  bhavati pañcadhā saptadhe atyādi bheda ukteḥ ‘param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate ‘sa tatra paryeti jakṣan krīḍan ramamāṇa iti ādau svarūpa abhivyakti ukteḥ ca atathā vidvān puṇya pāpe vidhūya nirañjanaḥ paramam sāmyam upaitī atyatra karma kṣaya ukteḥ ca ‘juṣṭam yadā paśyati anyam īśam asya mahimānam iti vīta śokaḥ pṛthak ātmānam preritāram ca matvā juṣṭaḥ tatas tena amṛta tvam etī ati bheda jñānāt mokṣa ukteḥ ca tvad mate api bheda bhoga ādi phaleṣu phala adhyāyāntya pāda stheṣu ‘jagat vyāpāra varjam ‘saṅkalpāt eva tu tad śruteḥ ‘bhoga mātra sāmya liṅgāt ce ati sūtreṣu prakrānta śuddha vidyā phalasya eva vaktavya tvāt ca parama mukti tvam eva iti ced na sa guṇa upāsanayā brahma lokam gatasya api ana sa punar āvartata ityādi śrutyā dainandina sarga ādi asaṃbandhasya pratipādanena avāntara muktau  api upapatteḥ ‘na tatra māye atyādi smṛtau ca māyā śabdasya mātsarya ādi paratvena mūla māyā virahā pratīteḥ anyathā śyāma avadāta tvāt iti virodha āpatteḥ ‘yaḥ  veda nihitam i atyatra śuddha brahma jñāna phala bhūtā yā sarva kāma avāptiḥ sā na vaiṣayika bhoga rūpā kiṃtu sarva vaiṣayika sukhānām aetasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvantī atiśrutyā brahma ānande antarbhāva ukteḥ tad abhiprāya iti na tad balāt nānā kāma avāpteḥ śuddha jñāna phala tvam bhūma vidyā phala ukti avasare sarva loka kāma cāra eka dhābhāva ādeḥ phalasya bhūma vidyā vākya upakrame prāṇa vidyā phala tvena uktasya jyotiṣṭoma prakaraṇe śrūyamāṇā hīna dvādaśa upasattāvat nirguṇa vidyāḥ tāvaka tvena api upapatteḥ svayaṃjyotiḥ iti ādau jakṣaṇa prabhṛtīnām bheda garbha tvena jakṣan  iva krīḍan  iva iti ādi bādhitatva vivakṣayā parama mukteḥ tatra uktyā tvad abhimata bheda garbha krīḍā ādīnām parama muktitva abhāvāt puṇya pāpe vidhūya iti atra parama sāmyasya aikya rūpa tayā karma kṣayasya aikya rūpa mukti phala tayā bheda garbha mukti phalatva abhāvāt juṣṭam iti atra anya padasya deha indriya ādi vilakṣaṇa ātma paratvena jīveśa paratva abhāvāt tathā ca bheda jñānasya mokṣa hetu tvam atas avagamyate mad mate bheda bhoga ādi pareṣu ‘saṅkalpāt eva tad śrute ariti ārabhya adhyāya parisamāpti paryanta adhikaraṇeṣu sa guṇa vidyā phalasya ukta tayā śuddha brahma vidyā phala apratipādaka tvāt  tasmāt  parama muktau bhedasya aprasakteḥ vyāvahārikatva upapattyā bheda śruteḥ vyāvahārika paratvam sthitam iti advaita siddhau bheda śruteḥ vyāvahārika bheda paratva upapattiḥ atha śabda antara ādeḥ ātma bheda sādhakatva asaṃbhavaḥ nanu pūrvatantre dvitīya adhyāye yaiḥ eva śabda antara ādibhiḥ karma bheda uktaḥ taiḥ eva jīveśa bhedaḥ api sidhyati tathā hi eṣa eva jīvam prabodhayati aetasmāt jīva uttiṣṭhatī ati viruddha artha dhātu niṣpanna ākhyāta rūpa śabda antarasya ‘nityaḥ paraḥ  nityaḥ  jīva iti pratyabhijñāyamāna punar śruti rūpa abhyāsasya dvāsuparṇa ityādi saṃkhyāyāḥ  aśabdam anaśnan  iti ādeḥ bhedakasya guṇa antarasya ‘yataḥ  vācaḥ  nivartanta iti ādi prakaraṇa antarasya jīveśau  iti nāmadheya dvayasya api sattvāt ca iti ced na pratyakṣa ādi sama kakṣyatayā śabda antara ādīnām bhedaka tve api tāttvika abheda avirodhi tvāt kiṃca adṛṣṭa caraḥ tvam mīmāṃsakaḥ yaḥ karma bhede śāstra bhede vā pramāṇa tvena klṛptānām śabda antara ādīnām cetana bhede pramāṇa tvam kalpayasi na hi anya bheda prayojakasya anya bheda prayojaka tā viśiṣṭa bhede prayojakasya api viśeṣaṇa bhedasya viśeṣya bhedakatva āpatteḥ ‘devadatta uttiṣṭhati śiṣyam bodhayati yajati dadāti juhotī atyādau  api bheda āpatteḥ na śabda antarasya kartṛ bhedaka tā iti advaita siddhau śabda antara ādeḥ ātma bhedakatva abhāvaḥ atha bheda śruteḥ ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅga bhaṅgaḥ nanu  ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅga upeta śruti gamya bhedasya katham atāt tvika tvam tathā hi ātharvaṇe dvāsuparṇā iti upakramaḥ paramam sāmyam upaiti iti upasaṃhāraḥ ‘tayoḥ anyaḥ anaśnan  anyaḥ anyam īśa am iti abhyāsaḥ śāstra eka gamya īśvara pratiyogikasya kāla traya ābādhya bhedasya śāstram vinā aprāpteḥ apūrva tā ‘puṇya pāpe vidhūye ati phalam ‘asya mahimānaḥ am iti stuti rūpaḥ artha vādaḥ atti anaścan  iti upapattiḥ atra ca ‘māyā mātram idam dvaita am iti ādau  iva dvi śabda eva bheda vācakaḥ tad ākṣepakaḥ  vā dvitva saṃkhyā eva aikya virodhinī iti vā bhavati upakramaḥ  bheda viṣayaḥ tad bhinnatva viśeṣitam eva ca tad gata bahu dharma yogi tvam tad sādṛśyam na tu viśeṣya mātram na ayam saḥ kiṃtu tad sadṛśaḥ na ayam tad sadṛśaḥ kiṃtu sa eva iti sādṛśya aikyayoḥ ekatara vidhānāya anyatara niṣedhāt ‘gaganam gagana ākāra am ityādi tu tad sadṛśa vastu antara niṣedha param gagana ādi eka deśasya tad eka deśa sādṛśya param vā iti upasaṃhāraḥ api bheda viṣaya eva abhyāsa tve api arthata eva eka prakāra tvam tantram na tu śabdataḥ atiprasaṅgāt  anyam īśam iti atra īśa gata anya tvam prati paśyati iti prakṛtaḥ  jīva eva pada nyāyena pratiyogitayā saṃbadhyata iti abhyāsaḥ api saṃbhavati iti ced  mā evam ātharvaṇe prathama muṇḍake ‘kasmin   u bhagavaḥ  vijñāte sarvam idam vijñātam bhavatī ati śaunaka praśna anantaram adve vidye veditavye iti vidyā dvayam avatārya ṛgveda ādi lakṣaṇām aparām uktvā ‘atha parā yayā tad akṣaram adhigamyate yad tad adreśyam agrāhyam agotram avarṇam i atyādinā para vidyā viṣayam akṣaram praśna anusāreṇa pratipādayatā abhedasya eva upakrānta tvāt anyathā tad uttaratva anupapatteḥ dvitīya muṇḍake apuruṣa eva idam viśvam brahma eva idam viśvam idam variṣṭha am iti madhye parāmarśāt  tṛtīya muṇḍaka ante ca ‘pare avyaye sarva ekībhavanti sa yaḥ  ha vai tad  paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavatī ati aikya lakṣaṇa phalena upasaṃhārāt ca muṇḍaka traya ātmikāyāḥ  upaniṣada aikya paratve sthite aasaṃyuktam prakaraṇa ādi ati nyāyena abhikramaṇa ādivat madhya sthita vākyasya api dvāsuparṇa ityādeḥ tad anukūla tve saṃbhavati mahāprakaraṇa virodhena viparīta tātparya kalpanayā bheda upakramatva abhāvāt aparamam sāmyam upaitī atyasya pūrva ukta nyāyena aikya para tayā bheda upasaṃhāratva abhāvāt atas  anaśnan  ityādinā na tāttvika bheda abhyāsaḥ na api īśasya śāstra gamya tayā tad pratiyogikaḥ tad dharmikaḥ  vā bhedaḥ apūrvaḥ īśa jñāna mātre tad apekṣāyām api pratyakṣeṇa tad sama kakṣyamānena ca tayoḥ prāpta tvāt  tvad ukta phala artha vādayoḥ aikya pakṣe api saṃbhavena na bheda asādhāraṇa liṅga tā anaśnan  iti ādeḥ kālpanika bhedena upapattyā tāttvika bheda upapattitva abhāvāt nanu antaryāmi brāhmaṇam ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅga upetam vākyam bhede pramāṇam tathā hi avettha nu tvam kāpya tam antaryāmiṇam i ati upakramaḥ ‘eṣa ta ātmā antaryāmī atyupasaṃhāraḥ  eṣa ta ātme atyādi ekāviṃśati kṛtvas abhyāsaḥ antaryāmi tvasya aprāpta tayā apūrva tā ‘sa vai brahma vidi atyādi phalam ‘tad ced tvam yājñavalkya sūtram avidvān  taṃca antaryāmiṇam brahma gavīrudajase mūrddhā te vipatiṣyatī ati nindā rūpaḥ artha vādaḥ ‘yasya pṛthivī śarīram yam pṛthivī na veda iti ādi upapattiḥ iti ced  mā evam ‘a ātmā iti eva upāsīte ati sūtrita brahma vidyā vivaraṇa rūpāyām catur adhyāyyāmanena hi etas sarvam veda iti eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna pratijñā pūrvakam ‘brahma vā idam agra āsīt tad ātmānam eva āveda aham brahma asmi iti tasmāt tad sarvam abhavadi ati abhedena upakramya ṣaṣṭha adhyāya ante maitreyī brāhmaṇe nigamana rūpe ‘yatra tu asya sarvam ātmā eva abhūt tad kena kam paśyedi atyādinā abhedena eva upasaṃhārāt  adhyāya catuṣṭayasya api abheda paratve sthite tad antargatasya brahma loka antara sūtra ātma pratipādana parasya uttara brāhmaṇa pratipādya nirupādhika sarva antara brahma pratipatti anukūlasya mahāprakaraṇa anurodhena tad virodhi bheda paratva abhāvāt tvad upanyasta liṅgānām bheda para tā nirṇāyaka tve api kalpita bheda para tayā tāttvika abheda avirodhi tvāt ata eva ‘na śārīraḥ ca ubhaye api hi bhedena enam adhīyata iti sūtra virodhaḥ na vā tad bhāṣya vyāhatiḥ iti advaita siddhau bheda śruteḥ ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅga bhaṅgaḥ atha aikya svarūpa upapattiḥ nanu aikyam ātma svarūpam uta anyat  na ādyaḥ ekatara pariśeṣa ādi āpatteḥ sa apekṣasya aikyasya nirapekṣā ātmatva ayogāt ca na antyaḥ satya tve advaita hāneḥ mithyātve tad tvam asi iti ādeḥ atattva avedaka tāpateḥ iti ced na ādyam eva anavadyam jñāna ānandayoḥ ātma aikye api yathā na ekatara pariśeṣa apatti ādikam kalpita ānandatva ādi dharmāt  tathā prakṛte api saṃbhavāt  aikye abhijñeya tvasya prāk ukteḥ tasya api nirapekṣa tayā nirapekṣā ātma svarūpatva avirodhāt ajñāna ādi adhiṣṭhāna tayā bhāsamāna ātma svarūpa tve api aikyasya tad gocara vṛtti viśeṣasya ajñāna nivartakasya idānīm asat tvāt saṃsāra upapatteḥ antye pakṣe doṣāḥ tu anukta upālambhā eva ata eva atiriktam aikyam na ekatva saṃkhyā na vā tad niṣṭhā aśeṣa dharmavat tvam na vā tad niṣṭhā sā dhāraṇa dharmavat tvam nirdharmake brahmaṇi teṣām abhāvāt  na api bheda virahaḥ bhedasya aikya viraha rūpa tvena anyonya āśrayāt na api tad vṛtti dharmān adhikaraṇa tvam śūnyasya api brahma aikya āpātāt iti nirastam tad avṛtti dharma anādhāratva upalakṣita svarūpasya abheda tvāt śūnyasya niḥsvarūpa tvāt  na śūnyasya aikya rūpa tā na ca tad avṛtti dharma niṣedhena tad vṛtti dharma vidhāna prasaṅgaḥ viśeṣa niṣedhasya śeṣa abhyanujñā phalaka tvāt iti vācyam śeṣa vidhāyaka tvasya sarvatra asaṃpratipatteḥ anyathā vāyau na nīla rūpam iti asya api gauram prati vidhāyakatva āpātāt  nanu abhede abhedatva pāramārthikatva asat vailakṣaṇya ādīni tattvataḥ santi vā navā ādye sa dvitīyatva āpattiḥ dvitīye abheda tvāt iha aniḥ iti ced na tattvataḥ svarūpa bhūtaiḥ eva taiḥ abheda rūpa tāyā advaitasya ca ahāni upapatteḥ na ca evam abhedasya ābādhita ātma svarūpa paryavasāne tasya ca ātma svarūpasya paraiḥ api saṃmata tvena tvad śāstra aviṣaya tvam iti vācyam jīvāvṛtti dharmān adhikaraṇatva upalakṣita ātma svarūpasya paraiḥ anaṅgīkārāt  tad evam ukte jīva brahma abhede ‘tattvam asi sa vā ayam ātmā brahma iti ādi śrutiḥ mānam iti advaita siddhau aikya svarūpa upapattiḥ atha jīva brahma abhede pramāṇam nanu sārvajñyāsā arvajñi ādi viśiṣṭayoḥ aikyam ayogyatva parāhatam katham udāhṛta śrutyā bodhyam iti   ced na saḥ ayam iti ādau  iva viruddha ākāra tyāgena śuddhayoḥ aikya bodhanāt  nanu viruddha ākāra tyāgaḥ kim avivakṣā mātreṇa uta anitya tvena uta mithyātvena na ādyaḥ viruddha ākārasya avivakṣāyām api anapāyāt  na hi ‘asat vā idam agra āsīt sarvam khalu idam brahme atyādi śrutyā sattva śūnya tvayoḥ cittva jaḍa tvayoḥ veha avivakṣā mātreṇa brahmaṇaḥ śūnyena jaḍena ca aikyam su vacam na dvitīyaḥ tattvam bhaviṣyasi iti nirdeśa āpattyā asi iti vartamāna nirdeśa ayogāt  daśa abhedena bheda abhedayoḥ sattva āpattyā tvayā api anaṅgīkārāt ca jīveśayoḥ svātantrya pāratantrī ādeḥ nitya tvāt ca na tṛtīyaḥ nirdoṣa śruti sākṣi siddhayoḥ viruddha dharmayoḥ mithyātva ayogāt iti ced na viruddha ākārasya avivakṣayā eva tyāgāt  tyāgaḥ ca brahma anubhava aviṣaya tvam na tu apāyaḥ tasya carama sākṣātkāra sādhya tvāt tathā ca tad tedaṃte iva anapete api sārvajñyāsā arvajñye na āśraya abheda virodhāya avivakṣā ca pradhāna prameya nirvāhāya na ca saḥ ayam iti atra tad tedantayoḥ na tyāgaḥ krameṇa ekatra tayoḥ avaśyaka tvāt ‘asadve atyādau ‘sarvam khalu idam brahme atyādau ca na śūnya jaḍā aikya āpattiḥ śūnya satoḥ cit jaḍayoḥ vā viruddha ākāra parityāgena jīva brahmaṇoḥ iva anusyūtasya ākārasya abhāvāt  asataḥ  niḥsvarūpa tvāt jaḍasya bādhya sva rūpa tvāt iti advaita siddhau jīva brahma abhede pramāṇam atha aikya śruteḥ upajīvya virodha abhāvaḥ nanu aikya śrutyā pratyakṣa siddham jīvam anūdya brahma tvam vā bodhanīyam śruti siddham brahma anūdya tasya jīva tvam vā ubhaya anuvādena abhedaḥ  vā vidheyaḥ sarvathā api upajīvya virodhāt na aikye prāmāṇyam pratyakṣeṇa jīvasya brahma bhinna tvena śrutyā ca sarvajñatva ādimad brahma grāhiṇyā tad hīna tvena anubhūyamāna ājīvāt bhinna tvena brahmaṇaḥ  jñāyamāna tvāt  na ca anumānena brahma upasthitiḥ tena api sarvajñatva ādinā brahmaṇaḥ  viṣayīkaraṇena upajīvya virodha tādavasthyāt iti ced na śakti graha ādau tayoḥ upajīvya tve api svaprameye anupajīvya tvāt tad uktam vācaspatye ayat  upajīvyam tad na bādhyate yad bādhyate tad na upajīvyam i ati yathā kathaṃcid apekṣā mātreṇa upajīvya tve na idam rajatam iti atra api idam rajatam iti asya upajīvyata āpatteḥ nanu yad hi yad apekṣam yasya bādhe svasya bādhāpattiḥ ca tad tasya upajīvyam prakṛte ca dharmyādi grāhakasya eva sva prāmāṇi agrāhaka tayā tad bādhe sva bādhāpattiḥ niṣedhya arpaṇa sthale tu na tathā na hi brahma svarūpa dharmi jñānā prāmāṇye aikya jñāna aprāmāṇyavat  pratiṣedhya jñāna aprāmāṇye pratiṣedhya jñāna aprāmāṇyam pratiṣedhya śāstra vilopa prasaṅgāt iti ced  satyam sārvajñi ādi viśiṣṭam na tāvat dharmi kiṃtu brahma svarūpa mātram viśiṣṭa dharmi jñāna prāmāṇyam aikya jñāna prāmāṇye na apekṣyate kiṃtu svarūpa jñāna prāmāṇya mātram anyathā aidam rajatami atyasya api dharmi jñāna tvena upajīvyatayā niṣedha jñāna prāmāṇye rajatatva viśiṣṭedaṃjñāna prāmāṇyam syāt  rajatatva vaiśiṣṭyasya dharmitvā prayojaka tvavat sārvajñi ādi vaiśiṣṭyasya api tad aprayojaka tvasya prakṛte api samāna tvāt  nanu evam asādhāraṇa sārvajñi ādi dharma avacchedena brahmaṇaḥ anuddeśya tve sādhāraṇa dharmeṇa sva rūpeṇa vā uddeśyatā vācyā tatra ādye iṣṭāpattiḥ cittvā ādi sādhāraṇa dharma aikyasya asmābhiḥ api aṅgīkārāt  dvitīye brahma aikya asiddhiḥ sādhāraṇa svarūpa mātra uddeśāt iti ced na brahma aikya asiddhiḥ iti atra brahma śabdena sārvajñi ādi viśiṣṭam ced abhimatam tadā iṣṭāpattiḥ tadā tvam ā ca lakṣitayoḥ eva padārthayoḥ aikya bodhasya prāk  pratipādita tvāt  ata eva śabdena asādhāraṇa brahma svarūpa uddeśasya asādhāraṇa dharmeṇa vinā asiddheḥ upajīvya virodha tā dā  asthyam iti nirastam asādhāraṇa dharmasya uddeśya samarpaṇe upalakṣaka tvāt  na ca u palakṣya tāvacchedaka abhāve upalakṣyatva asiddhiḥ cittvasya tattve siddha sādhanāt iti vācyam svarūpa upalakṣaṇe upalakṣya tāvat chedakasya anapekṣaṇāt yad tu cit tvena aikye siddha sādhanam tad na cittvā aikyasya iṣṭa tve api tad āśraya ekyasya tava aniṣṭa tvāt iṣṭau ca avivādāt  ata eva ‘puroḍāśa kapālena tuṣān upavapatī atyatra adhiṣṭhāna lakṣaṇāyām anyatas  prāpta tuṣa upavāpa vidhāna rūpa iṣṭa siddhivat atra na lakṣaṇayā abhīṣṭa siddhiḥ yena lakṣaṇā syāt iti nirastam cittvā aikyasya prāpta tve api āśraya ekyasya aprāptasya lakṣaṇa aprāpaṇīyasya sattvāt  saḥ ayam iti atra api ukta prakārasya avaśya vācya tvāt na ca tattā viśiṣṭasya tatra uddeśya tā yadvat tayā jñāta sa eva yad anvayadhīḥ tattvasya viśeṣaṇa tvasya tad tādau saṃbhavāt iti vācyam datta uttara tvāt  nanu evam paramāṇuḥ sa avayavaḥ īśvaraḥ  na sarvajñaḥ aādityaḥ  yūpa iti ādau  upajīvya virodhaḥ  na syāt  utpanna śiṣṭa guṇa vidhau sa guṇa utpatti vākya virodhaḥ ca na syāt  tatra api parama aṇutva ādi viśiṣṭam na dharmī kiṃtu sva rūpa mātram iti su vaca tvāt iti ced na paramāṇu ādeḥ sva rūpeṇa api sāvayavatva ādikam prati dharmi tve parama aṇutva ādikam dharmi samāna sattākam paramāṇu ādau na syāt  tadīya asam asattāka tvasya tad sāvayavatva bodhaka prābalyā adhīna tvāt tad prābalye anumāna abhāvāt pratyuta bhrānta vākya tvena durbala tvāt  ādityaḥ  yupa iti atra abhedaḥ  na prameyaḥ stuti dvārāni aśeṣa tvāt stuteḥ ca pratyakṣa aviruddhaiḥ guṇaiḥ api saṃbhave pratyakṣa viruddha artha kalpanā yogāt utpanna śiṣṭa guṇa vidhau tu utpatti vākya sthita āmikṣā ādi padasya dravya sāmānya paratve tad pada vaiyarthya āpattiḥ ‘tad hita artha asya iti sarva nāmnā yajati codanā dravya devatā kriyam i ati nyāyena yāga codana mātreṇa ca dravya sāmānya lābhāt prakṛte ananya śeṣa tayā prabala tvāt  pramāṇa vākya tvāt ca tad virodha aikya pratipādaka tayā svarūpa lakṣaṇāyāḥ  yuktatama tvāt ca nanu rūpya rūpa niṣedhya arpakasya apekṣitasya api parīkṣitatva abhāvāt yadi api durbala tvam upajīvyatva mātrasya prābalyā prayojaka tvāt  tathā api iha niṣedhya arpaka bheda śrutiḥ sākṣi pratyakṣam ca nirdoṣa tvāt  parīkṣitam api prabalam tad virodhāt  katham aikya paratvam iti ced na nirdoṣāyāḥ  api śruteḥ bheda paratvasya eva abhāvena tad virodhasya aikya śrutau  asaṃbhāvita tvāt na hi śruteḥ upakrama ādi ṣaḍvidha tātparya liṅga śūnya artha paratvam tad niyāmaka abhāvāt anyathā ati prasaṅgāt  sākṣiṇaḥ api nirdoṣatva mātreṇa parīkṣitatva abhāvāt duḥkha abhāva ādau  āropita sukha ādeḥ api prāmāṇikatva āpatteḥ mad mate prātibhāsika mātrasya sākṣi siddhasya mithyātvāt  sākṣiṇaḥ api nirdoṣa ja vṛtti uparakta tvena abādhyatva asiddheḥ ukta tvāt ca pramāṇa tad abhāva vyavasthā api prātibhāsika vya avahārikayoḥ karaṇa saṃsargi doṣa prayuktatva aprayukta tvābhyām vyāvahārikasya caitanya mātra stha ajñāna doṣa prayukta tvāt tasmāt upajīvyavirodha abhāvāt pratyuta abheda śruteḥ eva sarva śeṣitayā bheda śrutim pratyupajīvya tvāt  bheda śruteḥ eva tad virodhena tad anukūla tayā neyatvāt  sarva virodha śūnyam tad tvam asya ādi vākyam tathā ca aikya param iti siddham iti aikyaśruteḥ upajīvya virodha abhāvaḥ atha tattvam asya ādi vākya artha nirūpaṇam nanu evam pada dvaye api lakṣaṇā syāt  tathā ca mad matam āśritya eka pada lakṣaṇa eva āśrayaṇīyā tathā hi   advā suparṇā sa yuje atyādau jīvasya brahma sāha caryā ukteḥ tad sāhacaryāt tad iti vyapadeśaḥ ‘vasanta ādibhyaṣṭha gi atyatra vasanta sahacarite adhyayane vasanta pada prayogasya mahābhāṣye ukta tvāt  ‘sat mūlāḥ prajāḥ sat āyatanā ityādi vākya śeṣāt  prasiddha tad āśrita tvāt vā tad iti vyapadeśaḥ ‘samarthaḥ pada vidhiḥ i ati sūtre samartha pada āśrita tvena pada vidhau samartha pada prayogasya mahābhāṣya ukteḥ ‘sat mūlāḥ somya imāḥ prajāḥ sarvā iti vākya śeṣāt  prasiddha tajja tvāt vā tad pada prayogaḥ ‘brāhmaṇaḥ asya mukham āsīdi atyādivat  ‘igyaṇaḥ saṃprasāraṇam i atyatra saṃprasāraṇāt jātaḥ  varṇaḥ saṃprasāraṇam iti bhāṣya ukteḥ ‘prāṇa bandhanam hi sosya mana iti vākya śeṣeṇa jīvasya īśa adhīnatva uktyā tad adhīna tvāt vā tad śabda prayogaḥ ‘dhānyam asi dhinuhi iti atra mantre taṇḍule dhānya pada prayogavat  atat sādṛśyāt vā tad pada prayogaḥ sārūpya ādi ati jaimini sūtre aādityaḥ  yūpa iti ādikam sādṛśyāt iti ukta tvāt  ‘tad guṇa sāra tvāt tu tad vyapadeśaḥ prājña vadi atyatra brahmasūtre brahma guṇa yogāt jīve tad vyapadeśa iti ukteḥ mahābhāṣye ca bahu gaṇa ityādi sūtre vatim vinā eva saṅkhyāvat iti vati arthaḥ  gamyate abrahma dattam brahma dattā iti āha tena vayam manyāmahe brahma dattavat ayam bhavati iti ukteḥ ca iti ced na abhede tātparye avadhṛte tad nirvāhaka lakṣaṇa ābāhulyasya adoṣa tvāt na hi lakṣaṇa aikya anurodhena tātparya parityāgaḥ tad uktam nyāya cintāmaṇau ‘tāt paryāt tu vṛttiḥ na tu vṛtteḥ tātparyaḥ am iti jahat ajahat lakṣaṇayā mukhya paratve saṃbhavati tad sahacarita ādi artha paratva kalpanasya anucita tvāt ca yathā abheda paratve na bodhakatva anupapattiḥ tathā uktam prāk  ‘dvā suparṇā sa yujā ityādinā na jīvasya brahmaṇā sahacaritatva uktiḥ kiṃtu antaḥkaraṇe na iti na tena sahacaritatva prasiddhiḥ api na vā sat mūlāḥ prajā ityādinā jīvasya tad āśritatva prasiddhiḥ prajā śabdasya prajāyamāna vācaka tvena jīvasya nityasya apratipādanāt  ata eva na tad janya tvena api tad śabda prayogaḥ ‘brāhmaṇaḥ  mukham i ati eva mukhāt jātatva hetutaḥ yathāvat ucyate tadvat jīvaḥ  brahma iti vāc bhavet  iti smṛtiḥ api asmṛtiḥ eva śruti virodhāt  yad tu tad guṇa sāra tvāt ityādinā jīve brahma guṇa yoga ukta iti uktam tad na buddhi guṇa sūkṣmatva yogāt jīve brahmaṇi iva sūkṣma tvam iti evaṃpara tvāt sūtrasya etena śākhā sa deśe candre śākhā itivat  jīva antaryāmitayā jīvasa deśe brahmaṇi tvam iti prayogaḥ ātmani tiṣṭhan  iti śruteḥ brāhmaṇaḥ  vai sarvā devatā ityādivat  jīva āśraya tvāt vā brahmaṇaḥ sarva kartṛ tvena yajamānaḥ prastara ityādivat  tad siddhyā vā brahmaṇi tvam iti vyapadeśa iti nirastam nanu jahat ajahat lakṣaṇāyām vācya antargata tvena prāk dhīsthasya bādhakāt  tyaktasya punar  svīkāraḥ jahat lakṣaṇāyām adhī sthasya atyaktasya eva svīkāraḥ tyakta svīkārāt varam adhīsthasya svīkāra iti ced na anupapattyā viśeṣaṇa tyāge api viśeṣya aṃśa atyāgāt  etena tad śabdāt  para tṛtīya ādi vibhakteḥ supām suluj iti ādinā prathama eka vacana ādeśaḥ  vā lugvā tathā ca tena tvam tiṣṭhasi iti vā tatas  sañjāta iti vā tasya tvam iti vā tasmin tvam iti vā arthaḥ ‘anena jīvena ātmanā anuprabhūtaḥ pepīyamānaḥ  modamānaḥ tiṣṭhati sat mūlāḥ somya imāḥ sarvāḥ prajā aitat ātmyam idam sarvam i atyādi vākya śeṣāt  tathā ca mīmāṃsakā ‘uta yad sunvanti sāmidhenīḥ tad anvāhuḥ i ati atra yad tad śabdayoḥ saptamī arthe prathamām svīkṛtya yatra sunvanti tatra havirdhāne sthitvā sāmidhenīḥ anubrūyāt iti vyākhyāñcakruḥ nyāyyam ca niravakāśa pradhāna bhūta aneka prātipadika svārasya āya saṅkhyā artha tvena sa avakāśā pradhāna eka vibhakti asvārasyam iti nirastam prodgātṝṇām iti atra vibhakti svārasya aya prātipadikasya anyathā ānayanavat atra api prātipadikasya eva anyathā nayanāt ca na ca ṣaṣṭhī bahuvacanasya prathama eka vacanavat anyatra avidhānena tasya anyathā ānayanam asaṃbhavi iti bahuvacana anusāraṇe prātipadikasya prastotra ādi chandaḥ geṣu lakṣaṇā aaśritā iti vācyam ‘saktūn juhotī atyatra iva anyatra nayanasya saṃbhāvita tvāt  kiṃca na tāvat  prātipadikasya niravakāśa tvam vibhakteḥ saṅkhyāyām iva viśeṣya aṃśe sa avakāśa tvāt  na api prādhānyam pradhāna artha vācaka pratyayasya eva prādhānyāt  tad uktam    prakṛti pratyayau   saha artham brūtaḥ tayoḥ pratyayaḥ prādhānyene ati na api prātipadikā aneka tvam svārasye tantram ‘gabhīrāyām nadyāam iti ādau anekatve api asvārasya darśanāt tātparyabalāt tatra tathā iti ced  samam prakṛte api yad tu ‘prayāja śeṣeṇa havīṃṣi abhidhāraya atītyatra prayāja śeṣam haviṣī upakṣipati iti tṛtīyā vibhakti asvārasyam asaktūn juhotī atyādau  api dvitīyā vibhakti asvārasyam tad agatyā ‘prayāja śeṣeṇe atyādau upayukta saṃskāra vyatirekeṇa prakāra antarasya asaṃbhavāt saktūn ityādau bhūta bhāvi upayoga abhāvena saṃskāryatva abhāvāt etena tasya tvam tattvam iti samastam padam iti  nirastam asamāsena eva ṣaṣṭhī artha lakṣaṇa ādi rahitena upapattau ṣaṣṭhī samāsasya anyāyya tvāt  anyathā sthapati adhikaraṇa virodha āpatteḥ nanu ‘a etad ātmyam idam sarvam tad satyam sa ātmā tad tvam asī atyatra tad padena na ātmā parāmṛśyate kiṃtu aitat ātmyam napuṃsaka tvāt  aitat ātmyam iti asya eṣa ca asau  ātmā ca etad ātmā tasya idam aitat ātmyam evam ca etadīyam vastu tvam asi iti arthaḥ na tu abhedaḥ etad ātmā yasya tadā etad ātmyam iti arthe bhāva pratyaya vaiyarthya āpatteḥ tatas  varam artha antara āśrayaṇam vicitrā hi tad hita gatiḥ iti vacanāt  ‘sa sraṣṭā ca eva saṃhartā niyantā rakṣitā hariḥ tena vyāptam idam sarvam aitat ātmyam atas  viduḥ iti smṛteḥ ca iti ced na tasya idam iti arthe ṣyañaḥ avidhānāt  prayoga adarśanāt ca sva arthe ca saukhyam iti ādi prayoga darśanāt tathā ca etad  sat  ātmā yasya sarvasya tad etad ātmā tasya bhāva aitat ātmyam sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca svārthika tvāt vā bhāva bhavitra urabheda upacārāt vā ‘yaḥ  vai bhūmā tad sukham i ativat  yad tu smṛtau  etad vyāpaka tvena aitat ātmya uktiḥ sā na yuktā eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna pratijñā virodhāt nanu śarīra vācinām deva manuṣya śabdānām śarīri paryantatva darśanāt  brahma śarīra bhūta jīva vāci tvaṃpadasya brahma paryanta tvena tattvam iti vyapadeśaḥ śarīra śarīri bhāva nibandhanaḥ ayasya ātmā śarīra am iti ādi śruteḥ iti mukhyam eva asmad mate pada dvayam iti ced na śarīri paryanta tvam iti tad lakṣaka tvam vā tatra api śakta tvam vā śarīra viṣaya vṛttyā eva tad pratipādaka tvam vā na ādyaḥ mukhyatva anupapādanāt  na dvitīyaḥ śarīra vācinām iti asādhāraṇyena nirdeśa anupapatteḥ pravṛtti nimitta manuṣyatva ādi jāteḥ śarīriṇya vṛtteḥ ukta tvāt ca na tṛtīyaḥ anya viṣaya vṛtteḥ anya anupayogena śarīra śarīriṇoḥ anādi bhrama siddha abheda nibandhanaḥ ayam prayogaḥ  vācyaḥ tathā ca atra api abheda nibandhana eva ayam prayogaḥ abhedaḥ tu bādhaka abhāvāt atra tāttvika iti eva viśeṣaḥ yad tu ‘a ādityaḥ  brahma iti avat  jīve brahmatva upāsana arthaḥ tattvam asi iti nirdeśa iti tad na anupāsana aprakaraṇa stha tvena dṛṣṭānta vaiṣamyāt  ukta rītyā vastu niṣṭhatve saṃbhavati tad tyāga ayogāt ca nanu sa ātmā tattvam asīti atra atattvam asi iti pada  chedaḥ aśabdaḥ anitya iti atra anitya iti pada  chedaḥ  yathā ghaṭa dṛṣṭānta anusāreṇa tathā atra api śakuni sūtra ādi dṛṣṭānta anusārāt na hi prathama khaṇḍe śakuni sūtrayoḥ sa yathā śakuniḥ sūtreṇa prabaddha iti uktayoḥ śakuni sūtrayoḥ ṣaṣṭhe lavaṇam etad ukam ityādinā uktayoḥ lavaṇa udakayoḥ saptame ‘puruṣam somya gandhārebhya ityādinā uktayoḥ puruṣa gandhāra deśayoḥ navame ca ‘apahā ārṣīt  steyam akārṣī adityādinā uktayoḥ stena apahāryayoḥ aikyam stena apahārya dṛṣṭānte hi spaṣṭam aikya jñāninaḥ anarthaḥ parakīya brahmatva abhimānī hi stenaḥ na tu vidyamāna brahmatva ajñāni iti ced na śakuni sūtra ādau dṛṣṭānte vidyamānaḥ api bhedaḥ  na ātat iti pada  cheda prayojakaḥ tam vinā eva tad upapatteḥ ghaṭa dṛṣṭāntaḥ tu na nityatva upapadyata iti vaiṣamyāt  tathā hi jvara ādi roga grastasya tad nirmoke svāsthye viśrāntivat ja agrat svapnayoḥ karaṇa vyāpāra janita śrama apanuttaye jīvasya devatā ātma svarūpa avasthānam iti asmin  arthe śakuni sūtra dṛṣṭānta iti anyathā eva upapatteḥ ‘svam apītaḥ  bhavatī ati śruteḥ nanu brahmaṇi sva śabdaḥ  na jīvā bheda abhiprāyaḥ kiṃtu ātmīyatva ādi arthaḥ svātantrya abhiprāyaḥ  vā ‘svātantryāt sva iti prokta iti āgamāt  ‘apītaḥ  bhavatī atyasya api tirohitaḥ san prāptaḥ  bhavati iti eva arthaḥ na tu abhinna iti apeḥ pidhāne iṇaḥ  dhātoḥ ca gatau niṣṭhāyāḥ kartari śakteḥ klṛpta tvāt  aikye yoga rūḍhyoḥ abhāvāt ca iti ced  na sva śabdasya svarūpe mukhyasya artha antara paratve gauṇī lakṣaṇayoḥ anyatara āpatteḥ abhede yoga rūḍhyoḥ abhāve api upasarga prakṛti pratyaya paryālocanayā labdha svarūpa prāpti rūpa arthasya abhede paryavasānāt  ata eva aikya artha tve apīta iti asya bhavateḥ ca akarmaka tayā śruta dvitīyā yogaḥ aśruta tṛtīyā kalpanam iti nirastam ata eva ayathā asmin  ākāśe śyenaḥ  vā suparṇaḥ  vā viparipatya śrāntaḥ saṃhatya pakṣau saṃlayāya eva dhrīyate evam eva ayam puruṣa iti suṣupti samaye śruti antare bhinna śyena nīḍa dṛṣṭāntoktiḥ iti ca nirastam sarva sāmyasya dṛṣṭānta tāyāma tantra tvāt na ca prājñena ātmanā saṃpariṣvaktaḥ sa iti suṣupti viṣaye bheda śrutyā tvad mate api bheda pareṇa suṣupī utkrāntyaḥ bhaidena iti sūtreṇa tvad pakṣe api jāgaraṇa iva suṣuptau  api āvidyaka jīva brahma bheda svīkāreṇa ca virodha iti vācyam yatas  jāgrat svapnayoḥ iva sphuṭatara vikṣepaḥ  na asti iti abhiprāyeṇa sva svarūpa prāpti uktiḥ na tu ātyantikā bheda abhiprāyeṇa anyathā suṣupti muktyoḥ aviśeṣa āpatteḥ yadi sajjagataḥ  mūlam tadā katham na upalabhyata iti āśaṅkāyām vidyamānam api vastu na upalabhyate anyathā tu upalabhyata iti amum artham spaṣṭīkartum lavaṇa udaka dṛṣṭānta iti tatra api anyathā upapatteḥ yadi evam lavaṇam iva indriyaiḥ
