anupalabhyamānam api jagat mūlam sat  upāya antareṇa upalabdhum śakyata iti tasya eva upalambhe ka upāya iti āśaṅkāyām ‘ācāryavān puruṣaḥ  vede ati upāyam vaktum gāndhāra puruṣa dṛṣṭānta iti tatra api anyathā eva upapatteḥ tathā ca ācāryavān vidvān yena krameṇa satā saṃbadhyate sa ka iti āśaṅkāyām satya abhisandhasya artha prāptiḥ anṛta abhisandhasya anartha prāptiḥ iti vaktum stenāḥ tena dṛṣṭānta iti tatra api anyathā eva upapatteḥ na ca satya anṛta dṛṣṭāntena pure apahārṣīt  ‘steyam akārṣīdi ati udāharaṇa ayogaḥ tad upapādaka tvena pṛthak  dṛṣṭāntatva bhāvāt nanu dvitīya khaṇḍe ‘nānā atyayānām vṛkṣāṇām rasāni atyādinā uktānām nānā vṛkṣa rasānām tṛtīye ‘imāḥ somya nadya ityādinā uktayoḥ nadī samudrayoḥ ca aikyam vaktum na hi śakyam na hi nānā vṛkṣa rasā anyonya bheda tyāgena prāk  siddhena madhunā aikyam āpadyante navā prāk  bheda bhrānti viṣayāḥ paścāt tad aviṣayāḥ kiṃtu tantava iva paṭam anyonya bhinnā eva prāc asiddham madhūtpādayanti na ca idam dārṣṭa antika anuguṇam nadī samudrat daṣṭānte api kim nadī samudra avayavinoḥ aikyam kiṃvā tad avayava jala aṇūnām uta dravya antara ārambhaḥ nādya dvitīyau māṣa rāśau prakṣiptam āṣatat avayavānām iva kṣīre prakṣipta nīra tadava yavānām iva ca anyonya miśrī bhāve api prāk bhinnānām paścāt api aikya ayogāt tṛtīye tu bheda eva evam dārṣṭa antikān anuguṇyam ceti ced na sphuṭa avacchedaka viraheṇa spaṣṭa bheda abhāva abhiprāyeṇa dṛṣṭāntānām upātta tvena dṛṣṭānte vāstava bheda abhedayoḥ audāsīnyena tvad ukta dūṣaṇa gaṇānām agaṇanīya tvāt ata eva sataḥ abhedasya ajñāna mātre dṛṣṭānta iti nirastam bheda sattāyām audāsīnyāt na ca evam asphuṭa bheda viṣaya tvasya ātyantikā bhede anupayogaḥ sūkṣma upādhi avacchinnasya mahā upādhi avacchinna aikyavat tad avacchinnasya api tad vilaye anavacchinna aikyam iti saṃbhāvanā buddhi janana dvāra upayogitva saṃbhavāt ataeva ‘tāḥ samudrāt  samudram eva apiyanti sa samudra eva bhavatī atyatra prakṛta nadīḥ udh diśya samudabhavana vidhāne suvarṇam kuṇḍalam bhavati itivat  tāḥ samudra eva bhavanti iti vyapadeśaḥ syāt  atas  nadyaḥ  niyata jala rāśi rūpāt  samudrāt  gacchanti tam praviśanti ca samudraḥ tu sa eva na etāsām samudra tvam iti vā samudra eva na tu nadī tvam prāpnoti iti vā arthaḥ sataḥ api anyonyam bhedasya ajñāna eva imau dṛṣṭāntau ataeva nānā rasa vākye dārṣṭa antike ‘evam eva khalu somya imāḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ sati saṃpadya na viduḥ sati saṃpatsyāmaha iti ta iha vyāghraḥ  ve ati nadī samudra vākye ca dāntike ‘sata āgamya na viduḥ sata āgacchām aha iti ‘ta iha vyāghraḥ  ve ati sataḥ  bhedasya ajñānena eva anartha ukta iti nirastam spaṣṭa bheda viṣaya tā abhāva abhiprāyeṇa dṛṣṭānta tvāt  yad ca bheda ajñāna nivandhana vyāghra ādi rūpa anartha parā śrutiḥ iti tad na sati saṃpadya iti asya āsanna tvāt  ‘na viduḥ i atyanena sat sampatti ajñānam ucyate na tu bheda ajñānam tathā ca sat saṃpatteḥ jñāna pūrvakatva abhāvāt tad tad vāsanayā tad tad vyāghra ādi bhāva eva bhavati iti etad paratvāt tasmāt dṛṣṭānta varyāṇām bhede tātparya hānitaḥ eteṣām anusāreṇa chedaḥ  na ātat iti sphuṭam nanu ādya khaṇḍe svapna antam me somya vijānīhi iti svātantrya śaṅkā anāspada suṣupti nidarśanena caturthe ca asya yad ekām śākhām jīvaḥ  jahāti ityādinā anvaya vyatireka uktyā aṣṭame ca puruṣam somya uta upatāpinam ityādinā svātantrya śaṅkā anāspada maraṇa nidarśanena īśvara adhīna tvasya ukta tvāt atat iti eva chedaḥ  yukta iti   ced na svapna antam iti ādeḥ suṣupti avasthāyām eva jīvatva vinirmuktam svam devatā rūpam darśayiṣyāmi iti anena abhiprāyeṇa uddālakena avatārita tvena īśvara adhīnatva paratva abhāvāt jalāt utthitānām vīcī taraṅga phena budbudānām punar tad bhāvam gatānām vināśaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ jīvānām pratyaham svarūpa tām gacchatām maraṇa pralayayoḥ ca nāśābhāvaḥ katham iti āśaṅkāyām tad parihāra tvena uktasya vṛkṣa śākhā nidarśanasya jīva adhiṣṭhitam śarīram jīvati tad apetam ca mriyate na tu jīvaḥ  mriyata iti etad paratvāt ‘jīva apetam vāva kila idam mriyate na jīvaḥ  mriyata iti vākya śeṣāt  yathā somya upatāpinam iti asya api ācāryavān vidvān kena krameṇa sat  saṃpadyata iti āśaṅkāyām tad krama pradarśana paratvena īśvara adhīna tve tātparya abhāvāt yad tu caturthe ‘jīvena ātmanā anuprabhūtaḥ pepīyamānaḥ  modamānaḥ tiṣṭhatī atyatra jīva śabda īśvara paraḥ modamāna iti saṃsāriṇaḥ pṛthak uktiḥ iti tad na modamāna iti asya dṛṣṭānta tvena prakrānta vṛkṣa viśeṣaṇa tvena saṃsāri paratva abhāvena jīva iti atra śruta artha tyāga ayogāt  yad ca pañcame etasya eva somya eṣaḥ aṇimna evam mahānyagrodhaḥ tiṣṭhati iti atra aṇima śabdaḥ sūkṣmeśvara paraḥ sa eṣaḥ aṇimā aitat ātmyam idam sarvam iti iha eva śrutau  īśvare tasya prayogāt  na tu dhānā paraḥ tāsām kim atra paśyasi iti aṇvya iva imā dhānā iti bhāva pratyaya rahitena strī liṅgena bahuvacana antena iva śabda śiraskena aṇu śabdena nirdiṣṭa tayā tad viparītāṇima śabdān arha tvāt ca iti ced na eṣaḥ aṇuḥ ātmā iti atra bhāva pratyaya rahita prayoga viṣaye api īśvare eṣaḥ aṇimā iti prayoga darśanena dhānāsu tathā vaktum śakya tvāt  na ca tarhi na nibhālaya sa iti ukta adṛśyatva ayogaḥ anubhūtāyām dhānāyām eva mahān nyagrodhaḥ tiṣṭhati sa tvayā anabhivyakta tvāt na jñāyata iti evaṃpara tvāt nanu yadi aṣṭame viduṣaḥ  brahma prāpti mātram vivakṣitam tadā tasya vāc manasi saṃpadyata ityādi tejaḥ parasyām devatāyām iti antam eva vākyam syāt  yāvat vā vāc manasi saṃpadyata ityādi vyartham syāt iti ced na laukika maraṇe yaḥ sat saṃpatti kramaḥ sa eva viduṣaḥ api viśeṣaḥ tu jñāna ajñāna kṛta iti amum artham pratipādayitum dṛṣṭānte anvaya vyatirekābhyām sat saṃpatti krama iti vaiyarthya abhāvāt na ca atat  satyam sa ātmā iti atra ātma śabdena aṇima śabda ukta īśvara eva gṛhyate na tu jīvaḥ  yad āpnoti yad ādatte yad ca atti viṣayān iha yad ca asya santatas  bhāvaḥ tasmāt ātmā iti gīyate iti vacanāt iti vācyam katama ātmā ityādau ātma śabdasya jīve prasiddha tvāt  vacana ukta viṣayāt tṛ tvasya jīva eva ca saṃbhavāt  tad parigrahasya eva ucita tvāt yad ca ‘tam eva ekam jānatha ātmānaḥ am iti vākya uktaḥ  na jīvaḥ tad vāci śabda abhāvāt iti siddhāntitam tad ātma śabdasya na jīve amukhyatva abhiprāyeṇa kiṃtu pradhāna ādau jīvasya tu ātma tve api paricchinna tayā jagatkartṛtva asaṃbhavāt vyudāsa iti evaṃparam jīvena ātmanā iti sāmānādhikaraṇya anupapatteḥ ca na ca jīva śabdena īśvara eva uktaḥ rūḍhi parityāge kāraṇa abhāvāt rūḍheḥ ca klṛpta tvāt  aham hi jīva saṃjña iti ādeḥ ca abheda pakṣe api saṃbhavāt  na ca prāṇa dhāraka tvam īśa mātra vṛtti jīva sādhāraṇa tvāt na ca trivṛt karaṇa pūrvaka nāma rūpa vyākaraṇasya jīve asaṃbhavaḥ asmad ādau  asaṃbhave api atrivṛt kṛta bhūta ārabdha liṅga śarīra abhimāninaḥ  hiraṇyagarbhasya nāma rūpa ātmaka prapañca vyākaraṇa saṃbhavāt na ca tarhi punar jīva praveśa ukti ayogaḥ atat teja aikṣata tā āpa aikṣanta imāḥ tisraḥ  devatā iti pūrvam eva cetanatva siddheḥ iti vācyam avyākṛta bhūta sṛṣṭau sākṣāt kāraṇatvavat brahmāṇḍa ādi sṛṣṭau na sākṣātkāraṇa tā kiṃtu sva abhinna jīva dvāreṇa iti evaṃpara tvāt kiṃca ‘ekam eva advitīyam iti upakramāt na śyena ādi dṛṣṭānta anusārāt atat iti pada  chedaḥ  yuktaḥ eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna pratijñāna virodhāt brahma jīva aikyasya aprasakta tvena niṣedha anupapatteḥ ca na ca ‘iṣṭāpūrtam manyamānā variṣṭha am iti ādau  iva śruti tātparya aparijñānena ‘tadha eka āhuḥ asat eva idam agra āsī adityādau  ivāna ādi kusamayena vā deha indriya ādīn prati svātantrya rūpasya aiśvaryasya sarvaiḥ api sva ātmani abhimanyamāna tvena pratyakṣeṇa vā prasaktiḥ ekyasya iti vācyam aikyatātparyasya pramita tvena su samaya tvasya vyavasthāpita tvena ca tātparyā parijñāna kusamaya prāpta tvasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  aikya liṅgasya api abhimānikatva abhāvena tena ced  prasaktiḥ tadā niṣeddhum aśakyatā eva deha indriya ādīnām jīvasya aikyena adhyasta tvāt  tān prati svātantrya abhimānasya sārvalaukikasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  yad kiñcid prati svātantryasya īśvara lakṣaṇatva abhāvāt ca etena ekam eva advitīyam iti samāthi adhikarāhityasya upakramāt aitat ātmyam iti tasya eva upasaṃhārāt  atattvam asi iti nava kṛtvas abhyāsāt śāstram vinā śāstra eka gagyasya īśvara bhedasya aprasakta tayā apūrva tvāt atha sampatsyata iti phala śravaṇāt  yena aśrutam bhavati iti artha vādāt  śakuni sūtra ādi dṛṣṭāntaiḥ upapādanāt ṣaḍvidhatātparya liṅgāni bheda parāṇi eva iti nirastam ekam eva iti atra sama abhyadhikara ahitya mātreṇa bheda upakramatva abhāvāt abhede api tad saṃbhavāt eka vijñānena sarva vijñāna pratijñāna virodhāt dvitīya abhāva mātrasya eva upakramāt ata eva abhyāsa upasaṃhārau  api bheda viṣayau na bhavataḥ abhede tu yathā apūrva tā tathā uktam phala arthavāda upapattīnām abheda eva saṃbhavāt ca tathā śākhā antara sthita abheda vākyānām upāsana aprakaraṇa sthitānām tu upāsana apara tayā nābheda para vākya virodhaḥ iti tattvam asi vākya artha nirūpaṇam atha aham brahma asmi ityādi aneka śruti smṛti artha kathanam bṛhat āraṇyaka sthitasya tu ‘brahma vā idam agra āsīt  tad ā ātmānam eva avedaham brahma asmī ati vākyasya anupāsana aprakaraṇa stha tayā abheda pramāpaka tvam eva na ca tad yaḥ yaḥ  devānām pratyabudhyata sa eva tad abhavat tathā ṛṣīṇām tathā manuṣyāṇām iti bheda para vākya śeṣa virodhaḥ tatra api deva ādiṣu prabuddham puruṣam nirdhārya ‘sa eva tad abhavat i ati brahma abheda paratvena bheda paratva abhāvāt na ca atra vākye brahmaṇa eva prakṛta tvāt na anena jīva brahma aikya siddhiḥ iti śaṅkyam yaḥ  devānām iti jīva parāmarśi vākya śeṣa anusāreṇa brahma padasya kārya brahma paratvāt śuddha brahma paratve ca bodha nimittasya tasmāt tad sarvam abhavat iti sārvātmya lakṣaṇa phala kīrtanasya ayuktatva āpatteḥ na ca anāma brahma iti upāsīta ādityaḥ  brahma ityādeśa iti ādau  iti śabda śiraskatayā nāma ādya bheda abhāvāt atra api iti śabda śiraskatayā brahma bheda abhāva iti śaṅkyam anupāsana aprakaraṇa stha tve nābheda avivakṣāyā nāma brahma ityādau  iva vaktum aśakyatvāt  na ca iti śabda vaiyarthyam ātmā iti eva upāsīta iti ādau  iva śabda jñānayoḥ svābhāvika sakarmakatva prāptau tad nirākaraṇa paratvena upayogāt yad ca  ahaṃśabdaḥ  jīva antaryāmiṇi mukhyaḥ aham manuḥ abhavam sūryaḥ ca iti antaryāmiṇī ahaṃśabda prayogāt  sarva antaryāmikaḥ viṣṇuḥ sarva nāmnā vidhīyate eṣaḥ aham tvam asau ca iti na tu sarva svarūpataḥ iti vacanāt ca iti tad na śāstra dṛṣṭyā tu upadeśaḥ  vāmadevavat iti nyāyena vāmadeva jīva caitanyasya vastu tas  brahma abhedena sūrya ādi bhāvasya ukta tayā antaryāmi paratva abhāvāt ‘tad ya u yaḥ  devānām pratyabudhyata sa eva tad abhava aditi pūrva vākye tattva bodha nimittaka brahma bhāvasya prakṛta tayā paśyan pratipede iti ādeḥ api bodha nimitta brahma bhāva para tayā antaryāmi paratva abhāvāt smṛteḥ api asādhāraṇa tad tad ātmani śakteḥ āvaśyaka tayā tad sahacāreṇa antaryāmiṇi eṣaḥ aham iti ādi prayogaḥ na tu sarva svarūpata iti niṣedhasya tu upahitayoḥ aikya abhāva nibandhana tvāt na virodhaḥ ata eva— viśiṣṭa caitanya rūpe vāmadeve viśiṣṭa caitanya rūpam anusūrya ādi bhāvaḥ  na saṃbhavati iti nirastam śāstra dṛṣṭyā tu ukta tvāt  na ca tarhi śuddha cityabhavam iti uttama puruṣa ayogaḥ bhūta pūrva gatyā saṃbhavāt  na ca aham bhūmimadāmāryāya ityādya yogaḥ na hi cit mātram bhūmi dātriti vācyam upahita citam ādāya teṣām upapatteḥ aham nāma abhavat tasya upaniṣad aham iti ādeḥ ca tādṛśa upāsana aparatvena śakti nirṇāyakatva abhāvāt tasmāt na antaryāmya bheda pareyam śrutiḥ antaryāmiṇi bheda aprasakteḥ ca na ca niyamya ānanti ādinā prasakti ekasmin  api jīve aneka avayava niyāmaka tvasya ekasmin  api rājanye aneka deśa niyāmaka tvasya ca darśanāt  sa yaḥ ca ayam puruṣe yaḥ ca asau  āditye sa ekaḥ  iti asya api na antaryāmi aikya para tā brahma vid āpnoti param ityādinā śuddhasya brahmaṇaḥ prakṛta tayā tasmin  upādhikṛta bhedasya tāttvikatva prasaktau tad nirākaraṇa artha tvena aikya upadeśa upapatteḥ na ca evam chāndogye ya eṣa āditye puruṣaḥ  dṛśyate saḥ aham asmi iti atra sa eva enān brahma gamayati iti atra bheda para uttara vākya virodhaḥ tasya upāsana aprakaraṇa stha tvena ahaṃgraha upāsana apara tayā virodha abhāvāt na ca upāsanā prakaraṇa sthita vākya balāt aikya asiddhau  api anupāsana aprakaraṇa sthitāt api tad asiddhiḥ śaṅkyā anya śeṣa tvasya tasya tad prayojakasya abhāvāt  atha yaḥ anyām devatām upāsta iti uttara vākyasya bheda jñāna nindā para tayā tad anusāreṇa pūrva vākyasya upāsanā paratva ayogāt yad tu brahma śabdaḥ atra brāhmaṇa artha iti na para brahma eka siddhiḥ anyathā pūrva vākye ātmānam eva āvedaham iti anena eva brahma iti jñānasya siddha tvāt  brahma asmi iti vyartham iti tad na ātma śabdena jīva caitanyam anūdya bṛṃhitatva ādi upalakṣita brahmacaitanya abheda vidhi paratvena sārthaka tvāt  tathā ca smṛtiḥ ‘aham hariḥ sarvam idam janārdana ityādikā api saṅgacchate yad tu  atha yaḥ anyām devatām upāste anyaḥ asau  anyaḥ aham asmi iti na sa veda yathā paśuḥ i ti atra antaryāmi bheda jñāna nindanam iti tad na antaryāmiṇaḥ aprakṛta tvāt  pada dvaya lakṣaṇa ādeḥ tātparya anurodhena labdha tvāt  yad tu atra yaḥ anyaḥ  jīvaḥ anyām vilakṣaṇām devatām upāste anyaḥ asau paramātmā aham asmi iti na sa veda yathā paśuḥ iti artha iti tad tuccham vyavahita anvaya doṣāt  aham śabda sannihitānya iti asya ya iti atra nayanāt  na ca ‘yasya yena artha saṃbandha iti nyāyena sannidhānāt yogyatāyāḥ prabala tvam iti śaṅkyam yathā sthita artha saṃbandhe api ukta krameṇa yogya tā sattvāt na ca iyam śrutiḥ svātantryeṇa anya sadbhāva niṣedhikā anyatva pratiyogini svātantrya upasthāpaka pada abhāvāt yad tu kaiścid upāsta iti śravaṇāt  prayatna sādhya jñāna vijātīya vṛtti antara rūpa upāsanāyā eva niṣedhaḥ na tu jñānasya iti uktam tad na  tad ya u yaḥ  devānām pratyabudhyate ati pūrva vākye na sa veda iti nindā vākye ca vedanasya eva nirdeśāt  madhya sthita upāsteḥ api jñāna paratvāt evam muṇḍake ‘sa yaḥ  ha vai tad paramam brahma veda brahmā eva bhavati iti etad api vākyam abheda param eva na ca dvitīya brahma śabdaḥ  jīva para eva tasya jāti jīva kamala āsana ādi aneka artha tvāt dve brahmaṇī iti ādau jīve brahma śabda prayoga saṃbhavāt ca yaḥ paramam brahma veda sa jīva eva bhavati na tu paramam brahma iti arthaḥ ataeva ādyaḥ  brahma śabdaḥ parama tvena viśeṣita iti vācyam jīve brahma pada prayoga saṃbhave api prakṛte para brahma upādānam eva ucitam jīva bhāvasya abrahma bhāvasya ca prāk eva siddha tayā brahma jñāna sādhyatva abhāvāt evam ca artha advitīya brahma bhavanam api paramatva viśeṣitam eva yad ca brahma bhavati iti asya brahma tattva rūpa brahmatva ākrāntaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ saṃpūjya brāhmaṇam bhaktyā śūdraḥ api brāhmaṇaḥ  bhavet  itivat  na hi śūdraḥ api pūjita vrāhmaṇa vyaktiḥ bhavati kiṃtu brāhmaṇatva jāti ākrānta iti tad na pūrva ukta yuktyā prakṛte vyakti abhedasya eva saṃbhavena dṛṣṭānta vaiṣamyāt  na ca ‘asya mahimānaḥ am iti vākya śeṣāt tadīya mahattva prāptiḥ eva na tu tad bhāva iti yuktam deha indriya ādi prapañca vilakṣaṇam yaḥ  veda prapañcam tad vibhūtim ca yaḥ  veda sa vīta śokaḥ  bhavati iti evaṃpara tvāt na ca  ayathā nadyaḥ syandamānā iti bhinna nadī dṛṣṭāntoktiḥ ayuktā iti vācyam spaṣṭa bheda vilayana mātra paratvena dṛṣṭānta upapatteḥ ukta tvāt  parāt  param puruṣam upaiti divyam iti na deśa antara stha brahma prāpti ukti parā tasyāḥ sa guṇa upāsanā phala tvena brahma vidyā phalatva asaṃbhavena svarūpa bhūta brahma prāpti paratvāt na ca dvaita mate nityam brahma bhūtasya apūrva brahma bhāva uktiḥ ayuktā iti vācyam kaṇṭha gata cāmīkara ādau bhrānti nivṛtti mātreṇa prāpta prāpti rūpa tayā phalatva darśanāt  na cāra upanivṛttera śabda tvam śruta artha āpatti gamya tayā śābdatva upapatteḥ ‘brahmā eva san brahmā api etī ati śrutiḥ api aikya parā na ca atra prathama vrahma padasya jīva paratva abhāve kartṛ karma bhāva virodhaḥ sākṣātkāra prāk kālīnaupādhika bhedam ādāya tādṛś nirdeśa upapatteḥ pare avyaye sarva ekībhavanti iti etad api abhede mānam na ca gāvaḥ sāyam goṣṭha ekībhavanti ekībhūtā nṛpāḥ sarve vavarṣuḥ pāṇḍavam śaraiḥ kīṭaḥ  bhramareṇa ekībhūta  iti sthāna aikya mata aikya sādṛśya nibandha na ekībhāvasya gaḥ nṛpa kīṭa bhramara ādau darśanāt  atra api taiḥ eva nimittaiḥ gauṇa ekībhāva iti vācyam mukhya tve saṃbhavati gauṇa tvasya ayogāt  brahma aikya mātra paratvena sakṛt uccaritasya na aneka artha paratva śaṅkā api na ca aikyasya prāk eva siddha tayā abhūta tad bhāva artha cvi pratyaya ayogaḥ sva gṛha nikṣipta ajñāta nidhivat  sataḥ api āvṛta tvena abhūta samatayā cvipratyaya upapatteḥ na ca pare avyaya iti śruta saptamī hāniḥ aśruta tṛtīyā kalpanā pattiḥ ca iti vācyam śruti antara anusāreṇa saptamyā ananusaraṇīya tvāt  na ca ‘paramam sāmyam upaiti parāt param puruṣam upaitī ati pūrva uttara vākya virodhaḥ tasya prāk eva nirāsāt  tathā antaryāmi prakaraṇa stham anānyaḥ atas asti draṣṭe ati vākyam akṣara prakaraṇa stham na anyat atas asti draṣṭri ati vākyam ca aikye pramāṇam na cāta iti anena prastutam sarva niyantāram parāmṛśya anyaḥ  draṣṭā na asti iti ukteḥ sva niyāmaka draṣṭṛ antara niṣedha āyāti na tu draṣṭṛ sāmānya niṣedhaḥ asmin grāme ayam eva sarva niyāmakaḥ  na anyaḥ puruṣaḥ asti iti ādau  anya śabdasya prastuta sadṛśāni apara tayā vyutpanna tvāt  samānam itara  chayenena iti atra itara śabdasya pūrva nirdiṣṭa sadṛśa paratva ukteḥ ca iti vācyam anena hi etad sarvam veda iti pratijñātasya eka vijñānena sarva vijñānasya upapādana artham anya tvena pratītena jīvena abheda bodhanāt  acetana vargasya atas anyat ārtam na iti na iti iti niṣedhāt ca jīva brahma abheda eva vākya prameyaḥ dṛṣṭānte tu abhedasya avivakṣita tvāt tvad ukta prakāra āśrayaṇe bādhaka abhāvāt na ca atra api antaryāmi vākye ya ātmanaḥ antaraḥ yama ātmā na veda yasya ātmā śarīram ya ātmānam antaraḥ  yamayatī ati pūrva vākyena aeṣa ta ātmā antaryāmyamṛtaḥ atas anyat ārtam i ati uttara vākye ca virodhaḥ tatra paramātmanaḥ anyam cetanam aṅgīkṛtya tasya ārti yukta tvena asvātantryasya eva uktiḥ iti vācyam pūrva vākyasya aupādhika bheda mātreṇa upapatteḥ uttara vākyena na cetanā antarasya ārti yogaḥ  vidhīyate kiṃtu ‘eṣaḥ antaryāmī te ātme ati jīva svarūpa bhūta antaryāmiṇaḥ  vyatiriktam sarvam ārtam vinaśvaram iti vā mithyā iti vā bodhanāt na virodha śaṅkā ataeva akṣara vākye api ‘etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ ityādi pūrva vākyena virodha iti apāstam kiṃca advitīyāt vai bhayam bhavatī ati bhedasya bhaya hetu tvena nindita tvāt api abheda eva upaniṣad gamyaḥ na ca asya virodhinaḥ samānāt  bhayam bhavati iti eva arthaḥ loke tādṛśāt eva bhayam bhavati iti loka siddha anuvādi tvāt  pūrvatra atasmāt ekākī bibheti uttaratra ‘tasmāt ekākī na ramata iti śravaṇāt ca iti vācyam yad madanyat na asti kasmāt na bibhemi iti tatas  eva asya bhayam vīyāya iti śruteḥ sāmānyatas  dvitīya mātra darśanasya eva bhaya hetu tvāt  viśeṣa kalpanā yogāt ekākī bibheti iti pūrva vākye parama artha darśana rahitasya tad nimitta bhaya saṃbhavāt ekākī bibheti iti uktam uttara vākye tasmāt ekākī na ramata iti atra iṣṭa saṃyoga janya rateḥ ekākinī bhāvāt ekākinaḥ  ratiḥ na asti iti uktam tatas ca atattva jña viṣaya ukta vākya anusāreṇa tattva jña viṣaya madhya vākyasya sva artha samarpaṇena api upayukta tvāt  tad virodhi artha paratva ayogāt etasmin  udaram antaram kurute atha tasya bhayam bhavati iti bheda nindayā api abheda siddhiḥ na ca etasmin  iti śravaṇāt  sva gata bheda niṣedhaḥ ayam na bheda mātra niṣedha iti   śaṅkyam alpa arthakāra śabda svārasya api arthaka utpāda svārasyāt etasya pratiyogi tvena anullekhāt ca bheda mātra niṣedha para tayā tad viśeṣa niṣedha paratva kalpanā yogāt evam aekaḥ  devaḥ sarva bhūteṣu gūḍha ityādi śrutiḥ api atra aikye pramāṇam na ca antaryāmi ekya pareyam śrutiḥ ayataḥ  vā imāni bhūtāni jāyante iti ādau  iva bhūta śabdasya cetana para tvāt iti vācyam dṛṣṭānta asaṃpratipatteḥ cetanasya jāyamānatva ādi ayogāt  bhūta hiṃsā niṣedha vākya iva cetanā adhiṣṭhita prāṇa śarīra ādeḥ eva bhūta śabda vācya tvāt ata eva ‘eka eva hi bhūtātmā bhūte bhūte vyavasthitaḥ ityādi smṛtiḥ api evam ‘yāvat moham tu bhedaḥ syāt  jīvasya ca parasya ca tatas  param na bhedaḥ asti bheda hetoḥ abhāvataḥ vibheda janake ajñāne nāśam ātyantikam gate ātmanaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  bhedam asantam kaḥ kariṣyati ityādi smṛtyā bhedasya avidyakatva pratīteḥ abheda eva tāttvika iti gamyate na ca atra bheda śabdaḥ  mitra bheda iti ādau  iva vaimatya arthaḥ tathā sati lakṣaṇa āpatteḥ anyonya abhāva ādeḥ eva mukhya tvāt  śruta artha tyāgasya anyāyya tvāt akṣetra jñam ca api mām viddhi sarva kṣetreṣu bhārata ityādi smṛtiḥ api atra mānam na ca kṣetrajñam sarvajñam mām sarva kṣetreṣu viddhi iti arthaḥ ‘mahābhūtāni ahaṅkāra iti ādi uktvā ‘etat kṣetram samāsena sa vikāram udāhṛtam iti anena ‘yasya pṛthivī śarīra amiti ādi śrutyā īśvara śarīra tayā uktam cetana acetana ātmakam sarvam kṣetram iti ukta tvāt iti vācyam sarva niyāmaka tayā sakala kṣetra saṃbandhasya prāk eva siddheḥ paunaruktyāpatteḥ tad tad kṣetra adhiṣṭhātṛ tvena kṣetrajña pada vācya jīvā bheda paratvasya eva ucita tvāt ata eva  kṣetrāṇi ca śarīrāṇi bījāni ca śubha aśubhe śrutāni vetti yoga ātmā tatas  kṣetrajña ucyate prakṛteḥ ca vikārāṇām draṣṭāram aguṇa ātmakam kṣetrajñam āhuḥ jīvam tu kartāram guṇa saṃvṛtam ityādi smṛtau kṣetrajña śabdasya sarva antaryāmi sarvajña paratve api prakṛte tad asaṃbhavaḥ jīve su prasiddha tvāt ca na ca śāstra sthā vā iti nyāyaḥ tasya ekatarāśā strīya viṣaya tvāt evam anyāni api vākyāni yathāsaṃbhavam aikye yojyāni tasmāt āgama aikye mānam iti advaita siddhau aham brahma asmi ityādi aneka śruti smṛti artha kathanam atha jīva brahma abheda anumānam evam anumānam api tatra mānam jīvāḥ paramātmanaḥ tattvataḥ  na bhidyante ātma tvāt  paramātmavat  nanu ātma tvam jātiḥ atra hetuḥ tathā ca abhede hetu ucchittiḥ eva pratikūla tarka iti ced na tattvataḥ abhede api vyāvahārika bhedena eva vyāvahārika jāteḥ anuccheda upapatteḥ jñātṛ tvāt iti api atra hetuḥ jīve upadheye antaḥkaraṇa upahita vṛtteḥ tasya asiddheḥ abhāvāt  vyavahāre sva bhinna jñāna anapekṣa tvam hetuḥ tava api jīvasya sva abhinna nitya jñānasya abādhya vyavahāra viṣaya tvāt abādhya tvam api atra hetuḥ na ca jaḍe vyabhicāraḥ tatra bādhya tvena hetoḥ abhāvāt  tāttvika bhedasya sarvatra asattvena vyabhicāra anavakāśāt na ca evam vyāvahārika bheda vyatirekaḥ api evam eva sādhyatām jīva paramātmanoḥ iti vācyam tatra pratyakṣa virodhasya eva bādhaka tvāt  śruti anugrahāt ca ābhāsa sāmya āpādanā prayojaka tvānavakāśāt ata eva vimatā jīvāḥ caitrāt tattvataḥ  na bhidyante jīva tvāt caitravat iti jīva aikye vimatā jīvā vastu tas  brahmaṇaḥ  na bhidyante vastu tvāt  brahmavat iti brahma jīva aikye ca yad anumānam tatra vyavahārataḥ api na bhidyanta iti api evam sādhya tām iti ābhāsa sāmyam  apāstam evam vimatāni śarīrāṇi caitra adhiṣṭhitāni śarīra tvāt  saṃmatavat  na ca etāvatā na jīva aikya siddhiḥ caitra adhiṣṭhita tve api anya adhiṣṭhitatva saṃbhavāt  caitra mātra adhiṣṭhita tve tu antaryāmī adhiṣṭhita tvena dṛṣṭānte sādhya vaikalya āpattiḥ iti vācyam caitra mātra saṃsāri adhiṣṭhita tvasya sādhya tvāt  caitra mātra bhoga āyatanāni iti vā sādhyam na ca bhoktṛ tvam antaḥkaraṇa viśiṣṭasya tad ca pratiśarīram bhinnam yad ca ekam śuddha caitanyam tad na bhoktṛ iti bādha iti vācyam bhoktṛ tvasya viśiṣṭa vṛtti tve api viśeṣya vṛttitva anapāyāt  na ca evam vimatāni śarīrāṇi caitra manasā eva yuktāni iti ābhāsa sāmyam manasaḥ api aikye vyavasthāyāḥ sarvathā anupapatteḥ śruti anugrahān anugrahābhyām viśeṣāt ca dṛṣṭi sṛṣṭi pakṣe tad abhyupagamāt ca ātmā dravyatva apara jātyā nānā na vibhu tvāt  ākāśavat  na ca pratikalpam ākāśasya bhedena sādhya vaikalyam paricchinna tvena sādhana vaikalyam ca ātma tvasya parama aṇutva ādivat ajāti tve api ātma bheda siddhyā ca artha antaram iti vācyam ātmatva adhikaraṇam dravyatva apara jātya eka kāle nānā na samāna kālīna mūrta mātra saṃyukta tvāt gaganavat iti atra tātparyāt  pakṣa viśeṣaṇa mahimnā ca na artha antaram vimataḥ  bhedaḥ mithyā ekasyām dṛśi kalpitaḥ  vā bheda tvāt  dṛśya tvāt vā candra bhedavat  ekasyām dṛśi kṣaṇika va ādi kalpita bhedavat vā mithyātvam prāk uktam eva na ca kalpita sādhāraṇa bhedatva asiddhiḥ bhede akalpita tvasya eva asiddheḥ ataeva candrasya kalpita dvitīya candrāt  bhedasya satya tvena dṛṣṭānte sādhya vaikalyam mukteḥ saṃsārāt  brahmaṇaḥ  anṛtāt  bhede ca vyabhicāra iti nirastam na ca evam abhedaḥ  mithyā abheda tvāt  deha ātmā bhedavat ityādi su sādham śūnya vāda āpatteḥ ukta tvāt  evam vimatā bheda dhīḥ mithyā bheda dhī tvāt candrabheda dhīvat na ca brahma anṛta bheda prati iti ādau vyabhicāraḥ tāsām api pakṣa sama tvāt  ābhāsa sāmyasya tāttvika tve pratyetavyatva anupapattyā eva nirāsaḥ ata eva ‘vimatam tāttvika sva antar bheda śūnyam mahat tvataḥ yad evam tad tathā yad vā kham tathā idam yatas tathā iti atra gaganasya sāvayava tvena na sādhya vaikalyam sva antar padena sva avayava atiriktasya ukteḥ evam saṃvid  sva antar gaṇika svābhāvika bheda hīnā upādhim antareṇa avibhāvyamāna bheda tvāt  gaganavat  na ca sādhya vaikalyam naiyāyika diśā dṛṣṭāntatva ukteḥ na ca icchādeḥ api ghaṭa paṭa ādi upādhi bhedena vibhāvyamāna bheda tayā vyabhicāraḥ teṣu iti vācyam icchā ādīnām ekāntaḥkaraṇa pariṇāma tvena tatra api sādhya sattvāt  vimataḥ  avyāpya vṛtti dharmān avacchinna pratiyogitākaḥ  bhedaḥ sva samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogī bheda tvāt  saṃyukta bhedavat  vimataḥ  bhedaḥ kevala anvayi ati anta abhāva pratiyogī padārtha tvāt nitya dravyavat  sva rūpeṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tve yathā na tuccha tvam pāramārthikatva ākāreṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tve brahmavat  sat rūpa tā upapattyā na yathārtha antaram tad  prāk uktam anyonya abhāva tvam sva samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi vṛtti traikālikā bhāva vṛtti tve sati abhāvatva sākṣāt vyāpya tvāt atyanta abhāva tvavat iti anumānam pūrva ukta saṃyukta pratiyogika bheda rūpa dṛṣṭānta siddhi artham na ca śuktau śukti bhedasya āropitasya sattvena siddha sādhanam asat anyathā ākhyāti vādinaḥ tava anaṅgīkṛta tvena tasya sādhya tvāt  na ca traikālika tve mithyātva ayogaḥ māyā cid saṃbandhasya kāla tvena sarva kāla sthiteḥ atad virodhi tvāt  naca avyāpya vṛtti tayā saṃyoga ādivat  samāna adhikaraṇa atyanta abhāva pratiyogi tvena artha antaram pakṣa viśeṣaṇa mahimnā avyāpya vṛtti tvasya asaṃbhavena tad ayogāt  anusandhānā dvaya vyavasthā ādikam prāk eva nirākṛtam aprayojakatva ābhāsa sāmya sat pratipakṣa upādhyādi pūrva ukta prapañca mithyātva anumānavat nirākaraṇīyam evam ātma tvam ekatva vyāpyam ātma mātra vṛtti tvāt caitra tvavat ityādi api draṣṭavyam iti advaita siddhau jīva brahma abheda anumānam atha aṃśa tvena api aikya siddhiḥ ‘pādaḥ asya viśvā bhūtānī ati ‘mama eva aṃśaḥ  jīva loke jīva bhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ iti smṛtau ca aṃśatva vyapadeśāt api jīva brahma abheda siddhiḥ yadi api brahma prati jīvasya aṃśa tvam na tāvat ārambhaka tvam brahmaṇaḥ anādi tvāt  na api khaṇḍa tvam acchedya tvāt  na api samudāyi tvam samudāyasya samudāyi ananya tvena vyavahāradaśāyām api saṃsāri anya śuddha brahma bhāva āpātāt  na api bhinna abhinna dravya tvam anaṅgīkārāt  na api ghaṭam prati khaṇḍa ghaṭasya iva pradeśa tvam niṣpradeśa brahma prati kalpanām vinā tad ayogāt  tathā api ghaṭa ākāśasya mahā ākāśam pratīva kalpita pradeśatva rūpam aṃśa tvam jīvasya avaccheda pakṣe saṃbhavati svatas  niraṃśe api aupādhika aṃśaḥ yathā yujyate tathā uktam purastāt  na tu sadṛśa tve tatas  nyūna tvam sthūla paṭam prati sūkṣma paṭasya api aṃśatva āpatteḥ vastu eka deśe mukhyasya aṃśa śabdasya svatas  niraṃśe api kalpita eka deśe prayogasya artha antare prayoga kalpanā apekṣayā abhyarhita tvāt aaṃśaḥ nānā vyapadeśāt anyathā ca api dāśakita va ādi tvam adhīyata eka iti sūtre ‘saḥ anveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavya etam evam viditvā muniḥ bhavati ya ātmani tiṣṭhanni atyādi bheda vyapadeśasya ‘brahma dāsā brahma dāśā brahme kitavā ute ati ātharvaṇa mantre abheda vyapadeśasya ca udāhṛta tvāt ca ukta artha parigrahasya ucita tvāt ātyantika bheda garbha artha antara svīkāre ca etad sūtra virodha āpatteḥ kutracid anyatra prayoga mātreṇa sarvatra etad kalpane bahu viplava āpatteḥ ca ataeva nanu jīvasya śuddha caitanya aṃśa tvam vā īśvara aṃśa tvam vā pādaḥ asya iti anayā śrutyā bodhyam na ādyaḥ pādaḥ asya viśvā bhūtāni iti śruta avidaṃśabdena sahasra śīrṣatva ādi viśiṣṭa prakṛta īśvarasya mama eva aṃśa iti smṛtau ca īśvare prayuktā asmad śabdena īśvarasya eva ukteḥ na antyaḥ tvad mate īśvarasya api upahita tvena ghaṭa ākāśam prati karaka ākāśasya īva īśvaram prati jīvasya aṃśatva ayogāt na ca gṛha ākāśa eva punar ghaṭena iva īśvara upādhinā avacchinnam eva caitanyam punar jīva upādhinā avacchidyata iti vācyam tathā tve hi muktasya śuddha brahma tvam na syāt  tasmāt tvad mate api na mukhyam aṃśa tvam na api aupādhikam vaktum śakyam atas  mad ukta prakāra eva ādaraṇīya iti nirastam artha antara parigrahe virodhasya ukta tvāt śruti smṛti gata sarva nāmnā sahasra śīrṣatva ādi upalakṣita caitanya parāmarśāt ukta dūṣaṇān avakāśāt ca tasmāt   tvam strī tvam pumān asi tvam kumāra uta vā kumārī tvam jīrṇaḥ  daṇḍena vañcasi tvam jātaḥ  bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ sarvāṇi rūpāṇi vicitya dhīraḥ nāmāni kṛtvā abhivat an yadāste ityādi śrutyā jīva brahma abhede pramite api mantṛmantavyatva ādi bhede vyapadeśa nirvāha artham kālpanikā aṃśa tvasya śruti smṛti vyāhata tvena tad balāt api abhedaḥ avagamyata iti siddham iti advaita siddhau aṃśa tvena api aikyā saddhiḥ atha jīva brahma abheda nirūpaṇam tathā jīva brahmaṇoḥ mukha pratimukhavat bimba pratibimba rūpa tvāt api abhedaḥ avagantavyaḥ nanu dṛṣṭānte nābhedaḥ saṃpratipannaḥ caitra ta  chāye bhinne itivat  caitra tad pratibimbe bhinna iti eva pārśva sthitena grahaṇāt  svena api sva kara tad pratibimbe bhinne iti grahaṇāt ca iti ced na āpātataḥ bheda pratītau  api sa yuktika pratyakṣeṇa bimba pratibimbayoḥ aikya siddhyā dṛṣṭāntatva upapatteḥ yathā lakṣaṇa aparijñāne bheda bhramavataḥ api bahi sthitaḥ caitraḥ  yad sva lakṣaṇaka tvena pratipannaḥ tatas  gṛhasthe tathā bhāti tasmin caitra eva ayam iti dhīḥ tathā grīvā stham mukham yad sva lakṣaṇakam pratipannam darpaṇa stham api tathā iti avadhārya tathā eva idam mukham iti sa eva ayam kara iti ca sva parasādhāraṇa pratītiḥ api anubhava siddhā na ca kiṃcid su accha tāmra ādau mukhe chāyā mātre pratīte api saṃsthāna viśeṣa apratītyā pratyabhijñāyā asiddhiḥ iti vācyam sarvatra apratītau  api nirmala darpaṇa ādau  eva tad siddhyā dṛṣṭānta siddheḥ nanu  sva netra golaka ādau svasya abhijñā virahāt pratyabhijñā api katham iti ced na darpaṇa āhata cakṣū raśmīnām agra avacchedena saṃbandhāt  sva netra golaka ādīnām abhijñāyāḥ sannihita pūrva samaya eva saṃbhavāt  yad tu sūrya pārśva sthite pratisūrye pratyabhijñā virahāt atra api pratyabhijñā virahaḥ iti tad na tatra upādheḥ atra iva anākalanena aupādhikatva anirṇayāt tathā ca upādhi nibandhanatva jñānam tad lakṣakatva jñānam ca abheda sākṣātkāre sāmagrī tasyām satyām darpaṇe mama mukham lagnam iti anubhava abhāva eva anubhava viruddhaḥ yad tu  caitra pratibimbaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ  na caitraḥ kiṃtu tena anumita iti viparīta anubhava virodhaḥ iti tad na vastutas abhede jñāte api upādhi avacchinnaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ anavacchinnaḥ anumita iti pratīti avirodhāt  śarad gaṅgayā varṣa ṛtugaṅgā anumānavat na ca evam pratimukhe pratyak mukhatva ādinā dṛśyamāne sva mukhe tad buddhiḥ syāt  bālānām ca sva pratibimbe bāla antara bhramaḥ  na syāt iti vācyam tayoḥ sva lakṣaṇakatva ajñāna nivandhana tvāt  ata eva kadācid  pratimukhe api mama mukham iti buddhi vyapadeśau na ca ayam vyavahāraḥ  bheda jñāna pūrvaka tvena mārge sva padavyām sva pada vyavahāravat  gauṇaḥ sva lakṣaṇakatva jñāna daśāyām bheda jñānasya asat kalpa tvāt nanu avivādaḥ syāt  bheda sākṣātkāre anyathā tvayā api kasya bhrama tvam ucyate na ca bhedam bhedakam ca sākṣātkurvan abhedam sākṣātkurvāṇaḥ  dṛṣṭa iti ced  śvaitya vyāpya śaṅkhatva sākṣātkāre pīta sākṣāt kāravat  upādhi māhātmyāt abhedam sākṣātkurvāṇaḥ  bhedam sākṣātkaroti iti aṅgīkriyate anubhavasya durapahnava tvāt  na ca evam upādānasya aikya ajñānasya aikya jñānena nivṛtteḥ bhrama anupapattiḥ tad nivartane upādhi virahasya api sahakāri tvāt  na ca evam tad jñāne sati tad na jānāmi iti ananubhavena tasya sva prāgabhāvam pratīva ajñānam pratyapi anya anapekṣasya eva nivartaka tvam iti vācyam na jānāmi iti vyavahāra prayojaka ajñāna aṃśa nivartane api bhramasya anubhūyamāna tvena tad upādāna aṃśasya nivṛttau jīvanmuktau prārabdha karmaṇa iva upādheḥ eva pratibandhaka tayā tad viraha apekṣāyāḥ  āvaśyaka tvāt  etena bheda bhramasya asya mūla avidyā upādānaka tve vyāvahārikatva āpattiḥ ajñāna anupādānaka tve apasiddhāntaḥ bimba pratibimba bhedasya satyatva āpattiḥ ca iti nirastam ukta nyāyena upapatteḥ yāvahārika tve api anupapatti abhāvāt ca tayoḥ aikye anumānam api pramāṇam atra yadi api atyanta sādṛśyam savya itara kara ādau vyabhicāri tathā api pratibimbaḥ  bimba abhinnaḥ tad gata sādhāraṇa dharmavat tvāt tad viruddha dharmān adhikaraṇa tvāt bimba ājanaka ajanya tvāt ca na ca dvitīya hetoḥ asiddhiḥ pratyak mukhatva ādi viruddha dharmasya upādhi kṛta tvena svābhāvika viruddha dharmān adhikaraṇa tvasya sattvāt  na ca bimba anantara jāte pratibimbe tṛtīya hetoḥ asiddhiḥ aikya vādinam prati bimba anantara tvasya eva asiddheḥ nanu pṛthak kārya anurodhena pariveṣa indracāpa  chāyā pratisūrya ādau  ivātrā api pṛthak kāraṇam kalpanīyam pratibimbam api hi chāyā viśeṣaḥ na hi bherī ghāta ādi klṛpta hetu abhāvāt dhvanau  uparate api śrūyamāṇaḥ pratidhvaniḥ na śabda antaram iti ced na pratibimbasya chāyā virodhinyāloke api saṃbhavena chāyā viśeṣatva asiddheḥ pratidhvaneḥ tu bhinna kāla tvena tad bhedasya prakṛte anupayogāt  kārya pārthakī siddhi uttara kāla kalpya kāraṇa bhedasya prathamam vaktum aśakyatvāt  klṛpta hetu bhāvena kāryasya eva bhāvāt ca pratyakṣasya bheda abhedayoḥ sama tvāt  yuktyā abheda eva prābalyāt ca ata eva uktam vivaraṇe ‘darpaṇa ādau na mukha vyakti antaram asti tad janaka śūnya tvāt śaśa śirasi viṣāṇavat i ati evam abheda dhiya upapādita tvāt  asyāḥ prābalyam vyakti antara hetu abhāvāt sā eva na asti iti apāstam prāk  na ca chāyā ādau  iva kāraka bhedasya kalpya tvena bheda buddhiḥ sa upapattikā tathā klṛpta dravya anantarbhāve tamaḥvat dravya antara tā eva iti vācyam anyonya āśraya āpatteḥ bheda sā upapattika tve dravya antaratva kāraṇa antara tvayoḥ kalpanam tasmin  ca sa upapattika tvam iti ataeva ‘na uparaktam na vāri stham i ati smārta vyavahāraḥ  mukhyaḥ na tu yathā citritaḥ siṃhaḥ yathā dāru mayī yoṣā yathā carmamayaḥ  mṛga ityādivat gauṇaḥ na ca tvad pakṣe api vāri stha śabdaḥ  na mukhyaḥ vāriṇi sūrya antara abhāvāt  gagana sthasya vāri sthatva ayogāt iti   vācyam vāri stha tvena upasthita aśeṣa vāri stha sūrya niṣedhāt nanu vāri stha tvena sūrya eva upasthitaḥ tayoḥ abhedaḥ  na pratyakṣa siddhaḥ na api yuktaḥ nyūna adhika parimāṇavattva calatva upādhi saṃyuktatva asaṃyuktatva tvac ādi grāhyatva agrāhyatva pratyak mutvā pratyak mukhatva ādinā kastūrī bimba pratibimbayoḥ saurabhā saurabha ādinā ca bheda siddheḥ iti ced na nyūna parimāṇa ādinā saurabha ādinā ca upādhi gatasya bhedaḥ sādhanīyaḥ tathā ca upādhi gata tvasya bimbe kalpita tvena pakṣa hetvoḥ asiddheḥ kalpita hetu ādinā tad samāna sattāka sādhya siddhau  avivādāt ca na api ayathā eṣā puruṣe chāyā etasmin  etad ātatam chāyā yathā puṃsadṛśī pum adhīnā ca dṛśyate evam eva ātmakāḥ sarve brahma ādyāḥ paramātmanaḥ iti śrutyā bheda iti vācyam kalpita bheda mātreṇa sādṛśya upapatteḥ tāttvika tve śruti tātparya abhāvāt aikya pratipādaka aneka śruti virodhāt ca nanu  tatsva lakṣaṇakasya eva darpaṇa stha tvena āropita tayā tad rūpa ādi yuktasya iva tad gandha ādi yuktasya api darpaṇa stha tvena pratītiḥ syāt iti ced na tad sva lakṣaṇaka tvena āropita tve api yāvat sva lakṣaṇaka tvena āropitatva anaṅgīkāreṇa gandha ādi prati iti āpādanasya aśakya tvāt nanu evam darpaṇe mukhasya abhāve upādheḥ pratibimba pakṣa pāti tvena mukha pratimukhayoḥ avadātatva śyāma tvavat jīva brahmaṇoḥ saṃsāri tvā saṃsāritva ādi vyavasthā katham iti ced  na āropitena ādarśa stha tvena viśiṣṭe pratibimbe tad dharmasya mālinya ādeḥ saṃbhavāt  na ca upādhi stha tvasya api āropya tvena katham mālinya āśraya tāvacchedaka tvam eka viśiṣṭe itara āropa abhāvāt iti vācyam āropa pūrva pratīta dharma viśiṣṭasya eva āropya āśraya tvāt na tu tasya satya tvam api iti para prakriyā nibandhana doṣa an avakāśāt na ca pratimukham eva darpaṇa stham na tu mukham iti pratibimba darpaṇa sthatva anubhavena katham pratibimba tvasya tad stha tvagarbhata iti vācyam avidyā upahitasya avidyā śraya tvavat darpaṇa upahitasya darpaṇa āśritatva saṃbhavāt etena  mālinya sthānīyasya saṃsārasya viśiṣṭa vṛtti tvāt  śuddha āśrita mokṣa sāmāna adhikaraṇyā yoga iti nirastam saṃsāraḥ tāvat upahita vṛttiḥ tathā ca upadheya aṃśam ādāya sāmānādhikaraṇya saṃbhavāt tathā ca vṛkṣa stha kapi saṃyoga ādhāra tā agreṇa iva mukhe mālinyam darpaṇa saṃbandhena avacchidyate etāvān eva viśeṣaḥ vṛkṣe saṃyogaḥ tu sāhajikaḥ mukhe aupādhikam mālinyam tena upahite upādhi avacchinna eva mukhe mālinya dhīḥ etena  darpaṇa mālinyasya mukha niṣṭha tve saṃsārasya api śuddha niṣṭhata āpattiḥ vṛkṣaḥ saṃyukta itivat  mukham malinam iti pratītyāpattiḥ mukham na malinam kiṃtu pratimukham iti anubhava virodha āpattiḥ ca iti nirastam nanu kastūrī ādi pratibimbasya sva lakṣaṇān anugamena katham bimba aikyam na ca tad ākāra tā mātreṇa tattvam tarhi chāyā pratimudrā pratimā ādīnām api tattvam syāt  pratyak mukhatva ādeḥ bhedakasya atra api sattvāt ca na ca pratyak mukhatva dhībhrāntā pratibimbam bimba abhimukham na iti kadāpi ananubhavāt iti ced na darpaṇa ādi pratibimbe sva lakṣaṇa anugamena bimba aikye vyavasthite pratibimbatva avacchedena eva tad kalpanāt  chāyā ādau sva lakṣaṇaka tvasya kutra api adarśanena sāmya abhāvāt  na api pratyak mukhatva ādi bhedakam malina tvavat upādhi kṛta tvāt  ata eva japā kusume rakta tā pratītivat  tad hīrdha antā darpaṇa āhatam cakṣuḥ pratyaṅmukham bhavati tasya ca sva abhimukha tayā grahaṇa sāmarthyāt ca anya abhimukhasya api mukha ādeḥ tathā agrahaṇa upapatteḥ ca tad uktaṃ ‘ darpaṇa abhihatā dṛṣṭiḥ parāvṛttya sva m ānanam vyāpnuvanti ābhimukhyena vyatyastam darśayet mukham na ca   parāvṛtya sva mukhasya eva grahaṇe pārśva sthasya mukha dvaya pratīti ayogaḥ sva mukhasya eva iti niyama asiddheḥ upādhi sannihita mātrasya eva tathā grahaṇāt  na ca   evam darpaṇa ādeḥ abhighātaka mātreṇa upakṣīṇa tayā darpaṇa iva darpaṇa bhede api aneka mukha pratītiḥ na syāt iti   vācyam abhighātaka an eka tvena cakṣuṣaḥ anekāgra sampattyā pratyagram sva abhighāta ka avacchedaka mukha grāhaka tayā dṛṣṭānta vaiṣamyāt  na ca maṇi darpaṇa kṛpāṇa ādiṣu viruddha rūpa aneka mukha pratītiḥ katham evam yujyata iti vācyam anvaya vyatireka siddha upādhi prābalya nibandhana tvāt iti gṛhāṇa na ca cakṣuḥ parivṛtti prakriyā brahma pratibimbe jīve na saṃbhavati iti   vācyam cākṣuṣa pratibimba mātra viṣaya tayā eva asya upapādita tvāt  na ca virala avayavasya jalasya netra abhighātaka tve jala antargata śilā ādi agrahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ sarva avacchedena abhighāta abhāvena antare api cakṣuṣaḥ praveśa saṃbhavāt  na ca evam bahu dūra vyavahita ūrdhva bhāga sūrya ādi grahaṇe pṛṣṭha bhāga sthasya vyavahitasya api grahaṇa āpattiḥ iti vācyam cakṣuṣaḥ  gamana āgamanābhyām viśeṣāt  na hi dūra stha sūrya grahaṇam vadatā pṛṣṭha kuḍya ādikam bhittvā cakṣuḥ gacchati iti uktam bhavati na ca evam śilā abhihatam api cakṣuḥ parāvṛtya mukham gṛhṇātu iti   vācyam tava api pratibimbam tatra utpadyatām iti āpatteḥ asvacchatayā parihārasya asmākam api sama tvāt  tava svaccha eva utpadyate mama tatas  eva cakṣuḥ parāvartate iti aṅgīkārāt  na ca evam pratibimba darśanena api bimba darśana janya sukha puṇya ādi prasaṅgaḥ yatra tad darśana mātra janya tā na anyatas  tatra iṣṭāpatteḥ yatra ca upādhi vinirmukta jñāna tvena viśiṣya janyatā tatra āpādaka abhāvāt na ca evam sūryakasya api sūryavat durdarśatva āpattiḥ golake sūrya tejaḥ sāmmukhyasya durdarśa tā prayojakasya sūryaka grahaṇa kāle abhāvāt na ca su accha darpaṇa iva kiṃcid svaccha tāmra ādau mukha saṃsthāna viśeṣa pratīti āpātaḥ upādhi gata atyanta svaccha tā vyatireka prayojaka mālinya ādeḥ eva tatra pratibandhaka tvāt  anyathā tava api tādṛś saṃsthāna viśeṣavat pratibimbam tatra katham na utpadyata iti asya duṣpariharatva āpatteḥ nanu avaccheda pakṣe dvi guṇīkṛtya vṛtti asaṃbhave api pratibimba pakṣe tad saṃbhavena antaryāmi tvam iti sva vacana virodhaḥ upādheḥ pratibimba pakṣa pāti tvam iti ukti ayogaḥ ca iti ced na sarva upādhi avacchinnatva eka deśa upādhi avacchinna tvābhyām upādhi kalpita bhedena ca sva uktyavirodha upapatteḥ ataeva   darpaṇe na mukham iti eva upādhi saṃsṛṣṭa tayā niṣidhyate na tu anedam rūpya amitivat  na etad mukham iti sva rūpeṇa nanu   na atra mukha  chāyā asti iti ananubhavena pratyuta etā  antam kālam atra pratisūrya āsīt itivat  pratimukham āsīt iti eva anubhavena pratibimbam iva ādarśa ityādi smṛtyā ca pratimukhe darpaṇa stha tvasya api abādha eva na hi bhūmau meghaḥ  na iti etāvatā megha  chāyā api tatra bādhitā iti ced na mukha pratimukhayoḥ eka sva lakṣaṇaka tvena aikya vyavasthityā mukhasya eva tad sthatva niṣedhena pratimukhasya tad sattva niṣedha saṃbhavāt megha  chāyā pratisūrya ādīnām na tathā iti na megha ādi niṣedhena chāyā ādi niṣedhaḥ smṛtiḥ tu prātītika artham ādāya dṛṣṭānta parā na ca evam pratibimbāt  bimba anumāna ucchedaḥ sādhya aviśeṣāt iti   vācyam upādhi kalpita bhedena viśeṣa upapatteḥ etena anekṣeta udyantam āditya am iti anena udyat pratibimba darśanasya api niṣedhaḥ syāt  vāri stha sūrya darśana niṣedhena ākāśa stha sūrya darśanasya api niṣedhaḥ ca syāt  pratibimba darśanena eva dṛṣṭvā snāyāt iti śāstra arthaḥ api anuṣṭhitaḥ syāt iti nirastam kalpita bhedāt eva śāstrīya vyavasthā upapatteḥ na ca audumbara tayā jñātena ana audumbareṇa audumbaraḥ  yūpaḥ  bhavati iti śāstra artha siddhi prasaṅgaḥ ātma tayā jñāta deha śravaṇa ādinā ātmā śrotavya iti śāstra artha siddhi prasaṅgaḥ ca iti   vācyam pramayā upapattau saṃbhavantyām bhrameṇa tad upapādanasya ayukta tvāt  nanu anādeḥ jīvasya na upādhi adhīnam pratibimba tvam kiṃtu tad adhīna tve sati tad sadṛśa tvam tad ca bheda vyāptam iti viruddhaḥ  hetuḥ uktaṃhi sūtra kṛtā ‘ata eva upamā sūryaka ādi avat iti ced  na upādhi adhīna tvam hi upādhau sati eva sattvam tad ca nānā āditva virodhi anādi jīvasya api tad saṃbhavāt ataeva pratibimba padasya bheda sādṛśya arthaka tvam ādāya viruddhatva uktiḥ hita vāyuktā tad evam pratibimbasya bimbena aikye vyavasthite brahma aikyam jīva jātasya siddham tad pratibimbanāt iti advaita siddhau bimba pratibimba nyāyena aikya siddhiḥ atha ātmanaḥ aṇutva bhaṅgaḥ nanu aṇu tvāt jīvasya katham vyāpakāt īśvarāt abheda iti ced na anityaḥ sarva gataḥ ‘sa vā eṣa mahān aja ātmā ityādi śrutyā jīvaḥ  na aṇuḥ pratyakṣa guṇa āśraya tvāt pratyakṣa tvāt ca ghaṭavat  ātma tvāt abhūta tvāt ca īśvaravat iti ādi anumānaiḥ ca jīvān aṇutva siddheḥ vipakṣe ca deha vyāpi sukha jñāna ādi anupalambhāpattiḥ bādhikā na ca  aṇuḥ hi eṣa ātmā yam vā ete sinītaḥ puṇyam ca pāpam ca   bāla agra śata bhāgasya śatadhā kalpitasya ca bhāgaḥ  jīvaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sa ca ānantyāya kalpata  iti śrutyā jīvaḥ aṇuḥ iti vācyam vyāpakatva pratipādaka bahu śruti virodhena durvijñeyatva paratvāt deha vyāpi guṇa upalambhasya anyathayitum aśakyatvāt etena jīvaḥ  na vyāpakaḥ utkrāntimat tvāt  gatimat tvāt kriyāvat tvāt ca khaga śarīravat  vipakṣe hetu ucchiti āpattiḥ bādhikā iti nirastam hetu asiddheḥ na ca ‘saḥ asmāt śarīrāt utkramya amum lokam adhigacchati amuṣmādimam lokam āgacchatī ati ādibhiḥ śrutibhiḥ ‘tatra cāndramasam jyotiḥ yogī prāpya nivartate ityādi smṛtibhiḥ ca hetu siddhiḥ iti vācyam utkramaṇa ādīnām buddhi gatānām tad upahite śrutyā pratipādanāt  na ca ‘nākasya pṛṣṭhe sukṛte anubhūtvā imam lokam hīnataram vā viśanti te aśubham anubhūyanta iti ādau śrutau sukha duḥkha ādi anubhava sā mānādhikaraṇyasya gatau  ukteḥ katham tasyāḥ  buddhi gata tvam iti vācyam ātmani sukha duḥkha ādi anubhavasya api buddhi upādhika tvena tad sāmāna adhikaraṇyasya gatau svābhāvikatva asa adhaka tvāt nanu asa enān brahma gamayatī atyādi śrutau ‘tatra prayātā gacchanti brahma brahma vidaḥ  janāḥ ityādi smṛtau ca gateḥ mukti sāmāna adhikaraṇyā ukteḥ katham asiddhiḥ iti ced na avyāpakasya eva avyāpakam pratyeva gamanam brahma ca vyāpakam tad prati gamana asaṃbhavena gamana padasya upādhi kṛta bhedarāhiti apara tayā gati mukti sāmānādhikaraṇyā pratipādaka tvāt  nanu‘ pradyotena eṣa ātmā niṣkrāmatī tyātma niṣṭhatva śruteḥ na asiddhiḥ anyathā mokṣa ādikam api buddheḥ eva syāt  na api śruteḥ buddhi upādhika gati ādi viṣaya tvam saṃbhavati tad yathā anaḥsu samāhitam utsarja dyāyāt evam eva ayam śārīra ātmā aprājñena ātmanā anvārūḍha utsarjan yātī ati svābhāvika gati āśraya śakaṭa dṛṣṭāntoktiḥ iti ced na eṣa iti buddhi upahitasya eva parāmarśena śuddha ātma niṣṭha tvasya gatau  anukteḥ mokṣe tu buddhi uparameṇa tad niṣṭha tu asya asaṃbhāvita tayā vaiṣamyāt  sarva sāmyasya dṛṣṭānta tāyāma prayojaka tvāt  tad balena svābhāvikatva paryanta tvasya asiddheḥ na ca ‘tam utkrāmantam prāṇaḥ anūtkrāmatī atyādi śrutau prāṇa ākhya buddhi gatitaḥ prāk eva jīve gati ukteḥ katham buddhi gatyā anyathā siddhiḥ iti   vācyam prāṇa ākhya aṃśena kriyāśakti śālinā paścāt gatau  api aṃśa antareṇa prathamam utkramaṇa saṃbhavāt  etena ‘mana udakrāmat mīlita iva aśnan piban  āste ve ati ādi śrutau manautkramaṇe api ātmanaḥ tad abhāva śravaṇāt ca katham tad gatyā eva gatimat tvam iti nirastam upahitasya upādhi nibandhana gatimat tve buddhi anupahitasya tad abhāva avirodhāt na ca   tathā ‘vidvān nāma rūpāt vimuktaḥ parāt param puruṣam upaiti divyam i atyādi śrutau nāma rūpa vimokṣa anantaram api gati śravaṇāt  katham sā aupādhikī iti vācyam parama puruṣasya sarvatra sannihita tvena tam prati gamana asaṃbhavena upaiti ityasya api pūrvavat artha antara paratvāt ataeva  param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate sa uttamaḥ sa tatra paryetī atyādi śrutiḥ api na gati arthā nanu buddhi gatena gati ādinā kim tad avacchinna ātmani gati ādi jāyate uta buddhi gatam eva āropyate uta upacaryate na ādyaḥ ghaṭa gatyā tad avacchinne nabhasi gati antara adarśanāt  anyathā yatas  ghaṭasya buddheḥ vā gatiḥ tatra ākāśasya ātmanaḥ  vā sa  chidra tvam syāt  anyatra dvi guṇīkṛtya vṛttiḥ ca syāt  na ca pratibimba pakṣe na ukta doṣa iti vācyam tasya vastu antaratva mate ukta doṣa abhāve api darpaṇa āhatā dṛṣṭiḥ parāvṛtya sva mukham gṛhṇāti iti tvad mate upādhigatyā bimbe na gatiḥ iti pratibimbe api asya ayogāt na antyau kartuḥ avacchinnasya etad ātma pradeśasya na bhoga āyatana loka prāptiḥ kiṃtu gatyā buddhyā avacchinnasya pradeśa antarasya vā iti svīkāre kṛta hāni ādi prasaṅgāt  kartuḥ bhoktuḥ ca avacchinnasya bhinna tvāt  abhinne vā anavacchinne kartṛtva ādi abhāvāt iti   ced na upādhigatyā upahite gati prayoga aupacārika eva na ca evam kṛta hāni ādi āpattiḥ yad buddhi avacchinnena yena eva ātmanā yad  kṛtam tad avacchinnena tena eva bhoga jananāt  na hi ātmanaḥ  niravayavasya pradeśaḥ asti yad tu avacchinnasya kartuḥ bhoktuḥ bheda iti uktam tad na avacchedya ātmanaḥ avacchedaka buddheḥ ca aikye avacchinne bhedasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  na ca ātma tvam aṇu niṣṭham dravyatva sākṣāya api ajāti tvāt pṛthivī tvavat iti anumānam vyāpaka āvṛtti tvasya upādhi tvāt sparśa ādi sāmāna adhikaraṇyasya api evam sādhana prasaṅgāt ca jīvaḥ  na vyāpakaḥ bhūtetara tve sati paratva asam avāyi kāraṇa anādhāra tve satya sarvajña tvāt śabda itara anitya viśeṣa guṇa āśraya tvāt saṃskāra āśraya tvāt ca ghaṭavat iti atra anātma tvam upādhiḥ anitya viśeṣa guṇa saṃskāra ādīnām upādhi vṛtti tvena asiddhiḥ ca evam mahat tvasya api su sādhana tvam ca jīvaḥ aṇuḥ jñāna asamavāyi kāraṇa saṃyoga āśraya tvāt manaḥvat  iti atra madhyama parimāṇava tvena manasaḥ  dṛṣṭānta asaṃpratipatteḥ jaḍa tvasya upādhi tvāt ca sarvatra ca atra vyāpi sukha jñāna ādi upalambhaḥ pratikūlaḥ tarkaḥ ekasya aṇoḥ ekadā vyavahita deśa dvaya avaccheda asaṃbhavena ‘pāde me sukham śirasi vedanā ityādi yugapad anubhava virodhaḥ ca na ca guṇinaḥ aṇu tve api guṇa vyāptyā vyāpi sukha jñāna anumāna virodhaḥ guṇa vyatirekeṇa asya asaṃbhāvita tvāt anyathā ghaṭa vyatirekeṇa api ghaṭa rūpam syāt  pradīpāt anyatra dṛśyamānā api prabhā na dīpa guṇaḥ kiṃtu anudbhūta sparśam dravya antaram na ca jāti samavāya ādeḥ dharmitaḥ anyatra vartamāna tvavat atra api guṇasya buddheḥ anyatra upalambhaḥ syāt  iti vācyam jāti samavāyādi vatra api tarhi vyāpakatva prasaṅgāt  dharmiṇaḥ  vihāya api sthitau tasyāḥ  niyāmaka abhāvāt na ca kāraṇa niyamāt niyamaḥ tarhi avyavahita samavāyi kāraṇa niyamāt eva niyame aṇu mātra deśa tā durvāra eva na ca vahneḥ auṣṇyam bahis na upalabhyeta samīpa vṛtti anudbhūta rūpa tejasaḥ tad iti ucyamāne vahneḥ auṣṇyam na sidhyet iti vācyam bādhake sati savidhe tejaḥ antara kalpane api dṛśyamāna vahnau  anubhūyamāna uṣṇa sparśe bādhaka abhāvena tasmin  tejaḥ ntaratva kalpanasya aśakya tvāt etena ketakī ādau paritas  gandha anubhavāt  guṇānām guṇinaiḥ apekṣyam na ca tatra ketakī ava yavānām paritas  prasaratām te gandhāḥ tarhi dravya kṣaya prasaṅgāt  na ca avayava antara praveśāt tad akṣayaḥ sphaṭika karaṇḍikā stha kastūrya ādau avayava antara praveśa kalpane māna abhāvāt iti nirastam samavāyinaiḥ apekṣye kāryasya nirāśrayatva āpattau tad pratyāsatti nibandhana kāraṇa antarasya api ucchede kāryatva hāneḥ eva tatra kalpanāyām māna tvāt  yad tu nityaḥ sarva gataḥ sthāṇuḥ iti atra ‘nitye sarva gate viṣṇau  aṇuḥ jīvaḥ  vyavasthitaḥ iti smṛti antara anusārāt sarva gata sthaḥ aṇuḥ ca iti vigrahaḥ iti tad na ‘a ākāśavat sarva gataḥ ca nityaḥ ‘sa vā eṣa mahān aja ātme ati śruti anusārī arthasya eva ucita tvāt aṇuḥ iti pada  chede tad virodha āpatteḥ yad tu krameṇa nānā deha saṃbandhāt aṇoḥ eva sarva gatatva uktiḥ iti tad na aśeṣa vāci sarva śabda saṅkoce māna abhāvāt yad api pratyakṣatva ādinā eva avyāpaka tvam sādhanīyam iti uktam tad na pratikūla tarkasya ukta tvāt vyāpakatva sādhane tasya eva anukūla tvena aprayojakatva abhāvāt ca nanu ātmanaḥ  vyāpaka tve ‘sarvāṇi śarīrāṇi sarvasya eva bhoga āyatanāni syuḥ sarva śarīra indriya ādīnām sarvadā sarva ātma saṃyukta tvāt karmaṇām api sādhāraṇa deha ādi kṛta tvena asādha araṇya ayogāt ahantu āra upādeḥ api niyāmaka mūla saṃbandha ādeḥ abhāvena naiyati āyogāt iti ced na tava api īśvarasya vyāpaka tvena sarva śarīrāṇām tad bhoga janakatva āpatteḥ samāna tvāt  na ca tad adṛṣṭa ajanya tvāt tad saṃyukta tve api na tatra bhoga jananam tarhi iha api samam na ca karmaṇām eva katham asādhāraṇyam pūrva tad karma janya tvāt  evam anādi tā eva anyathā īśa ātmani tava api agateḥ caitra bhoga janaka aṅkura ādeḥ tad adṛṣṭa janya tvāt ātma samavetasya adṛṣṭasya sākṣāt aṅkura asaṃbandhāt ātma dvāraka saṃbandhasya vācya tāyām ātmanaḥ  vibhu tvam na ca caitra bhoga ahetoḥ api aṅkura ādeḥ ātma dvārā adṛṣṭa saṃbandhe api tad ajanya tvena tasya atantra tvam iti vācyam janaka adṛṣṭa nirūpita ātma dvāraka sannikarṣasya atiprasaṅga abhāvena tantra tvāt janakatā tu adṛṣṭasya phala eka unneyā evam eva upapattau pratiyogi abhāva vācya vācaka jñāna jñeya ādau  iva adṛṣṭa kāryayoḥ api saṃbandha antara svīkāre māna abhāvaḥ yad tu kārīrya dṛṣṭasya vṛṣṭyā saha tad uddeśena vihita kriyā janyatva ādi rūpaḥ saṃbandhaḥ asti iti uktam tad na tatra api yajamāna ātma dvāraka saṃyukta samavāyasya eva jala kṣaraṇa ādi prayojaka tvāt  etad ca sarvam para rītya uktam sva mate ca vyavasthā prāk uktā eva tathā ca ‘buddheḥ guṇena ātma guṇena ca eva hi āra agra mātraḥ  hi avaraḥ api dṛṣṭa iti śrutau buddhi guṇenāra agra mātratva ukteḥ svābhāvikam eva vibhu tvam na ca atra ātma guṇenāra agra mātra tvam buddheḥ guṇena ca avara tvam iti vyutkrama yojanā tad yathā aṇunaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ prakāśaḥ  vyāptaḥ evam eva asya puruṣasya prakāśaḥ  vyāptaḥ aṇuḥ hi eva eṣa puruṣa iti śruti anusārāt iti vācyam vyāpakatva bodhaka aneka śruti virodhena buddheḥ guṇena iti etad anusāreṇa ca asyā eva aupādhika aṇutva paratvāt puruṣasya iti ṣaṣṭhyā arāhoḥ śira iti ādivat upacarita artha tvāt ca tathā ca na vyutkrameṇa anvayaḥ tasmāt aṇu tvam na ātma bhedakam iti advaita siddhau ātmanaḥ aṇutva bhaṅgaḥ sthitāni grantheṣu prakaṭam upadiṣṭāni gurubhiḥ guṇaḥ vā doṣaḥ  vā na mama para vākyāni vadataḥ param tu asmin  asti śrama phalam idam yad nija dhiyā śrutīnām yuktī nām akali guru vācām ca viṣayaḥ tṛtīyaḥ paricchedaḥ atha manana nididhi āsanayoḥ śravaṇa aṅgatva upapattiḥ tad evam aikātmye vyavasthite tad sākṣātkārāya śravaṇam aṅgi manana nididhi āsane tad aṅgatayā mumukṣubhiḥ anuṣṭheye tad uktam vivaraṇe ‘śravaṇam aṅgi pramāṇasya prameya avagamam pratyavyavadhānāt  manana nididhi āsane tu cittasya pratyagātma pravaṇa saṃskāra pariniṣpanna tad ekāgra vṛtti kārya dvāreṇa brahma anubhava hetu tām pratipadyete iti phala upakārī aṅge nanu śravaṇam tāvat vicāra rūpam śābda jñāne na karaṇam vedena dharma iva brahmaṇi pramīyamāṇe vicārasya anumāna ādau tarkasya iva śabda rūpe tad jñāna rūpe vā karaṇe itikartavya tā mātra tvāt iti ced na śabda śakti tātparya avadhāraṇam tāvat  vicāraḥ avadhṛta tātparyakaḥ ca śabdaḥ karaṇam iti vicārasya karaṇa koṭi praveśena iti kartavya tātva abhāvāt aṅgitva nirṇayāt  tad uktam vidyā sāgare anumitau liṅga jñānavat tātparya viśiṣṭa śabda jñānam karaṇam atas tāt parya avadhāraṇa rūpa vicārasya aṅgi tvam na ca ā kāṅkṣa ādi sahita śabda jñānasya eva karaṇatva saṃbhave tātparya bhrama nirāsa upakṣīṇa tayā ukta tātparyajñānasya karaṇa koṭi praveśe mananādeḥ api tad koṭi praveśaḥ syāt iti yuktam evam sa ākāṅkṣa ādi dhiyaḥ api nirākāṅkṣa ādi bhrama nirāsakatva mātreṇa upayoga āpattau ākāṅkṣādikam api karaṇa koṭi praviṣṭam na syāt  na ca anyonya āśrayaḥ sāmānyatas artha avagamanena tātparya graha saṃbhavāt anyathā nānā artha ādau vinigamana ādikam ca na syāt  tathā ca sarvatra tātparyajñānasya ājanaka tve api yatra tātpari saṃśaya viparyaya uttaram śābda dhīḥ tatra tātparyajñānasya hetu tā grāhyā saṃśaya viparyaya uttara pratyakṣe viśeṣa darśanasya iva ata eva na vivaraṇa virodhaḥ api nanu tātparyajñānasya karaṇa koṭi praveśe vede api tātparya bhram saṃbhavāt bāhya āgame api tātparya pramā saṃbhavāt  śābda jñāna karaṇasya duṣṭa tvāt uṣṭatva vyavasthā na syāt  iti ced na vede kadācid  kasyacid  kutracid tātparya bhrame api nirduṣṭa tvena yathārtha tātparyam asti eva para āgame tu pauruṣeya tayā pratāraṇa ādimad puruṣa praṇīta tayā duṣṭa tvena na tathā iti duṣṭa tvāt uṣṭatva vyavasthā saṃbhavāt tātparya aṃśasya avaghāta ādeḥ iva yāge śabde sannipatya upakāraka tayā karaṇa koṭi praviṣṭa tvena aṅgi tvam na ca dṛṣṭānte karaṇa dravya śeṣa tvāt tathā sarva sāmyasya dṛṣṭāntatva aprayojaka tvāt  nanu sannipatya upakāraka tve api na phala upakāraka manana nididhi āsana rūpa aṅgam prati śeṣitā anyathā prayāja ādikam pratyavaghāta ādiḥ śeṣī syāt iti ced na viśiṣṭa yāga praviṣṭa tayā śeṣi tve iṣṭa āpatteḥ asādhāraṇyena śeṣitā tu asādhāraṇa phala upakāraka tve syāt  asaṃbhāvanā viśeṣa nivṛtti rūpa asādhāraṇa upakāra janaka tvāt  sā api śravaṇasya saṃbhāvitā eva ata eva uktam cit sukha ācāryaiḥ   karaṇībhūta śabda gata atiśaya hetu tvāt śravaṇasya karaṇa tvena aṅgi tvam manana nididhi āsanayoḥ tu sahakāri bhūta citta gata atiśaya hetu tvāt phala upakāri aṅgatā iti na ca evam soma yāga sahakāri bhūta dīkṣaṇīya ādi aṅgasya tad gata atiśaya hetu abhiṣava grahaṇa ādikam pratyaṅgatva prasaṅga iti vācyam pūrvavat ukta uttara tvāt  tad uktam tava śuddhau ‘karaṇībhūta śabda dharma śakti tātparya viṣaya tvāt śravaṇasya karaṇa antarbhāvena aṅgitvam iti na ca śabdena aparokṣa jñaptau apratiruddha aparokṣa jñaptau ca utpādyāyām manana nididhi āsanayoḥ iva parokṣa jñaptau  apratiruddha parokṣa jñaptau ca utpādyāyām śravaṇasya api apekṣita tayā trayāṇām api phala upakārī aṅga tvam eva iti katham paraspara aṅga aṅgibhāva iti vācyam manana nididhi āsane phale janayitavye śabdasya sahakāriṇam sampādayataḥ śravaṇam tu tasya janakatām eva iti viśeṣāt  yatra ca na evam tatra tulyavat aṅga tā eva etena ayaḥ  vṛṣṭi kāmaḥ  yaḥ annādya kāmaḥ  yaḥ svarga kāmaḥ sa saubhareṇa stuvīta hīṣiti vṛṣṭi kāmāya nidhanam kuryāt  ūrgiti annādya kāmāya ū iti svarga kāmāye ati śrutānām vṛṣṭi ādi phalāya saubhara iti kartavyatā nidhana gata hīṣa ādīnām śravaṇa manana ādivat  parasparam aṅga aṅgi bhāva prasaṅga iti nirastam karaṇa svarūpa saṃpādakatva sahakāri saṃpādakatva rūpa tad prayojakasya atra iva tatra abhāvāt na ca evam karaṇa apūrva utpattau yāga arthasya avaghāta ādeḥ parama apūrva utpattau tad arthaḥ prayāja ādiḥ śeṣaḥ syāt iti vācyam ekaphala ubhayoḥ yāga arthatva abhāvena viśeṣāt  nanu klṛptam parokṣa jñānam loke śabdasya phalam tathā ca śabda atiśaya ādhāyakasya śravaṇasya sākṣātkāra phala janaka aṅgi tvam katham iti ced  sākṣāt tvam na jātiḥ navā indriya janyatva ādikam niyāmakam kiṃtu viṣaya gata ajñāna nivartaka tvam eva aparokṣa tve prayojakam tathā ca ajñāna nivartaka tvam viṣaya paryanta tvena tad ca ātma paryanta tvāt atra asti eva iti na aṭaṣṭa kalpanā ittham ca prakaraṇa balāt api siddham asya aṅgi tvam śravaṇasya phala saṃbandhena prādhānya siddhau  itikartavya tā kāṅkṣāyāḥ saṃbhavāt  nanu yadi api na citta aikāgryasya sūkṣma vastu jñāna hetu tvam dṛṣṭam asti tathā api mananam na citta aikāśya hetu yukti anusandhāna rūpa mananasyā yuktatva śaṅkā nivartaka tāyā eva dṛṣṭa tvena citta aikāśya hetutva kalpane sati dṛṣṭā ahāni āpatteḥ manana vidheḥ pūrva vidhitva apātāt ca ‘matiḥ yāvat ayukta te ti smṛti virodhāt ca iti ced na tādṛś chaṅkāyām satyām nānā koṭau citta vikṣepasya tasyāḥ ca nivṛttau yukta tvena avadhāraṇa viṣaya koṭau citta pravaṇa tāyāḥ tāvat paryanta tvasya dṛṣṭa tvena dṛṣṭa hānya pūrva vidhi smṛti virodha abhāvāt nididhi āsanasya tu viparīta bhāvanā nivartaka tā sakala siddhā nanu tad nivṛtteḥ na jñāna hetu tā dṛṣṭā rūpya saṃskāra anuvṛttau  api śukti sākṣātkāra darśanāt iti ced  ‘iyam śuktiḥ i ati jñāna anantaram tad rajata tayā jñātam iti smṛteḥ jñāna gocara saṃskāra sattve api tad rajatam iti asmaraṇena viparīta saṃskāra nivṛtteḥ tatra api sattvāt  nanu śabda sāmarthya rūpeṇa liṅgena atatas tu tam paśyate niṣkalam dhyāyamāna ityādi vākyena nididhi āsanasya phala saṃbandhāt  prakaraṇena ca śravaṇa ādikam nididhi āsane sannipatya aṅgam iti ced na nididhi āsana padasya barhiḥ deva sadanam iti ādau  iva sākṣātkāra rūpa phala saṃvandhe na śaktiḥ iti śabda sāmarthya abhāvāt vākye api yogya tā āvolāt śravaṇam eva adhyāhriyate tathā ca tad śravaṇāt dhyāyamānaḥ  niṣkalam brahma paśyati iti anukūla arthasya eva paryavasānāt  tasmāt  ‘draṣṭavyaḥ śrotavya iti darśanena avyavahita pāṭha rūpa sannidhānāt śravaṇasya darśanena sākṣāt anvayāt aṅgi tvam nididhi āsana rūpa bhāvanā prakarṣa janya tve sākṣātkara asya kāminī sākṣāt kāravat apramātvā apātaḥ na ca mūla pramāṇa dārḍhyāt pramātvam tarhi tad eva sākṣātkaraṇam astu kim tad upajīvi nyāyena etena nididhi āsana saha kṛta manaḥ karaṇa tvam api nirastam iti advaita siddhau manana nididhi āsanayoḥ śravaṇa aṅga tvam atha vivaraṇa ukta niyama upapattiḥ tad ca śravaṇa ādikam viṣaya avagamam pratyanvaya vyatireka siddha upāya iti tadvidheḥ na apūrva vidhi tvam kiṃtu niyama vidhi tvam eva nanu atra śravaṇasya aparokṣa phalam prati sādhana tvam tad ca anyatas  na avagatam iti apūrva vidhi tvam iti ced na gāndharva śāstra vicāre ṣaḍja ādi sākṣātkāre hetu tāyā dṛṣṭa tvāt  na ca etāvatā śāstra vicāraḥ sarvatra artha sākṣātkāra hetuḥ iti na siddham dharma śāstra vicāre vyabhicārāt iti vācyam aparokṣa arthaka śāstra vicāra tvena sākṣātkāra janaka tāyāḥ tad darśana balena siddheḥ ātmā ca ṣaḍja ādivat aparokṣaḥ na dharma ādiḥ na ca aparokṣe vicāra vaiyarthyam na hi yadi aparokṣam tad tad vicāryata iti niyama iti vācyam aparokṣe vicāryatva niyama abhāvavat avicāryatva niyamaḥ api na asti ṣaḍja ādau  aparokṣe api vicāryatva darśanāt  tadvat eva sāphalya saṃbhavāt ca sandigdhatva saprayojana tvayoḥ eva sarvatra vicārya tve prayojaka tvāt  etena vicārya śāstra arthasya sākṣātkāra yogyasya sākṣātkāre sa hetuḥ iti na yujyate kāla antare sākṣāt kariṣyamāṇa tvena tad yogye vicārya śāstra arthe svarga nidhi ādau vicāreṇa tad abhāvāt iti nirastam nidhi ādi sākṣatkāre tad asat nikarṣāt ajāte api vicārasya tad hetu tā na gacchati tatra vicāra indriya sahakāri tvena tad vilambena vilambāt  prakṛte tu śābda tvāt  sākṣātkārasya na tad apekṣā aparokṣa yogya artha sākṣātkāra tvena kāryatvasya tādṛśa arthaka śāstra vicāra tvena sādhana tvasya sattvāt  etena prakṛta kārya vijātīya kārye prakṛta vicāra vijātīya vicārasya hetu tāklṛpti mātreṇa tasya apūrva vidhitva tyāge apūrva vidhi mātra uccheda āpāta iti nirastam nanu pākṣika prāptau niyamaḥ sā ca sādhana antara prāptau na ca rūpa ādi rahita ātma jñāne tad prāptiḥ asti iti ced na nirviśeṣa ātmani māna antara aprāptau  api ātmani sāmānyatas tad prāptiḥ asti iti niyama saṃbhavāt  yathā apūrvīyeṣu vrīhi viśeṣeṣu nakha vidala na ādeḥ aprāptau  api vrīhi sāmānye tad prāptyā vrīhīn avahanti iti niyama vidhiḥ nanu vrīhīn avahanti iti atra vrīhi padam apūrvīya dravya param na tu vrīhi mātra param anyathā yaveṣu avaghāta aupadeśikaḥ  na syāt  nīvāreṣu ca vrīhitvā abhāvena atidiṣṭaḥ api bādhyeta iti navame sthāpita tvena āpūrvīya dravya eva nakha vidalana ādi prāptiḥ vaktavyā anyathā vaituṣya mātre avaghāta niyame dravya arjane yājana ādi upāya niyamavat  tasya puruṣa arthatva prasaṅgena laukikeṣu api vrīhiṣu dalane pratyaveyāt iti ced na niyamyamāna avaghātasya āpūrvīya dravya mātra viṣaya tve api sāmānya viṣaya ka prāptyā eva niyama upapattau viśeṣa viṣaya prāpteḥ anapekṣita tvāt  na ca nirviśeṣa sa viśeṣa rūpa viśiṣṭa dvaya anugate viśeṣa abhāva ādi dvārā vedānta vedye cit mātre na māna antara prāptiḥ iti vācyam ubhaya anugate sa viśeṣa tayā prameya tāyām māna antara prāpteḥ sattvāt  sajātīye prāptyā api yatra sajātīya antare niyama saṃbhavaḥ tadā kim u vācyam ekasmin  eva ātmani avasthā viśeṣeṇa māna antara prāptyā viśeṣa antare niyama iti na ca evam viśeṣa antare prāptyā viśeṣa antara niyame vaiyadhikaraṇyam iti vācyam vyakti sāmāna adhikaraṇyā abhāve api ananya gatyā sāmānya dharmam ādāya sāmānādhikaraṇya aṅgīkārāt  nanu atra ani ā eva gatiḥ asti apūrvīyavrīhiṣu niyama adṛṣṭa ajanakasya api dalanasya prāptiḥ asti na hi yatra tena vaituṣya sampādanam tatra tad prāptiḥ kiṃtu śakta tvena prasakti mātram iti ced na evam tad yogya tvam iti paryavasitaḥ arthaḥ tad ca tad jātīye anvayī na tu tatra tathā ca vaiyadhikaraṇya tādavasthyam prakṛte ca sa viśeṣa nirviśeṣa rūpa daśā dvaya anugata eka ātma viṣaya tayā vaiyadhi karaṇya śaṅkā anavakāśaḥ ca tattva kaumudīkṛtaḥ tu  yathā mantra artha jñānasya kalpa sūtra ātmīya grāhaka vākyādinā api prāpta tvena pakṣe aprāpta mantra sādhya tvam niyamyate mantraiḥ eva smṛtiḥ sādhyeti tathā vedānta mūla strī śūdra sādhāraṇa smṛti purāṇa ādi prāptyā pakṣe aprāpta vedānta śravaṇa ādi paripūraṇa arthe niyamaḥ atasmāt  na brāhmaṇaḥ avaidikam adhīyīta iti śruteḥ ‘śrotavyaḥ śruti vākyebhyaḥ ityādi smṛteḥ ce ati āhuḥ na ca ‘iti hāsa purāṇābhyām vedam samupabṛṃhaye aditya ādi smṛti virodhaḥ avicārite upabṛṃhaṇa ayogāt iti vācyam vedānta tātpari nirṇayāya tad vicāra apekṣāyām api brahma jñāne tad vicāra apekṣā virahāt na ca karma viṣaya ka smṛtibhiḥ karma jñānasya iva brahma viṣayāt  bhārata ādeḥ itihāsāt api sākṣāt brahma jñānasya udayāt brahma jñāne api tad apekṣā iti vācyam ubhayatra api smṛti ādeḥ svātantryeṇa apramāṇa tayā śruti tātparya nirṇāyaka tvāt  ataeva uktaṃ ‘ vedam samupabṛṃhayet i ati na tu veda artham jānīyāt iti yad tu  aśrotavyaḥ śruti vākyebhyaḥ iti ādikam śruti mūla pramāṇa abhiprāyakam  iti tad na pañcamī pratīta hetutvasya sākṣāt  saṃbhave pāramparya kalpanā yogāt na ca viprakīrṇa nānā śākhā artha saṃgraha ādi rūpeṇa itihāsa ādinā tattva niścaya darśanāt sati ca tasmin vividiṣā dvārā tad arthāya antaḥkaraṇa śuddheḥ anapekṣita tvāt  āparokṣyasya viṣaya bhāvāt eva siddhyā veda janya brahma jñāne itihāsa janyāt adhikasya aparokṣyasya ananubhavena tasya niyama adṛṣṭa asādhya tvāt jñānasya ca sva prāgabhāva nivartana iva ajñāna nivartane adṛṣṭa nirapekṣa tvāt  anyasya ca niyama adṛṣṭa sādhyasya abhāvāt  na niyama vidhiḥ iti vācyam ‘tam etam veda anuvacanene ati ādi śruti balāt  yajña ādi janya adṛṣṭasya niyama adṛṣṭasya ca vividiṣā dvāraka antaḥkaraṇa śuddheḥ eva sarva adṛṣṭa sādhyāyāḥ saṃbhavena jñāna svarūpa upakāri tayā tad sādhya ajñāna nivṛttau tad apekṣa tvāt ca vidyā yukta tad ayukta karma janya phala gata cira acira svarūpa atiśayavat  niyama adṛṣṭa janya sākṣātkāre tad ajanya tattva niścaya apekṣayā atiśaya kalpanasya āvaśyaka tvāt ca niyama vidhitva saṃbhavāt  tasmāt  niyama adṛṣṭa sādhyasya vyāvartyasya api saṃbhavāt  śravaṇa ādeḥ niyamanam sarvathā eva upapadyate iti ata eva śūdra praṇīta ātma prabandha ādi prāpti nimittaka aprāpta aṃśa pūraṇa arthaḥ  niyama vidhiḥ iti ācārya antara uktiḥ api vyākhyātā iti vivaraṇa ukta niyama upapattiḥ atha śravaṇa ādeḥ vidheyatva upapattiḥ nanu kim idam śravaṇam nāma śakti tātparya avadhāraṇam vā tad viśiṣṭa śabda avadhāraṇam vā tātparya pramāpaka liṅga avadhāraṇam vā āgama ācārya upadeśa jajñānam vā na ādyaḥ avācye brahmaṇi śakti asaṃbhavāt  tātparyam api na tāvat āpāta dhī janyasya vicāra nivartyasya saṃśayasya dharmiṇi tasya prāk eva niścita tvena tad niścaya artham tātparya niścaya sādhanasya vicārasya vaiyarthyāt  anyathā vicāra anantaram api saṃśaya ādi prasaṅgāt  na api saṃśaya dharmi gata prakāra viśeṣe tad viśiṣṭe tad upalakṣite vā akhaṇḍa artha tā hāneḥ avadhāraṇasya jñāna tve vidheya tvasya tvayā anaṅgīkārāt  ata eva na dvitīya ādi na api guru mukhāt vedāntānām brahmaṇi saṃyojanam śravaṇam tasya ādya pakṣān atirekāt na api vākya viśeṣa prayoga rūpa vāda kathā śravaṇam tatra śravaṇa padā prayogāt  ataeva manana nididhi āsanayoḥ api na vidhiḥ tayoḥ api jñāna anatirekāt iti   ced na ādya pakṣasya eva kṣoda kṣama tvāt  na ca tatra śabda śakti asaṃbhavaḥ  doṣaḥ śuddhe śakti asaṃbhave api viśiṣṭa śakteḥ tad bodha upayoginyā avadhāraṇīyāyāḥ saṃbhavāt  tātparyasya api saṃśaya dharmiṇaḥ  niścita tvena tatra asaṃbhave api saṃśaya koṭi upalakṣite nirviśeṣe saṃbhavena vicāra avaii arthyāt  na ca akhaṇḍa artha tā hāniḥ sva rūpa mātra upalakṣaka tayā akhaṇḍa artha tāyāḥ  upapādita tvāt  na ca avadhāraṇasya jñāna rūpa tayā avidheya tā tasya tarka tvena jñāna vijātīya cetaḥ vṛtti antara tvāt sureśvara ācāryaiḥ ‘śravaṇa ādi kriyā tāvat  kartavyā iha prayatna ta iti śravaṇa ādau kriyā pada prayogāt  evam eva manana nididhi āsanayoḥ api vidheya tvam unneyam na ca tātparya rūpe viṣaye upakrama ādi rūpe ca pramāṇe sati jāyamānasya tasya jñāna bahis bhāva anupapattiḥ tad bahis bhūta vāc dhenu upāsana ādau pramāṇa vastu paratantratva adarśanāt iti   vācyam mad mate liṅgasya prāmāṇya anabhyupagamena sati pramāṇa iti asya eva abhāvāt upakrama ādeḥ pramāṇatva pakṣe tad pūrva kālīna tvena asya pramāṇe sati iti etad aṃśa asiddheḥ tasmāt  śravaṇa ādeḥ adhīrūpa tayā manaḥ vyāpāra tvena vidheyatva upapattiḥ siddhānta bindu kalpa latikayoḥ vistaraḥ yad ca anuvāditva ādi varṇanam vācaspatye tad  prasthāna antara tvāt na vidhi tvā ukti virodhi iti advaita siddhau śravaṇa ādeḥ vidheyatva upapattiḥ atha jijñāsā sūtrasya śravaṇa vidhi mātra mūlaka tvam evam vicāra vidhāyaka śravaṇa vidhiḥ eva jijñāsā sūtra mūlam na ca vicāra vidhau śravaṇa sādhya aparokṣa jñāna adhīnāyāḥ  aparokṣa jñāna kāmanāyā adhikāri viśeṣaṇatva aṅgīkāreṇa anyonya āśraya āpāta iti vācyam adhīta vedasya vidita pada padārtha saṅgatikasya āpātatas  jāyamāna parokṣa jñāna adhīna aparokṣa jñāna kāmanāyāḥ  adhikāri viśeṣaṇa tvena ukta anyonya āśrayān avatārāt  na ca jijñāsā sūtra uktaḥ  vicāraḥ tattva nirṇāyaka nyāya anusandhāna rūpaḥ anyathā nyāya grathana ātmaka śāstra ārambha siddhaye tad kartavya tokti ayukteḥ itarasya veda iti kartavya tātva anupapatteḥ ca śravaṇam ca na ukta nyāya anusandhāna rūpam mananābheda prasaṅgāt  atas  na śravaṇa vidhi jijñāsā sūtrayoḥ mūla mūli bhāva iti   vācyam jijñāsā sūtrasya śravaṇa vidhi samāna viṣaya ka tayā mūla mūli bhāva abhāve api śravaṇa vidhi viṣaya śakti tātparya avadhāraṇa ātmaka śravaṇa ākṣipta upakrama upasaṃhāra ādi tātparya liṅga vicāram ādāya samāna viṣayatva saṃbhavena tad upapatteḥ mananam tu śrutasya arthasya yuktibhiḥ cintanam iti na tad abhedaḥ api artha ākṣipta vicārasya iti kartavyatā tve api tātparya avadhāraṇa rūpe śravaṇe uktasya aṅgitvasya anapāyāt yad tu yuktibhiḥ anucintanam nāma yadi śravaṇa niścitasya tātparyasya tad viṣaya śabdasya vā smaraṇam pratyabhijñānam vā saṃskāra dārḍhya phalakam śravaṇa samāna ākāram abhijñā antaram vā tarhi tasya āvaśyaka śravaṇa āvṛttyā eva siddheḥ manana vidhi vaiyarthyam trividhasya api tasya śravaṇa anantargata yukti anapekṣa tvena ‘śrotavyaḥ śruti vākyebhyaḥ  mantavyaḥ ca upapattibhiḥ i ati smṛti virodhaḥ ca ‘śravaṇam yāvat ajñānam matiḥ yāvat ayukta tā iti mananasya śravaṇa anivartitā yuktatva śaṅkā nivartakatva pratipādaka smṛti virodhaḥ ca iti tad na anucintanasya śruta artha viṣaya ka yuktā yuktatva ādi saṃśaya nivartaka yukti anusandhāna rūpa tvena vivakṣita tayā tvad ukta doṣān avakāśāt na ca evam yukta ayuktatva saṃśaya ādeḥ saṃśaya pūrva pakṣa siddhāntāt mīmāṃsā śāstra grathitāt saṃśaya ādi nivartakāt nyāya jātāt anyena anivṛtteḥ tādṛśa nyāya grathana ātmaka mīmāṃsā śāstra ārambha upayukta vicāra kartavyatām pratipādayat ādi sūtram manana vidhi mūlam eva syāt  na tu śravaṇa vidhi mūlam iti vācyam tātparya viṣaya yuktā yuktatva ādi saṃśaya ādi nivartaka vicāra apekṣayā tātparya nirṇāyaka śravaṇa ākṣipta liṅga vicārasya abhyarhita tayā tad ākṣepaka śravaṇa vidhi mūla tvasya eva vaktum śakya tvāt  yukta ayuktatva vicārasya anuṣaṅgika tvāt ca yad vā samanvaya adhyāya ukta tātparya niścāyaka upakrama ādi yukti anusandhānam śravaṇam dvitīya adhyāya ukta artha asattva śaṅkā nivartaka yukti anusandhānam mananam nanu evam vivaraṇa ukti virodhaḥ yauktikā saṃbhāvanā viparīta bhāvanā nirāsi tarkāṇām prathama jñāna antarbhūta tvāt ityādinā arthāpattīnām api śravaṇa antar gatim uktvā  brahma ātmatva viparīta bhāvanā pracaya nimitta tad ekāgra vṛtti ayogya tvam asaṃbhāvanā viparīta bhāvanā tu śarīra adhyāsa saṃskāra pracayaḥ  ityādinā asaṃbhāvanā nivartakasya mananasya artha niścaya anantara bhāvi bhāvanā pracaya hetu citta ekāgrya hetu tāyā eva ukta tvāt iti ced na bhinna prasthāna tayā vivaraṇa virodhasya akiṃcitkara tvāt na ca jijñāsā sūtrasya aṃśe manana vidhi mūlatva apātaḥ samanvaya ukta vicārasya abhyarhita tayā śravaṇa vidhi mūla tvasya eva vaktavyatva upapatteḥ nanu ‘mantavyaḥ ca upapattibhiḥ iti smṛti gata upapatti śabdasya matiḥ yādava yukta tā iti smṛti sthā yukta śabdasya ‘śrotavyaḥ śruti vākyebhyaḥ iti śruti śabdasya iva sāmānya paratva ahānena ‘a ādau yad śraddhayā siddham paścāt nyāyena sādhitam iti nyāyena yukti anapekṣa śraddhā mātreṇa prativākyam ayam asya vākyasya artha  iti guru mukhāt veda artha grahaṇam śravaṇam paścāt  nyāya anusandhānam mananam iti bheda saṃbhave yuktiṣu eva śravaṇa mananabheda kathana ayoga iti   ced na vākya artha grahaṇasya prama rūpa tayā avidheya tvasya ukta tvāt  nanu—uktasya vākya artha grahaṇasya śravaṇa ādi traya anantarbhāve caturthasya api mumukṣu anuṣṭheyatva āpāta iti ced na tasya jñāna rūpa tayā anuṣṭhānān arha tvāt śraddhā mātrāt  svata eva jāta tvena apuṃtantra tvāt ca na ca evam kevalam guru mukhāt tad artham śrutavati śrutam anena iti prayoga anupapattiḥ vidheya tvāni athā anupapattyā artha antara tve sthite asya prayogasya gauṇa tā ādinā kathaṃcid upapādanīya tvāt ataeva smṛti gata upapatti ayukta tā padayoḥ na sāmānya para tā na ca pramāṇa bhūta śruti tātparye niścite artha sattva artham upapatti apekṣā yogena mananasya artha asattva rūpā prāmāṇya śaṅkā nivartaka tve vaktavye niścita prāmāṇyasya puṃsaḥ mananā bhāva prasaṅga iti vācyam tādṛśam prati tad abhāvasya iṣṭa tvāt  kṛṣṇale atideśa prāptasya avaghātasya dvāra bādhena bādha darśanāt  tasmāt tātparya avadhāraṇam śravaṇam tad ca liṅga vicāra adhīnam iti vicāra kartavyatā parama ādya sūtram śravaṇa vidhi mūlakam na tu manana vidhi mūlakam iti siddham jijñāsā sūtrasya śravaṇa vidhi mātra mūlaka tvam iti advaita siddhau jijñāsā sūtrasya śravaṇa vidhi mātra mūlakatva upapattiḥ atha vicārasya śravaṇa vidhi mūlatva upapattiḥ nanu tvad mate karma kāṇḍa vicāraḥ  yathottara kratu vidhi prayuktaḥ tathā brahma kāṇḍa vicāraḥ api jñāna vidhi prayukta iti eva kim na syāt  uttara kratu vidhibhiḥ sva anuṣṭhāpya artha nirṇaya anta vicārasya iva ‘tarati śokam ātma vidi atyādinā śoka nivṛtti hetu tvena avagatena ātma jñānena sva siddhaye vedānta vicārasya ākṣepāt  yuktam ca anekeṣām kratu vidhīnām ākṣepaka tvāt api ekasya eva ākṣepaka tvam iti ced na yadi api kāryeṇa kāraṇa ākṣepaḥ saṃbhavati tathā api tasya vaidhatva siddhi artham vidhi mūla tvasya avaśyam vaktavya tvāt anyathā karma kāṇḍa vicārasya api karma jñānāt eva ākṣepe adhyayana vidheḥ vā uttara kratu vidhīnām vā ākṣepakatva uktiḥ ayuktā syāt  manana vidhi mūla tvam vadatā tvayā api asya ākṣepasya avaśyam pariharaṇīya tvāt  etena artha avagama paryanta adhyayana vidhi prayukta tvasya karma vicāravat  brahma vicāre api saṃbhave na śravaṇa vidhi prayukta tvam na ca sākṣātkāra phala kam āvṛtti guṇakam anana ādi aṅgakam idam śravaṇam adhyayana vidhi prayukta śravaṇa mātrāt bhinnam iti vidhi antaram yuktam iti vācyam brahma vicārasya api adhyayana vidhi prayukta tve api sākṣātkārasya aparokṣa ekarasa ātma viṣaya tvena eva siddheḥ āvṛtteḥ ca vidhi antara aṅgīkāre api avaghātavat adṛṣṭa phala tvena vaktavya tvāt karma kāṇḍe api tātparya avadhāraṇa paryanta vicāra āvṛtteḥ apekṣita tvāt  tatas  param brahmakāṇḍe api tadā vṛtteḥ anapekṣita tvāt mananasya ca karma kāṇḍe api tad artha niścayāya apekṣita tvāt adhyayana vidhi vihita eka deśa āraṇyaka adhyayana anuvādena vākya antareṇa araṇya ādi aṅga antara vidhānavat muṇḍaka kārīryādi adhyayana anuvādena śiraḥ vrata bhūmi bhojana ādi aṅga vidhānavat ‘tām caturbhiḥ ādatta iti artha prāpta abhyādāna anuvādena saṃkhyā vidhānavat ca adhyayana vidhi ākṣipta vicāra eka deśa anuvādena tu ad rītyā manana ādi aṅga vidhānasya saṃbhavāt iti nirastam manana vidhi mūlatva vādinaḥ api samāna tvāt adhyayana vidheḥ svādhyāya avāpti phalaka tayā artha jñāna phalakatva abhāvāt adhyetavya iti karma pradhāna tavya pratyayena svādhyāyasya eva phalatva avagamāt na ca tasya apuruṣa artha tayā phalavat artha avabodha paryantam vyāpāraḥ ‘citrayā yajeta paśu kāma iti ādau  api kāmyamāna paśu ādeḥ api aphalatva āpatteḥ paraṃparayā puruṣa artha sādhana tayā phalatve prakṛte api tasya saṃbhavāt  tasmāt śravaṇa vidhi mūlam vicāra vidhāyaka jijñāsā sūtrasya na tu manana vidhiḥ iti siddham iti advaita siddhau vicārasya śravaṇa vidhi mūlatva upapattiḥ atha vācaspati ukta svādhyāya vidhi vicāra ākṣepakatvasya upapattiḥ prasthāna antare tu adhyayana vidheḥ eva avagama paryanta tvāt  kāṇḍa dvaya vicāra ākṣepaka tvam śravaṇa ādiṣu ca na vidhiḥ teṣām anvaya vyatireka siddha sākṣātkāra sādhana tāka tvāt iti uktam na ca adhyayana abhāve pratyavāya śravaṇa adhyayanasya nityatāyāḥ  api avagamāt katham tasya artha avagama paryanta tvam iti vācyam artha jñāna artha tve api adhyayana vidhera vaiyarthyāya adhītena eva vedena kartavyatām jñātvā anuṣṭhitam karma phalāya alam ityādi niyama āśrayaṇāt asati adhyayane yathā ukta nitya ādi karma anuṣṭhāna asiddhyā pratyavāya śravaṇa upapattiḥ tathā ca artha jñāna arthasya api adhyayanasya phalataḥ nitya tvam iti kecid  aparetu  ana dhyayane saṃdhyā anupāsana iva sākṣāt  pratyavāya śravaṇena adhyayanasya adṛṣṭa tve api artha jñānasya api dṛṣṭa tvāt apekṣita tvāt ca tādarthyam api iti ubhaya artha tā paśu puroḍāśa ādivat iti  āhuḥ atra ca adhyayana vidheḥ nitya tve sati ubhaya vicāra ākṣepaka tvam pareṇa api aṅgīkṛtam tad ayuktam jijñāsā sūtrasya manana vidhi mūlatva vādinaḥ tasya tad aṅgīkārān arha tvāt ayuktatva śaṅkā nivartaka manana rūpa vicārasya api adhyayana vidhi ākṣipta tvena tatra vidhi vaiyarthāt  sūtrasya tad mūlatva asiddheḥ iti advaita siddhau vācaspati ukta svādhyāya vidhi vicāra ākṣepakatvasya upapattiḥ atha jñānasya puruṣa tantra tā bhaṅgaḥ yad tu śabda ja jñāna svarūpam eva śravaṇam vidheyam iti tad na āpāta darśanasya tad vinā jāyamāna tvāt  na ca tad bhinne prativākyam asya vākyasya ayam artha iti siddhārtha ukta rūpa guru upadeśena aneka śākhā stha vākya artha jñānam vedānta rūpa vākya artha vicārasya sāmānyatas  sādhana tvena prāpta tvāt  na ca yathā ghaṭa ādau  itara bhede siddhe api pṛthivī itarebhyaḥ  bhidyata iti atra na siddha sādhanam yathā ca sthāna prakaraṇa adhikaraṇa ukta rītyā rājasūya antargata iṣṭi paśu someṣu prātisvika rūpeṇa ca udakata iti kartavya tā prāptau  api rājasūya rūpe tad aprāptiḥ tathā vedānta vicāratva upahite brahma jñāna hetu tāyāḥ  aprāpteḥ apūrva vidhitā iti vācyam sāmānyatas  prāpta sādhana sādhya bhāvam anādṛtya viśeṣa upādhinā aprāpta sādhanatva prāptaye apūrva vidhi aṅgīkāre jyotiṣṭoma ādi vākya vicāre api tena rūpeṇa tad vākya artha jñānam pratyaprāpta sādhana tā siddhaye apūrva vidhi antara kalpanā patteḥ etena nididhi āsanasya avyakta svabhāva brahma sākṣātkāra hetu tā na anyatas  prāptā iti sa tāvat apūrva vidhiḥ tathā ajñāta ādau nididhi āsana asaṃbhavena śravaṇa mananayoḥ nididhyāsane liṅgāt eva prāptau  api niyata viṣayaka nididhi āsana viṣaya guṇāni aguṇeṣu liṅgena tayoḥ aprāpteḥ tad vidhiḥ api apūrva vidhiḥ eva evam ca śravaṇa mananayoḥ nididhyāsitavya guṇa aṃśe dṛṣṭa dvāreṇa anyatra tu adṛṣṭa dvāreṇa nididhi āsana aṅgatā iti nirastam śravaṇa ādīnām nirguṇa viṣaya tayā sa guṇa viṣayatva abhāvāt viparīta aṅga aṅgi bhāvasya sthāpita tvāt ca sūkṣma artha gocara nididhi āsanasya tādṛśa artha viṣayaka sākṣātkāra hetu tāyā dṛṣṭa tvena apūrvatva abhāvāt ca nanu atra śrūyamāṇa liṅga ādeḥ kā gatiḥ iti ced  śilā tala prayukta kṣura taikṣṇyavat kuṇṭhī bhāvāt  jartilayavāgvā vā juhuyāt iti ādau  iva artha vāda tvam eva na ca  pratni avekṣitam ājyam bhavati ‘viduṣā karma kartavyam tasmāt  paśyeta nityaśas  ityādinā jñānasya api vidhānam dṛṣṭam iti   vācyam tatra tad hetu indriya saṃyoga ādeḥ vidheya tvāt  ananya gatyā lakṣaṇāyāḥ  iṣṭa tvāt  na ca ana vidhau paraḥ śabda artha iti anena virodhaḥ ‘gobhiḥ śrīṇīta matsara am iti ādau vidhi vākye api lakṣaṇa adarśanena tasya autsargika tvāt artha vāda anurodhena vidhau na paraḥ śabda artha iti arthaka tvāt ca na ca sākṣātkṛta sādhya tvasya indriya saṃprayoge api abhāvāt indriya niṣṭha kriyā dvārā paraṃparayā kṛti sādhya tvasya jñāne api saṃbhavāt  anicchataḥ  durgandha ādi jñānavat aniṣṭa saṃprayogasya api darśanāt ca jñāna sāmyam saṃyogasya iti vācyam svarga ādau  iva sva icchā dhīna kṛti sādhya tvasya vidheya tā prayojakasya jñāne abhāvāt  saṃprayogasya tu tad vaiparītyena viśeṣāt  na ca ‘bhakṣehī ati bhakṣa mantreṣu tṛpteḥ anuniṣpāditayā ananuṣṭheya tvena tṛpti prakāśaka bhāgasya tatra vibhajya viniyoga abhāve api avekṣaṇasya anuṣṭheya tvāt  tad prakāśaka bhāgasya avekṣaṇe viniyoga iti tṛtīyā adhyāya ukti virodha iti vācyam indriya saṃprayoga rūpa avekṣaṇasya tṛpti ādivat anuniṣpāditva abhāvena anuṣṭheya tayā tad prakāśaka bhāgasya tasmin vibhajya viniyoga iti evaṃpara tvāt yad ca  eka śrotra gata aneka gakāreṣu bubhutsā prayatnābhyām abhīṣṭa gakāra jñāna darśanena jñānasya api vidheya tvam iti tad na anabhimata viṣaya vaimukhyasya eva bubhutsā prayatna sādhya tayā jñānam prati tayoḥ ajanaka tvāt  na ca  ayat eva vidyayā karotī ati vidyāyā aṅgatva śravaṇāt  avihitasya ca aṅgatva anupapattyā vidyāyā vidheya tvam iti vācyam tasya vākyasya udgītha upāsanā prakaraṇa stha tayā tatratī avidyā padasya upāsana apara tayā vihita tvena aṅgatva avirodhāt  ‘tad nirdhāraṇā niyamaḥ tad dṛṣṭeri atyatra vidyāyā aṅga avabaddhāyā aṅgatva nirāse api na vidheyatva hāniḥ nanu yathā durgandha ādi jñānasya icchā viṣayatva abhāve api brahma jñānasya tad viṣaya tvam yathā ca jñāna antarasya niyama adṛṣṭa asādhya tve api brahma jñānasya tad sādhya tvam yathā parvata ādi jñānasya nayana unmīlane sati prayatna antara nirapekṣa tve api dhruva arundhatyādi jñāne tad sāpekṣa tvam tathā ati sūkṣma brahma jñānasya icchā prayatna sādhyatva saṃbhava iti ced na prāmāṇika dṛṣṭa vijātīya kiṃcid dharma darśanena aprāmāṇika vaijātyasya kalpayitum aśakyatvāt  prayatna anvaya vyatirekayoḥ ca jñāna sādhana janane upakṣīṇa tayā dhruva arundhatya ādi nidarśanānyatha asiddha tayā tad nyāyena brahma jñāne kṛti sādhya tvasya vaktum aśakya tvāt ca na ca śāstra artha jñānasya niyamena puṃtatratva darśanāt  brahmaṇaḥ ca śāstra artha tvāt tad jñānasya puṃtatratvam iti vācyam tatra api jñāna sādhanasya eva puṃtatra tvāt  yad ca praśasta apraśasta jñānayoḥ vidhi niṣedha darśanam tad api jñāna kāraṇa viṣayakam eva yad ca icchā ādinā utpatti nirodhayoḥ anubhavaḥ saḥ api karaṇa vyāpāra viṣayaka eva na ca evam nāma ādiṣu brahma upāsanāyām tvayā vidheya tvena aṅgīkṛtāyām puṃtatra tvam na sidhyet  tatra api manaḥ dhāraṇa ādeḥ eva puṃtantra tvasya vaktum śakya tvāt iti vācyam jñāna vidhi ukta anupapatteḥ tatra abhāvena nirodha ādīnām anya paratvasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  na ca ukta jñāna rūpa śravaṇa ādiṣu ati prayatna sādhya tvasya anubhava siddha tvāt vidheya tvam iti vācyam anubhavān yathā siddheḥ ukta tvāt  na ca tvayā api nididhi āsanasya parokṣa jñāna santāna rūpasya vidheya tvam vadatā santāninām jñānānām api vidheya tvam aṅgīkartavyam eva tad avidhāne santati vidhāna anupapatteḥ iti vācyam āvṛtti guṇa yogasya eva vidheya tvāt  upaniṣadam āvartayet iti atra iva na ca śravaṇa ādeḥ jñānān ātmaka tve śravaṇam yāvat ajñānam iti ajñāna virodhitva smṛteḥ
