śravaṇena ajñānam nivṛttam iti anubhavasya ca anupapattiḥ iti vācyam āvṛtti guṇa yoga vākya artha pramiti upayukta tātpari nirṇaya dvārā upakrama ādi liṅga vicāra ātmaka śravaṇa ādeḥ ajñāna ādi virodhitayā smṛti anubhavayoḥ upapatteḥ ‘vijñāya prajñām kurvīte ati ādau jñāna vidhau  ukta anupapattyā prajñā śabdasya vicāra lākṣaṇikatva upapatteḥ na ca tvayā vidheya tvena aṅgīkṛtasya dhyānasya jñāna bhinna tve tasya sva viṣaye vyavahāra janaka tvam na syāt iti vācyam tad anya jñānena eva tad kāraṇatayā aavaśyakena tad viṣaye vyavahāra upapatteḥ pramāṇavataḥ asya gauravasya adoṣa tvāt ata eva dhyāna viṣaye jānāmi iti anubhava smaraṇe tad bhinna jñāna prayukta tayā vyākhyāte tasya abhidhyānāt iti śrutau dhyānasya māyā ākhyā vidyā nivartaka tve api tad uktiḥ dhyāna anantara bhāvi sākṣātkāra dvāra abhiprāya iti na tayā virodhaḥ yad tu upāsīta iti upakramya ‘ya evam vede ati upasaṃhāreṇa tvayā api vidheya tvena aṅgīkṛtāyām upāsanāyām vididhātu prayogeṇa upāsanāyāḥ jñānatva avagamāt  anyatra api jñāna tvam na vidheyatva virodhi iti tad na ukta anupapattyā videḥ tatra amukhya tvena eva jñānatva avagamaka tvāt  dhātu aneka artha tvena vā na ca  māna tantra tā mātreṇa katham apuṃtantra tā pratigrahītra ādi tantrasya api dāna ādeḥ tad darśanāt iti vācyam na hi anya tantra tā mātreṇa avidheya tvam brūmaḥ kiṃtu pum icchābhiḥ yad kāraṇe sati anyathā kartum aśakyatvam iti advaita siddhau jñānasya puruṣa tantra tā bhaṅgaḥ atha jñāna vidhi bhaṅgaḥ kiṃca vidhīyamānam jñānam kim śābdam kim vā tad abhyāsaḥ yad vā tattvam anapekṣi āropita viṣaya tayā dhyānam kim vā aparokṣya phalakam jñāna antaram na ādyaḥ karma kāṇḍa iva gṛhīta saṅgateḥ svatas siddha tvena kṛtya sādhya tayā vidhyaviṣaya tvāt  na ca karmakāṇḍe aapi āpāta janyasya svatas siddha tve api vimarśa janyasya kṛti sādhya tvam anyathā adhyayana vidheḥ uttara kratu vidheḥ vā tad ākṣepaka tā na syāt iti vācyam tad janaka vicāra eva vidheya tā prayojaka kṛti sādhyatva paryavasānena tādṛśa jñāne api asaṃbhavāt na dvitīyaḥ sa kim mokṣāya vidhīyate sākṣātkārāya vā na ādyaḥ tasya naiyogika tvena svarga ādivat anityatva āpātāt  na ca bandha dhvaṃsasya naiyogika tve api dhvaṃsa tvāt  śruti ādi balāt ca nityatva upapattiḥ iti vācyam na hi tad naya iva tu annaye api bandha dhvaṃsa mātram muktiḥ kiṃtu loka antara prāptiḥ tasya amukta doṣa tādavasthyāpattiḥ na ca anāvṛtti śrutyā nitya tvam ‘tad yathā iha karma citaḥ  lokaḥ kṣīyate evam eva amutra puṇya citaḥ  lokaḥ kṣīyate iti śrutyā naiyogikasya anityatva avagamāt na ca etad śruti virodhena tasya anityatva ābodhaka tvam ‘yat kṛtakam tad anityam i ati yukti upodbalita tayā prābalyāt  na dvitīyaḥ tad  kim dṛṣṭa phalakam adṛṣṭa phalakam vā na ādyaḥ parokṣa jñāna abhyāsena tattva sākṣātkāra adarśanāt  na dvitīyaḥ pramāṇa āyatta tvāt tasya ata eva na tṛtīyaḥ dhyānasya jñāna rūpatva abhāvāt ca na caturthaḥ śabdasya api prāmāṇya abhāva āpātāt brahmaṇi pramāṇībhūta jñāna kartavya tāyām eva prāmāṇyāt  na ca mahātāt paryam ādāya brahmaṇi api prāmāṇyam tādṛśa jñānasya api pramāṇa āyatta tayā vidhi phala tvāt  tasmāt  pratnyavekṣitam ājyam iti ādau  api jñānasya avidhānāt dhyānasya api vijñāna vyatireka sādhanāt  sūkṣma śāstra artha buddhau kṛtī anvaya vyatirekayoḥ tad sādhana viṣaya tayā anyathā siddha tvāt ca na ātma jñānam vidhātum śakyate tad evam śravaṇasya jñāna rūpa tve vidheyatva anupapattiḥ tasmāt  jñāna vijātīyam śravaṇam aparokṣa jāna janaka śabda iti kartavya tā rūpa vicāra ātmakam manana nididhi āsana aṅgakam prameya avagamam pratyaṅga tayā pradhāna bhūtam aparokṣa jñāna phalaka tayā vidhīyata iti siddham iti advaita siddhau jñāna vidhi bhaṅgaḥ atha śabdāt aparokṣa upapattiḥ nanu katham aparokṣa jñāna janaka tvam śabdasya māna abhāvāt iti ced na ‘tad hāsya vijajñau tamasaḥ pāram darśayatī ati ādeḥ ‘vedānta vijñāna su niścita arthā iti ādeḥ ca māna tvāt  pūrva vākye tad janaka aparokṣa jñānasya upadeśa mātra sādhyatva ukteḥ dvitīya śrutau śābda jñānasya vipadena viśeṣa viṣaya tvasya lābhāt  supadena aparokṣatva ukteḥ na ca vijajñau  iti iti ādeḥ parokṣa jñānena api caritārtha tā atamasaḥ pāram darśayatī ati uttara vākya svarasena aparokṣa jñāna paratva siddheḥ na ca grāma mārga upadeṣṭari grāmam darśa yati itivat  paramparayā prayojaka tayā upacāraḥ sākṣāt sādhana tve bādhaka abhāvena tasya atra anyāyya tvāt upadeśa atirikta kāraṇasya nārada sanatkumāra ākhyāyikāyāma pratīteḥ ca na ca manasā eva anudraṣṭavyam iti ādi śruti virodhaḥ tasyāḥ citta ekāgya paratvāt na ca supadasya aprāmāṇya śaṅkā viraha para tvena dvitīya vākyena tena aparokṣa rūpa tā prāptiḥ anyathā vedānta bodhyasya vicāra kartavyatā ādeḥ ca aparokṣatva āpātāt iti  vācyam niścita padena eva aprāmāṇya śaṅkā viraha ādeḥ labdha tayā supadasya atad paratvāt na api vedānta bodhyasya brahma atiriktasya api evam āparokṣya āpattiḥ artha padasya mukhyatas tātparya viṣaya para tvāt vedānta bodhyatāyāḥ  brahma mātra paryavasanna tvāt ca evam anumānam api atra mānam aparokṣa tvam tattvam asya ādi vākya janya jñāna vṛtti aparokṣa jñāna niṣṭhāti anta abhāva apratiyogi tvāt jñāna tvavat na ca karma kāṇḍa janya jñāna vṛttī iti evam api sādhyeta iti vācyam vipakṣa bādhaka sattva asattvābhyām viśeṣāt  tathā hi   tad tvam asya ādi vākyasya aparokṣa jñāna ajanaka tve aparokṣa bhrama nivṛttiḥ na syāt  na ca manasā eva aparokṣa jñānam manasaḥ kutra api asādhāraṇyena pramākaraṇatva abhāvāt ātmanaḥ sva prakāśa tvāt  sukha ādīnām sa akṣi vedya tvāt  na ca śabde aparokṣa jñāna janaka tvavat  anyatra āklṛptam eva manasi tad kalpanīyam evam hi sarva aṃśasya eva manasi kalpya tvena viśeṣāt  na ca evam jyotiṣṭoma ādi viṣayaka karma kāṇḍa janya jñāne kalpakam asti tatra hi kalpanīyam anuṣṭhānāya vā phalāya vā na ādyaḥ parokṣa jñānāt eva tad saṃbhavāt tatas  eva anuṣṭhānāt phala siddheḥ na dvitīyaḥ api na ca vimataḥ śabdaḥ  na aparokṣa dhī hetuḥ śabda tvāt iti pratisādhanam ‘da śamaḥ tvamasī ati ādau  eva vyabhicārāt  na ca tatra api indriyam eva karaṇam śabdaḥ tad sahakārī iti  vācyam kvacid  bahulatame tamasi locana hīnasya api tad vākyāt aparokṣa bhrama nivartakasya daśamaḥ asmi iti aparokṣa jñānasya darśanāt  yatra api indriya sadbhāvaḥ tatra api tad aprayojakam eva na ca dharmavān  tvam asi parvataḥ agnimān itya ādau viśeṣya aparokṣa tve api viśeṣaṇa pārokṣyavat  atra api daśama tve pārokṣyam astu iti vācyam atra parokṣa tve aparokṣa bhrama anivṛtti prasaṅgāt  nanu evam api śabdasya aparokṣa jñāna janaka tvam kim svābhāvikam uta aparokṣa viṣaya nimittakam na ādyaḥ atiprasaṅgāt  na dvitīyaḥ jīvāḥ paramātmanaḥ  na bhidyante ātma tvāt ityādinā jāyamāna anumiteḥ śravaṇāt  prāc āpatatas  vedānta janyāyāḥ  bhāṣā prabandha janyāyāḥ  anadhīta vedānta janyāyāḥ  aikya pratīteḥ ca aparokṣyāpātāt  śravaṇa niyama ādeḥ aniyamāt  kiṃca arthasya aparokṣyam na tāvat aparokṣa buddhi viṣayatva rūpam brahmaṇi asya sattve api daśamatva ādau  abhāvāt caitra aparokṣa jñāne maitrasya śabda ādinā āparokṣya adarśanāt ca na api aparokṣa vyavahāra viṣaya tvam vyavahāra aparokṣyasya tādṛś artha bheda viṣayakatva rūpa tve anyonya āśrayāt aparokṣaḥ ayam iti evaṃrūpa tve ajñāna āvṛte api tad abhāvāt tvayā api na prakāśata ityādi vyavahāra artham eva āvaraṇa kalpanāt  ukta vyavahāra yogyatva rūpa tve vyavahita ghaṭe śabdāt aparokṣa jñāna prasaṅgāt  aparokṣa jñāna janyatva rūpa tve ca vakṣyamāṇa pakṣa antar bhāvāt tasmāt arthasya aparokṣa dhī viṣaya tvam eva aparokṣa tvam vācyam tatra ca etad jñāna viṣaya tvena tad uktau  anyonya āśrayaḥ jñāna antara abhiprāye tu keṣāṃcid aparokṣe svarga ādau  asmākam śabdāt aparokṣa dhī prasaṅgāt  eka pum abhiprāye tu pūrva aparokṣe śabda ādinā idānīm aparokṣa dhī prasaṅgāt  eka kāla abhiprāye pratyakṣa agnau liṅgāt śabdāt vā āparokṣyam syāt iti ced na yam śābda bodham ādāya yasya bodhya tvam tad sākṣātkāra artham tad abhinna artha avagāhitva nimittakam iti ukta doṣān avakāśāt na ca evam pratyakṣa antarbhāvaḥ śabdasya syāt iti vācyam bodhya bhinna arthaka śabda atirikta tve sati pratyakṣa pramākaraṇa tvasya pratyakṣasya antarbhāve tantra tvāt nanu ‘manasā eva anudraṣṭavya amiti ādeḥ iva manaḥ karaṇa tā pratipādakasya prakṛte abhāvāt  anaupadeśikam śabdasya sākṣātkāra karaṇa tvam iti ced na ‘tam tu aupaniṣadam puruṣam pṛcchāmī atyādau tatra sādhuḥ iti tad anya asādhu tve sati tad sādhutva rūpa sādhu artha vihita tad hita śrutyā eva māna tvāt  nanu manasaḥ karaṇa tve api aupaniṣadatvasya nididhi āsana apekṣita tayā anyathā siddhiḥ na ‘yat manasā na manuta iti manasaḥ karaṇatva niṣedhāt  na ca ‘yataḥ  vācaḥ  nivartanta iti śabdasya api karaṇatva anupapattiḥ aupaniṣadatva śruti anusāreṇa tasyāḥ śaktyā abodhakatva paratvāt tad uktaṃ ‘ cakitam abhidhatte śrutiḥ apī ati na ca ‘manasā eva anudraṣṭavyam i ati tṛtīyā śruti anusāreṇa na manuta iti asya eva apakva manaḥ viṣaya tayā anyathā ānayana sāmyam iti vācyam evam sāmye api manasaḥ karaṇa tve hi adhika kalpanā śabdasya karaṇa tve tu alpa kalpanā iti viśeṣāt  tasmāt tattvam asya ādi vākyasya aparokṣa jñāna janaka tvāt avidyā nivṛtti ātmaka mokṣa sādhana brahma sākṣātkārāya manana ādi aṅgakam śravaṇam aṅgi niyama vidhi viṣaya iti siddham iti advaita siddhau śabdāt aparokṣa upapattiḥ viśveśvara ākhyasya guroḥ prasādāt advaita siddhiḥ madhusūdanasya abhūt abhūmiḥ khalu dūṣaṇānām guṇaiḥ ameyaiḥ avagumbhita śrīḥ sa saṃbhramam apekṣayā para guṇa unnatiḥ duḥsahā nitāntam anapekṣayā nija pumartha hāniḥ parā atas  sumatayaḥ yathā anayam upekṣya durmatsaram prayojana vaśa anugāḥ kuruta mad kṛtau satkṛtim caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ atha avidyā nivṛtti nirūpaṇam nanu muktiḥ tāvat avidyā nivṛttiḥ na saṃbhavati tathā hi—sā kimātma rūpā tad bhinnā vā na ādyaḥ asādhyatva āpatteḥ dvitīye api kim satī mithyā vā ādye advaita hāniḥ dvitīye avidyā tad kārya anyataratva āpattiḥ iti ced na carama vṛtti upalakṣitasya ātmanaḥ ajñāna hāni rūpa tvāt tathā ca upalakṣaṇa sādhya tayā eva mukteḥ api sādhya tā na ca upalakṣaṇa nivṛttyā mukteḥ api nivṛttiḥ pāke nivṛtte api pācakā nivṛtti darśanāt  tad uktaṃ  anivṛttiḥ ātmā mohasya jñāta tvena upalakṣitaḥ upalakṣaṇa nāśe api syāt muktiḥ pācaka ādivat  iti na ca vṛtti upalakṣitasya paścāt iva pūrvam api sattvena moha kāle api tad dhānya āpattiḥ pūrvam asiddhasya upalakṣaṇatva ayogāt na hi pāka saṃbandhāt  pūrvam pācakaḥ  bhavati tathā vyavahriyate vā yad tu  pāka kartṛ tvam eva pācaka tvam tadā apacati tad prayogaḥ  bhūta pūrva nyāyena aupacārikaḥ yadi tu pāka kartṛ tā avacchedaka avacchinna tvam tad kartṛtva atyanta abhāva anadhikaraṇa tvam vā tad dvayam api paścāt asti na ca evam muktau  ātmā atiriktam yogyatva ādikam asti cit mātram tu prāk api asti iti asādhyata āpattiḥ pāka upalakṣita tvavat vṛtti upalakṣita tvasya adhika tve sa viśeṣa tā āpattiḥ iti tad na upalakṣya svarūpasya asādhya tve api upalakṣaṇa gata sādhyatva upapatteḥ ghaṭa ākāśe utpattivat  yad vā avidyā nivṛttiḥ tad virodhi vṛttiḥ eva yāvat kārya utpatti virodhi kāryam eva dhvaṃsa iti aṅgīkārāt  na ca vṛttau naṣṭāyām virodhinaḥ kārya antarasya anuyāt  tadā api dhvaṃsa sattvena sa na dhvaṃsa iti vācyam yāvat virodhi kārya udayam eva tathā tvāt  yāvat vibhāgam tasya dhvaṃsa rūpa tve api vibhāga dhvaṃsasya adhikaraṇa rūpa tāvat caramavṛtti paryantam virodhi kārya rūpa tve api dhvaṃsasya carama vṛtti dhvaṃsasya adhikaraṇa rūpa tā eva nanu iyam prakriyā kim anyatra iha eva vā na ādyaḥ bimba pratibimba aikya ajñāna nivṛttiḥ api jñāta tad ā aikya rūpa iti tad aikya dhī kāle sa upādhika tad bheda bhrama upādāna ajñāna anuvṛtti ayogāt na antyaḥ niyāmaka abhāvāt na ca iha nivṛtteḥ jñāta adhiṣṭhāna atireke viśva mithyātva śruti paryālocanayā nivṛtteḥ api nivṛtti āpattiḥ niyāmikā tasyāḥ  jñānāt viśvā nivṛtti paratvena svatātparya viṣaya nivṛtti itara mithyātva para tvāt iti ced na na tāvat ādye doṣaḥ sa upādhika bhrame upādhi viraha kālīnasya eva tasya tathā tvāt  na api dvitīyaḥ na iti na iti iti śruteḥ svārasyena ātma atirikta sarva nivṛttau  eva tātparyāt  na ca vṛtti upalakṣita ātmā jīvanmuktau  api asti iti tadā api mokṣa āpattiḥ mukti mātra āpādanasya iṣṭa tvāt  parama mukteḥ carama sākṣātkāra upalakṣita ātma svarūpa tvena tad āpādaka abhāvāt na ca carama sākṣātkāra nivṛtteḥ ātma tve asādhyatva āpattiḥ avidyā nivṛtteḥ asādhya tve apravṛtti āpattivat  atra tad abhāvāt na ca jīvanmukti prayojaka vṛtti apekṣayā parama mukti prayojaka vṛttau ānanda abhivyakti gata viśeṣa abhāve cara makṣaṇena carama śvāsena vā upalakṣita ātmā muktiḥ iti kim na syāt iti vācyam prārabdha karma prayukta vikṣepa vikṣepābhyām abhivyakti viśeṣasya aṅgīkārāt  etena vedānta śravaṇa ādi sādhyaḥ pum arthaḥ  vācyaḥ na ca sa tvad mate vaktum śakyaḥ mukti anusyūta sukha jñapti rūpasya ātmanaḥ puruṣa artha tvenā api asādhya tvāt vṛtteḥ sādhya tve api svatas apum artha tvāt tasmāt ātma vyatirikta eva vṛtti sādhya āvaraṇa nivṛtti rūpaḥ ānanda prakāśaḥ pum arthaḥ  vācyaḥ tathā ca katham ātmā eva nivṛttiḥ iti  apāstam prāpta prāpti rūpa tayā phalasya ānanda prakāśasya svarūpataḥ asādhya tve api tad tirodhāyaka ajñāna nivartaka vṛtteḥ sādhyatva mātreṇa sādhyatva upapatteḥ kaṇṭha gata cāmīkara ādau tathā darśanāt  tasmāt ajñāna hāniḥ ātma svarūpam tad ākārā vṛttiḥ vā iti siddham ye tu pañcama prakāra ādi pakṣāḥ te tu manda buddhi vyutpādana arthā iti na tad samarthanam arthayāmaḥ iti advaita siddhau avidyā nivṛtti nirūpaṇam atha avidyā nivartaka nirūpaṇam avidyā nivartakam ca yadi api na sva prakāśa brahma rūpa jñāna mātram tasya tad sādhaka tvāt tathā api śravaṇa ādi sādhya aparokṣa vṛtti samārūḍham tad eva ata eva etad apāstam  kim sva prakāśa cit avidyā nivartikā tad ākārā aparokṣa vṛttiḥ vā na ādyaḥ tasyāḥ  idānīm api sattvāt  na dvitīyaḥ asatyāt satya siddheḥ ayogāt  ajñāne na jānāmi iti jñapti rūpa cit virodhasya anubhavena ājñapti rūpa vṛtti virodhasya asaṃbhavāt citā prakāśa māna sukha ādau  ajñāna adarśanāt ca kiṃca icchā nivartya dveṣavat jāti nibandhana vṛtti nivarti asya ajñānasya aviśeṣaṇa sattva āpattiḥ iti vṛtti upārūḍha citaḥ  vā cit pratibimba dhāriṇyā vṛtteḥ vā nivartaka tvāt  na ca asatyāyāḥ satya utpādakatva virodhaḥ abhāvasya bhāva janakatvavat asya saṃbhavāt  pratibhāsikasya vyāvahārika sukha janakatva darśanāt ca na api na jānāmi iti jñapti rūpa cit virodhi tvā anubhava virodhaḥ cit asaṃsṛṣṭa vṛtteḥ virodhi tvasya anaṅgīkārāt  yad tu uktam dveṣavat  satya tvam iti tad na adhiṣṭhāna tattva sākṣātkāratva nibandhana nivartaka tvasya śukti ādi jñānavat atra api saṃbhavena tad nivartya rūpyavat  satyatva anāpatteḥ yad tu uktam carama vṛtteḥ ghaṭa ādi vṛttyā cit viṣaya tve aviśeṣaḥ iti tad na avacchinna anavacchinna viṣaya tayā viśeṣāt  yad tu sva nivartaka tve sthiti virodhaḥ sva upādāna nivartaka tvam tu adṛṣṭa caram iti tad na anyatra adṛṣṭasya api pramāṇa balāt atra eva kalpanāt  tathā hi ‘māyām tu prakṛtim vidyā ādi atyavagata māyā upādānaka tvasya api ātma tattva sākṣātkārasya ‘tarati śokam ātma vid  saḥ avidyā granthim vikirati iha somye atyādinā tad nivartaka tvasya ca pramita tvāt  vṛtti pratibimbita citaḥ  nivartaka tve tu na ukta vacasaḥ śaṅkā api tad uktan— atṛṇādeḥ bhāsikā api eṣā sūrya dīptiḥ tṛṇam dahet  sūryakāntam upāruhya tad nyāyam viniyojayet  na ca aparokṣa vṛttau satyām cit apratibimba nibandhana nivṛtti vilamba adarśanāt  na viśiṣṭe nivartaka tā iti vācyam śuddha jaḍasya śuddha citaḥ ca jaḍa tayā tad bhāsaka tayā ca ajñāna anivartaka tayā viśiṣṭe nivartaka tāyā āvaśyaka tvāt  yad tu nivartakam jñānam api na śuddha viṣayakam tasya adṛśya tvāt na api viśiṣṭa viṣayakam tasya adhyasta tvena bhramatva āpatteḥ iti tad na upahitasya viṣaya tve api upādheḥ aviṣaya tvena abhrama tvāt  yad tu antyasya jñānasya kim nivartakam svayam anyat vā na ādyaḥ anya nirapekṣa pratiyoginaḥ  dhvaṃsa janaka tve kṣaṇikatva āpatteḥ dagdha dāru dahanasya api īśvara icchā ādinā eva nāśāt kataka rajaḥ tu na paṅkam nāśayati na api svam viśleṣa mātra darśanāt  na antyaḥ śuddha ātmanaḥ kiṃcid api pratyahetutvāt  tad anyasya ca nivartya tvāt  iti tad na tantu nāśasya paṭa nāśa prayojakatva darśanena sva upādāna avidyā nāśasya eva tad na aśaka tvāt na ca avidyā nāśe tad upalakṣita ātmā vā vṛttiḥ vā pūrvatra śuddhasya ahetṛ tvam dvitīye pratiyogi mātrasya eva na aśaka tā paryavasānam iti vācyam ubhayathā api adoṣāt vṛttim ādāya eva brahmaṇa upahita tvena śuddhatva abhāvāt pratiyoginaḥ pratiyogi tvena na aśaka tāyām itara anapekṣa tve hi kṣaṇika tvam rūpa antara avacchedena yad  kāraṇam tasya apekṣaṇe na tad iti upādāna nāśatva avacchinnasya svasya eva kṣaṇikatva anāpādakam na aśaka tvam syāt  dvitīya kāraṇa nirapekṣa pratiyoginaḥ pratiyogi sva upādāna nāśatva rūpa dvaya avacchinnasya na aśakatva upapatteḥ vastutas tu avidyā nivṛtteḥ vṛtti rūpa tayā na nivartaka khaṇḍana avakāśaḥ vṛtti nivṛtteḥ ātma rūpa tayā na tajanaka khaṇḍana avakāśaḥ api iti sarvam avadātam iti advaita siddhau avidyā nivartaka nirūpaṇam atha mukteḥ ānanda rūpa tvena puruṣa artha tvam nanu tvad mate muktau na duḥkha uccheda mātram kiṃtu niratiśaya ānanda sphuraṇam api tad uktam ‘tasmāt avidyā aḥ tamayaḥ  nitya ānanda pratītitaḥ niḥśeṣa duḥkha ucchedāt ca puruṣa arthaḥ paraḥ  mataḥ iti tatra na sukha ātma tā tāvat puruṣa arthaḥ sukhī syām itivat  sukham syāmiti icchāyā adarśanāt  pum artha tāyāḥ  icchā niyamya tvāt anyathā bauddha mata siddha ātma nā aśādiḥ api pum arthaḥ syāt  ata eva na aparakīyam sukham pum arthaḥ tayā icchā virahāt  gauravāt ca sukha sādhane parakīye api svakīye pum artha tvasya aparakīye api asvakīye apum artha tvasya ca darśanena iṣṭatva aviśeṣāt sukhe api tad kalpanāt ca duḥkha tad sādhanayoḥ svakīyatayā eva apum artha tvasya darśanena sukha ādeḥ api tathā eva puruṣa artha tvāt ca iti ced na sukha ādau hi pum artha tā na aparakīyatva prayuktā na api svakīyatva prayuktā gauravāt  kiṃtu sākṣāt krayamāṇa tayā saṃbandhasya ca anityatva sādhana pāratantrī ādeḥ iva āvarjanīya sannidhika tvāt na ca īśvarasya api asmad ādi sukham pum arthaḥ syāt iti vācyam heya tayā ajñāta tve sati iti asya api tatra prayojaka tvāt īśvara ādinā ca ātma ādi sukhasya heya tve na eva jñānāt  svarūpa sukhe ceṣṭā patteḥ na ca gauravam sva saṃbandhi tvena pum artha tā vādinaḥ api nilīna sukhe puruṣa artha tā nivṛtti artham tathā avaśyam varṇanīya tvāt  yad tu sākṣātkāre api svakīyatayā puruṣa artha tā pakṣe muktasya sukha sākṣātkāra rūpa tayā tam pratyapi tasya apuruṣa artha tā āpattiḥ svetarā saṃbandhi tvena svasya puruṣa artha tve mukta svarūpeṇa sukhena saṃsāri itara asaṃbandhena saṃsāriṇaḥ puruṣa artha prasaṅgaḥ iti tad na sākṣāt krayamāṇa tvena eva hi pum artha tā mukta sukha sākṣātkārasya tam prati pum artha tve api na saṃsāriṇaḥ tathā tam pratyabhāsamāna tvāt  bhāne vā asaṃsāri tvena iṣṭāpattiḥ yad tu pratyakṣa prakāśa māna tvena sukham pum arthaḥ  iti tad api etena vyākhyātam pratyakṣa prakāśa māna tvena sākṣāt krayamāṇa tāyāḥ  eva ukteḥ yad tu sukha tvena prakāśamānam sukham pum arthaḥ na ca tad para mate mokṣe asti iti tad na sākṣāt krayamāṇa tvena eva atiprasaṅga nirāse adhika ukteḥ gauravaka tvāt  iti advaita siddhau mukteḥ ānanda rūpa tvena puruṣa artha tvam atha cit mātrasya mokṣa bhāgitva upapattiḥ nanu kasya ayam mokṣaḥ pum arthaḥ kim aham arthasya āhosvit cit mātrasya na ādyaḥ tvad mate aham arthasya mukti ananvayāt  na antyaḥ ‘aham muktaḥ syāmi ativat cit mātram muktam syāt iti icchāyā ananubhavāt iti ced na aham artha gatam cit aṃśam mukti kālān vayanam prati pum arthasya mokṣe saṃbhava iti ukta prāya tvāt na ca sukhasya duḥkha abhāva mātra tve vaiśeṣika mokṣavat apum artha tā atireke sa dvitīya tvam iti vācyam duḥkha abhāva atireke api ātmān atirekāt na ca ātmanaḥ sukha mātra tve sukha prakāśa abhāvena apum artha tvam ubhaya ātmaka tve ca akhaṇḍa arthatva hāniḥ iti vācyam sukha prakāśayoḥ eka ātma rūpa tayā ubhayatvasya eva abhāvāt na ca artha bheda abhāve sukha prakāśa iti saha prayoga ayogaḥ avidyā kalpita duḥkha jaḍa ātmakatva rūpa vyāvarya bhedena tad upapatteḥ yad tu duḥkha abhāvasya sukhasya ca tattvataḥ  duḥkhāt bhede apasiddhāntaḥ abhede tu apum artha tā iti tad na duḥkhasya kalpita tvena tad bhedasya tad samāna yoga kṣema tayā tāttvikatva abhāvena apasiddhānta abhāvāt yad tu sva prakāśasya sukhasya svatas  sphuraṇe api duḥkha abhāvasya asphuraṇāt apum artha tā   iti tad na duḥkha abhāvasya ātmān atirekeṇa ātma abhinne sukhe sphurati tasya api sphuraṇāt  tattvena asphuraṇasya aprayojaka tāyā ukta tvāt  tasmāt sva prakāśa cid abhinnam sukham pum arthaḥ iti cit mātrasya mokṣa bhāgitva upapattiḥ atha jīvanmukti upapattiḥ tad ca jīvanmuktānām sva anubhava siddham jīvanmuktaḥ ca tattva jñānena nivṛtta āvidyaḥ api anuvṛtta deha ādi pratibhāsaḥ na ca tattva jñānāt avidyā nāśe sadyas śarīra pāta āpattiḥ nivṛtta sarpa bhramasya api saṃskārāt  bhaya kampa anuvṛttivat  daṇḍa saṃyoga nāśe api cakra bhramaṇavat ca saṃskāra anuvṛtteḥ avidyā nivṛttau  api tad kārya anuvṛtti saṃbhavāt na ca kriyā jñānayoḥ eva saṃskāraḥ na anyasya iti vācyam niḥsārita puṣpāyām sampuṭikāyām puṣpa vāsanā darśanāt  vimataḥ  nāśaḥ saṃskāra vyāptaḥ saṃskāra nāśa anya tve sati nāśatvāt jñāna nāśavat iti anumānāt ca saṃskāraḥ kāryaḥ api dhvaṃsa iva nirupādānakaḥ avidyā iva ca śuddha ātma āśrita iti na avidyā sāpekṣaḥ na ca—bhāva kāryasya adhyastasya saṃskāra deha ādi tad hetu prārabdha karma ādeḥ sthiti arthaḥ tad upādāna ajñāna anuvṛtti āpāta iti vācyam vinaśyat avasthasya samavāyi kāraṇam vinā sthiti darśanāt  na ca kṣaṇa mātra sthitau  api katham bahu kṣaṇa sthitiḥ iti vācyam sati upapādake kṣaṇa gaṇa kalpanāyā aprayojaka tvāt  tatra kṣaṇa mātram sthitiḥ samavāyasya ajanaka tvāt  atra tu pratibandhaka abhāva saha kṛta hetoḥ tāvat kālam abhāvāt ata eva pūrva jñāna anivṛttasya adhyastasya tad anadhika viṣayeṇa katham nivṛttiḥ iti—nirastam pratibandhaka abhāva sahakāra asahakārābhyām viśeṣāt  jīvanmukti daśa āyām ānanda sphūrya upādana miṣṭam eva tattve jñāte dvi candra ādivat doṣāt bādhita anuvṛtti saṃbhavāt ca na ca tatra iva atra jñāna anivartya doṣa abhāvena vaiṣamyam yāvat pratibandhaka sattvam jñāna anivartyasya doṣasya atra api saṃbhavāt  sarva jñāna anivartyasya tasya kutra api asaṃpratipatteḥ tad uktam ‘nahi jātyā eva kaścid doṣaḥ astī ati yad vā avidyā leśa anuvṛttyā deha ādi anuvṛttiḥ nanu leśaḥ  na avayavaḥ ajñānasya niravayava tvāt  ata eva avidyā dagdha paṭa nyāyena tāvat tiṣṭhati iti api nirastam niravayave etad nyāya asaṃbhavāt iti ced na ākārasya iva leśa śabda artha tvāt ‘indraḥ  māyābhiḥ puru rūpa iyata ityādi śrutyā avidyāyāḥ  aneka ākāratva avagamāt  ākāri nivṛttau  api ākārasya anuvṛtti vyakti nivṛttau  api jāteḥ iva nanu kaḥ ayam ākāraḥ  nāma jātiḥ vā śakti ādi rūpaḥ  dharmaḥ  vā suvarṇa kuṇḍala ādivat avasthā viśeṣaḥ  vā na ādyau tayoḥ deha ādi bhrama upādāna tve avidyātva āpātāt  anupādāna tve ca upādāna antara abhāvena deha ādi bhrama utpatti ayogāt ātma anya tvena jñāna nivartya tvena ca avidyā tad kārya ani ataratva avaśyaṃbhāvena ajñāne nivṛtte sthiti ayogāt ca ata eva na tṛtīyaḥ ‘avasthāvantam vinā avasthāyāḥ sthiti ayoga ādi ati ced na aneka śakti mat avidyāyāḥ prapañce pāramārthikatva ādi bhrama hetu śakteḥ prapañce artha kriyā samarthatva sampādaka śakteḥ ca prārabdha karma sama kālīna tattva sākṣātkāreṇa nivṛttau  api aparokṣa pratibhāsa yogya artha ābhāsa janikāyāḥ śakteḥ anuvṛtteḥ tadvatī vidyā api tiṣṭhati eva iti na ukta doṣa avakāśaḥ na ca avidyāyām katham mukta iti vyapadeśaḥ śakti nāśa mātrāt ataeva samaye sarva śakti mada jñāna nāśaḥ tad jātīyena apratiruddhena pratyayena tathā ca śrutiḥ ‘tasya abhidhyānāt yojanāt tattva bhāvāt bhūyas ca ante viśva māyā nivṛtti ariti na ca bhūya iti asya yojanāt iti anena anvayāt na leśa anuvṛttau  asyāḥ śruteḥ mānatā iti vācyam viśeṣaṇa anvaya apekṣayā viśeṣya anvayasya abhyarhita tvāt tattva bhāvāt iti anena vyavadhānāt  anta iti pada vaiyarthyāt ca viparīta yojanasya asaṅgateḥ na ca leśa sthitau karma anuvṛttiḥ tad anuvṛttau ca jñāna pratibandhena leśa sthitiḥ iti anyonya āśraya iti vācyam na tāvat  jñaptau ‘bhūyas ca ante viśva māyā nivṛttiḥ i atyādi śruteḥ eva leśa anuvṛtteḥ avagata tvāt na api sthitau eka kālīna tvena doṣa abhāvāt yad vā ajñānasya sūkṣma avasthā leśaḥ yathā ‘tasmāt  phale pravṛttasya yāga ādeḥ śakti mātrakam utpattau  api paśu ādeḥ apūrvam na tatas  pṛthak  iti vārtikena yāge gate api yoga sūkṣma avasthā rūpam apūrvam yāge sādhana tā nirvāhakam aṅgīkriyate tathā ajñāne gate api tad sūkṣma avasthā rūpaḥ  leśaḥ  deha ādi pratīti anukūlaḥ svīkriyate svarga janaka tā grāhaka śruteḥ iva atra api jīvanmukti śruteḥ tādṛś artha svīkārāt tasmāt avidyā leśa anuvṛttyā jīvanmuktiḥ upapannatarā iti advaita siddhau jīvanmukti upapattiḥ atha muktau tāratamya bhaṅgaḥ yad tu  para mate aparokṣa jñāninaḥ api sva yogya parama ānanda hetu parama kāṣṭha āpanna bhakti abhāve tad sādhyasya mocakasya īśvara prasādasya abhāvena prārabdha karmaṇā saṃsāra anuvṛttau jīvanmuktiḥ tad bhāve tu prasādasya api bhāvena niśśeṣa duḥkhā nivṛtti viśiṣṭa svatonīca ucca bhāva āpanna svarūpa ānanda āvirbhāva rūpā muktiḥ iti tad na ‘tāvat eva asya ciram i atyādi śrutyā asya utpanna tattva sākṣātkārasya prārabdha karma kṣaya mātram apekṣaṇīyam kaivalya saṃpatti artham iti pratipādanena īśvara prasāda apekṣāyāḥ  vaktum aśakyatvāt  smṛti purāṇa ādīnām śruti virodhena stuti paratvāt  ‘yam eva eṣa vṛṇute tena labhyaḥ tasya eṣa ātmā vivṛṇute tanūm svā am iti bhakti janyeśvara prasādasya api tad sākṣātkāra svarūpa eva upayogasya bodhita tvena smṛti ādīnām api tad anusāra tvāt vaiparītyena sādhya sādhana bhāve māna abhāvāt na ca prārabdha karma kṣaye prasāda viniyogaḥ prasāda nirapekṣa bhogāt eva tad siddheḥ na api muktau  ucca nīca bhāvaḥ tasya dvitīya sāpekṣa tve tadā asaṃbhavāt  ‘paramam sāmyam upaitī ati sāmya śruteḥ ca sa atiśaya tve mukteḥ svarga ādivat anitya tvam syāt  adhika darśane duḥkha dveṣa ādikam ca syāt  nanu— muktau atāratamyam kim bheda abhāvāt uta sati api bhede tad sāmyāt na ādyaḥ śrutyā bheda siddheḥ na antyaḥ sāmyam kim jīveśvarayoḥ uta jīvānām eva na ādyaḥ tayoḥ vibhu tvā aṇutva śeṣa śeṣi bhāva svātantrya āpāra tantrya ādinā tāratamyāt  aneka īśvara āpattyā jagat pravṛtti ayogāt  tad dvaya tāratamya pratipādaka smṛtibhiḥ ‘jagat vyāpāra varjami ati ādi sūtraiḥ utkṛṣṭatva nikṛṣṭatva grāhaka anumānaiḥ virodhāt ca na antyaḥ jīvān prati śeṣiṇaḥ  lakṣmī tattvāt  tān prati niyāmakāt viṣvaksenāditaḥ ca jīvānām nikṛṣṭa tvāt  ‘sā eṣā ānandasye ati ādi taittirīya ādi śrutibhiḥ ‘muktānām api siddhānām nārāyaṇa parāyaṇaḥ su durlabhaḥ praśānta ātmā koṭiṣu api mahā mune ityādi smṛtibhiḥ ‘vṛddhi hrāsa bhāj tvam antar bhāvāt ubhaya sāmañjasyāt evam i atyādi sūtraiḥ ukta śruti tarka anugṛhītaiḥ anumānaiḥ virodhāt ca iti ced na bheda abhāvena tāratamya asiddheḥ yathā ca śruti ādeḥ na bheda paratvam tathā prāk eva gatam yad tu dvitīya pakṣam āśaṅkya dūṣaṇam tad akāṇḍa tāṇḍavam bheda sattve abheda ātmaka parama sāmya abhāvāt tad sattve bhedasya eva abhāvāt kiṃca tāratamya abhidhānam parama muktau uta brahma loka ādi vāsa rūpa aparama muktau vā na ādyaḥ ‘evam mukti phala aniyamaḥ tad avasthā avadhṛteḥ tad avasthā  adhṛteḥ iti tṛtīyā antya adhikaraṇe ‘a aihikam api aprastuta pratibandhe tad darśana ādi ati etad sūtra ukta jñāna gata aihikatva amuṣmikatva rūpa viśeṣavat muktau  api tāratamyam āśaṅkya niṣedhāt  dvitīye tu iṣṭāpattiḥ yad tu mukta jīva bhogaḥ īśvara bhogān nikṛṣṭaḥ jīva bhoga tvāt  saṃsāri bhogavat  evam jīva jñāna ādikam api pakṣīkṛtya prayoga ūhanīyaḥ īśvara ānandaḥ jīvānandāt utkṛṣṭaḥ tad niyāmaka ānanda tvāt yad evam tad evam yathā sevaka ānandāt sevya ānandaḥ īśvaraḥ jīva svabhāva ānanda ādita utkṛṣṭa svabhāva ānanda ādimān tad prepsu tve sati tatra śakta tvāt  yaḥ  yad prepsu tve sati yatra śaktaḥ sa tadvān yathā saṃmataḥ ityādīni tāratamya sādhaka ani iti tad na ādye muktasya brahma rūpa tayā upādhi kṛta jīvatva abhāvena āśraya asiddheḥ īśvaratva abhāvena sādhya aprasiddheḥ svarūpa asiddheḥ ca dvitīya ādi anumāne jīva īśvara vibhāga kāle tāratamya sādhanam ced siddha sādhanam tad bhinne kāle ced  pūrva doṣa anativṛttiḥ asa eṣa ānandasye ati ādi śrutibhiḥ mānuṣa ānandam ārabhya brahma ānanda paryanteṣu uttara uttara śataguṇatva rūpa tāratamyam upādhi tāratamyena vadantībhiḥ nirupādhike svarūpa ānande tāratamyasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  etena prakṛtā bandha nivṛttiḥ svasa jātīya bandha nivṛtti āśraya pratiyogika tāratamyavat niṣṭhā bandha nivṛtti tvāt  nigalavondha nivṛttivat iti nirastam tāratamyasya guṇa gata jāti tvena bandha nivṛtti āśraya ātmani vaktum aśakyatvāt  ata eva nivṛtti gata tāratamya sādhanam api apāstam nivṛtteḥ niratiśaya tvāt ānandasya sva rūpa tayā ubhaya vādi siddha tvena guṇatva abhāvena tatra api tasya vaktum aśakyatvāt  etena sva rūpa sukhānām pratyekam eka tvena aṇu tvena ca saṃkhyā parimāṇa kṛta vaiṣamya abhāve api jala sudhā pāna janya sukhayoḥ iva madhura madhurataratva āt ivat ca sva rūpa kṛta vaiṣamyam muktau  iti nirastam vaiṣayika sukhe sādhana tāratamya prayukta tāratamye api svarūpa ānande tad abhāvāt ca na ca sa ālokya ādi muktiḥ sāyujya ādi muktitaḥ apakṛṣṭa iti prasiddhi virodhaḥ para apara mukti rūpa tayā tad upapatteḥ sāyujya ādi muktāvat kṛṣṭatva vyapadeśaḥ apakṛṣṭatva abhāva mātreṇa nanu sāyujyam na aikyam ‘candramasaḥ sāyujya salokatām āpnotī atyādi śrutyā sati api bhede sāyujya ukteḥ ‘sayujaḥ paramātmānam praviśya ca bahis gatāḥ iti ādau sayujām praveśa mātra ukteḥ ca sa yujaḥ  bhāvaḥ sāyujyam iti yuja śabdena saṃbandhasya eva ukteḥ ‘sālokyam api sāmīpyam sārūpyam yoga eva ca iti smṛtau sāyujye saṃbandha vācaka yoga śabda prayogāt ca tasmāt sāyujyam nāma kṣīra nīravat  anya deha āviṣṭa graha devatā ādivat ca saṃśleṣa mātram na tu aikyam iti ced  na vyāpakena īśvareṇa saṃśleṣasya nitya siddha tvena apum artha tvāt na ca etad loka sthitasya jīvasya loka antara sthita alaukika śarīra avacchinnena īśvareṇa saṃśleṣaḥ sādhyaḥ ‘atra brahma samaśnuta iti śruteḥ utkramaṇa gamana ādi sādhya brahma loka avāptivat upādhya vacchinna jīvasya anavacchinna brahma abheda rūpa parama mukteḥ pāralaukika phalatva abhāvāt ‘brahma vid āpnoti parami atyādau avāpteḥ brahma rūpa tvavat  sāyujyasya api tad rūpa tāyāḥ  aṅgīkaraṇīya tvāt ca ‘candramasaḥ sāyujyam i atyādau ekaḥ  pādhya vacchinnasya upādhi antara avacchinnena aikya anupapattivat atra anupapatteḥ abhāvāt  prasiddha artha svīkāre bādhakasya ukta tvāt ca sāyujya śabdaḥ tāvat vibhaktatva abhāva abhiprāyakaḥ yad ca uttara uttaram śataguṇa ānanda prakāśaka vākyeṣu prativākyam muktāvakāma hata śabda prayogāt  mānuṣa ānandavat akāma hata muktā ānande api tāratamyam  iti tad na ‘etasya eva ānandasya anyāni bhūtāni mātrām upajīvantī ati sarveṣām laukika ānandānām parama ānanda antarbhāva abhidhāna upapatteḥ na tu tasya tasya akāma hatasya tāvān eva ānanda iti yena tatra api tāratamyam kalpyeta tathā ca ‘saḥ aśnate sarvān kāmān ‘kāmasya yatra āptāḥ kāmāḥ tatra mām amṛtam kṛdhī atyādi śruteḥ ‘sa hi muktaḥ akām hata ityādi brahmāṇḍa ukteḥ ca na virodhaḥ nanu ekasya eva śrotriyasya sarvatra parāmarśe mānuṣa ānanda ādibhyaḥ sa avadhāraṇa śata guṇita manuṣya gandharva ādi aneka ānandā ekasmin viruddhāḥ bhinnāḥ cedakāma hatatva ādeḥ eka rūpa tayā śrutasya avyavasthāpaka tvāt ānanda vyavasthā ayogaḥ atha vyavasthā artham etad padākāma etad itara pada kāmaḥ ca lakṣyate tadā aśruta kalpanā bādhaḥ ca na hi indra ādi pade vā rāja pade vā niṣkāmasya bhikṣukasya indra ādi ānanda anubhavaḥ asti tasmāt śrutyā pūrva vākyena āmuktānām tāratamyam uktvā ‘śrotriyasya ce atyādinā ‘yaḥ ca śrotriya aityādinā ca uttara vākyena muktasya tad ucyata iti ced na sarveṣu vākyeṣu akāma hatasya muktasya ekatve api tad ānande sarva ānandānām antar bhāvāt sa eva tasmin tasmin  ānande vaktavye parāmṛśyate tad tad indra ādi sāmyena tasya sarvatra abhidhāna upapatteḥ aadhikam praviṣṭam na tu tad ha aniḥ i ati nyāyāt  sāmye hi tad sajātīya dharmavat tvam tantram na tu tad itara dharmān adhikaraṇa tvam api gauravāt  yad ca mukta sukham paraspara tāratamyavat  paraspara tāratamyavat sādhanaka tvāt  saṃmatavat iti tad na asiddheḥ nanu muktiḥ prayāga maraṇa bhagavat dveṣa ādi sādhya iti mate jñāna karma samuccaya sādhya iti mate ca prayāga maraṇa ādīnām varṇa āśrama karmaṇām ca viṣama tvāt  na asiddhiḥ jñāna eka sādhya iti mate api ‘kaḥ tam madāmadam devam mad anyaḥ  jñātum arhati ‘sarve guṇā brahmaṇā eva hi upāsyā na anyaiḥ devaiḥ kim u sarvaiḥ manuṣyaiḥ i atyādi śrutyā ‘brahma ādi tad veda na ced asamyak anye kutaḥ deva muni indra varyāḥ ityādi smṛtibhiḥ deva ādi manuṣya ādi stha mukti hetu brahma jñāna gatasya bahu bahutara śākhā śravaṇa sādhya tvasya bahu bahutara guṇa viṣaya tvam vinā ayogena arthāpattyā ca tad siddhiḥ iti ced na kevala karma pakṣe samuccaya pakṣe vā karma sādhya tvena mukteḥ anityatva āpatteḥ ‘nā anyaḥ panthāḥ ityādi śruti virodhāt ca tṛtīya pakṣe tu udāhṛta śrutīnām brahma vidyā durlabhatva pratipādana para tvena tad ukta sādhana sādhyatva apratipādaka tvāt  na ca artha āpattyā tasiddhiḥ brahma sākṣātkārasya nirguṇa viṣaya tayā guṇa viṣayatva ayogāt yad tu ‘yaḥ ta āśiṣa āśāste na sa bhṛtyaḥ sa vai vaṇij  sa vai bhṛtyaḥ sa ca svāmī guṇa labdhau na kāmukau mumukṣoḥ amumukṣuḥ tu paraḥ ca ekānta bhaktimān ityādi smṛtyā mumukṣu bhakti apekṣayā amumukṣoḥ bhaktasya adhikya ukteḥ tad ādhikyasya loka rīti siddha tvāt ca ‘bhaktiḥ siddheḥ garīyasī atismṛtyā alpa bhakti sādhya mukti apekṣayā adhika mukti hetu bhakteḥ api ādhikyasya ukteḥ ca iti tad na ‘yaḥ ta āśiṣaḥ ityādinā phalam anicchataḥ  guṇa lobhena yā bhaktiḥ tasyāḥ tu garīyaḥ tvam yad  pratipāditam tad tattva sākṣātkāre tvarā sampādakam na tu mukti tāratamyākṣepakam abhaktiḥ siddhe ariti ādinā pratipāditam garīyaḥ tvam api tad janakatva mātreṇa putrāt pituḥ iva yad tu—‘anye tu evam ajānantaḥ śrutvā anyebhya upāsate te api ca atitaranti eva mṛtyum śruti parāyaṇāḥ iti atra api śabdena ‘striyaḥ  vaiśyāḥ tathā śudrāḥ te api yānti parām gatim kim punar brāhmaṇāḥ puṇyā bhaktā rājarṣayaḥ tathā iti atra kaim utyena ca sādhana tāratamyena sādhye tad pratītiḥ iti tad na na hi taraṇe api iti asya anvayaḥ kiṃtu adhikāriṇi tathā ca vilambita taraṇa rūpa phala sambandha mātra paryavasānāt  kaimutyasya api tvarā phala lābha mātreṇa upapatteḥ sādhana mātra tāratamyasya phala tāratamya aprayojaka tvāt ca na hi daṇḍa tāratamyena ghaṭa tāratamyam kvacid api dṛśyate yad tu sādhanasya uttama tvena sādhyam uttamam āpnuyuḥ brahma ādayaḥ krameṇa eva yathā ānanda śrutau śrutāḥ iti brahmāṇḍe aadhikam tava vijñānam adhikā ca gatiḥ tave ati sākṣāt mokṣa dharme ca sādhana tāratamyena sādhye tad uktiḥ iti tad na sādhana uttama tvena sādhya uttama tvasya aparama mukti viṣaya tvāt vijñāna gata adhikya ukteḥ api sākṣātkāra prayojaka sa guṇa viṣayaka jñāna paratvāt ca ata eva dahara ādi vidyānām adhika alpa guṇa viṣayaka tvena sādhana tāratamyam yad para abhimatam tad api evam iti na kaścid doṣaḥ tasmāt svarūpa ānandasya sva prakāśa ātma rūpiṇaḥ prāpti muktiḥ na tatra asti tāratamyam kathaṃcana iti advaita siddhau muktau tāratamya bhaṅgaḥ yaḥ  lakṣmyā nikhila anupekṣya vibudha an ekaḥ  vṛtaḥ sva icchayā yaḥ sarvān smṛta mātra eva satatam sarva ātmanā rakṣati yaḥ cakreṇa nikṛtya nakram akarot muktam mahā kuñjaram dveṣeṇa api dadāti yaḥ  nija padam tasmai namaḥ  viṣṇave śrī mādhava sarasvatyaḥ  jayanti yaminām varāḥ vayam yeṣām prasādena śāstra arthe pariniṣṭhitāḥ sahaja saralām premṇā dīrghām samasta viśodhinīm sakṛt api kṛpā dṛṣṭim santaḥ  diśantu bhavadvidhāḥ katham api satī pūtā sadyas tayā viṣayīkṛtā mama kṛtiḥ iyam hitvā doṣān bhavatu ati sahuṇā gurūṇām māhātmyāt nija vividha vidyā paricayāt  śruteḥ yad me samyak manana pariniṣpannam abhavat  para brahma ānanda sphuraṇam akhila anartha śamanam tad etasmin granthe nikhilam atiyatnena nihitam iha kumati rata tve tattva vādī varākaḥ pralapati yad akāṇḍe khaṇḍanābhāsamuccais  prativacanam amuṣmai tasya kaḥ  vaktu vidvān na hi rutam anurauti grāma siṃhasya siṃhaḥ kutarka garala ākulam bhiṣajitum manaḥ  durdhiyām mayā ayam uditaḥ  mudā viṣa vighātimatraḥ  mahān anena sakala āpadām vighaṭanena yad me abhavat  param sukṛtam arpitam tad akhila īśvare śrīpatau granthasya etasya yaḥ kartā stūyatām vā sa nindya tām mayi na asti eva kartṛ tvam ananyā anubhava ātmani śrī vyāsa śaṅkara sura īśvara padma pādān vedānta śāstra su nibandha kṛtaḥ tathā anyān vidyā pradān i ha yati pravarān dayālūn sarvān gurūn satatam eva namāmi bhaktyā siddhīnām iṣṭa naiṣkarmya brahma gānām iyam cirāt  advaita siddhiḥ adhunā caturthī samajāyata
